yuṣmad asmat pratyaya gocarayoḥ viṣaya viṣayiṇoḥ tamaḥ prakāśa vat viruddha svabhāvayoḥ itaretara bhāva aupapattau siddhāyām tad dharmāṇām api sutarām itaretara bhāva aupapattiḥ iti atas asmad pratyaya gocare viṣayiṇi cit ātmake yuṣmad pratyaya gocarasya viṣayasya tad dharmāṇām ca adhyāsaḥ tad viparyayeṇa viṣayiṇaḥ tad dharmāṇām ca viṣaye adhyāsaḥ mithyā iti bhavitum yuktam tathā api ayoyasmi ayoya ātmaka tām ayoya dharmān ca adhyasya itaretara aviveke atyata viviktayoḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ mithyājñā aimittaḥ satya aṛte mithuīkṛtya aham idam mama idam iti aisārgikaḥ ayam loka vyavahāraḥ āhakaḥ ayam adhyāsaḥ ucyate smṛti rūpaḥ paratra pūrva dṛṣṭa avabhāsaḥ tam iti vadati kecid tu yatra yad adhyāsaḥ bhrama iti aye tu yatra yad adhyāsaḥ tasya eva viparīta dharma tva kalpa ām ācakṣate iti sarvathā api tu vyabhicarati tathā ca loke aubhavaḥ śuktikā hi rajata vat avabhāsate ekaḥ cadraḥ sa dvitīya vat iti katham puas pratyagātmay a viṣaye adhyāsaḥ viṣaya tad dharmāṇām sarvaḥ hi puras avasthite viṣaye viṣayātaram adhyasyati yuṣmad pratyaya apetasya ca aviṣaya tvam bravīṣi ucyate tāvat ayam asmad pratyaya viṣaya tvāt aparokṣa tvāt ca pratyagātma prasiddheḥ a ca ayam asti eva viṣaye viṣayātaram adhyasitavyam iti apratyakṣe api hi ākāśe bālāḥ tala mali atā ādi adhyasyati evam aviruddhaḥ pratyagātmay api ātma adhyāsaḥ tam etam evaṃlakṣaṇam adhyāsam paṇḍitāḥ avidyā iti mayate ca vastu svarūpa avadhāraṇam vidyām āhuḥ tatra evam sati yatra yad adhyāsaḥ doṣeṇa vā aṇu mātreṇa api sa sambadhyate tam etam avidyā ākhyam itaretara adhyasam puraskṛtya sarve pramāṇa prameya vyavahārāḥ laukikāḥ vaidikāḥ ca pravṛttāḥ sarvāṇi ca śāstrāṇi vidhi pratiṣedha mokṣa parāṇi katham avidyāvat viṣayāṇi pramāṇāi śāstrāṇi ca iti ucyate deha idriya ādiṣu pramātṛ tva aupapattau pramāṇa pravṛtti aupapatteḥ hi idriyāṇi pratyakṣa ādi vyavahāraḥ saṃbhavati a ca adhiṣṭhāam vyavahāraḥ saṃbhavati a ca a adhyasta ātma bhāve dehe kaścid vyāpriyate a ca etasmin sarvasmin asati asaṅgasya ātmanaḥ pramātṛ tvam upapadyate ca pramātṛ tvam atareṇa pramāṇa pravṛttiḥ asti tasmāt avidyāvat viṣayāṇi eva pratyakṣa ādīni śāstrāṇi ca paśu ādibhiḥ ca aviśeṣāt yathā hi paśu ādayaḥ śabda ādibhiḥ śrotra ādīnām sati śabda ādi vijñāe pratikūle jāte aukūle ca pravartate yathā daṇḍa udyata karam puruṣam abhimukham upalabhya gām hatum ayam icchati iti palāyitum ārabhate harita tṛṇa pūrṇa pāṇim upalabhya tam prati abhimukhībhavati evam puruṣāḥ api krūra dṛṣṭī ākrośataḥ khaḍga udyata karāḥ balavataḥ upalabhya tad viparītā prati pravartate atas paśu ādibhiḥ puruṣāṇām pramāṇa prameya vyavahāraḥ paśu ādīām ca prasiddhaḥ aviveka puraḥasaraḥ pratyakṣa ādi vyavahāraḥ vyutpattimatām api puruṣāṇām pratyakṣa ādi vyavahāraḥ tad kālaḥ iti śāstrīye tu vyavahāre yadi api buddhi pūrva kārī adhikriyate tathā api adhikāre apekṣyate aupayogāt adhikāra virodhāt ca prāk ca tathābhūta ātma vijñāāt pravartamāam śāstram avidyāvat viṣaya tvam ātivartate tathā hi brāhmaṇaḥ yajeta ityādī śāstrāṇi varṇa āśrama vayaḥ avasthā ādi viśeṣa adhyāsam āśritya pravartate adhyāsaḥ tad buddhiḥ iti avocāma tat yathā putra bhāryā ādiṣu vikaleṣu sakaleṣu vā aham eva vikalaḥ sakalaḥ vā iti bāhya dharmāḥ adhyasyati tathā deha dharmāḥ sthūlaḥ aham kṛśaḥ aham gauḥ aham tiṣṭhāmi gacchāmi laṅghayāmi ca iti tathā idriya dharmā mūkaḥ kāṇaḥ klībaḥ badhiraḥ adhas aham iti tathā ataḥkaraṇa dharmā kāma saṃkalpa vicikitsā adhyavasāya ādī evam aham aśeṣa isva pracāra sākṣiṇi pratyagātmay adhyasya tam ca sarva sākṣiṇam tad viparyayeṇa ataḥkaraṇa ādiṣu adhyasyati evam ayam a ādiḥ a aisargikaḥ adhyāsaḥ mithyā pratyaya rūpaḥ kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva pravartakaḥ sarva loka pratyakṣaḥ asya a artha hetoḥ prahāṇāya ātma eka tva vidyā pratipattaye sarve ārabhyate sic yathā ca ayam arthaḥ sarveṣām tathā vayam asyām śārīraka mīmāṃsāyām pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ vedāta mīmāṃsā śāstrasya vyācikhyāsitasya idam ādimam sūtram prathama udhyāyaḥ prathamaḥ pādaḥ atha atas brahma jijñāsā jijñāsā adhikaraṇam atra atha śabdaḥ parigṛhyate ādhikāra arthaḥ brahma jijñāsāyāḥ a adhikārya tvāt maṅgalasya ca vākya arthe samavayā abhāvāt artha atara prayuktaḥ eva hi athaśabdaḥ śrutyāḥ maṅgala prayojaḥ bhavati pūrva prakṛta apekṣāyāḥ ca phalataḥ āataryā vyatirekāt sati ca āataryā artha tve yathā dharma jijñāsā pūrva vṛttam veda adhyayam evam brahma jijñāsā api yat pūrva vṛttam tat vaktavyam svādhyāya adhyaya āataryam tu iha karma avabodha āataryam viśeṣaḥ dharma jijñāsāyāḥ prāk api brahma jijñāsā upapatteḥ yathā ca kramasya vivakṣita tvāt a tathā iha kramaḥ vivakṣitaḥ śeṣa śeṣi tve adhikṛta adhikāre vā pramāṇa abhāvāt dharma brahma jijñāsayoḥ phala jijñāsya bhedāt ca abhyudaya phalam dharma jñāam tat iḥśreyasa phalam tu brahma jñāam bhavyaḥ ca dharmaḥ jijñāsyaḥ a jñā a kāle sti puruṣa vyāpāra tatra tvāt iha tu bhūtam brahma jijñāsyam a puruṣa vyāpāra tatram coda ā pravṛtti bhedāt ca yā hi codaā dharmasya lakṣaṇam sā sva viṣaye iyuñjāā eva puruṣam avabodhayati brahmacodaā tu puruṣam avabodhayati eva kevalam avabodhasya yathā akṣa artha saṃikarṣeṇa artha avabodhe tadvat tasmāt kim api vaktavyam yat brahma jijñāsā upadiśyate iti ucyate iha amutra artha bhoga virāgaḥ śama dama ādi sādha a saṃpad mumukṣu tvam ca teṣu hi satsu prāk api dharma jijñāsāyāḥ ūrdhvam ca śakyate brahma jijñāsitum jñātum ca a viparyaye tasmāt athaśabde upadiśyate atas śabdaḥ hetvarthaḥ yasmāt vedaḥ eva agihotra ādīām śreyaḥ sādhaāām aitya phalatām darśayati tat yathā iha karma citaḥ lokaḥ kṣīyate evam eva amutra puṇya citaḥ lokaḥ kṣīyate iti ādiḥ tathā brahma jñāāt api param puruṣa artham darśayati brahma vid param ityādiḥ tasmāt brahma jijñāsā kartavyā brahmaṇaḥ jijñāsā brahma jijñāsā brahma ca vakṣyamāṇa lakṣaṇam yatas iti atas eva a brahma śabdasya jāti ādi artha ataram āśaṅkitavyam brahmaṇaḥ iti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī a śeṣe jijñāsya apekṣa tvāt jijñāsāyāḥ ca śeṣa ṣaṣṭhī parigrahe api brahmaṇaḥ jijñāsā karma tvam as virudhyate viśeṣa eṣṭha tvāt evam api pratyakṣam brahmaṇaḥ karma tvam utsṛjya sāmāya dvāreṇa parokṣam karma tvam kalpayataḥ vyarthaḥ prayāsaḥ syāt a vyarthaḥ brahma āśrita aśeṣa vicāra pratijñā ārtha tvāt iti ced a pradhā a parigrahe tad apekṣitāām api artha ākṣipta tvāt brahma hi tasmi pradhāe jijñāsā karmaṇi parigṛhīte yaiḥ jijñāsitaiḥ brahma jijñāsitam a bhavati artha ākṣiptāy eva iti a pṛthak sūtrayitavyāi yathā rājā asau gacchati iti ukte sa parivārasya rājñaḥ uktam bhavati tadvat śruti augamāt ca yatas vai imāi bhūtāi jāyate ityādyāḥ śrutayaḥ tat vijijñāsasva tat brahma iti pratyakṣam eva brahmaṇaḥ jijñāsā karma tvam darśayati tat ca karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī parigrahe bhavati tasmāt brahmaṇaḥ iti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī jñātum icchā jijñāsā avagati paryatam sa vācyāyāḥ icchāyāḥ karma phala viṣaya tvāt icchāyāḥ hi hi pramāṇeā avagatum iṣṭam brahma brahma avagatiḥ hi puruṣa arthaḥ tasmāt brahma jijñāsitavyam tat puar brahma prasiddham aprasiddham vā syāt yadi prasiddham a jijñāsitavyam atha aprasiddham śakyam jijñāsitum iti ucyate asti tāvat brahma iti aśuddha buddha mukta svabhāvam sarvajñam sarva śakti samavitam brahma śabdasya hi pratīyate bṛṃhateḥ dhātoḥ artha augamāt sarvasya ātma tvāt ca brahma astitva prasiddhiḥ sarvaḥ hi ātma astitvam pratyeti a ā aham asmi iti yadi hi ātma astitva prasiddhiḥ syāt sarvaḥ lokaḥ ā aham asmi iti pratīyāt ātmā ca brahma yadi tarhi loke brahma prasiddham asti tatas jñātam eva iti ajijñāsya tvam tad viśeṣam prati vipratipatteḥ deha mātram caitaya viśiṣṭam ātmā iti prākṛtāḥ laukāyatikāḥ ca idriyāṇi eva ātmā iti apare iti vijñāa mātram kṣaṇikam iti eke iti apare asti deha ādi vyatiriktaḥ saṃsārī kartā bhoktā iti apare bhoktā eva kevalam a kartā iti eke asti tad vyatiriktaḥ īśvaraḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva śaktiḥ iti kecid ātmā sa bhoktuḥ iti apare evam bahavaḥ vipratipaāḥ yukti vākya tad ābhāsa samāśrayāḥ sataḥ tatra a vicārya yat kiṃcid iḥśreyasāt ca iyāt tasmāt tad avirodhi tarka upakaraṇā prastūyate brahma jijñāsitavyam iti uktam kiṃlakṣaṇam tat brahma iti atas āha bhagavān sūtrakāraḥ asya yatas jama ādi adhikaraṇam jamaḥ utpattiḥ ādiḥ asya iti tad guṇa saṃvijñāḥ bahuvrīhiḥ jama sthiti bhaṅgam samāsa arthaḥ ca ādi tvam śrutiirdeśa apekṣam vastu vṛtta apekṣam ca śrutiirdeśaḥ tāvat yatas vā imā idam anyā anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya any bhūtāi jāyate iti asmi vākye krama darśaāt vastu vṛttam api labdha sattākasya dharmiṇaḥ sthiti pralaya saṃbhavāt asya iti pratyakṣa ādi saṃidhāpitasya dharmiṇaḥ idam ā irdeśaḥ ṣaṣṭhī yatas iti kāraṇaiḥ deśaḥ asya jagataḥ āma rūpābhyām vyākṛtasya a eka kartṛ bhoktṛ saṃyuktasya pratiiyata deśa kā laimitta kriyā phala āśrayasya a citya raca a rūpasya yatas sarvajñāt sarva śakteḥ kāraṇāt bhavati tat brahma iti vākya śeṣaḥ api bhāva vikārāṇām triṣu iti iha grahaṇam yāska paripaṭhitāām tu jāyate sti ityādīām grahaṇe teṣām jagataḥ sthiti kāle mūlakāraṇāt utpatti sthitiāḥ ā jagataḥ a gṛhītāḥ syuḥ iti āśaṅkyeta iti yā utpattiḥ brahmaṇaḥ kāraṇāt tatra eva sthitiḥ pralayaḥ ca te gṛhyate ca yathā ukta viśeṣaṇasya jagataḥ yathā ukta viśeṣaṇam īśvaram muktvā ayataḥ aṇubhyaḥ vā abhāvāt vā saṃsāriṇaḥ vā utpatti ādi saṃbhāvayitum śakyam ca svabhāvataḥ viśiṣṭa deśa kāla aimittāām iha upādāāt etat saṃsāri vyatirikta īśvara astitva ādi sādhaam iha api tat sūtrāṇām hi sūtraiḥ udāhṛtya vicāryate vākya artha vicāraṇa adhyavasāaiḥ vṛttā hi brahma avagatiḥ āumā ādi pramāṇa ataraiḥ vṛttā satsu tu vedāta vākyeṣu jagataḥ ādi kāraṇa vādiṣu tad artha ārḍhyāya api vedāta vākya avirodhi pramāṇam śrutyā eva ca tarkasya api abhyupeta tvāt tathā hi śrotavyaḥ matavyaḥ iti śrutiḥ paṇḍitaḥ medhāvī upasaṃpadyeta evam eva iha ācārya vā puruṣaḥ veda iti ca puruṣa buddhi sāhāyyam darśayati a dharma jijñasāyām iva śruti ādayaḥ eva pramāṇam brahma jijñāsāyām kiṃtu śruti ādayaḥ ubhava ādayaḥ ca yathāsaṃbhavam iha pramāṇam bhūta vastu viṣaya tvāt ca brahma jñāasya kartavye hi viṣaye āubhava apekṣā asti iti śruti ādīām eva prāmāṇyam syāt puruṣa adhī ātma lābha tvāt ca kartavyasya kartum a kartum ayathā vā kartum śakyam laukikam vaidikam ca karma yathā gacchati padbhyām ayathā vā a vā gacchati iti tathā atirātre ṣoḍaśiam gṛhṇāti ā atirātre ṣoḍaśiam gṛhṇāti udite juhoti audite juhoti iti vidhi pratiṣedhāḥ ca atra arthavataḥ syuḥ vikalpa utsarga apavādāḥ ca a tu vastu evam aivam asti āsti iti vā vikalpyate vikalpaāḥ tu puruṣa buddhi apekṣāḥ puruṣa buddhi apekṣam kim tarhi vastutatram eva tat hi sthāṇau ekasmin sthāṇuḥ vā puruṣaḥ yaḥ vā iti tattva jñāam bhavati tatra puruṣaḥ yaḥ vā iti mithyā jñāam sthāṇuḥ eva iti tattva jñāam vastu tatra tvāt evam bhūta vastu viṣayāṇām prāmāṇyam vastu tatram tatra evam sati api eva bhūta vastu viṣaya tvāt bhūta vastu viṣaya tve brahmaṇaḥ pramāṇa atara viṣaya tvam eva iti a arthikā eva prāptā svabhāvataḥ viṣaya viṣayāṇi idriyāṇi a brahma viṣayāṇi sati hi idriya viṣaya tve brahmaṇaḥ idam brahmaṇā saṃbaddham kāryam iti gṛhyeta kārya mātram eva tu gṛhyamāṇam kim brahmaṇā saṃbaddham kim keacid vā saṃbaddham iti a śakyam tasmāt jama ādi sūtram kim tarhi vedāta vākya pradarśa artham kim puas tat vedāta vākyam yat sūtreṇa iha bhṛguḥ vai vāruṇiḥ varuṇam pitaram upasasāra adhīhi bhagavaḥ brahma iti iti upakramya āha yatas vai imāi bhūtāi jāyate jīvati yat prayati abhisaṃviśati tat vijijñāsasva tat brahma iti tasya ca irṇaya vākyam āadāt hi eva khalu imāi bhūtāi jāyate jīvati prayati abhisaṃviśati iti api evaṃjātīyakāi vākyāi iti aśuddha buddham ukta svabhāva sarvajña sva rūpa kāraṇa viṣayāṇi udāhartavyāi sarvajñam brahma iti upakṣiptam tat eva āha śāstrayoitvāt sarvajñam brahma iti upakṣiptam tat eva āha mahataḥ ṛgveda ādeḥ śāstrasya mahataḥ ṛgveda ādeḥ śāstrasya mahataḥ ṛgveda ādeḥ śāstrasya pradīpa vat sarva artha avadyotiḥ sarvajña kalpasya kāraṇam brahma hi īdṛśasya śāstrasya ṛgveda ādi lakṣaṇasya sarvajña guṇa āvitasya sarvajña ādayataḥ yat yat vistara artham śāstram yasmāt puruṣa viśeṣāt saṃbhavati yathā vyākaraṇa ādi jñeya eka deśa artham api saḥ iti prasiddham loke kimu vaktavyam deva tiryak mauṣya varṇa āśrama ādi pravibhāga hetoḥ ṛgveda ādi ākhyasya sarvajña ākarasya yasmai mahataḥ bhūtāt saṃbhavaḥ asya mahataḥ bhūtasya etat yat ṛgvedaḥ ityādi śruteḥ tasya mahataḥ bhūtasya sarvajña tvam sarva śaktimat tvam ca iti athavā yathā uktam ṛgveda ādi śāstram kāraṇam pramāṇam asya brahmaṇaḥ yathāvat svarūpa adhigame śāstrāt eva pramāṇāt jagataḥ jama ādi kāraṇam brahma adhigamyate iti abhiprāyaḥ śāstram udāhṛtam pūrva sūtre yatas vā imāi bhūtāi jāyate ityādi kimartham tarhi idam sūtram yāvatā pūrva sūtreṇa eva evaṃjātīyakam śāstram udāharatā brahmaṇaḥ darśitam ucyate tatra sūtra akṣareṇa spaṣṭam jama ādi sūtreṇa kevalam upayastam iti āśaṅkyeta tām āśaṅkām ivartayitum idam sūtram pravavṛte iti katham brahmaṇaḥ śāstra pramāṇaka tvam ucyate yāvatā āmāyasya kriyā artha tvāt āarthakyam iti kriyā para tvam śāstrasya pradarśitam atas vā kriyā vidhi śeṣa tvam vā hi saṃbhavati pratyakṣa ādi viṣaya tvāt ca heya upādeya rahite puruṣa artha abhāvāt atas eva saḥ arodīt iti evamādīām āarthakyam mā bhūt iti tu ekavākya tvāt stuti arthe syuḥ iti stāvaka tve ārthavat tvam uktam matrāṇām ca iṣe tvā ityādīām karma samavāyi tvam uktam atas kvacid api veda vākyāām vidhi saṃsparśam dṛṣṭā vā ca pariiṣṭhite vastu svarūpe vidhiḥ saṃbhavati kriyā viṣaya tvāt vidheḥ tasmāt karma apekṣita kartṛ devatā ādi sva rūpa prakāśa kriyā vidhi śeṣa tvam atha brahmaṇaḥ iti prāpte ucyate tat tu samavayāt samavayā adhikaraṇam tuśabdaḥ pūrvapakṣa vyāvṛtti arthaḥ tat brahma sarvajñam sarva śakti jagat utpatti sthiti laya kāraṇam vedāta śāstrāt avagamyate katham samavayāt sarveṣu hi tātparyeṇa etasya arthasya samaugatāi sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam ātmā vai idam ekaḥ eva agre āsīt tat etat brahma apūrvam a aparam a ataram a bāhyam ayam ātmā brahma brahma brahma eva idam amṛtam purastāt ca tad gatāām padāām brahma sva rūpa viṣaye samavaye yuktā yuktā prasaṅgāt a ca teṣām kartṛ devatā ādi svarūpa pratipāda apara tā avasīyate tat kam paśyet ityādi kriyā kāraka phalaiḥ ākaraṇa śruteḥ a ca pariiṣṭhita vastu svarūpa tve pi pratyakṣa ādi viṣaya tvam brahmaṇaḥ tat tvam asi iti brahma ātma bhāvasya śāstram yat tu heya upādeya rahita tvāt upadeśa āarthakyam iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ heya upādeya śūya brahma ātmatā avagamāt eva sarva kleśa prahāṇāt puruṣa artha siddheḥ devatā ādi pratipāda aparasya tu sva vākya gata upāsa artha tve pi a kaścid virodhaḥ a tu tathā brahmaṇaḥ upāsaā vidhi śeṣa tvam saṃbhavati ekatve heya upādeya śūya tayā kriyā kāraka ādi dvaita vijñā upamarda upapatteḥ a hi dvaita vijñāasya sti brahmaṇaḥ pratipādyeta yadi api veda vākyāām vidhi saṃsparśam dṛṣṭam tathā api ātma vijñāasya phala paryata tvā a tad viṣayasya śāstrasya prāmāṇyam śakyam pratyākhyātum śāstra prāmāṇyam śāstra prāmāṇyam apekṣyeta tasmāt siddham brahmaṇaḥ śāstra pramāṇaka tvam atra apare pratyavatiṣṭhate yadi api śāstra pramāṇakam brahma tathā api pratipatti vidhi viṣaya tayā eva śāstreṇa brahma samarpyate yathā alaukikāy api vidhi śeṣa tayā śāstreṇa samarpyate tadvat kutas etat pravṛtti ivṛtti prayoja aparatvāt śāstrasya tathā hi śāstra tātparya vidām dṛṣṭaḥ hi tasya arthaḥ karma avabodha iti kriyāyāḥ pravartakam tasya upadeśaḥ upadeśaḥ tad bhūtāām samāmāyaḥ āmāyasya kriyā artha tvāt āarthakyam iti ca atas puruṣam kvacid viṣaya viśeṣe pravartayat kutaścid viṣaya viśeṣāḥ ca arthavat śāstram tad śeṣa tayā upayuktam api tathā eva arthavat tvam syāt sati ca vidhi paratve yathā vidhīyate evam amṛta tva kāmasya brahma jñāam vidhīyate iti yuktam iha jijñāsya vailakṣaṇyam uktam karmakāṇḍe bhavya uktam dharmaḥ jijñāsyaḥ iha tu bhūtam ityaiḥ vṛttam brahma jijñāsyam iti tatra dharma jñā phalāt vilakṣaṇam brahma jñā phalam bhavitum arhati ārhati evam bhavitum kārya vidhi prayuktasya eva brahmaṇaḥ ātmā vai are draṣṭavyaḥ yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā saḥ veṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ ātmā iti eva upāsīta ātmāam eva lokam upāsīta brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati ityādiṣu satsu satsu saḥ aḥ ātmā kim tat brahma iti ākāṅkṣāyām sarve upayuktāḥ ityaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva gataḥ iti aśuddha buddha mukta svabhāvaḥ brahma iti evamādayaḥ tad upāsaāt ca śāstra dṛṣṭaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ mokṣaḥ phalam bhaviṣyati tu saptadvīpā vasumatī rājā asau gacchati ityādi vākya vat āarthakyam eva syāt rajjuḥ iyam sarpaḥ ityādau dṛṣṭam tathā iha api syāt syāt etat evam yadi rajju sva rūpa śravaṇa mātreṇa iva sarpa bhrātiḥ saṃsāri tva bhrātiḥ brahma sva rūpa śravaṇa mātreṇa tu tu iva ṛtate śruta brahmaṇaḥ pi yathāpūrvam sukha duḥkha ādi saṃsāri dharma darśaāt śrotavyaḥ matavyaḥ ididhyāsitavyaḥ iti ca śravaṇa uttara kālayoḥ vidhi darśaāt tasmāt pratipatti vidhi viṣaya tayā eva śāstra pramāṇakam brahma abhyupagatavyam iti atra abhidhīyate a karma brahma vidyā phalayoḥ vailakṣaṇyāt śārīram vācikam māasam ca karma śruti smṛti siddham dharma ākhyam yad viṣayā jijñāsā atha atas dharma jijñāsā iti sūtritā adharmaḥ u pi hiṃsā ādiḥ pratiṣedha coda ālakṣaṇa tvāt jijñāsyaḥ parihārāya tayoḥ coda ālakṣaṇayoḥ artha aarthayoḥ dharma adharmayoḥ phale pratyakṣe sukha duḥkhe śarīra vāc viṣaya idriya saṃyoga jaye brahma ādiṣu sthāvarāteṣu prasiddhe mauṣya tvāt ārabhya brahmāteṣu dehavatsu sukha tāratamyam tatas ca tad hetoḥ dharmasya api tāratamyam gamyate dharma tāratamyāt adhikāri tāratamyam prasiddham ca arthi tva sāmarthya vidvas tā ādi kṛtam adhikāri tāratamyam tathā ca eva vidyā samādhi viśeṣāt uttareṇa pathā gamaam kevalaiḥ dhūma ādi krameṇa pathā gamaam tatra api sukha tāratamyam tad sādhaa tāramyam ca śāstrāt yāvat saṃpātam uṣitvā iti asmāt gamyate tathā mauṣī ādiṣu sukha lavaḥ eva iti gamyate tāratamye tathā ūrdhva gateṣu adhas gateṣu ca dehavatsu duḥkha tāratamya darśaāt tad hetoḥ adharmasya ca tāratamyam gamyate evam avidyā ādi doṣavatām dharma adharma tāratamya aimittam śarīra upādāa pūrvakam sukha duḥkha tāratamyam aityam saṃsāra rūpam śruti smṛti yāya prasiddham tathā ca śrutiḥ a ha vai sa śarīrasya sataḥ priya apriyayoḥ apahatiḥ asti iti yathā varṇitam saṃsāra rūpam auvadati aśarīram vāva satam a priya apriye spṛśataḥ iti priya apriya sparśa a pratiṣedhāt mokṣa ākhyasya aśarīra tvasya pratiṣidhyate iti gamyate dharma kārya tve hi priya apriya sparśa a pratiṣedhaḥ opapadyeta aśarīra tvam eva dharma kāryam iti ced a tasya svābhāvika tvāt aśarīram śarīreṣu a avastheṣu avasthitam vibhum matvā dhīraḥ śocati aprāṇaḥ hi śubhraḥ a saṅgaḥ hi ayam puruṣaḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ atas mokṣa ākhyam aśarīra tvam ityam iti siddham tatra kiṃcid pariṇāmi ityam syāt vikriyamāṇe api tat eva idam iti buddhiḥ yathā yathā vā sāṃkhyāām guṇāḥ idam tu pāramārthikam kūṭasthaityam vyoma vat sarva vyāpi sarva vikriyā rahitam iti atṛptam svayam jyotiḥ svabhāvam yatra dharma adharmau saha kāryeṇa kāla trayam ca opāvartete tat etat aśarīra tvam mokṣa ākhyam ayatra dharmāt ayatra adharmāt ayatra asmāt kṛta akṛtāt ayatra bhūtāt ca bhavyāt ca ityādi śrutibhyaḥ atas tat brahma yasya iyam jijñāsā prastutā tat yadi kartavya śeṣa tve upadiśyeta ca kartavyea sādhyaḥ ced mokṣaḥ abhyupagamyeta aityaḥ eva syāt tatra evam sati yathā ukta karma phaleṣu eva tāratamya avasthiteṣu aityeṣu kaścid atiśayaḥ mokṣaḥ iti prasajyeta ityaḥ ca mokṣaḥ sarvaiḥ mokṣa vādibhiḥ abhyupagamyate atas brahma upadeśaḥ yuktaḥ api ca brahma veda brahma eva bhavati kṣīyate ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare brahmaṇaḥ vidvā a bibheti kutas caa abhayam vai si tat ātmā am eva avet aham brahma asmi iti tasmāt tat sarvam abhavat tatra kaḥ mohaḥ kaḥ śokaḥ eka tvam iti evamādyāḥ śrutayaḥ eva mokṣam darśayatyaḥ u madhye kāryātaram vārayati tathā tat ha etat paśya ṛṣiḥ vāmadevaḥ pratipede ham mauḥ abhavam sūryaḥ ca iti brahma darśa a sarva ātma bhāvayoḥ madhye kartavya ātara vāraṇāya udāhāryam yathā tiṣṭha gāyati iti tiṣṭhati gāyatyoḥ madhye tad kartṛkam kārya ātaram āsti iti gamyate tvam hi pitā smākam avidyāyāḥ param pāram tārayasi śrutam hi eva me bhagavat dṛśebhyaḥ tarati śokam ātma vid iti saḥ ham bhagavaḥ śocāmi tam mā bhagavān śokasya pāram tārayatu tasmai mṛdita kaṣāyāya tamasaḥ pāram darśayati bhagavā iti ca evamādyāḥ śrutayaḥ phalam darśayati tathā ca ācārya praṇītam yāya upabṛṃhitam sūtram uttara uttara apāye apavargaḥ iti mithyājñā apāyaḥ ca brahma ātma eka tva vijñāāt bhavati ca idam brahma ātma eka tva vijñāam saṃpad rūpam yathā vai viśvedevāḥ eva sa tea lokam jayati iti ca adhyāsa rūpam yathā mao brahma iti upāsīta ādityaḥ brahma iti ādeśaḥ iti ca maaāditya ādiṣu brahma dṛṣṭi adhyāsaḥ viśiṣṭa kriyā yaḥ gaimittam vāyuḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ prāṇaḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ itivat āpi ājya avekṣaṇa ādi karma vat karma aṅga saṃskāra rūpam saṃpad ādi rūpe hi brahma ātma eka tva vijñāe bhyupagamyamāe tat tvam asi aham brahma asmi ayam ātmā brahma iti evamādīām vākyāām brahma ātma eka tva vastu pratipāda a paraḥ pīḍyeta bhidyate hṛdayagrathiḥ chidyate sarva saṃśayāḥ iti ca evamādīn avidyā a vṛtti phala śravaṇāy uparudhyera brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati iti saṃpad ādi rūpa tve saṃpad ādi rūpa tve tasmai a saṃpad ādi rūpam brahma ātma eka tva vijñāam atas brahma vidyā kim tarhi vastu tatra eva evaṃbhūtasya brahmaṇas ca a kayācid yuktyā śakyaḥ kārya āupraveśaḥ kalpayitum a ca brahmaṇaḥ eva tad viditāt atha u a viditāt adhi iti vidi kriyā karma tva pratiṣedhāt tam ke vijāīyāt iti ca tathā upāsti kriyā karma tva pratiṣedhaḥ u bhavati yat vācā abhyuditam vāc abhyudyate iti aviṣaya tvam brahmaṇaḥ tat eva brahma tvam viddhi ā idam yat idam upāsate iti aviṣaya tve brahmaṇaḥ iti ced a avidyā kalpita bheda evṛtti paratvāt śāstrasya hi śāstram idaṃtayā viṣaya bhūtam brahma pratipipādayiṣati kim tarhi pratyagātma tve aviṣaya tayā pratipādayat avidyā kalpitam vedya veditṛ veda ādi bhedam apaayati tathā ca śāstram yasya amatam tasya matam matam yasya a veda saḥ avijñātam vijāatām vijñātam avijāatām a dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭāram paśyeḥ a śruteḥ śrotāram śrṛṇuyāḥ a mateḥ matāram mavīthāḥ a vijñāteḥ vijñātāram iti ca evamādi atas iti a mukta ātma svarūpa samarpaṇā iti a mokṣasya aitya tva doṣaḥ yasya tu utpādyaḥ mokṣaḥ tasya māasam vācikam kāyikam vā kāryam apekṣate iti yuktam tathā vikārya tve ca tayoḥ pakṣayoḥ mokṣasya dhruvam aitya tvam a hi dadhi ādi vikāryam utpādyam vā ghaṭa ādi dṛṣṭam loke kārya apekṣā svātma svarūpa tve satī a āpya tvāt svarūpa vyatirikta tve brahmaṇaḥ āpya tvam sarvagata tve iti āpta svarūpa tvāt sarveṇa brahmaṇaḥ ākāśasya iva saṃskāryaḥ mokṣaḥ vyāpāram apekṣeta saṃskāraḥ hi saṃskāryasya vā syāt vā a tāvat saṃbhavati mokṣasya āpi iti aśuddha brahma svarūpa tvā mokṣasya sva ātma dharmaḥ eva sa tirobhūtaḥ mokṣaḥ kriyayā ātmai saṃskriyamāṇe bhivyajyate yathā ādarśe saṃskriyamāṇe bhāsvara tvam dharmaḥ iti ced a kriyā āśraya tva aupapatteḥ ātmanaḥ yad āśrayā kriyā tam a vikurvatī labhate yadi ātmā sva āśraya kriyayā vikriyeta aitya tvam ātmanaḥ prasajyeta avikāryaḥ yam ucyate iti bādhyera tat ca aiṣṭam tasmai a sva āśrayā kriyā ātman saṃbhavati tu kriyāyāḥ aviṣaya tvā tayā ātmā saṃskriyate deha āśrayayā kriyayā dehī saṃskriyamāṇaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ a deha ādi saṃhatasya eva avidyā gṛhītasya ātmaaḥ saṃskriyamāṇa tvāt pratyakṣam hi sāācama ādeḥ deha samavāyi tvam tayā deha āśrayayā tad saṃhataḥ eva kaścid avidyayā ātma tve parigṛhītaḥ saṃskriyate iti yuktam yathā dhātu sāmyea tad saṃhatasya ārogya phalam aham arogaḥ iti yatra buddhiḥ utpadyate evam aham śuddhaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ iti yatra buddhiḥ utpadyate sa saṃskriyate sa ca saṃhataḥ eva ahaṃkartrā ahaṃpratyaya viṣayeṇa sarvāḥ kriyāḥ tad phalam ca saḥ eva āśāti tayoḥ ayaḥ pippalam svādu atti ayaḥ bhicākaśīti iti matra varṇāt bhoktā iti āhuḥ maīṣiṇaḥ iti ca tathā ekaḥ devaḥ sarva bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarva vyāpī sarva bhūta atarātmā karma adhyakṣaḥ sarva bhūta adhivāsaḥ sākṣī cetā kevalaḥ irguṇaḥ ca iti sa paryāgāt śukram akāyam avraṇam a sāviram śuddham a pāpa viddham iti ca etau matrau iti aśuddha tām ca brahmaṇaḥ darśayataḥ brahma bhāvaḥ ca mokṣaḥ tasmai a saṃskāryaḥ pi mokṣaḥ atas mokṣam prati śakyam keacid darśayitum tasmāt ekam muktvā kriyāyāḥ iha opapadyate jñāam kriyā a vailakṣaṇyāt kriyā sā yatra vastu svarūpaiḥ apekṣā eva codyate ca yathā yasyai devatāyai haviḥ gṛhītam syāt tām maasā dhyāyet vaṣaṭ kariṣye iti saṃdhyām maasā dhyāyet iti ca evamādiṣu citaam yadi api māasam tathā api puruṣeṇa kartum a kartum ayathā vā kartum śakyam puruṣa tatra tvāt tu pramāṇa jayam pramāṇam ca yathā bhūta vastu viṣayam atas kartum a kartum ayathā vā kartum a śakyam kevalam vastutatram eva tat puruṣatatram tasmāt māasa tve mahat vailakṣaṇyam yathā ca puruṣaḥ vāva gautama āgiḥ yoṣā vāva gautama āgiḥ iti atra yoṣit puruṣayoḥ agi buddhiḥ māasī bhavati kevala coda ājaya tvāt tu kriyā eva sā puruṣa tatrā ca yā tu prasiddhe gau a gi buddhiḥ sā puruṣa tatrā kim tarhi pratyakṣa viṣaya vastu tatra eva iti eva etat a kriyā evam sarva pramāṇa viṣaya vastuṣu veditavyam tatra evam sati yathā bhūta brahma ātma viṣayam api tad viṣaye liṅ ādayaḥ śrūyamāṇāḥ api aiyojya viṣaya tvāt kuṇṭhībhavati upala ādiṣu prayukta kṣura taikṣṇya ādi vat aheya aupādeya vastu viṣaya tvāt tarhi ātmā vā are draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ ityādīi vidhi chāyāi svābhāvika pravṛtti viṣaya vimukhīkaraṇa arthāi iti brūmaḥ yaḥ hi bahirmukhaḥ pravartate puruṣaḥ iṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣṭam anupraviṣ me bhūyāt aiṣṭam mā bhūt iti a ca tatra ātyatikam puruṣa artham labhate tam ātyatika puruṣa artha vāñchiam svābhāvikāt kārya karaṇa saṃghāta pravṛtti gocarāt vimukhīkṛtya pratyagātma srotaḥ tayā pravartayati ātmā vā are draṣṭavyaḥ ityādi tasya ātma āveṣaṇāya pravṛttasya aheyam aupādeyam ca ātma tattvam upadiśyate idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kam paśyet vijñātāram are vijñātāram are ayam ātmā brahma ityādibhiḥ yat api a kartavya pradhāam ātma jñāam vā bhavati iti tat tathā eva iti abhyupagamyate alaṃkāraḥ hi ayam asmākam yat brahma ātmau agatau satyām sarva kartavya tā hāiḥ kṛtakṛtya tā ca iti tathā ca śrutiḥ ced vijāīyāt ayam asmi iti pūruṣaḥ kim iccha kasya kāmāya śarīram iti etat buddhvā buddhim āsyāt kṛtakṛtyaḥ ca bhārataḥ iti ca smṛtiḥ tasmai a pratipatti vidhi śeṣa tayā brahmaṇaḥ samarpaṇam yat api kecid āhuḥ kevala vastu vādī veda bhāgaḥ āsti iti te aupaiṣadasya puruṣasya a yaśeṣa tvāt eva adhigataḥ saṃsārī brahma sva rūpaḥ utpādi ādi caturvidha dravya vilakṣaṇaḥ sva prakaraṇa sthaḥ āsau āsti iti ādhigamyate iti vā śakyam vaditum saḥ eṣaḥ eti eti ātmā iti ātma śabdāt ca pratyākhyātum aśakya tvāt yaḥ eva irā kartā tasya eva ātma tvāt ātmā ahaṃpratyaya viṣaya tvāt upaiṣatsu eva vijñāyate iti aupapaam a pratyukta tvāt a hi ahaṃpratyaya viṣaya kartṛ vyatirekeṇa tad sākṣī sarva bhūta sthaḥ samaḥ ekaḥ kūṭasthaityaḥ puruṣaḥ vidhi kāṇḍe tarka samaye vā kaścid adhigataḥ sarvasya ātmā atas sa a kaścid pratyākhyātum śakyaḥ vidhi śeṣa tvam vā etum ātma tvāt eva ca sarveṣām a heyaḥ āpī upādeyaḥ sarvam hi viaśyat vikāra jātam viaśyati puruṣaḥ hi vikriyā hetu abhāvāt ca kūṭasthaityaḥ atas eva iti aśuddha buddha mukta svabhāvaḥ tasmāt puruṣāḥ a param kiṃcid sā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ tam tu aupaiṣadam puruṣam pṛcchāmi iti ca aupaiṣada tva viśeṣaṇam puruṣasya upaiṣatsu upapadyate atas bhūta vastu paraḥ veda bhāgaḥ sāhasa mātram yat api śāstra tātparya vidām dṛṣṭaḥ hi tasya arthaḥ iti evamādi tat dharma jijñāsā viṣaya tvāt vidhi pratiṣedha śāstra abhiprāyam draṣṭavyam api ca āmāyasya kriyā artha tvāt āarthakyam a tad arthāām iti etat bhūta upadeśāām āarthakya prasaṅgaḥ bhūtam ced vastu upadiśati kūṭasthaityam bhūtam upadiśati iti kaḥ hetuḥ hi bhūtam kriyā bhavati akriyā tve pi bhūtasya kriyā sādhaa tvāt kriyā artha eva bhūta upadeśaḥ iti ced ā eṣa doṣaḥ kriyā artha tve eva kriyā artha tvam tu tasya bhavati yadi kim tava syāt iti ucyate aavagata ātma vastu upadeśaḥ ca tathā eva bhavitum arhati tad avagatyā mithyājñāasya saṃsāra hetoḥ kriyate iti aviśiṣṭam arthavat tvam api ca brāhmaṇaḥ hatavyaḥ iti ca evamādyā upadiśyate ca sā kriyā kriyā sādhaam akriyā arthāām upadeśaḥ arthakaḥ ced brāhmaṇaḥ a hatavyaḥ ityādi ivṛtti upadeśāām āarthakyam prāptam tat ca aiṣṭam a ca a svabhāva prāpta hati artha au rāgeṇa añaḥ śakyam aprāpta kriyā artha tvam kalpayitum a vyatirekeṇa añaḥ ca eṣa svabhāvaḥ yat bhāvam bodhayati iti abhāva buddhiḥ ca audāsīye kāraṇam sā ca svayam eva upaśāmyati tasmāt prasakta kriyā aivṛtti audāsīyam eva brāhmaṇaḥ hatavyaḥ ityādiṣu pratiṣedha artham mayāmahe prajāpati vrata ādibhyaḥ tasmāt draṣṭavyam yat api uktam vastu mātram aarthakam syāt saptadvīpā vasumatī ityādi vat iti tat parihṛtam rajjuḥ iyam sarpaḥ iti dṛṣṭa tvāt śruta brahmaṇaḥ pi yathāpūrvam saṃsāri tva darśaāḥ a rajju sva rūpa kathaa vat arthavat tvam iti uktam atra ucyate āvagata brahma ātma bhāvasya yathāpūrvam saṃsāri tvam śakyam darśayitum veda pramāṇa jaita brahma ātma bhāva virodhāt hi śarīra ādi ātma abhimāiḥ duḥkha bhaya ādimat tvam dṛṣṭam iti tasya eva veda pramāṇa jaita brahma ātma avagame tad abhimāai vṛttau tat eva mithyājñā aimittam duḥkha bhaya ādimat tvam bhavati iti śakyam kalpayitum hi gṛhasthasya dhaā abhimāiḥ dhaā apahāra aimittam duḥkham dṛṣṭam iti tasya eva pravrajitasya dhaā abhimāa rahitasya tat eva dhaā apahāra aimittam duḥkham bhavati a ca kuṇḍaliaḥ kuṇḍali tva abhimāaimittam sukham dṛṣṭam iti tasya eva kuṇḍala viyuktasya kuṇḍali tva abhimāa rahitasya tat eva kuṇḍali tva abhimāaimittam sukham bhavati tat uktam śrutyā aśarīram vāva satam a priya apriye spṛśataḥ iti śarīre patite śarīra tvam syāt a jīvataḥ iti ced a sa śarīram tu asya mithyājñā aimitta tvāt hi ātmaaḥ śarīra ātma abhimā a lakṣaṇam mithyājñāam muktvā ayataḥ sa śarīra tvam śakyam kalpayitum aśarīra tvam a karma aimitta tvāt iti avocāma tat kṛta dharma adharma aimittam sa śarīra tvam iti ced aśarīra tvam śarīra saṃbadhasya asiddha tvāt dharma adharmayoḥ ātma kṛta tva asiddheḥ śarīra saṃbadhasya dharma adharmayoḥ tad kṛta tvasya ca itaretara āśraya tva prasaṅgāt kriyā samavāya abhāvāt kartṛ tva aupapatteḥ rāja prabhṛtīām dṛṣṭam kartṛ tvam iti ced teṣām kartṛ tva upapatteḥ a tu śarīra ādibhiḥ sva svāmi bhāva saṃbadha nimittam kiṃcid śakyam kalpayitum mithyā abhimāaḥ tu pratyakṣaḥ vyākhyātam atra āhuḥ deha ādi vyatiriktasya ātmanaḥ ātmīye deha ādau aham gauṇaḥ mithyā iti ced a prasiddha vastu bhedasya gauṇa tva mukhya tva prasiddheḥ yasya hi prasiddhaḥ vastu bhedaḥ yathā kesara ādi māā ākṛti viśeṣaḥ vaya vyatirekābhyām siṃha śabda pratyaya bhāj mukhyaḥ yaḥ siddhaḥ tatas ca ayaḥ puruṣaḥ prāyikaiḥ kraurya śaurya ādibhiḥ siṃha guṇaiḥ siddhaḥ tasya tasmin puruṣe siṃha śabda pratyayau gauṇau bhavataḥ ā prasiddha vastu bhedasya tasya tva eva bhavataḥ a gauṇau yathā mada adhakāre sthāṇuḥ ayam iti a gṛhyamāṇa viśeṣe puruṣa śabda pratyayau sthāṇu viṣayau yathā vā śuktikāyām akasmāt rajatam idam iti śabda pratyayau tadvat deha ādi saṃghāte aham iti śabda pratyayau ātma a ātma avivekena utpadyamāau katham gauṇau śakyau vaditum api paṇḍitāām aja avi pālāām iva a viviktau śabda pratyayau bhavataḥ tasmāt deha ādi vyatirikta ātma astitva vādiām dehāt āvaham pratyayaḥ mithyā eva a gauṇaḥ tasmāt mithyāpratyaya nimitta tvāt sa śarīra tvasya siddham jīvataḥ pi viduṣaḥ śarīra tvam tathā ca brahma vidviṣayā śrutiḥ tat yathā valmīke mṛtā pratyastā śayīta evam eva idam śarīram śete atha ayam aśarīraḥ mṛtaḥ prāṇaḥ brahma eva tejaḥ eva iti sa cakṣuḥ a cakṣuḥ iva sa karṇaḥ karṇaḥ iva sa vāc avāc iva sa maāḥ amaāḥ iva sa prāṇo prāṇaḥ iva iti ca smṛtiḥ api sthita prajñasya kā bhāṣā ityādyā sthita prajñasya lakṣaṇāya ācakṣāṇāḥ viduṣaḥ darśayati tasmai ā avagata brahma ātma bhāvasya yathāpūrvam saṃsāri tvam yasya tu yathāpūrvam saṃsāri tvam ā asau avagata brahma ātma bhāvaḥ iti aavadyam yat uktam śravaṇāt parācīayoḥ maa aididhyāsayoḥ a svarūpa paryavasāyi tvam iti a śravaṇa vat avagati artha tvā maa aididhyāsayoḥ yadi hi avagatam brahma a yatra viiyujyeta bhavet tadā vidhi śeṣa tvam tu tat asti maa ai didhyāsaayoḥ api śravaṇa vat avagati artha tvāt tasmai a pratipatti vidhi viṣaya tayā śāstra pramāṇaka tvam brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhavati iti atas svatatram eva brahma śāstra pramāṇakam iti siddham evam ca sati atha atas brahma jijñāsā iti tad viṣayaḥ pṛthak śāstra ārambhaḥ upapadyate pratipatti vidhi para tve hi atha atas dharma jijñāsā iti eva ārabdha tvāt pṛthak śāstram ārabhyet ārabhyamāṇam ca evam ārabhyeta atha atas pariśiṣṭa dharma jijñāsā iti atha atas kratu artha puruṣa arthayoḥ jijñāsāḥ iti vat brahma ātma aikya avagatiḥ tu apratijñātā iti tad arthaḥ yuktaḥ śāstra ārambhaḥ atha atas brahma jijñāsā iti tasmāt aham brahma asmi iti etat eva sarve vidhayaḥ sarvāṇi ca itarāṇi hi aheya aupādeya advaita ātma avagatau satyām apramātṛkāṇi ca pramāṇāi bhavitum arhati iti api ca āhuḥ gauṇa mithyā ātmanaḥ sattve putra deha ādi bādhaāt sat brahma ātmā aham iti evam bodhe kāryam katham bhavet prāk pramātṛ tvam ātma aḥ aviṣṭaḥ syāt pramātā eva pāpma doṣa ādi varjitaḥ deha ātma pratyayaḥ kalpitaḥ laukikam tadvat eva idam pramāṇam tu ātma aiścayāt iti evam tāvat brahma ātma avagati prayojaāām brahma ātmai tātparyeṇa atareṇa api uktam brahma ca sarvajñam sarva śakti jagat utpatti sthiti laya kāraṇam iti uktam sāṃkhya ādayaḥ tu pariiṣṭhitam vastu pramāṇa atara gamyam eva iti tad para tayā eva yojayati sarveṣu eva vedātavākyeṣu sṛṣṭi viṣayeṣu kāryeṇa kāraṇam pradhā apuruṣa saṃyogāḥ iti āumeyāḥ iti sāṃkhyāḥ kāṇādāḥ tu etebhyaḥ eva vākyebhyaḥ īśvaram imitta kāraṇam aumimate aṇūn ca samavāyi kāraṇam evam tārkikāḥ vākya ābhāsa yukti ābhāsa avaṣṭambhāḥ pūrvapakṣa vādiaḥ iha uttiṣṭhate tatra brahma ātma avagati para tva pradarśaāya vākya ābhāsa yukti ābhāsa pratipattayaḥ pūrvapakṣīkṛtya tatra sāṃkhyāḥ pradhāam triguṇam acetaam svatatram jagat kāraṇam iti āhuḥ sarvajñasya sarva śakteḥ brahmaṇaḥ jagat kāraṇa tvam pradarśayati iti avocaḥ yojayitum śakyate sarva śakti tvam tāvat sva vikāra viṣayam upapadyate evam sarvajña tvam api upapadyate katham yat tvam sa sattva dharmaḥ sattvāt saṃjāyate iti smṛteḥ ca sattva dharmeṇa kārya karaṇavataḥ puruṣāḥ sarvajñāḥ yogiḥ prasiddhāḥ sattvasya hi sarvajña tvam prasiddham a kevalasya a kārya karaṇasya puruṣasya upalabdhi mātrasya sarvajña tvam kiṃcijjñatvam vā kalpayitum śakyam triguṇa tvāt tu pradhā asya sarvajñā akāraṇa bhūtam sattvam pradhā avasthāyām api vidyate iti pradhā asya acetaasya eva sataḥ sarvajña tvam upacaryate vedāta vākyeṣu avaśyam ca tvayā api sarvajñam brahma iti abhyupagacchatā sarvajña aśaktimat tvena eva sarvajña tvam abhyupagatavyam hi sarvadā sarva viṣayam jñāam kurvat eva brahma vartate tathā hi jñā asya itya tve jñā akriyām prati svātatryam brahmaṇaḥ hīyeta atha aityam tat iti jñā akriyāyāḥ uparame uparameta api brahma tadā sarvajña aśaktimat tve eva sarvajña tvam āpatati api ca prāk utpatteḥ brahma iṣyate tvayā ca śarīra idriya ādīām abhāve jñā utpattiḥ kasyacid api ca pradhāasya a eka ātmakasya pariṇāma saṃbhavāt kāraṇa tva upapattiḥ mṛd ādi vat āsaṃhatasya eka ātmakasya brahmaṇaḥ iti evam prāpte idam sūtram ārabhyate īkṣateḥ āśabdam īkṣati adhikaraṇam a sāṃkhya parikalpitam acetaam pradhāam jagataḥ kāraṇam śakyam āśrayitum aśabdam hi tat katham aśabda tvam īkṣateḥ īkṣitṛ tva śravaṇāt kāraṇasya katham evam hi śrūyate sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam iti upakramya tat aikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya iti tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti tatra idam śabda vācyam āma rūpa vyākṛtam jagat prāk utpatteḥ sat ātmā avadhārya tasya eva prakṛtasya sat śabda vācyasya īkṣaṇa pūrvakam tejaḥ prabhṛteḥ sraṣṭṛ tvam darśayati tathā yatra ātmā vai idam ekaḥ eva agre āsīt āyat kiṃcaa miṣat saḥ īkṣata lokāḥ u sṛjai iti saḥ imān lokāḥ asṛjata iti īkṣā pūrvikām eva sṛṣṭim ācaṣṭe kvacid ca ṣoḍaśa kalam puruṣam prastutya āha saḥ īkṣāṃcakre sa prāṇam asṛjata iti īkṣateḥ iti ca dhātvarthairdeśaḥ bhipretaḥ yajateḥ iti vat a dhātuirdeśaḥ yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vid yasya jñāa mayam tapaḥ tasmāt etat brahma āma rūpam ca jāyate iti evamādīn api sarvajña īśvara kāraṇa parāṇi vākyāi udāhartavyāi yat tu uktam sattva dharmeṇa sarvajñam pradhāam bhaviṣyati iti te upapadyate hi pradhā avasthāyām guṇa sāmyāt sattva dharmaḥ saṃbhavati sarvajñam bhaviṣyati iti tat api ā upapadyate yadi guṇa sāmye sati sattva vyapāśrayām jñā aśaktim āśritya sarvajñam pradhā am ucyeta kāmam rajaḥ tamaḥ vyapāśrayām api jñā a pratibadhaka śaktim āśritya kiṃcijjñam ucyeta api ca āsākṣikā sattva vṛttiḥ abhidhīyate a ca acetaasya pradhāasya sākṣi tvam asti tasmāt aupapam pradhāasya sarvajña tvam yogiām tu cetaa tvāt sattva utkarṣa aimittam sarvajña tvam upapam iti audāharaṇam atha puraḥ sa akṣi imittam īkṣitṛ tvam pradhā asya api kalpyeta ayaḥ piṇḍa ādeḥ dagdhṛ tvam tathā sati yaimittam īkṣitṛ tvam pradhā asya tat eva sarvajñam brahma mukhyam jagataḥ kāraṇam iti yuktam yat puar uktam brahmaṇaḥ api a mukhyam sarvajña tvam upapadyate iti ajñā akriya tve jñā akriyām prati svātatrya asaṃbhavāt iti atra ucyate idam tāvat praṣṭavyaḥ katham sarvajña tva hāiḥ iti yasya hi sarva viṣaya avabhāsa akṣamam asti saḥ sarvajñaḥ iti vipratiṣiddham aitya tve hi jñāasya kadācid asarvajña tvam api syāt sti jñāaitya tve jñā aviṣayaḥ svātatrya vyapadeśaḥ opapadyate iti ced a pratata auṣṇya prakāśe savitari dahati prakāśayati iti svātatrya vyapadeśa darśaāt savituḥ dāhya prakāśya saṃyoge sati dahati prakāśayati iti vyapadeśaḥ syāt a tu brahmaṇaḥ prāk utpatteḥ viṣamaḥ a asati api karmaṇi savitā prakāśate iti kartṛ tva vyapadeśa darśaāt evam asati api jñā a karmaṇi brahmaṇaḥ tadā aikṣata iti kartṛ tva vyapadeśa upapatteḥ a vaiṣamyam karma apekṣāyām tu brahmaṇi īkṣitṛ tva śrutayaḥ sutarām kim puas tat karma yat prāk utpatteḥ īśvara jñāasya viṣayaḥ bhavati iti tattva āyatvābhyām airvacaīye āma rūpe avyākṛte vyācikīrṣite iti brūmaḥ yad prasādāt hi yogiām api atīta āāgata viṣayam pratyakṣam jñāam icchati yoga śāstra vidaḥ kim vaktavyam tasya iti asiddhasya īśvarasya sṛṣṭi sthiti saṃhṛti viṣayam bhavati iti yat api uktam prāk utpatteḥ brahmaṇaḥ iti tat codyam avatarati savitṛ prakāśa vat brahmaṇaḥ api ca avidyā ādimataḥ saṃsāriṇaḥ śarīra ādi apekṣā jñā utpattiḥ syāt a jñā a pratibadha kāraṇa rahitasya īśvarasya matrau ca imau īśvarasya śarīra ādi a apekṣa tām ca darśayataḥ a tasya kāryam karaṇam ca vidyate a tad samaḥ ca abhyadhikaḥ ca dṛśyate parā asya śaktiḥ vividhā eva śrūyate svābhāvikī jñā abala kriyā ca iti a pāṇi pādaḥ grahītā paśyati a cakṣuḥ sa śrṛṇoti a karṇaḥ sa vetti vedyam a ca tasya asti vettā tam āhuḥ agryam puruṣam mahātam iti ca au ā asti tava ayaḥ saṃsārī sti draṣṭā āyo to sti vijñātā ityādi śruteḥ tatra kim idam ucyate saṃsāriṇaḥ śarīra ādi apekṣā jñā utpattiḥ eśvarasya iti atra ucyate satyam eśvarāt ayaḥ saṃsārī tathā api deha ādi saṃghāta upādhi saṃbadhaḥ iṣyate eva ghaṭa karaka giri guhā ādi upādhi saṃbadhaḥ iva vyomaḥ tad kṛtaḥ ca śabda pratyaya vyavahāraḥ lokasya dṛṣṭaḥ ghaṭa chidram karaka chidram ityādiḥ ākāśa a vyatireke tad kṛtā ca ākāśe ghaṭa ākāśa ādi bheda mithyā buddhiḥ dṛṣṭā tathā iha api deha ādi saṃghāta upādhi saṃbadha aviveka kṛta īśvara saṃsāri bheda mithyā buddhiḥ dṛśyate ca ātman eva sataḥ deha ādi saṃghāte ātmani ātma tva abhi iveśaḥ mithyā buddhi mātreṇa pūrva pūrveṇa sati ca evam saṃsāri tve deha ādi apekṣam īkṣitṛ tvam upapadyate saṃsāriṇaḥ yat api uktam pradhā asya a eka ātmaka tvā mṛd ādi vat kāraṇatva upapattiḥ ā saṃhatasya brahmaṇaḥ iti tat pratyuktam yathā tu tarkeṇa api brahmaṇaḥ eva kāraṇa tvam śakyate tathā prapañcayiṣyati a vilakṣaṇa tvāt asya iti evamādiā atra āha yat uktam jagat kāraṇam īkṣitṛ tva śravaṇāt iti tat ayathā api upapadyate acetae pi cetaa vat upacāra darśaāt yathā kūlasya ālakṣya kūlam pipatiṣati iti acetae pi kūle upacāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tadvat acetae pi pradhāe pratyāsa a sarge ceta a vat upacāraḥ bhaviṣyati tadā aikṣata iti yathā loke kaścid cetaḥ sātvā bhuktvā ca aparāhṇe grāmam gamiṣyāmi iti īkṣitvā ataram tathā eva iyam ea pravartate tathā api mahat ādi ākāreṇa pravartate tasmāt ceta a vat upacaryate kasmāt puas kāraṇāt vihāya mukhyam īkṣitṛ tvam aupacārikam kalpyate tat tejaḥ aikṣata tāḥ āpaḥ aikṣata iti ca a cetaayoḥ api ap tejasoḥ ceta a vat upacāra darśaāt tasmāt sat kartṛkam api īkṣaṇam aupacārikam iti gamyate upacāra prāye vacaāt iti evam prāpte idam sūtram ārabhyate gauṇaḥ ātma śabdāt yat uktam pradhāam acetaam sat śabda vācyam aupacārikam īkṣitṛ tvam ap tejasoḥ iva iti tat asat kasmāt ātma śabdāt sat eva somya idam agre āsīt iti upakramya tat aikṣata tat tejaḥ asṛjata iti ca tejobaāām sṛṣṭim uktvā tat eva prakṛtam sat ca devatā śabdea parāmṛśya āha sā iyam devatā aikṣata hata aham imāḥ tisraḥ devatāḥ āma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti tatra yadi guṇa vṛttyā īkṣitṛ kalpyeta tat eva prakṛta tvāt sā iyam devatā iti parāmṛśyeta a tadā devatā jīvam ātma śabdena abhidadhyāt jīvaḥ hi śarīra adhyakṣaḥ prāṇāām dhārayitā tad prasiddheḥ ca sa katham acetaasya pradhā asya ātmā bhavet ātmā hi svarūpam ācetaasya pradhā asya cetao jīvaḥ svarūpam bhavitum arhati atha tu brahma mukhyam īkṣitṛ parigṛhyeta tasya jīva viṣayaḥ ātma śabda prayogaḥ upapadyate tathā sa yaḥ eṣaḥ oṇimā etat ātmyam idam sarvam tat satyam saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi śvetaketo iti atra saḥ ātmā iti prakṛtam sat aṇima ātmā ātma śabdena upadiśya tat tvam asi śvetaketo iti śvetaketoḥ ātma tvena upadiśati ap tejasoḥ tu viṣaya tvāt acetaa tvam āma rūpa vyākaraṇa ādau ca ca ātma śabda vat mukhya tve kāraṇam asti iti yuktam kūla vat gauṇa tvam īkṣitṛ tvasya tayoḥ api sat adhiṣṭhita tva apekṣam eva īkṣitṛ tvam sataḥ tu ātma śabdāḥ a gauṇam īkṣitṛ tvam iti uktam atha ucyeta bhavati ātma śabdaḥ ātmaḥ sarva artha kāri tvāt yathā rājñaḥ sarva artha kāriṇi bhṛtye bhavati ātma śabdaḥ mama ātmā bhadraseaḥ iti hi hi bhoga apavargau kurvat upakaroti rājñaḥ iva bhṛtyaḥ saṃdhi vigraha ādiṣu athavā ekaḥ eva ātma śabdaḥ athavā ekaḥ eva ātma śabdaḥ bhaviṣyati bhūtātmā idriya ātmā iti ca prayoga darśaāt yathā ekaḥ eva jyotiḥ śabdaḥ tatra kutas etat ātma śabdāt īkṣateḥ a gauṇa tvam iti atas uttaram paṭhati taiṣṭhasya mokṣa upadeśāt bhavitum arhati saḥ ātmā iti prakṛtam sat aṇimāam ādāya tat tvam asi śvetaketo iti śvetaketoḥ mokṣayitavyasya taiṣṭhām upadiśya veda tasya tāvat eva ciram saṃpatsye iti mokṣa upadeśāt yadi hi acetaam pradhāam sat śabda vācyam tat asi iti grāhayet mumukṣum tadā viparīta vādi śāstram puruṣasya a arthāya iti apramāṇam syāt a tu irdoṣam idam śāstram apramāṇam kalpayitum yuktam yadi ca ajñasya sataḥ mumukṣoḥ aceta ama ātmā ama ātmā iti upadiśet pramāṇa bhūtam śāstram sa tad ātma dṛṣṭim parityajet tad vyatiriktam pratipadyeta tathā sati puruṣa arthāt vihayeta aartham vā ṛcchet tasmāt yathā svarga ādi arthi ogi hotra ādi sādhaam yathābhūtam upadiśati tathā mumukṣoḥ api saḥ ātmā tattvam asi śvetaketo iti yathābhūtam eva ātmāam upadiśati iti yuktam evam ca sati satya abhisaṃdhasya mokṣa upadeśaḥ upapadyate ayathā hi amukhye sat ātma tattva upadeśe aham uktham asmi iti vidyāt syāt tatra mokṣa upadeśaḥ opapadyeta tasmāt sat aṇimaya ātma śabdasya gauṇa tvam bhṛtye tu svāmi bhṛtya bhedasya pratyakṣa tvāt gauṇaḥ ātma śabdaḥ mama ātmā bhadraseaḥ iti api ca kvacid gauṇaḥ śabdaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti śabda pramāṇakā irthe yāyyā sarvatra āāśvāsa prasaṅgāt yat tu uktam ceta acetaayoḥ sādhāraṇaḥ ātma śabdaḥ kratu jvalaayoḥ iva jyotiḥ śabdaḥ iti taa a ekārtha tvasya āyāyya tvāt tasmāt ceta a viṣayaḥ eva mukhyaḥ ātma śabdaḥ ceta a tva upacārāt bhūta ādiṣu prayujyate bhūtātmā idriya ātmā iti ca sādhāraṇa tve pi ātma śabdasya prakaraṇam upapadam vā śakyate a ca atra acetaasya kiṃcid kāraṇam asti prakṛtam tu sa dīkṣitṛ saṃihitaḥ ca cetaaḥ śvetaketuḥ a hi cetaasya śvetaketoḥ acetaa ātmā saṃbhavati iti avocāma tasmāt ceta a viṣayaḥ iha ātma śabdaḥ iti jyotiḥ śabdaḥ api laukike prayogeṇa jvalaaḥ eva rūḍhaḥ arthavāda kalpitea tu kratau pravṛttaḥ iti adṛṣṭātaḥ athavā pūrva sūtra anusāreṇa athavā pūrva sūtra anusāreṇa athavā pūrva sūtra anusāreṇa athavā pūrva sūtra anusāreṇa athavā pūrva sūtra anusāreṇa athavā pūrva sūtra anusāreṇa athavā pūrva sūtra anusāreṇa athavā pūrva sūtra anusāreṇa athavā pūr eva ātma śabdam vyākhyāya tatas svatatraḥ eva pradhā a kāraṇaiḥ ākaraṇa hetuḥ vyākhyeyaḥ taiṣṭhasya mokṣa upadeśāt iti pradhāam sat śabda vācyam kutas ca a pradhāam sat śabda vācyam heya tva avacaāt ca heya tva avacaāt ca heya tva avacaāt ca heya tva avacaāt ca heya tva avacaāt ca heya tva avacaāt ca heya tva avacaāt ca sat śabda vācyam saḥ ātmā tattvam asi iti iha upadiṣṭam syāt sa tad upadeśa śravaṇāt a ātma jña tayā śāstram tasya heya tvam brūyāt yathā arudhatīm didarśayiṣuḥ tad samīpa sthām sthūlām tārām amukhyām prathamam arudhatī iti grāhayitvā tām pratyākhyāya paścāt arudhatīm eva grāhayati tat vai ayam ātmā iti brūyāt ca evam avocat sa mātra ātma avagati iṣṭhā eva hi ṣaṣṭha prapāṭhake parisamāptiḥ dṛśyate caśabdaḥ pratijñā virodha abhyuccaya pradarśa arthaḥ sati api heya tva vacae pratijñā virodhaḥ prasajyeta kāraṇa vijñāāt hi sarvam vijñātam iti pratijñātam uta tam ādeśam aprākṣyaḥ ye aśrutam śrutam bhavati amatam matam avijñātam vijñātam iti katham u bhagavaḥ saḥ ādeśaḥ bhavati iti yathā somya eke mṛd piṇḍe sarvam mṛ mayam vijñātam syāt vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ āmadheyam mṛttikā iti eva satyam evam somya saḥ ādeśaḥ bhavati iti vākya upakrame śravaṇāt ca sat śabda vācye pradhāe bhogya varga kāraṇe heya tve a heya tve a vā vijñāte bhoktṛ vargaḥ vijñātaḥ bhavati a pradhā a vikāra tvāt bhoktṛ vargasya tasmāt pradhāam sat śabda vācyam kutas ca a pradhāam sat śabda vācyam sva apyayāt tat eva sat śabda vācyam kāraṇam prakṛtya śrūyate yatra etat puruṣaḥ svapiti satā somya tadā saṃpaaḥ bhavati svam api itas bhavati tasmāt eam svapiti iti ācakṣate svam hi api itas bhavati iti eṣā śrutiḥ svapiti iti etat puruṣasya loka prasiddham sva śabde eha ātmā ucyate yaḥ prakṛtaḥ sat śabda vācyaḥ tam apītaḥ bhavati apigataḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ api pūrvasya eteḥ laya artha tvam prasiddham prabhava apyayau iti utpatti pralayayoḥ prayoga darśaāt jīvaḥ jāgarti tad vāsaā viśiṣṭaḥ bhavati saḥ eva asat śabda vācyaḥ bhavati saḥ eva asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat asat a upādhi dvaya uparame suṣupta avasthāyām upādhi kṛta viśeṣa abhāvāt iva iti svam hi api itas bhavati iti ucyate yathā hṛdaya śabdaiḥ śrutyā darśitam sa vai eṣaḥ ātmā hṛdi tasya etat eva hṛdi ayam iti tasmāt hṛdayam iti yathā darśayati śrutiḥ āpaḥ eva tat aśitam ayate tejaḥ eva tat pītam ayate iti ca evam svam ātmā ayam sat śabda vācyam apītaḥ bhavati iti imam artham darśayati a ca cetaaḥ ātmā acetaam pradhāam sva rūpa tvea pratipadyeta yadi puas pradhāam eva ātmīya tvāt sva śabdea eva ucyeta evam api cetaḥ cetaam apyeti iti viruddham āpadyeta śrutyataram ca saṃpariṣvaktaḥ a bāhyam kiṃcaa veda ātaram iti suṣupta avasthāyām cetae apyayam darśayati atas sarveṣām cetaāām sat śabda vācyam jagataḥ kāraṇam syāt ācetaam pradhāam kutas ca a pradhāam jagataḥ kāraṇam gati sāmāyāt yadi tārkika samaye iva bhiā kāraṇa avaga gatiḥ abhaviṣyat kvacid cetaam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam kvacid acetaam pradhāam kvacid ayat eva iti tatas kadācid pradhā a kāraṇa vāda aurodhe api īkṣati ādi śravaṇam akalpayiṣyat tu etat asti samā eva hi sarveṣu ceta a kāraṇa avagatiḥ yathā ageḥ jvalataḥ sarvāḥ diśaḥ visphuliṅgāḥ vipratiṣṭhera evam eva etasmāt ātmaaḥ sarve prāṇāḥ yathāyataam vipratiṣṭhate prāṇebhyaḥ devāḥ devebhyaḥ lokāḥ iti tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti ātmanaḥ eva idam sarvam iti ātmanaḥ eṣa prāṇaḥ jāyate iti ca ātmanaḥ kāraṇa tvam darśayati sarve ātma śabdaḥ ca iti avocāma mahat ca prāmāṇya kāraṇam etat yat vedāta vākyāām ceta a kāraṇa tve cakṣuḥ ādīām iva rūpa ādiṣu atas gati samāyāt sarvajñam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam kutas ca sarvajñam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam śruta tvāt ca sva śabde ā eva ca sarvajñaḥ īśvaraḥ jagataḥ kāraṇam iti śrūyate śvetāśvatarāṇām matra upaiṣadi sarvajñam īśvaram prakṛtya sa kāraṇam a ca asya kaścid ca asya kaścid a ca adhipaḥ iti tasmāt sarvajñam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam veti siddham yatas iti ārabhya śruta tvāt ca iti sūtraiḥ teṣām sarvajñaḥ sarva śaktiḥ īśvaraḥ jagataḥ teṣām pratipāditam ca sarve iti vyākhyātam atas parasya kim iti ucyate dvirūpam hi brahma avagamyate āma rūpa vikāra bheda upādhi viśiṣṭam tad viparītam ca sarva upādhi vivarjitam yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tat itaraḥ itaram paśyati yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kaḥ ia kam paśyet yatra āyat paśyati āyat śṛṇoti āyat vijāāti sa bhūmā atha yatra āyat paśyati ayat śṛṇoti ayat vijāāti tat alpam yaḥ vai bhūmā tat amṛtam atha yat alpam martyam sarvāṇi rūpāṇi vicitya kṛtvā abhivada yat āste iṣkalam iṣkriyam śātam amṛtasya param setum dagdha idhaam iva aalam eti eti a sthūlam a aṇu a hrasvam a dīrgham iti yūam ayat saṃpūrṇam ayat iti ca evam sahasraśas brahmaṇaḥ dvi rūpa tām darśayati tatra avidyā avasthāyām brahmaṇaḥ upāsya upāsaka ādi lakṣaṇaḥ sarvaḥ vyavahāraḥ tatra kāicid brahmaṇaḥ abhyudaya arthāi kāicid krama mukti arthāi kāicid karma samṛddhi arthāi teṣām bhedaḥ ekaḥ eva tu paraḥ ātmā īśvaraḥ taiḥ taiḥ guṇa viśeṣaiḥ viśiṣṭaḥ upāsyaḥ yadi api bhavati tathā api yathāguṇa upāsaam eva bhidyate tam yathā yathā upāsate tat eva bhavati iti śruteḥ yathā kratuḥ asimat loke puruṣaḥ bhavati tathā itas pretya bhavati iti ca smṛteḥ ca yam yam vā api smara bhāvam tyajati ate kalebaram tam tam eva eti kauteya sadā tad bhāva bhāvitaḥ iti yadi api ekaḥ ātmā sarva bhūteṣu sthāvara jaṅgameṣu gūḍhaḥ tathā api citta upādhi viśeṣa tāratamyāt ātmaaḥ kūṭasthaityasya ekarūpasya api uttarottaram āviṣkṛtasya tāratamyam aiśvarya śakti viśeṣaiḥ śrūyate tasya yaḥ ātmā āvistarām veda iti atra smṛtau api yat yat vibhūtimat sattvam śrīmat ūrjitam eva vā tat tat eva avagaccha tvam mama tejaḥ oṃśa saṃbhavam iti yatra yatra vibhūti ādi atiśayaḥ sa saḥ īśvaraḥ iti upāsya tayā codyate evam iha api āditya maṇḍale hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣaḥ sarva pāpma udaya liṅgāt paraḥ eva iti vakṣyati evam ākāśaḥ tat liṅgāt ityādiṣu draṣṭavyam evam sadyas mukti kāraṇam api upādhi viśeṣa dvāreṇa upadiśyamāam api avivakṣita upādhi saṃbadha viśeṣam saṃdihyamāam bhavati yathā iha eva tāvat iti evam ekam api brahma apekṣita upādhi saṃbadham ca upāsya tvea jñeya tvea ca vedāteṣu upadiśyate iti pradarśayitum paraḥ grathaḥ ārabhyate yat ca gati sāmāyāt iti uktam tat api vākya atarāṇi brahma viṣayāṇi vyācakṣāṇā brahma viparīta kāraṇa eṣedhā prapañcyate āada maya ubhyāsāt āada maya adhikaraṇam taittirīyake aamayam prāṇa mayam maomayam vijñā amayam tasmāt vai etasmāt vijñā amayāt taraḥ ātmā aadamayaḥ iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha āada maya śabde an param eva brahma ucyate yat prakṛtam satyam jñāam aatam brahma iti kim brahmaṇorthātaram iti kim tāvat prāptam brahmaṇorthātaram amukhya ātmā aada mayaḥ syāt kasmāt a amaya ādi a mukhya ātma pravāha patita tvāt atha api syāt sarva atara tvāt mukhyaḥ eva ātmā iti a syāt priya ādi avayava yogāt śārīra tva śravaṇāt ca mukhyaḥ ced ātmā syāḥ a priya ādi saṃsparśaḥ syāt iha tu tasya priyam eva śiraḥ ityādi śrūyate śārīra tvam ca śrūyate tasya eṣaḥ eva śārīraḥ ātmā yaḥ pūrvasya iti tasya pūrvasya vijñā amayasya eṣaḥ eva śārīraḥ ātmā yaḥ eṣaḥ āada mayaḥ iti arthaḥ ca sa śarīrasya sataḥ priya apriya saṃsparśaḥ vārayitum śakyaḥ tasmāt saṃsārī eva aada mayaḥ ātmā iti evam prāpte idam ucyate āada mayaḥ bhyāsāt paraḥ eva ātmā āada mayaḥ bhavitum arhati kutas abhyāsāt parasmin eva hi ātman āada śabdaḥ bahu kṛtvas bhyasyate āada mayam prastutya rasaḥ vai saḥ iti tasya eva rasa tvam uktvā ucyate hi eva ayam bhavati kaḥ hi eva āyāt kaḥ prāṇyāt yat eṣaḥ ākāśaḥ syāt eṣa hi eva aadayāti sā eṣā aadasya mīmāsā bhavati etam āada mayam ātmā upasaṃkrāmati āadam brahmaṇaḥ vidvā bibheti kutas caa iti āadam brahma iti iti ca śrutyatare ca brahma iti brahmaṇi eva āada śabdaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ evam āada śabdasya bahu kṛtvas brahmaṇi abhyāsāt āadamayaḥ ātmā brahma iti gamyate yat tu uktam aamaya ādi amukhya ātma pravāha patita tvāt āadamayasya api amukhya tvam iti ā asau doṣaḥ āadamayasya sarva atara tvāt mukhyam eva hi śāstram loka buddhim ausarat a mayam śarīram prasiddham uttaram uttaram ātmā iti grāhayat pratipatti saukarya apekṣayā sarvātaram mukhyam upadideśa iti śliṣṭataram yathā arudhatī darśae bahvīṣu api tārāsu amukhyāsu arudhatīṣu darśitāsu yāḥ atyā pradarśyate sā mukhyā eva ārudhatī bhavati evam iha api āada mayasya sarva atara tva amukhyam ātma tvam yat tu brūṣe mukhyasya ātma iti adoṣaḥ śārīra tvam api a sākṣāt eva śārīra tvam saṃsāri vat tasmāt āadamayaḥ paraḥ eva ātmā vikāra śabdāḥ ā iti ce a prācuryāt atra āha āadamayaḥ paraḥ ātmā bhavitum arhati kasmāt vikāra śabdāt ayam ayaḥ śabdaḥ vikāra vacaḥ samadhigataḥ iti mayaṭaḥ vikāra artha tvāt tasmāt aamaya ādi śabda vat vikāra viṣayaḥ eva ayam iti ced a prācurya arthe api mayaṭaḥ smaraṇāt tad prakṛta vacae mayaṭ iti hi pracura tāyām api mayaṭ smaryate yathā aamayaḥ yajñaḥ iti aa pracura ucyate evam āada pracuram brahmāada mayam ucyate āada pracura tvam ca brahmaṇaḥ mauṣya tvāt ārabhya uttarasmi uttarasmi sthāe śataguṇaḥ āadaḥ iti uktvā brahmāadasya iḥ atiśaya tva avadhāraṇāt tasmāt prācurya arthe mayaṭ tad hetu vyapadeśāt ca itas ca prācurya arthe mayaṭ yasmāt āada hetu tvam brahmaṇaḥ vyapadiśati śrutiḥ eṣa hi eva āadayāti iti āadayati iti arthaḥ yaḥ hi āadayati sa pracurāadaḥ iti prasiddham bhavati yathā loke yaḥ yeṣām dha ekatvam āpādayati sa pracuradhaaḥ iti gamyate tadvat tasmāt prācurya arthe pi mayaṭaḥ saṃbhavāt āadamayaḥ paraḥ eva ātmā mātravarṇikam eva ca gīyate itas ca āadamayaḥ paraḥ eva ātmā yasmāt brahma vid param iti upakramya satyam brahma iti asmi matre yat brahma prakṛtam satya jñāāata viśeṣaṇaiḥ yasmāt ākāśa ādi krameṇa sthāvara jaṅgamāi bhūtāy ajāyata yat ca bhūtāi sṛṣṭvā guhāyām avasthitam sarvātaram yasya vijñāāya ayotaraḥ ātmā ayotaraḥ ātmā iti prakrātam brahma iha gīyate iti matra brāhmaṇayoḥ ca ekārtha tvam yuktam avirodhāt ayathā hi prakṛta hāā prakṛta prakriye syātām a ātmā abhidhīyate etaiṣṭhā eva ca bhārgavī vāruṇī vidyā brahma iti iti tasmāt āadamayaḥ paraḥ eva ātmā upapatteḥ itas ca āadamayaḥ paraḥ eva ātmā etaraḥ itaraḥ īśvarāt ayaḥ saṃsārī jīvaḥ iti arthaḥ a jīva āada maya śabdena abhidhīyate kasmāt aupapatteḥ āada mayam hi prakṛtya śrūyate saḥ ukāmayata bahu syām prajāyeya iti sa tapaḥ utapyata sa tapaḥ taptvā id sarvam asṛjata yat idam kiṃca iti tatra prāk śarīra ādi utpatteḥ sṛjyamāāām ca vikārāṇām sraṣṭuḥ avyatirekaḥ sarva vikāra sṛṣṭiḥ ca parasmāt bheda vyapadeśāt ca itas ca saṃsārī yasmāt āada maya adhikāre rasaḥ vai saḥ bhavati iti jīva aada mayau vyapadiśati a hi labdhā eva labdhavyaḥ bhavati katham tarhi ātmā āveṣṭavyaḥ param vidyate iti śruti smṛtī yāvatā a labdhā eva labdhavyaḥ bhavati iti uktam bāḍham tathā api sataḥ tattva aavabodha aimittaḥ mithyā eva deha ādiṣu a ātmasu ātma tva aiścayaḥ laukikaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ ātmā ātmā a aviṣṭaḥ aveṣṭavyaḥ alabdhaḥ labdhavyaḥ aśrutaḥ śrotavyaḥ amataḥ matavyaḥ avijñātaḥ vijñātavyaḥ iti ādi bheda vyapadeśaḥ upapadyate pratiṣidhyate eva tu paramārthataḥ sarvajñāt parameśvarāt ayaḥ draṣṭā śrotā vā draṣṭā ityādiā parameśvaraḥ tu avidyā kalpitāt śārīrāt kartuḥ bhoktuḥ ayaḥ yathā sūtreṇa ākāśam adhirohataḥ saḥ eva māyāvī paramārtha rūpaḥ bhūmiṣṭhaḥ ayaḥ yathā vā ghaṭa ākāśāt ākāśaḥ ayaḥ īdṛśam ca vijñā ātma paramātma bhedam āśritya aupapatteḥ bheda vyapadeśāt ca iti uktam kāmāt ca ca sā ukāmayata bahu syām prajāyeya iti iti kāmayitṛ tva airdeśāt ca āumāikam api sāṃkhya parikalpitam pradhāam kāraṇa tvea vā apekṣitavyam īkṣateḥ āśabdam iti irākṛtam api pradhāam pūrva sūtra udāhṛtām kāmayitṛ tva śrutim āśritya prasaṅgāt irākriyate gati sāmāya prapañca asmi asya ca tad yogam śāsti itas ca a pradhāe jīve vāada maya śabdaḥ yasmāt asmi āada maye prakṛte ātmai pratibuddhasya asya jīvasya tat yogam śāsti tat yogaḥ tad yogaḥ tad bhāva āpattiḥ muktiḥ iti arthaḥ tad yogam śāsti śāstram yadā hi eva eṣa etasmin pratiṣṭhām vidate atha saḥ ubhayam gataḥ bhavati yadā hi eva eṣa etasmin udaram ataram kurute atha tasya bhayam bhavati iti etat uktam bhavati yadā etasmin api ataram a tādātmya rūpam paśyati tadā saṃsāra bhayā iva ṛtate yadā tu etasmin tādātmyea pratitiṣṭhati tadā saṃsāra bhayā iva ṛtate iti tat ca paramātma parigrahe ghaṭate a pradhā a parigrahe jīva parigrahe vā tasmāt āada mayaḥ paramātmā iti siddham idam tu iha vaktavyam sa vai eṣa puruṣa arasa mayaḥ tasmāt vai etasmāt aarasamayāt ayā utaraḥ ātmā prāṇa mayaḥ tasmāt ayā utaraḥ ātmā maomayaḥ tasmāt ayā utaraḥ ātmā vijñāa mayaḥ iti ca vikāra arthe mayaṭ pravāhe sati eva akasmāt katham iva mayaṭaḥ prācurya artha tvam brahma viṣaya tvam ca āśrīyate iti mātravarṇika brahma adhikārāt iti ced a a amaya ādīām api tarhi brahmatva prasaṅgaḥ atra āha yuktam a amaya ādīām abrahmatvam tasmāt tasmāt ucyamāa tvāt āadamayāt tu a kaścid ayaḥ ātaraḥ ātmā ucyate brahmatvam ayathā brahmatvam ayathā iti atra ucyate yadi api aamaya ādibhyaḥ iva aadamayāt ātmā iti a śrūyate tathā api āadamayasya brahmatvam yatas āadamayam prakṛtya śrūyate tasya priyam eva śiraḥ modaḥ dakṣiṇaḥ pakṣaḥ pramodaḥ uttaraḥ pakṣaḥ āadaḥ ātmā brahma puccham pratiṣṭhāḥ iti tatra yat brahma iha matravarṇe prakṛtam satyam jñāam brahma iti tat iha brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti ucyate tad vijijñāpayiṣayā eva a amaya ādayaḥ pañca kośāḥ kalpyate tatra kutas brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti ucyate brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti ucyate iva idam puccham pratiṣṭhā ityādi tatra katham brahmaṇaḥ svapradhā atvam śakyam vijñātum prakṛta tvāt iti brūmaḥ brahmaṇi a prakṛta tvam hīyate āada mayasya brahma tvāt iti atra ucyate tathā sati tat eva brahma āada mayaḥ ātmā avayavī tat eva ca brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā avayava iti asāmañjasyam syāt tu yuktam brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti atra eva brahmaiḥ deśe āśrayitum brahma śabda saṃyogāt āadamaya vākye brahma śabda saṃyoga abhāvāt iti api ca brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti uktvā idam ucyate tat api eṣa ślokaḥ bhavati asaḥ eva sa bhavati asat brahma iti veda ced asti brahma iti ced veda satam tatas viduḥ iti asmin ca śloke aukṛṣya adamayam brahmaṇaḥ eva bhāva abhāva vedaayoḥ guṇa doṣa abhidhāāt gamyate brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti atra brahmaṇaḥ eva iti bhāva abhāva āśaṅkā yuktā priyamoda ādi viśiṣṭasya āada mayasya sarva loka prasiddha tvāt katham puas svapradhāam sat brahma brahma puccha tve nirdiśyate brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ pucchavat puccham pratiṣṭhā parāyaṇam ekaīḍam laukikasya aad a jātasya brahmā aadaḥ iti etat vivakṣyate āvayava tvam etasya eva aadasya āyāi bhūtāi mātrām upajīvati iti śrutyatarāt api ca aad mayasya brahmatve sa viśeṣam brahma abhyupagatavyam sa viśeṣam brahma abhyupagatavyam tu brahma vākyaśeṣe śrūyate vāc maasayoḥ agocara tva abhidhāāt yatas vācaḥ a prāpya maasā saha brahmaṇaḥ vidvā bibheti kutas iti api ca a ad apracuraḥ iti ukte duḥkha alpīyaḥ tvam api gamyate prācuryasya loke pratiyogi alpatva apekṣa tvāt tathā ca sati yatra āyat paśyati āyat śṛṇoti āyat vijāāti sa bhūmā iti bhūmi brahmaṇi tad vyatirikta abhāva śrutiḥ uparudhyeta pratiśarīram ca priya ādi bhedāt brahma tu a pratiśarīram bhidyate satyam jñāam brahma iti āatya śruteḥ ekaḥ devaḥ sarva bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarva vyāpī sarva bhūta atarātmā iti ca śrutyatarāt a cāada maya abhyāsaḥ śrūyate prātipadika artha mātram eva hi sarvatra abhyasyate rasaḥ vai saḥ bhavati kaḥ hi eva āyāt kaḥ prāṇyāt yat eṣaḥ ākāśaḥ a syāt sā eṣā aadasya mīmāṃsā bhavati āadam brahmaṇaḥ vidvā a bibheti kutas caa iti āadaḥ brahma iti iti ca yadi ca āada maya śabdasya brahma viṣaya tvam bhavet tatas uttareṣu āada mātra prayogeṣu api āada maya abhyāsaḥ kalpyeta a tu āada mayasya brahmatvam asti priya śiraḥ tva ādibhiḥ hetubhiḥ iti avocāma tasmāt śrutyatare brahma iti āada pada prātipadikasya brahmaṇi prayoga darśaāt yat eṣaḥ ākāśe syāt iti brahma viṣayaḥ prayogaḥ tu āada maya abhyāsaḥ iti avagatavyam yaḥ tu ayam etam āada maya śabdasya abhyāsaḥ etam āada mayam ātmā am upasaṃkrāmati iti a tasya brahma viṣaya tvam asti vikāra ātma upasaṃkramitavyāām pravāhe patita tvāt au a a da mayasya upasaṃkramitavyasya a a maya ādi vat a brahmatve sati ā eva viduṣaḥ brahma prāptiḥ phalam bhavet ā eṣa doṣaḥ viduṣaḥ puccha pratiṣṭhā bhūta brahma prāpteḥ phalasya tat api eṣa ślokaḥ bhavati yatas vācaḥ iva ṛtate ca yā tu bahu syām prajāyeya iti iti iyam śrutiḥ udāhṛtā sā brahma puccham pratiṣṭhāḥ iti saṃihitatareṇa brahmaṇā saṃbadhyamāā āada mayasya brahma tām pratibodhayati tad apekṣa tvāt ca uttarasya grathasya rasaḥ vai saḥ ityādeḥ āada maya viṣaya tā iti brahmaṇi pum liṅgaiḥ deśaḥ opapadyate doṣaḥ tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmā ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti atra brahmaṇaḥ prakṛta tvāt yat tu bhārgavī vāruṇī vidyā āadaḥ brahma iti vyajāāt iti tasyām mayaṭ a śravaṇāt priyaśiraḥ tva ādi a śravaṇāt ca yuktam āadasya brahma tvam tasmāt aṇu mātram api viśeṣam a āśritya a svatas eva priya śiraḥ tva ādi brahmaṇaḥ upapadyate a ca iha sa viśeṣam brahma pratipipādayiṣitam vikāra arthaḥ eva mayaṭ vijñeyaḥ a prācurya arthaḥ sūtrāṇi tu evam vyākhyeyāi brahma puccham pratiṣṭhāḥ iti atra kim brahma vivakṣyate uta brahma vivakṣyate uta puccha śabdāt prāpte ucyate ātmā iti atra brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti eva brahma upadiśyate abhyāsāt asaḥ eva sa bhavati iti asmi brahmaṇa eva kevalasya abhyasyamāa tvāt vikāra śabdāḥ prācuryāt prācuryāt puccham iti avayava śabdāḥ a svapradhāa tvam brahmaṇaḥ iti yat uktam tasya parihāraḥ vaktavyaḥ atrā ucyate doṣaḥ prācuryāt api avayava śabda upapatteḥ prācuryam prāya āpattiḥ avayava prāye iti arthaḥ hi śiraḥ ādiṣu avayaveṣu ukteṣu avayava ātarāṇi uktvā avayava prāya āpattyā brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti āha āvayava vivakṣayā yatkāraṇam abhyāsāt iti svapradhāa tvam brahmaṇaḥ samarthitam tad hetu vyapadeśāt ca sarvasya hi vikāra jātasya brahma vyapadiśyate id sarvam asṛjata yat idam kiṃca iti a ca kāraṇam sat brahma sva vikārasya a da mayasya mukhyayā vṛttyā avayavaḥ upapadyate aparāṇi api sūtrāṇi yathāsaṃbhavam puccha vākyaiḥ diṣṭasya eva brahmaṇaḥ upapādakāi draṣṭavyāi atas tad dharma upadeśāt idam āmāyate atha yaḥ eṣa utarāditye hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣaḥ dṛśyate hiraṇya śmaśruḥ hiraṇya keśaḥ ā praṇakhāt sarvaḥ eva suvarṇaḥ tasya yathā kapyāsam puṇḍarīkam evam akṣiṇī tasya uditi āma saḥ eṣa sarvebhyaḥ pāpmabhyaḥ uditaḥ udeti ha vai sarvebhyaḥ pāpmabhyaḥ yaḥ evam veda iti adhidaivatam atha adhyātmam api atha yaḥ puruṣaḥ dṛśyate ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kim vidyā karma atiśaya vaśāt prāpta utkarṣaḥ kaścid saṃsārī sūrya maṇḍale cakṣuṣi śrūyate kim vā iti asiddhaḥ parameśvaraḥ iti kim tāvat prāptam saṃsāri iti kutas rūpavat tva śravaṇāt āditya puruṣe tāvat hiraṇya śmaśruḥ ityādi rūpam udāhṛtam akṣi puruṣe pi tat eva atideśe prāpyate tasya etasya tat eva rūpam yat amuṣya rūpam iti a ca parameśvarasya rūpavat tvam yuktam a śabdam a sparśam a rūpam avyayam iti śruteḥ ādhāra śravaṇāt ca yaḥ eṣa utarāditye yaḥ eṣa utarakṣiṇi iti a hi a ādhārasya sva mahima pratiṣṭhitasya sarva vyāpi aḥ parameśvarasya ādhāraḥ upadiśyeta sa bhagavaḥ kasmipratiṣṭhitaḥ iti sve mahimi iti ākāśa vat sarva gataḥ ca ityaḥ iti ca śrutī bhavataḥ aiśvarya maryādā śruteḥ ca saḥ eṣa ye ca amuṣmāt parāñcaḥ lokāḥ teṣām ca īṣṭe ca iti āditya puruṣasya aiśvarya maryādā saḥ eṣa ye ca etasmāt arvāñcaḥ lokāḥ teṣām ca īṣṭe ca iti akṣi puruṣasya ca parameśvarasya maryādāvat aiśvaryam yuktam eṣa sarva īśvara eṣa bhūta adhipatiḥ eṣa bhūta pālaḥ eṣa setuḥ vidharaṇaḥ eṣām iti aviśeṣa śruteḥ tasmāt akṣi ādityayoḥ atas parameśvaraḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ atas tad dharma upadeśāt iti yaḥ eṣa utarāditye yaḥ eṣa utarakṣiṇi iti ca śrūyamāṇaḥ puruṣaḥ parameśvaraḥ eva a saṃsārī kutas tad dharma upadeśāt tasya hi parameśvarasya dharmāḥ iha upadiṣṭāḥ tat yathā tasya uditi āmaḥ iti śrāvayitvā tasya ādityapuruṣasya saḥ eṣa sarvebhyaḥ pāpmabhyaḥ uditaḥ iti tat eva ca tat eva ca iti sarva pāpma apagamaḥ ca paramātmaaḥ eva śrūyate yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā ityādau tathā cākṣuṣe puruṣe sā eva ṛc tat sāma tat uktham tat yajuḥ tat brahma iti ṛk sāma ādi ātmaka tām dhārayati sā ca parameśvarasya upapadyate sarva kāraṇa tvāt sarva ātmaka tva upapatteḥ pṛthivī agi ādi ātmake ca adhidaivatam ṛk sāme vāc prāṇa ādi ātmake ca adhyātmam aukramya āha tasya ṛc ca sāma ca geṣṇau iti adhidaivatam tathā adhyātmam api yau amuṣya geṣṇau tau geṣṇau iti tat ca sarva ātmaka tve sati eva upapadyate tat yaḥ ime vīṇāyām gāyati etam tu eva te gāyati tasmāt te iti ca laukikeṣu api gāeṣu asya eva gīya māa tvam darśayati tat ca parameśvara parigrahe eva ghaṭate yat yat vibhūtimat sattvam śrīmat ūrjitam eva vā tat tat eva avagaccha tvam mama tejaḥ oṃśa saṃbhavam iti bhagavadgītā ādarśaāt loka kāma īśitṛ tvam api iraṅkuśam śrūyamāṇam parameśvaram gamayati yat tu uktam hiraṇya śmaśru tva ādi rūpavat tva śravaṇam parameśvare opapadyate iti atra brūmaḥ syāt parameśvarasya api icchā vaśā māyā mayam rūpam sādhaka augraha artham māyā hi eṣā mayā sṛṣṭā yamām paśyasi ārada sarva bhūta guṇaiḥ yuktam mā evam mām jñātum arhasi iti smaraṇāt api ca yatra tu pārameśvaram rūpam upadiśyate bhavati tatra śāstram aśabdam asparśam arūpam avyayam ityādi sarva kāraṇa tvāt tu vikāra dharmaiḥ api kaiścid viśiṣṭaḥ parameśvaraḥ upāsya tve nirdiśyate sarva karmā sarva kāmaḥ sarva gadhaḥ sarva rasaḥ ityādi tathā bhaviṣyati yat api ādhāra śravaṇāt parameśvara iti atrā ucyate sva mahima pratiṣṭhasya api ādhāra viśeṣa upadeśaḥ upāsa arthaḥ bhaviṣyati sarvagata tvāt brahmaṇaḥ vyoma vat sarvātaratva upapatteḥ aiśvarya maryādā śravaṇam api adhyātma adhidaivata vibhāga apekṣam upāsa artham eva tasmāt parameśvaraḥ eva akṣi ādityayoḥ atas upadiśyate bheda vyapadeśāt ca ayaḥ asti ca āditya ādi śarīra abhimā jīvebhyaḥ yaḥ īśvara ūtaryāmī yaḥ āditye tiṣṭha ādityāt ataraḥ yam ādityaḥ ataraḥ ya a veda yasya ādityaḥ śarīram yaḥ ādityam ataraḥ yamayati eṣa te ātmā ataryāmī amṛtaḥ iti śruti atare bheda vyapadeśāt tatra hi ādityāt ataraḥ yam ādityaḥ a veda iti vedituḥ ādityāt vijñā ātma oya utaryāmī spaṣṭam irdiśyate saḥ eva iha apyatara āditye puruṣaḥ bhavitum arhati śruti sāmāyāt tasmāt parameśvaraḥ eva iha upadiśyate iti siddham ākāśaḥ tad liṅgāt ākāśa adhikaraṇam idam āmaati asya lokasya kā gatiḥ iti ākāśaḥ iti ha uvāca sarvāṇi ha vai imāi bhūtāy ākāśāt eva samutpadyate ākāśam prati astam yati ākāśaḥ hi eva ebhyaḥ jyāyāḥ ākāśaḥ parāyaṇam iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim ākāśa śabdena param brahma abhidhīyate uta bhūtākāśam iti kutas saṃśayaḥ ubhayatra prayoga darśaāt bhūta viśeṣe tāvat su prasiddhaḥ loka vedayoḥ ākāśa śabdaḥ brahmaṇi api kvacid dṛśyate yatra vākyaśeṣa vaśāt asādhāraṇa guṇa śravaṇāt brahma bhavati yathā yat eṣaḥ ākāśaḥ syāt iti ākāśaḥ ha vai āmaḥ āma rūpayoḥ te yad atarā tat brahma iti ca evamādau atas saṃśayaḥ kim puar atra yuktam bhūtākāśam iti kutas tat hi prasiddhatareṇa prayogeṇa śīghram buddhim ārohati a ca ayam ākāśa śabdaḥ ubhayoḥ sādhāraṇaḥ śakyaḥ vijñātum a eka artha tva prasaṅgāt tasmāt brahmaṇi gauṇaḥ eva ākāśa śabdaḥ bhavitum arhati vibhu tva ādibhiḥ hi bahubhiḥ dharmaiḥ sadṛśam brahma bhavati ca mukhya saṃbhave gauṇaḥ rthaḥ grahaṇam arhati saṃbhavati ca iha mukhyasya eva ākāśasya grahaṇam bhūtākāśa parigrahe vākya śeṣaḥ o upapadyate sarvāṇi ha vai imāi bhūtāni ākāśāt eva samutpadyate ityādiḥ ā eṣa doṣaḥ bhūtākāśasya api vāyu ādi krameṇa kāraṇa tva upapatteḥ vijñāyate hi tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ ākāśāt vāyuḥ vāyoḥ agiḥ ityādi jyāyaḥ tu aparāyaṇa tve api bhūta atara apekṣayā upapadyete bhūtākāśasya api tasmāt ākāśa śabde bhūtākāśasya grahaṇam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ ākāśaḥ tad liṅgāt ākāśa śabdena iha brahmaṇaḥ grahaṇam yuktam kutas tad liṅgāt parasya hi brahmaṇaḥ idam liṅgam sarvāṇi ha vā ākāśāt eva samutpadyate iti parasmāt hi brahmaṇaḥ bhūtāām utpattiḥ iti bhūtākāśasya api vāyu ādi krameṇa kāraṇa tvam darśitam satyam darśitam tathā api mūla kāraṇasya brahmaṇaḥ parigrahāt ākāśāt eva iti avadhāraṇam sarvāṇi iti ca bhūta viśeṣaṇam syāt tathā ākāśam prati astam yati iti brahma liṅgam ākāśaḥ hi eva ebhyaḥ jyāyāḥ ākāśaḥ parāyaṇam iti ca jyāyaḥ tu a parāyaṇa tve jyāyaḥ tvam hi a āpekṣikam paramātman eva ekasmin jyāyāḥ pṛthivyāḥ jyāyāḥ atarikṣāt jyāyāḥ divaḥ jyāyāḥ ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ iti tathā parāyaṇa tvam api parama kāraṇa tvāt eva upapaataram bhavati śrutiḥ ca brahma rātiḥ dātuḥ parāyaṇam iti api tu adoṣeṇa śālāvatyasya pakṣam kiṃcid kiṃcid parigṛhītaḥ tam ca ākāśam udgīthe saṃpādya upasaṃharati saḥ eṣa paras varīyāḥ udgīthaḥ saḥ eṣaḥ atas iti tat ca āatyam brahma liṅgam yat uktam bhūtākāśam prasiddhi balea prathamataram pratīyate iti atra brūmaḥ prathamataram pratītam api tad vākyaśeṣa gatā brahma guṇāḥ dṛṣṭvā darśitaḥ ca brahmaṇi api ākāśa śabdaḥ ākāśaḥ ha vai āmaḥ ityādau tathā ākāśa paryāya vācī api brahmaṇi prayogaḥ dṛśyate ṛcaḥ akṣare parame vyoma devāḥ adhi viśve iṣeduḥ sā eṣā bhārgavī vāruṇī vidyā parame vyoma pratiṣṭhitā kam brahma kham brahma kham purāṇam iti ca evamādau vākya upakrame pi vartamāasya ākāśa śabdasya vākyaśeṣa vaśāt yuktā brahma viṣayatva avadhāraṇā agiḥ adhīte uvākam iti hi vākya upakrama gataḥ api agi śabdaḥ māṇavaka viṣayaḥ dṛśyate tasmāt ākāśa śabdam brahma iti siddham atas eva prāṇaḥ prāṇa adhikaraṇam udgīthe prastotar yā devatā prastāvam avāyattā iti upakramya śrūyate katamā sā devatā iti prāṇaḥ iti ha uvāca sarvāṇi ha vai imāi bhūtāi prāṇam eva abhisaṃviśati prāṇam abhyujjihate sā eṣā devatā prastāvam avāyattā iti tatra saṃśayaiḥ ṇayau pūrvavat eva draṣṭavyau somya prāṇasya prāṇam iti ca evamādau brahma viṣayaḥ prāṇa śabdaḥ dṛśyate vāyu vikāre tu prasiddhataraḥ loka vedayoḥ atas iha yuktam iti bhavati saṃśayaḥ kim vāyu vikārasya pañca vṛtteḥ prāṇasya yuktam tatra hi prasiddhataraḥ prāṇa śabdaḥ iti avocāma pūrvavat iha api tad liṅgāt brahmaṇaḥ eva grahaṇam yuktam iha api hi vākyaśeṣe bhūtāām pārameśvaram karma pratīyate a mukhye api prāṇe bhūta saṃveśa udgama asya darśa evam hi āmāyate yadā vai puruṣaḥ svapiti prāṇam tarhi vāc apyeti prāṇam cakṣuḥ prāṇam śrotram prāṇam sa yadā prabudhyate prāṇāt eva adhi puas jāyate iti pratyakṣam ca etat svāpa kāle prāṇa vṛttau a parilupyamāāyām idriya vṛttayaḥ parilupyate prabodha kāle ca puas prādurbhavati iti idriya sāra tvāt ca bhūtāām aviruddhaḥ mukhye prāṇe api bhūta saṃveśa odgama avādī vākyaśeṣaḥ api ca āditya oam ca udgītha pratihārayoḥ devate prastāva devatāyāḥ a ca tayoḥ brahmatvam asti tad sāmāyāt ca prāṇasya api a brahmatvam iti evam prāpte sūtrakāraḥ āha atas eva prāṇaḥ iti tad liṅgāt iti pūrva sūtre atas eva tad liṅgāt prāṇa śabdam api param brahma bhavitum arhati prāṇasya api hi brahma liṅga saṃbadhaḥ śrūyate sarvāṇi ha vai imā idam bhūtāi prāṇam eva abhisaṃviśati prāṇam abhyujjihate iti prāṇa aimittau sarveṣām bhūtāām utpatti pralayau ucyamāau prāṇasya brahmatām gamayataḥ mukhya prāṇa parigrahe pi saṃveśa udgama adarśa amaviruddham svāpa prabodhayoḥ darśaāt iti atra ucyate svāpa prabodhayoḥ idriyāṇām eva kevalāām prāṇa āśrayam saṃveśa odgama amaviruddham dṛśyate sarveṣām bhūtāām iha tu sa idriyāṇām sa śarīrāṇām ca jīva āviṣṭāām bhūtāām sarvāṇi ha vai imāi bhūtāi iti śruteḥ yadā api bhūta śrutiḥ mahābhūta viṣayā parigṛhyate tadā api brahma liṅga tvam aviruddham saha api viṣayaiḥ idriyāṇām svāpa prabodhayoḥ prāṇe pi ayam prāṇāt ca prabhavam śrṛṇumaḥ yadā suptaḥ svapam paśyati atha asmi prāṇaḥ eva ekadhā bhavati vāc sarvaiḥ āmabhiḥ saha apyeti iti tatra api tad liṅgāt prāṇa śabdam brahma iva yat puas uktam prāṇasya abrahmatvam iti tat ayuktam vākyaśeṣa balea prāṇa śabdasya brahma viṣaya tāyām pratīyamāāyām saṃidhāasya akiṃcitkara tvāt yat puas prāṇa śabdasya pañca vṛttau prasiddhatara tvam tat ākāśa śabdasya iva pratividheyam tasmāt siddham prastāva devatāyāḥ prāṇasya brahmatvam atra kecid udāharati prāṇasya prāṇam hi somya iti ca tat ayuktam śabda bhedāt prakaraṇāt ca saṃśaya aupapatteḥ yathā pituḥ pitā iti prayoge ayaḥ pitā ṣaṣṭhīirdiṣṭāt prathama airdiṣṭaḥ pituḥ pitā iti gamyate tadvat prāṇasya prāṇam iti śabda bhedāt prasiddhāt prāṇāt ayaḥ prāṇasya prāṇaḥ iti hi saḥ eva tasya iti bhedaiḥ deśa arhaḥ bhavati yasya ca prakaraṇe yaḥ irdiśyate saḥ eva tatra prakaraṇī irdiṣṭaḥ iti gamyate yathā jyotiṣṭoma adhikāre vasate vasate jyotiṣā yajeta iti atra jyotiḥ śabdaḥ jyotiṣṭoma viṣayaḥ bhavati tathā parasya brahmaṇaḥ prakaraṇe hi somya maaḥ iti śrutaḥ prāṇa śabdaḥ vāyu vikāra mātram katham avagamayet atas saṃśaya aviṣaya tvā ā etat udāharaṇam yuktam prastāvadevatāyām tu prāṇe saṃśaya pūrvapakṣaiḥ ṇayā upapāditāḥ jyotiścaraṇa abhidhāāt jyotiścaraṇa adhikaraṇam idam atha yat atas paras divaḥ jyotiḥ dīpyate viśvatas pṛṣṭheṣu sarvatas pṛṣṭheṣu auttameṣu uttameṣu lokeṣu idam vāva tat yat idam asmi atas puruṣe jyotiḥ iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha jyotiḥ śabde āditya ādikam jyotiḥ abhidhīyate kim vā paraḥ ātmā iti artha atara viṣayasya api prāṇa śabdasya tad liṅgāt brahma viṣaya tvam uktam iha tu tad liṅgam eva asti āsti iti vicāryate kim tāvat prāptam āditya ādikam eva parigṛhyate iti kutas prasiddheḥ jyotiḥ iti hi imau śabdau paraspara pratidva dvi viṣayau prasiddhau cakṣuḥ vṛtteḥ śārvara ādikam tamaḥ ucyate tasyāḥ eva au grāhakam āditya ādikam jyotiḥ tathā dīpyate iti iyam api śrutiḥ āditya ādi viṣayā prasiddhā hi brahma dīpyate iti mukhyām śrutim arhati dyu maryāda tva śruteḥ ca a hi carācara bījasya brahmaṇaḥ sarva ātmakasya dyauḥ maryādā yuktā kāryasya tu jyotiśaḥ dyauḥ maryādā syāt paras divaḥ jyotiḥ iti ca brāhmaṇam kāryasya api jyotiṣaḥ sarvatra dyu maryādāvat tvam asamañjasam astu tarhi a trivṛt kṛtam tejaḥ prathama jam a a trivṛt kṛtasya tejasaḥ iti idam eva prayojaam yat upāsya tvam iti ced a prayoja a tara prayuktasya eva āditya ādeḥ upāsya tva darśaāt tāsām trivṛtam trivṛtam ekaikām karavāṇi iti ca a viśeṣa śruteḥ a ca a trivṛt kṛtasya api tejasaḥ dyu maryāda tvam prasiddham astu tarhi trivṛt kṛtam eva tat tejaḥ jyotiḥ śabdam api divaḥ vagamyate igya ādikam jyotiḥ iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ sarvatra api gamyamā asya jyotiṣaḥ paras divaḥ iti upāsa arthaḥ pradeśa viśeṣa parigrahaḥ virudhyate a tu brahmaṇaḥ pradeśa viśeṣa kalpaā bhāgiī sarvatas pṛṣṭheṣu auttameṣu uttameṣu lokeṣu iti ca ādhāra bahutva śrutiḥ kārye jyotiṣi upapadyatetarām idam vāva tat yat idam asmi atas puruṣe jyotiḥ iti ca kaukṣeye jyotiṣi param jyotiḥ dṛśyate sārūpya aimittāḥ ca adhyāsāḥ bhavati yathā tasya bhūḥ iti śiraḥ śiraḥ ekam etat akṣaram iti kaukṣeyasya tu jyotiṣaḥ prasiddham a brahma tvam tasya eṣā dṛṣṭiḥ tasya eṣā śrutiḥ iti ca auṣṇya ghoṣa viśiṣṭa tvasya śravaṇāt tat etat dṛṣṭam ca śrutam ca iti upāsīta iti ca śruteḥ cakṣuṣyaḥ ca śrutaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda iti ca alpa phala śravaṇāt abrahmatvam mahate hi phalāya iṣyate jyotiṣaḥ asti brahmatva liṅgam a ca pūrvasmi api vākye brahma gāyatrī vai idam sarvam bhūtam iti atha api kathaṃcid pūrvasmi vākye brahma syāt evam api a tasya iha asti tatra hi tri pādasya amṛtam divi iti śrūyate atra puras divaḥ jyotiḥ iti tasmāt prākṛtam jyotiḥ iha grāhyam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ jyotiḥ iha brahma grāhyam kutas caraṇa abhidhāāt pāda abhidhāāt iti arthaḥ pūrvasmi hi vākye catuṣpād brahma tāvā asya mahimā tatas jyāyāḥ ca puruṣaḥ pādaḥ usya sarvā tri pādasya amṛtam divi matreṇa tatra yat catuṣpadaḥ brahmaṇaḥ tri pād amṛtam tat eva iha pratyabhijñāyate tat parityajya prākṛtam jyotiḥ kalpayataḥ prakṛta hāā prakṛta prakriye prasajyeyātām a kevalam jyotiḥ vākye eva śabdena abhidhīyate tathā sati brahmaṇaḥ api caitaya rūpasya samasta jagat avabhāsa hetutvāt jyotiḥ śabdaḥ tam eva sarvam tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti tat devāḥ jyotiṣām jyotiḥ āyuḥ ha upāsata pratipeda iham maura bhavam sūryaḥ ca iti tadvat tat yoga yaḥ devāām pratyabudhyata saḥ eva tat abhavat iti śruteḥ yat puaruktam mām eva iti uktvā vigraha carmaiḥ idraḥ svam ātmānam tuṣṭāva tvāṣṭra vadha ādibhiḥ iti tat parihartavyam atra ucyate a tāvat tvāṣṭra vadha ādīnām yasmāt evaṃkarmā aham iti katham tarhi iti katham tarhi yad kāraṇam tasya me tatra loma ca astuti mausaṃdadhāti tasya me tatra loma ca astuti mausaṃdadhāti mīyate sa yaḥ mām veda a ha vai tasya ca karmaṇā loke mīyate ityādiā etat uktam bhavati yasmāt īdṛśāi api krūrāṇi karmāṇi kṛtavataḥ mama brahma bhūtasya loma api a hiṃsyate sa yaḥ yaḥ pi mām veda a tasya kaścitā api karmaṇā lokaḥ hiṃsyate iti vijñeyam tu brahma eva prāṇaḥ asmi prajñā ātmā iti vakṣyamāṇam tasmāt brahma vākyam etat jīva mukhya prāṇa liṅgāḥ eti ce ā upāsā traividhyāt āśrita tvāt iha tad yogāt yadi api devatā ātma upadeśaḥ tathā api a brahma vākyam bhavitum arhati kutas jīva liṅgāt mukhya prāṇa liṅgāt ca jīvasya tāvat asmi vākye vispaṣṭam liṅgam upalabhyate a vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt ityādi atra hi vāc ādibhiḥ karaṇaiḥ vyāpṛtasya kārya karaṇa adhyakṣasya jīvasya vijñeya tvam abhidhīyate tathā mukhya prāṇa liṅgam api atha khalu prāṇaḥ eva prajñā ātmā idam śarīram parigṛhya utthāpayati iti śarīra dhāraṇam ca mukhya prāṇasya dharmaḥ prāṇa saṃvāde tau ariṣṭhaḥ prāṇaḥ uvāca mā moham āpat yathā aham eva etat pañcadhā ātmā am pravibhajya etat bāṇam avaṣṭabhya vidhārayāmi iti śravaṇāt ye tu imam śarīram parigṛhya iti paṭhati teṣām imam jīvam idriya grāmam vā parigṛhya śarīram utthāpayati iti vyākhyeyam prajñā ātma tvam api jīve tāvat ceta a tvāt mukhye pi prāṇe eva evam jīva mukhya prāṇa parigrahe ca prāṇa prajñā ātmaoḥ saha vṛtti tvena abhedairdeśaḥ svarūpeṇa ca iti ubhayathā api upapadyate yaḥ vai prāṇaḥ sā prajñā yā vai prajñā sa prāṇaḥ saha hi etau asmin śarīre vasataḥ saha utkrāmataḥ iti brahma parigrahe tu kim kasmāt bhidyeta tasmāt iha jīva mukhya prāṇayoḥ ubhau vā pratīyeyātām brahma iti ced evam upāsā traividhyāt evam sati trividham upāsaam prasajyeta jīva upāsaam mukhya prāṇa upāsaam brahma upāsaam ca iti yuktam upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām hi vākya eka vākya tvam avagamyate mām eva vijāīhi iti upakramya prāṇaḥ asmi prajñā ātmā tam mām āyuḥ amṛtam iti upāssva iti uktvā ate saḥ eṣa prāṇaḥ eva iti eka rūpau upakrama upasaṃhārau dṛśyete tatra artha eka tvam yuktam āśrayitum ca pariṇetum śakyam bhūtamātrāṇām prajñāmātrāṇām ca brahmaṇaḥ yatra arpaṇā upapatteḥ āśrita tvāt ca a yatra api brahma liṅga vaśāt prāṇa śabdasya brahmaṇi pravṛtteḥ iha api ca hitatama upayāsa ādi brahma liṅga yogāt brahma upadeśaḥ eva ayam iti gamyate yat tu mukhya prāṇa liṅgam darśitam idam śarīram parigṛhya utthāpayati iti tat asat prāṇa vyāpārasya api paramātma āyatta tvāt paramātmay upacaritum śakya tvāt martyaḥ jīvati kaḥ ca itareṇa tu jīvati yasmin etau upāśritau iti śruteḥ yat api a vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt ityādi jīva liṅgam darśitam tat api a brahma pakṣam ivārayati a hi brahmaṇaḥ tattvam asi aham brahma asmi ityādi śrutibhyaḥ buddhi ādi upādhi kṛtam tu viśeṣam āśritya brahma eva sa jīvaḥ kartā bhoktā ca iti ucyate tasya upādhi kṛta viśeṣa parityāge svarūpam brahma darśayitum a vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt ityādiā pratyagātma abhimukhīkaraṇa arthaḥ upadeśaḥ virudhyate yat vācā abhyuditam vāc abhyudyate tat eva brahma tvam viddhi yat idam upāsate ityādi ca śrutyataram vacaḥ ādi kriyā vyāpṛtasya eva ātmanaḥ brahmatvam darśayati yat puar etat uktam saha hi etau asmin śarīre vasataḥ saha utkrāmataḥ iti prāṇa prajñā ātmaoḥ bheda darśaam brahma vādī opapadyate iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ jñā akriyā śakti dvaya āśrayayoḥ buddhi prāṇayoḥ pratyagātma upādhi bhūtayoḥ bhedaiḥ deśa upapatteḥ upādhi dvaya upahitasya tu pratyagātmanaḥ svarūpeṇa abhedaḥ iti atas prāṇaḥ eva prajñā ātmā iti ekīkaraṇam aviruddham athavā opāsā traividhyāt āśrita tvāt iha tad yogāt iti asya ayam ayaḥ arthaḥ brahma vākye api jīva mukhya prāṇa liṅgam virudhyate katham upāsā traividhyāt trividham iha brahmaṇaḥ upāsaam vivakṣitam prāṇa dharmeṇa prajñā dharmeṇa svadharmeṇa ca tatra āyuḥ amṛtam iti upāssva āyuḥ prāṇaḥ iti idam śarīram parigṛhya utthāpayati iti tasmāt etat eva uktham upāsīta iti ca prāṇa dharmaḥ atha yathā asyai prajñāyai sarvāṇi bhūtāya ekībhavati tat vyākhyāsyāmaḥ iti upakramya vāc eva asyāḥ ekam aṅgam adūduhat tasyai parastāt prativihitā bhūtamātrā prajñayā vācam samāruhya vācā sarvāṇi āmāya apoti ityādiḥ prajñā dharmaḥ tāḥ vai etāḥ daśa eva bhūtamātrāḥ adhiprajñam daśa prajñāmātrāḥ adhibhūtam yadi bhūtamātrāḥ a syuḥ a prajñāmātrāḥ syuḥ yadi prajñāmātrāḥ a syuḥ a bhūtamātrāḥ syuḥ rūpam sidhyet tat yathā rathasya areṣu emiḥ arpitāḥ arpitāḥ evam eva etāḥ bhūtamātrāḥ prajñāmātrāsu arpitāḥ prajñāmātrāḥ prāṇa īrpitāḥ saḥ eṣa prāṇaḥ eva prajñā ātmā ityādiḥ brahma dharmaḥ tasmāt brahmaṇaḥ eva etat upādhi dvaya dharmeṇa svadharmeṇa ca ekam upāsaam trividham vivakṣitam maomayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ ityādau upādhi dharmeṇa brahmaṇaḥ upāsaam āśritam iha api tat yujyate vākyasya upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām eka artha tva avagamāt prāṇa prajñā ātma brahma liṅga avagamāt ca tasmāt brahma vākyam eva etat iti siddham iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye prathama adhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ murat prathamaḥ udhyāyaḥ dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ sarvatra prasiddha upadeśāt sarvatraprasiddhi adhikaraṇam idam āmāyate sarvam khalu idam brahma tat jalāiti śātaḥ upāsīta atha khalu kratu mayaḥ puruṣaḥ yathā a kratuḥ asimat loke puruṣaḥ bhavati tathā itas pretya bhavati sa kratum kurvīta maomayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha maomaya tva ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ śārīraḥ ātmā upāsyatvena upadiśyate āhosvit param brahma iti kim tāvat prāptam śārīraḥ iti kutas tasya hi kārya karaṇa
