adhipateḥ prasiddhaḥ a parasya brahmaṇaḥ a prāṇaḥ hi a a āḥ śubhraḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ sarvam khalu idam brahma iti sva śabde eva brahma upāttam katham iha śārīre ātmā upāsya tve āśaṅkyate ā eṣa doṣaḥ vākyam brahma upāsa a vidhi param kim tarhi śama vidhi param yatkāraṇam sarvam khalu idam brahma tat jalaiḥ iti śātaḥ upāsīta iti āha etat uktam bhavati yasmāt sarvam idam vikāra jātam brahma eva tad ja tvāt talla tvāt tad aa tvāt ca a ca sarvasya eka ātma tve rāga ādayaḥ saṃbhavati tasmāt śātaḥ upāsīta iti a ca śama vidhi para tve vākye brahma upāsaam śakyate tu sa kratum kurvīta iti vidhīyate kratuḥ saṃkalpaḥ tasya ca śrūyate maomayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ iti jīva liṅgam atas brūmaḥ jīva viṣayam etat upāsaam iti sarva karmā sarva kāmaḥ ityādi api śrūyamāṇam paryāyeṇa jīva viṣayam upapadyate eṣa me ātmā atas hṛdayeṇīyaḥ vrīheḥ vā yavāt vā iti ca hṛdaya āyata atvam aṇīyaḥ tvam cāra agra mātrasya jīvasya avakalpate brahmaṇaḥ ityādi api iti atra brūmaḥ a tāvat aṇīyaḥ tvam jyāyaḥ tvam ca ubhayam ekasmin samāśrayitum śakyam virodhāt ca prathama śruta tvāt aṇīyaḥ tvam yuktam āśrayitum jyāyaḥ tvam tu brahma bhāva apekṣayā bhaviṣyati iti ca jīva viṣaya tve etat brahma iti tat api prakṛta parāmarśa ārtha tvāt jīva viṣayam eva tasmāt aomaya tva ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ jīvaḥ upāsyaḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ param eva brahma iha maomaya tva ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ upāsyam kutas sarvatra prasiddha upadeśāt yat sarveṣu prasiddham jagat kāraṇam iha ca sarvam khalu idam brahma iti vākya upakrame śrutam tat eva maomaya tva ādi dharmaiḥ viśiṣṭam upadiśyate iti yuktam evam ca sati prakṛta hāā prakṛta prakriye vākya upakrame śama vidhi vivakṣayā brahma a sva vivakṣayā iti uktam atra ucyate yadi api śama vidhi vivakṣayā brahma tathā api maomaya tva ādiṣu upadiśyamāeṣu tat eva brahma saṃihitam bhavati jīvaḥ tu a saṃihitaḥ a ca sva śabdena upāttaḥ iti vaiṣamyam vivakṣita guṇa upapatteḥ ca vaktum iṣṭāḥ vivakṣitāḥ yadi api apauruṣeye vede vaktuḥ abhāvāt ecchā arthaḥ saṃbhavati tathā api upādāea phaleā upacaryate loke pi yad śabda abhihitam upādeyam bhavati tat vivakṣitam iti ucyate yat aupādeyam tat avivakṣitam iti tadvat vede pi upādeya tve abhihitam vivakṣitam bhavati itarat avivakṣitam tu veda vākya tātparyā tātparyābhyām avagamyete tat iha ye vivakṣitāḥ guṇāḥ upāsaāyām upādeya tve upadiṣṭāḥ satya saṃkalpa prabhṛtayaḥ te parasmin brahmaṇi upapadyate satya saṃkalpa tvam as iti evam anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya any hi sṛṣṭi sthiti saṃhāreṣu apratibaddha śakti tvāt paramātmā eva avakalpate ca yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā iti atra satya kāmaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ iti śrutam ākāśa ātmā iti ca ākāśa vat ātmā asya iti arthaḥ sarvagata tva ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ saṃbhavati ākāśe sāmyam brahmaṇaḥ jyāyā pṛthivyāḥ ityādi ca etat eva darśayati yat api ākāśaḥ ātmā asya iti vyākhyāyate tat api saṃbhavati sarva jagat kāraṇasya brahmaṇaḥ ākāśa ātma tvam atas eva sarva karmā ityādi evam iha upāsya tayā vivakṣitāḥ guṇāḥ brahmaṇi upapadyate yat tu uktam maomayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ iti jīva liṅgam a tat brahmaṇi upapadyate iti tat api brahmaṇi upapadyate iti brūmaḥ sarva ātma tvāt dhi brahmaṇaḥ bhavati tathā ca brahma viṣaye śruti smṛtī bhavataḥ tvam strī tvam pumān asi tvam kumāraḥ uta vā kumārī tvam jīrṇaḥ vañcasi tvam jātaḥ bhavasi viśvatomukhaḥ iti sarvatas pāṇi pādam tat sarvatas akṣi śiraḥ mukham sarvatas śrutimat loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati iti ca aprāṇaḥ hi amaāḥ śubhraḥ iti śrutiḥ śuddha brahma viṣayā iyam tu śrutiḥ maomayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ iti saguṇa brahma viṣayā iti viśeṣaḥ atas vivakṣita guṇa upapatteḥ param eva brahma gamyate aupapatteḥ tu a śārīraḥ pūrveṇa sūtreṇa brahmaṇi vivakṣitāām guṇāām upapattiḥ uktā śārīre teṣām aupapattiḥ ucyate tuśabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ brahma eva uktea maomaya tva ādi guṇam a tu śārīraḥ jīvaḥ maomaya tva ādi guṇaḥ yatkāraṇam satya saṃkalpaḥ ākāśa ātmā avākī aādaraḥ jyāyāpṛthivyāḥ iti ca evaṃjātīyakāḥ guṇāḥ a śārīre śārīra iti śarīre bhavaḥ iti arthaḥ śarīre bhavati satyam śarīre bhavati a tu śarīre eva bhavati jyāyā pṛthivyāḥ jyāyāḥ atarikṣāt ākāśa vat sarva gataḥ ca iti ca vyāpi tva śravaṇāt jīvaḥ tu śarīre eva bhavati tasya śarīrāt ayatra vṛtti abhāvāt karma kartṛ vyapadeśāt ca itas ca a śārīraḥ yasmāt karma kartṛ vyapadeśaḥ bhavati etam itas pretya abhisaṃbhavitāsmi iti etam iti prakṛtam maomaya tva ādi guṇam upāsyam ātmā vyapadiśati abhisaṃbhavitāsmi iti śārīram upāsakam kartṛ tvea prāpaka tvea abhisaṃbhavitāsmi iti prāptāsmi iti arthaḥ ca satyām gatau ekasya karma kartṛ vyapadeśaḥ yuktaḥ tathā upāsya upāsaka bhāvaḥ api bheda adhiṣṭhāaḥ eva tasmāt api a śārīraḥ maomaya tva ādi viśiṣṭaḥ śabda viśeṣāt itas ca śārīrāt ayaḥ maomaya tva ādi guṇaḥ yasmāt śabda viśeṣaḥ bhavati samāa prakaraṇe śrutyatare yathā vrīhiḥ vā yavaḥ vā śyāmākaḥ vā śyāmāka taṇḍulaḥ vā evam ayam atarātma puruṣaḥ hiraṇmayaḥ iti śārīrasya ātmanaḥ yaḥ śabdaḥ abhidhāyakaḥ saptamī atas atarātmā eti tasmāt viśiṣṭaḥ yaḥ prathamātaḥ puruṣa śabdaḥ tasmāt tayoḥ bhedaḥ adhigamyate smṛteḥ ca smṛtiḥ ca śārīra paramātmaoḥ bhedam darśayati īśvaraḥ sarva bhūtānām tiṣṭhati māyayā ityādyāḥ atra āha kaḥ yaḥ yaḥ pratiṣidhyate aupapatteḥ tu a śārīraḥ ityādiā śrutiḥ tu draṣṭā śrotā iti evaṃjātīyakā vārayati tathā smṛtiḥ api kṣetrajñam ca api mām viddhi sarva kṣetreṣu bhārataḥ iti evaṃjātīyakā iti atra ucyate satyam eva etat paraḥ eva ātmā deha idriya maaḥ buddhi upādhibhiḥ bālaiḥ śārīraḥ iti upacaryate yathā ghaṭa karaka ādi upādhi vaśāt aparicchiam api abhaḥ tadvat tad apekṣayā ca karma kartṛ tva ādi bheda vyavahāraḥ as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tatra as tat virudhyate prāk tat tvam asi iti ātma ekatva upadeśa grahaṇāt gṛhīte tu ātma ekatve badha mokṣa ādi sarva vyavahāra parisamāptiḥ eva syāt arbhaka okastvāt tad vyapadeśāt ca iti evam vyoma vat ca arbhakam alpam okaḥ īḍam eṣa me ātmā atas hṛdaye iti ca aṇīyāḥ vrīheḥ vā yavāt vā iti aṇīyaḥ tva vyapadeśāt śārīraḥ eva ara agra mātraḥ jīvaḥ iha upadiśyate a sarva gataḥ paramātmā iti yat uktam tat parihartavyam atra ucyate doṣaḥ doṣaḥ tāvat paricchia deśasya sarvagata tva vyapadeśaḥ katham api upapadyate sarvagatasya tu sarva deśeṣu kayācid apekṣayā saṃbhavati yathā samasta vasudhā adhipatiḥ api hi saḥ ayodhyā adhipatiḥ iti vyapadiśyate kayā sarva gataḥ aṇīyān ca vyapadiśyate iti icāyya tvāt evam iti brūmaḥ evam aṇīyaḥ tva ādi guṇa gaṇa upetaḥ īśvaraḥ tatra hṛdaya puṇḍarīke icāyyaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ upadiśyate yathā sālagrāme hariḥ tatra asya buddhi vijñāam grāhakam prasīdati vyoma vat ca etat draṣṭavyam yathā sarva gatam api sat vyoma sūcī pāśa ādi apekṣayā ca iti vyapadiśyate evam brahmā api tat evam icāyya tva apekṣam brahmaṇaḥ ca a pāramārthikam tatra yat āśaṅkyate hṛdaya āyata atvāt brahmaṇaḥ hṛdayāām ca pratiśarīram ca śuka ādīām ca śuka ādīām tadvat prasaṅgaḥ iti tat api parihṛtam bhavati sambhoga prāptiḥ iti ce a vaiśeṣyāt vyoma vat sarva gatasya brahmaṇaḥ cit rūpa tayā ca śārīrāt a viśiṣṭa tvāt sukha duḥkha ādi saṃbhogaḥ api a viśiṣṭaḥ prasajyeta ekatvāt ca a hi parasmāt ātmanaḥ ayaḥ kaścid ātmā saṃsārī vidyate āyaḥ atas asti vijñātā ityādi śrutibhyaḥ tasmāt parasya eva brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhoga prāptiḥ iti ced a vaiśeṣyāt a tāvat sarva prāṇi hṛdaya saṃbadhāt cit rūpa tayā ca śārīra vat brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhoga prasaṅgaḥ vaiśeṣyāt viśeṣaḥ hi bhavati śārīra parameśvarayoḥ ekaḥ kartā bhoktā dharma adharma ādi sādhaḥ sukha duḥkha ādimān ca ekaḥ tad viparītaḥ apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇaḥ etasmāt a ayoḥ viśeṣāt ekasya bhogaḥ etarasya yadi ca vastu śaktim a āśritya kārya saṃbadhaḥ abhyupagamyeta ākāśa ādīām api dāha ādi prasaṅgaḥ api codya parihārau yat api ekatvāt brahmaṇaḥ ātma atara abhāvāt śārīrasya bhoge brahmaṇaḥ bhoga prasaṅgaḥ iti atra vadāmaḥ idam tāvat devāām priyaḥ praṣṭavyaḥ katham ayam tvayā ātma atara abhāvaḥ adhyavasitaḥ iti tat tvam asi aham brahma asmi āyaḥ atas asti vijñātā ityādi śāstrebhyaḥ iti ced yathāśāstram tarhi śāstrīyaḥ ūrthaḥ pratipattavyaḥ labhyam śāstram ca tat tvam asi iti apahata pāpma tva ādi viśeṣaṇam brahma śārīrasya ātma tve upadiśat śārīrasya eva tāvat upabhoktṛ tvam vārayati kutas tad upabhoge brahmaṇaḥ upabhoga prasaṅgaḥ atha agṛhītam śārīrasya brahmaṇā ekatvam tadā mithyājñā aimittaḥ śārīrasya upabhogaḥ a paramārtha rūpasya brahmaṇaḥ saṃsparśaḥ a hi bālaiḥ tala malia tā ādibhiḥ vyomi tala malia tā ādi viśiṣṭam eva paramārthataḥ vyoma bhavati tat āha a vaiśeṣyāt iti aikatve api brahmaṇaḥ upabhoga prasaṅgaḥ vaiśeṣyāt viśeṣaḥ hi bhavati mithyājñā asamyagjñāayoḥ mithyājñā a kalpitaḥ upabhogaḥ samyagjñā adṛṣṭam ekatvam ca mithyājñā akalpite upabhoge samyagjñā adṛṣṭam vastu saṃspṛśyate śakyaḥ īśvarasya kalpayitum attā carācara grahaṇāt attṛ adhikaraṇam kaṭhavallīṣu paṭhyate yasya brahma ca kṣatram ca ubhe bhavataḥ odaḥ mṛtyuḥ yasya upasecaam kaḥ itthā veda yatra saḥ iti atra pratīyate tatra kim agirattā syāt uta jīvaḥ athavā paramātmā iti saṃśayaḥ viśeṣa a avadhāraṇāt trayāṇām kim tāvat prāptam agiratta iti kutas iti śruti prasiddhibhyām jīvaḥ vai attā syāt tayoḥ ayaḥ pippalam svādu atti iti darśaāt a paramātmā iti darśaāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ attā atra paramātmā bhavitum arhati kutas carācara grahaṇāt carācaram hi sthāvara jaṅgamam pratīyate tādṛśasya saṃbhavati paramātmā tu vikāra jātam saṃbhavati paramātmā tu vikāra jātam upasaṃhara sarvam atti iti upapadyate carācara grahaṇam upalabhyate katham siddha vat carācara grahaṇam hetu tve upādīyate sarvasya prāṇi ikāyasya sarvasya prāṇi nikāyasya brahma kṣatrayoḥ ca prādhāyāt pradarśa ārtha tva upapatteḥ yat tu āttṛ tvam saṃbhavati iti darśaāt iti atra ucyate karma phala bhogasya pratiṣedhakam etat darśaam tasya saṃihita tvāt a vikāra saṃhārasya pratiṣedhakam sarva vedāteṣu sṛṣṭi sthiti saṃhāra kāraṇa tve brahmaṇaḥ prasiddha tvāt tasmāt paramātmā eva iha attā bhavitum arhati prakaraṇāt ca itas ca paramātmā eva iha attā bhavitum arhati yatkāraṇam prakaraṇam idam paramātma aḥ jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit ityādi prakṛta grahaṇam ca yāyyam ka itthā veda yatra saḥ iti ca durvijñāa tvam paramātma liṅgam guhām praviṣṭau hi tad darśaāt guhā praviṣṭa adhikaraṇam kaṭhavallīṣu eva paṭhyate ṛtam pibatau sukṛtasya loke guhām praviṣṭau parame para ardhe chāyā ātapau brahma vidaḥ vadati pañca āgayaḥ ye ca triṇāciketāḥ kaṭhaḥ iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha buddhi jīvau irdiṣṭau uta jīva paramātmāām iti yadi buddhi jīvau tatas kārya karaṇa saṃghātāt vilakṣaṇaḥ jīvaḥ pratipāditaḥ bhavati tat api iha pratipādayitavyam yā iyam prete vicikisā eke ā ayam asti iti ca eke etad vidyām auśiṣṭaḥ tvayā aham varāṇām eṣa varaḥ tṛtīyaḥ iti pṛṣṭa tvāt atha jīva paramātma tatas jīvāt vilakṣaṇaḥ paramātmā pratipāditaḥ bhavati tat api iha pratipādayitavyam ayatra dharmāt ayatra adharmāt ayatra asmāt kṛta akṛtāt ayatra bhūtāt ca bhavyāt ca yat tat paśyasi tat vada iti pṛṣṭa tvāt atra āha ākṣeptā ubhau api etau pakṣau a saṃbhavataḥ kasmāt ṛta pāam hi karma phala upabhogaḥ sukṛtasya loke iti liṅgāt tat ca cetaasya kṣetrajñasya saṃbhavati buddheḥ pibatau iti dvayoḥ darśayati śrutiḥ atas buddhi kṣetrajña pakṣaḥ tāvat saṃbhavati atas eva kṣetrajña paramātma pakṣaḥ api saṃbhavati ayobhicākaśīti iti matra varṇāt iti atra ucyate ā eṣa doṣaḥ chatriṇaḥ gacchati iti eke api chatriṇā bahūām a chatriṇām chatri tva upacāra darśaāt evam eke api pibatā dvau pibatau ucyeyātām yat vā jīvaḥ tāvat pibati īśvaraḥ tu pāyayati pāyaya api pibati iti ucyate pācayitari api paktṛ tva prasiddhi darśaāt buddhi kṣetrajña parigrahaḥ api saṃbhavati karaṇe kartṛ tva upacārāt edhāṃsi pacati iti prayoga darśaāt a ca adhyātma adhikāreyau kaucid dvau ṛtam pibatau saṃbhavataḥ tasmāt buddhi jīvau syātām jīva paramātma au vā iti saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam buddhi kṣetrajñau iti kutas guhām praviṣṭau iti viśeṣaṇāt yadi śarīram guhā yadi vā hṛdayam ubhayathā api buddhi kṣetrajñau guhām praviṣṭau upapadyete a ca sati saṃbhave sarva gatasya brahmaṇaḥ viśiṣṭa deśa tvam yuktam kalpayitum sukṛtasya loke iti ca karma gocara aatikramam darśayati paramātmā tu a sukṛtasya vā duṣkṛtasya vā gocare vartate a karmaṇā vardhate o kaīyā iti śruteḥ chāyā ātapau iti ca ceta āceta ayoḥ irdeśaḥ upapadyate chāyā ātapa vat paraspara vilakṣaṇa tvāt tasmāt buddhi kṣetrajñau iha ucyeyātām iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ vijñāātma paramātmāau iha ucyeyātām kasmāt ātmaau hi tau ubhau api cetaau sama a svabhāvau saṃkhyā śravaṇe ca sama a svabhāveṣu eva loke pratītiḥ dṛśyate asya goḥ dvitīyaḥ uveṣṭavyaḥ iti ukte gauḥ eva dvitīyaḥ uviṣyate āśvaḥ puruṣaḥ vā tat iha dvitīya āveṣaṇāyām cetaaḥ paramātmā eva pratīyate guhā hita tva darśaā paramātmā pratyetavyaḥ iti guhā hita tva darśaāt eva paramātmā pratyetavyaḥ iti vadāmaḥ guhā hita tvam tu śruti smṛtiṣu asakṛt paramātma eva dṛśyate guhā hitam gahvareṣṭham purāṇam yaḥ veda ihitam guhāyām parame vyoma ātmā aviccha guhām praviṣṭam ityādyāsu sarva gatasya api brahmaṇaḥ upalabdhi arthaḥ deśa viśeṣa upadeśaḥ virudhyata iti etat api uktam eva sukṛta loka varti tvam tu chatri tva vat ekasmin api ubhayoḥ aviruddham chāyā ātapau iti api aviruddham chāyā ātapa vat paraspara vilakṣaṇa tvāt saṃsāri tva asaṃsāri tvayoḥ avidyā kṛta tvāt saṃsāri tvasya pāramārthika tvāt ca asaṃsāri tvasya tasmāt vijñā ātma paramātmau guhām praviṣṭau gṛhyete kutas ca vijñā ātma paramātmau gṛhyete viśeṣaṇāt ca viśeṣaṇam ca vijñā ātma paramātmaoḥ eva bhavati ātmāam rathiam viddhi śarīram ratham eva tu ityādiā pareṇa rathi ratha ādi rūpaka kalpaayā vijñā ātmāam rathiam saṃsāra mokṣayoḥ kalpayati tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam iti paramātmāam gatavyam kalpayati tathā tam durdarśam gūḍham aupraviṣṭam guhā hitam gahvareṣṭham purāṇam devam matvā dhīraḥ harṣa śokau jahāti iti pūrvasmi api grathe etau eva viśeṣitau prakaraṇam ca idam paramātmā brahma vidaḥ vadati kaṭhaḥ iti ca vaktṛ viśeṣa upādāam paramātma parigrahe ghaṭate tasmāt iha jīva paramātma au ucyeyātām eṣaḥ eva yāyaḥ dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyau iti evamādiṣu api tatra api hi adhyātma adhikārāḥ a prākṛtau suparṇau ucyete tayoḥ ayaḥ pippalam svādu atti iti ada a liṅgāt vijñā ātmā bhavati iti aaśa aceta a tvābhyām paramātmā ca tau eva draṣṭṛ draṣṭavya bhāve viśiaṣṭi vṛkṣe puruṣaḥ śocati juṣṭam yadā paśyati ayam īśam asya mahimā am iti vīta śokaḥ iti aparaḥ āha dvār suparṇāḥ iti siddhātam bhajate paiṅgi rahasyabrāhmaṇe ayathā vyākhyāta tvāt tayoḥ ayaḥ pippalam svādu atti iti sattvam aaśca ayaḥ abhicākaśīti iti aaśca ayaḥ abhipaśyati jñaḥ tau etau sattva kṣetrajñau iti sattva śabdaḥ jīvaḥ kṣetrajña śabdaḥ paramātmā iti yat ucyate taa anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya sattva kṣetrajña śabdayoḥ ataḥkaraṇa śārīra para tayā prasiddha tvāt tatra eva ca vyākhyāta tvāt tat etat sattvam svapam paśyati atha yaḥ yam śārīraḥ upadraṣṭā sa kṣetrajñaḥ tau etau sattva kṣetrajñau iti āpyasya adhikaraṇasya pūrvapakṣa bhāvam bhajate a hi atra śārīraḥ kṣetrajñaḥ saṃsāra dharmeṇa upetaḥ vivakṣyate katham tarhi sarva saṃsāra dharma atītaḥ brahma svabhāvaḥ caitaya mātra svarūpaḥ jñaḥ iti vacaāt tattvam asi kṣetrajñam ca api mām viddhi ityādi śruti smṛtibhyaḥ ca tāvatā ca vidyā upasaṃhāra darśam evam eva avakalpate tau etau sattva kṣetrajñau ha vā evaṃvidi kiṃcaa rajaḥ ādhvaṃsate ityādi katham tayoḥ ayaḥ pippalam svādu atti iti sattvam iti acetae sattve ucyate śrutiḥ acetaasya sattve bhoktṛ tva vacaam iti ucyate śrutiḥ acetaasya sattvasya bhoktṛ tvam vakṣyāmi iti pravṛttā kim tarhi cetaasya kṣetrajñasya abhoktṛ tvam brahma svabhāvatām ca vakṣyāmi iti tad artham sukha duḥkha ādi vikriyāvati sattve bhoktṛ tvam adhyāropayati idam hi kartṛ tvam bhoktṛ tvam ca sattva kṣetrajñayoḥ itaretara svabhāva aviveka kṛtam kalpyate paramārthataḥ tu āyatarasya api saṃbhavati acetaa tvāt sattvasya avikriya tvāt ca kṣetrajñasya avidyā pratyupasthāpita svabhāva tvāt ca sattvasya sutarām saṃbhavati tathā ca śrutiḥ yatra vai ayat iva syāt tatra ayaḥ yat paśyet ityādiā avidyā viṣayaḥ eva kartṛ tva ādi vyavahāram darśayati yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kam paśyet ityādiā ca vivekiḥ kartṛ tva ādi vyavahāram iva ārayati ataraḥ upapatteḥ atara adhikaraṇam yaḥ eṣa u kṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate eṣaḥ ātmā iti ha uvāca etat amṛtam abhayam etat brahma iti tat yadi api asmi sarpiḥ vā udakam vā siñcati eva gacchati ityādi śrūyate tatra saṃśayaḥ kim ayam pratibimba ātmā akṣi adhikaraṇaḥ atha vijñā ātmā uta devatā ātmā idriyasya adhiṣṭhātā athavā īśvara iti kim tāvat prāptam chāyā ātmā puruṣa pratirūpaḥ iti kutas tasya dṛśyamāa tva prasiddheḥ yaḥ eṣa ukṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate iti ca prasiddha vat upadeśāt vijñāātmao vā ayam iḥ deśaḥ iti yuktam sa hi cakṣuṣā rūpam paśyan cakṣuṣi saṃihitaḥ bhavati ātma śabdaḥ ca asmi pakṣe ukūlaḥ bhavati āditya puruṣaḥ vā cakṣuṣaḥ u grāhakaḥ pratīyate raśmibhiḥ eṣaḥ asmi pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti śruteḥ amṛta tva ādīām ca api kathaṃcid saṃbhavāt eśvaraḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ parameśvaraḥ eva akṣiṇi abhyataraḥ puruṣaḥ iha upadiṣṭaḥ iti kasmāt upapatteḥ upapadyate hi parameśvare guṇa jātam ātmatvam tāva mukhyayā vṛttyā parameśvare upapadyate saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi iti śruteḥ amṛta tva abhaya tve ca asakṛt śrūyete tathā etat etat yathā hi parameśvaraḥ sarva doṣaiḥ aliptaḥ apahata pāpma tva ādi śravaṇāt tathā akṣi sthāam sarva lepa rahitam upadiṣṭam tat yadi api asmi sarpiḥ vā udakam vā siñcati vartmaī eva gacchati iti śruteḥ saṃyat vāma tva ādi guṇa upadeśaḥ ca avakalpate etam saṃyat vāma iti ācakṣate etam hi sarvāṇi vāmāi abhisaṃyati eṣaḥ u eva vāmaīḥ eṣa hi sarvāṇi ayati eṣaḥ u eva bhāmaīḥ eṣa hi sarveṣu lokeṣu bhāti iti ca atas upapatteḥ ataraḥ parameśvaraḥ sthā ādi vyapadeśāt ca katham puar ākāśa vat sarva gatasya brahmaṇaḥ akṣi alpam upapadyate iti atra ucyate bhavet eṣā avakḷptiḥ yadi etat eva ekam bhavet sati hi api yaḥ pṛthivyām tiṣṭhe teṣu hi cakṣuḥ api irdiṣṭam yaḥ cakṣuṣi tiṣṭhe iti sthā ādi vyapadeśāt iti ādi grahaṇe etat darśayati a kevalam brahmaṇaḥ kim tarhi āma rūpam iti evaṃjātīyakam api a āma rūpasya dṛśyate tasya uditi hiraṇya śmaśruḥ ityādi hirguṇam api sat brahma āma rūpa gataiḥ guṇaiḥ sa guṇam upāsa artham tatra tatra upadiśyate iti etat api uktam eva sarva gatasya api brahmaṇaḥ upalabdhi artham virudhyate sālagrāmaḥ iva viṣṇoḥ iti etat api uktam eva sukha viśiṣṭa abhidhāāt eva ca api ca vivaditavyam kim brahma a vā iti sukha viśiṣṭa abhidhāāt eva brahma tvam siddham sukha viśiṣṭam hi brahma yat vākya upakrame prakrātam prāṇaḥ brahma kam brahma kham brahma iti tat eva iha abhihitam prakṛta parigrahasya yāyya tvāt ācāryaḥ tu te gatim vaktā iti ca gati mātra abhidhāa pratijñāāt katham puar vākya upakrame sukha viśiṣṭam brahma vijñāyate iti ucyate prāṇaḥ brahma kam brahma kham brahma iti etat agīām vacaam śrutvā upakosalaḥ uvāca aham yat prāṇaḥ brahma kam ca kham ca tu iti tatra idam prativacaam yat vāva kam tat eva kham yat eva kham tat eva kam iti tatra kham śabdaḥ bhūtākāśe loke yadi tasya kaṃ śabdaḥ sukha vācī opādīyeta tathā sati kevale bhūtākāśe brahma śabdaḥ āma ādiṣu iva pratīka abhiprāyeṇa prayuktaḥ iti pratītiḥ syāt tathā kaṃ śabdasya viṣaya idriya saṃparka ja ete sāmaye sukhe prasiddha tvāt yadi tasya khaṃśabdaḥ laukikam sukham brahma iti pratītiḥ syāt itara itara viśeṣitau tu kaṃ khaṃ śabdau sukha ātmakam brahma gamayataḥ tatra dvitīye brahma śabde upādīyamāe kam kham brahma iti eva ucyamāe kaṃ śabdasya syāt bhūt iti ubhayoḥ kaṃ khaṃ śabdayoḥ brahma śabda śiraḥ tvam kam brahma kham brahma iti iṣṭam hi sukhasya api guṇasya guṇi vat dhyeya tvam tat evam vākya upakrame sukha viśiṣṭam brahma upadiṣṭam pratyekam ca gārhapatya āda yogayaḥ svam svam mahimā upadiśya eṣā somya ca iti upasaṃharataḥ pūrvatra brahma iti jñāpayati ācāryaḥ tu te gatim vaktā iti ca vārayati yathā puṣkarapalāśe śliṣyate evam evaṃvidi pāpam karma śliṣyate iti ca akṣi sthāam puruṣam vijāataḥ puruṣasya brahmatvam darśayati tasmāt prakṛtasya eva brahmaṇā ukṣi sthāatām saṃyat vāma tva ādi guṇatām ca uktvā arciḥ ādikām tad vidaḥ gatim vakṣyāmi iti upakramate yaḥ eṣa ukṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate eṣaḥ ātmā iti ha uvāca iti itas ca akṣi sthāaḥ puruṣaḥ parameśvaraḥ yasmāt brahma vidaḥ yā gatiḥ devayāā ākhyā prasiddhā śrutau atha uttareṇa tapasā brahmacaryeṇa śraddhayā vidyayā ādityam abhijayate etat vai prāṇāām āyataam etat amṛtam abhayam etat parāyaṇam etasmāt puarāvartate iti smṛtau api agiḥ jyotiḥ ahar śuklaḥ ṣaṣ māsāḥ uttarāyaṇam tatra prayātā gacchati brahma brahman vidaḥ iti sa eva iha akṣi puruṣa vidaḥ dṛśyate atha yat u ca eva asmin śavyam kurvati yadi ca ārciṣam eva abhisaṃbhavati iti upakramya ādityāt cadramasam cadramasaḥ vidyutam tat puruṣaḥ umāavaḥ saḥ eābrahma gamayati eṣa deva pathaḥ brahma pathaḥ pratipadyamāā imam āvartam āvartate iti tat iha brahma vid viṣayayā prasiddhayā gatyā akṣi sthāasya brahmatvam a avasthiteḥ asambhavāt ca etaraḥ yat puar uktam chāyā ātmā vijñā ātmā devatā ātmā vā syāt akṣi sthāaḥ iti atra ucyate a chāyā ātma ādiḥ itaraḥ iha grahaṇam arhati kasmāt a avasthiteḥ cakṣuṣi saṃbhavati yadā eva hi kaścid puruṣaḥ cakṣuḥ āsīdati tadā cakṣuṣi puruṣa chāyā dṛśyate apagate tasmin dṛśyate yaḥ eṣa ukṣiṇi puruṣaḥ iti ca śrutiḥ saṃidhāāt sva cakṣuṣi dṛśyamāam puruṣam upāsya tve upadiśati ca upāsaā kāle chāyākaram kaṃcid puruṣam cakṣuḥ samīpe saṃidhāpya upāste iti yuktam kalpayitum asya eva śarīrasya āśam aśyati iti śrutiḥ a avasthita tvam darśayati ca sādhāraṇe sati a cakṣuṣi eva avasthita tvam śakyam vaktum brahmaṇaḥ tu dṛṣṭaḥ upalabdhi arthaḥ hṛdaya ādi deśa viśeṣa ca api amṛta tva ādīām guṇāām asaṃbhavaḥ yadi api vijñāātmā eva tathā api a vidyā kām a karma kṛtam martya tvam adhyāropitam bhayam ca iti amṛta tva abhaya tve opapadyete saṃyat vāma tva ādayaḥ ca etasmi aaiśvaryāt eva devatā ātmaaḥ tu raśmibhiḥ eṣaḥ u smi pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti śruteḥ yadi api cakṣuṣi syāt tathā api ātmatvam saṃbhavati parāk rūpatvāt amṛta tva ādayaḥ saṃbhavati utpatti pralaya śravaṇāt amara tvam api devāām cira kāla avasthā a apekṣam aiśvaryam api parameśvara āyattam a svābhāvikam bhīṣā asmāt vātaḥ pavate bhīṣā udeti sūryaḥ bhīṣā asmāt agiḥ ca idraḥ ca mṛtyuḥ dhāvati pañcamaḥ iti matra varṇāt tasmāt parameśvaraḥ eva ayam akṣi sthāaḥ pratyetavyaḥ asmin ca pakṣe dṛśyate iti prasiddha vat śāstra ādi apekṣam vidvat viṣayam praroca artham iti vyākhyeyam ataryāmi adhidaiva ādiṣu tad dharma vyapadeśāt ataryāmi adhikaraṇam yaḥ imam ca lokam param ca lokam sarvāṇi ca bhūtāyataraḥ yamayati iti upakramya śrūyate yaḥ pṛthivyām tiṣṭha pṛthivyāḥ ataraḥ yam pṛthivī veda yasya pṛthivī śarīram yaḥ pṛthivīm ataraḥ yamayati eṣa te ātmā ataryāmī amṛtaḥ ityādi atra adhidaivatam adhilokam adhivedam adhiyajñam adhibhūtam adhyātmam ca kaścid atas avasthitaḥ yamayitā ataryāmī iti śrūyate sa kim adhidaiva ādi abhimāī devatā ātmā kaścid kim vā prāpta aṇima ādi aiśvaryaḥ kaścid yogī kim vā paramātmā kim vā arthātaram kiṃcitaḥ iti apūrva saṃjñā darśaāt saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat pratibhāti saṃjñāyāḥ aprasiddha tvāt arthātareṇa kaścid bhavitavyam iti athavā āi rūpita rūpam arthātaram kiṃcid api śakyam asti iti abhyupagatum ataryāmi śabdaḥ tasmāt pṛthivī ādi abhimāī kaścid syāt tathā ca śrūyate pṛthivī eva ityādi sa ca kārya karaṇavat tvāt pṛthivī ādi atas yuktam yamayitṛ tvam vā kasyacid siddhasya yamayitṛ tvam syāt a tu paramātmā pratīyate akārya karaṇa tvāt iti evam prāpte idam ucyate yotaryāmi adhidaiva ādiṣu śrūyate sa paramātmā eva syāt āyaḥ iti kutas tad dharma vyapadeśāt tasya hi paramātmanaḥ dharmāḥ dṛśyate pṛthivī ādi tāvat adhidaiva ādi bheda bhiam samastam vikāra jātam atas tiṣṭha yamayati iti paramātmanaḥ yamayitṛ tvam dharmaḥ upapadyate sarva vikāra kāraṇa tve sati sarva śakti upapatteḥ eṣa te ātmā ataryāmī amṛtaḥ iti ca ātma tva amṛta tve mukhye paramātma upapadyete yam pṛthivī a veda iti ca pṛthivī devatāyāḥ avijñeyam ataryāmiṇam darśayati pṛthivī devatā hi aham asmi pṛthivī iti ātmā tathā ityādi vyapadeśaḥ ityādi vyapadeśaḥ upapadyate iti yat tu a kārya karaṇasya yamayitṛ tvam upapadyate iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ tad kārya karaṇaiḥ eva tasya kārya karaṇavat tva upapatteḥ tasya api ayaḥ iyatā iti a avasthā doṣaḥ ca saṃbhavati bheda abhāvāt bhede hi sati a avasthā doṣa upapattiḥ tasmāt paramātmā eva ataryāmī ca smārtam ataddharma abhilāpāt syāt etat adṛṣṭa tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ sāṃkhya smṛti kalpitasya pradhā asya api upapadyate tasya taiḥ abhyupagamāt apratarkyam avijñeyam prasuptam iva sarvatas iti hi smarati tasya api iyatṛ tvam sarva vikāra kāraṇa tvāt upapadyate tasmāt pradhāam ataryāmi śabdam syāt īkṣaterā śabdam iti atra irākṛtam api sat atas uttaram ucyate ca smārtam pradhā a mataryāmi śabdam bhavitum arhati kasmāt a tad dharma abhilāpāt yadi api a dṛṣṭa tva ādi vyapadeśaḥ pradhā asya saṃbhavati tathā api a draṣṭṛ tva ādi vyapadeśaḥ saṃbhavati taiḥ abhyupagamāt adṛṣṭaḥ draṣṭā aśrutaḥ śrotā amataḥ mata avijñātaḥ vijñātā iti hi vākyaśeṣaḥ iha bhavati ātmatvam api a pradhāasya upapadyate yadi śārīraḥ tarhi ataryāmī bhavatu śārīraḥ hi ceta atvāt draṣṭā śrotā matā vijñātā ca bhavati ātmā ca pratyak tvāt amṛtaḥ ca dharma adharma phala upabhoga upapatteḥ adṛṣṭa tva ādayaḥ ca dharmāḥ śārīre su prasiddhāḥ darśa ādi kriyāyāḥ kartari pravṛtti virodhāt a dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭāram paśyeḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ca tasya ca kārya karaṇa saṃghātam ataryamayitum śīlam bhoktṛ tvāt tasmāt śārīra utaryāmī iti atas uttaram paṭhati śārīraḥ ca ubhaye pi hi hi śārīraḥ ca ātaryāmī syāt kasmāt yadi api draṣṭṛ tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ tasya saṃbhavati tathā api ghaṭa ākāśa vat upādhi paricchia tvāa ca śakoti api ca ubhaye api hi śākhiaḥ kāṇvāḥ mādhyaṃdiāḥ cātaryāmiṇaḥ śārīram śārīram ca ādhīyate yaḥ yaḥ tiṣṭhe iti kāṇvāḥ yaḥ ātmai tiṣṭhe iti mādhyaṃdiāḥ yaḥ ātmai tiṣṭhe iti asmin tāvat pāṭhe bhavati ātma śabdaḥ śārīrasya vācakaḥ yaḥ vijñāe tiṣṭhe iti asmin api pāṭhe śārīraḥ ucyate vijñā a mayaḥ hi śārīraḥ iti tasmāt śārīra ādayaḥ īśvara utaryāmī iti siddham katham puar ekasmin dehe dvau draṣṭārau upapadyete yaḥ ca ayam īśvara utaryāmī yaḥ ca ayam itaraḥ śārīraḥ kā puariha a upapattiḥ virudhyeta atra hi prakṛtāt ataryāmiṇaḥ yam draṣṭāram śrotāram matāram vijñātāram ca ātmā pratiṣedhati iyatratara pratiṣedha artham etat vacam iti ced a iyatratara aprasaṅgāt aviśeṣa śravaṇāt ca atra ucyate avidyā pratyupasthāpita kārya karaṇa upādhi nimittaḥ yam śārīra ataryāmiṇoḥ bheda vyapadeśaḥ a pāramārthikaḥ ekaḥ hi pratyagātmā bhavati a dvau pratyagātmāau saṃbhavataḥ ekasya eva tu bheda vyavahāra upādhi kṛtaḥ yathā ghaṭa ākāśaḥ mahā ākāśaḥ iti tatas ca jñātṛ jñeya ādi bheda śrutayaḥ ca sarvam etat upapadyate tathā ca śrutiḥ yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tat itaraḥ itaram paśyati iti avidyā viṣaye sarvam vyavahāram darśayati yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kea kam paśyet iti vidyā viṣaye sarvam vyavahāram vārayati adṛśya tva ādi guṇakaḥ dharma ukteḥ adṛśya tva ādi adhikaraṇam atha parā yayā tat akṣaram adhigamyate yat tat a dreśyam a grāhyam a gotram a varṇam a cakṣuḥ śrotram tat apāṇi pādam vibhum sarva gatam su sūkṣmam tat avyayam yat bhūtayoim paripaśyati dhīrāḥ iti śrūyate tatra saṃśayaḥ kim ayam adṛśya tva ādi guṇakaḥ syāt uta śārīraḥ āhosvit parameśvara iti tatra pradhāam acetaam yuktam tatra tatra iti puruṣaḥ ca cetaau iha eti brūmaḥ a hi kevalasya cetaasya tatra keśa loma yoitvam vā asti cetaḥ dhiṣṭhitam hi acetaam ūrṇaābhi śarīram sūtrasya puruṣa śarīram ca keśalomām iti prasiddham api ca pūrvatra adṛṣṭa tva ādi abhilāpa saṃbhave pi draṣṭṛ tva ādi abhilāpa asaṃbhavāt pradhāe abhyupagatam iha tu adṛśya tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ pradhāe saṃbhavati ca atra dharmaḥ kaścid abhilapyate yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vid iti ayam katham bhūta yoiḥ pratijñāyate iti atra ucyate yayā tat akṣaram adhigamyate yat tat adreśyam iti akṣara śabdena adṛśya tva ādi guṇakam śrāvayitvā śrāvayiṣyati akṣarāt paratas paraḥ iti tatra yaḥ parokṣarāt śrutaḥ sa sarvajñaḥ sarva vid saṃbhaviṣyati yadā tu akṣara śabdaiḥ diṣṭam yadā tu imitta vācī tadā śārīraḥ api syāt dharma adharmābhyām bhūta jātasya iti evam prāpte abhidhīyate yaḥ yam adṛśya tva ādi guṇakaḥ sa parameśvaraḥ eva syāt āyaḥ iti katham etat avagamyate dharma ukteḥ parameśvarasya hi dharmaḥ iha ucyamānaḥ dṛśyate yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vid iti a hi sarvajña tvam sarva vid tvam vā saṃbhavati avakṣara śabdaiḥ diṣṭāt bhūtayoḥ parasya eva etat sarvajña tvam sarva vid tvam ca asya atra ucyate saṃbhavati yatkāraṇam akṣarāt saṃbhavati iha viśvam iti prakṛtam saṃbhavati yatkāraṇam akṣarāt saṃbhavati iha viśvam iti prakṛtam sarvajñam irdiśya yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vidyasya jñāa mayam tapaḥ tasmāt etat brahma āma rūpam aam ca jāyate iti sarvajña tvam sarva vid tvam ca dharmaḥ ucyate iti gamyate akṣarāt paratas paraḥ iti atra api ca prakṛtāt kaścid abhidhīyate katham etat avagamyate provāca tām tat tvattaḥ bahma vidyām iti prakṛtasya eva akṣarasya pratijñāta tvāt katham tarhi akṣarāt paratas paraḥ iti vyapadiśyate iti uttara sūtre tat vakṣyāmaḥ api ca atra dve vidye veditavye ukte parā ca eva aparā ca iti tatra aparām ṛgveda ādi lakṣaṇām vidyām uktvā bravīti atha parā yayā tat akṣaram adhigamyate ityādi tatra parasyāḥ vidyāyāḥ śrutam yadi parameśvarāt ayat adṛśya tva ādi guṇakam akṣaram parikalpyeta parā vidyā syāt para apara vibhāgaḥ hi ayam vidyayoḥ abhyudaya aiḥśreyasa phala tayā parikalpyate ca vidyā iḥśreyasa phalā keacid abhyupagamyate tisraḥ ca vidyāḥ pratijñāyera parasya paramātmanaḥ dve eva tu vidye veditavye kasmin bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati iti sarva ātmake brahmaṇi sarva ātmake brahmaṇi sarva ātmake brahmaṇi pradhāe bhogya vyatirikte vā bhoktari api ca sa brahma vidyām sarva vidyā pratiṣṭhām atharvāya jyeṣṭhaputrāya prāha iti brahma vidyām prādhāye upakramya para apara vibhāge parām vidyām akṣara adhigamaiḥ darśaya tasyāḥ brahma vidyā tvam darśayati sā ca brahma vidyā samākhyā tad adhigamyasya akṣarasya abrahmatve bādhitā syāt aparā ṛgveda ādi lakṣaṇā karma vidyā brahma vidyā upakrame upayasyate brahma vidyā praśaṃsāyai plavāḥ hi ete adṛḍhāḥ yajña rūpāḥ aṣṭādaśa uktam avaram yeṣu karma etat śreyaḥ mūḍhāḥ jarām mṛtyum te ca aparām vidyām tatas viraktasya para vidyā adhikāram darśayati parīkṣya sa gurum eva abhigacchet samidh pāṇiḥ śrotriyam brahmaiṣṭham iti yat tu uktam acetasām pṛthivī ādīām bhavitavyam iti tat ayuktam hi dṛṣṭāta dārṣṭātikayoḥ atyata sāmyea bhavitavyam iti api ca sthūlāḥ pṛthivī ādayaḥ api ca sthūlāḥ pṛthivī ādayaḥ dṛṣṭāta tveopāttāḥ iti a sthūlaḥ eva dārṣṭātikaḥ bhūtayoiḥ abhyupagamyate tasmāt adṛśya tva ādi guṇakaḥ parameśvaraḥ eva viśeṣaṇa bheda vyapadeśābhyām ca etarau itas ca parameśvaraḥ eva bhūtayoiḥ etarau śārīraḥ vā kasmāt viśeṣaṇa bheda vyapadeśābhyām viśiaṣṭi hi prakṛtam śārīrāt vilakṣaṇa tve divyaḥ hi amūrtaḥ puruṣaḥ sabāhya abhyataraḥ hi ajaḥ aprāṇaḥ hi amaāḥ śubhraḥ iti a hi etat divya tva ādi viśeṣaṇam avidyā pratyupasthāpita āma rūpa pariccheda abhimāiḥ kalpayataḥ śārīrasya upapadyate tasmāt sākṣāt aupaiṣadaḥ puruṣaḥ iha ucyate tathā pradhāāt api prakṛtam vyapadiśati akṣarāt paratas paraḥ iti akṣaram avyākṛtam āma rūpa bīja śakti rūpam bhūta sūkṣmam īśvara āśrayam tasya eva upādhi bhūtam sarvasmāt vikārāt paraḥ tasmāt paratas paraḥ iti vyapadiśa iha vivakṣitam darśayati kiṃcid svatatram tattvam abhyupagamya tasmāt bheda vyapadeśaḥ ucyate kim tarhi yadi śruti avirodhe avyākṛta ādi śabda vācyam bhūta sūkṣmam parikalpyeta kalpyatām tasmāt bheda vyapadeśāt parameśvaraḥ bhūta yoiḥ iti etat iha pratipādyate kutas ca parameśvaraḥ rūpa upayāsāt ca api ca akṣarāt paratas paraḥ iti etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ iti prāṇa prabhṛtīām pṛthivī paryatāām tattvāām sargam uktvā tasya eva sarva vikāra ātmakam rūpam paśyāmaḥ agiḥ mūrdhā cakṣuṣī cadra sūryau diśaḥ śrotre vāc vivṛtāḥ ca vedāḥ vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ hṛdayam viśvam asya padbhyām pṛthivī hi eṣa sarva bhūta atarātmā iti tat ca parameśvarasya eva ucitam sarva vikāra kāraṇa tvāt a śārīrasya ayam rūpa upayāsaḥ saṃbhavati sarva bhūta atarātma tva asaṃbhavāt tasmāt parameśvaraḥ eva etarau iti gamyate katham bhūta yoeḥ ayam rūpa upayāsaḥ iti gamyate prakaraṇāt eṣaḥ iti ca prakṛti ākarṣaṇāt hi prakṛtyā etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ eṣa sarva bhūta atarātmā iti vacaam eva bhavati yathā upādhyāyam prakṛtya etasmāt adhīṣva eṣa veda vedāṅga pāragaḥ iti vacaam upādhyāya viṣayam bhavati tadvat katham adṛśya tva ādi guṇakasya vigrahavat rūpam saṃbhavati sarva ātma tva vivakṣayā idam ucyate a tu vigrahavat tva vivakṣayā iti adoṣaḥ aham aham aham aham aham ahamaādaḥ ityādi vat aye puar rūpa upayāsaḥ etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ sarva idriyāṇi ca kham vāyuḥ jyotiḥ āpaḥ pṛthivī viśvasya dhāriṇī iti hi pūrvatra prāṇa ādi tattva jātam uttaratra api ca tasmāt agiḥ samidhaḥ yasya sūryaḥ iti evamādi atas ca sarvāḥ oṣadhayaḥ rasāḥ ca iti iha eva katham akasmāt rūpam upayasyet sarva ātma tvam api sṛṣṭim parisamāpya upadekṣyati puruṣaḥ eva idam viśvam karma ityādiā śruti smṛtyoḥ ca trailokya śarīrasya prajāpateḥ jama ādi upalabhāmahe hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartata agre bhūtasya jātaḥ patiḥ ekaḥ āsīt sa dādhāra pṛthivīm dyām uta imām kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema iti samavartata iti ajāyata iti arthaḥ tathā sa vai śarīrī prathamaḥ sa vai puruṣaḥ ucyate ādikartā sa bhūtāām brahma agre samavartata iti ca vikāra puruṣasya api sarva bhūta atara ātma tvam saṃbhavati sarva bhūtāām adhyātmam avasthāāt asmi pakṣe puruṣaḥ eva idam viśvam karma ityādi sarva rūpa upayāsaḥ parameśvara pratipatti hetuḥ iti vyākhyeyam vaiśvāaraḥ sādhāraṇa śabda viśeṣāt kaḥ a ātmā kim brahma iti ātmā am eva imam vaiśvāaram saṃprati adhyeṣi tam eva o brūhi iti ca upakramya ca vaiśvāaram prati eṣām mūrdha ādi bhāvam upadiśya āmāyate yaḥ tu etam evam prādeśa mātram abhivimāam ātmāam vaiśvāaram upāste sa sarveṣu lokeṣu sarveṣu bhūteṣu sarveṣu ātmasu atti tasya ha vai etasya ātmaaḥ vaiśvāarasya mūrdhā eva su tejāḥ cakṣuḥ viśva rūpaḥ vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ pṛthak vartmā ātmā saṃdehaḥ bahulaḥ vastiḥ eva rayiḥ pṛthivī eva pādau uraḥ eva vediḥ loma ai barhiḥ hṛdayam gārhapatyaḥ āsyam āhavaīyaḥ ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kim vaiśvāara śabdena jāṭhara ogī upadiśyate uta bhūtāgiḥ atha devatā athavā śārīraḥ āhosvit parameśvaraḥ iti kim saṃśaya kāraṇam vaiśvāaraḥ iti jāṭhara bhūtāgi devatāām sādhāraṇa śabda prayogāt ātmā iti ca śārīra parameśvarayoḥ tatra yāyyam kasya vā bhavati saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam jāṭhara ogiḥ iti kutas tatra hi viśeṣeṇa kvacid prayogaḥ dṛśyate ayam agiḥ vaiśvāaraḥ yaḥ yamataḥ puruṣe pacyate yat idam adyate ityādau agi mātram vā syāt prayoga darśaāt viśvasmai agim devāḥ vaiśvāaram ketu mahām akṛṇvaḥ ityādau agi śarīrā vā devatā syāt tasyām api prayoga darśaāt vaiśvāarasya sumatau syāma rājā hi kam iti evamādyāyāḥ śruteḥ devatāyām aiśvarya ādi upetāyām saṃbhavāt atha ātma śabda sāmādhikaraṇyāt upakrame ca kaḥ a ātmā kim brahma iti kevala ātma śabda prayogāt ātma śabda vaśe vaiśvāara śabdaḥ pariṇeyaḥ iti ucyate tathā api śārīraḥ ātmā syāt tasya vaiśvāara saṃikarṣāt prādeśa mātram iti ca viśeṣaṇasya saṃbhavāt tasmāeśvaraḥ vaiśvāaraḥ iti evam prāptam tatra idam ucyate vaiśvāaraḥ paramātmā bhavitum arhati kutas sādhāraṇa śabda viśeṣāt sādhāraṇa śabdayoḥ viśeṣaḥ sādhāraṇa śabda viśeṣaḥ yadi api etau ubhau api ātma vaiśvāara śabdau sādhāraṇa śabdau vaiśvāara śabdaḥ tu trayāṇām sādhāraṇaḥ ātma śabdaḥ ca dvayoḥ tathā api viśeṣaḥ dṛśyate parameśvara para tvam tayoḥ abhyupagamyate tasya ha vā etasya ātmaaḥ vaiśvāarasya mūrdhā eva su tejāḥ ityādiḥ atra hi parameśvaraḥ eva dyu mūrdha tva ādi viśiṣṭaḥ uvasthātara gataḥ gamyate kāraṇa tvāt kāraṇasya hi sarvābhiḥ kārya gatābhiḥ avasthābhiḥ avasthāvat tvāt dyu loka ādi avayava tvam upapadyate sa sarveṣu lokeṣu sarveṣu bhūteṣu sarveṣu ātmasu aam atti iti ca sarva loka ādi āśrayam phalam śrūyamāṇam parama kāraṇa parigrahe saṃbhavati eva ha asya sarve pāpmāaḥ pradūyate iti ca tad vidaḥ sarva pāpma pradāha śravaṇam kaḥ aḥ ātmā kim brahma iti ca ātma brahma śabdābhyām upakramaḥ iti brahma liṅgāi parameśvaram eva gamayati tasmāt parameśvaraḥ eva vaiśvāaraḥ smaryamāṇam aumāam syāt iti itas ca parameśvara eva vaiśvāaraḥ yasmāt parameśvarasya eva agirā āsyam dyauḥ mūrdhā iti īdṛśam trailokya ātmakam rūpam smaryate yasya agirā āsyam dyauḥ mūrdhā kham ābhiḥ caraṇau kṣitiḥ sūryaḥ cakṣuḥ diśaḥ śrotram tasmai loka ātmai amaḥ iti tat smaryamāṇam rūpam mūla bhūtām śrutim aumāpayat asya vaiśvāara śabdasya parameśvara paratve aumāam liṅgam gamakam syāt iti arthaḥ iti śabdaḥ hetvarthe yasmāt idam gamakam tasmāt api vaiśvāaraḥ paramātmā eva iti arthaḥ yadi api stutiḥ iyam tasmai amaḥ iti tathā api stuti tvam api āsati mūla bhūte veda vākye samyak rūpeṇa saṃbhavati dyām mūrdhāam yasya viprāḥ vadati kham vai ābhiṃ cadra sūryau diśaḥ śrotre viddhi pādau kṣitim ca saḥ uciti ātmā sarva bhūta praṇetā iti evaṃjātīyakā ca smṛtiḥ iha udāhartavyā śabda ādibhyaḥ utas pratiṣṭhāāt ca tathā dṛṣṭi upadeśāt asambhavāt puruṣam api atra āha a parameśvaraḥ vaiśvāaraḥ bhavitum arhati kutas śabda ādibhyaḥ utas pratiṣṭhāāt ca śabdaḥ tāvat vaiśvāara śabdaḥ a parameśvare saṃbhavati arthātare rūḍha tvāt tathā agi śabdaḥ saḥ eṣaḥ gir vaiśvāaraḥ iti ādi śabdāt hṛdayam gārhapatyaḥ tat yat bhaktam prathamam āgacchet tat homīyam ityādiā ca prāṇa āhuti adhikaraṇa tā saṃkīrtaam etebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ jāṭharaḥ vaiśvāaraḥ pratyetavyaḥ tathā atas pratiṣṭhāam api śrūyate puruṣa itas pratiṣṭhitam veda iti tat ca jāṭhare saṃbhavati yat api uktam mūrdhā eva su tejāḥ ityādeḥ viśeṣāt kāraṇāt paramātmā vaiśvāaraḥ iti atra brūmaḥ kutas yat ubhayathā api viśeṣa pratibhāe sati parameśvara viṣayaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ āśrayaṇīyaḥ jāṭhara viṣaya iti athavā bhaviṣyati tasya api hi bhaviṣyati tasya api hi matra varṇe avagamyate yaḥ pṛthivīm dyām uta imām ātatāa rodasī atarikṣam ityādau athavā tad śarīrāyāḥ devatāyāḥ aiśvarya yogāt dyu loka ādi avayava tvam bhaviṣyati tasmāt parameśvaraḥ vaiśvāaraḥ iti atra ucyate a tathā dṛṣṭi upadeśāt iti a śabda ādibhyaḥ kāraṇebhyaḥ parameśvarasya yuktam kutas tathā dṛṣṭi upadeśāt parameśvara dṛṣṭiḥ hi jāṭhare vaiśvāare iha upadiśyate mao brahma iti upāsīta ityādi vat athavā jāṭhara vaiśvāara upādhiḥ parameśvaraḥ iha draṣṭavya tvena upadiśyate mao mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ bhā rūpaḥ ityādi vat yadi ca iha parameśvaraḥ an anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anya vivakṣyeta kevalaḥ eva jāṭhara ogiḥ vivakṣyeta tatas mūrdhā eva su tejāḥ ityādeḥ viśeṣasya asaṃbhavaḥ eva syāt yathā tu devatā bhūta āgi vyapāśrayeṇa api ayam viśeṣaḥ upapādayitum śakyate tathā uttara sūtre vakṣyāmaḥ yadi ca kevalaḥ eva jāṭharaḥ vivakṣyeta puruṣa itas pratiṣṭhita tvam kevalam tasya syāt a tu puruṣa tvam puruṣam api vājasaeyiḥ saḥ eṣa ogiḥ vaiśvāaraḥ yat puruṣaḥ sa yaḥ ha etam evam agim vaiśvāaram puruṣam puruṣa itas pratiṣṭhitam veda iti parameśvarasya tu sarva ātma tvāt puruṣa tvam puruṣa itas pratiṣṭhita tvam ca ubhayam upapadyate ye tu puruṣavidham api iti sūtra avayavam paṭhati teṣām eṣaḥ ṛthaḥ kevala jāṭhara parigrahe puruṣa itas pratiṣṭhita tvam kevalam syāt a tu puruṣavidha tvam puruṣavidham api vājasaeyiḥ puruṣavidham puruṣa itas pratiṣṭhitam veda iti puruṣavidha tvam ca prakaraṇāt yat adhidaivatam dyumūrdha tva ādi yat ca adhyātmam prasiddham mūrdha tva ādi cubuka pratiṣṭhita tvātam tat parigṛhyate atas eva devatā bhūtam ca yat uktam bhūtāgeḥ api mūrdhā eva su tejāḥ iti ādi avayava kalpaam tasya eva bhaviṣyati iti tad śarīrāyāḥ devatāyāḥ vaiśvarya yogāt iti tat parihartavyam atas ūrcyate atas eva uktebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ devatā vaiśvāaraḥ tathā bhūtāgiḥ api api vaiśvāaraḥ hi bhūtāgeḥ auṣṇya prakāśa mātra ātmakasya dyu mūrdha tva ādi kalpaā upapadyate vikārasya vikāra atara ātma tva asaṃbhavāt tathā devatāyāḥ sati api aiśvarya yoge a dyu mūrdha tva ādi kalpaā smbhavati akāraṇa tvāt parameśvara adhī aiśvarya tvāt ca ātma śabda saṃbhavaḥ ca sarveṣu pakṣeṣu sthitaḥ eva sākṣāt api avirodham jaimiiḥ pūrvam jāṭhara āgi pratīkaḥ jāṭhara āgi upādhikaḥ vā parameśvaraḥ upāsyaḥ iti uktam atas pratiṣṭhita tvāt yaurodhea idāīm tu sākṣāt api parameśvara upāsa a parigrahe kaścid virodhaḥ iti jaimiiḥ ācāryaḥ ca atra ucyate atas pratiṣṭhita tva vacaam hi iha puruṣavidham puruṣa itas pratiṣṭhitam vede iti jāṭhara āgi abhiprāyeṇa idam ucyate tasya a prakṛta tvāt a saṃśabdita tvāt ca katham tarhi yat prakṛtam mūrdha ādi cubuka ateṣu puruṣa avayaveṣu puruṣavidha tvam kalpitam tad abhiprāyeṇa idam ucyate puruṣavidham puruṣa itas pratiṣṭhitam vede iti yathā vṛkṣe śākhām pratiṣṭhitām paśyati iti tadvat athavā yaḥ prakṛtaḥ paramātmā adhyātmam adhidaivatam ca puruṣavidha tva upādhiḥ tasya yat kevalam sākṣi rūpam tad abhiprāyeṇa idam ucyate puruṣavidham puruṣa itas pratiṣṭhitam veda iti ca paramātma parigrahe tad viṣayaḥ eva vaiśvāara śabdaḥ vartiṣyate viśvaḥ ca ayam araḥ ca iti viśveṣām vā ayam araḥ viśve vā arāḥ asya iti viśvāaraḥ paramātmā sarva ātma tvāt viśvāaraḥ eva vaiśvāaraḥ taddhita uaya arthaḥ rākṣasa vāyasa ādi vat paramātma viṣayaḥ eva bhaviṣyati gārhapatya ādi kalpam prāṇa āhuti adhikaraṇa tvam ca sarva ātma tvāt upapadyate katham puas parameśvara parigrahe prādeśa mātra śrutiḥ upapadyate iti tām vyākhyātum ārabhate abhivyakteḥ iti āśmarathyaḥ atimātrasya api parameśvarasya prādeśa mātra tvam abhivyakti nimittam syāt abhivyajyate kila prādeśa mātra parimāṇaḥ parameśvaraḥ upāsakāām kṛte pradeśa viśeṣeṣu vā hṛdaya ādiṣu upalabdhi sthāeṣu viśeṣeṇa abhivyajyate atas parameśvare pi prādeśa mātra śrutiḥ abhivyakteḥ upapadyate iti āśmarathyaḥ ācāryaḥ ausmṛteḥ bādariḥ prādeśa mātra hṛdaya pratiṣṭhitea vā ayam prādeśa mātraḥ iti ucyate yathā prastha mitāḥ yavāḥ prasthāḥ iti ucyate tadvat yadi api ca yaveṣu sva gatam eva parimāṇam prastha saṃbadhāt vyajyate ca iha parameśvara gatam kiṃcid parimāṇam asti yat hṛdaya saṃbadhāt vyajyeta tathā api prayuktāyāḥ prādeśa mātra śruteḥ saṃbhavati yathā kathaṃcid ausmaraṇam iti ucyate vā ayam a prādeśa mātraḥ prādeśa mātra śruti arthavat tāyai evam parameśvare prādeśa mātra śrutiḥ iti bādariḥ ācāryaḥ mayate ca eam asmi ātma ati ca eam parameśvaram asmi mūrdha cubuka atarāle jābālāḥ yaḥ eṣaḥ atas vyaktaḥ ātmā saḥ vimukte pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti saḥ vimuktaḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti varaṇāyām āsyām ca madhye pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti kā vai varaṇā kā ca āsi iti tatra ca imām eva āsikām sarvāṇīdriya kṛtāi pāpāi vārayati iti sā varaṇā sarvāṇīdriya kṛtāi pāpāi āśayati iti sā āsī iti api katamat ca asya sthāam bhavati iti bhruvoḥ ghrāṇasya ca yaḥ saṃdhiḥ saḥ eṣa dyu lokasya parasya ca saṃdhiḥ bhavati iti tasmāt upapaā parameśvare prādeśa mātra śrutiḥ abhivimāa śrutiḥ pratyagātma tva abhiprāyā pratyagātma tayā sarvaiḥ prāṇibhiḥ abhivimīyate iti abhivimāaḥ abhigataḥ vā ayam pratyagātma tvāt vimāaḥ ca mā aviyogāt iti abhivimāaḥ abhivimimīte vā sarvam jagat kāraṇa tvāt iti tasmāt parameśvaraḥ vaiśvāaraḥ iti siddham iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye prathama adhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ murat prathama udhyāyaḥ tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ sva śabdāt dyu bhū ādi adhikaraṇam idam śrūyate yasmin yauḥ pṛthivī cātarikṣam otam saha prāṇaiḥ ca sarvaiḥ tam eva ekam ātmā amayāḥ vācaḥ vimuñcatha amṛtasya eṣa setuḥ iti atra yat etat kiṃcid avagamyate tat kim param brahma syāt āhosvit arthātaram iti saṃdihyate tatra arthātaram kim api āyatam syāt iti prāptam kasmāt amṛtasya eṣa setuḥ iti śravaṇāt pāravāhi loke setuḥ prakhyātaḥ ca parasya brahmaṇaḥ pāravat tvam śakyam abhyupagatum iti śravaṇāt arthātare ca āyatae parigṛhyamāṇe smṛti prasiddham pradhāam parigrahītavyam tasya kāraṇa tvāt āyata a tva upapatteḥ śruti prasiddhaḥ vā vāyuḥ syāt vāyuḥ vāva gautama tat sūtram vai gautama sūtreṇa ayam ca lokaḥ paraḥ ca lokaḥ sarvāṇi ca bhūtāi saṃdṛbdhāi bhavati iti vāyoḥ api vidhāraṇa tva śravaṇāt śārīraḥ vā syāt tasya api bhoktṛ tvāt bhogyam prapañcam pratyāyata a tva upapatteḥ iti evam prāpte idam āha dyu bhū ādi āyatam iti dyauḥ ca bhūḥ ca dyu bhuvau dyu bhuvau ādī yasya tat idam dyu bhū ādi yat etat asmin vākye dyauḥ pṛthivī atarikṣam maaḥ prāṇāḥ iti evamātmakam jagat tasya āyatam param brahma bhavitum arhati kutas sva śabdāt ātma śabdāt iti arthaḥ ātma śabdaḥ hi iha bhavati tam eva ekam iti ātma śabdaḥ ca paramātma parigrahe samyak avakalpate ārthātara parigrahe kvacid ca śrūyate sa mūlāḥ somya imāḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ sat āyataāḥ sat pratiṣṭhāḥ iti sva śabdena eva ca iha purastāt upariṣṭāt ca brahma saṃkīrtyate puruṣaḥ eva idam viśvam karma tapaḥ brahma para amṛtam iti brahma eva idam amṛtam purastāt brahma paścāt brahma dakṣiṇatas ca uttareṇa iti ca tatra tu āyata āyata avat bhāva śravaṇāt sarvam brahma iti ca sāma ādhikaraṇyāt yathā hi a eka ātmakaḥ vṛkṣaḥ śākhā skadhaḥ mūlam ca iti evam āārasaḥ vicitraḥ ātmā iti āśaṅkā saṃbhavati tām sa avadhāraṇam āha tam eva ekam jāatha ātmāam iti etat uktam bhavati a kārya prapañca viśiṣṭaḥ vicitraḥ ātmā vijñeyaḥ kim tarhi avidyā kṛtam kārya prapañcam vidyayā pravilāpayataḥ tam eva ekam āyata abhūtam ātmāam jāatha ekarasam iti yathā yasmin āste devadattaḥ tadā ayaḥ iti ukte devadattam devadattam vijñeya tvam upadiśyate vikāra aṛta abhisaṃdhasya ca apavādaḥ śrūyate mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpoti yaḥ iha ā eva paśyati iti sarvam brahma iti tu sāmāādhikaraṇyam prapañca vilāpa artham a ekarasa tā pratipāda artham sa yathā kṛtsaḥ rasa ghaaḥ eva evam vai areyam ātmā a taras bāhyaḥ kṛtsaḥ prajñā aghaaḥ eva iti ekarasa tā śravaṇāt param brahma yat tu uktam setu śruteḥ setoḥ ca pāravat tva upapatteḥ brahmaṇā ūrtha atareṇa bhavitavyam iti atra ucyate vidhāraṇa tva mātram eva setu śrutyāḥ vivakṣyate a pāravat tva ādi hi mṛd dāru mayaḥ loke setuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti atra api mṛd dāru mayaḥ eva setuḥ abhyupagamyate setu śabda arthaḥ api vidhāraṇa tva mātram eva setu śabda vyutpatteḥ aparaḥ āha tam eva ekam iti yat etat saṃkīrtitam ātma jñāam yat ca etat ayā vācaḥ vimuñcatha iti tat atra amṛta tva sādhaa tvāt amṛtasya eṣa setuḥ iti setu śrutyā saṃkīrtyate tu tatra yat uktam setu śruteḥ brahmaṇā ṛtha atareṇa bhavitavyam iti etat ayuktam mukta upasṛpya vyapadeśāt itas ca param eva brahma dyubhva ādi āyatam dṛśyate muktaiḥ upasṛpyam mukta upasṛpyam deha ādiṣu aātmasu aham asmi iti ātma buddhiḥ avidyā tatas tad pūjā ādau rāgaḥ tad paribhava ādau ca dveṣaḥ tad uccheda darśaāt bhayam mohaḥ ca iti evam ayam aata bhedaḥ artha vrātaḥ saṃtataḥ sarveṣām pratyakṣaḥ tad viparyayeṇa avidyā rāga dveṣa ādi doṣa muktaiḥ upasṛpyam upagamyam etat iti prakṛtya vyapadeśaḥ bhavati katham bhidyate hṛdayagrathiḥ chidyate sarva saṃśayāḥ kṣīyate ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare iti uktvā bravīti tathā vidvāḥ āmarūpāt vimuktaḥ parātparam puruṣam upaiti divyam iti brahmaṇaḥ ca mukta upasṛpya tvam prasiddham śāstre yadā sarve pramucyate kāmāḥ hṛdi śritāḥ atha martyaḥ mṛtaḥ bhavati atra brahma iti evamādau tu prasiddham api ca tam eva ekam vācaḥ vimuñcatha amṛtasya eṣa setuḥ iti vāc vimoka pūrvakam vijñeya tvam iha dyu bhu ādi āyataasya ucyate tat ca śrutyatare brahmaṇaḥ dṛṣṭam tam eva dhīraḥ vijñāya prajñām kurvīta brāhmaṇaḥ hi tat iti tasmāt api dyu bhu ādi āyataam param brahma yathā brahmaṇaḥ pratipādakaḥ vaiśeṣikaḥ hetuḥ uktaḥ vaiśeṣikaḥ hetuḥ pratipādakaḥ asti iti āha sāṃkhya smṛti parikalpitam pradhāam iha pratipattavyam kasmāt a tad śabdāt tasya acetaasya pradhā asya pratipādakaḥ śabdaḥ tad śabdaḥ a tad śabdaḥ a tad śabdaḥ hi atra acetaasya pradhā asya pratipādakaḥ kaścid śabdaḥ usti yaḥ acetaam pradhā vā avagamyeta tad viparītasya cetaasya pratipādaka śabdaḥ utra asti yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vid ityādiḥ atas eva prāṇabhṛt ca yadi api prāṇabhṛtaḥ ātma tvam ca saṃbhavati tathā api sarvajña tva ādi asaṃbhave sati asmāt eva a tad śabdāt prāṇabhṛt api a dyu bhū ādi āyata a tve āśrayitavyaḥ a prāṇabhṛtaḥ dyu bhū ādi āyata a tvam api samyak saṃbhavati pṛthak yoga karaṇam uttara artham kutas ca a prāṇabhṛt dyu bhū ādi āyata a tve āśrayitavyaḥ bheda vyapadeśāt bheda vyapadeśaḥ ca iha bhavati tam eva ekam iti jñeya jñātṛ bhāvea tatra prāṇabhṛt tau a mumukṣu tvāt jñātā pariśeṣāt ātma śabda vācyam brahma jñeyam dyu bhu ādi āyataam iti gamyate a prāṇabhṛt kutas ca a prāṇabhṛt dyu bhu ādi āyata tveā āśrayitavyaḥ prakaraṇāt prakaraṇam ca idam paramātmanaḥ kasmin bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati iti sarva vijñā apekṣaṇāt paramātmani hi sarva ātmake vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam syāt a kevale prāṇabhṛti kutas ca a prāṇabhṛt dyu bhū ādi āyata a tve āśrayitavyaḥ sthiti adaābhyām ca dyu bhū ādi āyataam ca prakṛtya dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyau iti atra sthiti adae tayoḥ ayaḥ pippalam svādu atti iti iti tābhyām ca sthiti adaābhyām īśvara kṣetrajñau tatra gṛhyete yadi ca īśvaraḥ vivakṣitaḥ tatas tasya prakṛtasya īśvarasya kṣetrajñāt pṛthak vacaam avakalpate ayathā hi aprakṛta vacaam ākasmikam asaṃbaddham syāt tava api kṣetrajñasya īśvarāt pṛthak vacaam ākasmikam eva prasajyeta a tasya avivakṣita tvāt kṣetrajñaḥ hi bhoktṛ tve ca pratiśarīram buddhi ādi upādhi saṃbaddhaḥ lokatas eva prasiddhaḥ āsau śrutyā tātparyeṇa vivakṣyate īśvaraḥ tu lokataḥ prasiddha tvāt śrutyā tātparyeṇa vivakṣyate iti tasya ākasmikam yuktam guhām praviṣṭau ātma au hi iti atra api etat darśitam dvā suparṇāḥ iti asyām ṛci īśvara kṣetrajñau ucyete iti yadā api vyākhyāeā asyām ṛci sattva kṣetrajñau ucyete tadā api a virodhaḥ kaścid katham prāṇabhṛt hi iha ghaṭa ādi chidra vat pratiśarīram gṛhyamāṇaḥ bhavati iti pratiṣidhyate yaḥ tu sarva śarīreṣu upādhibhiḥ bhavati iti pratiṣidhyate yaḥ tu sarva śarīreṣu upādhibhiḥ paraḥ eva sa bhavati yathā ghaṭa ādi chidrāṇi ghaṭa ādibhiḥ upādhibhiḥ mahā ākāśaḥ eva bhavati tadvat prāṇabhṛtaḥ parasmāt aya tva aupapatteḥ pratiṣedhaḥ opapadyate tasmāt sattva ādi upādhi abhimāiaḥ eva dyu bhvā ādi āyataa tva pratiṣedhaḥ tasmāt param eva brahma dyu bhvā ādi āyataam tat etat adṛśya tva ādi guṇakaḥ dharma ukteḥ siddham tasya eva hi bhūtayoi vākyasya madhye idam paṭhitam yasmin yauḥ pṛthivī cātarikṣam iti prapañca artham tu bhūmā samprasādāt adhyupadeśāt bhūma adhikaraṇam idam samāmaati bhūmā tu eva vijijñāsitavyaḥ iti bhūmā aam bhagavaḥ vijijñāsa yatra āyat paśyati āyat śṛṇoti āyat sa bhūmā atha yatra ayat paśyati ayat śṛṇoti ayat tat alpam ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kim prāṇaḥ bhūmā syāt āhosvit paramātmā iti kutas saṃśayaḥ bhūmā iti tāvat bahutvam abhidhīyate bahoḥ lopaḥ ca bahoḥ iti bhūma śabdasya bhāva pratyaya ātatā smaraṇāt kimātmakam tat bahutvam iti viśeṣa ākāṅkṣāyām prāṇaḥ vai āśāyāḥ bhūyāḥ iti prāṇaḥ bhūmā iti pratibhāti tathā śrutam hi eva me bhagavat dṛśebhyaḥ tarati śokam ātma vid iti saḥ ham bhagavaḥ śocāmi tam mā bhagavān śokasya pāram tārayatu iti prakaraṇa utthāt paramātmā bhūmā iti api pratibhāti tatra yāyyam kasya vā bhavati saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam prāṇaḥ bhūmā iti kasmāt yathā hi asti bhagavaḥ āmaḥ bhūyaḥ iti vāc vāva āmaḥ bhūyasī iti tathā asti bhagavaḥ vācaḥ bhūyaḥ iti mao vāva vācaḥ bhūyaḥ iti ca āma ādibhyaḥ hi ā prāṇāt bhūyaḥ praśaprativacaa pravāhaḥ pravṛttaḥ prāṇāt param dṛśyate asti bhagavaḥ prāṇāt bhūyaḥ iti adaḥ vāva prāṇāt bhūyaḥ iti prāṇam eva tu āma ādibhyaḥ āśātebhyaḥ bhūyāṃsam prāṇaḥ vai āśāyāḥ bhūyāḥ sa prapañcam uktvā prāṇa darśiṇaḥ ca ativādi tvam ativādyasi iti ativādyasmi iti brūyāḥ apahuvīta iti eṣa tu vai ativadati yaḥ satyena ativadati iti prāṇa vratam ativādi tvam aukṛṣya a parityajya eva prāṇam satya ādi paraṃparayā bhūmai avatāraya prāṇam eva bhūmai mayataḥ iti gamyate katham puas prāṇe bhūmai vyākhyāyamāe yatra āyat paśyati iti etat bhūmaḥ lakṣaṇa param vyākhyāyeta iti ucyate suṣupta avasthāyām prāṇa grasteṣu karaṇeṣu darśa ādi vyavahāraiḥ vṛtti darśaāt saṃbhavati prāṇasya api yatra āyat paśyati iti etat lakṣaṇam tathā ca śrutiḥ a śrṛṇoti a paśyati ityādiā sarva karaṇa vyāpāra prati astamaya rūpām suṣupti avasthām uktvā prāṇa āgayaḥ eva etasmin pure jāgrati iti tasyām eva avasthāyām pañca vṛtteḥ prāṇasya jāgaraṇam bruvatī prāṇa pradhāām suṣupti avasthām darśayati yat ca etat bhūmaḥ sukha tvam śrutam yaḥ vai bhūmā tat sukham iti tat api aviruddham atra eṣa devaḥ paśyati atha yat etasmin śarīre sukham bhavati iti suṣupti avasthāyām eva sukha śravaṇāt yat ca yaḥ vai bhūmā tat amṛtam iti tat api prāṇasya aviruddham prāṇaḥ vai amṛtam iti śruteḥ katham puas prāṇam tarati śokam ātma vid iti ātma vividiṣayā prakaraṇasya utthāam upapadyate prāṇaḥ eva iha ātmā vivakṣitaḥ iti brūmaḥ tathā hi prāṇaḥ ha pitā prāṇaḥ mātā prāṇaḥ bhrātā prāṇaḥ svasā prāṇaḥ ācāryaḥ prāṇaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ iti prāṇam eva sarva ātmā am karoti yathā vai arāḥ ābhau samarpitā evam asmi prāṇe sarvam samarpitam iti ca ca saṃbhavati vaipulya ātmikā bhūma rūpa tā prāṇasya tasmāt prāṇaḥ bhūmā iti evam prāptam tatas idam ucyate paramātmā eva iha bhūmā bhavitum arhati a prāṇaḥ kasmāt saṃprasādāt adhyupadeśāt saṃprasādaḥ iti suṣuptam ucyate samyak prasīdati asmi iti bṛhadāraṇyake ca svapa jāgarita sthāābhyām saha pāṭhāt tasyām ca saṃprasāda avasthāyām prāṇaḥ jāgarti iti prāṇaḥ utra saṃprasādaḥ abhipreyate prāṇāt ūrdhvam bhūme upadiśyamāa tvāt iti arthaḥ prāṇaḥ eva ced bhūmā syāt saḥ eva tasmāt ūrdhvam upadiśyeta iti āśliṣṭam etat syāt a hi āmā eva āmaḥ bhūyas iti āmaḥ ūrdhvam upadiṣṭam kim tarhi āmoyat arthātaram upadiṣṭam vāc ākhyam vāc vāva āmaḥ bhūyasī iti tathā vāc ādibhyaḥ api ā prāṇāt arthātaram eva tatra tatra ūrdhvam upadiṣṭam tadvat prāṇāt ūrdhvam upadiśyamānaḥ bhūmā prāṇāt arthātarabhūtaḥ bhavitum arhati iha ā asti praśaḥ asti bhagavaḥ prāṇāt bhūyaḥ iti ā api prativacam asti prāṇāt vāva bhūyaḥ asti iti katham prāṇāt adhi bhūmā upadiśyate iti ucyate prāṇa viṣayam eva ca ativādi tvam uttaratra ākṛṣyamāṇam paśyāmaḥ eṣa tu vai ativadati yaḥ satyena ativadati iti tasmai āsti prāṇāt adhyupadeśaḥ iti atra ucyate a tāvat prāṇa viṣayasya eva ativādi tvasya etat aukarṣaṇam iti śakyam vaktum viśeṣa vādāt yaḥ satyeā ativadati iti viśeṣa vādaḥ api ayam prāṇa viṣayaḥ eva bhaviṣyati katham yathā eṣa ugihotrī yaḥ satyam vadati iti ukte tarhi agihotreṇa eva tat satya vadaam tu agihotriṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ ucyate tathā eṣa tu vai ativadati yaḥ satyena ativadati iti ukte tarhi ā iti brūmaḥ śruti artha parityāga prasaṅgāt śrutyā hi atra pratīyate yaḥ saḥ utivadati iti ā atra prāṇa vijñāasya asti prakaraṇāt tu prāṇa vijñāam saṃbadhyeta tatra śrutiḥ parityaktā syāt prakṛta vyāvṛtti arthaḥ ca tuśabdaḥ saṃgaccheta eṣa tu vai ativadati iti satyam tu eva vijijñāsitavyam iti ca prayatātara karaṇam artha atara vivakṣām sūcayati tasmāt yathā eka veda praśaṃsāyām prakṛtāyām eṣa tu mahābrāhmaṇaḥ yaḥ caturaḥ vedāḥ adhīte iti eka vedebhyaḥ ṛthātara bhūtaḥ catur vedaḥ praśasyate tādṛś etat draṣṭavyam ca bhavitavyam iti tvāt artha atara vivakṣāyāḥ tatra tatra śrutvā tūṣṇīṃbhūtam āradam svayam eva saat kumāraḥ vyutpādayati yat vikāra aṛta viṣayeṇa ativādi tvam aativādi tvam eva tat eṣa tu vai ativadati yaḥ satyeā ativadati iti tatra satyam iti param brahma ucyate paramārtha rūpa tvāt satyam brahma iti ca śruti atarāt tathā vyutpātitāya āradāya saḥ ham bhagavan iti evam pravṛttāya iti evam pravṛttāya vijñā ādi sādhaa paraṃparayā upadiśati tatra yat prāṇāt adhi satyam vaktavyam pratijñātam tat eva iha bhūmā iti ucyate iti gamyate tasmāt asti prāṇāt adhi bhūme upadeśaḥ iti atas prāṇa ādayaḥ paramātmā bhūmā bhavitum arhati iti evam ca iha ātma vividiṣayā bhaviṣyati prāṇaḥ eva iha ātmā vivakṣitaḥ iti etat api upapadyate hi prāṇasya mukhyayā vṛttyā ātma tvam asti a āyaḥ pathā iti tam mā bhagavān śokasya pāram tārayatu iti ca upakramya upasaṃharati tasmai mṛdita kaṣāyāya tamasaḥ pāram darśayati iti tamaḥ iti śoka ādi kāraṇam avidyā ucyeta ātmataḥ prāṇaḥ iti ca brāhmaṇam bhaviṣyati bhūmā atra prāṇaḥ eva iti ced sa bhagavaḥ iti sve mahimi ityādi bhūma eva ā prakaraṇa samāpteḥ aukarṣaṇāt vaipulya ātmikā ca bhūma rūpatā sarva kāraṇa tvāt paramātman sutarām upapadyate dharma upapatteḥ ca api ca ye śrūyate dharmāḥ te paramātmani upapadyate yatra āyat paśyati āyat śṛṇoti sa bhūmā iti darśa ādi vyavahāra abhāvam bhūmai avagamayati ca ayam darśa ādi vyavahāra abhāvaḥ yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kam paśyet iti ādi śruti atarāt yaḥ api asau suṣupti avasthāyām darśa ādi vyavahāra abhāvaḥ uktaḥ saḥ upi ātmaaḥ eva asaṅga tva vivakṣayā uktaḥ a prāṇa svabhāva vivakṣayā paramātma prakaraṇāt yat api tasyām avasthāyām sukham uktam tat api ātmaaḥ eva sukha rūpa tva vivakṣayā uktam yatas āha eṣaḥ usya paramaḥ āadaḥ mātrām upajīvati iti iha api yaḥ vai bhūmā tat sukham sukham asti bhūmā eva sukham iti brahma eva sukham darśayati yaḥ vai bhūmā tat amṛtam iti amṛta tvam api iha śrūyamāṇam parama kāraṇam gamayati vikārāṇām amṛta tvasya āpekṣika tvāt iti ca śruti atarāt tathā ca satya tvam sva mahima pratiṣṭhita tvam sarvagata tvam sarva ātma tvam iti ca ete dharmāḥ śrūyamāṇāḥ paramātmayā iva upapadyate tasmāt bhūmā paramātmā iti siddham akṣaram ambara atadhṛteḥ akṣara adhikaraṇam kasmin khalu ākāśaḥ otaḥ ca potaḥ ca iti sa ha uvāca etat vai tat akṣaram gārgi brāhmaṇāḥ abhivadati a sthūlam a aṇu ityādi śrūyate tatra saṃśayaḥ kim akṣara śabda varṇa ucyate kim vā parameśvaraḥ iti tatra akṣara samā māye ityādau akṣara śabdasya varṇe prasiddha tvāt prasiddhi atikramya ca ayukta tvāt oṃkāraḥ eva idam sarvam ityādau ca śruti atare varṇasya api upāsya tve sarva ātmaka tva avadhāraṇāt varṇa api ca ayukta tvāt eva akṣara śabdaḥ iti evam prāpte ucyate paraḥ eva ātmā akṣara śabda vācyaḥ kasmāt ambarāta dhṛteḥ pṛthivyādeḥ ākāśātasya vikāra jātasya dhāraṇāt tatra hi pṛthivyādeḥ samasta vikāra jātasya kāla traya vibhaktasya ākāśaḥ eva tadā ūtam ca protam ca iti ākāśe pratiṣṭhita tvam uktvā kasmiu khalu ākāśaḥ otaḥ ca protaḥ ca iti aea idam akṣaram avatāritam tathā ca upasaṃhṛtam etasmin khalu akṣare gārgi ākāśaḥ otaḥ ca protaḥ ca iti ca iyam ambara āta dhṛtiḥ brahmaṇaḥ yatra saṃbhavati yat api oṃkāraḥ eva idam sarvam iti tat api brahma pratipatti sādhaa tvāt stuti artham draṣṭavyam kṣarati ca iti iti atva vyāpi tvābhyām akṣaram param eva brahma syāt etat kāryasya ced kāraṇa adhī tvam abhyupagamyate pradhā a kāraṇa vādiḥ upi iyam upapadyate katham ambarāta dhṛteḥ brahmatva pratipattiḥ iti atas uttaram paṭhati sā ca praśāsaāt sā ca ambarāta dhṛtiḥ parameśvarasya eva karma kasmāt praśāsaāt praśāsaam hi iha śrūyate etasya vai akṣarasya praśāsae gārgi sūryācadramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ ityādi praśāsaam ca pārameśvaram karma a acetaasya praśāsaam bhavati a hi acetaāām ghaṭa ādi kāraṇāām mṛd ādīām ghaṭa ādi viṣayam praśāsaam asti aya bhāva vyāvṛtteḥ ca aya bhāva vyāvṛtteḥ ca kāraṇāt brahma eva akṣara śabda vācyam tasya eva ambarāta dhṛtiḥ karma āyasya kasyacid kim idam aya bhāva vyāvṛtteḥ iti ayasya bhāvaḥ ya bhāvaḥ tasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ aya bhāva vyāvṛttiḥ iti tasyāḥ etat uktam bhavati yat ayat brahmaṇā ukṣara śabda vācyam iha āśaṅkyate tad bhāvāt idam ambarāta vidhāraṇam akṣaram vyāvartayati śrutiḥ tat vai etat akṣaram gārgi a dṛṣṭam draṣṭṛ a śrutam śrotṛ a matam matṛ a vijñātam vijñātṛ iti tatra a dṛṣṭa tva ādi vyapadeśaḥ pradhā asya api saṃbhavati draṣṭṛ tva ādi vyapadeśaḥ tu a tasya saṃbhavati aceta a tvāt tathā draṣṭṛ āyadataḥ asti śrotṛ āyadataḥ asti matṛ iti ātma bheda pratiṣedhāt a śārīrasya api upādhi mata ukṣara śabda vācya tvam iti ca upādhimat tā pratiṣedhāt a hi śārīraḥ bhavati tasmāt param eva brahma akṣaram iti iścayaḥ īkṣati karma vyapadeśāt saḥ īkṣati karma adhikaraṇam etat vai satyakāma param ca aparam ca brahma yat oṃkāraḥ tasmāt vidvāḥ ava iti iti prakṛtya śrūyate yaḥ puar etam tri mātreṇa ūm iti param puruṣam abhidhyāyīta iti kim asmi vākye param brahma abhidhyātavyam upadiśyate āhosvit aparam iti param aparam vā ekataram aveti iti prakṛta tvāt saṃśayaḥ tatra aparam idam brahma iti prāptam kasmāt sa tejasi sūrye saṃpaaḥ saḥ sāmabhiḥ uīyate brahma lokam iti ca tad vidaḥ hi para brahma vid deśa paricchiam phalam aśuvīta iti yuktam sarva gata tvāt parasya brahmaṇaḥ param puruṣam iti viśeṣaṇam opapadyate ā eṣa doṣaḥ piṇḍa apekṣayā prāṇasya paratva upapatteḥ iti evam prāpte abhidhīyate param eva brahma iha abhidhyātavyam upadiśyate kasmāt īkṣati karma vyapadeśāt īkṣatiḥ darśaam darśa a vyāpyam īkṣati karma īkṣati karma tve ā asya abhidhyātavyasya puruṣasya vākyaśeṣe vyapadeśaḥ bhavati saḥ etasmāt jīva ghaāt parātparam puriśayam puruṣam īkṣate iti tatra abhidhyāyateḥ atathābhūtam api vastu karma bhavati maoratha kalpitasya api abhidhyāyati karma tvāt īkṣateḥ tu tathābhūtam eva vastu loke karma dṛṣṭam iti atas paramātmā eva ayam vyapadiṣṭaḥ iti gamyate saḥ eva ca iha para puruṣa śabdābhyām abhidhyātavyaḥ pratyabhijñāyate paraḥ puruṣaḥ uktaḥ īkṣaṇe tu parātparaḥ katham itaraḥ itaratra pratyabhijñāyate iti atra ucyate para puruṣa śabdau tāvat ubhayatra sādhāraṇau ca atra prakṛtaḥ abhidhyātavyaḥ paraḥ puruṣaḥ parāmṛśyate tasmāt parātparaḥ yam īkṣitavyaḥ puruṣaḥ yaḥ syāt kaḥ tarhi jīvaghaaḥ iti ucyate mūrtiḥ jīva lakṣaṇaḥ ghaaḥ jīvaghaaḥ saidhava khilya vat yaḥ paramātmā jīva rūpaḥ khilya bhāvaḥ upādhi kṛtaḥ paraḥ ca viṣaya idriyebhyaḥ saḥ utra jīvaghaaḥ iti aparaḥ āha sa sāmabhiḥ uīyate brahma lokam iti diṣṭaḥ yaḥ brahma lokaḥ paraḥ ca loka atarebhyaḥ saḥ utra iti ucyate jīvāām hi sarveṣām karaṇa parivṛtāām sarva karaṇa ātmai hiraṇyagarbhe saṃghāta upapatteḥ bhavati brahma lokaḥ jīva ghaaḥ tasmāt paraḥ yaḥ puruṣaḥ paramātmā īkṣaṇa karma bhūtaḥ saḥ karma bhūtaḥ iti gamyate param puruṣam iti ca viśeṣaṇam paramātma parigrahe eva avakalpate paraḥ hi puruṣaḥ paramātmā eva bhavati yasmāt param kiṃcid ayaḥ asti param kiṃcid sā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ iti ca śruti atarāt param ca aparam ca brahma yat oṃkāraḥ iti ca vibhajya param puruṣam abhidhyātavyam bruva param eva brahma param puruṣam gamayati yathā pāda udaraḥ tvacā evam ha vai sa pāpmaā iti paramātma iha abhidhyātavyam sūcayati atha yat uktam phalam yujyate iti atra ucyate paramātma abhidhyāyiḥ phalam brahma loka prāptiḥ krameṇa ca samyak darśa utpattiḥ iti krama mukti abhiprāyam etat bhaviṣyati iti adoṣaḥ daharaḥ uttarebhyaḥ dahara adhikaraṇam atha yat idam asmi brahma pure daharam puṇḍarīkam veśma daharaḥ usmi atara ākāśaḥ tasmi yat atas tat aveṣṭavyam tat vāva vijijñāsitavyam ityādi vākyam samāmāyate tatra yaḥ yam dahare hṛdaya puṇḍarīke daharaḥ ākāśaḥ śrutaḥ sa kim bhūtākāśaḥ atha vijñāātmā athavā paramātmā iti saṃśayyate kutas saṃśayaḥ ākāśa brahma pura śabdābhyām ākāśa śabdaḥ hi ayam bhūtākāśe parasmin ca brahmaṇi dṛśyate tatra kim bhūtākāśaḥ eva daharaḥ syāt kim vā paraḥ iti saṃśayaḥ tathā brahma puram iti kim brahma āmā tasya idam puram śarīram brahma puram athavā parasya eva brahmaṇaḥ puram brahma puram iti tatra jīvasya parasya daharākāśa tve saṃśayaḥ tatra ākāśa śabdasya bhūtākāśe rūḍha tvāt bhūtākāśaḥ eva dahara śabdaḥ iti prāptam tasya ca dahara āyata āpekṣayā dahara tvam yau āvai ayam ākāśaḥ tāvā eṣa utarhṛdaye ākāśaḥ iti ca bāhya abhyatara bhāva kṛta bhedasya upamā upameya bhāvaḥ dyāvāpṛthivī ādi ca samāhitam avakāśa ātma ākāśasya ekatvāt athavā jīvaḥ daharaḥ iti prāptam brahma pura śabdāt jīvasya hi idam puram sat śarīram brahma puram iti ucyate tasya sva karmaṇā upārjita tvāt bhaktyā ca tasya brahma śabda vācya tvam hi parasya brahmaṇaḥ śarīreṇa sva svāmi bhāvaḥ tatra dṛṣṭam yathā rājñaḥ jīvaḥ prāyeṇa hṛdaye pratiṣṭhitam iti atas jīvasya eva idam syāt dahara tvam api tasya eva ārā agra upamita tvāt avakalpate ākāśa upamita tva ādi ca brahma abheda vivakṣayā bhaviṣyati a ca atra daharasya ākāśasya āveṣṭavya tvam vijijñāsitavya tvam ca śrūyate iti atas uttaram brūmaḥ parameśvaraḥ eva atra daharākāśaḥ bhavitum arhati a bhūtākāśaḥ jīvaḥ vā kasmāt uttarebhyaḥ vākyaśeṣa gatebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ tathā hi aveṣṭavya tayā abhihitasya daharākāśasya tam ced brūyuḥ iti upakramya kim tat atra vidyate yat aveṣṭavyam yat vāva vijijñāsitavyam iti evam ākṣepa pūrvakam bhavati sa brūyāt yau vāva ayam ākāśaḥ tāvāeṣa utar hṛdaye ākāśe ubhe asmin yāvāpṛthivī atas eva samāhite ityādi tatra puṇḍarīka dahara tve prāpta dahara tvasya ākāśasya prasiddha ākāśa aupamye dahara tvam bhūtākāśa tvam daharasya ākāśasya iva ṛtayati iti gamyate yadi api ākāśa śabdaḥ bhūtākāśe rūḍhaḥ tathā api tea eva tasya upamā opapadyate iti bhūtākāśa śaṅkā bhavati bhavati bhede upamā upameya bhāvaḥ saṃbhavati iti uktam a evam saṃbhavati agatikā hi iyam gatiḥ api ca kalpayitvā bhedam upamā upameya bhāvam varṇayataḥ a bāhya ākāśa parimāṇa tvam upapadyeta parameśvarasya api jyāyāḥ ākāśāt iti śrutyatarāt ā eva ākāśa parimāṇa tvam upapadyate ā eṣa doṣaḥ puṇḍarīkaveṣṭa aprāpta dahara tva eva ṛtti paratvāt vākyasya a tāvattva pratipāda aparatvam ubhaya pratipādae hi vākyam bhidyeta a ca kalpita bhede puṇḍarīka veṣṭite ākāśa eka deśe samādhām upapadyate eṣaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā vijaraḥ vimṛtyuḥ viśokaḥ vijighatsaḥ pipāsaḥ satya kāmaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ iti ca ātma tva apahata pāpma tva ādayaḥ ca guṇāḥ bhūtākāśe saṃbhavati yadi api ātma śabdaḥ jīve saṃbhavati tathā api itarebhyaḥ kāraṇebhyaḥ jīva āśaṅkā api bhavati bhavati dahara tvam śakyam dahara tvam śakyam iti ced yad ātmatayā jīvasya sarvagata tva ādi vivakṣyeta tasya eva brahmaṇaḥ sākṣāt sarvagata tva ādi vivakṣyatām iti yuktam yat api uktam brahmapuram iti purasya upalakṣita tvāt rājñaḥ iva jīvasya eva idam pura eka deśa varti tvam astu iti atra brūmaḥ parasya eva idam brahmaṇaḥ puram sat śarīram brahmapuram iti ucyate brahma śabdasya tasmimukhya tvāt tasya api asti upalabdhi adhiṣṭhā tvāt saḥ etasmāt jīva ghaāt parātparam puriśayam puruṣam īkṣate saḥ vai ayam puruṣaḥ sarvāsu pūrṣu puriśayaḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ athavā jīvapure eva asmi brahma saṃihitam upalakṣyate yathā sālagrāme viṣṇuḥ saṃihitaḥ iti tadvat tat yathā iha karma citaḥ lokaḥ kṣīyate evam eva amutra puṇya citaḥ lokaḥ kṣīyate iti ca karmaṇā amata vat phalatvam uktvā atha yaḥ vrajati etān ca satya akāmān teṣām sarveṣu lokeṣu kāmacāraḥ bhavati iti prakṛta daharākāśa vijñāasya ata phalatvam vada paramātma tvam asya sūcayati yat api etat uktam daharasya ākāśasya āveṣṭavya tvam vijijñāsitavya tvam ca śrutam atra brūmaḥ yadi ākāśaḥ āveṣṭavya tve uktaḥ syāt ayam ākāśaḥ tāvā eṣa utar hṛdaye ākāśaḥ ityādi ākāśa svarūpa pradarśaḥ opapadyeta etat api atar varti vastu sadbhāva darśaāya eva pradarśyate tam ced brūyuḥ yat idam asmi brahmapure daharam puṇḍarīkam veśma daharaḥ smi atara ākāśaḥ kim tat atra vidyate yat aveṣṭavyam yat vāva vijijñāsitavyam iti ākṣipya parihāra avasare ākāśa aupamya upakrameṇa dyau ā pṛthivyā ādīām atas samāhita tva pradarśaāt evam evam hi sati yat atas samāhitam dyāvāpṛthivī ādi tat aveṣṭavyam vijijñāsitavyam ca uktam syāt tatra vākya śeṣaḥ o upapadyeta asmi kāmāḥ samāhitāḥ eṣaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā iti hi prakṛtam dyāvāpṛthivī ādi samādhā ādhāram ākāśam ākṛṣya atha yaḥ iha ātmā auvidya vrajati etān ca satyā kāmāḥ iti samuccaya arthe caśabde ātmā aum kāma ādhāram āśritān ca kāmāḥ vijñeyāḥ vākya śeṣaḥ darśayati tasmāt vākya upakrame daharaḥ eva ākāśaḥ hṛdaya puṇḍarīka adhiṣṭhāḥ saha atas sthaiḥ samāhitaiḥ pṛthivī ādibhiḥ satyaiḥ ca kāmaiḥ vijñeyaḥ uktaḥ iti gamyate sa ca uktebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ parameśvaraḥ iti sthitam gati śabdābhyām tathā hi dṛṣṭam liṅgam ca daharaḥ parameśvaraḥ uttarebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ iti uktam te eva uttare hetavaḥ idāīm prapañcyate itas ca parameśvaraḥ eva daharaḥ yasmāt dahara vākya śeṣe parameśvarasya eva pratipādakau gati śabdau bhavataḥ imāḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ ahar ahar gacchatyaḥ etam brahma lokam a vidati iti tatra prakṛtam daharam brahma loka śabdena abhidhāya tad viṣayā gatiḥ prajā śabda vācyāām jīvāām abhidhīyamānā daharasya brahma tām gamayati tathā hi aharahar jīvāām suṣupta avasthāyām brahma viṣayam dṛṣṭam śrutyatare satā somya tadā bhavati iti evamādau loke api kila gāḍham suṣuptam ācakṣate brahmībhūtaḥ brahma tām gataḥ iti tathā brahma loka śabdaḥ api prakṛte dahare prayujyamānaḥ jīva bhūta ākāśa āśaṅkām gamayati brahma loka śabdaḥ gamayet gamayet yadi brahmaṇaḥ loke iti ṣaṣṭhī samāsa vṛttyā vyutpādyeta brahmā eva lokaḥ brahma lokaḥ iti param eva brahma gamayiṣyati etat eva ca aharahar brahma loka gamanam dṛṣṭam brahma loka śabdasya sāmāādhikaraṇya vṛtti parigrahe liṅgam hi ahar ahar imāḥ prajāḥ kārya brahma lokam satyaloka ākhyam gacchati iti śakyam kalpayitum dhṛteḥ ca mahimā usya asmi upalabdheḥ dhṛteḥ ca hetoḥ parameśvaraḥ eva ayam daharaḥ katham iti hi prakṛtyāḥ ākāśa aupamya pūrvakam tasmin eva ca ātma śabdam prayujya apahatapāpma tva ādi guṇa yogam ca upadiśya tam eva a ativṛtta prakaraṇam atha yaḥ ātmā sa setuḥ vidhṛtiḥ eṣām iti tatra vidhṛtiḥ iti ātma śabda sāmādhikaraṇyāt vidhārayitā ucyate kticaḥ kartari smaraṇāt yathā udaka saṃtāasya vidhārayitā loke setuḥ kṣetra saṃpadām a saṃbhedāya evam ayam ātmā eṣām adhyātma ādi bheda bhiāām lokāām varṇa āśrama ādīām ca vidhārayitā setuḥ a saṃbhedāya a saṃkarāya iti evam iha prakṛte dahare vidharaṇa lakṣaṇam mahimāam darśayati ayam ca mahimā parameśvaraḥ eva śrutyatarāt upalabhyate etasya vai akṣarasya gārgi sūryācadramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ ityādeḥ tathā yatra api iścite parameśvara vākye śrūyate eṣa sarva īśvaraḥ eṣa bhūta adhipatiḥ eṣa bhūta pālaḥ eṣa setuḥ vidharaṇaḥ eṣām loka a āma saṃbhedāya iti evam dhṛteḥ ca hetoḥ parameśvaraḥ eva ayam daharaḥ prasiddheḥ ca itas ca parameśvaraḥ eva daharaḥ usmiatarākāśaḥ iti ucyate yatkāraṇam ākāśa śabdaḥ parameśvare prasiddhaḥ ākāśaḥ vai āmaḥ āma rūpayoḥ irvahitā sarvāṇi ha vai imāi bhūtāya ākāśāt eva samutpadyate iti ādi prayoga darśaāt jīve tu dṛśyate bhūtākāśaḥ tu satyām api ākāśa śabda prasiddhau grahītavyaḥ iti uktam itara parāmarśāt saḥ iti ca ā asambhavāt yadi daharaḥ iti parameśvaraḥ parigṛhyeta asti hi itarasya api jīvasya vākyaśeṣe parāmarśaḥ atha yaḥ eṣa saṃprasādaḥ usmāt śarīrāt samutthāya param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya sve a rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate eṣaḥ ātmā iti ha uvāca iti atra hi saṃprasāda śabdaḥ śrutyatare suṣupta avasthāyām dṛṣṭa tvāt avasthāvatam jīvam śakoti upasthāpayitum ārthātaram tathā śarīra vyapāśrayasya eva jīvasya śarīrāt samutthāam saṃbhavati yathā ākāśa vyapāśrayāṇām vāyu ādīām ākāśāt samutthāam tadvat yathā ca adṛṣṭaḥ api loke parameśvara viṣayaḥ ākāśa śabdaḥ parameśvara dharma samabhivyāhārāt ākāśaḥ vai āmaḥ āma rūpayoḥ irvahitā iti evamādau parameśvara viṣayaḥ abhyupagataḥ evam jīva viṣayaḥ api bhaviṣyati tasmāt itara parāmarśāt daharaḥ asmi atara ākāśaḥ iti atra saḥ eva jīvaḥ ucyate iti ced syāt kasmāt asaṃbhavāt hi jīvaḥ buddhi ādi upādhi pariccheda abhimāī saḥ ākāśe upamīyeta ca upādhi dharma abhimaya māasya apahata pāpma tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ saṃbhavati prapañcitam ca etat prathame sūtre atireka āśaṅkā parihārāya atra tu paṭhiṣyati ca upariṣṭāt parāmarśaḥ iti uttarāt ced āvirbhūta sva rūpaḥ tu itara parāmarśāt yā jīva āśaṅkā jātā sā asaṃbhavā irā kṛtā atha idāīm mṛtasya iva amṛta sekāt puas jīva āśaṅkāyāḥ kriyate uttarasmāt prājāpatyāt vākyāt tatra hi yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā iti apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇakam aveṣṭavyam vijijñāsitavyam ca pratijñāya yaḥ eṣaḥ akṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyata eṣaḥ ātmā iti akṣi stham draṣṭāram jīvam ātmā irdiśati etam tu eva te bhūyas auvyākhyāsyāmi iti ca tam eva puas puaḥ parāmṛśya yaḥ eṣa svape carati eṣaḥ ātmā iti tat yatra etat suptaḥ samastaḥ saṃprasaḥ svapam eṣaḥ ātmā iti ca jīvam eva avasthātara gatam vyācaṣṭe tasya eva ca apahata pāpma tva ādi darśayati etat amṛtam abhayam etat brahma iti āha khalu ayam evam saṃprati ātmā am ayam aham asmi iti o eva imāi bhūtāi iti ca suṣupta avasthāyām doṣam upalabhya etam tu eva te bhūyas iti ca upakramya eṣa saṃprasādaḥ asmāt śarīrāt samutthāya param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya sve rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate saḥ uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ iti jīvam eva śarīrāt samutthitam uttamam puruṣam darśayati tasmāt asti saṃbhavaḥ jīve pārameśvarāṇām dharmāṇām atas daharaḥ asmi iti jīvaḥ eva uktaḥ iti ced kaścid brūyāt tam prati brūyāt āvirbhūta svarūpaḥ tu iti tuśabdaḥ pūrvapakṣa vyāvṛtti arthaḥ ottarasmāt api vākyāt iha jīvasya āśaṅkā saṃbhavati iti arthaḥ kasmāt yatas tatra api āvirbhūta svarūpaḥ jīvaḥ vivakṣyate āvirbhūtam sva rūpam asya iti āvirbhūta svarūpaḥ bhūta pūrva gatyā etat uktam bhavati yaḥ eṣaḥ akṣiṇi iti akṣi lakṣitam draṣṭāram śarīra ātma tayā vyutthāpya etam tu eva te iti puas puas tam eva vyākhyeya tve ākṛṣya svapa suṣupta upayāsa krameṇa param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svea rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate iti yat asya pāramārthikam svarūpam param brahma tad rūpatayā eam jīvam vyācaṣṭe rūpeṇa yat tat param jyotiḥ upasaṃpattavyam śrutam tat param brahma tat ca apahata pāpma tva ādi dharmakam tat eva ca jīvasya pāramārthikam svarūpam tat tvam asi ityādi śāstrebhyaḥ etarat upādhi kalpitam yāvat eva hi sthāṇau iva puruṣa buddhim dvaita lakṣaṇām avidyām aham brahma asmi iti a pratipadyate tāvat jīvasya jīva tvam yadā tu deha idriya maaḥ buddhi saṃghātāt vyutthāpya śrutyā pratibodhyate āsi tvam deha idriya maaḥ buddhi saṃghātaḥ saṃsārī kim tarhi tat yat satyam saḥ ātmā caitaya mātra svarūpaḥ tat tvam asi iti tadā ātmā pratibudhya asmāt śarīra ādi abhimāāt samuttiṣṭha saḥ eva ātmā bhavati sa yaḥ ha vai tat paramam brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati ityādi śrutibhyaḥ tat eva ca asya pāramārthikam sva rūpam śarīrāt samutthāya svea rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate katham puas svam ca rūpam ca iṣpadyate iti saṃbhavati kūṭasthaityasya suvarṇa ādīām tu dravya atara saṃparkāt abhibhūta sva rūpāṇām a abhivyakta a sādhāraṇa viśeṣāṇām kṣāra prakṣepa ādibhiḥ sva rūpeṇa abhiiṣpattiḥ syāt tathā akṣatra ādīām ahai abhibhūta prakāśāām abhibhāvaka viyoge rātrau sva rūpeṇa abhiṣpattiḥ syāt a tu ityasya keacid abhibhavaḥ saṃbhavati a saṃsargi tvāt vyoma iva dṛṣṭa virodhāt ca dṛṣṭi śrutim ati vijñātayaḥ hi jīvasya sva rūpam tat ca śarīrāt a samutthitasya api jīvasya eva dṛśyate sarvaḥ hi jīvaḥ paśya śrṛṇva vyavaharati ayathā vyavahāra a upapatteḥ tat ced śarīrāt samutthitasya prāk dṛṣṭaḥ vyavahāraḥ virudhyeta atas kimātmakam idam śarīrāt kim ātmikā vā sva rūpeṇa abhiiṣpattiḥ iti atra ucyate prāk viveka vijñā utpatteḥ śarīra idriya maaḥ buddhi viṣaya veda upādhibhiḥ aviviktam iva jīvasya dṛṣṭi ādi jyotiḥ svarūpam bhavati yathā śuddhasya sphaṭikasya svācchyam śauklyam ca svarūpam prāk viveka grahaṇāt rakta īlā ādi upādhibhiḥ aviviktam iva bhavati pramāṇa jaita viveka grahaṇāt tu ca svea rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate iti ucyate prāk api tathā eva sa tathā deha ādi upādhya viviktasya eva sataḥ jīvasya śruti kṛtam viveka vijñāam śarīrāt samutthāam viveka vijñāa phalam sva rūpeṇa abhiiṣpattiḥ kevala ātma sva rūpa avagatiḥ tathā viveka aviveka mātreṇa eva ātmanaḥ aśarīra tvam sa śarīra tvam ca matra varṇāt aśarīram śarīreṣu iti api kauteya a karoti a lipyate iti ca sa śarīra tva aśarīra tva viśeṣa abhāva smaraṇāt tasmāt viveka vijñā abhāvāt sa āvirbhūta svarūpaḥ sa āvirbhūta svarūpaḥ iti ucyate a tu a yādṛśau āvirbhāva a āvirbhāvau svarūpasya saṃbhavataḥ sva rūpa tvāt eva evam mithyājñā a kṛtaḥ eva jīva parameśvarayoḥ bhedaḥ a vastu kṛtaḥ vyoma vat asaṅga tva aviśeṣāt kutas ca etat evam pratipattavyam yatas yaḥ eṣa u kṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate iti upadiśya etat amṛtam abhayam etat brahma iti upadiśati yaḥ kṣiṇi prasiddhaḥ draṣṭā vibhāvyate saḥ mṛta abhaya lakṣaṇāt brahmaṇaḥ yaḥ ced syāt tatas syāt praticchāyā ātmā ayam prajāpateḥ mṛṣāvādi tva prasaṅgāt tathā dvitīye pi paryāye yaḥ eṣa svape carati iti a prathama paryāya irdiṣṭāt akṣi puruṣāt draṣṭuḥ etam tu eva te bhūyas uvyākhyāsyāmi iti upakramāt kiṃca aham adya svape hastiam adrākṣam tam paśyāmi iti dṛṣṭam eva pratibuddhaḥ pratyācaṣṭe draṣṭāram tu tam eva yaḥ eva aham svapam adrākṣam saḥ eva aham jāgaritam paśyāmi iti tathā tṛtīye pi paryāye āha khalu ayam evam saṃprati ayam aham asmi iti eva imāi bhūtāi iti suṣupta avasthāyām viśeṣa vijñā abhāvam eva darśayati a vijñātāram pratiṣedhati yat tu tatra viāśam eva apītaḥ bhavati iti tat api viśeṣa vijñāa viāśa abhiprāyam eva a vijñātṛ viāśa abhiprāyam a hi vijñātuḥ vijñāteḥ viparilopaḥ vidyate viāśi tvāt iti tathā caturthe pi paryāye etam tu eva te bhūyas uvyākhyāsyāmi o iti upakramya maghava martyam vai idam śarīram saṃprasāda śabda uditam jīvam rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate iti darśaya parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ mṛta abhaya svarūpāt ayam jīvam darśayati kecid tu paramātma vivakṣāyām etam tu eva te iti jīva ākarṣaṇam etam eva vākya upakrama sūcitam apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇakam ātmā te bhūyas uvyākhyāsyāmi iti kalpayati teṣām etam iti saṃihita avalambiī viprakṛṣyeta bhūyas śrutiḥ ca uparudhyeta paryāya atara abhihitasya etam tu eva te iti ca pratijñāya prāk caturthāt paryāyāt ayam ayam vyācakṣāṇasya prajāpateḥ pratāraka tvam prasajyeta tasmāt yat avidyā pratyupasthāpitam apāramārthikam jaivam rūpam kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva rāga dveṣa ādi doṣa kaluṣitam tad viparītam apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇakam pārameśvaram svarūpam vidyayā pratipadyate rajju ādī apare tu pāramārthikam eva jaivam rūpam iti smadīyāḥ ca kecid teṣām sarveṣām ātma ekatva samyagdarśa a pratipakṣa bhūtāām pratiṣedhāya idam śārīrakam ārabdham ekaḥ eva parameśvaraḥ kūṭasthaityaḥ vijñāadhātuḥ avidyayā māyayā māyāvi vat a ekadhā vibhāvyate āyaḥ vijñāadhātuḥ asti iti yat tu idam parameśvara vākye jīvam āśaṅkya pratiṣedhati sūtra kāraḥ āsaṃbhavāt tatra ayam abhiprāyaḥ iti aśuddha buddha mukta svabhāve kūṭasthaitye ekasmin asaṅge tad viparītam jaivam rūpam vyomi iva tala mala ādi parikalpitam tat ātma ekatva pratipāda aparaiḥ vākyaiḥ yāya upetaiḥ dvaita vāda pratiṣedhaiḥ ca apaeṣyāmi iti jīvāt aya tvam draḍhayati jīvasya tu a parasmāt aya tvam pratipipādayiṣati kim tu eva avidyā kalpitam loka prasiddham jīva bhedam evam hi pravṛttāḥ karma vidhayaḥ a virudhyate iti mayate pratipādyam tu śāstra artham ātma ekatvam eva darśayati śāstra dṛṣṭyā tu upadeśaḥ vāmadeva vat ityādiā varṇitaḥ ca asmābhiḥ karma vidhi virodha parihāraḥ parāmarśaḥ atha yaḥ yam dahara vākyaśeṣe jīva parāmarśaḥ darśitaḥ atha yaḥ eṣa saṃprasādaḥ ityādiḥ sa dahare parameśvare a jīva upāsa upadeśaḥ prakṛta viśeṣa upadeśaḥ iti aarthaka tvam āha jīva parāmarśaḥ jīva svarūpa paryavasāyī kim tarhi parameśvara svarūpa paryavasāyī katham saṃprasāda śabda uditaḥ jīvaḥ jāgarita vyavahāre deha idriya pañjara adhyakṣaḥ bhūtvā tad ca śaraṇam prepsuḥ ubhaya rūpāt api śarīra abhimāāt samutthāya suṣupta avasthāyām param jyotiḥ ākāśa śabditam param brahma upasaṃpadya viśeṣa vijñāavat tvam ca parityajya svea rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate yat asya upasaṃpattavyam param jyotiḥ svea rūpeṇa ayam abhiiṣpadyate sa eṣaḥ ātmā apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇaḥ upāsyaḥ iti evamarthaḥ yam jīva parāmarśaḥ parameśvara vādiḥ api upapadyate alpa śruteḥ iti ced tat uktam yat api uktam daharaḥ asmi iti ākāśasya alpatvam śrūyamāṇam parameśvare ā upapadyate jīvasya tu ārā agra upamitasya alpatvam avakalpate iti tasya parihāraḥ vaktavyaḥ uktaḥ hi asya parihāraḥ parameśvare api āpekṣikam alpatvam avakalpate iti arbhaka okaḥ tvāt tad vyapadeśāt ca e ti ce a icāyya tvāt evam vyoma vat ca iti atra saḥ eva iha parihāraḥ ausaṃdhātavyaḥ iti sūcayati śrutyā eva ca idam alpatvam pratyuktam prasiddhe ākāśe upami māayā ayam ayam ākāśaḥ tāvā eṣa utar hṛdaye ākāśaḥ iti aukṛteḥ tasya ca aukṛti adhikaraṇam a tatra sūryaḥ bhāti a vidyutaḥ bhāti kutas yam agiḥ tam eva sarvam tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti iti samāmaati tatra yam sarvam yasya ca bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti sa kim tejaḥ dhātuḥ kaścid uta prājñaḥ ātmā iti vicikitsāyām tejaḥ dhātuḥ iti tāvat prāptam kutas tejaḥ dhātūām eva sūrya ādīām bhā a pratiṣedhāt tejaḥ svabhāvakam hi cadra tārakā ādi tejaḥ svabhāvake eva sūrye bhāsate iti prasiddham tathā saha sūryeṇa sarvam idam bhāsate saḥ upi tejaḥ svabhāvaḥ eva kaścid iti avagamyate tejaḥ svabhāvakaḥ eva upapadyate iti vat tasmāt tejaḥ dhātuḥ kaścid iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ prājñaḥ eva ayam ātmā bhavitum arhati kasmāt aukṛteḥ aukaraṇam aukṛtiḥ yat etat tam eva bhātam aubhāti sarvam iti aubhāam tat prājña parigrahā iva kalpate bhā rūpaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ iti hi tu tejaḥ dhātum kaṃcid sūrya ādayaḥ iti prasiddham sama tvāt ca tejaḥ dhātūām sūrya ādīām a tejaḥ dhātum ayam pratyapekṣā asti yam hi pradīpaḥ hi pradīpaḥ yat api uktam yat api uktam dṛśyate iti iyamaḥ tasya ca iti caturtham pādam asya ślokasya sūcayati tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti iti ca tad hetukam sūrya ādeḥ ucyamāam prājñam ātmāam gamayati tat devāḥ jyotiṣām jyotiḥ āyuḥ ha upāsata imṛtam iti hi tejaḥ tareṇa tu sūrya ādi tejaḥ vibhāti iti aprasiddham viruddham ca tejaḥ tareṇa tejaḥ tarasya pratighātāt athavā a sūrya ādīām eva śloka paripaṭhitāām idam tad hetukam vibhāam ucyate kim tarhi sarvam idam iti aviśeṣa śruteḥ sarvasya eva asya āma rūpa kriyā kāraka phala jātasya yā abhivyaktiḥ sā brahma jyotiḥ sattā aimittā yathā sūrya jyotiḥ sattā aimittā sarvasya rūpa jātasya abhivyaktiḥ tadvat a tatra sūryaḥ bhāti iti ca tatraśabdam āhara prakṛta grahaṇam darśayati prakṛtam ca brahma yasmin yauḥ pṛthivī cātarikṣam otam ca hiraṇmaye pare kośe virajam brahma iṣkalam tat śubhram jyotiṣām jyotiḥ tat yat ātma vidaḥ viduḥ iti katham tat jyotiṣām jyotiḥ iti atas idam utthitam tatra sūryaḥ bhāti iti yat api uktam sūrya ādīām tejasām bhā a pratiṣedhaḥ tejaḥ dhātau sūryaḥ iva itareṣām iti tatra tu saḥ eva tejaḥ dhātuḥ ayaḥ asti saṃbhavati iti upapāditam brahmaṇi api ca eṣām bhā a pratiṣedhaḥ uvakalpate yatas yat upalabhyate tat sarvam brahmaṇā eva jyotiṣā upalabhyate brahma tu jyotiṣā upalabhyate svayam jyotiḥ svarūpa tvāt sūrya ādayaḥ tasmin bhāyuḥ brahma hi brahma hi brahma hi tu vyajyate ātmā eva ayam jyotiṣā āste a gṛhyaḥ a hi gṛhyate ityādi śrutibhyaḥ api ca smaryate api ca īdṛś rūpa tvam
