prājñasya eva ātmaaḥ smaryate bhagavadgītāsu a tat bhāsayate sūryaḥ a śaśāṅkaḥ a pāvakaḥ yat gatvā a iva ṛtate tat dhāma paramam mama iti yat āditya gatam tejaḥ jagat bhāsayate akhilam yat ca ramasi yat ca āgau tat tejaḥ viddhi māmakam iti ca śabdāt eva pramitaḥ pramita adhikaraṇam aṅguṣṭha mātraḥ puruṣaḥ madhye tiṣṭhati iti śrūyate tathā aṅguṣṭha mātraḥ puruṣaḥ jyotiḥ iva adhūmakaḥ bhūta bhavyasya sa eva adya saḥ u śvas etat vai tat iti ca tatra yaḥ yam aṅguṣṭha mātraḥ puruṣaḥ śrūyate sa kim vijñāātmā kim vā paramātmā iti saṃśayaḥ tatra parimāṇa upadeśāt vijñāātmā iti tāvat prāptam bhavyasya iti a hi ayaḥ parameśvarāt bhūta bhavyasya iḥ aṅkuśam īśitā etat vai tat iti ca prakṛtam pṛṣṭam iha ausaṃdadhāti etat vai tat yat pṛṣṭam brahma iti arthaḥ pṛṣṭam ca iha brahma ayatra dharmāt paramātmaaḥ parimāṇa upadeśaḥ iti atra brūmaḥ hṛdi apekṣayā tu mauṣya adhikāra tvāt sarvagatasya api paramātmanaḥ hṛdaya ivasthā am apekṣya aṅguṣṭha mātra tvam idam ucyate ākāśasya iva vaṃśa parva apekṣam arati mātra tvam hi añjasā atimātrasya paramātmanaḥ oṅguṣṭha mātra tvam upapadyate a ca ayaḥ paramātmanaḥ iha grahaṇam arhati īśā a śabda ādibhyaḥ iti uktam prati prāṇi bhedam hṛdayāām a avasthita tvāt tad apekṣam api aṅguṣṭha mātra tvam upapadyate iti atas uttaram ucyate mauṣya adhikāra tvāt iti śāstram hi aviśeṣa pravṛttam api mauṣyāḥ eva adhikaroti śakta tvāt arthi tvāt a paryudasta tvāt upaaya ādi śāstrāt ca iti varṇitam etat adhikāra lakṣaṇe mauṣyāṇām ca iyata parimāṇaḥ kāyaḥ iyata parimāṇam eva ca eṣām aṅguṣṭha mātram hṛdayam atas mauṣya adhikāra tvāt śāstrasya mauṣya hṛdaya avasthā āpekṣam aṅguṣṭha mātra tvam upapaam yat api uktam parimāṇa upadeśāt smṛteḥ ca saṃsārī eva ayam aṅguṣṭha mātraḥ pratyetavyaḥ iti tat pratyucyate saḥ ātmā tattvam asi ityādi vat saṃsāriṇaḥ eva sataḥ uṅguṣṭha mātrasya brahma tvam idam upadiśyate iti dvi rūpā hi pravṛttiḥ kvacid paramātma svarūpaiḥ ūpaṇa parā kvacid paramātma ekatva upadeśa parā tat atra paramātma aikatvam upadiśyate āṅguṣṭha mātra tvam kasyacid etam eva artham pareṇa sphuṭīkariṣyati aṅguṣṭha mātraḥ puruṣotarātmā sadā hṛdaye saṃiviṣṭaḥ tam svāt śarīrāt pravṛhe muñja ādi veṣīkām dhairyeṇa tam vidyāt śukram amṛtam iti tad upari api bādarāyaṇaḥ saṃbhavāt devatā adhikaraṇam aṅguṣṭha mātra śrutiḥ mauṣya hṛdaya apekṣā mauṣya adhikāra tvāt śāstrasya iti uktam ucyate bāḍham mauṣyāḥ adhikaroti śāstram a tu mauṣyāḥ eva iti iha teṣām mauṣyāṇām upariṣṭāt ye deva ādayaḥ tāḥ api adhikaroti śāstram iti bādarāyaṇaḥ ācāryaḥ kasmāt saṃbhavāt saṃbhavati hi teṣām api arthi tva ādi adhikāra kāraṇam tatra arthi tvam deva ādīām api saṃbhavati tathā sāmarthyam api teṣām saṃbhavati matra arthavāda itihāsa purāṇa lokebhyaḥ vigrahavat tva ādi avagamāt ca teṣām kaścid pratiṣedhaḥ asti ca upaaya a śāstreṇa eṣām adhikāraḥ upaaya asya veda adhyaya artha tvāt teṣām ca svayam pratibhāta veda tvāt api ca eṣām vidyā grahaṇa artham brahmacarya ādi darśayati ekaśatam ha vai varṣāṇi maghavā prajāpatau brahmacaryam uvāsa bhṛguḥ vai vāruṇiḥ varuṇam pitaram upasasāra adhīhi bhagavaḥ brahma ityādi yat api karmasu a adhikāra kāraṇam uktam a devānām devatātara abhāvāt iti a ṛṣīṇām iti tad vidyāsu asti a hi idra ādīām virudhyeta virodhaḥ karmaṇi iti syāt etat yadi vigrahavat tva ādi abhyupagame deva ādīām vidyāsu adhikāraḥ varṇyeta vigrahavat tvāt ṛtvij ādi vadidra ādīām api svarūpa saṃidhāea karma aṅga bhāvaḥ abhyupagamyeta tadā ca virodhaḥ karmaṇi syāt yāga aṅga bhāvaḥ dṛśyate ca saṃbhavati bahuṣu yāgeṣu yugapad ekasya idrasya sva rūpa saṃidhā upapatteḥ iti ced āyam asti virodhaḥ kasmāt a eka pratipatteḥ ekasya api yugapad a eka svarūpa pratipattiḥ saṃbhavati katham etat avagamyate darśaāt tathā hi kati devāḥ iti upakramya trayaḥ ca trī ca śatā trayaḥ ca trī ca sahasrā iti katame te iti asyām virodhaḥ śabde parihṛtaḥ yāvatā vasavaḥ rudrāḥ ādityāḥ viśvedevāḥ marutaḥ iti ete rthāḥ aityāḥ eva utpattimat tvāt tat aitya tve ca tad vāciām vaidikāām vasu ādi śabdāām aitya tvam prasiddham hi loke eva utpadyate ākṛtayaḥ ākṛtibhiḥ ca śabdāām saṃbadhaḥ a vyaktibhiḥ vyaktīām āatyāt saṃbadha grahaṇa a upapatteḥ vyaktiṣu utpadyamāāsu api gavādi śabdeṣu kaścid virodhaḥ dṛśyate tathā deva ādi vyakti prabhava abhyupagame pi ākṛti itya tvāt kaścid vasu ādi śabdeṣu virodhaḥ iti draṣṭavyam ākṛti viśeṣaḥ tu matra arthavāda ādibhyaḥ vigrahavat tva ādi avagamāt avagatavyaḥ vā idra ādi śabdāḥ tatas ca śabde śabda vyavahāra yogya artha vyakti iṣpattiḥ atas prabhavaḥ iti ucyate katham avagamyate śabdāt prabhavati jagat iti pratyakṣa aumāābhyām pratyakṣam hi śrutiḥ prāmāṇyam prati aapekṣa tvāt smṛtiḥ prāmāṇyam prati sāpekṣa tvāt te hi śabda pūrvām sṛṣṭim darśayataḥ ete iti vai prajāpatiḥ devāḥ asṛjata asṛgram iti mauṣyāḥ idavaḥ iti pitṛm stiraḥ pavitram iti grahāḥ āśavaḥ iti stotram viśvāḥ iti mayī divyā yatas sarvāḥ pravṛttayaḥ iti utsarga upi ayam vācaḥ saṃpradāya pravarta ātmakaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ a yādṛśasya utsargasya asaṃbhavāt tathā āma rūpam ca bhūtāām karmaṇām ca veda śabdebhyaḥ eva ādau sarveṣām aḥ pratyakṣam etat tathā prajāpateḥ api sraṣṭuḥ sṛṣṭeḥ pūrvam vaidikāḥ śabdāḥ maasi prādurbabhūvuḥ paścāt tad augatāḥ sasarja iti gamyate tathā ca śrutiḥ sa bhūḥ iti vyāharat sa bhūmim asṛjata iti evamādikā bhūḥ ādi śabdebhyaḥ eva maasi prādurbhūtebhyaḥ bhūḥ ādi lokā sṛṣṭā darśayati kimātmakam śabdam abhipretya idam śabda prabhava tvam ucyate sphoṭam iti āha varṇa pakṣe hi śabdebhyaḥ deva ādi vyaktīām prabhavaḥ iti aupapam syāt varṇāḥ pratyuccāraṇam ayathā ca ayathā ca pratīyamāa tvāt tathā hi devadattaḥ yat adhīte yajñadattaḥ yat adhīte iti ca ayam varṇa viṣayaḥ yathātva pratyayaḥ bādhaka pratyaya abhāvāt ca varṇebhyaḥ ṛtha avagatiḥ yuktāḥ hi ekaikaḥ varṇa ṛtham pratyāyayet vyabhicārāt ca varṇa samudāya pratyayaḥ asti krama varti tvāt varṇānām varṇa ūrtham pratyāyayiṣyati iti yadi ucyeta hi śabdaḥ svayam pratīyamānaḥ artham pratyāyayet dhūma ādi vat ca pūrva pūrva varṇa aubhava jaita saṃskāra sahitasya ati avarṇasya pratītiḥ asti apratyakṣa tvāt saṃskārāṇām kārya pratyāyitaiḥ saṃskāraiḥ varṇa ūrtham pratyāyayiṣyati iti ced a saṃskāra kāryasya api smaraṇasya krama varti tvāt tasmāt sphoṭaḥ eva śabdaḥ sa ca ekaika varṇa pratyaya āhita saṃskāra bīja itya varṇa pratyaya jaita paripāke pratyayi yeka pratyaya viṣaya tayā jhaṭiti pratyavabhāsate ca ayam eka pratyayaḥ varṇa viṣayā smṛtiḥ tasya ca pratyuccāraṇam bheda pratyayasya varṇa viṣaya tvāt tasmāityāt śabdāt sphoṭa rūpāt abhidhāyakāt kriyā kāraka phala lakṣaṇam jagat abhidheya bhūtam prabhavati iti varṇāḥ eva tu śabdaḥ iti bhagavān upavarṣaḥ te eva iti pratyabhijñāāt sādṛśyāt pratyabhijñāam keśa ādiṣu iva iti ced a pratyabhijñāasya pramāṇa atareṇa bādhā upapatteḥ pratyabhijñāam ākṛti nimittam iti ced a vyakti pratyabhijñāāt yadi hi pratyuccāraṇam gavā ādi vyakti vat ayā ayā varṇa vyaktayaḥ pratīyera tatas ākṛti nimittam syāt tu etat asti varṇa vyaktayaḥ eva hi pratyuccāraṇam pratyabhijñāyate dvis go śabdaḥ uccāritaḥ iti hi pratipattiḥ tu dvau go śabdau iti pratīyate devadatta yajñadattayoḥ eva bheda pratīteḥ iti uktam atra abhidhīyate sati varṇa viṣaye pratyabhijñāe saṃyoga vibhāga abhivyaṅgya tvāt varṇāām abhivyañjaka vaicitrya aimittaḥ yam varṇa viṣayaḥ vicitraḥ pratyayaḥ svarūpa aimittaḥ api ca varṇa vyakti bheda vādi api pratyabhijñā asiddhaye varṇa ākṛtayaḥ kalpayitavyāḥ tāsu ca para upādhikaḥ bheda pratyayaḥ iti abhyupagatavyam tat varam varṇa vyaktiṣu eva para upādhikaḥ bheda pratyayaḥ svarūpa aimittam ca pratyabhijñām iti kalpa ālāghavam eṣaḥ eva ca varṇa viṣayasya bheda pratyayasya bādhakaḥ pratyayaḥ yat pratyabhijñām katham hi ekasmin kāle uccārayatām ekaḥ eva sa gakāraḥ yugapad a eka rūpaḥ syāt udāttaḥ ca audāttaḥ ca svaritaḥ ca sāuāsikaḥ ca ca iti atha vā dhvai kṛtaḥ yam bheda pratyayaḥ varṇa kṛtaḥ iti adoṣaḥ kaḥ ayam yaḥ dūrāt udātta ādi pratyayā bhaviṣyati itarathā hi varṇāām pratyabhijñāyamāāām i r bheda tvāt saṃyoga vibhāga kṛtāḥ udātta ādi viśeṣāḥ kalpyera saṃyoga vibhāgāām ca apratyakṣa tvāt tad āśrayāḥ viśeṣāḥ varṇeṣu adhyavasātum śakyate iti atas eva ete udātta ādi pratyayāḥ syuḥ api ca varṇāām pratyabhijñāyamānāām bhedaḥ bhavet iti a hi ayasya bhede a bhidyamānasya bhedaḥ bhavitum arhati a hi vyakti bhede jātim varṇebhyaḥ ca artha pratīteḥ saṃbhavāt kalpayāmi aham sphoṭam pratyakṣam eva tu avagacchāmi ekaika varṇa grahaṇa āhita saṃskārāyāḥ buddhau jhaṭiti pratyavabhāsaāt iti ced a asyāḥ api buddheḥ varṇa viṣaya tvāt ekaika varṇa grahaṇa uttara kālā hi iyam ekā buddhiḥ gauḥ iti samasta varṇa viṣayā ārthātara viṣayā katham etat avagamyate yatas syām api buddhau gakāra ādayaḥ varṇāḥ a tu dakāra ādayaḥ yadi hi asyāḥ buddheḥ gakāra ādibhyaḥ sphoṭaḥ viṣayaḥ syāt tatas dakāra ādayaḥ iva gakāra ādayaḥ pi asyāḥ buddheḥ vyāvartera tu tathā asti tasmāt iyam eka buddhiḥ varṇa viṣayā eva smṛtiḥ a eka tvāt varṇāām aika buddhi viṣaya tā upapadyate iti uktam tat prati brūmaḥ saṃbhavati eka buddhi viṣaya tvam paṅktiḥ daśa śatam sahasram ityādi darśaāt yā tu gauḥ iti ekaḥ yam śabda iti buddhiḥ sā bahuṣu eva varṇeṣu aupacārikī eva atra āha yadi varṇāḥ eva eka buddhi viṣaya tām padam syuḥ jārāḥ rājā kapiḥ pikaḥ ityādiṣu pada viśeṣa pratipattiḥ syāt te eva hi varṇāḥ itaratra itaratra ca pratyavabhāsate iti atra vadāmaḥ sati api samasta varṇa pratyavamarśe yathā eva pipīlikāḥ paṅkti buddhim ārohati evam eva hi varṇāḥ pada buddhim ārokṣyati tatra varṇāām aviśeṣe krama viśeṣa kṛtā pada viśeṣa pratipattiḥ virudhyate vṛddha vyavahāre ca ime varṇāḥ sataḥ sva vyavahāre pi samasta pratyavamarśiyām buddhau tādṛśāḥ eva tam tam artham avyabhicāreṇa pratyāyayiṣyati iti varṇa vādiḥ laghīyasī sphoṭa vādiḥ tu adṛṣṭa kalpaā ca varṇāḥ ca ime krameṇa gṛhyamāṇāḥ sphoṭam vyañjayati sa sphoṭaḥ rtham vyaakti iti garīyasī syāt atha api pratyuccāraṇam aye ye varṇāḥ syuḥ tathā api varṇa sāmāyāām avaśya abhyupagatavya tvāt varṇeṣu artha pratipāda a prakriyā racitā sā sāmāyeṣu saṃcārayitavyā tatas ca iti ebhyaḥ śabdebhyaḥ deva ādi vyaktīām prabhavaḥ iti aviruddham atas eva ca ityatvam kartuḥ asmaraṇāt iti sthite vedasya ityatve deva ādi vyakti prabhava abhyupagame tasya virodham āśaṅkya atas prabhavāt iti parihṛtya idāīm tat eva veda aitya tvam sthitam draḍhayati atas eva ca itya tvam iti atas eva iyatā ākṛteḥ deva ādeḥ jagataḥ veda śabda prabhava tvāt veda śabda aitya tvam api pratyetavyam tathā ca matravarṇaḥ vācaḥ padavīyam āyan tām avavida ṛṣiṣu praviṣṭām iti sthitām eva vācam auviām darśayati vedavyāsaḥ ca evam eva smarati lebhire tapasā svayaṃbhuvā iti ca avṛttau api smṛteḥ ca atha api syāt yadi paśu ādi vyakti vat deva ādi vyaktayaḥ pi saṃtatya evā utpadyeraḥ irudhyeran ca tatas bhidhā ābhidheya abhidhātṛ vyavahāra avicchedāt virodhaḥ śabde parihriyeta yadā tu khalu sakalam trailokyam parityakta āma rūpam pralīyate prabhavati iti śruti smṛti vādāḥ vadati tadā katham avirodhaḥ iti tatra idam abhidhīyate iti tadā api saṃsārasya aādi tvam tāvat abhyupagatavyam pratipādayiṣyati ca ācāryaḥ saṃsārasya aādi tvam upapadyate ca api upalabhyate ca iti a ādau ca saṃsāre yathā svāpa prabodhayoḥ pralaya prabhava śravaṇe pi pūrva prabodha vat uttara prabodhe pi kaścid virodhaḥ evam kalpa atara prabhava pralayayoḥ api iti draṣṭavyam svāpa prabodhayoḥ ca pralaya prabhavau śrūyete yadā suptaḥ svapam a kaṃcaa paśyati atha asmi prāṇa eva ekadhā bhavati tadā eam vāc sarvaiḥ āmabhiḥ saha api eti cakṣuḥ sarvaiḥ rūpaiḥ saha apyeti śrotram sarvaiḥ śabdaiḥ saha apyeti maaḥ sarvaiḥ dhyāaiḥ saha apyeti sa yadā pratibudhyate yathā āgeḥ jvalataḥ sarvāḥ diśaḥ visphuliṅgāḥ vipratiṣṭhere evam eva etasmāt ātmanaḥ sarve prāṇāḥ yathāyataam vipratiṣṭhate prāṇebhyaḥ devāḥ devebhyaḥ lokāḥ iti syāt etat svāpe puruṣa atara vyavahāra avicchedāt svayam ca suṣupta prabuddhasya pūrva prabodha vyavahāra ausaṃdhā asaṃbhavāt aviruddham mahāpralaye tu sarva vyavahāra ucchedāt ca kalpa atara vyavahārasya ausaṃdhātum aśakya tvāt vaiṣamyam iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ satya api mahāpralaye mahāpralaye parameśvara āugrahāt īśvarāṇām yadi api prākṛtāḥ dṛśyate iti tathā api tat prākṛta vat īśvarāṇām bhavitavyam yathā hi prāṇi tva aviśeṣe mauṣya ādi stamba paryateṣu jñā aiśvarya ādi pratibadhaḥ pareṇa pareṇa dṛśyate tathā mauṣya ādiṣu eva hiraṇyagarbha paryateṣu jñā aiśvarya ādi abhivyaktiḥ api pareṇa pareṇa bhūyasī bhavati iti etat śruti smṛti vādeṣu asakṛt eva ā aukalpa ādau prādurbhavatām pāramaiśvaryam śrūyamāṇam vaditum tatas ca atīta kalpa auṣṭhita prakṛṣṭa jñā a karmaṇām īśvarāṇām hiraṇyagarbha ādīām vartamāa kalpa ādau prādurbhavatām parameśvara augṛhītāām supta pratibuddha vat tathā ca śrutiḥ yaḥ brahmāṇam vidadhāti pūrvam yaḥ vai vaidāḥ ca prahiṇoti tasmai devam ātma buddhi prakāśam mumukṣuḥ vai śaraṇam aham prapadye iti smarati ca śauaka ādayaḥ madhucchadaḥ prabhṛtibhiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ dāśatayyaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ iti prativedam ca evam eva kāṇḍa ṛṣi ādayaḥ smaryate śrutiḥ api eva darśayati yaḥ ha vai matreṇa yājayati vā adhyāpayati vā sthāṇum varcchati gartam vā pratipadyate iti upakramya tasmāt matre matre vidyāt iti prāṇiām ca sukha prāptaye dharmaḥ vidhīyate duḥkha parihārāya ca adharmaḥ pratiṣidhyate dṛṣṭa āuśravika sukha duḥkha viṣayau ca rāga dveṣau bhavataḥ a vilakṣaṇa viṣayau iti atas dharma adharma phala bhūta uttarottarā sṛṣṭiḥ iṣpadyamāā pūrva sṛṣṭi sadṛśī eva smṛtiḥ ca bhavati teṣām ye karmāṇi prāk sṛṣṭyām pratipedire tāyā iva te prapadyate sṛjyamāāḥ puas puas hiṃsra ahiṃsre mṛdu krūre dharma adharma āvṛta aṛte tad bhāvitāḥ prapadyate tasmāt tat tasya rocate iti pralīyamāam api ca idam jagat śakti avaśeṣam eva pralīyate śakti mūlam eva ca prabhavati itarathā ākasmika tva prasaṅgāt ca a eka ākārāḥ śaktayaḥ śakyāḥ kalpayitum tatas ca vicchidya vicchidya api udbhavatām bhūḥ ādi loka pravāhāṇām deva tiryak mauṣya lakṣaṇāām ca prāṇi ikāya pravāhāṇām varṇa āśrama dharma phala vyavasthāām ca ādau saṃsāre iyata tvam idriya viṣaya saṃbadha eyata tva vat pratyetavyam hi idriya viṣaya saṃbadha ādeḥ vyavahārasya pratisargam ayathātvam ṣaṣṭha idriya viṣaya kalpam śakyam utprekṣitum atas ca sarva kalpāām tulya vyavahāra tvāt eva pratisargam kṛtvā anupūrva anupūrva anupūrva anupūrva anupūrva anupūrva anupūrva a viśeṣāḥ prādurbhavati mahāsarga mahāpralaya lakṣaṇāyām jagataḥ abhyupagamyamāāyām a kaścid śabda prāmāṇya ādi virodhaḥ samāaāma rūpatām ca śruti smṛtī darśayataḥ sūryācadramasau dhātā yathāpūrvam akalpayat divam ca pṛthivīm cātarikṣam atho suvar iti yathā pūrvasmin kalpe jagat klṛptam tathā asmin api kalpe parameśvaraḥ akalpayat iti arthaḥ tathā agiḥ vai akāmayata devāḥ āsyām iti saḥ etam agaye kṛttikābhyaḥ puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālam iḥ avapat iti akṣatra iṣṭi vidhau yogiḥ iḥ avapat yasmai vāgaye tayoḥ samāaāma rūpa tām darśayati iti evaṃjātīyakā śrutiḥ iha udāhartavyā smṛtiḥ api ṛṣīṇām yāḥ ca vedeṣu dṛṣṭayaḥ prasūtāḥ tāya iva ebhyaḥ dadāti ajaḥ yathā ṛtuṣu ṛtu liṅgāi paryaye dṛśyate tathā bhāvāḥ yuga ādiṣu yathā tathā bhāvāḥ yuga ādiṣu yathā sāṃprataiḥ iha devāḥ devaiḥ atītaiḥ hi rūpaiḥ āmabhiḥ eva ca iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ madhu ādiṣu asambhavāt aadhikāram jaimiiḥ iha deva ādīām api brahmavidyāyām asti adhikāraḥ iti yat pratijñātam tat paryāvartyate kasmāt madhu ādiṣu asaṃbhavāt brahmavidyāyām adhikāra abhyupagame hi vidyā tva aviśeṣāt madhu ādi vidyāsu api adhikāraḥ abhyupagamyeta ca evam saṃbhavati katham asau vā ādityaḥ deva madhu iti atra mauṣyāḥ ādityam madhu adhyāsena upāsīra deva ādiṣu hi upāsakeṣu abhyupagamyamāeṣu ādityaḥ katham ayam ādityam upāsīta vasavaḥ rudrāḥ ādityāḥ marutaḥ sādhyāḥ ca pañca deva gaṇāḥ krameṇa tat tat amṛtam upajīvati iti upadiśya sa yaḥ etat evam amṛtam veda ekaḥ bhūtvā eva mukhena etat eva amṛtam dṛṣṭvā tṛpyati iti ādiā vasu ādi upajīvya amṛtāi vasu ādi mahima prāptim darśayati vasu ādayaḥ tu kā kam vā ayam vasu ādi mahimā prepseyuḥ tathā agiḥ pādaḥ vāyuḥ pādaḥ ādityaḥ pādaḥ diśaḥ pādaḥ vāyuḥ vā saṃvargaḥ ādityaḥ brahma iti ādeśaḥ ityādiṣu devatā ātma upāsaeṣu anya teṣām eva devatā ātmanām adhikāraḥ saṃbhavati tathā imām eva gautama bharadvājau ayam vai gautamaḥ yam bharadvājaḥ ityādiṣu api teṣām eva ṛṣīṇām adhikāraḥ saṃbhavati kutas ca jyotiṣi bhāvāt ca yat idam jyotiḥ maṇḍalam dyu sthāam ahar rātrābhyām bambhramat jagat avabhāsayati tasmin āditya ādayaḥ devatā vacaāḥ śabdāḥ prayujyate loka prasiddheḥ vākyaśeṣa prasiddheḥ ca ca jyotiḥ maṇḍalasya hṛdaya ādiāḥ vigraheṇa arthi tva ādiāḥ vā yogaḥ vagatum śakyate mṛd ādi vat aceta atva avagamāt vyākhyātāḥ syāt etat matra arthavāda itihāsa purāṇa lokebhyaḥ vigrahavat tva ādi avagamāt ayam adoṣaḥ iti ced kiṃcid svatatram pramāṇam asti pratyakṣa ādibhyaḥ eva avyabhicarita viṣayebhyaḥ pramāṇebhyaḥ prasiddha eva arthaḥ lokāt prasiddhaḥ iti ucyate ca atra pratyakṣa ādīām ayatamam pramāṇam asti itihāsa purāṇāām api pauruṣeya tvāt pramāṇa atara mūla tām ākāṅkṣati arthavādāḥ api vidhi eka vākya tvāt stuti arthāḥ vigraha ādi sadbhāve kāraṇa bhāvam pratipadyate api kasyacid arthasya pramāṇam iti ācakṣate tasmāt abhāvaḥ deva ādīām adhikārasya bhāvam tu bādarāyaṇaḥ sti hi tuśabdaḥ pūrvapakṣam vyāvartayati bādarāyaṇaḥ tu ācāryaḥ bhāvam adhikārasya deva ādīām api yadi api madhu ādi vidyāsu devatā ādi vyāmiśrāsu asaṃbhavaḥ udhikārasya tathā api asti hi śuddhāyām brahmavidyāyām saṃbhavaḥ arthi tva sāmarthya a pratiṣedha ādi apekṣa tvāt adhikārasya ca kvacid asaṃbhavaḥ iti etāvatā yatra saṃbhavaḥ tatra api adhikāra upodyeta mauṣyāṇām api sarveṣām brāhmaṇa ādīām sarveṣu rājasūya ādiṣu adhikāraḥ saṃbhavati tatra yaḥ saḥ utra api bhaviṣyati brahma vidyām ca prakṛtya bhavati liṅga darśaam śrautam deva ādi adhikārasya sūcakam tat yaḥ yaḥ devāām pratyabudhyata saḥ eva tat abhavat tathā ṛṣīṇām tathā mauṣyāṇām iti te ha ūcuḥ hata tam ātmā avicchāmaḥ yam ātmā aviṣya sarvān ca lokān apaḥ iti sarvān ca kāmāḥ iti idraḥ ha vai devāām abhipravavrāja virocaḥ asurāṇām ityādi ca smārtam api ca gadharva yājñavalkya saṃvāda ādi yat api uktam jyotiṣi bhāvāt ca iti atra brūmaḥ jyotiḥ ādi viṣayāḥ api āditya ādayaḥ devatā vacaāḥ śabdāḥ cetaāvatam aiśvarya ādi upetam tam tam devatā ātmāam samarpayati matra arthavāda ādiṣu tathā vyavahārāt asti hi aiśvarya yogāt devatā āām jyotiḥ ādi ātmabhiḥ ca avasthātum yathā iṣṭam ca tam tam vigraham grahītum sāmarthyam tathā hi śrūyate subrahmaṇya arthavāde medhātitheḥ meṣaḥ iti medhātithim ha idraḥ meṣaḥ bhūtvā jahāra iti smaryate ca ādityaḥ puruṣaḥ bhūtvā upajagāma ha iti mṛd ādiṣu api cetaāḥ adhiṣṭhātāraḥ abhyupagamyate mṛd abravīt āpobruvaḥ ityādi darśaāt jyodiḥ ādeḥ tu bhūtadhātoḥ āditya ādiṣu api acetaa tvam abhyupagamyate cetaāḥ tu adhiṣṭhātāraḥ devatā ātmāo matra arthavāda ādiṣu vyavahārāt iti uktam yat api uktam matra arthavādayoḥ devatā vigraha ādi prakāśa a sāmarthyam iti atra brūmaḥ pratyaya apratyayau hi sadbhāva asadbhāvayoḥ kāraṇam āya artha tvam a artha tvam vā tathā hi aya artham api prasthitaḥ pathi patitam tṛṇa parṇa ādi asti iti eva pratipadyate atra āha viṣamaḥ upayāsaḥ tatra hi tṛṇa parṇa ādi viṣayam pratyakṣam pravṛttam asti tad astitvam pratipadyate atra stuti arthe rthavāde a pravṛttiḥ śakyā adhyavasātum hi mahāvākye rtha pratyāyake pṛthak pratyāyaka tvam asti yathā a surāṃ pibet iti vākye pada traya saṃbadhāt surā pāa pratiṣedhaḥ eva ekaḥ ṛthaḥ avagamyate a puaḥ surām pibet iti pada dvaya saṃbadhāt surā pāa vidhiḥ api iti atra ucyate viṣamaḥ upayāsaḥ yuktam yat surā pāa pratiṣedhe vidhi uddeśa arthavādayoḥ tu arthavāda sthāi pṛthak avayam pratipadya kaimarthya vaśe kāmam vidheḥ stāvaka tvam pratipadyate yathā hi vāyavyam śvetam ālabheta bhūta kāmaḥ iti atra vidhi uddeśa varti vāyavya ādi padāām vidhinā vāyuḥ vai kṣepiṣṭhā devatā vāyum eva svea bhāgadheyena upadhāvati saḥ eva eam bhūtim gamayati maitrāyaṇī saṃhitā iti eṣām arthavāda gatāām padāām a hi bhavati vāyuḥ vai ālabheta iti kṣepiṣṭhā devatāḥ vai ālabheta ityādi tu pratipadye evam viśiṣṭa daivatyam idam karma iti vidhim stuvati tat yatra yovātara vākya arthaḥ pramāṇa atara gocaraḥ bhavati tatra pravartate yatra pramāṇa atara viruddhaḥ tatra yatra tu tat ubhayam tatra kim pramāṇa atara abhāvāt guṇavādaḥ syāt āhostvit pramāṇa atara avirodhāt vidyamāārthavādaḥ iti pratīti śaraṇaiḥ vidyamāārthavādaḥ āśrayaṇīyaḥ a guṇāuvādaḥ vyākhyātaḥ api ca vidhibhiḥ eva idra ādi daivatyāi havīṃṣi codayadbhiḥ apekṣitam idra ādīām sva rūpam a hi sva rūpa rahitāḥ idra ādayaḥ cetasyā āropayitum śakyate a ca cetasya ārūḍhāyai tasyai tasyai devatāyai haviḥ pradātum śakyate śrāvayati ca yasyai devatāyai haviḥ gṛhītam syāt tām dhyāyet vaṣaṭ kariṣye iti ca śabda mātram artha svarūpam saṃbhavati śabda arthayoḥ bhedāt tatra yādṛśam svarūpam avagatam avagatam tat tādṛśam pratyākhyātum yuktam itihāsa purāṇam api mārgeṇa saṃbhavam atra arthavāda mūlaka tvāt prabhavati devatā vigraha ādi sādhayitum pratyakṣa ādi mūlam api saṃbhavati bhavati hi asmākam apratyakṣam api ciraṃtan pratyakṣam tathā ca vyāsa ādayaḥ deva ādibhiḥ pratyakṣam vyavaharati iti smaryate yaḥ tu brūyāt pūrveṣām api ā asti deva ādibhiḥ vyavahartum sāmarthyam iti sa jagat vaicitryam pratiṣedhet idāīm iva ca sārvabhaumaḥ kṣatriyaḥ asti iti brūyāt tatas ca uparudhyāt idāīm iva ca tatas ca vyavasthā vidhāyi śāstram aarthakam kuryāt tasmāt dharma utkarṣa vaśāt cirantan deva ādibhiḥ pratyakṣam vyavajahuḥ iti śliṣyate api ca smarati svādhyāyāt iṣṭadevatā saṃprayogaḥ ityādi smaryamāṇaḥ a śakyate sāhasa mātreṇa pratyākhyātum śrutiḥ ca yoga māhātmyam prakhyāpayati samutthite pañca ātmake yoga guṇe pravṛtte a tasya rogaḥ a jarā mṛtyuḥ prāptasya śarīram iti ṛṣīṇām api yuktam tasmāt sa mūlam itihāsa purāṇam loka prasiddhiḥ api a sati saṃbhave yuktā tasmāt matra ādibhyaḥ deva ādīām vigrahavat tva ādi avagamaḥ tatas ca arthi tva ādi saṃbhavāt deva ādīām api brahmavidyāyām adhikāraḥ evam eva upapadyate śugasya tad a ādara śravaṇāt tad ādravaṇāt sūcyate hi apaśūdrā adhikaraṇam yathā mauṣya adhikāra aiyamam apodya deva ādīām api vidyāsu adhikāraḥ uktaḥ tathā eva śūdrasya api adhikāraḥ syāt iti etām āśaṅkām ivartayitum idam adhikaraṇam ārabhyate tatra śūdrasya api adhikāraḥ syāt iti tāvat prāptam arthi tva sāmarthyayoḥ saṃbhavāt tasmāt śūdraḥ yajñe avaklṛptaḥ iti vat śūdraḥ vidyāyām a avaklṛptaḥ iti iṣedha śravaṇāt yat ca karmasu a adhikāra kāraṇam śūdrasya a agi tvam a tad vidyāsu adhikārasya apavādakam a hi āhavaīya ādi rahitā vidyā veditum a śakyate bhavati ca śrautam liṅgam śūdra adhikārasya upodbalakam saṃvarga vidyāyām hi jāaśrutim pautrāyaṇam śuśrūṣum śūdra śabde parāmṛśati aha hāre tvā śūdra tava eva saha gobhiḥ astu iti vidura prabhṛtayaḥ ca api smaryate tasmāt adhikriyate śūdraḥ vidyāsu iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ a śūdrasya adhikāraḥ veda adhyaya ābhāvāt hi vidita veda arthaḥ veda artheṣu adhikriyate a ca śūdrasya veda adhyayaam asti upaaya a pūrvaka tvāt veda adhyayaasya upaayaasya ca varṇa traya viṣaya tvāt yat tu arthi tvam a tat asati sāmarthya idhikāra kāraṇam bhavati sāmarthyam api a laukikam kevalam adhikāra kāraṇam bhavati śāstrīya ṛthe śāstrīyasya sāmarthyasya apekṣita tvāt śāstrīyasya ca sāmarthyasya yat ca idam śūdraḥ yajñe avaklṛptaḥ iti tat yāya pūrvaka tvāt vidyāyām api a avaklṛpta tvam dyotayati yāyasya sādhāraṇa tvāt yat puas saṃvarga vidyāyām śūdra śabda śravaṇam liṅgam tad liṅgam hi liṅga darśaam dyotakam bhavati a ca atra kāmam ca ayam śūdra śabdaḥ saṃvarga vidyāyām eva ekasyām śūdram adhikuryāt tad viṣaya tvāt a sarvāsu vidyāsu arthavāda stha tvāt tu a kvacid api ayam śūdram adhikartum utsahate śakyate ca ayam śūdra śabda udhikṛta viṣaye yojayitum katham iti ucyate kamvaraḥ eam etat satam raikvam āttha iti asmāt haṃsa vākyāt śrutavataḥ jāaśruteḥ pautrāyaṇasya śuc utpede tām ṛṣiḥ raikvaḥ śūdra śabde sūcayāṃbabhūva gamyate jātiśūdrasya adhikārāt katham sūcyate iti ucyate tad ādravaṇāt śucam abhidudrāva śucā vā abhidudruve śucā vā raikvam abhidudrāva iti śūdraḥ avayava artha saṃbhavāt rūḍhi arthasya ca asaṃbhavāt dṛśyate ca ayam arthaḥ ūsyām ākhyāyikāyām kṣatriya tva gateḥ ca uttaratra liṅgāt itas ca a jātiśūdraḥ yatkāraṇam kṣatriya tvam asya uttaratra kṣatriya tvam asya uttaratra kṣatriyeṇa samabhivyāhārāt liṅgāt gamyate uttaratra hi saṃvarga vidyā vākyaśeṣe caitrarathiḥ abhipratārī kṣatriyaḥ saṃkīrtyate atha ha śauakam ca kāpeyam abhipratāriṇam ca kākṣaseim pariviṣyamāṇau brahmacārī bibhikṣe iti caitrarathi tvam ca abhipratāriṇaḥ kāpeya yogāt avagatavyam kāpeya yogaḥ hi citrarathasya avagataḥ vai citraratham kāpeyāḥ ayājayaḥ iti samāāvayāām ca prāyeṇa samāāvayāḥ yājakāḥ bhavati tasmāt caitrarathi rāma ekaḥ kṣatra patiḥ ajāyata iti ca kṣatra pati tva avagamāt kṣatriya tvam asya avagatavyam kṣatriyeṇa abhipratāriṇā saha samāāyām saṃvarga vidyāyām jāa śruteḥ api kṣatriya tvam sūcayati samāāām eva hi prāyeṇa samabhivyāhārā bhavati kṣattṛ preṣaṇa ādi aiśvarya yogāt ca kṣatriya tva avagatiḥ atas a śūdrasya adhikāraḥ saṃskāra parāmarśāt tad abhāva abhilāpāt ca itas ca a śūdrasya adhikāraḥ yat vidyā pradeśeṣu upaaya ādayaḥ saṃskārāḥ parāmṛśyate tam ha upaiye adhīhi bhagavaḥ iti ha upasasāda brahma parā manas anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhāna anuṣṭhā brahmaiṣṭhāḥ param brahma āveṣamāṇāḥ eṣa ha vai tat sarvam vakṣyati iti te ha samidh pāṇayaḥ bhagavatam pippalādam iti ca iti api pradarśitā eva upaaya aprāptiḥ bhavati śūdrasya ca saṃskāra abhāvaḥ abhilapyate śūdraḥ caturthaḥ varṇaḥ ekajātiḥ iti eka jāti tva smaraṇāt a śūdre pātakam ca saṃskāram arhati iti ādibhiḥ ca tad abhāvaiḥ dhāraṇe ca pravṛtteḥ itas ca a śūdrasya adhikāraḥ śūdra tva abhāve iḥ dhārite jābālam gautamaḥ upaetum auśāsitum ca pravavṛte ā etat abrāhmaṇaḥ vivaktum arhati samidham somya āhara upa tvā eṣye a satyāt agāḥ iti śruti liṅgāt śravaṇa adhyaya artha pratiṣedhāt smṛteḥ ca itas ca a śūdrasya adhikāraḥ yat asya smṛteḥ śravaṇa adhyaya artha pratiṣedhaḥ bhavati veda śravaṇa pratiṣedhaḥ veda adhyaya a pratiṣedhaḥ tad artha pratiṣedhaḥ śūdrasya smaryate śravaṇa pratiṣedhaḥ tāvat atha ha asya vedam upaśrṛṇvataḥ trapu jatubhyām śrotra pratipūraṇam iti ha vai etat śamaśāaṃ aṃga adhyayana artha pratiṣedhaḥ iti ha vai etat śamaśāam aṃga artha pratiṣedhaḥ iti ha vai etat śamaśāam aṃga artha pratiṣedhaḥ yat śūdraḥ tasmāt śūdra samīpe ādhyetavyam iti ca atas eva adhyaya a pratiṣedhaḥ yasya hi samīpe pi ādhyetavyam bhavati sa katham aśrutam adhīyīta bhavati ca veda uccāraṇe jihvā chedaḥ dhāraṇe śarīra bhedaḥ iti atas eva ca arthāt pratiṣedhaḥ bhavati a śūdrāya matim dadyāt iti iti ca yeṣām pūrva kṛta saṃskāra vaśāt vidura dharmavyādha prabhṛtīām jñā utpattiḥ teṣām śakyate phala prāptiḥ pratiṣeddhum jñā asya aikātika phala tvāt śrāvayet caturaḥ varṇāḥ iti ca itihāsa purāṇa adhigame cāturvarṇyasya adhikāra smaraṇāt veda pūrvakaḥ tu śūdrāṇām iti sthitam kampaāt kampa adhikaraṇam avasitaḥ prāsaṅgikaḥ adhikāra vicāraḥ prakṛtām eva idāīm vākya artha vicāraṇām pravartayiṣyāmaḥ yat idam vākya artha vicāraṇām pravartayiṣyāmaḥ yat idam artha vicāraṇām pravartayiṣyāmaḥ yat idam artha vicāra kiṃca jagat sarvam prāṇaḥ ejati mahat bhayam vajram udyatam ye etat viduḥ amṛtāḥ te bhavati iti etat vākyam iti dhātvartha augamāt lakṣitam asmin vākye sarvam idam jagat prāṇa āśrayam spadate mahat ca kiṃcid bhaya kāraṇam vajra śabditam udyatam tad vijñāāt ca amṛta tva prāptiḥ iti śrūyate tatra kaḥ asau prāṇaḥ kim tat bhayāakam vajram iti apratipatteḥ vicāre kriyamāṇe prāptam tāvat prasiddheḥ pañca vṛttiḥ vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ iti prasiddheḥ eva syāt vāyoḥ ca idam māhātmyam saṃkīrtyate katham sarvam idam jagat pañca vṛttau vāyau prāṇa śabdite pratiṣṭhāya ejati ca mahat bhayāakam vajram udyamyate vāyau hi vivartamāe vidyut staayitu vṛṣṭi aśaayaḥ vivartate iti ācakṣate vāyu vijñāāt eva ca idam amṛta tvam tathā hi śrutyataram vāyuḥ eva vyaṣṭiḥ vāyuḥ samaṣṭiḥ apa puar mṛtyum jayati yaḥ evam veda iti tasmāt vāyuḥ ayam iha pratipattavyaḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ brahma eva idam iha pratipattavyam kutas pūrva uttara ālocaāt pūrva uttarayoḥ hi gratha bhāgayoḥ brahma eva upalabhāmahe iha eva katham akasmāt atarāle vāyum pratipadyemahi pūrvatra tāvat tat eva śukram tat brahma tat eva amṛtam ucyate tasimat lokāḥ śritāḥ sarve tat u ātyeti kaḥ ca iti brahma tat eva iha api tat eva iha api saṃidhāāt jagat sarvam prāṇaḥ ejati iti ca loka āśraya tva pratyabhijñāāt gamyate prāṇa śabdaḥ upi ayam paramātmayā iva prayuktaḥ prāṇasya prāṇam iti ejayitṛ tvam api idam paramātma eva upapadyate a vāyu mātrasya tathā ca uktam martyaḥ jīvati kaḥ ca a itareṇa tu jīvati yasmin etau upāśritau iti uttaratra api bhayāt asya agiḥ tapati bhayāt tapati sūryaḥ bhayāt idraḥ ca vāyuḥ ca mṛtyuḥ dhāvati pañcamaḥ iti brahmā eva a vāyuḥ sa vāyukasya jagataḥ bhaya hetu tva abhidhāāt tat eva iha api saṃidhāāt mahat bhayam vajram udyatam iti ca bhaya hetu tvam pratyabhijñā āirdiṣṭam iti gamyate vajra śabdaḥ upi ayam bhaya hetu tva sāmāyāt prayuktaḥ yathā hi vajram udyatam mama eva śirasi ipatet yadi aham asya śāsaam kuryām iyam ea rāja ādi śāsae pravartate evam idam a c iva āyu sūrya ādikam jagat asmāt eva brahmaṇaḥ bibhyat iyam ea sva vyāpāre pravartate iti bhayāakam vajra upamitam brahma tathā ca brahma viṣayam śrutyataram bhīṣā asmāt vātaḥ pavate bhīṣā udeti sūryaḥ bhīṣā asmāt agiḥ ca idraḥ ca mṛtyuḥ dhāvati pañcamaḥ iti amṛta tva phala śravaṇāt api brahma eva idam iti gamyate brahma jñāāt hi amṛta tva prāptiḥ tam eva viditvā ati mṛtyum eti āyaḥ pathā iti matravarṇāt yat tu vāyuvijñāāt kvacid amṛta tvam abhihitam tat āpekṣikam tatra eva iti vāyu ādeḥ ārta tva abhidhāāt prakaraṇāt api atra paramātma aiścayaḥ ayatra dharmāt ayatra adharmāt ayatra asmāt kṛta akṛtāt ayatra bhūtāt ca bhavyāt ca yat tat paśyasi tat vada iti paramātmanaḥ pṛṣṭa tvāt jyotiḥ darśaāt jyotiḥ adhikaraṇam eṣa saṃprasādaḥ usmāt śarīrāt samutthāya param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya sve a rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate iti śrūyate tatra saṃśayyate kim jyotiḥ śabdam cakṣuḥ viṣayatama upaham tejaḥ kim vā param brahma iti kim tāvat prāptam prasiddham eva tejaḥ jyotiḥ śabdam iti kutas jyotiḥ śabdasya rūḍha tvāt jyotiḥ caraṇa abhidhāāt iti atra hi prakaraṇāt jyotiḥ śabdaḥ svārtham parityajya brahmaṇi vartate ca iha tadvat kiṃcid svārtha parityāge kāraṇam dṛśyate tathā ca āḍīkhaṇḍe atha yatra etat asmāt śarīrāt utkrāmati atha etaiḥ eva raśmibhiḥ ūrdhvam ākramate iti mumukṣoḥ āditya prāptiḥ abhihitā tasmāt prasiddham eva tejaḥ jyotiḥ śabdam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ param eva brahma jyotiḥ śabdam kasmāt darśaāt tasya hi iha prakaraṇe vaktavya tve āuvṛttiḥ dṛśyate yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā iti apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇakasya ātmaaḥ prakaraṇa ādau aveṣṭavya tve vijijñāsitavya tve ca pratijñāāt etam tu eva te bhūyas uvyākhyāsyāmi iti a ausaṃdhāāt aśarīram vāva satam a priya apriye spṛśataḥ iti ca aśarīra tāyai jyotiḥ saṃpatteḥ asya abhidhāāt brahma bhāvāt ca ayatra aśarīra tā upapatteḥ param jyotiḥ saḥ uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ iti ca viśeṣaṇāt yat tu uktam mumukṣoḥ āditya prāptiḥ abhihitā iti ā asau ātyatikaḥ mokṣaḥ gati utkrāti saṃbadhāt hi ātyatike mokṣe gati utkrātī staḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ ākāśaḥ artha atara tva ādi vyapadeśāt artha atara tva ādi vyapadeśa adhikaraṇam ākāśaḥ vai āmaḥ āma rūpayoḥ te yat atarā tat brahma tat amṛtam saḥ ātmā iti śrūyate tat kim ākāśa śabdam param brahma kim vā prasiddham eva bhūtākāśam iti vicāre bhūta parigrahaḥ yuktaḥ ākāśa śabdasya tasmin rūḍha tvāt āma rūpaiḥ vahaṇasya ca avakāśa dā a dvāreṇa tasmin yojayitum śakya tvāt sraṣṭṛ tva ādeḥ ca spaṣṭasya brahma liṅgasya aśravaṇāt iti evam prāpte idam ucyate param eva brahma iha ākāśa śabdam bhavitum arhati kasmāt artha atara tva ādi vyapadeśāt te yat atarā tat brahma iti hi āma rūpābhyām arthātara bhūtam ākāśam vyapadiśati a ca brahmaṇaḥ ayaḥ āma rūpābhyām arthātaram saṃbhavati sarvasya vikāra jātasya āma rūpābhyām eva vyākṛta tvāt āma rūpayoḥ api irvahaṇam iraṅkuśam api brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhavati āma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti brahma kartṛka tva śravaṇāt jīvasya api pratyakṣam āma rūpa viṣayam asti bāḍham asti abhedaḥ tu iha vivakṣitaḥ eva ca sraṣṭṛ tva ādi brahma liṅgam abhihitam bhavati tat brahma tat amṛtam saḥ ātmā iti ca brahma vādasya liṅgāt ākāśaḥ tad liṅgāt iti asya eva ayam prapañcaḥ suṣupti utkrātyoḥ bhede suṣupti adhikaraṇam bṛhadāraṇyake ṣaṣṭhe prapāṭhake katamaḥ ātmā iti yaḥ yam vijñā a mayaḥ prāṇeṣu hṛdi atas jyotiḥ puruṣaḥ iti upakramya bhūyāātma viṣayaḥ prapañcaḥ kṛtaḥ tat kim saṃsāri svarūpa mātrā avākhyā aparam vākyam uta asaṃsāri svarūpa pratipāda aparam iti viśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam saṃsāri svarūpa mātra viṣayam eva iti kutas upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām upakrame yaḥ yam vijñā amayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti śārīra liṅgāt upasaṃhāre ca sa vā asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya asya eṣa mahā ajaḥ ātmā yaḥ yam vijñā a mayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti tad aparityāgāt madhye pi tasya eva prapañcaāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ parameśvara upadeśa param eva idam vākyam a śārīra mātrau ākhyā a param kasmāt suṣuptau utkrātau ca śārīrāt bhedea parameśvarasya vyapadeśāt suṣuptau tāvat ayam puruṣaḥ saṃpariṣvaktaḥ a bāhyam kiṃcaa veda ātaram iti śārīrāt bhedea parameśvaram vyapadiśati tatra puruṣaḥ śārīraḥ syāt tasya veditṛ tvāt bāhya abhyatara veda aprasaṅge sati tad pratiṣedha saṃbhavāt prājñaḥ parameśvaraḥ sarvajñatva lakṣaṇayā prajñayā iti ama viyogāt tathā utkrātau api ayam śārīraḥ ātmā utsarjayāti iti jīvāt bhedea parameśvaram vyapadiśati tatra api śārīraḥ jīvaḥ syāt śarīra svāmi tvāt prājñaḥ tu saḥ eva parameśvaraḥ tasmāt suṣupti utkrātyoḥ bhedea vyapadeśāt parameśvaraḥ eva atra vivakṣitaḥ iti gamyate yat uktam ādya tamadhyeṣu śārīra liṅgāt tad para tvam asya vākyasya iti atra brūmaḥ upakrame tāvat yaḥ yam vijñā a mayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti a saṃsāri svarūpam vivakṣitam kim tarhi saṃsāri svarūpam pareṇa brahmaṇā asya eka tām vivakṣati yatas dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva iti evamādi uttaragratha pravṛttiḥ saṃsāri dharmaiḥ ākaraṇa parā lakṣyate tathā upasaṃhāre api yathopakramam eva upasaṃharati sa vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ ātmā yaḥ yam vijñā amayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti yaḥ yam vijñā amayaḥ prāṇeṣu saṃsārī lakṣyate sa vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ ātmā parameśvaraḥ eva asmābhiḥ pratipāditaḥ iti arthaḥ yaḥ tu madhye sa prācīm api diśam prasthāpitaḥ pratīcīm api diśam pratiṣṭheta yatas saṃsāri tvam vā vivakṣati kim tarhi avasthā rahitatvam asaṃsāri tvam ca katham etat avagamyate yat atas ūrdhvam vimokṣāya eva brūhi iti pade pade pṛcchati yat ca bhavati a saṅgaḥ hi ayam puruṣaḥ iti pade pade prativakti aavāgatam puṇye aavāgatam pāpea tīrṇaḥ hi tadā sarvān śokāhṛdayasya bhavati iti ca tasmāt asaṃsāri svarūpa pratipāda aparam eva etat vākyam iti avagatavyam pati ādi śabdebhyaḥ itas ca asaṃsāri svarūpa pratipāda aparam eva etat vākyam iti avagatavyam yat asmin vākye pati ādayaḥ śabdāḥ asaṃsāri svarūpa pratipāda aparāḥ saṃsāri svabhāva pratiṣedha āḥ ca bhavati sarvasya vaśī sarvasya īśaḥ sarvasya adhipatiḥ iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ asaṃsāri svabhāva pratipāda aparāḥ sa a sādhuā karmaṇā anuprāptavyam asaṃsāri svabhāva prat bhūyāḥ iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ saṃsāri svabhāva pratiṣedhaāḥ tasmāt asaṃsārī parameśvaraḥ iha uktaḥ iti avagamyate iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye prathama adhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ murat prathama udhyāyaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ āumāikam api ekeṣām iti ced a śarīra rūpaka viyasta gṛhīteḥ darśayati ca āumāika adhikaraṇam āumāikam api aumāairūpitam api pradhāam ekeṣām śabda vat upalabhyate kāṭhake hi paṭhyate mahataḥ param avyaktam avyaktāt puruṣaḥ paraḥ iti tatra ye eva yatkramāḥ ca mahat avyakta puruṣāḥ smṛti prasiddhāḥ tad eva eva iha pratyabhijñāyate tatra avyaktam iti smṛti prasiddheḥ ca a vyaktam avyaktam iti vyutpatti saṃbhavāt smṛti prasiddham pradhāam abhidhīyate atas tasya śabdavat tvāt aśabda tvam aupapam tat eva ca jagataḥ kāraṇam śruti smṛti yāya prasiddhibhyaḥ iti ced etat evam hi etat kāṭhaka vākyam smṛti prasiddhayoḥ mahat avyaktayoḥ astitva param a hi atra yādṛśam smṛti prasiddham svatatram kāraṇam triguṇam tādṛśam pratyabhijñāyate śabda mātram hi atra avyaktam iti pratyabhijñāyate sa ca śabdaḥ a vyaktam avyaktam iti yaugika tvāt sūkṣme su durlakṣye ca prayujyate a ca ayam kasmin cit rūḍhaḥ yā tu pradhāa vādiām rūḍhiḥ sā teṣām eva pāribhāṣikī satī a kāraṇa bhāvam pratipadyate ca krama mātra sāmāyāt bhavati asati tad rūpa pratyabhijñāe gām iti amūḍhaḥ adhyavasyati prakaraṇaiḥ ūpaṇāyām ca atra a para parikalpitam pradhāam pratīyate śarīra rūpaka viyasta gṛhīteḥ śarīram hi atra parigṛhyate kutas prakaraṇāt pariśeṣāt ca tathā ātma śarīra ādīnām rathi ratha ādi rūpaka klṛptim darśayati viddhi śarīram ratham eva tu buddhim tu sārathim viddhi maaḥ pragraham eva ca idriyāṇi hayāḥ āhuḥ viṣayān teṣu gocarāḥ ātma idriya mao yuktam bhoktā iti āhuḥ maīṣiṇaḥ iti taiḥ ca idriya ādibhiḥ asaṃyataiḥ saṃsāram adhigacchati saṃyataiḥ tu adhvaḥ pāram tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam iti iti kim tat adhvaḥ pāram viṣṇoḥ paramam padam iti asyām ākāṅkṣāyām tebhyaḥ eva prakṛtebhyaḥ idriya ādibhyaḥ pāram tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam darśayati idriyebhyaḥ parāḥ hi arthāḥ arthebhyaḥ ca param maaḥ maasaḥ tu parā buddhiḥ buddheḥ ātmā mahā paraḥ mahataḥ param avyaktam avyaktāt puruṣaḥ paraḥ param kiṃcid sā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ iti tatra ye eva idriya ādayaḥ pūrvasyām prakṛtāḥ te eva iha parigṛhyate tatra idriya mao buddhayaḥ tāvat pūrvatra iha ca arthāḥ tu ye śabda ādayaḥ viṣayāḥ teṣām ca idriyebhyaḥ paratvam idriyāṇām ca graha tvam viṣayāṇām atigraha tvam iti śruti prasiddheḥ viṣayebhyaḥ ca paratvam maaḥ mūla tvāt viṣaya idriya vyavahārasya tu parā buddhiḥ buddhim hi āruhya bhogya jātam bhoktāram upasarpati buddheḥ ātmā mahā paraḥ yaḥ saḥ ātmāam rathiam viddhi iti rathi tvena upakṣiptaḥ kutas ātma śabdāt bhoktuḥ ca bhoga upakaraṇāt paratva upapatteḥ mahat tvam ca asya svāmi tvāt upapaam athavā mahāmatiḥ brahmā pūḥ buddhiḥ khyātiḥ īśvaraḥ prajñā saṃvid citiḥ ca eva smṛtiḥ ca paripaṭhyate iti smṛteḥ yaḥ brahmāṇam vidadhāti pūrvam yaḥ prajñā anubhūtiḥ vai vedān ca prahiṇoti tasmai iti ca śruteḥ yā prathama jasya hiraṇyagarbhasya buddhiḥ sā sarvāsām buddhīām paramā pratiṣṭhā sā iha mahāātmā iti ucyate sā ca pūrvatra buddhi grahaṇea eva gṛhītā satī hiruk iha upadiśyate tasyāḥ api asmadīyābhyaḥ buddhibhyaḥ paratva upapatteḥ etasmin tu pakṣe paramātma viṣayeṇa eva pareṇa grahaṇam draṣṭavyam paramārthataḥ tu paramātma vijñāātmaoḥ bheda abhāvāt tat evam śarīram eva ekam pariśiṣyate teṣu itarāṇi idriya ādīni eva parama pada didarśayiṣayā samaukrāma pariśiṣyamāṇe idriya maaḥ buddhi viṣaya veda a saṃyuktasya hi avidyāvataḥ bhoktuḥ śarīra ādīnām saṃsāra mokṣa gati rūpaṇea pratyagātma brahma avagatiḥ iha vivakṣitā tathā ca eṣa sarveṣu bhūteṣu gūḍha utmā prakāśate dṛśyate tu agryayā buddhyā sūkṣmayā sūkṣma darśibhiḥ iti vaiṣṇavasya parama padasya duravagama tvam uktvā tad avagama artham yogam darśayati yacchet vāc maasī prājñaḥ tat yacchet ātmai mahati iyat chet tat yacchet śātaḥ ātmai iti etat uktam bhavati vācam maasi saṃyacchet vāc ādi bāhya idriya vyāpāram utsṛjya maaḥ mātreṇa avatiṣṭheta viṣaya vikalpa abhimukham vikalpa doṣa darśa ea jñā a śabda uditāyām buddhau adhyavasāya svabhāvāyām dhārayet tām api buddhim mahati bhoktari agryāyām vā buddhau iyacchet prakaraṇavati parasmin puruṣe parasyām kāṣṭhāyām pratiṣṭhāpayet iti ca tat evam pūrva apara ālocaāyām sūkṣmam tu tad arha tvāt uktam etat prakaraṇa pariśeṣābhyām śarīram avyakta śabdam a pradhāam iti idam idāīm āśaṅkyate katham avyakta śabda artha tvam śarīrasya yāvatā sthūla tvāt spaṣṭataram idam śarīram vyakta śabda artham aspaṣṭa vacaḥ tu avyakta śabdaḥ iti atas uttaram ucyate sūkṣmam tu iha śarīram vivakṣyate sūkṣmasya avyakta śabda artha tvāt yadi api sthūlam idam śarīram svayam avyakta śabdam arhati tathā api tasya tu ārambhakam bhūta sūkṣmam avyakta śabdam arhati prakṛti śabdaḥ ca vikāre dṛṣṭaḥ yathā gobhiḥ śrīṇīta matsaram iti śrutiḥ ca tat ha idam tarhi avyākṛtam āsīt iti idam eva vyākṛta āma rūpa vibhiam jagat prāc avasthāyām parityakta vyākṛta āma rūpam bīja śakti avastham avyakta śabda yogyam darśayati tad adhī atvāt arthavat atra āha yadi jagat idam bīja ātmakam prāk avastham avyakta śabda arham abhyupagamyeta ca śarīrasya api avyakta śabda arha tvam pratijñāyeta saḥ eva tarhi pradhā a kāraṇa vādaḥ evam sati āpadyeta asya eva jagataḥ prāk avasthāyāḥ iti atra ucyate yadi vayam svatatrām kāṃcid prāc avasthām jagataḥ kāraṇa tveā abhyupagacchema prasañjayema tadā pradhā akāraṇa vādam tu iyam asmābhiḥ prāc avasthā jagataḥ bhyupagamyate svatatrā sā ca avaśya abhyupagatavyā arthavatī hi sā arthavatī hi tayā parameśvarasya sraṣṭṛ tvam sidhyati śakti rahitasya tasya pravṛtti aupapatteḥ muktāām ca autpattiḥ kutas vidyayā tasyāḥ bīja śakteḥ dāhāt avidyā ātmikā hi sā bīja śaktiḥ avyakta śabdaiḥ deśyā parameśvara āśrayā māyā mayī mahāsuṣuptiḥ yasyām sva rūpa pratibodha rahitāḥ śerate saṃsāriṇaḥ jīvāḥ tat etat avyaktam kvacid ākāśa śabdaiḥ diṣṭam etasmin u khalu akṣare gārgya ākāśaḥ otaḥ ca protaḥ ca iti śruteḥ kvacid akṣara śabda uditam akṣarāt paratas paraḥ iti śruteḥ kvacid māyā iti sūcitam māyām tu prakṛtim tu maheśvaram iti matra varṇāt avyaktā hi sā māyā tat idam mahataḥ param avyaktam iti uktam avyakta prabhava tva amahataḥ yadā hairaṇyagarbhī buddhiḥ mahā yadā tu jīvaḥ mahā tadā api avyakta adhī atvāt jīva bhāvasya mahataḥ param avyaktam iti uktam avidyā hi avyaktam jīvasya sarvaḥ saṃvyavahāraḥ saṃtataḥ vartate tat ca avyakta gatam mahataḥ para tvam abheda upacārāt tad vikāre śarīre parikalpyate sati api śarīra vat idriya ādīām tad vikāra tva aviśeṣe śarīrasya eva abheda upacārāt avyakta śabde grahaṇam idriya ādīām sva śabdaiḥ eva gṛhīta tvāt pariśiṣṭa tvāt ca śarīrasya tu varṇayati dvividham hi śarīram sthūlam sūkṣmam ca sthūlam yat idam upalabhyate sūkṣmam yat uttaratra vakṣyate tad atara pratipattau raṃhati saṃpariṣvaktaḥ iti tat ca ubhayam api śarīram aviśeṣāt pūrvatra saṃkīrtitam iha tu sūkṣmam avyakta śabde parigṛhyate sūkṣmasya avyakta śabda arha tvāt tad adhī a tvāt ca jīvāt tasya paratvam yathārtha adhī a tvāt idriya vyāpārasya idriyebhyaḥ paratvam arthāām iti taiḥ tu etat vaktavyam aviśeṣeṇa śarīra dvayasya pūrvatra saṃkīrtita tvāt prakṛta tva pariśiṣṭa tvayoḥ katham sūkṣmam eva śarīram iha gṛhyate sthūlam api iti āmātasya artham pratipattum prabhavāmaḥ āmātam āmātam ca avyakta padam sūkṣmam eva pratipādayitum etarat vyakta tvāt tasya iti ced a eka vākya tā dhī a tvāt arthaṃpratipatteḥ a hi ime pūrva uttare āmāte ekavākyatām a āpadya kaṃcid artham pratipādayataḥ ca ākāṅkṣā matareṇa ekavākyatā pratipattiḥ asti tatra aviśiṣṭāyām śarīra dvayasya grāhya tva ākāṅkṣāyām yathākāṅkṣam ekavākyatā eva bādhitā bhavati kutas pratipattiḥ ca evam matavyam duḥśodha tvāt sūkṣmasya eva śarīrasya iha grahaṇam sthūlasya tu dṛṣṭa bībhatsa tayā su śodha tvāt agrahaṇam iti yatas kasyacid vivakṣyate hi atra śodha a vidhāyi kiṃcid ākhyātam asti aa araiḥ diṣṭa tvāt tu kim tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam iti idam iha vivakṣyate tathā hi idam asmāt param idam asmāt param iti uktvā puruṣāḥ param kiṃcid iti āha sarvathā api tathā kiṃcid chidyate jñeya tvāt ca ca sāṃkhyaiḥ smaryate guṇa puruṣa atara jñāāt kaivalyam iti vadadbhiḥ hi guṇa svarūpam a jñātvā guṇebhyaḥ puruṣasya ataram śakyam jñātum iti kvacid ca vibhūti viśeṣa prāptaye jñeyam iti smarati a ca idam iha avyaktam jñeya tve ucyate pada mātram hi avyakta śabdaḥ ā iha avyaktam jñātavyam upāsitavyam ca iti vākyam asti a puruṣa artham iti śakyam pratipattum tasmāt api abhidhīyate asmākam tu viṣṇoḥ eva paramam padam darśayitum ayam upayāsaḥ iti aavadyam vadati iti ce a prājñaḥ hi prakaraṇāt atra āha sāṃkhyaḥ iti asiddham katham śrūyate hi uttaratra avyakta śabda uditasya pradhāasya a śabdam a sparśam a rūpam avyayam ca yat mahataḥ param dhruvam icāyya tam mṛtyu mukhāt pramucyate iti atra hi yādṛśam mahataḥ param smṛtau tādṛśam eva tasmāt pradhāam eva idam tat eva ca avyakta śabdaiḥ diṣṭam iti atra brūmaḥ eha prājñaḥ hi iha paramātmā iti gamyate kutas prakaraṇāt prājñasya hi prakaraṇam vitatam vartate puruṣāḥ a param kiṃcid sā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ ityādi irdeśāt eṣa sarveṣu bhūteṣu guḍha utmā prakāśate iti ca tasya eva jñeya tva ākāṅkṣaṇāt yacchet vāc prājñaḥ iti ca tad jñāāya eva vāc ādi saṃyamasya vihita tvāt mṛtyu mukha pramokṣaṇa phala tvāt ca a hi pradhā a mātram icāyya mṛtyu mukhāt pramucyate iti sāṃkhyaiḥ iṣyate cetaḥ ātma vijñāāt hi mṛtyu mukhāt pramucyate iti teṣām abhyupagamaḥ sarveṣu vedāteṣu prājñasya eva ātma o śabda ādi dharma tvam abhilapyate tasmai vā trayāṇām eva ca evam upayāsaḥ ca ca ca a pradhā asya avyakta śabda vācya tvam jñeya tvam vā yasmāt trayāṇām eva asmi asmi kaṭhavallīṣu vara pradā asāmarthyāt vaktavya tayā upayāsaḥ dṛśyate tad viṣayaḥ eva ca upayāsaḥ vā asti tatra tāvat sa tvam agim svargyam adhyeṣi mṛtyo prabrūhi tam mahyam iti agi viṣayaḥ praśaḥ yā iyam prete vicikitsā eke ā ayam asti iti ca eke etad vidyām auśiṣṭaḥ tvayā aham varāṇām eṣa varaḥ tṛtīyaḥ iti jīva viṣayaḥ praśaḥ ayatra dharmāt ayatra adharmāt ayatra asmāt kṛta akṛtāt ayatra bhūtāt ca bhavyāt ca yat tat paśyasi tat vada iti paramātma viṣayaḥ api loka ādim agim tam uvāca tasmai yā iṣṭakā yāvatīḥ vā yathā vā iti agi viṣayam hata te idam pravakṣyāmi guhyam brahma yathā ca maraṇam prāpya ātmā bhavati gautama prapadyate śarīra tvāya sthāṇum yathākarma yathāśrutam iti vyavahitam jīva viṣayam a jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit ityādi bahu prapañcam paramātma viṣayam a evam pradhā a viṣayaḥ praśoḥ asti a pṛṣṭa tvāt ca aupayasaīya tvam tasya iti atra āha yaḥ yam ātma viṣayaḥ praśaḥ yā iyam prete vicikitsā iti kim saḥ eva ayam a yatra dharmāt ayatra adharmāt iti puar aukṛṣyate kim vā tatas yaḥ uyam apūrvaḥ praśaḥ utthāpyate iti kim ca atas saḥ eva ayam praśaḥ puar aukṛṣyata iti yadi ucyeta tadā dvayoḥ ātma viṣayayoḥ praśayoḥ ekatā āpatteḥ agi viṣayaḥ ātma viṣayaḥ ca dvau eva praśau iti atas vaktavyam trayāṇām iti apūrvaḥ praśaḥ utthāpyate iti ucyeta tatas yathā eva vara pradā a vyatirekeṇa praśa kalpaāyām adoṣaḥ evam praśa vyatirekeṇa api pradhā upayāsa kalpaāyām adoṣaḥ syāt iti atra ucyate a evam vayam iha varapradā a vyatirekeṇa kaṃcid kalpayāmaḥ vākya upakrama sāmarthyāt varapradā upakramā hi mṛtyu aciketaḥ saṃvāda rūpā vākya pravṛttiḥ samāpteḥ lakṣyate mṛtyuḥ kila aciketase pitrā prahitāya trī varā pradadau aciketāḥ kila teṣām vareṇa pituḥ saumaasyam vavre dvitīye āgi vidyām tṛtīye ātma vidyām yā iyam prete iti varāṇām eṣa varaḥ tṛtīyaḥ iti liṅgāt tatra yadi dharmāt iti apūrvaḥ praśaḥ utthāpyeta tatas praśa kalpaāt vākyam bādhyeta praṣṭavya bhedāt apūrvaḥ yam praśaḥ bhavitum arhati apūrvaḥ hi praśaḥ jīva viṣayaḥ yā iyam prete vicikitsā ā asti iti jīvaḥ ca dharma ādi gocara tvāt dharmāt iti praśam arhati prājñaḥ tu dharma ādi atīta tvāt ayatra dharmāt iti praśam arhati praśa chāyā ca a lakṣyate pūrvasya astitva āstitva viṣaya tvāt uttarasya dharma ādi atīta vastu viṣaya tvāt ca tasmāt pratyabhijñā abhāvāt praśa bhedaḥ a pūrvasya eva uttaratra ākarṣaṇam iti ced a jīva prājñayoḥ ekatva abhyupagamāt bhavet praṣṭavya bhedāt praśa bhedaḥ yadi ayaḥ jīvaḥ prājñāt syāt a tu aya tvam asti tattvam asi ityādi śruti atarebhyaḥ iha ca ayatra dharmāt iti asya praśasya prativacam jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit iti śārīra parameśvarayoḥ abhedam darśayati sati hi prasaṅge pratiṣedhaḥ bhāgī bhavati prasaṅgaḥ ca jama maraṇayoḥ śarīra saṃsparśāt śārīrasya bhavati a parameśvarasya tathā svapātam jāgaritātam ca ubhau mahātam vibhum ātmāam matvā dhīraḥ a śocati iti svapa jāgarita dṛśaḥ jīvasya eva mahat tva vibhu tva viśeṣaṇasya śoka vicchedam darśaya a prājñāt jīvaḥ iti darśayati hi śoka vicchedaḥ iti tathā agre yat eva iha tat amutra yat amutra tat iha mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum yaḥ iha ā eva paśyati iti jīva prājña bheda dṛṣṭim apavadati tathā ayam varam aciketaḥ vṛṇīṣva iti ārabhya taiḥ taiḥ kāmaiḥ aciketāḥ yadā cacāla aciketāḥ mṛtyuḥ aciketasam ca vidyā abhīpsiam aciketasam aciketasam aciketasam a tvā kāmāḥ bahavaḥ lolupate iti praśasya api tadīyam uvāca tam durdarśam gūḍham devam matvā dhīraḥ harṣa śokau jahāti iti jīva prājñayoḥ abhedaḥ eva iha vivakṣitaḥ iti gamyate yat praśaimittām ca praśaṃsām mahatīm mṛtyoḥ pratyapadyata aciketāḥ yadi tam vihāya praśaṃsāataram ayam eva praśam upakṣipet eva sā sarvā praśaṃsā prasāritā syāt tasmāt yā iyam prete iti asya eva aukarṣaṇam ayatra dharmāt iti yat tu praśat chāyā vailakṣaṇyam uktam tat adūṣaṇam tadīyasya eva viśeṣasya pūrvatra hi deha ādi vyatiriktasya ātma ostitvam pṛṣṭam uttaratra tu tasya eva asaṃsāri tvam iti yāvat hi avidyā tāvat dharma ādi gocaratvam jīvasya jīva tvam ca tu prājñaḥ eva tat tvam asi iti śrutyā pratyāyyate a ca avidyāvat tve tad apagame ca kaścid viśeṣaḥ asti yathā kaścid sam tamase patitām kāṃcid rajjum ahim mayamāaḥ bhītaḥ vepamāaḥ palāyate tam ca aparaḥ brūyāt mā bhaiṣīḥ ā ayam ahiḥ rajjuḥ eva iti sa ca tad upaśrutya ahi kṛtam bhayam utsṛjet vepathum ca tu ahi buddhi kāle tad apagama kāle ca vastuḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ syāt tathā eva etat api draṣṭavyam tatas ca jāyate mriyate vā iti evamādi api bhavati sūtram tu avidyā kalpita jīva prājña bheda apekṣayā yojayitavyam ekatve api hi ātma viṣayasya prāyaṇa avasthāyām deha vyatirikta astitva mātra vicikitsaāt kartṛ tva ādi saṃsāra svabhāva aapohaāt ca pūrvasya paryāyasya jīva viṣaya tvam utprekṣyate uttarasya tu dharma ādi atyaya saṃkīrtaāt prājña viṣaya tvam iti tatas ca yuktā pradhā akalpaāyām tu anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya any iti vaiṣamyam mahadvat ca yathā mahat śabdaḥ sāṃkhyaiḥ sattā mātre pi prathama je prayuktaḥ a tam eva vaidike api prayoge abhidhatte buddheḥ ātmā mahā paraḥ mahātam vibhum ātmāam veda aham etam puruṣam mahātam iti evamādau ātma śabda prayoga ādibhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ tathā avyakta śabdaḥ api a vaidike prayoge pradhāam abhidhātum arhati atas ca āsti āumāikasya śabdavat tvam camasa vat aviśeṣāt camasa adhikaraṇam puar api pradhāa vādī aśabda tvam pradhā asya asiddham iti āha kasmāt matra varṇāt ajām ekām lohita śukla kṛṣṇām vahvīḥ prajāḥ sarūpāḥ ajaḥ hi ekaḥ juṣamāṇaḥ u śete jahāti eām bhukta bhogām ajoyaḥ iti atra hi matre lohita śukla kṛṣṇa śabdaiḥ rajaḥ sattva tamāṃsi abhidhīyate lohitam rajaḥ rañja ātmaka tvāt śuklam sattvam prakāśa ātmaka tvāt kṛṣṇam tamaḥ āvaraṇa ātmaka tvāt teṣām sāmya avasthā avayava dharmaiḥ vyapadiśyate lohita śukla kṛṣṇā iti a jāyate iti ca ajā syāt mūlaprakṛtiḥ avikṛtiḥ iti abhyupagamāt avajā śabdaḥ chāgyām rūḍhaḥ bāḍham sā tu rūḍhiḥ iha āśrayitum śakyā vidyā prakaraṇāt sā ca bahvīḥ prajāḥ traiguṇya avitāḥ jaayati tām prakṛtim ajaḥ ekaḥ puruṣaḥ juṣamāṇaḥ prīyamāṇaḥ vā viraktaḥ jahāti eām prakṛtim bhukta bhogām kṛta bhoga apavargām parityajati mucyata iti arthaḥ tasmāt śruti mūlā eva kāpilā iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ matreṇa śrutimat tvam sāṃkhya vādasya śakyam āśrayitum hi ayam matraḥ svātatryeṇa kaṃcid api vādam samarthayitum utsahate sarvatra api yayā kayācid kalpa ayā ajā tva ādi saṃpāda opapatteḥ sāṃkhya vādaḥ eva iha abhipretaḥ iti viśeṣa avadhāraṇa kāraṇa abhāvāt camasa vat yathā hi arvāc bilaḥ camasaḥ ūrdhva budhaḥ iti asmin atre svātatryeṇa ayam āma asau camasa abhipretaḥ iti a śakyate iyatum sarvatra api yathā kathaṃcid arvāc bila tva ādi kalpa upapatteḥ evam iha api aviśeṣaḥ ajām ekām iti asya matrasya śakyate iyatum tatra tu idam tat śiraḥ eṣa hi arvāc bilaḥ camasaḥ ūrdhva buddhaḥ iti vākya śeṣāt camasa viśeṣa pratipattiḥ bhavati iha kā iyam ajā pratipattavyā iti atra brūmaḥ jyotiḥ upakramā tu tathā hi adhīyate eke parameśvarāt jyotiḥ pramukhā tejaḥ baa lakṣaṇā caturvidhasya bhūta grāmasya prakṛti bhūtā iyam ajā pratipattavyā tuśabdaḥ bhūta traya lakṣaṇā eva iyam ajā vijñeyā a guṇa traya lakṣaṇā kasmāt tathā hi eke parameśvarāt utpattim teṣām eva rohita ādi rūpa tām yat rohitam rūpam tejasaḥ tat rūpam yat śuklam tat apām yat kṛṣṇam tat iti eva iha pratyabhijñāyate rohita ādi śabda sāmāyāt rohita ādīām ca śabdāām rūpa viśeṣeṣu mukhya tvāt bhākta tvāt ca guṇa viṣaya tvasya asaṃdigdha ca saṃdigdhasya tathā iha api brahma vādiḥ vadati kiṃkāraṇam brahma iti upakramya te apaśya deva ātma śaktim iti pārameśvaryāḥ śakteḥ samasta jagat vidhāyiyāḥ vākya upakrame vagamāt vākyaśeṣe māyām tu prakṛtim vidyā tu maheśvaram iti yaḥ yoim yoim adhitiṣṭhati ekaḥ iti ca tasyāḥ eva avagamāḥ svatatrā kācid prakṛtiḥ atreṇa āmāyate iti śakyate vaktum prakaraṇāt tu sā eva daivī śaktiḥ avyākṛtā ām arūpā āma rūpayoḥ prāk avasthā matreṇa āmāyate iti ucyate tasyāḥ ca sva vikāra viṣayeṇa trairūpyeṇa trairūpyam uktam katham trairūpyeṇa tri rūpā ajā pratipattum śakyate yāvatā a tāvat tejobaeṣu aja ākṛtiḥ asti ca tejobaāām jāti śravaṇāt a jāti nimittaḥ pi ajā śabdaḥ saṃbhavati iti atas uttaram paṭhati kalpa upadeśāt ca madhu ādi vat avirodhaḥ yaugikaḥ kim tarhi ajā rūpaka klṛptiḥ tejaḥ baa lakṣaṇāyāḥ carācara yoḥ upadiśyate yathā hi loke yadṛcchayā kācid ajā rohita śukla kṛṣṇa varṇā syāt bahu barkarā sarūpa barkarā ca tām ca kaścid ajaḥ juṣamāṇaḥ uśayīta kaścid ca eām bhukta bhogām jahyāt evam iyam api bhūtaprakṛtiḥ tri varṇā bahu sarūpam carācara lakṣaṇam vikāra jātam a viduṣā ca kṣetrajñeā upabhujyate viduṣā ca parityajyate iti a ca idam āśaṅkitavyam ekaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ u śete ayaḥ jahāti iti atas kṣetrajña bhedaḥ pāramārthikaḥ pareṣām iṣṭaḥ a hi iyam kṣetrajña bheda pratipipādayiṣā kiṃtu badha mokṣa vyavasthā pratipipādayiṣā eva eṣā prasiddham tu bhedam aūdya pratipādyate bhedaḥ tu upādhi nimittaḥ mithyājñā akalpitaḥ a pāramārthikaḥ ekaḥ devaḥ sarva bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarva vyāpī sarva bhūta atarātmā ityādi śrutibhyaḥ madhu ādi vat yathā madhu tvam vācaḥ ca dyu loka ādīnām iti evaṃjātīyakam kalpyate evam idam aajāyāḥ ajā tvam kalpyate iti arthaḥ tasmāt avirodhaḥ tejaḥ baeṣu ajā śabda prayogasya a saṃkhyā upasaṃgrahāt api saṃkhyā upasaṃgrahāt adhikaraṇam evam parihṛte api ajāmatre evam pratyavatiṣṭhate ākāśaḥ ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ tam eva mayaḥ iti asmin atre pañca iti pañca saṃkhyā viṣayā aparā pañca saṃkhyā śrūyate pañca śabda dvaya darśaāt te ete pañca pañcakāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ saṃpadyate tayā ca pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyayā yāvataḥ saṃkhyeyā ākāṅkṣyate tāvatī eva ca sāṃkhyaiḥ saṃkhyāyate mūlaprakṛtiḥ avikṛtiḥ mahat ādyāḥ prakṛti vikṛtayaḥ sapta ṣoḍaśakaḥ ca a prakṛtiḥ a vikṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ iti tayā śruti prasiddhayā pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyayā teṣām smṛti prasiddhāām pañcaviṃśateḥ tattvāām upasaṃgrahāt prāptam puas śrutimat tvam eva pradhā ādīām tatas brūmaḥ a saṃkhyā upasaṃgrahāt api pradhā ādīām śrutimat tvam pratyāśā kartavyā kasmāt ā abhāvāt ā hi etāi pañcaviṃśatiḥ tattvāi ā eṣām pañcaśas pañcaśas sādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ asti pañcaviṃśateḥ atarāle parāḥ pañca pañca saṃkhyāḥ a hi dvi tva ādikāḥ saṃkhyāḥ atha ucyeta pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyā eva iyam avayava dvāreṇa lakṣyate yathā pañca sapta ca varṣāṇi a vavarṣa śatakratuḥ iti dvādaśa vārṣikīm aāvṛṣṭim kathayati tadvat iti tat api opapadyate ayam eva asmi pakṣe doṣaḥ yat lakṣaṇa āśrayaṇīyā syāt paraḥ ca atra pañca śabdaḥ samastaḥ iti bhāṣika svareṇa eka pada tva aiścayāt prayoga atare ca tvā iti aikapadya ekasvarya eka vibhaktika tva avagamāt samasta tvāt ca a vīpsā pañca pañca iti tea a pañcaka dvaya grahaṇam pañca pañca iti a ca pañca saṃkhyāyāḥ ekasyāḥ pañca saṃkhyayā parayā viśeṣaṇam pañca pañcakāḥ iti upasarja asya eva puraḥ pañca saṃkhyayā viśeṣyamāṇāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ pratyeṣyate yathā pañca pañca pūlyaḥ iti pañcaviṃśatiḥ pūlāḥ pratīyate tadvat ā iti brūmaḥ yuktam yat pañca pūlī śabdasya samāhāra abhiprāya tvāt kati iti satyām bheda ākāṅkṣāyām pañca pañca pūlyaḥ iti viśeṣaṇam iha tu pañca iti āditas eva bheda upādāāt kati iti asatyām bheda ākāṅkṣāyām pañca pañca jaāḥ iti viśeṣaṇam bhavet bhavat api idam viśeṣaṇam pañca saṃkhyāyāḥ eva bhavet tatra ca uktaḥ doṣaḥ tasmāt pañca iti a pañcaviṃśati tattva abhiprāyam atirekāt ca a pañcaviṃśati tattva abhiprāyam atirekaḥ hi bhavati ātma ākāśābhyām pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyāyāḥ ātmā tāvat iha pratiṣṭhām yasmi iti saptamī sūcitasya tam eva mayaḥ ātmā iti ātma tve ākarṣaṇāt ātmā ca puruṣaḥ sa ca pañcaviṃśati avatargataḥ eva iti tasya eva ādhāra tvam ādheya tvam ca yujyeta artha atara parigrahe vā tattva saṃkhyā atirekaḥ siddhāta viruddhaḥ prasajyeta tathā ākāśaḥ ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti ākāśasya api pañcaviṃśata avatargatasya yāyyam artha atara parigrahe ca uktam dūṣaṇam katham ca saṃkhyā mātra śravaṇe satya śrutāām pañcaviṃśati tattvāām upasaṃgrahaḥ pratīyeta jaa śabdasya tattveṣu arūḍha tvāt artha atara upasaṃgrahe api saṃkhyā upapatteḥ katham tarhi pañca pañcajaāḥ iti ucyate diś saṃkhye saṃjñāyām iti viśeṣa smaraṇāt saṃjñāyām eva pañca śabdasya samāsaḥ tatas ca rūḍha tva abhiprāyeṇa eva kecid vivakṣyate a sāṃkhya tattva abhiprāyeṇa te kati iti asyām ākāṅkṣāyām puaḥ pañca iti prayujyate ye kecid te ca pañca eva iti arthaḥ sapta ṛṣayaḥ sapta iti yathā ke te pañcajaāḥ tat ucyate prāṇa ādayaḥ vākya śeṣāt yasmin pañca pañcajaāḥ iti atas uttarasmin atre brahma svarūpaiḥ ūpaṇāya prāṇa ādayaḥ pañca prāṇasya prāṇam uta cakṣuṣaḥ cakṣuḥ uta śrotrasya ye maasaḥ viduḥ iti te tra vākya śeṣa gatāḥ vivakṣyate katham puas prāṇa ādiṣu tattveṣu vā katham tu prasiddhi atikrame vākya śeṣa vaśāt prāṇa ādayaḥ eva grahītavyāḥ bhavati prāṇa ādayaḥ jaa śabda bhājaḥ bhavati puruṣa śabdaḥ prāṇeṣu prayuktaḥ te vai ete pañca brahma puruṣāḥ iti atra prāṇaḥ ha pitā prāṇaḥ ha mātā ityādi ca brāhmaṇam samāsa balāt ca samudāyasya rūḍha tvam aviruddham katham puara sati prathama prayoge rūḍhiḥ śakyā āśrayitum śakyā udbhid ādi vat iti āha hi aprasiddha arthaḥ śabdaḥ samabhivyāhārāt tad viṣayaḥ yathā udbhidā yajeta yūpam vedim karoti iti tathā ayam api pañcajaa śabdaḥ saṃjñā bhāvaḥ saṃjñī ākāṅkṣī vākya śeṣa samabhivyāhṛteṣu prāṇa ādiṣu vartiṣyate kaiścid tu devāḥ pitaraḥ asurāḥ rakṣāṃsi ca pañca pañcajaāḥ vyākhyātāḥ ayaiḥ ca catvāraḥ varṇāḥ iṣāda pañcamāḥ parigṛhītāḥ kvacid ca yat pāñcajayayā viśā iti prajā paraḥ prayogaḥ pañcajaa śabdasya dṛśyate tad parigrahe api iha a kaścid virodhaḥ ācāryaḥ tu a pañcaviṃśateḥ tattvāām iha pratītiḥ asti iti evaṃpara tayā prāṇa ādayaḥ vākyaśeṣāt iti jagāda bhaveyuḥ tāvat prāṇa ādayaḥ mādhyaṃdiāām prāṇa ādiṣu kāṇvāām tu katham prāṇa ādayaḥ pañca jaāḥ bhaveyuḥ prāṇa ādiṣu iti atas uttaram paṭhati asatī api jyotiṣā teṣām pañca saṃkhyā pūryeta te api hi iti atas pūrvasmin atre brahma svarūpaiḥ ūpaṇāya eva jyotiḥ adhīyate tat devāḥ jyotiṣām jyotiḥ iti katham puar ubhayeṣām api tulya vat idam jyotiḥ paṭhyamāam pañca saṃkhyayā keṣāṃcid gṛhyate apekṣā bhedāt iti āha mādhyaṃdiāām hi jyotiṣi apekṣā bhavati tad alābhāt tu kāṇvāām bhavati apekṣā apekṣā bhedāt ca matre jyotiṣaḥ grahaṇa agrahaṇe yathā grahaṇa agrahaṇe tadvat tat evam tāvat śruti prasiddhiḥ kācid pradhā aviṣayā asti smṛti yāya prasiddhī tu parihariṣyete ca ākāśa ādiṣu yathā vyapadiṣṭa ukteḥ kāraṇa tva adhikaraṇam pratipāditam brahmaṇaḥ lakṣaṇam pratipāditam brahma viṣayam gati sāmāyam pratipāditam ca pradhā asya aśabda tvam tatra idam aparam āśaṅkyate a jama ādi kāraṇatvam brahmaṇaḥ brahma viṣayam vā gati sāmāyam pratipādayitum śakyam kasmāt sṛṣṭiḥ upalabhyate krama ādi vaicitryāt tathā hi kvacid ātman ā ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti ākāśa ādikā sṛṣṭiḥ āmāyate kvacid tejaḥ ādikā tat tejaḥ sṛjataḥ iti kvacid prāṇa ādikā sa prāṇam asṛjata prāṇāt śraddhām iti kvacid akrameṇa eva sa imān lokāḥ asṛjata ambhaḥ marīcīḥ maramā apaḥ iti tathā kvacid asat pūrvikā sṛṣṭiḥ paṭhyate asat vai idam agre āsīt tatas vai sat ajāyata iti asat eva idam agre āsīt tat sat āsīt tat samabhavat iti ca kvacid asat vādaiḥ ākaraṇe a sat pūrvikā prakriyā pratijñāyate tat ha eke āhuḥ asat eva idam agre āsīt iti upakramya kutas tu khalu somya evam syāt iti ha uvāca katham asataḥ sat jāyeta iti sat tu eva somya idam agre āsīt iti kvacid svayam kartṛkā eva vyākriyā jagataḥ tat ha idam tarhi avyākṛtam āsīt ca vyākriyate iti evam ca vikalpasya aupapatteḥ ca jagat kāraṇa avadhāraṇa para tā yāyyā smṛti yāya prasiddhibhyām tu kāraṇa atara parigrahaḥ yāyyaḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ sati api prativedātam sṛjyamāeṣu ākāśa ādiṣu krama ādi dvārake sraṣṭari kiṃcid vigāam asti kutas yathā vyapadiṣṭa ukteḥ yathābhūtaḥ hi ekasmin vedāte sarvajñaḥ sarva īśvaraḥ sarva ātmā ekaḥ dvitīyaḥ vyapadiṣṭaḥ tathābhūtaḥ eva vyapadiśyate tat yathā satyam brahma iti atra tāvat pareṇa ca tad viṣayeṇa brahma brahma brahma sarveṣām atas bahu syām prajāyeya iti ca ātma viṣayeṇa vikārāṇām sraṣṭuḥ abhedam abhāṣata tathā idam sarvam asṛjata yat idam kim ca iti samasta jagat sṛṣṭi nirdeśea prāk sṛṣṭeḥ advitīyam sraṣṭāram ācaṣṭe tat atra yat lakṣaṇam brahma vijñātam tat lakṣaṇam eva a yatra api vijñāyate sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam tat aikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya iti tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti tathā ātmā vai idam ekaḥ eva agre āsīt miṣat saḥ īkṣata lokau sṛjai iti ca evaṃjātīyakasya vākya jātasya kvacid ākāśa ādikā sṛṣṭiḥ kvacid tejaḥ ādikā iti evaṃjātīyakam ca kārya viṣayeṇa kāraṇam api brahma bhavitum arhati iti śakyate vaktum atiprasaṅgāt samādhāsyati ca ācāryaḥ kārya viṣayam api viyat aśruteḥ iti ārabhya bhavet api kāryasya vigīta tvam apratipādya tvāt a hi ayam sṛṣṭi ādi prapañcaḥ pratipipādayiṣitaḥ a hi tad pratibaddhaḥ kaścid puruṣa arthaḥ dṛśyate śrūyate vā a ca kalpayitum śakyate upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām tatra tatra brahma viṣayaiḥ vākyaiḥ sākam eka vākya tāyāḥ darśayati ca sṛṣṭi ādi prapañcasya brahma pratipatti artha tām somya somya apaḥ mūlam aviccha adbhiḥ somya śuṅgea tejaḥ mūlam aviccha tejasā somya śuṅgea sa mūlam avicchaḥ iti mṛd ādi dṛṣṭātaiḥ ca kāryasya vaditum sṛṣṭi ādi prapañcaḥ śrāvyate iti gamyate tathā ca saṃpradāya vidaḥ vadati mṛd loha visphuliṅga ādyaiḥ sṛṣṭiḥ yā upāyaḥ upāyaḥ bhedaḥ kathaṃca iti brahma pratipatti pratibaddham tu phalam śrūyate brahma vid param tarati śokam ātma vid tam eva viditvā ati mṛtyum eti iti pratyakṣa avagamam ca idam phalam tat tvam asi iti a saṃsāri ātma tva pratipattau satyām saṃsāri ātma tva vyāvṛtteḥ yat puas kāraṇa viṣayam darśitam asat vai idam agre āsīt ityādi tat parihartavyam atra ucyate samākarṣāt asat vai idam agre āsīt iti śrāvyate yatas asau eva sa bhavati asat brahma iti veda ced asti brahma iti ced veda tatas viduḥ iti asat vāda apavāde āstitva lakṣaṇam brahma a maya ādi kośa paramparayā pratyagātmā aṃ dhārya saḥ kāmayate iti tam eva prakṛtam samākṛṣya sa prapañcām sṛṣṭim tasmāt śrāvayitvā tat satyam iti ācakṣate iti ca upasaṃhṛtya tat api eṣa ślokaḥ bhavati iti tasmin eva prakṛta ṛthe ślokam imam udāharati asat vai idam agre āsīt iti yadi tu asaiḥ ātmakam asmin śloke ibhipreyeta udāharaṇāt asaṃbaddham vākyam āpadyeta prāyeṇa sat śabdaḥ prasiddhaḥ iti tad vyākaraṇa abhāva apekṣayā prāk utpatteḥ sat eva brahma asat iva āsīt iti upacaryate eṣā eva asat eva idam agre āsīt iti atra api tat sat āsīt iti samākarṣaṇāt atyata abhāva abhyupagame hi tat sat āsīt iti kim samākṛṣyeta tat ha eke āhuḥ asat eva idam agre āsīt iti atra api a śrutyatara abhiprāyeṇa ayam ekīya mata upayāsaḥ kriyāyām iva vikalpasya asaṃbhavāt tasmāt śruti parigṛhīta sat pakṣa dārḍhyāya eva ayam mada mati parikalpitasya asat pakṣasya iti draṣṭavyam tat ha idam tarhi avyākṛtam āsīt iti atra api a iḥ adhyakṣasya jagataḥ vyākaraṇam kathyate saḥ eṣaḥ iha praviṣṭaḥ ā a kha agrebhyaḥ iti adhyakṣasya vyākṛta kārya samākarṣāt iḥ adhyakṣe vyākaraṇa abhyupagame prakṛta avalambiā samākṛṣyeta cetaasya ca ayam ātmaaḥ śarīra iupraveśaḥ śrūyate aupraviṣṭasya ceta a tva śravaṇāt paśyan cakṣuḥ śrṛṇvan śrotram iti api ca yādṛśam idam adya tve āma rūpābhyām vyākriyamāṇam jagat sādhyakṣam vyākriyate evam ādisarge api iti gamyate dṛṣṭa viparīta kalpa ā upapatteḥ śrutyataram api āma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti sādhyakṣām eva jagataḥ vyākriyām darśayati vyākriyatam iti api karma kartari lakāraḥ sati eva parameśvare vyākartari saukaryam apekṣya draṣṭavyaḥ yathā lūyate kedāraḥ svayam evā iti sati eva pūrṇake lavitari yat vā karmaṇi eva eṣa lakāraḥ ūrtha ākṣiptam kartṛ ataram apekṣya draṣṭavyaḥ yathā gamyate grāmaḥ iti jagat vāci tvāt bālāki adhikaraṇam kauṣītaki brāhmaṇe bālāki ajātaśatru saṃvāde śrūyate yaḥ vai bālākaḥ eteṣām puruṣāṇām kartā yasya vā etat karma sa vai veditavyaḥ iti tatra kim jīvaḥ veditavya tveā upadiśyate uta mukhyaḥ prāṇaḥ uta paramātmā iti viśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam prāṇaḥ iti kutas yasya vā etat karma iti śravaṇāt parispada lakṣaṇasya ca karmaṇaḥ prāṇa āśraya tvāt vākyaśeṣe ca atha asmin prāṇaḥ eva ekadhā bhavati iti prāṇa śabda śravaṇāt prāṇa śabdasya ca mukhye prāṇe prasiddha tvāt ye ca ete āditye puruṣaḥ ca dramasi puruṣaḥ iti evamādayaḥ puruṣāḥ teṣām api bhavati prāṇaḥ kartā prāṇa avasthā viśeṣa tvāt āditya ādi devatā ātmaām katamaḥ ekaḥ devaḥ iti prāṇaḥ iti sa brahma tyad iti ācakṣate iti śruti atara prasiddheḥ jīvaḥ vā ayam iha veditavya tayā upadiśyate tasya api dharma adharma lakṣaṇam karma śakyate śrāvayitum yasya vā etat karma iti saḥ upi bhoktṛ tvāt bhoga upakaraṇa bhūtāām eteṣām puruṣāṇām ca kartā upapadyate vākyaśeṣe jīva liṅgam avagamyate yatkāraṇam veditavya tayā upayastasya puruṣāṇām kartuḥ veda āya upetam bālākim prati bubodhayiṣuḥ ajātaśatruḥ suptam puruṣam āmatrya āmatraṇa śabda aśravaṇāt prāṇa ādīnām bhoktṛ tvam pratibodhya yaṣṭi ghāta utthāpaāt prāṇa ādi vyatiriktam jīvam bhoktāram pratibodhayati tathā parastāt api jīva liṅgam avagamyate tat yathā śreṣṭhī svaiḥ bhuṅkte yathā vā svāḥ bhuñjati evam eva eṣa prajñā ātmā etaiḥ ātmabhiḥ bhuṅkte evam eva ete ātmā etam ātmāam bhuñjati iti prāṇabhṛt tvāt ca jīvasya upapaam prāṇa śabda tvam tasmāt jīva mukhya prāṇayoḥ ayataraḥ iha grahaṇīyaḥ parameśvaraḥ tad liṅga avagamāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ parameśvaraḥ eva ayam eteṣām puruṣāṇām kartā syāt kasmāt upakrama sāmarthyāt iha hi bālākiḥ ajātaśatruṇā saha brahma te bravāṇi saṃvaditum upacakrame sa ca katicid āditya ādi adhikaraṇā puruṣāḥ amukhya brahma dṛṣṭi bhājaḥ uktvā tūṣṇīm babhūva tam ajātaśatruḥ mṛṣā vai khalu mā saṃvadiṣṭhāḥ brahma te bravāṇi iti amukhya brahma vādi tayā apodya tad kartāram ayam veditavya tayā upacikṣepa yadi saḥ u pi amukhya brahma dṛṣṭi bhāj syāt upakramaḥ bādhyeta tasmāt parameśvaraḥ eva ayam bhavitum arhati kartṛ tvam ca eteṣām puruṣāṇām a parameśvarāt ayasya svātatryeṇa avakalpate yasya vā etat karma iti api ā ayam parispada lakṣaṇasya dharma adharma lakṣaṇasya vā karmaṇaḥ irdeśaḥ tayoḥ ayatarasya api aprakṛta tvāt asaṃśabdita tvāt ca ā api puruṣāṇām ayam irdeśaḥ eteṣām puruṣāṇām kartā iti eva teṣām irdiṣṭa tvāt puruṣa viṣayasya karoti arthasya kriyā phalasya vā ayam irdeśaḥ kartṛ śabde eva tayoḥ upātta tvāt pāriśeṣyāt pratyakṣa saṃihitam jagat sarva āma etat śabde irdiśyate kriyate iti ca tat eva jagat karma jagat api aprakṛtam asaṃśabditam ca satyam etat tathā api asati saṃidhāea saṃihita vastu mātrasya ayam irdeśaḥ iti gamyate a viśiṣṭasya pūrvatra ca jagat eka deśa bhūtāām puruṣāṇām viśeṣa upādāāt aviśeṣitam jagat eva iha upādīyate iti gamyate etat uktam bhavati yaḥ eteṣām puruṣāṇām jagat eka deśa bhūtāām kartā viśeṣeṇa yasya vā kṛtsam eva jagat aviśeṣitam karma iti vā śabdaḥ eka deśa avacchia kartṛ tva vyāvṛtti arthaḥ ye brahmatva abhimatāḥ puruṣāḥ kīrtitāḥ teṣām abrahmatva khyāpaāya evam evam ced tat vyākhyātam atha yat uktam vākyaśeṣa gatāt jīva liṅga a mukhya prāṇa liṅgāt ca tayoḥ eva ayatarasya iha grahaṇam yāyyam a parameśvarasya iti tat parihartavyam atra ucyate parihṛtam ca etat opāsā traividhyāt āśrita tvāt iha tad yogāt iti atra trividham hi atra upāsaam evam sati prasajyeta jīva upāsaam mukhya prāṇa upāsaam brahma upāsaam ca iti upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām hi brahma viṣaya tvam asya vākyasya avagamyate tatra upakramasya tāvat brahma viṣaya tvam darśitam upasaṃhārasya api sarveṣām ca bhūtāām śraiṣṭhyam svārājyam ādhipatyam paryeti yaḥ evam veda iti sati a vākya erṇayeta eva idam api vākyam irṇīyeta yasya vā etat karma ityasya brahma viṣaya tvāt tasmāt atra jīva mukhya prāṇa śaṅkā puar utpadyamāā iva ṛtyate prāṇa śabdaḥ api brahma viṣayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ hi somya maaḥ iti atra jīva liṅgam api upakrama upasaṃhārayoḥ brahma viṣaya tvāt abheda abhiprāyeṇa yojayitavyam tu jaimiiḥ api ca evam eke api ca ā eva atra vivaditavyam jīva pradhāam vā idam vākyam syāt brahma pradhāam vā iti jīva parāmarśam brahma pratipatti artham asmin vākye jaimiiḥ ācāryaḥ kasmāt prāṇa ādi vyatirikte jīve pratibodhite puar jīva vyatirikta viṣayaḥ dṛśyate kva eṣa etat bālāke puruṣaḥ ūśayiṣṭa kva vā etat abhūt kutas etat āgāt iti yadā suptaḥ svapam paśyati atha asmi prāṇaḥ eva ekadhā bhavati ityādi etasmāt ātmanaḥ sarve prāṇāḥ yathāyataam vipratiṣṭhate prāṇebhyaḥ devāḥ devebhyaḥ lokāḥ iti ca suṣupti kāle ca pareṇa brahmaṇā jīvaḥ ekatām gacchati parasmāt ca brahmaṇaḥ prāṇa ādikam jagat jāyate iti tasmāt yatra asya jīvasya svāpaḥ upādhi jaita viśeṣa vijñā a rahitam svarūpam yatas tat bhraṃśa rūpam saḥ utra paramātmā veditavya tayā śrāvitaḥ iti gamyate api ca evam eke bālākya jātaśatru saṃvāde spaṣṭam tad vyatiriktam yaḥ eṣa vijñā a mayaḥ puruṣaḥ kva eṣa tadā abhūt kutas etat āgāt iti yaḥ eṣa vijñā a mayaḥ puruṣaḥ kva eṣa tadā abhūt kutas etat āgāt iti yaḥ eṣa utar hṛdaye ākāśaḥ tasmin śete iti ākāśa śabdaḥ ca paramātmai prayuktaḥ daharaḥ smi atara ākāśaḥ iti atra sarve ete ātmā vyuccarati iti ca upādhimatām ātma āmayataḥ vyuccaraṇam āmaataḥ paramātmā aam eva kāraṇa tve āmaati iti gamyate prāṇaiḥ ākaraṇasya api prāṇa ādi vyatirikta upadeśaḥ abhyuccayaḥ vākyāvayāt vākyāvaya adhikaraṇam brṛhadāraṇyake maitreyī brāhmaṇe abhidhīyate a vai are patyuḥ kāmāya iti upakramya a vai are sarvasya kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati ātmā astu kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati ātmā vai are draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ matavyaḥ ididhyāsitavyaḥ vai are darśaea matyā vijñāea idam sarvam viditam iti tatra etat vicikitsyate kim vijñā ātmā eva ayam draṣṭavya śrotavya tva ādi rūpeṇa upadiśyate āhosvit paramātmā iti kutas bhoktrā upakramāt vijñā ātma upadeśaḥ iti pratibhāti bhoktrā upakramāt vijñā ātma upadeśaḥ iti pratibhāti sarva vijñā upadeśāt paramātma upadeśaḥ iti kim tāvat prāptam vijñā ātma upadeśaḥ iti kasmāt upakrama sāmarthyāt pati jāyā putra vitta ādikam hi bhogya bhūtam sarvam jagat ātma artha tayā priyam bhavati iti priya saṃsūcitam bhoktāram ātmāam upakramya idam ātmao syāt madhye pi idam mahat bhūtam aatam apāram a pretya saṃjñā asti iti prakṛtasya eva mahataḥ bhūtasya draṣṭavyasya bhūtebhyaḥ eva idam draṣṭavya tvam darśayati tathā vijñātāram are iti darśayati bhoktṛ artha tvāt bhogya jātasya aupacārikam draṣṭavyam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ paramātma upadeśaḥ eva ayam kasmāt vākya avayāt vākyam hi idam paurvāparyeṇa avekṣyamāṇam paramātmā aam lakṣyate katham iti tat upapādyate amṛta tvasya tu āśāsti iti yājñavalkyāt upaśrutya syām kim aham kuryām yat eva bhagavā aveda tat eva me brūhi iti amṛta tvam āśāsāāyai maitreyyai yājñavalkyaḥ ātma vijñāam upadiśati a ca ayatra paramātma vijñāāt amṛta tvam asti iti śruti smṛti vādāḥ vadati tathā ca sarva vijñāam ucyamāam tatra ca etat aupacārikam āśrayitum śakyam yat kāraṇam sarva vijñāam tat eva upapādayati brahma tam parādāt yaḥ yatra ātmā brahma veda ityādiā yaḥ hi svātatryeṇa labdha sadbhāvam paśyati tam mithyādarśiam tat eva mithyādṛṣṭam brahma kṣatra ādikam jagat parākaroti iti bheda dṛṣṭim apodya idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā iti sarvasya vastu jātasya ātmā a vyatirekam avatārayati dudubhi ādi dṛṣṭātaiḥ ca tam eva a vyatirekam draḍhayati asya mahataḥ bhūtasya ca prakṛtasya ātmanaḥ āma rūpa karma prapañca kāraṇatām vyācakṣāṇaḥ gamayati tathā eva ekāyaa prakriyāyām api sa viṣayasya sa idriyasya sa ataḥkaraṇasya prapañcasya kṛtsam prajñā aghaam vyācakṣāṇaḥ gamayati tasmāt paramātmaaḥ eva ayam darśa ādi upadeśaḥ iti gamyate yat puar uktam priya saṃsūcita upakramāt vijñā ātmaaḥ eva ayam darśa ādi upadeśaḥ iti atra brūmaḥ pratijñā siddheḥ liṅgam āśmarathyaḥ asti atra pratijñā vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā iti ca tasyāḥ pratijñāyāḥ siddhim sūcayati etat liṅgam yat priya saṃsūcitasya ātmanaḥ draṣṭavya tva ādi saṃkīrtaam yadi hi vijñāātmā paramātma oyaḥ syāt tatas vijñāātmā vijñāyate iti yat pratijñātam tat hīyeta tasmāt pratijñā siddhi artham vijñāātma paramātmaoḥ abheda aṃśe upakramaṇam iti āśmarathyaḥ ācāryaḥ utkramiṣyate evambhāvāt iti auḍulomiḥ eva deha idriya maaḥ buddhi saṃghāta upādhi saṃparkāt kaluṣībhūtasya deha ādi saṃghātāt utkramiṣyataḥ paramātma aikya upapatteḥ idam abhedena upakramaṇam iti auḍulomiḥ ācāryaḥ mayate śrutiḥ ca evam bhavati eṣa saṃprasādaḥ smāt śarīrāt samutthāya param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svea rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate iti kvacid ca jīva āśrayam api āma rūpam jñāpayati yathā adyaḥ samudre staṃgacchati āma rūpe vihāya tathā vidvāḥ āma rūpāt vimuktaḥ parāt param puruṣam upaiti divyam iti yathā loke adyaḥ sva āśrayam eva āma rūpam vihāya samudram upayati evam jīvaḥ api sva āśrayam eva āma rūpam vihāya param puruṣam upaiti iti hi tatra arthaḥ pratīyate dṛṣṭāta dārṣṭātikayoḥ tulya tāyai avasthiteḥ iti kāśakṛtsaḥ asya eva idam abhede upakramaṇam iti kāśakṛtsaḥ ācāryaḥ tathā ca brāhmaṇam āma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti evaṃjātīyakam parasya eva ātmanaḥ jīva bhāve avasthāam darśayati ca sarvāṇi rūpāṇi vicitya kṛtvā abhivada yat āste iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ ca tejaḥ prabhṛtīām sṛṣṭau jīvasya pṛthak sṛṣṭiḥ śrutāḥ parasmāt ātma oyaḥ tad vikāraḥ jīvaḥ syāt kāśakṛtsasya ācāryasya avikṛtaḥ parameśvaraḥ jīvaḥ āyaḥ iti matam āśmarathyasya tu yadi api jīvasya parasmāt aaya tvam abhipretam tathā api pratijñā siddheḥ iti sāpekṣa tva abhidhāāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ kiyā api abhipretaḥ iti gamyate auḍulomi pakṣe spaṣṭam eva avasthā tara apekṣau bheda abhedau gamyete tatra kāśakṛtsīyam matam śruti ausārī iti gamyate tattvam asi ityādi śrutibhyaḥ evam ca sati amṛta tvam avakalpate vikāra ātmaka tve hi vikārasya prakṛti saṃbadhe pralaya prasaṅgāḥ a tajjñāāt amṛta tvam avakalpeta atas ca sva āśrayasya āma rūpasya asaṃbhavāt upādhi āśrayam āma rūpam jīve upacaryate atas eva utpattiḥ api jīvasya kvacid śrāvyamāṇā upādhi āśrayā eva veditavyā yat api uktam prakṛtasya eva mahataḥ bhūtasya draṣṭavyasya bhūtebhyaḥ eva idam draṣṭavya tvam darśayati iti tatra api iyam eva tri sūtrī yojayitavyā pratijñā siddheḥ liṅgam āśmarathyaḥ idam atra pratijñātam vidite sarvam idam viditam bhavati idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā iti ca upapāditam ca sarvasya āma rūpa karma prapañcasya eka prasava tvāt eka pralaya tvāt ca dudubhi ādi dṛṣṭātaiḥ ca kārya kāraṇayoḥ tasyāḥ eva pratijñāyāḥ siddhim sūcayati etat liṅgam mahataḥ bhūtasya bhūtebhyaḥ kathitam iti āśmarathyaḥ ācāryaḥ abhede hi sati sarva vijñāam pratijñātam avakalpate iti utkramiṣyataḥ evaṃbhāvāt iti auḍulomiḥ utkramiṣyataḥ pareṇa ātma aikya saṃbhavāt idam abheda abhidhāam iti auḍulomiḥ ācāryaḥ mayate avasthiteḥ iti kāśakṛtsaḥ asya eva idam abheda abhidhāam iti kāśakṛtsaḥ ācāryaḥ mayate etat etebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ samutthāya a pretya saṃjñā asti iti katham etat a bheda abhidhāam doṣaḥ etat ātma uccheda abhiprāyam atra eva mā bhagavā amūmuha a pretya saṃjñā asti iti paryauyujya svayam eva śrutyā arthātarasya darśita tvāt a vā are ham moham bravīmi vā are yam ātmā a ucchitti dharmā mātrā saṃsargaḥ tu asya bhavati iti etat uktam bhavati kūṭasthaityaḥ eva ayam ātmā sti mātrābhiḥ tu asya bhūta idriya lakṣaṇābhiḥ avidyā kṛtābhiḥ a saṃsargaḥ vidyayā bhavati saṃsarga abhāve ca tad kṛtasya viśeṣa vijñāasya abhāvāt a pretya saṃjñā asti iti uktam iti yat api uktam vijñātāram are iti śabdeā upasaṃhārāt vijñāātmaaḥ eva idam draṣṭavyam iti tat api pariharaṇīyam api ca yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tat itaraḥ itaram paśyati iti ārabhya avidyā viṣaye tasya eva darśa ādi lakṣaṇam viśeṣa vijñāam prapañcya yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kam paśyet iti ādiā vidyā viṣaye tasya eva darśa ādi lakṣaṇasya viśeṣa vijñāasya abhāvam abhidadhāti ca viṣaya abhāve pi ātmāam vijāīyāt iti āśaṅkya vijñātāram are vijāīyāt iti āha tatas ca viśeṣa vijñā abhāva upapāda a para tvāt vākyasya vijñāa dhātuḥ eva kevalaḥ sa bhūta pūrva gatyā iti gamyate darśitam tu purastāt kāśakṛtsīyasya pakṣasya śrutimat tvam atas ca vijñā ātma paramātmaoḥ avidyā pratyupasthāpita āma rūpa racita deha ādi upādhi nimittaḥ bhedaḥ avidyā pāramārthikaḥ iti eṣaḥ rthaḥ sarvaiḥ vedātavādibhiḥ abhyupagatavyaḥ sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam ātmā eva idam sarvam brahmā eva idam sarvam idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā sti draṣṭā atas sti draṣṭṛ iti evaṃrūpābhyaḥ śrutibhyaḥ smṛtibhyaḥ ca vāsudevaḥ sarvam iti kṣetrajñam ca api mām viddhi sarva kṣetreṣu bhārata samam sarveṣu bhūteṣu tiṣṭhatam parameśvaram iti evaṃrūpābhyaḥ bheda darśa apavādāt ca ayaḥ sau ayaḥ ham asmi iti a sa veda yathā paśuḥ mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum yaḥ iha ā eva paśyati iti evaṃjātīyakāt sa vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ ātmā ajaraḥ maraḥ mṛtaḥ brahma iti ca sarva vikriyā pratiṣedhāt ayathā ca mumukṣūṇām ca hi vijñāam sarva ākāṅkṣā aivartakam ātma viṣayam iṣyate iti ca śruteḥ tatra kaḥ mohaḥ kaḥ śokaḥ eka tvam aupaśyataḥ iti ca sthita prajña lakṣaṇa smṛteḥ ca sthite ca kṣetrajña param ātma eka tva viṣaye samyak darśae kṣetrajñaḥ paramātmā iti āma mātra bhedāt kṣetrajñaḥ yam paramātmā paramātmā ayam kṣetrajñāt iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ ātma bheda viṣayaḥ yam ekaḥ hi ayam ātmā bahudhā abhidhīyate iti a hi satyam jñāam brahma yaḥ veda ihitam guhāyām iti kāṃcid eva ekām guhām adhikṛtya etat uktam a ca brahmaṇaḥ yaḥ guhāyām sti tat sṛṣṭvā tat eva auprāviśat iti sraṣṭuḥ eva praveśa śravaṇāt ye tu kurvati te śreyaḥ uddhāram samyak darśam eva bādhate kṛtakam aityam ca mokṣam kalpayati ca a saṃgacchate iti prakṛtiḥ ca pratijñā dṛṣṭātā uparodhāt prakṛti adhikaraṇam yathā abhyudaya hetu tvāt dharmaḥ jijñāsyaḥ evam iḥśreyasa hetu tvāt brahma api jijñāsyam iti uktam brahma ca yatas iti lakṣitam tat ca lakṣaṇam ghaṭa rucaka ādīām mṛd suvarṇa ādi vat prakṛti tve kulāla suvarṇakāra ādi vaimitta tve ca bhavati vimarśaḥ kimātmakam puar brahmaṇaḥ kāraṇatvam syāt iti tatra imittakāraṇam eva tāvat kevalam syāt iti pratibhāti kasmāt īkṣā pūrvaka kartṛ tva śravaṇāt īkṣā pūrvakam hi brahmaṇaḥ kartṛ tvam avagamyate saḥ īkṣāṃcakre sa prāṇam asṛjata ityādi śrutibhyaḥ īkṣā pūrvakam ca kartṛ tvam imittakāraṇeṣu eva kulāla ādiṣu dṛṣṭam ca kriyā phala siddhiḥ loke dṛṣṭā sa ca ādi kartari api yuktaḥ saṃkramayitum īśvara tva prasiddheḥ ca īśvarāṇām hi imitta kāraṇa tvam eva kevalam pratīyate tadvat parameśvarasya api imitta kāraṇa tvam eva yuktam pratipattum kāryam ca idam jagat sāvayavam acetaam aśuddham ca dṛśyate kāraṇe api tasya bhavitavyam kārya kāraṇayoḥ sārūpya darśaāt brahma ca a evaṃlakṣaṇam avagamyate iṣkalam iṣkriyam śātam iravadyam irañjaam ityādi śrutibhyaḥ pāriśeṣyāt brahmaṇaḥ yat upādāakāraṇam aśuddhi ādi guṇakam smṛti prasiddham abhyupagatavyam brahma kāraṇatva śruteḥ imitta tva mātre paryavasāāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ prakṛtiḥ ca upādāakāraṇam ca brahma abhyupagatavyam imitta kāraṇam ca a kevalam imitta kāraṇam eva kasmāt pratijñā dṛṣṭātā uparodhāt evam hi pratijñā dṛṣṭātau śrautau pratijñā tāvat uta tam ādeśam aprākṣyaḥ ye aśrutam śrutam bhavati amatam matam avijñātam vijñātam iti tatra ca eke vijñātea sarvam ayat avijñātam api vijñātam bhavati iti pratīyate tat ca upādā kāraṇa vijñāe saṃbhavati upādā kāraṇa a vyatirekāt kāryasya imitta kāraṇa a vyatirekaḥ tu kāryasya loke takṣṇaḥ prāsāda vyatireka darśaāt yathā somya sarvam mṛ mayam vijñātam syāt vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ āmadheyam mṛttikā iti eva satyam iti upādā akāraṇa gocaraḥ tathā sarvam loha mayam vijñātam syāt sarvam kārṣṇāyasam vijñātam syāt iti ca tathā yatra api bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati iti pratijñā yathā pṛthivyām oṣadhayaḥ saṃbhavati iti dṛṣṭātaḥ tathā khalvare dṛṣṭe śrute mate vijñāte idam sarvam viditam iti pratijñā sa yathā dudubheḥ hayamāasya bāhyān śabdān śakuyāt grahaṇāya dudubheḥ tu dudubhyā ghātasya vā śabdaḥ gṛhītaḥ iti dṛṣṭātaḥ evam yathāsaṃbhavam pratijñā dṛṣṭātau prakṛti tva sādhaau pratyetavyau yatas iti iyam api pañcamī yatas vā imāi bhūtāi jāyate iti atra prakṛtiḥ iti viśeṣa smaraṇāt prakṛti lakṣaṇe eva apādāe draṣṭavyāḥ imitta tvam tu adhiṣṭhātratara abhāvāt adhigatavyam yathā hi loke mṛd suvarṇa ādikam upādā akāraṇam kulāla suvarṇakāra ādi adhiṣṭhātṛ apekṣya pravartate brahmaṇaḥ upādā akāraṇasya brahmaṇaḥ upādā akāraṇasya prāk utpatteḥ ekam eva advitīyam iti avadhāraṇāt adhiṣṭhātṛ atara abhāvaḥ api veditavyaḥ adhiṣṭhātari hi sarva vijñānasya asaṃbhavāt pratijñādṛṣṭāta uparodhaḥ eva syāt tasmāt adhiṣṭhātṛ atara abhāvāt ātmaaḥ kartṛ tvam upādāātara abhāvāt ca prakṛti tvam kutas ca ātmaaḥ kartṛ tva prakṛti tve abhidhyā upadeśāt ca abhidhyā upadeśaḥ ca ātmaaḥ kartṛ tva prakṛti tve gamayati sā u kāmayata bahu syām prajāyeya iti tat aikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya iti ca tatra abhidhyā a pūrvikāyāḥ svātatrya pravṛtteḥ kartā iti gamyate bahu syām iti pratyagātma viṣaya tvāt bahu bhava abhidhyā asya prakṛtiḥ iti api gamyate sākṣāt prakṛti tvasya ayam abhyuccayaḥ itas ca prakṛtiḥ brahma yat kāraṇam sākṣāt brahma eva kāraṇam upādāya ubhau prabhava pralayau āmāyete sarvāṇi ha vai imāi bhūtāya ākāśāt eva samutpadyate ākāśam pratyastam yati iti yat hi yasmāt prabhavati yasmin ca pralīyate tat tasya upādāam prasiddham yathā vrīhi yava ādīām pṛthivī sākṣāt iti ca sūcayati ākāśāt eva iti prati asta mayaḥ ca kāryasya dṛṣṭaḥ ātma kṛteḥ pariṇāmāt itas ca prakṛtiḥ brahma yatkāraṇam brahma prakriyāyām tat ātmā am svayam akuruta iti ātmanaḥ karma tvam kartṛ tvam ca darśayati ātman am iti karma tvam
