svayam akuruta iti kartṛ tvam katham puas pūrva siddhasya sataḥ vyavasthitasya kriyamāṇa tvam śakyam saṃpādayitum pariṇāmāt iti brūmaḥ pūrva siddhaḥ api hi sa ātmā viśeṣeṇa vikāra ātmā pariṇamayāmāsa ātmā am iti ca pariṇāmaḥ mṛd ādyāsu prakṛtiṣu upalabdhaḥ svayam iti ca pratīyate pariṇāmāt iti vā pṛthak sūtram tasya eṣa ṛthaḥ itas ca prakṛtiḥ brahma yatkāraṇam brahmaṇaḥ eva ca pariṇāmaḥ sat ca tyad ca abhavaiḥ uktam ca iti ādi eti ca hi gīyate itas ca prakṛtiḥ brahma yatkāraṇam brahma yoiḥ iti api paṭhyate kartāram īśam puruṣam brahmayoim iti yat bhūtayoim paripaśyati dhīrāḥ iti ca yoi śabdaḥ ca prakṛti vacaḥ samadhigataḥ loke pṛthivī iti strī yoeḥ api asti eva avayava dvāreṇa garbham prati upādā kāraṇa tvam yoi śabdaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti vākya śeṣāt tu atra prakṛtivacaatā parigṛhyate yathā ūrṇaābhiḥ sṛjate gṛhṇate ca iti evaṃjātīyakāt tat evam prakṛti tvam brahmaṇaḥ prasiddham yat puar idam uktam īkṣā pūrvakam kartṛ tvam imitta kāraṇeṣu eva kulāla ādiṣu loke dṛṣṭam tat pratyucyate a loka vat iha bhavitavyam hi ayam aumā agamyaḥ ṛthaḥ śabda gamya tvāt tu asya arthasya yathāśabdam iha bhavitavyam śabdaḥ ca īkṣituḥ īśvarasya prakṛti tvam pratipādayati iti avocāma puas ca etat sarvam vistareṇa prativakṣyāmaḥ sarve vyākhyātāḥ vyākhyātāḥ sarva vyākhyā adhikaraṇam īkṣateḥ āśabdam iti ārabhya pradhā a kāraṇa vādaḥ sūtraiḥ eva puas puas āśaṅkyaḥ irākṛtaḥ tasya hi pakṣasya upodbalakāi kāicid liṅga ābhāsāi mada matī prati bhāti iti sa ca kārya kāraṇa āaya tva abhyupagamāt pratyāsaḥ vedāta vādasya devala prabhṛtibhiḥ ca kaiścid dharmasūtra kāraiḥ sva gratheṣu āśritaḥ tad pratiṣedhe eva tīva kṛtaḥ āṇu ādi kāraṇavāda pratiṣedhe te tu brahma kāraṇavāda pakṣasya pratipakṣa tvāt pratiṣeddhavyāḥ teṣām api upodbalakam vaidikam kiṃcid liṅgam mada matī prati bhāyāt iti atas sarve ṇu ādi kāraṇavādāḥ api pratiṣiddha tayā vyākhyātāḥ veditavyāḥ teṣām api pradhā a vat aśabda tvāt śabda virodhi tvāt ca iti vyākhyātāḥ vyākhyātāḥ iti pada abhyāsaḥ dhyāya parisamāptim dyotayati iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye prathamaḥ dhyāyaḥ murat dvitīyaḥ udhyāyaḥ prathamaḥ pādaḥ smṛti a avakāśa doṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti āya smṛti a avakāśa doṣa prasaṅgāt smṛti adhikaraṇam yat uktam brahma eva sarvajñam jagataḥ kāraṇam iti tat ayuktam kutas smṛti a avakāśa doṣa prasaṅgāt smṛtiḥ ca tatra ākhyā parama ṛṣi praṇītā śiṣṭa parigṛhītāḥ ayāḥ ca tad ausāriṇyaḥ smṛtayaḥ tāḥ evam sati a avakāśāḥ prasajyera tāsu hi a cetaam pradhāam svatatram jagataḥ kāraṇam mava ādi smṛtayaḥ tāvat artham samarpayatyaḥ sa avakāśā bhavati asya varṇasya asmi kāle īdṛśaḥ ca ācāraḥ ittham ittham samāvarta ittham saha dharmacāriṇī saṃyogaḥ iti tathā puruṣa arthān catur varṇa āśrama dharmāḥ vidadhati evam kāpila ādi smṛtīām auṣṭheye viṣaye avakāśaḥ sti mokṣa sādhaam eva hi samyak darśaam adhikṛtya tāḥ praṇītāḥ yadi tatra api a avakāśāḥ syuḥ āarthakyam eva āsām prasajyeta vyākhyātavyāḥ katham puar īkṣati ādibhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ brahmā eva sarvajñam jagataḥ kāraṇam iti avadhāritaḥ śruti arthaḥ ākṣipyate bhavet ayam ākṣepaḥ svatatra prajñāām paratatra prajñāḥ tu prāyeṇa svātatryeṇa śruti artham avadhārayitum a śakuvataḥ prakhyāta praṇetṛkāsu smṛtiṣu avalambera ca śruti artham pratipitsera asmad kṛte ca vyākhyāe a viśvasyuḥ bahu māāt smṛtīām praṇetṛṣu kapila prabhṛtīām ca ārṣam jñāam a pratihatam smaryate śrutiḥ ca bhavati ṛṣim prasūtam kapilam yaḥ tam agre bibharti jāyamāam ca paśyet iti tasmai ā eṣām matam ayathārtham śakyam saṃbhāvayitum tarka avaṣṭambhe ca te ṛtham pratiṣṭhāpayati tasmāt api vyākhyeyāḥ iti ākṣepaḥ tasya samādhiḥ āya smṛtya avakāśa doṣa prasaṅgāt iti yadi smṛti a avakāśa doṣa prasaṅge īśvara kāraṇa vādaḥ ākṣipyeta evam api ayāḥ smṛtayaḥ avakāśāḥ prasajyera tāḥ udāhariṣyāmaḥ yad tat sūkṣmam avijñeyam iti param brahma prakṛtya sa hi atarātmā bhūtāām kṣetrajñaḥ ca iti kathyate iti ca uktvā tasmāt avyaktam triguṇam dvijasattama iti āha tathā yatra api avyaktam puruṣe brahmaiḥ guṇe saṃpralīyate iti āha atas ca saṃkṣepam imam śrṛṇudhvam ārāyaṇaḥ sarvam idam purāṇaḥ sa sarga kāle ca karoti sargam saṃhāra kāle ca tat atti bhūyas iti purāṇe bhagavadgītāsu ca aham kṛtsasya jagataḥ prabhavaḥ pralayaḥ tathā iti eva ca prakṛtyā āpastambaḥ paṭhati tasmāt kāyāḥ prabhavati sarve sa mūlam śāśvatikaḥ saḥ ityaḥ iti evam aekaśas smṛtiṣu api īśvaraḥ ca prakāśyate smṛti bale a eva uttaram pravakṣyāmi iti darśitam tu śrutīām īśvara kāraṇa vādam prati tātparyam vipratipattau ca smṛtīām avaśya kartavye yatara parigrahe yatara parityāge ca śruti ausāriṇyaḥ smṛtayaḥ pramāṇam a apekṣyāḥ itarāḥ tat uktam pramāṇa lakṣaṇe virodhe tu aapekṣam syāt asati hi iti atareṇa kaścid upalabhate iti śakyam saṃbhāvayitum imitta abhāvāt śakyam kapila ādīām siddhāām apratihata jñāa tvāt iti ced a siddheḥ api sa apekṣa tvāt hi siddhiḥ sa ca dharmaḥ codaā lakṣaṇaḥ tatas ca pūrva siddhāyāḥ codaāyāḥ śakyate siddha vyapāśraya kalpaāyām api bahu tvāt siddhāām pradarśitā prakāreṇa smṛti vipratipattau satyām a śruti vyapāśrayāt ayaḥ irṇaya kāraṇam asti paratatra prajñasya api ākasmāt smṛti viśeṣa viṣayaḥ pakṣapātaḥ yuktaḥ kasyacid kvacid pakṣapāte sati puruṣam ati vaiśvarūpyeṇa tattva avyavasthā aprasaṅgāt tasmāt tasya api smṛti vipratipatti upayāse ca sa mārge prajñā saṃgrahaṇīyā yā tu śrutiḥ kapilasya jñā atiśayam pradarśayatī pradarśitā tayā śruti viruddham api kāpilam matam śraddhātum śakyam kapilam iti śruti sāma āya mātra tvāt ayasya ca kapilasya sagara putrāṇām prataptuḥ smaraṇāt ca prāpti rahitasya a sādhaka tvāt bhavati ca āyā maoḥ māhātmyam prakhyāpayatī śrutiḥ yat vai kiṃca mauḥ avadat tat bheṣajam iti ca sarva bhūteṣu ca ātmāam sarva bhūtāi ca ātmai saṃpaśyaḥ ātma yājī vai svārājyam adhigacchati iti sarva ātma tva darśaam praśaṃsatā kāpilam matam idyate iti gamyate kapilaḥ hi ātma bheda abhyupagamāt mahābhārate api ca bahavaḥ puruṣāḥ brahma uta aho eke eva tu iti vicārya bahavaḥ puruṣāḥ rāja sāṃkhya yoga vicāriṇām iti para pakṣam upayasya tat bahūām puruṣāṇām hi yathā ekā ucyate tathā tam puruṣam viśvam ākhyāsyāmi guṇa adhikam iti upakramya ātmā tava ca ye ca āye dehi saṃjñitāḥ sarveṣām sākṣi bhūtaḥ a grāhyaḥ kaścid kvacid viśvamūrdhā viśva bhujaḥ viśva pāda akṣiāsikaḥ ekaḥ carati bhūteṣu svaira cārī yathāsukham iti sarva ātmatā eva śrutiḥ ca sarva ātmatāyām bhavati sarvāṇi bhūtāni ātmā eva abhūt tatra kaḥ mohaḥ kaḥ śokaḥ eka tvam aupaśyataḥ iti evaṃvidhāḥ atas ca siddham ātma bheda kalpaayā api kāpilasya tatrasya ca a kevalam sva tatra prakṛti kalpaayā eva iti vedasya hi svārthe prāmāṇyam raveḥ iva rūpa viṣaye puruṣa vacasām tu mūla atara apekṣam vaktṛ smṛti vyavahitam ca iti viprakarṣaḥ tasmāt veda viruddhe viṣaye doṣaḥ kutas ca smṛti a avakāśa doṣa prasaṅgaḥ doṣaḥ itareṣām ca aupalabdheḥ pradhā itarāṇi smṛtau kalpitāi mahat ādīi vede loke ca upalabhyate bhūta idriyāṇi tāvat loka veda prasiddha tvāt śakyate smartum a loka veda prasiddha tvāt tu mahat ādīām ṣaṣṭhasya iva idriya arthasya smṛtiḥ avakalpate yat api kvacid tatparam iva śravaṇam avabhāsate tat api atatparam vyākhyātam āumāikam api ekeṣām iti atra kārya smṛteḥ aprāmāṇyāt kāraṇa smṛteḥ api aprāmāṇyam yuktam iti abhiprāyaḥ tasmāt api doṣaḥ tarka avaṣṭambham tu a vilakṣaṇa tvāt iti ārabhya umathiṣyati yogaḥ pratyuktaḥ yoga pratyukti adhikaraṇam yoga smṛtiḥ api pratyākhyātā draṣṭavyā iti atidiśati tatra api śruti virodhe svatatram eva kāraṇam mahat ādīi ca kāryāṇi a loka veda prasiddhāi kalpyate evam sati pūrveṇa eva etat gatam kimartham puar atidiśyate asti hi atra abhyadhikā āśaṅkā samyak darśa ābhyupāyaḥ hi yogaḥ veda vihitaḥ śrotavyaḥ matavyaḥ ididhyāsitavyaḥ iti sthāpya samam śarīram śvetāśvatara upaiṣadi dṛśyate liṅgāi ca vaidikāi yoga viṣayāṇi sahasraśas upalabhyate tām yogam iti mayate sthirām idriya dhāraṇām kaṭhaḥ iti vidyām etām yoga vidhim ca kṛtsam kaṭhaḥ iti yoga śāstre api atha tad darśa abhyupāyaḥ yogaḥ iti yogaḥ aṅgīkriyate atas atas artha eka deśa tvāt aṣṭaka ādi smṛti vat yoga smṛtiḥ api bhaviṣyati iti iyam api adhikā śaṅkā atideśe artha eka deśa saṃpratipattau api artha eka deśa vipratipatteḥ pūrva uktāyāḥ satīṣu api adhyātma viṣayāsu bahvīṣu smṛtiṣu sāṃkhya yoga smṛtyoḥ eva irā karaṇe yatas kṛtaḥ sāṃkhya yogau hi loke prakhyātau śiṣṭaiḥ ca parigṛhītau liṅge ca śraute upabṛṃhitau tad kāraṇam jñātvā devam mucyate sarva pāśaiḥ iti irā karaṇam tu a bhū vedaiḥ apekṣeṇa yoga mārgeṇa vā iḥśreyasam adhigamyate iti śrutiḥ hi vaidikāt ātma eka tva vijñāāt ayaḥ iḥśreyasa sādhaam vārayati tam eva viditvā ati mṛtyum eti āyaḥ pathā vidyate iti dvaitiḥ hi te sāṃkhyāḥ yogāḥ ca ātma eka tva darśiḥ yat tu uktam tad kāraṇam iti vaidikam eva tatra jñāam dhyāam ca sāṃkhya yoga śabdābhyām abhilapyete pratyāsatteḥ iti avagatavyam tu virudhyete eva sāṃkhya yoga smṛtyoḥ sāvakāśa tvam tat yathā a saṅgaḥ hi ayam puruṣaḥ iti evamādi śruti prasiddham eva puruṣasya viśuddha tvam sāṃkhyaiḥ abhyupagamyate tathā ca yaugaiḥ api atha parivrāj vivarṇa vāsāḥ parigrahaḥ iti evamādi śruti prasiddham eva sarvāṇi tarka smaraṇāi api tarka upapattibhyām tattva jñāāya upakurvati iti ced upakurvatu tu tattva jñāam tu maute tam bṛhatam tam tu aupaiṣadam puruṣam pracchāmi iti evamādi śrutibhyaḥ a vilakṣaṇa tvāt asya tathātvam ca śabdāt avilakṣaṇa tva adhikaraṇam brahma asya jagataḥ imitta kāraṇam prakṛtiḥ ced yasya pakṣasya ākṣepaḥ smṛti imittaḥ parihṛtaḥ tarka aimittaḥ idāīm ākṣepaḥ parihriyate kutas asmi avadhārite āgama arthe tarka aimittasya ākṣepasya avakāśaḥ dharme iva brahmaṇi api a apekṣaḥ āgamaḥ bhavitum arhati bhavet ayam yadi āgama mātra prameyaḥ yam arthaḥ syāt auṣṭheya rūpaḥ iva dharmaḥ tu brahma avagamyate ca pramāṇa atarāṇām asti avakāśaḥ yathā pṛthivī ādiṣu yathā ca paraspara virodhe satī eka vaśe itarā īyate evam pramāṇa atara virodhe tad vaśe eva śrutiḥ īyeta dṛṣṭa sādharmyeṇa ca adṛṣṭam artham samarpayatī yuktiḥ aubhavasya saṃikṛṣyate viprakṛṣyate tu śrutiḥ aitihya mātreṇa sva artha abhidhāāt ca avidyāyāḥ mokṣa sādhaam ca dṛṣṭa phala tayā iṣyate śrutiḥ api śrotavyaḥ matavyaḥ iti śravaṇa vyatirekeṇa vidadhatī tarkam api atra ādartavyam darśayati atas tarka aimittaḥ ākṣepaḥ kriyate a vilakṣaṇa tvāt asya iti yat uktam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam prakṛtiḥ iti kasmāt vilakṣaṇa tvāt asya vikārasya prakṛtyāḥ idam hi brahma kārya tveā abhipreyamāṇam jagat brahma vilakṣaṇam acetaam aśuddham ca dṛśyate brahma ca jagat vilakṣaṇam śuddham ca śrūyate a ca vilakṣaṇa tve prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ hi rucaka ādayaḥ vikārāḥ mṛd prakṛtikā bhavati śarāva ādayaḥ vā suvarṇa prakṛtikāḥ mṛdā eva tu mṛdavitā vikārāḥ prakriyate ca suvarṇāvitāḥ tathā idam api jagat acetaam sukha dukha moha āvitam sat acetaasya eva sukha duḥkha moha ātmakasya kāraṇasya kāryam bhavitum arhati a vilakṣaṇasya brahmaṇaḥ brahma vilakṣaṇa tvam ca asya avagatavyam aśuddham hi idam jagat sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka tayā pratīyate prīti paritāpa viṣāda ādi hetu tvāt svarga araka ādi uccāvaca prapañca tvāt ca acetaam ca idam jagat prati kārya kāraṇa bhāve upakaraṇa bhāva upagamāt hi sāmye sati upakārya upakāraka bhāvaḥ bhavati a hi pradīpau parasparasya upakurutaḥ au cetaam api kārya kāraṇam bhoktuḥ upakariṣyati a svāmi bhṛtyayoḥ api a cetaa aṃśasya eva cetaam pratyupakāraka tvāt yaḥ hi ekasya cetaasya parigrahaḥ buddhi ādiḥ acetaa bhāgaḥ saḥ eva ayasya cetaasya upakaroti tu svayam eva cetaaḥ cetaātarasya upakaroti apakaroti vā hi akartāraḥ cetaāḥ iti sāṃkhyāḥ tasmāt acetaam kārya kāraṇam ca kāṣṭha loṣṭa ādīām cetaa tve kiṃcid pramāṇam asti prasiddhaḥ ca ayam cetaḥ a ceta a vibhāgaḥ loke tasmāt brahma vilakṣaṇa tvāā idam jagat tad prakṛtikam yaḥ api kaścid ācakṣīta śrutyā jagataḥ ceta a prakṛtika tām tad bale eva samastam jagat cetaam avagamiṣyāmi prakṛti rūpasya tu caitayasya pariṇāma viśeṣāt bhaviṣyati yathā spaṣṭa caitayānām svāpa mūrchā ādi avasthāsu caitayam vibhāvyate evam kāṣṭha loṣṭa ādīām api caitayam vibhāvayiṣyate etasmāt eva ca vibhāvita tva a vibhāvita tva kṛtāt viśeṣāt rūpa ādi bhāva abhāvābhyām ca kārya kāraṇānām ātmaām ca virotsyate yathā ca pārthiva tva aviśeṣe api viśeṣāt paraspara upakāri tvam bhavati evam iha api bhaviṣyati pravibhāga prasiddhiḥ api atas eva virotsyate iti kathaṃcid cetaa tva acetaa tva lakṣaṇam vilakṣaṇa tvam parihriyeta śuddhi aśuddhi tva lakṣaṇam tu vilakṣaṇa tvam ca itarat api vilakṣaṇa tvam parihartum śakyate iti āha tathātvam ca śabdāt iti hi idam loke samastasya cetaa tvam cetaa prakṛtika tva śravaṇāt śabda śaraṇa tayā kevalayā utprekṣeta tat ca virudhyate yatas śabdāt api tathātvam avagamyate tathātvam iti prakṛti vilakṣaṇa tvam kathayati śabdaḥ eva ca a vijñāam ca iti kasyacid vibhāgasya acetaa tām śrāvayan cetaāt brahmaṇaḥ vilakṣaṇam acetaam jagat śrāvayati cetaa tvam api kvacid acetaa tva abhimatāām bhūta idriyāṇām śrūyate yathā mṛd abravīt āpobruvaḥ iti tat tejaḥ aikṣata tāḥ āpaḥ aikṣata iti ca evamādyā bhūta viṣayā cetaa tva śrutiḥ idriya viṣayāḥ api te heme prāṇāḥ ahaṃśreyase vivadamāāḥ brahma jagmuḥ iti te ha vācam ūcuḥ tvam udgāya iti iti evamādya idriya viṣayā iti atas uttaram paṭhati abhimāi vyapadeśaḥ tu viśeṣa augatibhyām tuśabdaḥ āśaṅkām a khalu mṛd abravīt iti evaṃjātīyakayā śrutyā bhūta idriyāṇām cetaa tvam yatas bhimāi vyapadeśaḥ eṣaḥ mṛd ādi abhimāiyaḥ vāc ādi abhimāiyaḥ ca cetaādevatāḥ vada asaṃvada ādiṣu cetaociteṣu vyavahāreṣu vyapadiśyate a bhūta idriya mātram kasmāt viśeṣa augatibhyām viśeṣaḥ hi bhoktṛṇām bhūta idriyāṇām ca cetaā cetaa pravibhāga lakṣaṇaḥ prāc abhihitaḥ sarva cetaa tāyām ca asau opapadyeta api ca kauṣītakiaḥ prāṇa saṃvāde devatā śabde viśiṣati etāḥ ha vai devatāḥ ahaṃśreyase vivadamānāḥ iti tāḥ vai etāḥ sarvāḥ devatāḥ prāṇe iḥśreyasam viditvā iti ca augatāḥ ca sarvatra abhimāiyaḥ cetaāḥ devatāḥ matra arthavāda itihāsa purāṇa ādibhyaḥ uvagamyate agiḥ vāc bhūtvā mukham prāviśat iti evamādikā ca śrutiḥ karaṇeṣu augrāhikām devatām augatām darśayati prāṇa saṃvāda vākyaśeṣe ca te ha prāṇāḥ prajāpatim pitaram etya ūcuḥ iti śreṣṭha tvaiḥ dhāraṇāya prajāpati gamaam tad vacaāt ca ekaika utkramaṇa āvayavyatirekābhyām prāṇa śraiṣṭhya pratipattiḥ tasmai bali haraṇam iti ca evaṃjātīyakaḥ usmad ādiṣu iva draḍhayati tat tejaḥ aikṣata iti api parasyāḥ eva devatāyāḥ adhiṣṭhātryāḥ sva vikāreṣu augatāyāḥ iyam īkṣā vyapadiśyate iti draṣṭavyam tasmāt vilakṣaṇam eva idam brahmaṇaḥ jagat vilakṣaṇa tvāt ca a brahma prakṛtikam iti ākṣipte pratividhatte dṛśyate tu tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati yat uktam vilakṣaṇa tvāt ā idam jagat brahma prakṛtikam iti dṛśyate hi loke prasiddhebhyaḥ puruṣa ādibhyaḥ utpattiḥ ca prasiddhebhyaḥ gomaya ādibhyaḥ vṛścika ādīām eva puruṣa ādi śarīrāṇi acetaāām keśa akha ādīām kāraṇāi acetaāi eva ca vṛścika ādi śarīrāṇi acetaāām gomaya ādīām kāryāṇi iti ucyate evam api kiṃcid acetaam upagacchati kiṃcid eti asti eva vailakṣaṇyam mahān ca ayam pāriṇāmikaḥ svabhāva viprakarṣaḥ puruṣa ādīām keśa akha ādīām ca rūpa ādi bhedāt tathā gomaya ādīām vṛścika ādīām ca atyata sārūpye ca prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ eva pralīyeta atha ucyeta asti kaścid pārthiva tva ādi svabhāvaḥ puruṣa ādīām keśa akha ādiṣu gomaya ādīām ca vṛścika ādiṣu iti brahmaṇaḥ tarhi sattā lakṣaṇaḥ svabhāvaḥ ākāśa ādiṣu dṛśyate ca brahma prakṛtika tvam jagataḥ dūṣayatā kim aśeṣasya brahma svabhāvasya āauvartaam vilakṣaṇa tvam abhipreyate uta yasya kasyacid atha vaktavyam prathame vikalpe samasta prakṛti vikāra bhāva uccheda prasaṅgaḥ a hi asati atiśaye prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ iti bhavati dvitīye ca asiddha tvam dṛśyate hi sattā lakṣaṇaḥ brahma svabhāvaḥ iti uktam tṛtīye tu dṛṣṭa atā abhāvaḥ kim hi tat abrahma prakṛtikam dṛṣṭam iti brahma kāraṇa vādiam pratyudāhriyeta samastasya asya vastu jātasya brahma prakṛtika tva abhyupagamāt āgama virodhaḥ tu prasiddhaḥ eva brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam prakṛtiḥ ca iti āgama tātparyasya prasādhita tvāt yat tu uktam brahmaṇi pramāṇa ātarāṇi saṃbhaveyuḥ iti tat api maoratha mātram rūpa ādi abhāvāt hi ā ayam arthaḥ pratyakṣasya gocaraḥ liṅga ādi abhāvāt ca āgama mātra samadhigamyaḥ eva tu ayam dharma vat tathā ca śrutiḥ su jñāāya preṣṭhaḥ iti kaḥ addhā veda kaḥ iha pravocat iyam visṛṣṭiḥ yata ābabhūva iti ca ete ṛcau api īśvarāṇām durbodhatām jagat kāraṇasya darśayataḥ smṛtiḥ api bhavati acityāḥ khalu ye bhāvāḥ a tān tarkeṇa yojayet iti avyaktaḥ yam acityaḥ yam avikāryaḥ yam ucyate iti ca a me viduḥ sura gaṇāḥ prabhavam a mahā ṛṣayaḥ aham ādiḥ hi devāām mahā ṛṣīṇām ca sarvaśas iti ca evaṃjātīyakāḥ yat api śravaṇa vyatirekeṇa maaam vidadhat śabdaḥ eva tarkam api ādartavyam darśayati iti uktam miṣeṇa śuṣka tarkasya atra ātmalābhaḥ saṃbhavati eva hi atra tarkaḥ ubhava aṅga tve āśrīyate ubhayoḥ itaretara vyabhicārāt avāgata tvam saṃprasāde ca sat ātma saṃpatteḥ prapañcasya brahma prabhava tvāt brahma avyatirekaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ tarka apratiṣṭhāāt iti ca kevalasya tarkasya vipralambhaka tvam darśayiṣyati samastasya jagataḥ cetaa tām utprekṣeta tasya api ca iti cetaā ceta a vibhāga śravaṇam caitayasya śakyate eva yojayitum parasya eva tu idam api vibhāga śravaṇam yujyate katham parama kāraṇasya hi atra samasta jagat ātmaā śrāvyate ca a vijñāam ca bhavat iti tatra yathā opapadyate vilakṣaṇa tvāt evam acetaasya api opapadyate pratyukta tvāt tu vilakṣaṇa tvasya yathā śrutyā eva kāraṇam grahītavyam bhavati asat iti ce pratiṣedha mātra tvāt yadi cetaam śuddham ca brahma tad viparītasya acetaasya aśuddhasya śabda ādimataḥ ca kāryasya kāraṇam iṣyeta asat tarhi kāryam prāk utpatteḥ iti prasajyeta aiṣṭam ca etat satkārya vādi astava iti ced ā eṣa doṣaḥ pratiṣedha mātra tvāt pratiṣedha mātram hi idam ā asya pratiṣedhasya pratiṣedhyam asti a hi ayam pratiṣedhaḥ prāk utpatteḥ sattvam kāryasya pratiṣeddhum katham yathā eva hi idāīm api idam kāryam sat evam prāk utpatteḥ api iti gamyate svatatram eva asti sarvam tam parādāt yaḥ yatra ātmā sarvam vedaḥ ityādi śravaṇāt kāraṇa ātmaā tu sattvam kāryasya prāc utpatteḥ aviśiṣṭam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam bāḍham tu śabda ādimat kāryam kāraṇa ātmā prāc utpatteḥ idāīm śakyate vaktum prāk utpatteḥ asatkāryam iti vistareṇa ca etat kārya kāraṇa āaya tva vāde vakṣyāmaḥ apītau tadvat prasaṅgāt asamañjasam atra āha yadi kāryam brahma kāraṇakam abhyupagamyeta tadā api itau pralaye pratisaṃsṛjyamāam kāryam kāraṇa avibhāgam āpadyamāam kāraṇam dūṣayet iti api itau kāraṇasya api brahmaṇaḥ kāryasya iva aśuddhi ādi rūpa tā prasaṅgāt sarvajñam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam iti asamañjasam idam aupaiṣadam api ca samastasya vibhāgasya avibhāga prāpteḥ puar utpattau iyam akāraṇa abhāvāt bhoktṛ bhogya ādi vibhāgena utpattiḥ iti asamañjasam api ca bhoktṛṇām pareṇa brahmaṇā avibhāgam gatāām karma ādi nimitta pralaye pi puar utpattau abhyupagamyamāāyām muktāām api puar utpatti prasaṅgāt asamañjasam atha idam jagat apītau api vibhaktam eva pareṇa brahmaṇā avatiṣṭheta evam api apītiḥ ca a saṃbhavati kāraṇa a vyatiriktam ca kāryam a saṃbhavati iti asamañjasam eva iti atra ucyate a tu dṛṣṭāta bhāvāt kiṃcid asāmañjasyam asti yat tāvat abhihitam kāraṇam api gacchat kāryam kāraṇam dūṣayet iti a tat dūṣaṇam kasmāt dṛṣṭāta bhāvāt sati hi dṛṣṭātāḥ yathā kāraṇam apigacchat kāryam kāraṇam ātmīyea dharmeṇa dūṣayati tat yathā śarāva ādayaḥ mṛd prakṛtikāḥ vikārāḥ vibhāga avasthāyām uccāvaca madhyama prabhedāḥ sataḥ puas prakṛtim apigacchataḥ a tām ātmīyea dharmeṇa saṃsṛjati rucaka ādayaḥ ca suvarṇa vikārāḥ apītau a puas suvarṇam ātmīyea dharmeṇa saṃsṛjati pṛthivī vikāraḥ caturvidhaḥ bhūta grāmaḥ dharmeṇa saṃsṛjati tvad pakṣasya tu a kaścid dṛṣṭātosti apītiḥ eva hi a saṃbhavet yadi kāraṇe kāryam svadharmeṇa eva avatiṣṭheta kārya kāraṇayoḥ kāryasya kāraṇa ātmatvam a tu kāraṇasya kārya ātmatvam ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhyaḥ iti atra vakṣyāmaḥ ati alpam ca idam ucyate kāryam dharmeṇa kāraṇam saṃsṛjet iti sthitau api hi prasaṅgaḥ kārya kāraṇayoḥ aaya tva abhyupagamāt idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā ātmā eva idam sarvam brahma eva idam amṛtam purastāt sarvam khalu idam brahma iti evamādyābhiḥ hi śrutibhiḥ aviśeṣeṇa triṣu api kāleṣu kāryasya śrāvyate tatra yaḥ parihāraḥ kāryasya tad dharmāṇām ca avidyā adhyāropita tvāt taiḥ kāraṇam saṃsṛjyate iti api itau api sa samaḥ asti ca ayam aparaḥ dṛṣṭātaḥ yathā svayam prasāritayā māyayā māyāvī triṣu api kāleṣu a saṃspṛśyate avastu tvāt evam paramātmā api saṃsāra māyayā a saṃspṛśyate iti yathā ca svapadṛś ekaḥ svapa darśa a māyayā saṃspṛśyate prabodha saṃprasādayoḥ a avāgata tvāt evam avasthā traya sākṣī ekaḥ vyabhicārī avasthā trayeṇa vyabhicāriṇā saṃspṛśyate māyā mātram hi etat yat paramātma vasthā traya ātma a avabhāsaam rajjvā iva sarpa ādi bhāve iti atra uktam vedātārtha saṃpradāya vidbhiḥ ācāryaiḥ a ādi māyayā suptaḥ yadā jīvaḥ prabudhyate ajam aidram a svapam advaitam budhyate tadā iti tatra yat uktam apītau kāraṇasya api kāryasya iva sthaulya ādi doṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti etat ayuktam yat puar etat uktam samastasya vibhāgasya avibhāga prāpteḥ iyam akāraṇam iti ayam api adoṣaḥ dṛṣṭa āta bhāvāt eva yathā hi suṣupti samādhi ādau api satyām svābhāvikyām avibhāga prāptau mithyā jñā asya apodita tvāt pūrvavat puar prabodhe vibhāgaḥ bhavati evam iha api bhaviṣyati śrutiḥ ca atra bhavati imāḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ sati saṃpadya a viduḥ sati saṃpadyāmahe iti te iha vyāghraḥ vā siṃhaḥ vā vṛkaḥ vā varāhaḥ vā kīṭaḥ vā pataṅgaḥ vā daṃśaḥ vā maśakaḥ vā yat yat bhavati tadā bhavati iti yathā hi avibhāge pi mithyājñā apratibaddhaḥ vibhāga vyavahāraḥ svapa vat avyāhataḥ sthitau dṛśyate evam apītau api mithyājñā a pratibaddhā eva muktāām muktāām puar utpatti prasaṅgaḥ pratyuktaḥ yaḥ vikalpaḥ utprekṣitaḥ atha idam jagat apītau api vibhaktam eva pareṇa brahmaṇā avatiṣṭheta iti saḥ upi a abhyupagamāt eva pratiṣiddhaḥ tasmāt samañjasam idam aupaiṣadam darśaam sva pakṣa doṣāt ca sva pakṣe ca ete sādhāraṇāḥ doṣāḥ prāduḥṣyuḥ katham iti ucyate yat tāvat abhihitam vilakṣaṇa tvā ā idam jagat brahma prakṛtikam iti pradhā aprakṛtikatāyām api etat śabda ādi hīāt śabda ādimataḥ jagataḥ utpatti abhyupagamāt atas eva ca vilakṣaṇa kārya utpatti abhyupagamāt samaḥ prāk utpatteḥ asatkārya vāda prasaṅgaḥ tathā apītau kāryasya kāraṇa avibhāga abhyupagamāt tadvat prasaṅgaḥ api samaḥ tathā mṛdita sarva viśeṣeṣu vikāreṣu apītau avibhāga ātma tām gateṣu idam asya puruṣasya upādāam idam asya iti prāk pralayāt pratipuruṣam ye iyatā bhedāḥ te tathā eva puar utpattau śakyate kāraṇa abhāvāt ca kāraṇa abhāva sāmyām uktāām api atha kecid bhedāḥ api itau avibhāgam āpadyate ced ye āpadyate teṣām iti evam ete doṣāḥ sādhāraṇa tvāḥ pakṣe codayitavyā bhavati iti adoṣa tām eva eṣām draḍhayati avaśya āśrayitavya tvāt tarka apratiṣṭhāāt api ayathā umā iyam iti ced evam api avimokṣa prasaṅgaḥ itas ca āgama gamye rthe tarkeṇa pratyavasthātavyam yasmai tarkāḥ apratiṣṭhitāḥ bhavati utprekṣāyāḥ tathā hi kaiḥ cit abhiyuktaiḥ yateḥ utprekṣitāḥ tarkāḥ abhiyuktataraiḥ dṛśyate taiḥ api utprekṣitāḥ satas tatas yaiḥ ābhāsyate iti a pratiṣṭhita tvam tarkāṇām śakyam āśrayitum puruṣam ati vairūpyāt atha kasyacid prasiddha māhātmyasya kapilasya ayasya vā saṃmataḥ tarkaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti āśrīyeta evam api apratiṣṭhita tvam eva prasiddha māhātmya abhimatāām api tīrthakarāṇām kapila kaṇabhuj prabhṛtīām paraspara vipratipatti darśaāt atha ucyeta ayathā vayam aumāsyāmahe yathā ā pratiṣṭhā doṣaḥ bhaviṣyati a hi pratiṣṭhitaḥ tarkaḥ eva ā asti iti śakyate vaktum etat api hi tarkāṇām apratiṣṭhita tvam tarkeṇa eva pratiṣṭhāpyate keṣāṃcid tarkāṇām apratiṣṭhita tva darśaeāyeṣām api sarva tarka apratiṣṭhāyām ca lokavyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgaḥ hi hi sukha duḥkha prāpti parihārāya lokaḥ dṛśyate śruti artha vipratipattau samyak arthaiḥ dhāraṇam tarkeṇa eva kriyate mauḥ api ca evam eva kriyate mauḥ api ca evam eva pratyakṣam aumāam ca śāstram ca vividha āgamam trayam su viditam kāryam dharma śuddhim abhīpsatā iti ārṣam dharma upadeśam ca yaḥ tarkeṇa ausaṃdhatte sa dharmam vedaḥ etaraḥ iti ca bruva ayam eva ca tarkasya alaṃkāraḥ evam hi sāvadya tarka parityāge evam hi sāvadya tarka parityāge tarkaḥ pratipattavyaḥ bhavati hi pūrvajaḥ mūḍhaḥ āsīt iti bhavitavyam iti kiṃcid asti pramāṇam tasmāt tarka apratiṣṭhā doṣaḥ iti ced evam api avimokṣa prasaṅgaḥ yadi api kvacid viṣaye tarkasya pratiṣṭhita tvam upalakṣyate tathā api prakṛte tāvat viṣaye prasajyate eva apratiṣṭhita tva doṣāt tarkasya a hi idam ati gambhīram bhāva yāthātmyam āgamam atareṇa utprekṣitum api śakyam rūpa ādi abhāvāt dhi ā ayam arthaḥ pratyakṣasya gocaraḥ liṅga ādi abhāvāt ca iti ca avocāma api ca mokṣaḥ iti sarveṣām mokṣa vādiām abhyupagamaḥ tat ca eka rūpam vastu tatra tvāt eka rūpeṇa hi avasthitaḥ yaḥ ṛthaḥ sa paramārthaḥ loke tad viṣayam samyak jñāam iti ucyate yathā agiḥ uṣṇaḥ iti tatra evam sati samyak jñāe puruṣāṇām vipratipattiḥ tarka jñāāām tu prasiddhā vipratipattiḥ yat dhi keacid tārkikeṇa idam eva iti pratiṣṭhāpitam tad apareṇa vyutthāpyate pratiṣṭhāpitam pareṇa vyutthāpyate iti ca prasiddham loke katham eka rūpa avasthita viṣayam tarka prabhavam samyak jñāam bhavet a ca pradhāa vādī tarka vidām uttamaḥ iti sarvaiḥ tārkikaiḥ parigṛhītaḥ tadīyam matam samyak jñāam iti pratipadyemahi a ca śakyate tīta āāgata vartamāāḥ tārkikāḥ ekasmi deśe kāle ca samāhartum eka rūpā eka artha viṣayā samyak matiḥ iti syāt vedasya tu itya tve vijñā utpatti hetu tve ca sati vyavasthita artha viṣaya tva upapatteḥ sarvaiḥ api tārkikaiḥ apahotum aśakyam atas siddham asya eva aupaiṣadasya jñā asya samyak jñā a tvam atas yatra samyak jñā a tva aupapatteḥ saṃsāra avimokṣaḥ eva prasajyeta atas āgama vaśea ca brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam prakṛtiḥ ca iti sthitam ete śiṣṭa aparigrahāḥ api vyākhyātāḥ śiṣṭa aparigraha adhikaraṇam vaidikasya darśaasya pratyāsa tvāt gurutara tarka bala upeta tvāt vedāusāribhiḥ ca kaiścid śiṣṭaiḥ parigṛhīta tvāt pradhā a kāraṇa vādam tāvat vyapāśritya yaḥ tarka aimittaḥ ākṣepaḥ sa parihṛtaḥ idāīm aṇu ādi vāda vyapāśrayeṇa api kaiścid mada matibhiḥ tarka aimittaḥ ākṣepaḥ āśaṅkyate iti atas tarka aimittaḥ ākṣepaḥ āśaṅkyate iti atas parigṛhyate iti parigrahāḥ a parigrahāḥ aparigrahāḥ śiṣṭāām aparigrahāḥ śiṣṭa aparigrahāḥ ete prakṛtea śiṣṭaiḥ mauvyāsa prabhṛtibhiḥ ye ṇu ādi kāraṇa vādāḥ te pi pratiṣiddha tayā vyākhyātāḥ irākṛtāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ tulya tvāt irākaraṇa kāraṇasya ā atra āśaṅkitavyam kiṃcid asti tulyam atra api parama gambhīrasya jagat kāraṇasya tarka a avagāhya tvam tarkasya ca a pratiṣṭhita tvam ayathā a vimokṣaḥ āgama virodhaḥ ca iti evaṃjātīyakam irā karaṇa kāraṇam bhoktṛ āpatteḥ avibhāgaḥ ced syāt loka vat bhoktṛ āpatti adhikaraṇam ayathā brahma kāraṇa vādaḥ yadi api śrutiḥ pramāṇam sva viṣaye bhavati tathā api pramāṇa atareṇa viṣaya apahāre bhavitum arhati yathā matra arthavādau sva viṣayāt syāt yathā dharma adharmayoḥ kim atas yadi evam atas idam ayuktam yat pramāṇa atara prasiddha artha bādhaam śruteḥ katham puas pramāṇa atara prasiddhaḥ rthaḥ śrutyā bādhyate iti atra ucyate prasiddhaḥ hi ayam bhoktṛ bhogya vibhāgaḥ loke bhoktā cetaḥ śārīraḥ bhogyāḥ śabda ādayaḥ viṣayāḥ iti yathā bhoktā devadattaḥ bhogyaḥ iti tasya ca vibhāgasya abhāvaḥ prasajyeta yadi bhoktā bhogya bhāvam āpadyeta bhogyam vā bhoktṛ bhāvam āpadyeta tayoḥ ca itaretara bhāva āpattiḥ parama kāraṇāt brahmaṇaḥ aya tvāt prasajyeta ca asya prasiddhasya vibhāgasya yuktam yathā tu adyatve bhoktṛ bhogyayoḥ vibhāgaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tathā atīta aāgatayoḥ api kalpayitavyaḥ tasmāt prasiddhasya asya bhoktṛ bhogya vibhāgasya abhāva prasaṅgāt ayuktam idam brahma kāraṇatā avadhāraṇam iti ced kaścid codayet tam prati brūyāt syāt loka vat iti upapadyate eva ayam asmad pakṣe vibhāgaḥ evam loke dṛṣṭa tvāt tathā hi samudrāt udaka ātman aya tve tad vikārāṇām itaretara vibhāgaḥ itaretara asaṃśleṣa ādi lakṣaṇaḥ ca vyavahāraḥ upalabhyate a ca samudrāt udaka ātman aya tve tad vikārāṇām itaretara bhāva āpattiḥ bhavati ca teṣām itaretara bhāvāām pattau api bhavati evam iha api a bhoktṛ bhogyayoḥ itaretara bhāva āpattiḥ ca parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ ya tvam bhaviṣyati yadi api bhoktā a brahmaṇaḥ vikāraḥ tat sṛṣṭvā tat eva auprāviśat iti sraṣṭuḥ eva avikṛtasya bhoktṛ tva śravaṇāt tathā api kāryam upādhi imittaḥ vibhāgaḥ ākāśasya iva ghaṭa ādi upādhi imittaḥ iti atas parama kāraṇāt brahmaṇaḥ aya tve pi upapadyate bhoktṛ bhogya lakṣaṇaḥ vibhāgaḥ uktam tad aaya tvam ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhyaḥ ārambhaṇa adhikaraṇam abhyupagamya ca imam vyāvahārikam bhoktṛ bhogya lakṣaṇam vibhāgam syāt loka vat iti parihāraḥ bhihitaḥ a tu ayam vibhāgaḥ paramārthataḥ sti yasmāt tayoḥ kārya kāraṇayoḥ aaya tvam avagamyate kāryam ākāśa ādikam bahu prapañcam jagat kāraṇam param brahma tasmāt kāraṇāt paramārthataḥ aya tvam vyatirekeṇa abhāvaḥ kāryasya avagamyate kutas ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhyaḥ ārambhaṇa śabdaḥ tāvat sarva vijñāam pratijñāya ucyate yathā somya ekea sarvam mṛ mayam vijñātam syāt vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ āmadheyam mṛttikā iti eva satyam iti etat uktam bhavati sarvam mṛd mayam ghaṭa śarāva udañca ādikam mṛd ātmaka tva aviśeṣāt vijñātam bhavet yatas vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ āmadheyam vācā eva kevalam asti iti ārabhyate vikāraḥ ghaṭaḥ śarāvaḥ kaścid asti āmadheya mātram hi etat aṛtam mṛttikā iti eva satyam iti eṣa brahmaṇaḥ tatra śrutāt vācā ārambhaṇa śabdāt dārṣṭātike brahma vyatirekeṇa kārya jātasya abhāvaḥ iti gamyate ca brahma kārya tām uktvā tejaḥ ba a kāryāṇām tejaḥ ba a vyatirekeṇa abhāvam bravīti apāgāt ageḥ agi tvam vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ āmadheyam trīṇi rūpāṇi iti eva satyam ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhyaḥ iti ādi śabdāt aitadātmyam idam sarvam tat satyam saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā brahma eva idam sarvam ātmā eva idam sarvam iti evamādi api ātma ekatva pratipāda aparam udāhartavyam saṃpadyate tasmāt yathā ghaṭa karaka ādi ākāśāām mahā ākāśāt yathā ca mṛgatṛṣṇikā udaka ādīām ūṣara ādibhyaḥ dṛṣṭa aṣṭa svarūpa tvāt svarūpeṇa tu aupākhya tvāt evam asya bhogya bhoktṛ ādi prapañca jātasya brahma vyatirekeṇa abhāvaḥ iti draṣṭavyam brahma yathā eka śākhaḥ evam brahma atas ekatvam ca ubhayam api satyam eva yathā vṛkṣaḥ iti ekatvam śākhāḥ iti ca āātvam yathā ca samudra ātma aikatvam phea taraṅga ādi ātma āātvam yathā ca mṛd ātma aikatvam ghaṭa śarāva ādi ātma āātvam tatra ekatva aṃśea mokṣa vyavahāraḥ setsyati tu karmakāṇḍa āśrayau laukika vaidika vyavahārau setsyataḥ iti evam ca mṛd ādi dṛṣṭātā aurūpā bhaviṣyati iti aivam syāt mṛttikā iti eva satyam iti prakṛti mātrasya dṛṣṭāte satya tva avadhāraṇāt vācā ārambhaṇa śabde ca vikāra jātasya aṛta tva abhidhāāt dārṣṭātike aitadātmyam idam sarvam tat satyam iti ca parama kāraṇasya eva ekasya satya tva avadhāraṇāt saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi śvetaketo iti ca śārīrasya brahma bhāva upadeśāt svayam prasiddham hi etat śārīrasya brahma ātmatvam upadiśyate a yata atara prasādhyam atas ca idam śāstrīyam brahma ātmatvam svābhāvikasya śārīra ātma tvasya bādhakam saṃpadyate rajju ādi buddhayaḥ iva sarpa ādi buddhīām bādhite ca śārīra ātma tve tad āśrayaḥ samastaḥ svābhāvikaḥ vyavahāraḥ bādhitaḥ bhavati yat prasiddhaye paraḥ brahmaṇaḥ kalpyeta darśayati ca yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kaḥ kam paśyet ityādiā brahma ātmatva darśiam prati samastasya kriyā kāraka phala lakṣaṇasya vyavahārasya abhāvam ca ayam vyavahāra abhāvaḥ abhidhīyate iti yuktam vaktum tat tvam asi iti ca aṛta abhisaṃdhasya satya abhisaṃdhasya ca mokṣam darśaya ekatvam eva ekam pāramārthikam darśayati mithyājñā avijṛmbhitam ca ubhaya satyatāyām hi katham vyavahāra gocaraḥ api jatuḥ aṛta abhisaṃdhaḥ iti ucyate mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpa iti yaḥ iha paśyati iti ca bheda dṛṣṭim apavada etat eva darśayati a ca asmi mokṣaḥ iti upapadyate samyak jñāā apaodyasya kasyacid mithyājñāasya saṃsāra kāraṇa tveā abhyupagamāt ubhaya satyatāyām hi katham iti ucyate ekatva ekātā abhyupagame āātva abhāvāt pratyakṣa ādīi laukikāi pramāṇāi vyāhayeraa sthāṇu ādiṣu iva tathā vidhi pratiṣedha śāstram api bheda apekṣa tvāt tad abhāve vyāhayeta mokṣa śāstrasya api śiṣya śāsitṛ ādi bheda apekṣa tvāt tad abhāve vyāghātaḥ syāt katham mokṣa śāstreṇa pratipāditasya ātma ekatvasya satya tvam upapadyeta iti atrā ucyate ā eṣa doṣaḥ sarva vyavahārāṇām eva prāk brahma ātmatā vijñāāt satya tva upapatteḥ prāk bodhāt yāvat hi a satya ātma ekatva pratipattiḥ tāvat pramāṇa prameya phala lakṣaṇeṣu vikāreṣu aṛta tva buddhiḥ a kasyacid utpadyate vikārāḥ eva tu aham mama iti avidyayā ātma ātmīyea bhāvea sarvaḥ jatuḥ pratipadyate svābhāvikīm brahma ātmatām hitvā tasmāt prāk brahma ātmatā prabodhāt sarvaḥ laukikaḥ vaidikaḥ ca vyavahāraḥ yathā suptasya prākṛtasya svape uccāvacāḥ eva pratyakṣa abhimatam bhavati prāk prabodhāt ca pratyakṣa ābhāsa abhiprāyaḥ tad kāle bhavati tadvat katham tu satyasya brahma ātmatvasya pratipattiḥ upapadyeta hi rajju sarpeṇa daṣṭaḥ mriyate mṛgatṛṣṇikā ambhasā kriyate iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ śaṅkā viṣa ādi nimitta maraṇa ādi kārya upalabdheḥ svapa darśa avasthasya ca sarpa daṃśa odaka sāā ādi kārya darśaāt tad kāryam api aṛtam eva iti ced brūyāt tatra brūmaḥ yadi api svapa darśa avasthasya sarpa daṃśa odaka sāā ādi kāryam aṛtam tathā api tad avagatiḥ satyam eva phalam pratibuddhasya api hi svapāt utthitaḥ sarpa daṃśa odaka ādi kāryam mithyā iti tat avagatim api mithyā iti kaścid deha mātra ātma vādaḥ dūṣitaḥ veditavyaḥ tathā ca śrutiḥ yadā karmasu kāmyeṣu striyam svapeṣu paśyati samṛddhim tatra iti satyāyāḥ phala samṛddheḥ prāptim darśayati tathā pratyakṣa darśaeṣu satyāyāḥ phala samṛddheḥ prāptim darśayati tathā pratyakṣa darśaeṣu keṣucid ariṣṭeṣu jāteṣu a ciram iva jīviṣyati iti vidyāt iti uktvā atha yaḥ svape puruṣam kṛṣṇam kṛṣṇa datam paśyati saḥ śā ityādiā satya maraṇam sūcyate iti darśayati prasiddham ca idam loke sādhu āgamaḥ sūcyate īdṛśeā asādhu āgamaḥ iti tathā akāra ādi satya akṣara pratipattiḥ dṛṣṭā rekhā ṛta akṣara pratipatteḥ api ca atyam idam pramāṇam ātma eka tvasya pratipādakam ā atas param kiṃcid ākāṅkṣyam asti yathā hi loke yajeta iti ukte kim katham iti ākāṅkṣyate tat tvam asi aham brahma asmi iti ukte kiṃcid ākāṅkṣyam asti sarva ātma eka tva viṣaya tvāt avagateḥ sati hi avaśiṣyamāṇe rthe ākāṅkṣā syāt a tu ātma ekatva vyatirekeṇa avaśiṣyamāṇaḥ yaḥ rthaḥ u sti yaḥ ākāṅkṣyeta a ca iyam avagatiḥ ā utpadyate iti śakyam vaktum tat ityādi śrutibhyaḥ avagati sādhaāām ca śravaṇa ādīām ca ca a ca iyam iyam avagatiḥ a arthikā bhrātiḥ vā iti śakyam vaktum avidyā a vṛtti phala darśaāt bādhaka jñāātara abhāvāt ca prāk ca ātma eka tva avagateḥ avyāhataḥ sarvaḥ satya aṛta vyavahāraḥ laukikaḥ vaidikaḥ ca iti avocāma tasmāt pramāṇea pratipādite ātma eka tve samastasya bheda vyavahārasya bādhita tvāt mṛd ādi dṛṣṭa ata praṇayaāt pariṇāma vat brahma śāstrasya abhimatam iti gamyate hi mṛd ādayaḥ rthāḥ loke samadhigatāḥ iti ā iti ucyate sa vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ ātmā ajaraḥ maraḥ mṛtaḥ bhayaḥ brahma saḥ eṣaḥ eti eti ātmā a sthūlam a aṇu ityādyābhyaḥ sarva vikriyā pratiṣedha śrutibhyaḥ brahmaṇaḥ kūṭastha tva avagamāt a hi ekasya brahmaṇaḥ pariṇāma dharma tvam tad rahita tvam ca śakyam pratipattum sthiti gati vat syāt iti ced a kūṭasthasya iti viśeṣaṇāt a hi kūṭasthasya brahmaṇaḥ sthiti gati vat a eka dharma āśraya tvam saṃbhavati kūṭastham ca ityam brahma sarva vikriyā pratiṣedhāt iti avocāma ca yathā brahmaṇaḥ ātma eka tva darśaam mokṣa sādhaam evam jagat ākāra pariṇāmi tva darśaam api svatatram eva kasmaicid phalāya abhipreyate pramāṇa abhāvāt kūṭastha brahma ātma eka tva vijñāāt eva hi phalam darśayati śāstram saḥ eṣaḥ eti eti ātmā iti upakramya abhayam vai jaaka si iti evaṃjātīyakam tatra etat siddham bhavati brahma prakaraṇe sarva dharma viśeṣa rahita brahma darśaāt eva phala siddhau satyām yat tatra aphalam śrūyate brahmaṇaḥ jagat ākāra pariṇāmi tva ādi tat viiyujyate phalavat saṃidhau aphalam tat aṅgam itivat a tu svatatram phalāya kalpyate iti a hi pariṇāmavat tva vijñāāt pariṇāmavat tvam ātmaaḥ phalam syāt iti vaktum yuktam kūṭastha aitya tva ātmanaḥ mokṣasya ekatva aikātyāt īśitṛ īśitavya abhāve īśvara kāraṇa pratijñā virodhaḥ iti ced a avidyā ātmaka āma rūpa bīja vyākaraṇa apekṣa tvāt sarvajñatvasya tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ ityādi vākyebhyaḥ iti aśuddha buddha mukta svarūpāt sarvajñāt sarva śakteḥ īśvarāt vā iti eṣaḥ rthaḥ pratijñātaḥ asya yatas iti sā pratijñā tad avasthā eva rthaḥ iha ucyate katham ocyate atyatam ātmanaḥ ekatvam advitīya tvam ca bruvatā śṛṇu yathā ocyate sarvajñasya īśvarasya ātma bhūte iva avidyā kalpite āma rūpe tattva ayatvābhyām airvacaīye saṃsāra prapañca bīja bhūte sarvajñasya īśvarasya māyā śaktiḥ prakṛtiḥ iti a śruti smṛtyoḥ abhilapyete tābhyām ayaḥ sarvajñaḥ īśvaraḥ ākāśaḥ vai āmaḥ āma rūpayoḥ te yat atarā tat brahma iti śruteḥ āma rūpe vyākaravāṇi sarvāṇi rūpāṇi vicitya ekam bījam bahudhā yaḥ karoti ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ca evam avidyā kṛta āma rūpa upādhi aurodhi īśvaraḥ bhavati vyom iva ghaṭa karaka ādi upādhi aurodhi sa ca svātma bhūtāḥ eva ghaṭa ākāśa sthāīyāḥ avidyā pratyupasthāpita āma rūpa kṛta kārya karaṇa saṃghāta aurodhiḥ pratīṣṭe vyavahāra viṣaye tat evam avidyā ātmaka upādhi pariccheda apekṣam eva īśvarasya īśvara tvam sarvajña tvam sarva śakti tvam ca a paramārthataḥ vidyayā apāsta sarva upādhi svarūpe ātmai īśitṛ īśitavya sarvajña tva ādi vyavahāraḥ upapadyate tathā ca uktam yatra āyat paśyati āyat śṛṇoti āyat sa bhūmā iti yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kaḥ kam paśyet ca evam paramārtha avasthāyām sarva vyavahāra abhāvam vadati sarve tathā īśvaragītāsu api a kartṛ tvam a karmāṇi lokasya sṛjati prabhuḥ a karma phala saṃyogam svabhāvaḥ tu pravartate ādatte kasyacid pāpam a ca eva sukṛtam vibhuḥ muhyati bhūta pāla etad setuḥ vidharaṇa eṣām loka a sambheda iti tathā ca īśvaragītāsu api īśvaraḥ sarva bhūta hṛd deśa tiṣṭhati bhrāmay sarva bhūta māyayā iti sūtrakāraḥ u pi paramārtha abhiprāyeṇa tad aaya tvam iti āha vyavahāra abhiprāyeṇa tu syāt loka vat iti mahā samudra ādi sthāīyatām brahmaṇaḥ kathayati a pratyākhyāya eva kārya prapañcam pariṇāma prakriyām ca āśrayati saguṇeṣu upāsaeṣu upayokṣyate iti bhāve ca upalabdheḥ itas ca kāraṇāt kāryasya yat kāraṇam bhāvaḥ eva kāraṇasya kāryam upalabhyate ābhāve tat yathā satyām mṛdi ghaṭaḥ upalabhyate satsu ca paṭaḥ ca iyam eāya bhāvā iyasya upalabdhiḥ dṛṣṭā a hi aśvaḥ go rayaḥ sa goḥ bhāvaḥ eva upalabhyate a ca kulāla bhāvaḥ eva ghaṭaḥ upalabhyate sati api imitta aimittika bhāva iyatvāt avayasya bhāve pi ayasya upalabdhiḥ iyatā dṛśyate yathā agi bhāve dhūmasya iti ā iti ucyate udvāpite ipi agau gopāla ghuṭikā ādi dhāritasya dhūmasya atha dhūmam kayācid avasthayā viśiṃṣyāt īdṛśaḥ asya anubhūtaḥ asya anubhūtaḥ asya anubhūtaḥ asya anubhūtaḥ asya anubhūtaḥ asya anubhūtaḥ asya anubhūtaḥ asya anubhūtaḥ asya anubhūtaḥ asya anubhūtaḥ asya anubhūtaḥ asya anubhūta bhavati iti hi buddhim kārya kāraṇayoḥ aaya tve hetum vayam vadāmaḥ a ca asau agi dhūmayoḥ vidyate bhāvāt ca upalabdheḥ iti vā sūtram a kevalam śabdāt eva kārya kāraṇayoḥ aaya tvam pratyakṣa upalabdhi bhāvāt ca tayoḥ aaya tvam iti arthaḥ bhavati hi pratyakṣa upalabdhiḥ kārya kāraṇayoḥ aaya tve tat yathā paṭe tatu vyatirekeṇa paṭaḥ kāryam kevalāḥ tu tatavaḥ pratyakṣam upalabhyate tathā tatuṣu aṃśavaḥ aṃśuṣu tad avayavāḥ aayā pratyakṣa upalabdhyā lohita śukla kṛṣṇāi trīṇi rūpāṇi tatas vāyu mātram ākāśa mātram ca iti aumeyam tatas param brahma ekam eva advitīyam tatra sarva pramāṇāām iṣṭhām avocāma sattvāt ca avarasya itas ca kāraṇāt kāryasya āaya tvam yat kāraṇam prāk utpatteḥ kāraṇa ātmā eva kāraṇe sattvam avarakālīasya kāryasya śrūyate sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ātmā vai idam eka eva agre āsīt ityādau idam śabda gṛhītasya kāryasya sāmāādhikaraṇyāt yat ca yad ātma yatra a vartate a tat tatas utpadyate yathā sikatābhyaḥ tailam tasmāt prāk utpatteḥ aaya tvāt utpaam api aayat eva kāraṇāt kāryam iti avagamyate yathā ca kāraṇam brahma triṣu kāleṣu sattvam vyabhicarati evam kāryam api jagatī traṣu kāleṣu sattvam vyabhicarati ekam ca sattvam kāraṇāt kāryasya asat vyapadeśāḥ ce a dharma atareṇa vākyaśeṣāt kvacid asat tvam api prāk utpatteḥ kāryasya vyapadiśati śrutiḥ asat eva idam agre āsīt iti asat vai idam agre āsīt iti ca tasmāt asat vyapadeśāḥ prāk utpatteḥ kāryasya sattvam iti ced ā iti brūmaḥ hi ayam atyatā sattva abhiprāyeṇa prāk utpatteḥ kāryasya asat vyapadeśaḥ kim tarhi vyākṛta āma rūpa tvāt dharmāt avyākṛta āma rūpa tvam dharma ataram dharma atareṇa ayam asat vyapadeśaḥ prāk utpatteḥ sata eva kāryasya kāraṇa rūpeṇa āayasya katham etat avagamyate vākyaśeṣāt yat upakrame saṃdigdha artham vākyam tat śeṣāḥ cīyate iha ca tāvat asat eva idam agre āsīt iti asat śabdena upakrame yat tat eva parāmṛśya sat iti viśiaṣṭi tat sat āsīt iti asataḥ ca āsīt śabda aupapatteḥ ca asat vai idam agre āsīt iti atra api tat ātmā aam svayam akuruta iti vākyaśeṣe tasmāt dharma atareṇa eva ayam asat vyapadeśaḥ prāk utpatteḥ kāryasya āma rūpa vyākṛtam hi vastu sat śabda arham loke prasiddham atas praṅ āma rūpa vyākaraṇāt asat iva āsīt iti upacaryate yukteḥ śabda atarāt ca yukteḥ ca prāk utpatteḥ kāryasya sattvam ca kāraṇāt avagamyate śabda atarāt ca yuktiḥ tāvat varṇyate dadhi ghaṭa rucaka ādi arthibhiḥ kāraṇāi loke dṛśyate a hi dadhi arthibhiḥ mṛttikā upādīyate a ghaṭa arthibhiḥ kṣīram tat asatkārya vāde opapadyeta a viśiṣṭe hi prāk utpatteḥ sarvasya sarvatra asattve kasmāt kṣīrāt eva dadhi utpadyate a mṛttikāyāḥ mṛttikāyāḥ eva ca ghaṭaḥ utpadyate a kṣīrāt atha aviśiṣṭe pi prāk asattve kṣīre eva dadhaḥ kaścid atiśayaḥ a mṛttikāyām mṛttikāyām eva ca ghaṭasya kaścid atiśayaḥ a kṣīre iti ucyeta atas tarhi atiśayavat tvāt prāk avasthāyāḥ asatkārya vāda hāiḥ satkārya vāda siddhiḥ ca śaktiḥ ca kāraṇasya kārya aiyama arthā āyāḥ asatī vā kāryam iyacchet asattva aviśeṣāt ca tasmāt kāraṇasya ātma bhūtā śaktiḥ śakteḥ ca ātma bhūtam kāryam api ca kārya kāraṇayoḥ dravya guṇa ādīām ca aśva mahiṣa vat bheda buddhi abhāvāt tādātmyam abhyupagatavyam samavāya kalpaāyām api samavāyasya samavāyibhiḥ saṃbadhe bhyupagamyamāe tasya tasya ayoyaḥ saṃbadhaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ iti a avasthā prasaṅgaḥ ca viccheda prasaṅgaḥ atha samavāyaḥ svayam saṃbadha rūpa tvāt a apekṣya eva aparam saṃbadham saṃbadhyeta saṃyogaḥ tarhi svayam tarhi svayam a apekṣya eva aparam samavāyam saṃbadhyeta tādātmya pratīteḥ ca dravya guṇa ādīām samavāya kalpa āarthakyam katham ca kāryam avayavi dravyam kāraṇeṣu avayava dravyeṣu vartamāam vartate kim samasteṣu avayaveṣu varteta uta pratyavayavam yadi tāvat samasteṣu varteta tatas vayavī aupalabdhiḥ prasajyeta samasta avayava saṃikarṣasya aśakya tvāt hi bahu tvam samasteṣu āśrayeṣu vyasta āśraya grahaṇea gṛhyate atha avayavaśas samasteṣu varteta tadā api ārambhaka avayava vyatirekeṇa avayaviḥ vayavāḥ kalpyera yaiḥ ārambhakeṣu avayaveṣu avayavaśas vayavī varteta kośa avayava vyatiriktaiḥ hi avayavaiḥ asiḥ kośam ca evam prasajyeta teṣu teṣu avayaveṣu vartayitum avayavāām avayavāām atha pratyavayavam varteta tadā ekatra vyāpāre yatra avyāpāraḥ syāt hi devadattaḥ srughe tat ahar eva pāṭaliputre saṃidhīyate srugha pāṭaliputraivāsioḥ go tva ādi vat pratyekam parisamāpteḥ a doṣaḥ iti ced a tathā pratīti abhāvāt yadi go tva ādi vat pratyekam parisamāptaḥ vayavī syāt yathā go tvam prati vyakti pratyakṣam gṛhyate evam avayavi api prati avayavam pratyakṣam gṛhyeta ca evam iyatam gṛhyate pratyeka parisamāptau ca avayaviḥ kāryeṇa adhikārāt tasya ca ekatvāt śṛṅgeṇa api staa kāryam kuryāt urasā ca ca evam dṛśyate prāk utpatteḥ ca kāryasya asattve utpattiḥ akartṛkā ca syāt utpattiḥ ca kriyā sā sa kartṛkā eva bhavitum arhati gati ādi vat kriyā ca syāt akartṛkā ca iti vipratiṣidhyeta ghaṭasya ca utpattiḥ ucyamāā ca ghaṭa kartṛkā kiṃtarhi iti kalpyā syāt tathā kapāla ādīām api utpattiḥ ucyamāāī akartṛkā eva kalpyeta tathā ca sati ghaṭaḥ utpadyate yukte utpadyate iti uktam syāt ca loke ghaṭa utpattiḥ iti ukte kulāla ādīām api utpadyamāatā pratīyate atha sva kāraṇa sattā saṃbadhaḥ evā utpattiḥ ātmalābhaḥ ca kāryasya iti ced katham alabdha ātmakam saṃbadhyeta iti vaktavyam satoḥ hi dvayoḥ saṃbadhaḥ saṃbhavati a sat asatoḥ asatoḥ vā abhāvasya ca prāk utpatteḥ iti maryādā karaṇam aupapaam satām hi loke kṣetra gṛha ādīām maryādā dṛṣṭā hi vadhyāputraḥ rājā babhūva prāk pūrṇavarmaṇaḥ bhiṣekāt iti evaṃjātīyake maryādā karaṇe vadhyāputraḥ rājā babhūva bhavati bhaviṣyati iti vā viśeṣyate yadi ca kāraka vyāpārāt ūrdhvam abhaviṣyat tatas idam api upāpatsyata kārya bhāvaḥ pi kāraka vyāpārāt ūrdhvam bhaviṣyati iti vayam tu paśyāmaḥ vadhyā putrasya kārya abhāvasya ca abhāva tva aviśeṣāt yathā badhyā putraḥ kāraka vyāpārāt ūrdhvam bhaviṣyati evam kārya abhāvaḥ pi kāraka vyāpārāt ūrdhvam bhaviṣyati iti evam sati kāraka vyāpāraḥ arthakaḥ prasajyeta yathā eva hi prāk siddha tvāt kāraṇa sva rūpa siddhaye a kaścid vyāpriyate evam prāk siddha tvāt tad aaya tvāt ca kāryasya sva rūpa siddhaye pi a kaścid vyāpriyeta vyāpriyate ca atas kāraka vyāpāra arthavat tvāya mayāmahe prāk utpatteḥ abhāvaḥ kāryasya iti ced ā eṣa doṣaḥ yatas kāryākāreṇa kāraṇam vyavasthāpayataḥ kāraka vyāpārasya arthavat tvam upapadyate kārya akāraḥ pi kāraṇasya ātma bhūtaḥ eva a ātma bhūtasya a ārabhya tvāt iti abhāṇi a ca viśeṣa darśa mātreṇa bhavati hi devadattaḥ saṃkucita hasta pādaḥ prasārita hasta pādaḥ ca viśeṣeṇa vastu aya tvam gacchati saḥ eva iti pratyabhijñāāt tathā api bhavati mama pitā mama bhrātā mama putraḥ iti tatra yuktam tatra yuktam a kṣīra ādīām api dadhi ādi ākāra saṃsthā asya pratyakṣa tvāt adṛśyamāāām api vaṭa dhā ādīām aṅkura ādi bhāve a darśa agocara tā āpattau jama saṃjñā teṣām eva avayavāām apacaya vaśāt adarśa āpattau uccheda saṃjñā tatra īdṛś jama uccheda ātarita tvāt ced asataḥ sattva āpattiḥ sataḥ ca asattva āpattiḥ tathā sati bheda prasaṅgaḥ tathā ca bālya yauva a sthāvireṣu api bheda prasaṅgaḥ pitṛ ādi vyavahāra lopa prasaṅagaḥ ca kṣaṇabhaṅga vādaḥ prativaditavyaḥ yasya tu prāk utpatteḥ asat kāryam tasya iḥ viṣayaḥ kāraka vyāpāraḥ syāt abhāvasya viṣaya tva aupapatteḥ samavāyi kāraṇa viṣayaḥ kāraka vyāpāraḥ syāt iti ced a aya viṣayeṇa kāraka vyāpāreṇa ayaiṣpatteḥ atiprasaṅgāt samavāyi kāraṇasya eva ātma atiśayaḥ kāryam iti ced a satkārya tā āpatteḥ tasmāt kṣīra ādīyā iva dravyāṇi kārya ākhyām labhate iti a kāraṇāt ayat kāryam varṣa śate api śakyam kalpayitum tathā mūla kāraṇam eva a atyāt kāryāt kāryākāreṇa aṭa vat sarva vyavahāra āspada tvam pratipadyate evam yukteḥ kāryasya prāk utpatteḥ sattvam ca kāraṇāt avagamyate śabda atarāt ca etat avagamyate pūrva sūtre sat vyapadeśiaḥ śabdasya udāhṛta tvāt tatoyaḥ sat vyapadeśī śabdaḥ śabdātaram sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam ityādi tat ha eke āhuḥ asat eva idam agre āsīt iti ca asat pakṣam upakṣipya katham asataḥ sat jāyeta iti ākṣipya sat eva somya idam agre āsīt iti avadhārayati tatra idam śabda vācyasya kāryasya prāk utpatteḥ sat śabda vācyā ia sāmāādhikaraṇyasya śrūyamāṇa tvāt sattva aaya tve prasidhyataḥ yadi tu prāk utpatteḥ asat kāryam syāt paścāt ca utpadyamāam kāraṇe samaveyāt tat ayat kāraṇāt syāt tatra ye a śrutam śrutam bhavati iti iyam pratijñā pīḍyeta sattva āaya tva avagateḥ tu iyam pratijñā samarthyate paṭa vat ca yathā ca saṃveṣṭitaḥ paṭaḥ vyaktam gṛhyate kim ayam paṭaḥ kim vā ayat dravyam iti saḥ eva prasāritaḥ yat saṃveṣṭitam dravyam tat paṭaḥ eva iti prasāraṇe abhivyaktaḥ gṛhyate yathā ca saṃveṣṭa a samaye paṭaḥ iti gṛhyamāṇaḥ api a viśiṣṭa āyāma vistāraḥ gṛhyate saḥ eva prasāraṇa samaye viśiṣṭa āyāma vistāraḥ gṛhyate paṭaḥ iti evam tatva ādi kāraṇa avastham paṭa ādi kāryam aspaṣṭam sat turī vema kuvida ādi kāraka vyāpāra abhivyaktam spaṣṭam gṛhyate atas saṃveṣṭita prasārita paṭa yad kāraṇāt kāryam iti arthaḥ yathā ca prāṇa ādi yathā ca loke prāṇa apā ādiṣu prāṇabhedeṣu prāṇāyāmeṣu iruddheṣu kāraṇa mātreṇa rūpeṇa vartamāeṣu jīva amātram kāryam ākuñca aprasāraṇa ādikam teṣu eva prāṇabhedeṣu pravṛtteṣu ākuñca aprasāraṇa ādikam api ca prāṇabhedāām prabhedavataḥ samīraṇa svabhāva aviśeṣāt evam kāryasya kāraṇāt aaya tvam atas ca kṛtsasya jagataḥ brahma kārya tvāt tad aaya tvāt ca siddhā eṣā śrautī pratijñā yena aśrutam śrutam bhavati amatam matam avijñātam vijñātam iti itara vyapadeśāt hita akaraṇa ādi doṣa prasaktiḥ itara vyapadeśa adhikaraṇam ayathā puas ceta akāraṇa vādaḥ ākṣipyate jagat prakriyāyām āśrīyamāṇāyām hita akaraṇa ādayaḥ doṣāḥ prasajyate kutas itara vyapadeśāt itarasya śārīrasya brahma ātma tvam vyapadiśati śrutiḥ saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi śvetaketo iti pratibodhaāt yat vā itarasya ca brahmaṇaḥ śārīra ātma tvam vyapadiśati tat sṛṣṭvā tat eva auprāviśat iti sraṣṭuḥ eva avikṛtasya brahmaṇaḥ śārīra ātma tva darśaāt āma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti ca parā devatā jīvam ātma śabdea vyapadiśatī brahmaṇaḥ iti darśayati tasmāt yat brahmaṇaḥ sraṣṭṛ tvam tat śārīrasya eva iti atas ca svatatraḥ kartā sa hitam eva ātmaaḥ saumaasya karam kuryāt āhitam hi kaścid aparatatraḥ a hi kaścid aparatatraḥ a hi kaścid aparatatraḥ a hi kaścid aparatatraḥ a hi kaścid aparatatraḥ a hi kaścid aparatatraḥ a hi kaścid aparatatraḥ a hi kaścid aparatatraḥ a hi kaścid aparatatraḥ a hi kaścid aparatatraḥ a hi kaścid aparatatraḥ a hi kaścid aparatatraḥ a hi kaścid aparatatra ca svayam atyataiḥ malaḥ sa deham ātma tveā upeyāt kṛtam api kathaṃcid yat duḥkha karam tat icchayā jahyāt sukha karam ca upādadīta smaret ca mayā idam jagat bimbam vicitram viracitam iti sarvaḥ hi lokaḥ spaṣṭam kāryam kṛtvā smarati mayā idam kṛtam iti yathā ca māyāvī svayam prasāritām māyām icchayā a āyāseā eva upasaṃharati evam śārīraḥ api imām sṛṣṭim upasaṃharet svakīyam api tāvat śarīram evam hita kriyā ādi adarśaāt ayāyyā cetaāt jagat prakriyā iti gamyate adhikam tu bhedaiḥ deśāt tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati yat sarvajñam sarva śakti brahma iti aśuddha buddha mukta svabhāvam śārīrāt adhikam ayat tat vayam jagataḥ sraṣṭṛ brūmaḥ doṣāḥ prasajyate a hi tasya hitam kiṃcid kartavyam asti ahitam vā parihartavyam iti amukta svabhāva tvāt a ca tasya jñā a pratibadhaḥ śakti pratibadhaḥ vā kvacid api asti sarvajña tvāt sarva śakti tvāt ca śārīraḥ tu a evaṃvidhaḥ tasmin prasajyate hita akaraṇa ādayaḥ doṣāḥ tu tam vayam jagataḥ sraṣṭāram brūmaḥ kutas etat bhedaiḥ deśāt ātmā vai are draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ matavyaḥ ididhyāsitavyaḥ saḥ u veṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ satā somya tadā saṃpaaḥ bhavati śārīraḥ ātmā iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ kartṛ karma ādi bhedaiḥ deśaḥ jīvāt adhikam brahma darśayati avabhedaiḥ deśaḥ api darśitaḥ tat tvam asi iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ katham bheda abhedau viruddhau saṃbhaveyātām ā eṣa doṣaḥ mahākāśa ghaṭa ākāśa yāyeḥ ubhaya saṃbhavasya tatra tatra pratiṣṭhāpita tvāt api ca yadā tat tvam asi iti evaṃjātīyakaiḥ abhedaiḥ deśe abhedaḥ pratibodhitaḥ bhavati apagatam bhavati tadā jīvasya saṃsāri tvam brahmaṇaḥ ca sraṣṭṛ tvam samastasya bheda vyavahārasya bādhita tvāt tatra kutas eva sṛṣṭiḥ kutas vā hita akaraṇa ādayaḥ doṣāḥ avidyā pratyupasthāpita āma rūpa kṛta kārya karaṇa saṃghāta upādhi aviveka kṛtā hi bhrātiḥ hita akaraṇa ādi lakṣaṇaḥ saṃsāraḥ a tu paramārthataḥ sti iti asakṛt avocāma a bādhite tu bheda vyavahāre saḥ veṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ iti evaṃjātīyake a bhedaiḥ deśeā avagamyamāam brahmaṇaḥ dhika tvam hita akaraṇa ādi doṣa prasaktim aśma ādi vat ca tad aupapattiḥ yathā ca loke keci mahārhāḥ maṇayaḥ vajra vaiḍūrya ādayaḥ aye madhyama vīryāḥ sūryakāta ādayaḥ aye prahīṇāḥ śva āyasa prakṣepaṇa arhāḥ pāṣāṇāḥ ca eka pṛthivī vyapāśrayāṇām api bījāām bahuvidham patra puṣpa phala gadha rasa ādi vaicitryam ca vicitrāṇi kāryāṇi bhavati evam ekasya api brahmaṇaḥ jīva prājña pṛthaktvam kārya vaicitryam ca upapadyate iti atas tad aupapattiḥ para parikalpita doṣa aupapattiḥ iti arthaḥ śruteḥ ca prāmāṇyāt vikārasya ca vācā ārambhaṇa mātra tvāt svapa dṛśya bhāva vaicitrya vat ca iti abhyuccayaḥ kṣīra vat hi upasaṃhāra darśa adhikaramam brahma ekam advitīyam jagataḥ kāraṇam iti yat uktam kasmāt upasaṃhāra darśaāt iha hi loke kulāla ādayaḥ ghaṭa paṭa ādīām kartāraḥ mṛd daṇḍa cakra sūtra salila ādi a eka kāraka upasaṃhāreṇa saṃgṛhīta sādhaāḥ sataḥ tat tat kāryam kurvāṇāḥ dṛśyate brahma ca asahāyam tava abhipretam tasya sati katham sraṣṭṛ tvam upapadyeta brahma jagat kāraṇam iti ced ā eṣa doṣaḥ yatas kṣīravat dravya svabhāva viśeṣāt upapadyate yathā hi loke kṣīram jalam vā svayam eva pariṇamate apekṣya bāhyam tathā iha api bhaviṣyati kṣīra ādi api dadhi ādi bhāvea pariṇamamāam apekṣate eva bāhyam auṣṇya ādikam katham ucyate kṣīra vat hi iti doṣaḥ svayam api hi kṣīram yām ca yāvatīm ca tāvatī eva tvāryate dadhi bhāvāya yadi ca svayam dadhi bhāva śīla tā syāt balāt dadhi bhāvam āpadyeta hi vāyuḥ ākāśaḥ vā balāt dadhi bhāvam āpadyate ca tasya pūrṇa tā saṃpādyate paripūrṇa śaktikam tu brahma śrutiḥ ca bhavati a tasya kāryam karaṇam ca vidyate a tad samaḥ ca abhyadhikaḥ ca dṛśyate parā asya śaktiḥ vividhā eva śrūyate svābhāvikī jñā abala kriyā ca iti tasmāt ekasya api brahmaṇaḥ vicitra śakti yogāt kṣīra ādi vat vicitra pariṇāmaḥ upapadyate deva ādi vat api loke syāt etat upapadyate kṣīra ādīām acetaāām a apekṣya api bāhyam dadhi ādi bhāvaḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt cetaāḥ kulāla ādayaḥ sādhaa sāmagrīm apekṣya eva tasmai tasmai kāryāya dṛśyate katham brahma cetaam sat asahāyam pravarteta iti deva ādi vat iti brūmaḥ yathā loke devāḥ pitaraḥ ṛṣayaḥ iti evamādayaḥ mahā prabhāvāḥ cetaāḥ api sataḥ apekṣya eva kiṃcid bāhyam abhidhyā a mātreṇa svatas eva śarīrāṇi śarīrāṇi ca irmimāṇā upalabhyate matra arthavāda itihāsa purāṇa prāmāṇyāt tatu ābhaḥ ca svatas eva tatū sṛjati balākā ca atareṇa eva śukram garbham dhatte padmiī ca a apekṣya kiṃcid sarotarāt sarotaram pratiṣṭhate evam brahma a apekṣya eva bāhyam svatas eva jagat srakṣyati sa yadi brūyāt ye ete deva ādayaḥ brahmaṇaḥ upāttāḥ te brahmaṇā bhavati śarīram eva hi acetaam deva ādīām tu cetaaḥ ātmā tatu ābhasya ca kṣudratara jatu bhakṣaṇāt lālā tatuḥ bhavati balākā ca staayituḥ avaśravaṇāt garbham dhatte padmiī ca cetaa prayuktā satī śarīreṇa sarotarāt sarotaram upasarpati vallī iva vṛkṣam a tu svayam eva acetasā sarotara upasarpaṇe vyāpriyate tasmai ā ete brahmaṇaḥ dṛṣṭātāḥ iti tam prati brūyāt ā ayam doṣaḥ kulāla ādi dṛṣṭāta vailakṣaṇya mātrasya vivakṣita tvāt iti yathā hi kulāla ādīām deva ādīām ca kulāla ādayaḥ kārya ārambhe bāhyam apekṣate a deva ādayaḥ tathā brahma a bāhyam apekṣiṣyata iti etāvat vayam vivakṣāmaḥ tasmāt yathā ekasya sāmarthyam dṛṣṭam tathā sarveṣām eva bhavitum arhati iti iti abhiprāyaḥ kṛtsa prasaktiḥ iravayava tva śabda kopaḥ vā kṛtsa prasakti adhikaraṇam brahma kṣīra ādi vat deva ādi vat ca a apekṣya bāhyam svayam pariṇamamāam jagataḥ kāraṇam iti sthitam śāstra artha pariśuddhaye tu kṛtsa prasaktiḥ kṛtsasya brahmaṇaḥ kārya rūpeṇa pariṇāmaḥ yadi brahma pṛthivī ādi vat sa avayavam abhaviṣyat tatas asya eka deśaḥ paryaṇaṃsyat eka deśaḥ ca avasthāsyata tu brahma śrutibhyaḥ uvagamyate iṣkalam iṣkriyam śātam iravadyam divyaḥ hi amūrtaḥ puruṣaḥ hi ajaḥ idam mahat bhūtam aatam apāram eva saḥ eṣa eti eti ātmā asthūlam aaṇu ityādyābhyaḥ sarva viśeṣa pratiṣedhibhyaḥ tatas ca eka deśa pariṇāma asaṃbhavāt kṛtsa pariṇāma prasaktau satyām mūla ucchedaḥ prasajyeta draṣṭavya tā upadeśa āarthakyam ca āpadyeta ayata dṛṣṭa tvāt kāryasya tad vyatiriktasya ca brahmaṇaḥ usaṃbhavāt aja tva ādi śabda vyākopaḥ ca atha etad doṣa parijihīrṣayā sāvayavam eva brahma abhyupagamyeta tathā api ye iḥ avayava tvasya pratipādakāḥ śabdāḥ udāhṛtāḥ te prakupyeyuḥ sāvayava tve ca āitya tva prasaṅgaḥ iti sarvathā ayam pakṣaḥ ghaṭayitum śakyate iti ākṣipati śruteḥ tu śabda mūla tvāt tuśabde ākṣepam pariharati khalu asmad pakṣe kaścid api doṣaḥ asti kutas śruteḥ yathā eva hi brahmaṇaḥ jagat utpattiḥ śrūyate evam vikāra vyatirekeṇa api śrūyate prakṛti vikārayoḥ vyapadeśāt sā iyam devatā aikṣata hata aham imāḥ tisraḥ devatāḥ āma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti tāvā asya mahimā tatas jyāyāḥ ca pūruṣaḥ pādaḥ usya viśvā tri pādasya amṛtam divi iti ca evaṃjātīyakāt tathā hṛdaya āyata atva vacaāt sat saṃpatti vacaāt ca yadi ca kṛtsam brahma kārya bhāvena upayuktam syāt satā somya tadā saṃpaaḥ bhavati iti suṣupti gatam viśeṣaṇam aupapam syāt brahmaṇā iti asaṃpaatvāt avikṛtasya ca brahmaṇaḥ bhāvāt tathā idriya gocaratva pratiṣedhāt brahmaṇaḥ vikārasya ca idriya gocaratva upapatteḥ tasmāt asti avikṛtam brahma śrūyamāṇa tvāt eva śrūyamāṇa tvāt eva śabda mūlam ca brahma śabda pramāṇakam edriya ādi pramāṇakam tat yathāśabdam abhyupagatavyam śabdaḥ ca ubhayam api brahmaṇaḥ pratipādayati akṛt sa prasaktim ca laukikāām api maṇi matra oṣadhi prabhṛtīām deśa kā laimitta vaicitrya vaśāt śaktayaḥ viruddhā eka kārya viṣayā dṛśyate tāḥ api tarkeṇa avagatum śakyate asya vastunaḥ etāvatya etad sahāyāḥ etad viṣayāḥ etad prayojaāḥ ca śaktayaḥ iti kim uta acitya svabhāvasya brahmaṇaḥ rūpam tathā ca āhuḥ paurāṇikāḥ acityāḥ khalu ye bhāvāḥ a tān tarkeṇa yojayet prakṛtibhyaḥ param yat ca tat acityasya lakṣaṇam iti tasmāt śabda mūlaḥ eva atīdriya artha yāthātmya adhigamaḥ śakyate viruddha ūrthaḥ pratyāyayitum ca brahma pariṇamate ca kṛtsam iti yadi iḥ avayavam brahma syāt ā eva pariṇameta kṛtsam eva vā pariṇameta atha kaścit rūpeṇa pariṇameta kaścit ca avatiṣṭheta iti rūpa bheda kalpāt sa avayavam eva prasajyeta kriyā viṣaye hi atirātre ṣoḍaśiam gṛhṇāti ā atirātre ṣoḍaśiam gṛhṇāti iti evaṃjātīyakāyām virodha pratītau api vikalpa āśrayaṇam virodha a parihāra kāraṇam bhavati iha tu vikalpa āśrayaṇe api a virodha parihāraḥ saṃbhavati tasmāt durghaṭam etat iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ avidyā kalpita rūpa bheda abhyupagamāt hi avidyā kalpitea rūpa bhedea sa avayavam vastu saṃpadyate a hi timira upahata iva cadramāḥ eva bhavati avidyā kalpitea ca ca āma rūpa lakṣaṇea rūpa bhede vyākṛta avyākṛta ātmake tattva airvacaīye brahma pariṇāma ādi sarva vyavahāra āspada tvam pratipadyate pāramārthike ca rūpeṇa sarva vyavahāra atītam apariṇatam avatiṣṭhate vācā ārambhaṇa mātra tvāt ca avidyā kalpitasya āma rūpa bhedasya iti brahmaṇaḥ kupyati ca iyam pariṇāma śrutiḥ pariṇāma pratipāda arthā tad pratipattau phala aavagamāt sarva vyavahāra hīa brahma ātma bhāva pratipāda arthā tu eṣā tad pratipattau phala avagamāt saḥ eṣaḥ eti eti ātmā iti upakramya āha abhayam vai jaaka prāptaḥ asi iti tasmāt asmad pakṣe a kaścid api doṣa prasaṅgaḥ asti hi api ca hi eva atra vivaditavyam katham ekasmin brahmaṇi sṛṣṭiḥ syāt iti yatas sṛṣṭiḥ paṭhyate a tatra rathāḥ a ratha yogāḥ bhavati atha sṛjate ityādiā loke pi deva ādiṣu māyāvya ādiṣu ca vicitrāḥ hasti aśva ādi sṛṣṭayaḥ dṛśyate tathā ekasmin api brahmaṇi sṛṣṭiḥ bhaviṣyati iti sva pakṣa doṣāt ca pareṣām api eṣa samāaḥ sva pakṣa doṣaḥ hi hi a paricchiam śabda ādi hīam pradhāam sa avayavasya śabda ādimataḥ kāryasya kāraṇam iti sva pakṣaḥ tatra api iḥ sa prasaktiḥ iḥ avayava tvāt pradhā asya iḥ avayava tva abhyupagama kopaḥ vā taiḥ iḥ avayavam abhyupagamyate sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi hi trayaḥ guṇāḥ teṣām sāmya avasthā taiḥ eva avayavaiḥ tat sa avayavam iti aivaṃjātīyake sa avayava tve prakṛtaḥ doṣaḥ parihartum pāryate yatas sattva rajaḥ tamasām api ekaikasya ekaikam eva ca itara dvaya ā u gṛhītam sajātīyasya prapañcasya iti sva pakṣa doṣa prasaṅgasya tarka apratiṣṭhāāt sāvayavatvam eva iti ced evam api aitya tva ādi doṣa prasaṅgaḥ atha śaktayaḥ eva kārya vaicitrya sūcitāḥ avayavāḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ tāḥ tu aviśiṣṭāḥ tathā aṇu vādiḥ api aṇuḥ aṇvatareṇa saṃyujyamānaḥ yadi saṃyujyeta tatas aṇu mātra tva prasaṅgaḥ saṃyujyeta tathā api iḥ avayava tva abhyupagama kopaḥ iti sva pakṣe pi eṣa doṣaḥ samāa tvāt ca pakṣe upakṣeptavyaḥ bhavati parihṛtaḥ tu sva pakṣe doṣaḥ sarva upetā ca tad darśaāt sarva upeta adhikaraṇam ekasya api brahmaṇaḥ vicitra śakti yogāt upapadyate vicitraḥ vikāra prapañcaḥ iti uktam tat puas katham avagamyate vicitra śakti yuktam param brahma iti tat ucyate sarva upetā ca tad darśaāt sarva śakti yuktā ca parā devatā iti abhyupagatavyam kutas tad darśaāt tathā hi darśayati śrutiḥ sarva śakti yogam parasyāḥ devatāyāḥ sarva karmā sarva kāmaḥ sarva rasaḥ sarvam idam abhyāttaḥ vākya ādaraḥ satya kāmaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vid etasya vai akṣarasya praśāsae gārgi sūryācadramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ vikaraṇa tvā ā iti ced tat uktam syāt etat vikaraṇām parām devatām śāsti śāstram acakṣuṣkam aśrotram avāgamaāḥ iti evaṃjātīyakam katham sā sarva śakti yuktā api satī kāryāya prabhavet deva ādayaḥ hi cetaāḥ sarva śakti yuktāḥ api sataḥ ādhyātmika kārya karaṇa saṃpaāḥ eva tasmai tasmai kāryāya prabhavataḥ vijñāyate katham ca eti eti iti pratiṣiddha sarva viśeṣāyāḥ devatāyāḥ sarva śakti yogaḥ saṃbhavet iti ced yat atra vaktavyam tat purastāt eva uktam śruti avagāhyam eva idam ati gambhīram brahma a tarka avagāhyam a ca yathā ekasya sāmarthyam dṛṣṭam bhavitavyam iti bhavitavyam iti pratiṣiddha sarve viśeṣasya api brahmaṇaḥ sarva śakti yogaḥ saṃbhavati iti etat api avidyā kalpita rūpa bheda upayāseā uktam eva tathā ca śāstram a pāṇi pādaḥ grahītā paśyati a cakṣuḥ sa śrṛṇoti a karṇaḥ iti a karaṇasya api brahmaṇaḥ sarva sāmarthya yogam darśayati a prayoja avat tvāt prayoja avat tva adhikaraṇam ayathā puas ceta akartṛ tvam jagataḥ ākṣipati a khalu cetaaḥ paramātmā idam jagat bimbam viracayitum arhati kutas prayoja avat tvāt pravṛttīām cetao hi loke buddhi pūrva kārī puruṣaḥ mada upakramām api tāvat pravṛttim ātma prayoja āupayogiīm ārabhamāṇaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kim uta gurutara saṃrambhām bhavati ca loka prasiddhi auvādiī śrutiḥ a vai are sarvasya kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati ātmā astu kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati iti gurutara saṃrambhā ca iyam pravṛttiḥ yat uccāvaca prapañcam jagat bimbam viracayitavyam yadi iyam api pravṛttiḥ cetaasya paramātmaaḥ ātma prayoja upayogiī parikalpyeta paritṛpta tvam paramātmaaḥ śrūyamāṇam bādhyeta prayoja a abhāve vā pravṛtti abhāvaḥ api syāt atha saḥ buddhi aparādhāt atareṇa eva ātma prayojaam pravartamāaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tathā paramātmā api pravartiṣyate iti ucyeta tathā sati sarvajña tvam paramātmanaḥ śrūyamāṇam bādhyeta tasmāt aśliṣṭā cetaāt sṛṣṭiḥ iti loka vat tu līlā kaivalyam tuśabde ākṣepam pariharati yathā loke kasyacid āpta eṣaṇasya rājñaḥ rāja amātyasya vā vyatiriktam kiṃcid kevalam līlā rūpāḥ pravṛttayaḥ krīḍā vihāreṣu bhavati yathā ca ucchvāsa praśvāsa ādayaḥ abhisaṃdhāya bāhyam kiṃcid svabhāvāt eva saṃbhavati evam īśvarasya api a apekṣya kiṃcid svabhāvāt eva kevalam līlā rūpā pravṛttiḥ bhaviṣyati a hi īśvarasya śrutitaḥ vā saṃbhavati a ca svabhāvaḥ paryauyoktum śakyate yadi api asmākam iyam gurutara saṃrambhā iva ābhāti tathā api parameśvarasya līlā eva kevalā iyam aparimita śakti tvāt yadi loke līlāsu api kiṃcid sūkṣmam utprekṣyeta tathā api kiṃcid utprekṣitum śakyate āpta kāma śruteḥ āpī apravṛttiḥ vā sṛṣṭi śruteḥ sarvajña śruteḥ ca ca iyam paramārtha viṣayā sṛṣṭi śrutiḥ avidyā kalpita āma rūpa vyavahāra gocara tvāt brahma ātma bhāva pratipāda apara tvāt ca iti etat api ā eva vismartavyam vaiṣamya aairghṛṇye a sāpekṣa tvāt tathā hi darśayati vaiṣamya airghṛṇya adhikaraṇam ca jagat jama ādi hetu tvam īśvarasya ākṣipyate pratijñātasya arthasya dṛḍhīkaraṇāya eśvaraḥ jagataḥ kāraṇam upapadyate kutas vaiṣamya airghṛṇya prasaṅgāt kāṃścid atyata sukha bhājaḥ karoti deva ādī kāṃścid atyata duḥkha bhājaḥ paśu ādī madhyama bhoga bhājaḥ mauṣya ādī iti evam viṣamām sṛṣṭim irmimāṇasya īśvarasya rāga dveṣa upapatteḥ śruti smṛti avadhārita svaccha tvāt īśvara svabhāva vilopaḥ prasajyeta tathā khala jaaiḥ api jugupsitam ati krūra tvam duḥkha yoga vidhāāt sarva prajā upasaṃhārāt ca prasajyeta tasmāt vaiṣamya airghṛṇya prasaṅgāḥ eśvaraḥ kāraṇam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ vaiṣamya aairghṛṇye eśvarasya prasajyete kasmāt sāpekṣa tvāt yadi hi irapekṣaḥ kevalaḥ īśvaraḥ viṣamām sṛṣṭim syātām etau doṣau vaiṣamyam airghṛṇyam ca asya tu ir apekṣasya irmātṛ tvam asti sa apekṣaḥ hi īśvaraḥ viṣamām sṛṣṭim irmimīte kim apekṣate iti ced dharma adharmau apekṣate iti vadāmaḥ atas viṣamā sṛṣṭiḥ iti ā ayam īśvarasya aparādhaḥ īśvaraḥ tu parjaya vat draṣṭavyaḥ yathā hi parjayaḥ vrīhi yava ādi sṛṣṭau sādhāraṇam kāraṇam bhavati vrīhi yava ādi vaiṣamye tu tad tad bīja gatāi eva a sādhāraṇāi sāmarthyāi bhavati evam īśvaraḥ deva mauṣya ādi sṛṣṭau sādhāraṇam kāraṇam bhavati deva mauṣya ādi vaiṣamye tu eva asādhāraṇāi karmāṇi kāraṇāi bhavati evam īśvaraḥ sa apekṣa tvāt a vaiṣamya airghṛṇyābhyām duṣyati katham avagamyate sa apekṣaḥ saṃsāram saṃsāram irmimīta iti tathā hi darśayati śrutiḥ eṣa hi eva sādhu karma kārayati tam yam ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ uiīṣate eṣaḥ u eva asādhu karma kārayati tam yam adhas iīṣate puṇyaḥ vai karmaṇā bhū pāpaḥ iti ca smṛtiḥ api prāṇi karma viśeṣa apekṣam eva īśvarasya āugrahītṛ tvam igrahītṛ tvam ca darśayati ye yathā mām prapadyate tān tathā eva bhajāmi aham / iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ a karma avibhāgāt iti ce ā ādi tvāt sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam iti prāk sṛṣṭeḥ avibhāga avadhāraṇā ā asti karma yat apekṣya viṣamā sṛṣṭiḥ syāt sṛṣṭi uttara kālam hi śarīra ādi vibhāga apekṣam karma karma apekṣaḥ ca śarīra ādi vibhāgaḥ iti itaretara āśraya tvam prasajyeta atas vibhāgāt ūrdhvam karma apekṣaḥ īśvaraḥ pravartatām prāk vibhāgāt vaicitrya aimittasya karmaṇaḥ bhāvāt tulyā eva ādyā sṛṣṭiḥ ced ā eṣa doṣaḥ a ādi tvāt saṃsārasya bhavet eṣa doṣaḥ yadi ādimā ayam saṃsāraḥ syāt aādau tu saṃsāre bīja aṅkura vat karmaṇaḥ sarga vaiṣamyasya ca pravṛttiḥ virudhyate katham avagamyate a ādiḥ eṣa saṃsāraḥ iti atas uttaram paṭhati upapadyate ca api upalabhyate ca upapadyate ca saṃsārasya a ādi tvam ādimat tve hi saṃsārasya akasmāt udbhūteḥ api ca sukha duḥkha udbhūti prasaṅgaḥ akṛta abhyāgama kṛta vipraṇāśa prasaṅgaḥ ca sukha duḥkha ādi vaiṣamyasya ca īśvaraḥ vaiṣamya hetuḥ iti uktam ca avidyā kevalā vaiṣamyasya kāraṇam eka rūpa tvāt rāga ādi kleśa vāsa ākṣipta karma apekṣā tu avidyā vaiṣamya karī syāt a ca karma atareṇa śarīram saṃbhavati a ca śarīram atareṇa karma saṃbhavati iti itaretara āśraya tva prasaṅgaḥ a ādi tve tu a kaścid doṣaḥ bhavati upalabhyate ca saṃsārasya a ādi tvam śruti smṛtyoḥ śrutau tāvat iti sarga pramukhe śārīram a ādiḥ saṃsāraḥ iti darśayati ādimattve tu prāk sa katham jīva śabde sarga pramukhe bhilapyeta ca dhārayiṣyati iti atas bhilapyeta a āgatāt hi atītaḥ balīyāḥ bhavati sūryācadramasau dhātā yathāpūrvam akalpayat iti ca matra varṇaḥ pūrva kalpa sadbhāvam darśayati smṛtau api a ādi tvam saṃsārasya upalabhyate a rūpam asya iha tathā upalabhyate a ca ādiḥ a ca saṃpratiṣṭhā iti purāṇe ca atīta a āgatāām ca kalpāām a parimāṇam asti iti sthāpitam sarva dharma upapatteḥ ca sarva dharma upapatti adhikaraṇam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam prakṛtiḥ ca iti asmi avadhārite veda arthe paraiḥ upakṣiptā vilakṣaṇa tva ādī doṣā paryahārṣīt ācāryaḥ idāīm parapakṣa pratiṣedha pradhāam prakaraṇam prāripsamāṇaḥ sva pakṣa parigraha pradhāam prakaraṇam upasaṃharati yasmāt asmi brahmaṇi kāraṇe parigṛhyamāṇe pradarśitea prakāreṇa sarve kāraṇa dharmāḥ upapadyate sarvajñam sarva śakti mahā māyam ca brahma iti tasmāt idam aupaiṣadam iti iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye dvitīya adhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ dvitīyaḥ udhyāyaḥ dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ca yadi api idam śāstram pravṛttam a tarka śāstra vat kevalābhiḥ yuktibhiḥ kaṃcid siddhātam sādhayitum dūṣayitum vā pravṛttam tathā api vyācakṣāṇaiḥ samyak darśa a pratipakṣa bhūtāi sāṃkhya ādi darśaāi tad arthaḥ paraḥ pādaḥ pravartate ca samyak darśa artha tvāt sva pakṣa sthāpaam prathamam kṛtam tat vyabhyarhitam para pakṣa pratyākhyāāt iti mumukṣūṇām mokṣa eva kevalam kartum yuktam kim para pakṣaiḥ ākaraṇea para dveṣa karaṇea bāḍham evam tathā api sāṃkhya ādi tatrāṇi pravṛttāy upalabhya bhavet api samyak darśaāya upādeyāi iti apekṣā tathā sarvajña bhāṣita tvāt ca śraddhā ca te iti atas tad asāra tā upapādaāya prayatyate īkṣateḥ āśabdam kāmāt ca sarve vyākhyātāḥ vyākhyātāḥ iti ca pūrvatra api sāṃkhya ādi pakṣa pratikṣepaḥ kṛtaḥ kim tat ucyate sāṃkhya ādayaḥ api udāhṛtya sva pakṣa āuguṇyena eva yojayataḥ vyācakṣate teṣām yat tat samyak vyākhyāam iti etāvat pūrvam kṛtam iha tu vākyaiḥ apekṣaḥ svatatraḥ tad yukti pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate iti eṣa viśeṣaḥ tatra sāṃkhyāḥ yathā ghaṭa śarāva ādayaḥ bhedāḥ mṛd ātma tayā avīyamāāḥ mṛd ātmaka sāmāya pūrvakāḥ loke dṛṣṭāḥ tathā sarve eva bāhya ādhyātmikāḥ bhedāḥ sukha duḥkha moha ātma tayā avīyamānāḥ sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka sāmāya pūrvakāḥ bhavitum arhati yat sukha duḥkha moha ātmakam sāmāyam tat triguṇam pradhāam mṛd vat acetaam cetaasya puruṣasya artham sādhayitum svabhāve eva vicitreṇa vikāra ātmaā pravartata iti tathā parimāṇa ādibhiḥ api liṅgaiḥ tat eva pradhāam tatra vadāmaḥ yadi ācetaam loke svatatram kiṃcid vikārāḥ dṛṣṭam geha prāsāda śaya āsa avihāra bhūmi ādayaḥ hi loke prajñāvadbhiḥ śilpibhiḥ yathākālam sukha duḥkha prāpti parihāra yogyāḥ racitāḥ dṛśyate tathā idam jagat akhilam pṛthivī ādi ā ā karma phala upabhoga yogyam bāhyam ādhyātmikam ca śarīra ādi dṛśyamāam prajñāvadbhiḥ saṃbhāvitatamaiḥ śilpibhiḥ ālocayitum aśakyam sat katham acetaam pradhāam racayet loṣṭa pāṣāṇa ādiṣu adṛṣṭa tvāt mṛd ādiṣu api kumbhakāra ādi adhiṣṭhiteṣu viśiṣṭa ākārā racaā dṛśyate tadvat pradhāasya api cetaātara adhiṣṭhita tva prasaṅgaḥ a ca mṛd ādi upādā svarūpa vyapāśrayeṇa eva dharmeṇa mūla kāraṇam avadhāraṇīyam a bāhya kumbhakāra ādi vyapāśrayeṇa iti kiṃci asti a ca evam sati kiṃcid virudhyate pratyuta śrutiḥ ceta a kāraṇa samarpaṇāt atas ca hetoḥ ācetaam jagat kāraṇam aumātavyam bhavati ca iti caśabde hetoḥ asiddhim hi bāhya ādhyātmikāām bhedāām sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka tayā avayaḥ upapadyate sukha ādīām ca atara tva pratīteḥ śabda ādīām ca a tad rūpa tva pratīteḥ taimitta tva pratīteḥ ca śabda ādi aviśeṣe ca bhāva a viśeṣāt sukha ādi viśeṣa upalabdheḥ tathā parimitāām bhedāām mūla aṅkura ādīām saṃsarga pūrvaka tvam dṛṣṭvā bāhya ādhyātmikāām bhedāām parimita tvāt saṃsarga pūrvaka tvam sattva rajaḥ tamasām api saṃsarga pūrvaka tva prasaṅgaḥ parimita tva aviśeṣāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tu prekṣā pūrvakaiḥ mitāām śaya āsa ādīām dṛṣṭaḥ iti a bhāva kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt bāhya ādhyātmikāām bhedāām aceta apūrvaka tvam śakyam kalpayitum pravṛtteḥ ca āstām tāvat iyam racaā tad siddhi arthā yā pravṛttiḥ sāmya avasthāāt pracyutiḥ sattva rajaḥ tamasām aṅga aṅgi bhāva rūpa āpattiḥ viśiṣṭa kārya abhimukha pravṛtti tā sā api ācetaasya pradhāasya svatatrasya upapadyate mṛd ādiṣu ratha ādiṣu ca hi mṛd ādayaḥ ratha ādayaḥ vā svayam acetaāḥ sataḥ cetaaiḥ kulāla ādibhiḥ aśva ādibhiḥ vā adhiṣṭhitāḥ viśiṣṭa kārya abhimukha pravṛttayaḥ dṛśyate dṛṣṭāt ca adṛṣṭa siddhiḥ atas pravṛtti aupapatteḥ api hetoḥ ācetaam jagat kāraṇam aumātavyam bhavati pravṛttiḥ kevalasya a dṛṣṭā satyam etat tathā api ratha ādeḥ a cetaasya pravṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā a tu a ceta a saṃyuktasya ceta asya pravṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā kim atra yuktam pravṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā tasya sā uta yat saṃprayuktasya dṛṣṭā tasya eva sā iti yasmi dṛśyate pravṛttiḥ tasya eva sā iti yuktam ubhayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt a tu kevalaḥ cetaḥ ratha ādi vat pratyakṣaḥ pravṛtti āśraya deha ādi saṃyuktasya eva tu sadbhāva siddhiḥ kevala aceta aratha ādi vailakṣaṇyam jīvat dehasya dṛṣṭam iti atas eva ca pratyakṣe dehe sati caitayasya darśaāt asati ca a darśaāt dehasya eva caitayam api iti lokāyatikāḥ tasmāt acetaasya eva pravṛttiḥ iti tat abhidhīyate a brūmaḥ tasya sā iti bhavatu tasya eva sā sā tu cetaāt bhavati iti brūmaḥ tad bhāve bhāvāt tad abhāve ca abhāvāt yathā kāṣṭha ādi vyapāśrayā api dāha prakāśa ādi lakṣaṇā vikriyā ca kevale jvalae jvalaāt eva bhavati tad saṃyoge darśaāt tad viyoge ca adarśaāt tadvat lokāyatikāām api cetaaḥ eva ratha ādīām pravartakaḥ dṛṣṭa iti avipratiṣiddham cetaasya pravartaka tvam tava deha ādi saṃyuktasya api ātmanaḥ vijñāa sva rūpa mātra vyatirekeṇa pravṛtti aupapatteḥ aupapaam pravartaka tvam iti ced a ayaskāta vat rūpa ādi vat ca pravṛtti rahitasya api pravartaka tva upapatteḥ yathā āyaskātaḥ maṇiḥ svayam pravṛtti rahitaḥ api ayasaḥ pravartakaḥ bhavati yathā ca rūpa ādayaḥ viṣayāḥ svayam pravṛtti rahitāḥ api cakṣuḥ ādīām pravartakā bhavati evam pravṛtti rahitaḥ upi īśvaraḥ sarva gataḥ sarva ātmā sarvajñaḥ sarva śaktiḥ ca sa sarvam pravartayet iti upapaam ekatvāt pravartya abhāve pravartaka tva aupapattiḥ iti ced a avidyā pratyupasthāpita āma rūpa māyā āveśa vaśe asakṛt pratyukta tvāt tasmāt saṃbhavati pravṛttiḥ sarvajña kāraṇa tve a tu aceta akāraṇa tve payaḥ mbu vat ced tatra api syāt etat yathā kṣīram acetaam svabhāvena eva vatsa vivṛddhi artham pravartate yathā ca jalam acetaam svabhāvea eva loka upakārāya syadate evam pradhāam api acetaam svabhāvea eva puruṣa artha siddhaye pravartiṣyate iti ā etat sādhu ucyate yatas tatra api payaḥ mbuoḥ cetaḥ dhiṣṭhitayoḥ eva ubhaya vādi prasiddhe ratha ādau acetae kevale pravṛtti adarśaāt śāstram ca yā upsu tiṣṭha yā upotaraḥ yamayati etasya vai akṣarasya praśāsae gārgi adyaḥ syadate iti evaṃjātīyakam samastasya loka parispaditasya īśvara adhiṣṭhita tām śrāvayati tasmāt sādhya pakṣa aikṣipta tvāt payaḥ mbu vat iti aupayāsaḥ cetaāyāḥ ca ca payasaḥ pravartaka tva upapatteḥ ca payasaḥ ākṛṣyamāṇa tvāt ca ambu opi atyatama apekṣā cetaḥ apekṣa tvam tu sarvatra upadarśitam upasaṃhāra darśa iti kṣīra vat hi iti atra tu bāhya aimittaiḥ apekṣam api sva āśrayam kāryam bhavati iti etat loka dṛṣṭyā śāstra dṛṣṭyā sarvatra eva īśvara apekṣa tvam āpadyamāam a parāṇudyate vyatireka avasthiteḥ ca a apekṣa tvāt sāṃkhyāām trayaḥ guṇāḥ sāmye avatiṣṭhamāāḥ a tu tad vyatirekeṇa pradhāasya pravartakam vā kiṃcid bāhyam apekṣyam avasthitam asti puruṣaḥ tu udāsīḥ a pravartakaḥ a iti atoapekṣam pradhāam a apekṣa tvāt ca kadācid pradhāam mahat ādi ākāreṇa pariṇamate pariṇamate iti etat ayuktam īśvarasya tu sarvajña tvāt sarva śakti tva a mahāmāya tvāt ca pravṛtti apravṛttī virudhyete ayatra abhāvāt ca ca tṛṇa ādi vat syāt etat yathā tṛṇa pallava udaka ādi imitta ataraiḥ apekṣam svabhāvāt eva kṣīra ādi ākāreṇa pariṇamate evam pradhāam api mahat ādi ākāreṇa pariṇaṃsyate iti katham ca imitta ataraiḥ apekṣam tṛṇa ādi iti gamyate imitta atara aupalambhāt yadi hi kiṃcid imitta ataram upalabhemahi tatas yathākāmam tṛṇa ādi upādāya kṣīram saṃpādayemahi a tu saṃpādayāmahe tasmāt svābhāvikaḥ tṛṇa ādeḥ pariṇāmaḥ tathā pradhā asya api syāt iti atra ucyate bhavet tṛṇa ādi vat svābhāvikaḥ pradhā asya api pariṇāmaḥ yadi tṛṇa ādeḥ api svābhāvikaḥ pariṇāmaḥ abhyupagamyeta a tu abhyupagamyate imitta atara upalabdheḥ katham imitta atara upalabdhiḥ ayatra abhāvāt eva hi upabhuktam tṛṇa ādi kṣīrībhavati a prahīṇam aaḍuha ādi upabhuktam vā yadi hi tṛṇa ādi kṣīrībhavet ca yathākāmam śakyam saṃpādayitum iti etāvatā bhavati bhavati hi kiṃcid kāryam māuṣa saṃpādyam kiṃcid daiva saṃpādyam mauṣyāḥ api tṛṇa ādi upādāya kṣīram saṃpādayitum prabhūtam hi kṣīram kāmayamāṇaḥ prabhūtam ghāsam cārayati tatas ca prabhūtam kṣīram labhate tasmāt tṛṇa ādi vat svābhāvikaḥ pradhā asya pariṇāmaḥ abhyupagame api artha abhāvāt svābhāvikī pradhā asya pravṛttiḥ bhavati iti sthāpitam atha api bhavataḥ svābhāvikīm eva pradhā asya pravṛttim abhyupagacchema tathā api doṣaḥ uṣajyeta eva kutas artha abhāvāt yadi tāvat svābhāvikī pradhā asya pravṛttiḥ a kiṃcid ayat iha apekṣate iti ucyeta tatas yathā eva sahakāri kiṃcid apekṣate evam kiṃcid apekṣiṣyate iti atas pradhāam puruṣasya artham sādhayitum pravartate iti iyam pratijñā hīyeta sa yadi brūyāt sahakārī eva kevalam āpekṣate a prayojaam api iti tathā api vivektavyam bhogaḥ vā syāt apavargaḥ vā ubhayam vā iti bhogaḥ ced kīdṛśaḥ ādheya atiśayasya puruṣasya bhogaḥ bhavet mokṣa prasaṅgaḥ ca apavargaḥ ced prāk api pravṛtteḥ apavargasya siddha tvāt pravṛttiḥ aarthikā syāt śabda ādi aupalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ ca ubhaya arthatā abhyupagame pi bhoktavyāām pradhā amātrāṇām mokṣa prasaṅgaḥ eva pravṛttiḥ hi saṃbhavati ca puruṣasya dṛkśakti sarga śakti vaiyarthya bhayāt ced pravṛttiḥ tarhi dṛkśakti auccheda vat sarga śakti aucchedāt saṃsāra aucchedāt mokṣa prasaṅgaḥ eva tasmāt pradhā asya puruṣa arthā pravṛttiḥ iti etat ayuktam puruṣa aśma vat iti ced tathā syāt etat yathā kaścid puruṣaḥ pravṛtti śakti vihīaḥ paṅguḥ aparam puruṣam pravṛtti śakti saṃpaam dṛś śakti vihīam adham adhiṣṭhāya pravartayati yathā vā ayaskātaḥ śmā svayam a pravartamānaḥ pi ayaḥ pravartayati evam puruṣaḥ pravartayiṣyati iti atra ucyate tathā api tāvat doṣaḥ āpatati pradhāasya svatatrasya pravṛtti abhyupagamāt puruṣasya ca pravartaka tva abhyupagamāt katham ca udāsīḥ puruṣaḥ pradhām pravartayet paṅguḥ api hi puruṣam vāc ādibhiḥ pravartayati puruṣasya kaścid api sti ca āpi ayaskāta vat saṃidhi mātreṇa pravartayet pravṛtti itya tva prasaṅgāt ayaskātasya tu aitya saṃidheḥ asti sva vyāpāraḥ saṃidhiḥ parimārja ādi apekṣā ca asya asti iti aupayāsaḥ puruṣa aśma vat iti tathā puruṣasya ca audāsīyāt tṛtīyasya ca tayoḥ saṃbadhayituḥ abhāvāt saṃbadhā upapattiḥ yogyatā aimitte ca saṃbadhe yogyatā ucchedāt pūrvavat ca iha api artha abhāvaḥ vikalpayitavyaḥ paramātma as tu svarūpa vyapāśrayam audāsīyam māyā vyapāśrayam ca pravartaka tvam iti asti atiśayaḥ aṅgi tva aupapatteḥ ca itas ca a pradhā asya pravṛttiḥ avakalpate yat hi sattva rajaḥ tamasām utsṛjya sāmyea svarūpa mātreṇa avasthāam sā pradhā avasthā tasyām avasthāyām aapekṣa svarūpāṇām svarūpa praṇāśa bhayāt parasparam pratyaṅga aṅgi bhāva aupapatteḥ bāhyasya ca kasyacid kṣobhayituḥ abhāvāt guṇa vaiṣamyaimittaḥ mahat ādi utpādaḥ asti syāt ayathā umitau ca jña śakti viyogāt atha api syāt ayathā vayam yathā ā ayam doṣaḥ prasajyeta a hi a apekṣa svabhāvāḥ kūṭasthāḥ ca asmābhiḥ guṇāḥ abhyupagamyate pramāṇa abhāvāt tu guṇāām svabhāvaḥ bhyupagamyate yathā yathā kārya utpādaḥ upapadyate tathā tathā eteṣām svabhāvaḥ bhyupagatavyaḥ calam guṇa vṛttam iti ca asti abhyupagamaḥ tasmāt sāmya avasthāyām api vaiṣamya upagama yogyāḥ eva guṇāḥ avatiṣṭhate iti evam api pradhā asya jña śakti viyogāt pūrva uktāḥ doṣāḥ tad avasthāḥ eva jña śaktim api tu ekam vaiṣamyam bhajera vā imitta abhāva aviśeṣāt sarvadā eva vaiṣamyam bhajera iti prasajyate eva ayam doṣaḥ vipratiṣedhāt ca asamañjasam paraspara viruddhaḥ ca ayam sāṃkhyāām abhyupagamaḥ kvacid sapta idriyāṇi aukrāmati kvacid ekādaśa tathā virodhaḥ ca smṛtyā tasmāt api asamañjasam sāṃkhyāām api asamañjasam eva tapya tāpakayoḥ jāti atara bhāva abhyupagamāt ekam hi brahma sarva ātmakam sarvasya prapañcasya kāraṇam abhyupagacchatām ekasya eva ātmanaḥ viśeṣau tapya tāpakau a jātyatara bhūtau iti abhyupagatavyam syāt yadi ca etau tapya tāpakau ekasya ātmanaḥ viśeṣau syātām sa tābhyām tapya tāpakābhyām iḥ mucyeta iti tāpa upaśātaye samyak darśam upadiśat śāstram aarthakam syāt hi auṣṇya prakāśa dharmasya pradīpasya tad avasthasya eva tābhyām upapadyate yaḥ api jala taraṅga vīcī phe ādi upayāsaḥ tatra api jala ātma antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar anta ekasya vīci ādayaḥ viśeṣāḥ āvirbhāva tirobhāva rūpeṇa eva iti vīci ādibhiḥ eḥ mokṣaḥ prasiddhaḥ ca ayam tapya tāpakayoḥ jātyatara bhāvaḥ loke tathā hi arthī ca arthaḥ lakṣyete yadi arthiḥ a syāt yasya arthiḥ yad viṣayam arthi tvam sa tasya iti asiddhaḥ eva iti a tasya tad viṣayam arthi tvam syāt yathā prakāśa ātmaaḥ pradīpasya iti asiddhaḥ eva iti a tasya tad viṣayam arthi tvam bhavati aprāpte hi artha īrthi tvam syāt iti tathā arthasya api artha tvam syāt yadi syāt svārtha tvam eva syāt ca etat asti saṃbadhi śabdau hi etau arthī ca arthaḥ ca iti dvayoḥ ca saṃbadhioḥ syāt aikasya eva tasmāt bhiau etau artha arthiau tathā artha arthiau api arthioukūlaḥ arthaḥ pratikūlaḥ aarthaḥ tābhyām ekaḥ paryāyeṇa ubhābhyām saṃbadhyate tatra arthasya alpīyaḥ tvāt bhūyaḥ tvāt ca aarthasya ubhau api artha arthau aarthaḥ eva iti tāpakaḥ saḥ ucyate tapyaḥ tu puruṣaḥ yaḥ ekaḥ paryāyeṇa ubhābhyām saṃbadhyate iti tayoḥ tapya tāpakayoḥ eka ātmatāyām mokṣa a upapattiḥ jāti atara bhāve tu tad saṃyoga hetu parihārāt syāt api kadācid mokṣa upapattiḥ iti atra ucyate a ekatvāt eva tapya tāpaka bhāva aupapatteḥ bhavet eṣa doṣaḥ yadi eka ātma tāyām tapya tāpakau viṣaya viṣayi bhāvam pratipadyeyātām a tu etat asti ekatvāt eva a hi agir ekaḥ sa svam ātmā aam dahati prakāśayati vā sati api auṣṇya prakāśa ādi dharma bhede pariṇāmi tve ca kim u kūṭasthe brahmaṇi ekasmin tapya tāpaka bhāvaḥ saṃbhavet kva ayam tapya tāpaka bhāvaḥ syāt iti ucyate kim paśyasi karma bhūtaḥ jīvat dehaḥ tapyaḥ tāpakaḥ savitā iti duḥkham sā cetayituḥ dehasya yadi hi dehasya eva taptiḥ syāt sā deha āśe svayam eva aśyati iti syāt iti ucyate deha abhāve pi kevalasya taptiḥ dṛṣṭā ca tvayā api taptiḥ āma vikriyā cetayituḥ kevalasya iṣyate deha cetaayoḥ saṃhata tvam aśuddhi ādi doṣa prasaṅgāt ca tapteḥ eva taptim abhyupagacchasi katham tava api tapya tāpaka bhāvaḥ sattvam tapyam tāpakam rajaḥ iti ced a tābhyām cetaasya saṃhata tva aupapatteḥ sattva aurodhi tvāt cetaaḥ api tapyate iva iti ced paramārthataḥ tarhi tapyate iti āpatati iva śabda prayogāt ced tapyate eva śabdaḥ doṣāya hi ḍuṇḍubhaḥ sarpaḥ iva iti etāvatā sa viṣaḥ bhavati sarpaḥ vā ḍuṇḍubha sarpaḥ iva iti etāvatā irviṣaḥ bhavati atas ca avidyā kṛtaḥ yam tapya tāpaka bhāvaḥ as pāramārthikaḥ iti abhyupagatavyam iti sati mama api kiṃcid duṣyati atha pāramārthikam eva tapya tvam abhyupagacchasi tava eva sutarām aiḥ mokṣaḥ prasajyeta ityatva abhyupagamāt ca tāpakasya tapya tāpaka śaktyoḥ ityatve pi saimitta saṃyoga apekṣa tvāt tapteḥ saṃyoga aimitta ādarśa ai vṛttau ātyatikaḥ saṃyoga uparamaḥ tatas ca ātyatikaḥ mokṣaḥ iti ced iti adarśaasya tamasaḥ ityatva abhyupagamāt guṇāām ca udbhava abhibhavayoḥ aiyata tvāt aiyataḥ saṃyoga aimitta uparamaḥ iti viyogasya api aiyata tvāt sāṃkhyasya eva aiḥ mokṣa uparihāryaḥ syāt aupaiṣadasya tu ātma ekatva abhyupagamāt ekasya ca viṣaya viṣayi bhāva aupapatteḥ vikāra bhedasya ca vācā
