ārambhaṇa mātra tva śravaṇāt vyavahāre tu yatra yathā dṛṣṭaḥ tapya tāpaka bhāvaḥ tatra tathā eva saḥ iti a codayitavyaḥ parihartavyaḥ vā bhavati pradhā a kāraṇa vādaḥ irākṛtaḥ paramāṇu kāraṇa vādaḥ idāīm irākartavyaḥ tatra ādau tāvat doṣaḥ utprekṣyate sa pratisamādhīyate tatra ayam vaiśeṣikāṇām abhyupagamaḥ kāraṇa dravya samavāyiḥ guṇāḥ kārya dravye guṇa ātaram ārabhate śuklebhyaḥ tatubhyaḥ śuklasya paṭasya prasava darśaāt tad viparyaya a darśaāt ca tasmāt cetaasya brahmaṇaḥ jagat kāraṇa tve abhyupagamyamāe kārye api jagati samaveyāt tad adarśaāt tu a cetaam brahma jagat kāraṇam bhavitum arhati iti imam abhyupagamam tadīyayā eva prakriyayā vyabhicārayati mahat dīrghavat vā hrasva parimaṇḍalābhyām mahat dīrgha adhikaraṇam eṣā teṣām prakriyā paramāṇavaḥ kila kaṃcid kālam aārabdha kāryāḥ yathāyogam rūpa ādimataḥ pārimāṇḍalya parimāṇāḥ ca tiṣṭhati te ca paścāt adṛṣṭa ādi puraḥsarāḥ saṃyoga sacivāḥ ca sataḥ dvyaṇuka ādi krameṇa kṛtsam kārya jātam ārabhate kāraṇa guṇāḥ ca kārye guṇātaram yadā dvau paramāṇū dvyaṇukam ārabhete tadā paramāṇu gatāḥ rūpa ādi guṇa viśeṣāḥ śukla ādayaḥ dvyaṇuke śukla ādi aparāḥ ārabhate paramāṇu guṇa viśeṣaḥ tu pārimāṇḍalyam dvyaṇuke pārimāṇḍalyam aparam ārabhate dvyaṇukasya parimāṇa atara yoga abhyupagamāt aṇu tva hrasva tve hi parimāṇe varṇayati yadā api dve dvyaṇuke catur aṇukam ārabhete tadā api śukla ādīām ārambhaka tvam aṇu tva hrasva tve tu dvyaṇuka samavāyī api caturaṇukasya mahat tva dīrgha tva parimāṇa yoga abhyupagamāt yadā api bahavaḥ paramāṇavaḥ vā dvyaṇukāi dvyaṇuka sahitaḥ vā paramāṇuḥ kāryam ārabhate tadā api tat evam yathā paramāṇoḥ parimaṇḍalāt sataḥ oṇu hrasvam ca dvyaṇukam jāyate mahat dīrgham ca tryaṇuka ādi a parimaṇḍalam yathā vā dvyaṇukāt aṇoḥ hrasvāt ca sataḥ mahat dīrgham ca tryaṇukam jāyate hrasvam evam jagat jaiṣyate iti abhyupagame kim tava atha atha ārambhakāṇi kāraṇa gatāi iti abhyupagacchāmi a tu guṇa atareṇa jagataḥ ākrāta tvam asti kāraṇa gatā cetaā kārye ārabheta hi acetaā cetaā virodhī kaścid guṇaḥ usti cetaā pratiṣedha mātra tvāt tasmāt pārimāṇḍalya ādi vaiṣamyāt cetaāyāḥ ārambhaka tvam iti mā evam maṃsthāḥ yathā kāraṇe vidyamāām api evam caitayasya api iti asya aṃśasya ca parimāṇa atara ākrāta tvam ca parimāṇa atara ākrāta tvam ca parimāṇa atara ākrāta tvam ca parimāṇa atara ākrāta tvam ca parimāṇa atara ākrāta tvam ca parimāṇa atara ākrāta tvam ca parimāṇa atara ākrāta tvam ca kāraṇam prāk parimāṇa atara ārambhāt pārimāṇḍalya ādīām ārambhaka tva upapatteḥ ārabdham api kārya dravyam prāk guṇa ārambhāt kṣaṇa mātram aguṇam tiṣṭhati iti abhyupagamāt ca parimāṇa atara ārambhe vyagrāṇi sva samā ajātīyam parimāṇa ātaram ārabhate parimāṇa ātarasya āya hetu tva abhyupagamāt kāraṇa bahu tvāt kāraṇa mahat tvāt pracaya viśeṣāt ca mahat tad viparītam aṇu dīrgha tva hrasva tve vyākhyāte iti hi sūtrāṇi ca ucyeta dravya atare guṇa atare vā ārabhyamāṇe sarveṣām eva kāraṇa guṇānām sva āśraya samavāya aviśeṣāt tasmāt svabhāvāt eva pārimāṇḍalya ādīām aārambhaka tvam tathā api iti draṣṭavyam saṃyogāt ca dravya ādīām vilakṣaṇāām utpatti darśaāt sama ajātīya utpatti vyabhicāraḥ dravye prakṛte guṇa udāharaṇam ayuktam iti ced a dṛṣṭātea vilakṣaṇa ārambha mātrasya vivakṣita tvāt ca dravyasya dravyam evā udāhartavyam guṇasya vā guṇaḥ evā iti hetuḥ asti sūtrakāraḥ api bhavatām dravyasya guṇam udājahāra pratyakṣa apratyakṣāṇām apratyakṣa tvāt saṃyogasya pañca ātmakam vidyate syāt pratyakṣam hi śarīram tasmai a pāñcabhautikam iti etat uktam bhavati guṇaḥ ca saṃyogaḥ dravyam śarīram dṛśyate tu iti ca atra api vilakṣaṇa utpattiḥ prapañcitā evam sati eva etat gatam eti brūmaḥ tat sāṃkhyam pratyuktam etat tu vaiśeṣikam prati kṛtaḥ śiṣṭa aparigrahāḥ api vyākhyātāḥ iti satyam etat tasya eva tu ayam vaiśeṣika parīkṣā ārambhe prapañcaḥ kṛtaḥ ubhayathā pi a tad abhāvaḥ paramāṇu jagat akāraṇa tva adhikaraṇam idāīm paramāṇu kāraṇa vādam irākaroti sa ca vādaḥ ittham samuttiṣṭhati paṭa ādīi hi loke sa avayavāi dravyāṇi svāugataiḥ eva saṃyoga sacivaiḥ dravyaiḥ ārabhyamāṇāi dṛṣṭāi yāvat kiṃcid sa avayavam tat sarvam svāugataiḥ eva saṃyoga sacivaiḥ taiḥ taiḥ dravyaiḥ ārabdham iti gamyate sa ca ayam avayava avayavi vibhāgaḥ yatas saḥ paramāṇuḥ sarvam ca idam giri samudra ādikam jagat sa avayavam sa avaya tvāt a kāryeṇa bhavitavyam iti atas jagataḥ kāraṇam iti kaṇabhuj abhiprāyaḥ catvāri bhūtāi sa avayavāi upalabhya caturvidhāḥ paramāṇavaḥ parikalpyate teṣām paratas vibhāga asaṃbhavāt pṛthivī ādīām paramāṇu paryata vibhāgaḥ bhavati sa pralaya kālaḥ tatas sarga kāle ca vāyavīyeṣu aṇuṣu adṛṣṭa apekṣam karma utpadyate tat karma sva āśrayam aṇum aṇvatareṇa saṃyuakti tatas dvi aṇuka ādi krameṇa vāyuḥ utpadyate evam agiḥ evam āpaḥ evam pṛthivī evam eva śarīram sa idriyam iti evam sarvam idam jagat aṇubhyaḥ saṃbhavati aṇu gatebhyaḥ ca rūpa ādibhyaḥ saṃbhavati iti kāṇādāḥ tatra idam abhidhīyate vibhāga avasthāām tāvat aṇūām saṃyogaḥ karma apekṣaḥ abhyupagatavyaḥ karmavatām saṃyoga darśaāt karmaṇaḥ ca kārya tva nimittam kim api abhyupagatavyam a abhyupagame imitta abhāvāt aṇuṣu ādyam karma syāt abhyupagame pi yadi prayata abhighāta ādiḥ vā yathā dṛṣṭam kim api karmaṇaḥ imittam abhyupagamyeta tasya asaṃbhavāt eva aṇuṣu ādyam karma syāt hi tasyām avasthāyām ātma guṇaḥ prayataḥ saṃbhavati śarīra abhāvāt śarīra pratiṣṭhe hi saṃyoge sati ātma guṇaḥ prayataḥ jāyate saṃyoge sati ātma guṇaḥ prayataḥ jāyate dṛṣṭam imittam pratyākhyātavyam sarga uttara kālam hi tat sarvam ādyasya karmaṇaḥ imittam saṃbhavati atha adṛṣṭam ādyasya karmaṇaḥ imittam iti ucyeta tat puarātma samavāyi vā syāt aṇu samavāyi vā ubhayathā api ādṛṣṭa aimittam aṇuṣu karma avakalpeta adṛṣṭasya acetaa tvāt a hi acetaam svatatram pravartate pravartayati vā iti sāṃkhya parīkṣāyām abhihitam tasyām avasthāyām acetaa tvāt ātma samavāyi tva abhyupagamāt ca ādṛṣṭam aṇuṣu karmaṇaḥ imittam syāt asaṃbadhāt adṛṣṭavatā puruṣeṇa asti saṃbadhaḥ iti ced saṃbadha sātatyāt pravṛtti sātatya prasaṅgaḥ iyāma kātara abhāvāt tat evam iyatasya kasyacid karma aimittasya abhāvāt aṇuṣu ādyam karma syāt saṃyogaḥ syāt saṃyoga abhāvāt ca dvi auṇaka ādi kārya jātam syāt saṃyogaḥ ca aṇoḥ aṇvatareṇa vā syāt vā sarva ātma ced upacaya aupapatteḥ aṇu mātra tva prasaṅgaḥ dṛṣṭa viparyaya prasaṅgaḥ ca pradeśavataḥ dravyasya pradeśavatā dravya atareṇa saṃyogasya dṛṣṭa tvāt ced sāvayava tva prasaṅgaḥ paramāṇūām kalpitāḥ pradeśāḥ syuḥ iti ced kalpitāām avastu tvāt avastu eva saṃyogaḥ iti syāt asati ca asamavāyi kāraṇe dvyaṇuka ādi kārya dravyam otpadyeta yathā ca ādisarge imitta abhāvāt saṃyoga utpatti artham karma saṃbhavati evam mahāpralaye pi vibhāga utpatti artham karma saṃbhavet hi tatra api kiṃci taimittam dṛṣṭam asti adṛṣṭam api bhoga prasiddhi artham pralaya prasiddhi artham iti atas syāt saṃyoga utpatti artham vibhāga utpatti artham vā karma atas ca saṃyoga vibhāga abhāvāt tad āyattayoḥ sarga pralayayoḥ abhāvaḥ prasajyeta tasmāt yam paramāṇu kāraṇa vādaḥ samavāya abhyupagamāt ca sāmyāt a avasthiteḥ samavāya abhyupagamāt ca tad abhāvaḥ iti saṃbadhyate dvābhyām ca aṇubhyām dvyaṇukam utpadyamāam aṇubhyām aṇvoḥ samavaiti iti abhyupagamyate bhavatā a ca evam abhyupagacchatā śakyate ṇu kāraṇatā samarthayitum kutas sāmyāt a avasthiteḥ yathā eva hi aṇubhyām sat dvyaṇukam samavāya lakṣaṇa tābhyām saṃbadhyate evam samavāyaḥ samavāyibhyaḥ sa samavāya lakṣaṇena eva samavāyibhiḥ saṃbadhyeta atyata bheda sāmyāt tatas ca yaḥ yaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ iti aavasthā eva prasajyeta iha pratyaya grāhyaḥ samavāyaḥ iti asaṃbaddhaḥ eva samavāyibhiḥ gṛhyate āsaṃbaddhaḥ vā tatas ca saṃbadhaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ prasajyeta iti ā iti ucyate saṃyogaḥ upi evam sati saṃyogibhiḥ iti asaṃbaddhaḥ eva iti samavāyavaḥ apekṣeta atha arthātara tvāt saṃyogaḥ saṃbadha ātaram apekṣeta samavāyaḥ u pi tarhi artha atara tvāt saṃbadhātaram apekṣeta a ca guṇa tvāt saṃyogaḥ saṃbadhātaram apekṣate a samavāyaḥ aguṇa tvāt iti yujyate vaktum apekṣā kāraṇasya tulya tvāt guṇa paribhāṣāyāḥ ca atatra tvāt tasmāt arthātaram samavāyam abhyupagacchataḥ prasajyeta eva a avasthā prasajyamāāyām ca a avasthāyām eka asiddhau sarva asiddheḥ dvābhyām aṇubhyām dvyaṇukam tasmāt api aupapaḥ paramāṇu kāraṇa vādaḥ eva ca bhāvāt api ca aṇavaḥ pravṛtti svabhāvāḥ vā ubhaya svabhāvāḥ vā aubhaya svabhāvāḥ vā abhyupagamyate gatyatara abhāvāt caturdhā api upapadyate pravṛtti svabhāva tve ityam eva pravṛtteḥ bhāvāt pralaya abhāva prasaṅgaḥ eva eva i vṛtteḥ bhāvāt sarga abhāva prasaṅgaḥ ubhaya svabhāva tvam ca virodhāt asamañjasam aubhaya svabhāva tve tu imitta vaśāt pravṛtti ivṛttyoḥ adṛṣṭa ādeḥ imittasya iti a pravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ atatra tve pi adṛṣṭa ādeḥ tasmāt api aupapaaḥ paramāṇu kāraṇa vādaḥ rūpa ādimat tvāt ca viparyayaḥ sa avayavāām dravyāṇām avayavaśas vibhajyamāāām yatas paraḥ vibhāgaḥ a paraḥ saṃbhavati te caturvidhāḥ rūpa ādimataḥ paramāṇavaḥ caturvidhasya rūpa ādimataḥ bhūtabhautikasya ārambhakāḥ ityāḥ ca iti yat vaiśeṣikāḥ abhyupagacchati sa teṣām abhyupagamaḥ eva yatas rūpa ādimat tvāt paramāṇūām aṇu tva aitya tva viparyayaḥ prasajyeta parama kāraṇa apekṣayā sthūla tvam aitya tvam ca teṣām abhipreta viparītam āpadyeta iti arthaḥ kutas evam loke dṛṣṭa tvāt yat hi loke rūpa ādimat vastu tat sva kāraṇa apekṣayā sthūlam aityam ca dṛṣṭam tat yathā paṭaḥ tatū apekṣya sthūlaḥ ityaḥ ca bhavati tatavaḥ ca aṃśū apekṣya sthūlāḥ aityāḥ ca bhavati tathā ca amī paramāṇavaḥ rūpa ādimataḥ taiḥ abhyupagamyate tasmāt te pi kāraṇavataḥ tad apekṣayā sthūlāḥ aityāḥ ca prāpuvati yat ca itya tve kāraṇam taiḥ uktam sat iti tat api evam sati aṇuṣu prakāreṇa aṇūām api kāraṇavat tva upapatteḥ yat api ityatve dvitīyam kāraṇam uktam aityam iti ca viśeṣataḥ pratiṣedha abhāvaḥ iti tat api ityatvam sādhayati asati hi yasmin kasmin itye itya śabde añaḥ samāsaḥ upapadyate a paramāṇu itya tvam eva apekṣyate tat ca asti eva ityam parama kāraṇam brahma ca śabda artha vyavahāra mātreṇa kasyacid arthasya prasiddhiḥ bhavati pramāṇa atara siddhayoḥ śabda arthayoḥ vyavahāra avatārāt yat api ityatve tṛtīyam kāraṇam uktam avidyā ca iti tat yadi evam satām kāraṇāām pratyakṣeṇa agrahaṇam avidyā iti tatas dvyaṇuka aityatā api āpadyeta atha a dravya tve sati iti viśeṣyeta tathā api akāraṇavat tvam eva ityatā nimittam āpadyeta tasya ca prāk eva ukta tvāt avidyā ca iti puaruktam syāt atha api kāraṇa vibhāgāt kāraṇa viāśāt ca āyasya tṛtīyasya viāśa hetoḥ asaṃbhavaḥ vidyā sā paramāṇūām itya tvam khyāpayati iti vyākhyāyeta āvaśyam vastu dvābhyām eva hetubhyām viaṣṭum arhati iti saṃyoga sacive hi ca dravye dravya ātarasya ārambhake etat evam syāt yadā tu apāsta viśeṣam sāmāyā ātmakam kāraṇam viśeṣavat avasthātaram āpadyamāam ārambhakam abhyupagamyate tadā upapadyate tasmāt rūpa ādimat tvāt syāt abhipreta viparyayaḥ paramāṇūām tasmāt api aupapaaḥ paramāṇu kāraṇa vādaḥ ubhayathā ca doṣāt sthūlā pṛthivī rūpa rasa sparśa guṇāḥ sūkṣmāḥ āpaḥ rūpa sparśa guṇam sūkṣmataram tejaḥ sparśa guṇaḥ sūkṣmatamaḥ vāyuḥ iti evam etāi catvāri catvāri sthūla sūkṣma sūkṣmatara sūkṣmatama tāratamya upetāḥ ca loke lakṣyate tadvat paramāṇavaḥ api upacita apacita guṇāḥ kalpera vā ubhayathā api ca eva syāt tāvat upacita apacita guṇa tve upacita guṇāām mūrti upacayāt aparamāṇu tva prasaṅgaḥ ca atareṇa api mūrti upacayam aparamāṇu tva prasaṅgaḥ mūrti upacayāt aparamāṇu tva prasaṅgaḥ ca atareṇa api mūrti upacayam aparamāṇu tva prasaṅgaḥ ca atareṇa api mūrti upacayam aparamāṇu tva pras guṇa upacayaḥ bhavati iti ucyeta kāryeṣu bhūteṣu guṇa upacaye mūrti upacaya darśaāt tu upacita apacita guṇa tve paramāṇu tva sāmya prasiddhaye yadi tāvat sarve ekaika guṇāḥ eva kalpyera tatas tejasi sparśasya upalabdhiḥ syāt apsu rūpa sparśayoḥ pṛthivyām ca rasa rūpa sparśāām kāraṇa guṇa pūrvaka tvāt kārya guṇāām atha sarve caturguṇāḥ eva kalpyera gadhasya upalabdhiḥ syāt tejasi gadha rasayoḥ vāyau ca gadha rūpa rasāām ca evam dṛśyate tasmāt api aupapaḥ paramāṇu kāraṇa vādaḥ aparigrahāt ca atyatam aapekṣā pradhā a kāraṇa vādaḥ ayam tu paramāṇu kāraṇa vādaḥ kaiścid api śiṣṭaiḥ api parigṛhītaḥ iti atyatam eva ādaraṇīyaḥ veda vādibhiḥ api ca vaiśeṣikāḥ tatra artha bhūtā ṣaṣ padārthā dravya guṇa karma sāmāya viśeṣa samavāya ākhyā atyata bhiā bhia lakṣaṇā abhyupagacchati yathā śvas śaśaḥ iti tathātvam ca abhyupagamya tad viruddham dravya adhīatvam śeṣāṇām abhyupagacchati te opapadyate katham yathā hi loke śaśa kuśa palāśa prabhṛtīām satām etaretara adhīatvam bhavati evam dravya ādīām api atyatabhiatvāt ā eva guṇa ādīām bhavitum arhati atha bhavati guṇa ādīām tatas dravya bhāve bhāvāt dravya abhāve bhāvāt dravyam eva saṃsthā ādi bhedāt bhavati yathā devadattaḥ ekaḥ eva saḥ avasthā tara yogāt a eka śabda pratyaya bhāj bhavati tadvat tathā sati sāṃkhya siddhāta prasaṅgaḥ sva siddhāta virodhaḥ ca āpadyeyātām ageḥ ayasya api sataḥ dhūmasya agi a dhī a tvam dṛśyate satyam dṛśyate bheda pratīteḥ tu iha tu śuklaḥ kambalaḥ rohiṇī dheuḥ īlam utpalam iti dravyasya eva tasya tasya viśeṣaṇea dravya guṇayoḥ agi dhūmayoḥ iva bheda pratītiḥ asti tasmāt dravya ātmaka tā guṇasya karma sāmāya viśeṣa samavāyāām dravya ātmaka tā vyākhyātā guṇāām dravya adhīatvam dravya guṇayoḥ ayuta siddha tvāt iti yadi ucyeta tat ayuta siddha tvam apṛthak deśa tvam vā syāt apṛthak kāla tvam vā apṛthak svabhāva tvam vā sarvathā api opapadyate apṛthak deśa tve tāvat sva abhyupagamaḥ virudhyeta katham tatva ārabdhaḥ hi paṭaḥ tatu deśaḥ bhyupagamyate a paṭa deśaḥ paṭasya tu guṇāḥ śukla tva ādayaḥ paṭa deśāḥ abhyupagamyate a tatu deśāḥ tathā ca āhuḥ dravyāṇi dravyātaram ārabhate guṇāḥ ca guṇa ātaram iti tatavaḥ hi kāraṇa dravyāṇi kārya dravyam paṭam ārabhate tatu gatāḥ ca guṇāḥ śukla ādayaḥ kārya dravye paṭe śukla ādi guṇa ātaram ārabhate iti hi te bhyupagacchati saḥ bhyupagamaḥ dravya guṇayoḥ apṛthak deśa tve bādhyeta atha apṛthak kāla tvam ayuta siddha tvam ucyeta savya dakṣiṇayoḥ api go viṣāṇayoḥ ayuta siddha tvam prasajyeta tathā apṛthak svabhāva tve tu ayuta siddha tve dravya guṇayoḥ ātma bhedaḥ saṃbhavati tasya saṃyogaḥ ayuta siddhayoḥ tu samavāyaḥ iti ayam abhyupagamaḥ mṛṣā eva teṣām prāk siddhasya kāryāt kāraṇasya ayuta siddha tva aupapatteḥ eva ayam abhyupagamaḥ syāt ayuta siddhasya kāryasya samavāyaḥ iti evam api prāk asiddhasya alabdha ātmakasya kāryasya opapadyate dvaya āyatta tvāt saṃbadhasya siddham bhūtvā saṃbadhyate iti ced prāk kāraṇa saṃbadhāt kāryasya siddhau abhyupagamyamāāyām ayuta siddhi abhāvāt kārya kāraṇayoḥ saṃyoga vibhāgau vidyete syāt yathā ca utpaa mātrasya akriyasya kārya dravyasya vibhubhiḥ ākāśa ādibhiḥ dravya ataraiḥ saṃbadhaḥ saṃyogaḥ eva abhyupagamyate a samavāyaḥ evam kāraṇa dravyeṇa api saṃbadhaḥ saṃyogaḥ eva syāt a samavāyaḥ saṃyogasya samavāyasya vā saṃbadhasya saṃbadhi vyatirekeṇa astitve kiṃcid pramāṇam asti saṃbadhi śabda pratyaya vyatirekeṇa saṃyoga samavāya śabda pratyaya darśaāt tayoḥ astitvam iti ced a eka tve svarūpa bāhya rūpa apekṣayā a eka śabda pratyaya darśaāt yathā ekaḥ pi sa devadattaḥ loke sva rūpam ca apekṣya bhavati mauṣyaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ śrotriyaḥ bālaḥ yuvā sthaviraḥ pitā putraḥ pautraḥ bhrātā jāmātā iti yathā ca ekā api satī rekhā eka daśa śata sahasra ādi śabda pratyaya bhedam tathā eva saṃbadhi śabda pratyaya vyatirekeṇa saṃyoga samavāya śabda pratyaya arha tvam iti upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya aupalabdheḥ abhāvaḥ vastu atarasya saṃbadhi viṣaya tve saṃbadha śabda pratyayayoḥ saṃtata bhāva prasaṅgaḥ svarūpa bāhya rūpa apekṣayā iti ukta uttara tvāt tathā aṇu ātma maasām a pradeśa tvā saṃyogaḥ saṃbhavati pradeśavataḥ dravyasya pradeśavatā dravya atareṇa saṃyoga darśaāt kalpitāḥ pradeśāḥ aṇu ātma maasām bhaviṣyati iti ced sarva artha siddhi prasaṅgāt iyāḥ eva a vidyamāāḥ viruddhaḥ viruddhaḥ vā arthaḥ kalpaīyaḥ ātodhikaḥ iti iyam ahetu abhāvāt kalpaāyāḥ ca sva āyatta tvāt prabhūta tva saṃbhavāt ca a ca vaiśeṣikaiḥ kalpitebhyaḥ ṣaḍbhyaḥ padārthebhyaḥ śatam sahasram vā arthāḥ a kalpayitavyāḥ iti hetuḥ asti tasmāt yasmai yasmai yat yat rocate tat tat sidhyet kaścid kṛpāluḥ prāṇiām duḥkha bahulaḥ saṃsāraḥ eva mā bhūt iti kalpayet ayaḥ vā muktāām api utpattim kalpayet kaḥ tayoḥ syāt kiṃca ayat dvābhyām paramāṇubhyām sa avayavasya dvyaṇukasya ākāśe eva saṃśleṣa a upapattiḥ hi ākāśasya ca jatu kāṣṭha vat saṃśleṣaḥ usti kārya kāraṇa dravyayoḥ āśrita āśraya bhāvaḥ yathā opapadyate iti avaśyam kalpyaḥ samavāyaḥ iti ced a itaretara āśraya tvāt kārya kāraṇayoḥ hi bheda siddhau āśrita āśraya bhāva siddhiḥ āśrita āśraya bhāva siddhau ca tayoḥ bheda siddhiḥ kuṇḍa badara vat iti itaretara āśraya tā syāt hi kārya kāraṇayoḥ bhedaḥ āśrita āśraya bhāvaḥ vā vedātava ādibhiḥ abhyupagamyate kāraṇasya eva saṃsthā amātram kāryam iti abhyupagamāt kiṃca ayat paramāṇūām yāvatyaḥ diśaḥ ṣaḍ aṣṭau daśa vā tāvadbhiḥ avayavaiḥ sa avayavāḥ te syuḥ sa avayava tvāt aityāḥ ca iti itya tvaiḥ avayava tva abhyupagamaḥ bādhyeta yān tvam kalpayasi te eva paramāṇavaḥ iti ced a sthūla sūkṣma tāratamya krameṇa ā parama kāraṇāt yathā pṛthivī dvyaṇuka ādi apekṣayā sthūlatamā vastu bhūtā api tatas sūkṣmam sūkṣmataram ca pṛthivī eka jātīyakam viaśyati tatas dvyaṇukam tathā paramāṇavaḥ api pṛthivī eka jātīyaka tvāt viaśyeyuḥ viaśyatā upi avayava vibhāge eva viaśyati iti ced doṣaḥ yatas ghṛta kāṭhiya vilaya avat api viāśa upapattim avocāma yathā hi ghṛta suvarṇa ādīām api a gi saṃyogāt drava bhāva āpattyā kāṭhiya viāśaḥ bhavati evam paramāṇūām api parama kāraṇa bhāva āpattyā mūrti ādi viāśaḥ bhaviṣyati tathā kārya ārambhaḥ pi bhavati kṣīra jala ādīām atareṇa api avayava saṃyoga ataram dadhi hima ādi kārya ārambha darśaāt tat evam asāratara tarka saṃdṛbdha tvāt īśvara kāraṇa śruti viruddha tvāt śruti pravaṇaiḥ ca śiṣṭaiḥ mavādibhiḥ a parigṛhīta tvāt atyatam eva a apekṣā asmi paramāṇu kāraṇa vāde kāryāḥ āryaiḥ śreyaḥ orthibhiḥ iti vākyaśeṣaḥ samudāyaḥ ubhaya hetuke tad aprāptiḥ samudāya adhikaraṇam vaiśeṣika rāddhātaḥ duryukti yogāt veda virodhāt śiṣṭa aparigrahāt ca āpekṣitavyaḥ iti uktam iti vaiāśika tva sāmyāt atarām apekṣitavyaḥ iti idam idāīm upapādayāmaḥ sa ca bahu prakāraḥ pratipatti bhedāt vieya bhedāt vā tatra ete trayaḥ vādiḥ bhavati kecid sarva astitva vādiḥ kecid vijñā astitva mātra vādiḥ iti tatra ye sarva astitva vādiḥ iti tatra ye sarva astitva vādiḥ bāhyam ātaram ca vastu abhyupagacchati bhūtam bhautikam ca cittam caittam ca tān tāvat pratibrūmaḥ tatra bhūtam pṛthivī dhātu ādayaḥ bhautikam rūpa ādayaḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ ca catuṣṭaye ca pṛthivī ādi paramāṇavaḥ kha rasa iha uṣṇa īraṇa svabhāvāḥ te saṃhayate iti tathā rūpa vijñā aveda āsaṃjñā saṃskāra saṃjñakāḥ te pi ādhyātmam sarva vyavahāra āspada bhāvena saṃhayate iti tatra idam abhidhīyate yaḥ yam ubhaya hetukaḥ ubhaya prakāraḥ samudāyaḥ pareṣām abhipretaḥ aṇu hetukaḥ ca bhūta bhautika saṃhati rūpaḥ skadha hetukaḥ ca ubhaya hetuke samudāye bhipreyamāṇe tad aprāptiḥ syāt samudāya aprāptiḥ samudāya bhāva aupapattiḥ iti arthaḥ kutas samudāyiām citta abhijvalaasya ca samudāya siddhi adhī atvāt ca kasyacid bhoktuḥ praśāsituḥ vā sthirasya saṃhatuḥ a abhyupagamāt i r apekṣa pravṛtti abhyupagame ca pravṛtti auparama prasaṅgāt āśayasya api aya tva a aya tvābhyām airūpya tvāt kṣaṇika tva abhyupagamāt ca iḥ vyāpāra tvāt pravṛtti aupapatteḥ tasmāt samudāya aupapattiḥ samudāya aupapattau ca tad āśrayā lokayātrā lupyeta itaretara pratyaya tvāt iti ce ā utpatti mātra aimitta tvāt yadi api bhoktā praśāsitā vā kaścid saṃhatā sthiraḥ abhyupagamyate tathā api avidyā ādīām itaretara kāraṇa tvāt upapadyate lokayātrā tasyām ca upapadyamāāyām a kiṃcid aparam apekṣitavyam asti te ca avidyā ādayaḥ avidyā saṃskāraḥ vijñāam rūpam ṣaṣ āyatanam sparśaḥ tṛṣṇā bhavaḥ jātiḥ jarā maraṇam śokaḥ paridevaā duḥkham iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ itaretara hetukāḥ saugate samaye kvacid saṃkṣiptāḥ irdiṣṭāḥ kvacid sarveṣām api ayam pratyākhyeyaḥ tat evam avidyā ādi kalāpe ghaṭīyatra vat aiśam āvartamāne ṛtha ākṣiptaḥ saṃghātaḥ iti ced a kasmāt utpatti mātra aimitta tvāt bhavet saṃghātaḥ yadi saṃghātasya imittam avagamyeta a tu avagamyate yatas itaretara pratyaya tve pi avidyā ādīām pūrva pūrvam uttara uttarasya utpatti mātra aimittam bhavat bhavet a tu saṃghāta utpatteḥ imittam saṃbhavati avidyā ādibhiḥ arthāt ākṣipyate saṃghātaḥ iti uktam atra ucyate yadi tāvat ayam abhiprāyaḥ avidyā ādayaḥ saṃghātam a labhamāā apekṣate saṃghātam iti tatas tasya saṃghātasya kiṃci imittam vaktavyam tat ca ityeṣu api aṇuṣu āśraya āśrayi bhūteṣu ca bhoktṛṣu satsu uktam vaiśeṣika parīkṣāyām kim aṅga kṣaṇikeṣu api aṇuṣu bhoktṛ rahiteṣu āśraya āśrayi śūyeṣu saṃbhavet atha ayam abhiprāyaḥ avidyā ādayaḥ eva saṃghātasya imittam iti katham tam eva āśritya ātmāam tasya eva imittam syuḥ atha saṃghātāḥ eva ādau saṃsāre saṃtatya āvartate tad āśrayāḥ ca avidyā ādayaḥ iti tadā api saṃghātāt vā sadṛśam eva utpadyeta vā sadṛśam visadṛśam vā utpadyeta iyama abhyupagame mauṣya pudgalasya deva tiryagyoiāraka prāpti abhāvaḥ aiyama abhyupagame api mauṣya pudgalaḥ kadācid aiyama abhyupagame api mauṣya pudgalaḥ kadācid hastī bhūtvā devaḥ vā mauṣyaḥ vā bhavet iti prāpuyāt ubhayam api abhyupagama viruddham api ca yad bhoga arthaḥ saṃghātaḥ syāt sa jīvaḥ sthiraḥ bhoktā iti tava abhyupagamaḥ tatas ca bhogaḥ bhoga arthaḥ eva saḥ prārthaīyaḥ tathā mokṣaḥ mokṣa arthaḥ eva iti mumukṣuṇā bhavitavyam ced prārthyeta ubhayam bhavitavyam avasthāyi tve kṣaṇika tva abhyupagama virodhaḥ tasmāt itaretara utpatti mātra nimitta tvam avidyā ādīām yadi bhavet bhavatu tu saṃghātaḥ sidhyet bhoktṛ abhāvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ uttara utpāde ca pūrva airodhāt uktam etat avidyā ādīām saṃghāta siddhiḥ asti iti tat api tu utpatti mātra aimitta tvam saṃbhavati iti idam idāīm upapādyate kṣaṇabhaṅga vādiḥ yam abhyupagamaḥ uttarasmi kṣaṇe utpadyamāe pūrvaḥ kṣaṇaḥ irudhyate iti ca evam abhyupagacchatā pūrva uttarayoḥ kṣaṇayoḥ hetu phala bhāvaḥ śakyate saṃpādayitum irudhyamāasya iruddhasya vā pūrva kṣaṇasya abhāva grasta tvāt uttara kṣaṇa hetu tva aupapatteḥ atha bhāva bhūtaḥ pūrva kṣaṇaḥ uttara kṣaṇasya hetuḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ tathā api opapadyate bhāva bhūtasya vyāpāra kalpaāyām atha bhāvaḥ eva asya vyāpāraḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ tathā api ā eva upapadyate hetu svabhāva a uparaktasya phalasya utpatti asaṃbhavāt svabhāva uparāga abhyupagame ca hetu svabhāvasya phala kāla avasthāyi tve sati kṣaṇa bhaṅga abhyupagama tyāga prasaṅgaḥ vā svabhāva uparāgeṇa hetu phala bhāvam abhyupagacchataḥ sarvatra tad prāpteḥ atiprasaṅgaḥ api ca utpāda erodhau vastuaḥ svarūpam eva vā syātām avasthātaram vā vastvataram eva vā sarvathā api upapadyate yadi tāvat vastuaḥ svarūpam evā utpāda erodhau syātām tatas vastu śabdaḥ utpāda erodha śabdau ca paryāyāḥ prāpuyuḥ atha asti kaścid viśeṣaḥ iti mayā itas utpāda erodha śabdābhyām abhilapyete iti evam api vastuaḥ kṣaṇika tva abhyupagama hāiḥ atha atyata vyatiriktau evā utpāda airodhau vastuaḥ syātām aśva mahiṣa vat tatas vastu utpāda airodhābhyām a saṃspṛṣṭam iti vastuaḥ śāśvata tva prasaṅgaḥ yadi ca utpāda airodhau syātām evam api draṣṭṛ dharmau tau a vastu dharmau iti vastuaḥ śāśvata tva prasaṅgaḥ eva tasmāt api asaṃgatam saugatam matam asati pratijñā uparodhaḥ yaugapadyam ayathā kṣaṇabhaṅga vāde uttarasya kṣaṇasya hetuḥ bhavati iti uktam atha asati eva hetau phala utpattim brūyāt tatas pratijñā uparodhaḥ syāt citta caittāḥ utpadyate iti iyam pratijñā hīyeta iḥ hetukāyām ca utpattau apratibadhāt sarvam sarvatra utpadyeta atha uttara kṣaṇa utpattiḥ yāvat tāvat avatiṣṭhate pūrva kṣaṇe iti brūyāt tatas yaugapadyam hetu phalayoḥ syāt tathā api pratijñā uparodhaḥ eva syāt kṣaṇikāḥ sarve saṃskārāḥ iti iyam pratijñā uparudhyeta pratisaṃkhyā pratisaṃkhyā irodha aprāptiḥ avicchedāt api ca vaiāśikāḥ kalpayati buddhi bodhyam trayāt ayat saṃskṛtam kṣaṇikam ca iti tat api ca trayam pratisaṃkhyā pratisaṃkhyā irodhau ākāśam ca iti ācakṣate trayam api ca etat avastu abhāva mātram iti buddhi pūrvakaḥ kila bhāṣyate tad viparītaḥ upratisaṃkhyā irodhaḥ āvaraṇa abhāva mātram ākāśam iti teṣām ākāśam parastāt pratyākhyāsyati irodha dvayam idāīm pratyācaṣṭe pratisaṃkhyā pratisaṃkhyā irodhayoḥ aprāptiḥ asaṃbhavaḥ iti arthaḥ kasmāt avicchedāt etau hi pratisaṃkhyā pratisaṃkhyā irodhau saṃtā a gocarau vā syātām bhāva gocarau vā a tāvat saṃtā a gocarau saṃbhavataḥ sarveṣu api saṃtā eṣu saṃtā a vicchedasya asaṃbhavāt bhāva gocarau saṃbhavataḥ a hi bhāvāām viāśaḥ saṃbhavati sarvāsu api avasthāsu aspaṣṭa pratyabhijñāsu api avasthāsu tasmāt para parikalpitasya irodha dvayasya a upapattiḥ ubhayathā ca doṣāt yaḥ yam avidyā ādi irodhaḥ pratisaṃkhyā irodha atas pātī para parikalpitaḥ sa samyak jñāāt vā sa parikarāt syāt svayam eva vā pūrvasmin vikalpe uttarasmin tu mārga upadeśa āarthakya prasaṅgaḥ evam ubhayathā api doṣa prasaṅgāt asamañjasam idam ākāśe ca aviśeṣāt yat ca teṣām eva abhipretam ākāśam ca irupākhyam iti tatra irodha dvayasya irupākhya tvam purastāt irākṛtam ākāśasya idāīm irākriyate ākāśe ca ayuktaḥ irupākhya tva abhyupagamaḥ pratisaṃkhyā pratisaṃkhyā irodhayoḥ iva vastu tva pratipatteḥ aviśeṣāt āgama prāmāṇyāt tāvat ātma artha anubhūtiḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ākāśasya ca vastu tva prasiddhiḥ tu śabda guṇa aumeya tvam vaktavyam guṇānām pṛthivī ādi vastu āśraya tva darśaāt api ca āvaraṇa abhāva mātram ākāśam icchatām ekasmi suparṇe patati āvaraṇasya suparṇa atarasya utpitsataḥ avakāśa tva prasaṅgaḥ yatra āvaraṇa abhāvaḥ tatra patiṣyati iti ced viśeṣyate tat tarhi vastu bhūtam eva ākāśam syāt a āvaraṇa abhāva mātram api ca āvaraṇa abhāva mātram saugatasya sva abhyupagama virodhaḥ prasajyeta saugate hi samaye pṛthivī bhagava kiṃsaṃiśrayā iti asmi vāyuḥ kiṃsaṃiśrayaḥ iti asya bhavati vāyuḥ ākāśa saṃiśrayaḥ iti tat ākāśasya a vastu tve samañjasam syāt tasmāt api ayuktam ākāśasya a vastu tvam api ca ca irodha dvayam ākāśam ca trayam api etaiḥ upākhyam avastu ca iti vipratiṣiddham vā saṃbhavati vastu āśraya tvāt dharma dharmi vyavahārasya dharma dharmi bhāve hi ghaṭa ādi vat vastu tvam eva syāt ca api ca vaiāśikaḥ sarvasya vastuaḥ kṣaṇikatām abhyupaye upalabdhuḥ api kṣaṇikatām abhyupeyāt ca sā saṃbhavati ausmṛteḥ aubhavam smaraṇam eva ausmṛtiḥ sā ca upalabdhi eka kartṛkā satī saṃbhavati puruṣa atara upalabdhi viṣaye puruṣa atarasya smṛti adarśaāt katham hi aham adā udrākṣam idam idāīm paśyāmi iti ca pratyayaḥ syāt api ca darśa a smaraṇayoḥ pratyabhijñā pratyayaḥ sarvasya lokasya prasiddhaḥ aham adā udrākṣam idam paśyāmi iti yadi hi tayoḥ kartā syāt tatas aham smarāmi adrākṣīt ayaḥ iti pratīyāt a tu evam pratyeti kaścid yatra evam pratyayaḥ tatra darśa a smaraṇayoḥ bhiam eva kartāram sarva lokaḥ uvagacchati smarāmi aham asau adā udrākṣīt iti iha tu aham adā udrākṣam iti darśa a smaraṇayoḥ vaiāśikaḥ upi ātmāam eva ekam kartāram avagacchati yathā iti vā tatra evam sati ekasya eva pratipattim pratyabhijāa eka kartṛkām ā uttamāt ucchvāsāt atītāḥ ca pratipattīḥ ātma eka kartṛkāḥ katham kṣaṇabhaṅga vādī vaiāśikaḥ āpatrapeta sa yadi brūyāt sādṛśyāt etat saṃpatsyate iti tam pratibrūyāt te idam sadṛśam iti dvaya āyatta tvāt sādṛśyasya kṣaṇabhaṅga vādiḥ sadṛśayoḥ dvayoḥ vastuoḥ grahītuḥ ekasya abhāvāt sādṛśya nimittam mithyā pralāpaḥ eva syāt syāt ced pūrva uttarayoḥ kṣaṇayoḥ sādṛśyasya grahītā ekaḥ tathā sati ekasya kṣaṇa dvaya avasthāāt kṣaṇika tva pratijñā pīḍyeta sadṛśam iti pratyaya ātaram eva idam a pūrva uttara kṣaṇa dvaya grahaṇa aimittam iti ced a pūrva uttara kṣaṇa dvaya grahaṇa aimittam iti ced idam iti ced sādṛśya viṣayam syāt sadṛśam iti vākya prayogaḥ arthakaḥ syāt sādṛśyam iti eva prayogaḥ prāpuyāt yadā hi loke prasiddhaḥ padārthaḥ parīkṣakaiḥ parigṛhyate tadā sva pakṣa siddhiḥ para pakṣa doṣaḥ vā ubhayam api ucyamāam parīkṣakāṇām ātma ca buddhi saṃtāam ārohati evam eva eṣa ṛthaḥ iti yat tat eva vaktavyam tatas yat ucyamāam bahu pralāpi tvam ātma kevalam prakhyāpayet ca ayam sādṛśyāt saṃvyavahāraḥ yuktaḥ tad bhāva avagamāt tad sadṛśa bhāva aavagamāt ca bhavet api kadācid bāhya vastui vipralambha saṃbhavāt tat eva idam syāt tad sadṛśam vā iti saṃdehaḥ upalabdhari tu saṃdehaḥ api as kadācid bhavati saḥ eva aham syām tad sadṛśaḥ vā iti yaḥ eva aham pūrvedyus adrākṣam saḥ eva aham adya smarāmi iti tasmāt api aupapaḥ vaiāśika samayaḥ āsatas dṛṣṭa tvāt itas ca aupapaaḥ vaiāśika samayaḥ yatas sthiram auyāyi kāraṇam a abhyupagacchatām abhāvāt bhāva utpattiḥ iti etat āpadyeta darśayati ca abhāvāt bhāva utpattim prādurbhāvāt iti viaṣṭāt hi kila bījāt aṅkuraḥ utpadyate tathā viaṣṭāt kṣīrāt dadhi mṛd piṇḍāt ca ghaṭaḥ kūṭasthāt ced kāraṇāt kāryam utpadyeta aviśeṣāt sarvam sarvatas utpadyeta tasmāt abhāva grastebhyaḥ bīja ādibhyaḥ abhāvāt bhāva utpattiḥ iti tatra idam ucyate āsataḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt iti ā bhāvāt bhāvaḥ utpadyate yadi abhāvāt bhāvaḥ utpadyeta abhāva tva aviśeṣāt kāraṇa viśeṣa abhyupagamaḥ arthakaḥ syāt hi bīja ādīām upamṛditāām yaḥ bhāvaḥ tasya abhāvasya śaśaviṣāṇa ādīām ca kaścid viśeṣaḥ sti bījāt eva aṅkuraḥ jāyate kṣīrāt eva dadhi iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ kāraṇa viśeṣa abhyupagamaḥ ṛthavāsyāt tu abhāvasya kāraṇa tva abhyupagame śaśaviṣāṇa ādibhyaḥ pi aṅkura ādayaḥ jāyera ca evam dṛśyate yadi abhāvasya api viśeṣaḥ bhyupagamyeta utpala ādīām iva tatas viśeṣa vat tvāt eva abhāvasya bhāva tvam utpala ādi vat prasajyeta abhāvaḥ kasyacid utpatti hetuḥ syāt abhāva tvāt eva śaśaviṣāṇa ādi vat abhāvāt ca bhāva utpattau abhāva āvitam eva sarvam kāryam syāt ca evam dṛśyate sarvasya ca vastuaḥ rūpeṇa ca ca śarāva ādayaḥ bhāvāḥ tatva ādi vikārāḥ keacid abhyupagamyate mṛd vikārāḥ eva tu bhāvāḥ lokaḥ pratyeti yat tu uktam svarūpa upamardam atareṇa kasyacid kūṭasthasya vastuaḥ kāraṇa tva aupapatteḥ abhāvāt bhāva utpattiḥ bhavitum arhati iti tat duruktam sthira svabhāvāām eva suvarṇa ādīām pratyabhijñāyamāām rucaka ādi kāraṇa bhāva darśaāt yeṣu api bīja ādiṣu sva rūpa upamardaḥ lakṣyate teṣu api āsau pūrva avasthā uttara avasthāyāḥ kāraṇam abhyupagamyate bīja ādi avayavāām aṅkura ādi kāraṇa bhāva abhyupagamāt tasmāt asadbhyaḥ śaśaviṣāṇa ādibhyaḥ sat utpatti adarśaāt sadbhyaḥ ca suvarṇa ādibhyaḥ sat utpatti darśaāt aupapaḥ abhāvāt bhāva utpatti abhyupagamaḥ api ca caturbhiḥ citta caittāḥ utpadyate paramāṇubhyaḥ ca bhūta bhautika lakṣaṇaḥ samudāyaḥ utpadyate iti abhyupagamya puara bhāvāt bhāva utpattim kalpayadbhiḥ abhyupagamam vaiāśikaiḥ lokaḥ ākulīkriyate api ca evam siddhiḥ yadi ca abhāvāt bhāva utpattiḥ abhyupagamyeta evam sati api syāt abhāvasya sulabha tvāt kṛṣīvalasya kṣetra karmaṇi aprayata māasya api sasya aiṣpattiḥ syāt kulālasya ca mṛd saṃskriyāyām aprayata māasya api amatra utpattiḥ vastra lābhaḥ svarga apavargayoḥ ca a kaścid kathaṃcid samīheta a ca etat yujyate abhyupagamyate vā keacid tasmāt aupapaoyam abhāvāt bhāva utpatti abhyupagamaḥ ābhāvaḥ upalabdheḥ ābhāva adhikaraṇam evam bāhya artha vādam āśritya samudāya aprāpti ādiṣu dūṣaṇeṣu udbhāviteṣu vijñāa vādī bauddhaḥ idāīm pratyavatiṣṭhate keṣāṃcid kila bāhye ālakṣya bāhya artha vāda prakriyā iyam viracitā āsau sugata abhiprāyaḥ tasya tu vijñāaikaskadhavādaḥ eva abhipretaḥ tasmin ca vijñāa vāde rūpeṇa ātasthe eva pramāṇa prameya phala vyavahāraḥ sarvaḥ upapadyate sati api bāhya arthe buddhi āroham atareṇa pramāṇa ādi vyavahāra avatārāt katham avagamyate atasthaḥ eva ayam sarva vyavahāraḥ bāhyaḥ ṛthaḥ asti iti tad asaṃbhavāt iti āha sa hi paramāṇavaḥ vā syuḥ tad samūhāḥ vā stambha ādayaḥ syuḥ tatra a tāvat paramāṇavaḥ stambha ādi pratyaya paricchedyāḥ bhavitum arhati paramāṇu ābhāsa jñā ā upapatteḥ tad samūhāḥ stambha ādayaḥ teṣām aśakya tvāt evam jāti ādī api pratyācakṣīta api ca aubhava mātreṇa jñāasya jāyamāasya prati viṣayam pakṣapātaḥ stambha jñāam kuḍya jñāam ghaṭa jñāam paṭa jñāam iti ā asau jñāa gata viśeṣam atareṇa upapadyate iti avaśyam viṣaya sārūpyam jñāasya aṅgīkartavyam aṅgīkṛte ca viṣaya ākārasya api ca svabhāva viveke yuktam pratibadha kāraṇa abhāvāt tasmāt api artha abhāvaḥ svapa ādi vat ca idam draṣṭavyam yathā hi svapa māyā marīci udaka gadharva agara ādi pratyayā grāhya grāhaka ākārā bhavati evam jāgarita gocarā api stambha ādi pratyayā bhavitum arhati iti avagamyate pratyaya tva aviśeṣāt katham asati bāhya arthe pratyaya vaicitryam upapadyate iti āha a ādau hi saṃsāre bīja aṅkura vat vaicitryam a vipratiṣidhyate api ca avayavi atirekābhyām vāsa āimittam eva jñā avaicitryam iti avagamyate svapa ādiṣu atareṇa api artham vāsa āimittasya jñā avaicitryasya ubhābhyām api āvābhyām abhyupagamyamāa tvāt atareṇa tu artha nimittasya jñā a vaicitryasya mayā tasmāt api abhāvaḥ bāhya arthasya iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ ābhāvaḥ upalabdheḥ iti a khalu abhāvaḥ bāhyasya arthasya adhyavasātum śakyate kasmāt upalabdheḥ upalabhyate hi prati pratyayam bāhyaḥ ṛthaḥ stambhaḥ kuḍyam ghaṭaḥ paṭaḥ iti ca upalabhyamāasya eva abhāvaḥ bhavitum arhati yathā hi kaścid sādhyāyām tṛptau svayam evam brūyāt ā aham bhuñje a vā tṛpyāmi iti tadvat idriya saṃikarṣeṇa svayam upalabhamāa eva bāhyam artham ā aham upalabhe a ca saḥ asti iti bruva katham upādeya vacaḥ syāt au ā aham evam bravīmi a kaṃcid artham upalabhe iti kim tu upalabdhi vyatiriktam opalabhe iti bravīmi bāḍham evam bravīṣi iraṅkuśa tvāt te tuṇḍasya a tu yukti upetam bravīṣi yatas upalabdhi vyatirekaḥ api balāt arthasya abhyupagatavyaḥ upalabdheḥ eva arthaḥ hi kaścid upalabdhim eva stambhaḥ kuḍyam ca iti upalabhate upalabdhi viṣaya tve eva tu stambha kuḍya ādī sarve laukikāḥ upalabhate atas ca evam eva sarve laukikāḥ upalabhate yat pratyācakṣāṇāḥ api bāhyam artham evam ācakṣate yat tat bahis vat avabhāsate iti te api hi sarva loka prasiddhām bahis avabhāsamāām saṃvidam pratyākhyātu kāmāḥ ca bāhyam artham bahis vat iti vatkāram kurvati itarathā hi kasmāt bahis vat iti brūyuḥ a hi viṣṇu mitraḥ vadhyā putra vat avabhāsate iti kaścid ācakṣīta tasmāt yathā aubhavam tattvam abhyupagacchadbhiḥ bahis eva avabhāsate iti yuktam abhyupagatum a tu bahis vat avabhāsate iti bāhyasya arthasya asaṃbhavāt bahis vat avabhāsate iti adhyavasitam sādhuḥ adhyavasāyaḥ yatas pramāṇa pravṛtti apravṛtti pūrvakau saṃbhava asaṃbhavau avadhāryete saṃbhava asaṃbhava pūrvake pramāṇa pravṛtti apravṛttī yat hi pratyakṣa ādīām pramāṇeā upalabhyate tat saṃbhavati yat tu a keacid api pramāṇena upalabhyate saṃbhavati iha tu yathāsvam sarvaiḥ eva pramāṇaiḥ katham vyatireka avyatireka ādi vikalpaiḥ saṃbhavati iti ucyeta upalabdheḥ eva ca viṣaya sārūpyāt viṣaya āśaḥ bhavati asati viṣaye viṣaya sārūpya aupapatteḥ bahis upalabdheḥ ca viṣayasya atas eva pratyaya viṣayayoḥ upāya upeya bhāva hetukaḥ a abheda hetukaḥ iti abhyupagatavyam api ca ghaṭa jñāam paṭa jñāam iti viśeṣaṇayoḥ ghaṭa paṭayoḥ bhedaḥ a viśeṣyasya jñāasya yathā śuklaḥ gauḥ kṛṣṇaḥ gauḥ iti śauklya kārṣṇyayoḥ eva bhedaḥ a go tvasya dvābhyām ca bhedaḥ ekasya siddhaḥ bhavati ekasmāt ca dvayoḥ tasmāt bhedaḥ tathā ghaṭa darśaam ghaṭa smaraṇam iti atra api pratipattavyam atra api hi viśeṣyayoḥ eva darśa a smaraṇayoḥ bhedaḥ a viśeṣaṇasya ghaṭasya yathā kṣīragadhaḥ kṣīra rasaḥ iti viśeṣyayoḥ eva bhedaḥ a viśeṣaṇasya kṣīrasya tadvat api ca dvayoḥ vijñāayoḥ upakṣīṇayoḥ itaretara grāhya grāhaka tva aupapattiḥ tatas ca vijñā abheda pratijñā kṣaṇika tva ādi dharma pratijñā sva lakṣaṇa sāmāya lakṣaṇa vāsya vāsaka tva avidyā upaplava sat asat dharma badha mokṣa ādi pratijñāḥ ca sva śāstra gatāḥ tāḥ hīyera kiṃca ayat vijñāam vijñāam iti abhyupagacchatā bāhya arthaḥ stambhaḥ kuḍyam iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ kasmai iti vaktavyam iti ced bāhyaḥ api arthaḥ udbhūyate eva iti yuktam abhyupagatum atha prakāśa ātmaka tvāt pradīpa vat svayam tathā bāhyaḥ api arthaḥ iti ced atyata viruddhām svātmaiḥ kriyām abhyupagacchasi dahati itivat aviruddham tu loka prasiddham iti ecchasi aho pāṇḍityam mahat darśitam a ca artha vyatiriktam api svayam kriyā virodhāt eva au vijñāasya sva rūpa vyatirikta grāhya tve tat api grāhyam tat api iti api ca pradīpa vat avabhāsa ātmaka tvāt jñāasya jñā ātaram kalpayataḥ sama tvāt avabhāsya avabhāsaka bhāva aupapatteḥ kalpa āarthakyam iti tat ubhayam api asat vijñā a grahaṇa mātre eva vijñā sākṣiṇaḥ grahaṇa ākāṅkṣā utpādāt aavasthā śaṅkā upapatteḥ sākṣi pratyayayoḥ ca svabhāva vaiṣamyāt upalabdhṛ upalabhya bhāva upapatteḥ svayaṃsiddhasya ca sākṣiṇā u pratyākhyeya tvāt kiṃca ayat pradīpa vat vijñāam avabhāsa kātaraiḥ apekṣam svayam eva prathate iti bruvatā a pramāṇa gamyam vijñāam iti uktam syāt bāḍham evam aubhava rūpa tvāt tu vijñāasya iṣṭaḥ aḥ pakṣaḥ tvayā iti ced cakṣuḥ sādhaasya pradīpa ādi prathaa darśaāt atas vijñāasya api avabhāsya tva aviśeṣāt sati avagatari pradīpa vat iti avagamyate sākṣiṇā uvagatuḥ svayaṃsiddha tām upakṣipatā svayam prathate vijñāam iti eṣaḥ eva mama pakṣaḥ tvayā vācoyuktyatareṇa āśritaḥ iti ced a vijñā asya utpatti pradhvaṃsa a eka tva ādi viśeṣavat tva abhyupagamāt atas pradīpa vat vijñā asya api vyatirikta avagamya tvam asmābhiḥ prasādhitam vaidharmyāt ca yat uktam sva pa ādi pratyaya vat jāgarita gocarāḥ api stambha ādi pratyayāḥ bhaveyuḥ pratyaya tva aviśeṣāt iti tat prativaktavyam atra ucyate a svapa ādi pratyaya vat jāgrat pratyayā bhavitum arhati kasmāt vaidharmyāt vaidharmyam hi bhavati svapa jāgaritayoḥ kim puar vaidharmyam bādhā bādhau iti brūmaḥ bādhyate hi svapa upalabdham vastu pratibuddhasya mithyā mayā upalabdhaḥ mahā jaa samāgamaḥ iti hi asti mama mahā jaa samāgamaḥ tu me babhūva bhrātiḥ udbabhūva iti evam māyā ādiṣu api bhavati yathāyatham bādhaḥ jāgarita upalabdham vastu stambha ādikam kasyāṃcid api avasthāyām bādhyate api ca smṛtiḥ eṣā upalabdhiḥ tu smṛti upalabdhyoḥ ca pratyakṣam ataram artha viprayoga saṃprayoga ātmakam iṣṭam putram smarāmi opalabhe upalabdhum icchāmi iti tatra evam sati a śakyate vaktum mithyā jāgarita upalabdhiḥ upalabdhi tvāt svapa upalabdhi vat iti ubhayoḥ ataram svayamaubhava tā ca sva aubhava apalāpaḥ kartum api ca aubhava virodha prasaṅgāt jāgarita pratyayāām vaktum aśakuvatā svapa pratyaya sādharmyāt vaktum iṣyate ca yaḥ yasya svatas saṃbhavati saḥ yasya sādharmyāt tasya saṃbhaviṣyati a hi udaka sādharmyāt śītaḥ bhaviṣyati darśitam tu vaidharmyam svapa jāgaritayoḥ yat api uktam jñā a vaicitryam iti tat prativaktavyam atra ucyate a bhāvaḥ upapadyate tvad pakṣe upalabdheḥ bāhyāām arthāām artha upalabdhi nimittāḥ hi pratyartham bhavati tu artheṣu kiṃimittāḥ vicitrāḥ bhaveyuḥ syāt syāt artha upalabdhyā vāsas upapatteḥ api ca viā api vāsas artha upalabdhi upagamāt tu artha upalabdhyā vāsas utpatti abhyupagamāt artha sadbhāvam eva avayavyatirekau api pratiṣṭhāpayataḥ api ca saṃskāra viśeṣāḥ saṃskārāḥ ca āśrayam atareṇa avakalpate evam loke dṛṣṭa tvāt ca tava vāsa āśrayaḥ kaścid asti pramāṇataḥ upalabdheḥ kṣaṇika tvāt ca yat api ālayavijñāam parikalpitam tat api kṣaṇika tva abhyupagamāt aavasthita svarūpam sat bhavitum arhati hi ekasmin asati kūṭasthe vā sarva artha darśii deśa kāla aimitta apekṣa vāsa ādhī smṛti pratisaṃdhā ādi vyavahāraḥ saṃbhavati sthira svarūpa tve api ca vijñāa vāde pi kṣaṇika tva abhyupagamasya api bāhya artha vāde dūṣaṇāy udbhāvitāi uttara utpāde ca pūrva airodhāt iti evamādīi evam etau dvau api vaiāśika pakṣau bāhya artha vādi pakṣaḥ vijñāa vādi pakṣaḥ ca śūyavādi pakṣaḥ tu sarva pramāṇa vipratiṣiddhaḥ iti tairākaraṇāya ādaraḥ kriyate hi ayam sarva pramāṇa siddhaḥ lokavyavahāraḥ yat tattvam a adhigamya apavāda abhāve utsarga prasiddheḥ sarvathā upapatteḥ ca kim sarva prakāreṇa yathā yathā ayam vaiāśika samayaḥ upapattimat tvāya parīkṣyate tathā tathā sikatā kūpa vat vidīryate eva a kāṃcid api atra upapattim paśyāmaḥ atas ca aupapaḥ vaiāśika tatra vyavahāraḥ api ca bāhya artha vijñāaśūya vāda trayam itaretara viruddham upadiśatā sugate spaṣṭīkṛtam saṃbaddha pralāpi tvam pradveṣaḥ vā prajāsu viruddha artha pratipattyā vimuhyeyuḥ imāḥ prajāḥ iti sarvathā api a ādaraṇīyaḥ yam sugata samayaḥ śreyaskāmaiḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ aikasmiasambhavāt ekasmiasaṃbhava adhikaraṇam irastaḥ sugata samayaḥ vivasaa samayaḥ idāīm irasyate sapta ca eṣām padārthāḥ saṃmatāḥ saṃkṣepataḥ tu dvau eva padārthau jīva ajīva ākhyau yathāyogam tayoḥ eva itara atarbhāvāt iti tayoḥ imam aparam prapañcam ācakṣate pañca astikāyāḥ jīva astikāyaḥ pudgala astikāyaḥ dharma astikāyaḥ dharma astikāyaḥ ākāśa astikāyaḥ ca iti sarveṣām api eṣām sarvatra ca imam sapta bhaṅgī ayam avatārayati syāt asti syāt asti syāt asti ca āsti ca syāt avaktavyaḥ syāt asti ca avaktavyaḥ ca syāt asti ca avaktavyaḥ ca syāt asti ca āsti ca avaktavyaḥ ca iti evam eva ekatva aityatva ādiṣu api imam sapta bhaṅgī ayam yojayati atra ācakṣmahe ā ayam abhyupagamaḥ yuktaḥ iti kutas ekasmin asaṃbhavāt hi ekasmin dharmiṇi yugapad sat asat tva ādi viruddha dharma samāveśaḥ saṃbhavati śīta uṣṇa vat ye ete sapta padārthāḥ etāvataḥ evaṃrūpāḥ ca iti te tathā eva vā syuḥ ā eva vā tathā syuḥ itarathā hi tathā vā syuḥ a tathā vā ityaiḥ dhārita rūpam jñāam saṃśaya jñāa vat apramāṇam eva syāt avaeka ātmakam vastu iti bhavitum arhati bhavitum arhati bhavitum arhati sarva vastuṣu sarva vastuṣu sarva vastuṣu sarva vastu syāt asti ityādi vikalpa upaipātāt airdhāraṇa ātmaka tā eva syāt evam ca syāt pakṣestitā syāt ca pakṣe āstitā iti evam sati katham pramāṇa bhūtaḥ sa tīrthakaraḥ pramāṇa prameya pramātṛ pramitiṣu airdhāritāsu upadeṣṭum śakuyāt katham vā tad abhiprāya āusāriṇaḥ tad upadiṣṭe rthe pravartera aikātika phala tvaiḥ dhāraṇe hi sati sarvaḥ sarvaḥ lokaḥ oākulaḥ pravartate sarvaḥ pravartate iti atas ca eṣām padārthāām avaktavya tvam saṃbhavati avaktavyāḥ ced ucyera ucyate ca avaktavyāḥ ca iti vipratiṣiddham ucyamāāḥ ca tathā eva avadhāryate āvadhāryate iti ca tathā tad avadhāraṇa phalam samyak darśaam asti vā āsti vā evam tad viparītam asamyak darśaam api asti vā āsti vā iti pralapa mattaḥ matta pakṣasya eva pakṣaḥ syāt a svarga apavargayoḥ ca pakṣe bhāvaḥ pakṣe ca abhāvaḥ tathā dharme sattvasya dharma atarasya asaṃbhavāt asattve ca evam sattvasya asaṃbhavāt asaṃgatam idam ārhatam matam irākṛtāḥ matavyāḥ yat tu pudgala saṃjñakebhyaḥ ṇubhyaḥ saṃghātāḥ saṃbhavati iti kalpayati tat pūrveṇa eva aṇuvādaiḥ ākaraṇe irākṛtam bhavati iti atas a pṛthak taiḥ ākaraṇāya prayatyate evam ca ātma akārtsyam yathā ekasmin dharmiṇi viruddha dharma asaṃbhavaḥ doṣaḥ syāt vāde prasaktaḥ evam jīvasya akārtsyam aparaḥ doṣaḥ prasajyeta katham śarīra parimāṇaḥ hi jīvaḥ iti ārhatā śarīra parimāṇa tāyām ca satyām ātmā iti atas ghaṭa ādi vat aitya tvam ātmanaḥ prasajyeta śarīrāṇām ca a avasthita parimāṇa tvāt mauṣya jīvaḥ mauṣya śarīra parimāṇaḥ bhūtvā hasti śarīram vyāpuyāt ca a kṛtsaḥ puttikā śarīre saṃmīyeta eṣa ekasmin api kaumāra yauva a sthāvireṣu doṣaḥ syāt etat jīvaḥ tasya tad avayavaḥ eva avayavāḥ alpe śarīre saṃkuceyuḥ mahati ca vikaseyuḥ iti teṣām jīva avayavāām vā a vā iti vaktavyam pratighāte tāvat āata avayavāḥ deśe saṃmīyera a pratighāte pi eka avayava deśa tva upapatteḥ sarveṣām avayavāām prathimā upapatteḥ jīvasya aṇu mātra tva prasaṅgaḥ syāt api ca śarīra mātra paricchiāām jīva avayavāām āatyam otprekṣitum api śakyam atha paryāyeṇa bṛhat śarīra pratipattau kecid jīva avayavāḥ upagacchati ca kecid apagacchati iti ucyeta tatra api ucyate ca paryāyāt api avirodhaḥ vikāra ādibhyaḥ ca paryāyeṇa api avayava upagama apagamābhyām etat deha parimāṇa tvam jīvasya avirodhena upapādayitum śakyate kutas vikāra ādi doṣa prasaṅgāt avayava upagama apagamābhyām hi aiśam āpūryamāṇasya apakṣīyamāṇasya ca jīvasya vikriyāvat tvam tāvat aparihāryam vikriyāvat tve ca carma ādi vat aityatvam prasajyeta tatas ca badha mokṣa abhyupagamaḥ bādhyeta karma aṣṭaka pariveṣṭitasya jīvasya alābū vat saṃsāra sāgare imagasya badha occhedāt ūrdhvagāmi tvam bhavati iti kiṃca ayat āgacchatām apagacchatām ca avayavāām āgama apāya dharmavat tvāt eva a ātmatvam śarīra ādi vat tatas ca avasthitaḥ kaścid avayavaḥ ātmā iti syāt ca saḥ śakyate ayam asau iti kiṃca ayat āgacchataḥ ca ete jīva avayavāḥ kutas prādurbhavati apagacchataḥ ca kva vā līyate iti vaktavyam a hi bhūtebhyaḥ prādurbhaveyuḥ bhūteṣu ca ilīyera abhautika tvāt jīvasya kaścid sādhāraṇaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ vā jīvāām pramāṇa abhāvāt kiṃca ayat aavadhṛta svarūpaḥ ca evam sati ātmā syāt āgacchatām apagacchatām ca avayavāām aiyata parimāṇa tvāt atas evamādi doṣa prasaṅgāt a paryāyeṇa api avayava upagama apagamau ātmanaḥ āśrayitum śakyete athavā pūrveṇa sūtreṇa śarīra parimāṇasya ātman upacita apacita śarīra atara pratipattau akārtsya prasañja a dvāreṇa a ityatāyām coditāyām syāt yathā raktapaṭāām tad saṃtā aityatā tadvat visicām api iti āśaṅkya sūtreṇa uttaram ucyate tāvat avastu tve airātmya vāda prasaṅgaḥ vastu tve pi vikāra ādi doṣa prasaṅgāt asya pakṣasya aupapattiḥ iti atya avasthiteḥ ca ubhaya etya tvāt aviśeṣaḥ api ca atyasya mokṣa avasthā bhāvi obhaya avasthā bhāvi obhaya avasthā jīva parimāṇasya itya tvam iṣyate jaiaiḥ tadvat pūrvayoḥ api ādya madhyamayoḥ jīva parimāṇayoḥ itya tva prasaṅgāt aviśeṣa prasaṅgaḥ syāt eka śarīra parimāṇatā eva syāt a upacita apacita śarīra atara prāptiḥ athavā atyasya jīva parimāṇasya avasthita tvāt pūrvayoḥ api avasthayoḥ avasthita parimāṇaḥ eva jīvaḥ syāt tatas ca aviśeṣeṇa sarvadā eva aṇuḥ mahā vā aṇuḥ aṇuḥ mahā vā aṇuḥ aṇuḥ mahā vā aṇuḥ aṇuḥ mahā jīvaḥ abhyupagatavyaḥ a śarīra parimāṇaḥ atas ca saugata vat ārhatam api matam asaṃgatam iti upekṣitavyam patyuḥ asāmañjasyāt pati adhikaraṇam idāīm kevala adhiṣṭhātṛ īśvara kāraṇa vādaḥ pratiṣidhyate tat katham avagamyate prakṛtiḥ ca pratijñā dṛṣṭātā uparodhāt abhidhyā upadeśāt ca iti atra ca ubhaya svabhāvasya īśvarasya svayam eva ācāryeṇa pratiṣṭhāpita tvāt yadi aviśeṣeṇa īśvara kāraṇa vāda mātram iha pratiṣidhyeta pūrva uttara virodhāt vyāhata abhivyāhāraḥ sūtrakāraḥ iti etat āpadyeta tasmāt aprakṛtiḥ adhiṣṭhātā kevalam imitta kāraṇam īśvaraḥ iti eṣa pakṣaḥ pratiṣidhyate sā ca iyam kecid tāvat sāṃkhya yoga vyapāśrayāḥ kalpayati pradhā apuruṣayoḥ adhiṣṭhātā kevalam imittakāraṇam īśvaraḥ itara itara vilakṣaṇāḥ pradhā apuruṣa īśvarāḥ iti māheśvarāḥ tu pañca padārthāḥ paśupati īśvareṇa paśu pāśa vimokṣaṇāya upadiṣṭāḥ paśupatiḥ imittakāraṇam iti tathā vaiśeṣika ādayaḥ api kecid kathaṃcid sva prakriyā ausāreṇa imittakāraṇam īśvaram iti atas uttaram ucyate patyuḥ asāmañjasyāt iti patyuḥ īśvarasya jagat kāraṇatvam upapadyate kasmāt asāmañjasyāt kim asāmañjasyam hi prāṇi bhedāḥ vidadhataḥ īśvarasya rāga dveṣa ādi doṣa prasakteḥ asmat ādi vat aīśvara tvam prasajyeta prāṇi karma apekṣita tvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced asāmañjasyam karma īśvarayoḥ pravartya pravartayitṛ tve itaretara āśraya doṣa prasaṅgāt a a ādi tvāt iti ced a vartamā a kāla vat atīteṣu api kāleṣu itaretara āśraya doṣa aviśeṣāt api ca doṣāḥ iti hi kaścid adoṣa prayuktaḥ sva arthe para arthe vā dṛśyate sva artha prayuktaḥ eva ca sarvaḥ para arthe pi pravartate iti evam api asāmañjasyam svārthavat tvāt īśvarasya a īśvara tva prasaṅgāt puruṣa viśeṣa tva abhyupagamāt ca īśvarasya puruṣasya ca audāsīya abhyupagamāt asāmañjasyam sambadhā upapatteḥ ca api asāmañjasyam eva a hi pradhā apuruṣa vyatiriktaḥ tareṇa pradhā apuruṣayoḥ īśitā tāvat saṃyoga lakṣaṇaḥ saṃbadhaḥ saṃbhavati pradhā apuruṣa īśvarāṇām sarvagata tvāt ca āpi samavāya lakṣaṇaḥ saṃbadhaḥ āśraya āśrayi bhāva airūpaṇāt api ayaḥ kaścid kārya gamyaḥ śakyate kalpayitum kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya eva adya api asiddha tvāt brahma vādiḥ katham iti ced tasya tādātmya lakṣaṇa saṃbadha upapatteḥ api ca brahma vādī kāraṇa ādi svarūpam tasya yathādṛṣṭam eva sarvam abhyupagatavyam iti sti parasya tu yathādṛṣṭam eva sarvam abhyupagatavyam iti ayam asti atiśayaḥ parasya api sarvajña praṇīta āgama sadbhāvāt āgama balam iti ced ā itara itara āśraya prasaṅgāt āgama pratyayāt sarvajña tva siddhiḥ sarvajña tva pratyayāt ca āgama siddhiḥ iti tasmāt evam api veda bāhyāsu yathāsaṃbhavam asāmañjasyam yojayitavyam adhiṣṭhā a upapatteḥ ca itas ca aupapattiḥ tārkika parikalpitasya īśvarasya sa hi kumbhakāraḥ iva adhiṣṭhāya pravartayet ca evam upapadyate hi apratyakṣam ca pradhāam īśvarasya adhiṣṭheyam saṃbhavati mṛd ādi vailakṣaṇyāt bhoga ādibhyaḥ syāt etat yathā karaṇa grāmam cakṣuḥ ādikam apratyakṣam ca puruṣaḥ adhitiṣṭhati evam pradhāam īśvaraḥ adhiṣṭhāsyati iti tathā api opapadyate bhoga ādi darśaāt hi karaṇa grāmasya adhiṣṭhita tvam gamyate ca atra bhoga ādayaḥ dṛśyate karaṇa grāma sāmye ca saṃsāriṇām iva īśvarasya api bhoga ādayaḥ prasajyera ayathā vā sūtra dvayam vyākhyāyate itas ca aupapattiḥ tārkika parikalpitasya īśvarasya hi loke sa śarīraḥ rājā rāṣṭrasya īśvaraḥ dṛśyate atas ca atas ca kalpayitum icchataḥ īśvarasya api kiṃcid śarīram varṇayitavyam syāt ca tat varṇayitum śakyate sṛṣṭi uttara kāla bhāvi tvāt śarīrasya prāk sṛṣṭeḥ tad aupapatteḥ ca īśvarasya pravartaka tva aupapattiḥ evam loke dṛṣṭa tvāt bhoga ādibhyaḥ atha loka darśa āusāreṇa īśvarasya api śarīram kalpyeta evam api opapadyate sa śarīra tve hi sati saṃsāri vat bhoga ādi prasaṅgāt īśvarasya api aīśvara tvam prasajyeta atavat tvam asarvajña tā vā itas ca aupapattiḥ tārkika parikalpitasya īśvarasya sa hi sarvajñaḥ taiḥ abhyupagamyate atas ca aataṃsam asaṃsāri vat asaṃsāri vat asaṃsāri vat asaṃsāri vat asaṃsāri vat asaṃsāri vat asaṃsāri vat asaṃsāri vat asaṃsāri vat asaṃsāri vat asaṃsāri vat asaṃsāri vat asaṃsāri vat asaṃsāri vat asaṃsāri vat asaṃsāri vat asa ca pradhā am ca puruṣāḥ mithas abhyupagamyate tatra sarvajñe īśvareṇa pradhā asya puruṣāṇām ātma aḥ ca iyattā paricchidyeta vā a vā paricchidyeta ubhayathā api doṣaḥ uṣaktaḥ eva katham pūrvasmin tāvat vikalpe iyattā paricchia tvāt pradhā apuruṣa īśvarāṇām atavat tvam avaśyaṃbhāvi evam loke dṛṣṭa tvāt yat hi loke iyattā paricchiam vastu ghaṭa ādi tat atavat dṛṣṭam tathā pradhā apuruṣa īśvara trayam api iyattā paricchia tvāt atavat syāt saṃkhyā parimāṇam tāvat pradhā a puruṣa īśvara traya rūpeṇa svarūpa parimāṇam api tad gatam īśvareṇa paricchidyeta puruṣa gatā ca mahā saṃkhyā tatas ca iyattā paricchiāām madhye ye teṣām saṃsāri tvam ca evam itareṣu api krameṇa saṃsārasya saṃsāriṇām ca syāt pradhāam ca sa vikāram puruṣa artham īśvarasya adhiṣṭheyam tad śūya tāyām īśvaraḥ kim adhitiṣṭhet kiṃviṣaye vā sarvajña tā īśvara te syātām pradhā apuruṣa īśvarāṇām ca evamatavattve sati ādimattva prasaṅgaḥ ca śūyavāda prasaṅgaḥ atha mā bhūt eṣa doṣaḥ iti uttaraḥ vikalpaḥ abhyupagamyeta a pradhā asya puruṣāṇām ātma aḥ ca iyattā īśvareṇa paricchidyate iti tatas īśvarasya sarvajñatva abhyupagama hāiḥ aparaḥ doṣaḥ prasajyeta tasmāt api asaṃgataḥ tārkika parigṛhītaḥ īśvara kāraṇa vādaḥ utpatti asambhavāt utpatti asaṃbhava adhikaraṇam yeṣām aprakṛtiḥ adhiṣṭhātā kevala aimitta kāraṇam īśvaraḥ bhimataḥ teṣām pakṣaḥ pratyākhyātaḥ yeṣām puraḥ prakṛtiḥ ca adhiṣṭhātā ca ubhaya ātmakam kāraṇam īśvara ubhimataḥ teṣām pakṣaḥ pratyākhyāyate śruti samāśrayaṇe api evaṃrūpaḥ eva īśvaraḥ prāc nirdhāritaḥ prakṛtiḥ ca adhiṣṭhātā ca iti śruti ausāriṇī ca smṛtiḥ pramāṇam iti sthitiḥ tat kasya hetoḥ eṣa pakṣaḥ pratyācikhyāsitaḥ iti ucyate yadi api evaṃjātīyakaḥ oṃśaḥ visaṃvāda gocaraḥ bhavati asti tu aṃśātaram visaṃvāda sthāam iti atas tad pratyākhyāāya ārambhaḥ tatra bhāgavatāḥ bhagavān eva ekaḥ vāsudevaḥ paramārtha tattvam sa caturdhā ātmā am pravibhajya pratiṣṭhitaḥ vāsudeva vyūha rūpeṇa saṃkarṣaṇa vyūha rūpeṇa pradyuma vyūha rūpeṇa airuddha vyūha rūpeṇa ca vāsudevaḥ paramātmā ucyate saṃkarṣaṇaḥ jīvaḥ pradyumaḥ teṣām vāsudevaḥ parā prakṛtiḥ itare saṃkarṣaṇa ādayaḥ kāryam tam itthaṃbhūtam parameśvaram bhagavatam abhigama upādā ijyā svādhyāya yogaiḥ varṣa śatam iṣṭvā kṣīṇa kleśaḥ bhagavatam eva pratipadyate iti tatra yat tāvat ucyate yaḥ asau ārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ vyaktāt prasiddhaḥ paramātmā sarva ātmā saḥ ātmā ātmā am ekadhā vyūhya avasthitaḥ iti te saḥ ekadhā bhavati tridhā bhavati ityādi śrutibhyaḥ paramātmaḥ ekadhā bhāvasya adhigata tvāt yat api tasya bhagavataḥ ajasram tat api pratiṣidhyate śruti smṛtyoḥ īśvara praṇidhā asya prasiddha tvāt yat puar idam ucyate vāsudevāt saṃkarṣaṇaḥ utpadyate saṃkarṣaṇāt ca pradyumaḥ pradyumāt ca airuddhaḥ iti atra brūmaḥ a vāsudeva saṃjñakāt paramātmanaḥ saṃkarṣaṇa saṃjñakasya jīvasya utpattiḥ saṃbhavati aitya tva ādi doṣa prasaṅgāt utpattimat tve hi jīvasya aitya tva ādayaḥ doṣāḥ prasajyera tatas ca bhagavat prāptiḥ mokṣaḥ syāt kāraṇa prāptau kāryasya pravilaya prasaṅgāt pratiṣedhiṣyati ca ācāryaḥ jīvasya utpattim ātmā aśruteḥ iti atvāt ca tābhyaḥ iti tasmāt asaṃgatā eṣā ca kartuḥ karaṇam itas ca asaṃgatā eṣā yasmāt hi loke kartuḥ devadatta ādeḥ karaṇam paraśu ādi utpadyamāam dṛśyate varṇayati ca bhāgavatāḥ kartuḥ jīvāt saṃkarṣaṇa saṃjñakāt karaṇam pradyuma saṃjñakam utpadyate kartṛ jāt ca tasmāt airuddha saṃjñakaḥ uhaṃkāraḥ utpadyate iti ca etat dṛṣṭātamatareṇa adhyavasātum śakumaḥ ca evaṃbhūtām śrutim upalabhāmahe vijñā ādi bhāve vā tad apratiṣedhaḥ atha api syāt a ca ete saṃkarṣaṇa ādayaḥ kim tarhi īśvarāḥ eva ete sarve jñā aiśvarya śakti bala vīrya tejobhiḥ aiśvarya dharmaiḥ avitā abhyupagamyate vāsudevāḥ eva ete sarve iḥ doṣāḥ iḥ adhiṣṭhāāḥ iḥ avadyāḥ ca iti tasmāt ayam yathā varṇitaḥ utpatti asaṃbhavaḥ doṣaḥ prāpa iti atra ucyate evam api tad apratiṣedhaḥ utpatti asaṃbhavasya apratiṣedhaḥ prāpa iti eva ayam utpatti asaṃbhavaḥ doṣaḥ prakāra atareṇa iti abhiprāyaḥ katham yadi tāvat ayam abhiprāyaḥ eva ete vāsudeva ādayaḥ catvāraḥ īśvarāḥ tulya dharmāṇaḥ ā eṣām eka ātmaka tvam asti iti tatas eka īśvara kalpa āarthakyam bhagavān eva ekaḥ vāsudevaḥ paramārtha tattvam iti abhyupagamāt atha ayam abhiprāyaḥ ekasya eva bhagavataḥ ete catvāraḥ vyūhāḥ tulya dharmāṇaḥ iti tathā api tad avasthaḥ eva utpatti asaṃbhavaḥ hi vāsudevāt saṃkarṣaṇasya utpattiḥ saṃbhavati saṃkarṣaṇāt ca pradyumasya pradyumāt ca airuddhasya atiśaya abhāvāt bhavitavyam hi kārya kāraṇayoḥ atiśaye yathā mṛd haṭayoḥ a hi asati atiśaye kāryam kāraṇam iti avakalpate a ca pañcarātra siddhātibhiḥ vāsudeva ādiṣu ekasmin sarveṣu vā jñā aiśvarya ādi tāratamya kṛtaḥ kaścid bhedaḥ abhyupagamyate vāsudevāḥ eva hi sarve vyūhāḥ iṣyate ca ete bhagavat vyūhāḥ catur saṃkhyāyām eva avatiṣṭhera brahma ādi stamba paryatasya samastasya eva jagataḥ bhagavat vyūha tva avagamāt vipratiṣedhāt ca vipratiṣedhaḥ ca asmi śāstre bahuvidhaḥ upalabhyate guṇa guṇi tva kalpa ādi lakṣaṇaḥ jñā aiśvarya śakti bala vīrya tejāṃsi guṇāḥ ātmā eva ete bhagavataḥ vāsudevāḥ ityādi darśaāt veda vipratiṣedhaḥ ca bhavati caturṣu vedeṣu param śreyaḥ labdhvā śāṇḍilyaḥ idam śāstram adhigatavā iti ādi veda eda ādarśaāt tasmāt asaṃgatā eṣā kalpaḥ iti siddham iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye dvitīya adhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ murat dvitīya udhyāyaḥ tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ a viyat aśruteḥ viyat adhikaraṇam kim asya ākāśasya utpattiḥ asti uta ā asti iti tatra tāvat pratipadyate a viyat aśruteḥ iti a khalu ākāśam utpadyate kasmāt aśruteḥ a hi asya utpatti prakaraṇe śravaṇam asti chādogye hi sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam iti sat śabda vācyam brahma prakṛtya tat aikṣata tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti ca pañcāām mahābhūtāām madhyamam tejaḥ ādi kṛtvā trayāṇām tejaḥ baāām utpattiḥ śrāvyate śrutiḥ ca aḥ ca atra śrutiḥ asti ākāśasya utpatti pratipādī tasmāt ākāśasya utpattiḥ iti asti tu tuśabdaḥ pakṣa atara parigrahe mā ām ākāśasya chādogye bhūt utpattiḥ śruti atare tu asti taittirīyakā hi satyam jñāam aatam brahma iti prakṛtya tasmāt vai etasmāt ātman ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti tatas ca śrutyoḥ vipratiṣedhaḥ kvacid tejaḥ pramukhā sṛṣṭiḥ kvacid ākāśa pramukhā iti eka vākyatā aayoḥ śrutyoḥ yuktā satyam sā yuktā a tu sā avagatum śakyate kutas tat tejaḥ sṛjataḥ iti sakṛt śrutasya sraṣṭuḥ sraṣṭavya dvaye tat tejaḥ sṛjata tat ākāśam asṛjata iti sakṛt śrutasya api kartuḥ kartavya dvaye saṃbadhaḥ dṛśyate yathā saḥ sūpam paktvā pacati iti evam tat ākāśam sṛṣṭvā tat tejaḥ sṛjataḥ iti yojayiṣyāmi ā evam yujyate prathama ja tvam hi chādogye tejasā uvagamyate taittirīyake ca ākāśasya a ca ubhayoḥ prathama ja tvam saṃbhavati itara śruti akṣara virodhaḥ api vyākhyātaḥ tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti atra api tasmāt ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ tasmāt tejaḥ saṃbhūtam iti sakṛt śrutasya a pādāasya saṃbhava asya ca viyat tejobhyām yugapad saṃbadhā upapatteḥ vāyoḥ agiḥ iti ca iti ca kaścid āha goṇī asambhavāt viyataḥ utpattiḥ aśruteḥ eva yā tu itarā śrutiḥ udāhṛtā sā gauṇī bhavitum arhati kasmāt asaṃbhavāt hi ākāśasya utpattiḥ saṃbhāvayitum śakyā śrīmat kaṇabhuj abhiprāya āusāri pu jīvatsu te hi kāraṇa sāmagrī asaṃbhavāt ākāśasya utpattim vārayati samavāyi asamavāyi imitta kāraṇebhyaḥ hi kila sarvam utpadyamāam samutpadyate dravyasya ca eka jātīyakam a ekam ca dravyam samavāyi kāraṇam bhavati ca ākāśasya eka jātīyakam a ekam ca dravyam ārambhakam asti yasmin samavāyi kāraṇe sati asamavāyi kāraṇe ca tad saṃyoge ākāśaḥ utpadyeta tad abhāvāt tu tad augraha pravṛttam imitta kāraṇam dūra apetam eva ākāśasya bhavati utpattimatām ca tejaḥ prabhṛtīām pūrva uttara kālayoḥ viśeṣaḥ saṃbhāvyate prāk utpatteḥ prakāśa ādi kāryam babhūva paścāt ca bhavati iti ākāśasya pūrva uttara kālayoḥ viśeṣaḥ saṃbhāvayitum śakyate kim hi prāk utpatteḥ aavakāśam asuṣiram acchidram babhūva iti śakyate idhyavasātum pṛthivī ādi vaidharmyāt ca vibhu tva ādi lakṣaṇāt ākāśasya aja tva siddhiḥ tasmāt yathā loke ākāśam kuru ākāśaḥ jātaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ gauṇaḥ prayogaḥ bhavati yathā ca ghaṭa ākāśaḥ karaka ākāśaḥ gṛha ākāśaḥ iti ekasya api ākāśasya evaṃjātīyakaḥ bheda vyapadeśaḥ gauṇaḥ bhavati vede api āraṇyā ākāśeṣu ālabhera iti evam utpatti śrutiḥ api gauṇī draṣṭavyā śabdāt ca śabdaḥ khalu api ākāśasya aja tvam khyāpayati yatas āha vāyuḥ cātarikṣam ca etat amṛtam iti a hi amṛtasya utpattiḥ upapadyate ākāśa vat sarva gataḥ ca ityaḥ iti ca ākāśea brahma sarvagata tva etya tvābhyām dharmābhyām upamimaḥ ākāśasya api tau dharmau sūcayati a ca tādṛśasya utpattiḥ upapadyate sa yathā a taḥ yam ākāśaḥ evam a atas ātmā veditavyaḥ iti ca ākāśa śarīram brahma ākāśaḥ ātmā iti ca a hi ākāśasya utpattimat tve brahmaṇaḥ viśeṣaṇam saṃbhavati sādhāraṇam brahma iti gamyate syāt ca ekasya brahma śabda vat idam pada uttaram sūtram syāt etat katham puar ekasya saṃbhūta śabdasya tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti asmin adhikāre pareṣu mukhya tvam saṃbhavati ākāśe ca gauṇa tvam iti atas uttaram ucyate syāt ca ekasya api saṃbhūta śabdasya viṣaya viśeṣa vaśāt gauṇaḥ mukhyaḥ ca prayogaḥ brahma śabda vat yathā ekasya api brahma śabdasya tapasā brahma vijijñāsasva tapaḥ brahma gauṇaḥ prayogaḥ ca mukhyaḥ yathā ca tapasi brahma śabdaḥ bhaktyā prayujyate añjasā tu vijñeye brahmaṇi tadvat katham abhasaḥ ekam eva advitīyam iti iyam pratijñā samarthyate abhasā sa dvitīyam brahma katham ca brahmaṇi vidite sarvam viditam syāt iti tat ucyate ekam eva iti tāvat sva kārya apekṣayā upapadyate yathā loke kaścid kumbhakāra kule pūrvedyus ca upalabhya aparedyus ca brūyāt mṛdā iva ekākiī pūrvedyus āsīt iti sa ca tayā avadhāraṇayā mṛd kārya jātam eva pūrvedyus āsīt iti abhipreyāt daṇḍa cakra ādi tadvat advitīya śrutiḥ adhiṣṭhātrataram vārayati yathā mṛdaḥ matra prakṛteḥ kumbhakāraḥ adhiṣṭhātā dṛśyate brahmaṇaḥ adhiṣṭhātā dṛśyate brahmaṇaḥ adhiṣṭhātā dṛśyate brahmaṇaḥ adhiṣṭhātā dṛśyate brahmaṇaḥ adhiṣṭhātā dṛśyate brahmaṇaḥ adhiṣṭhātā dṛśyate brah jagat prakṛteḥ ayaḥ adhiṣṭhātā asti iti ca abhasā api sa dvitīyam brahma prasajyate hi hi ca prāk utpatteḥ brahma abhasoḥ lakṣaṇāyatvam asti kṣīra udakayoḥ iva saṃsṛṣṭayoḥ vyāpi tva amūrta tva ādi dharma sāmāyāt sarga kāle tu brahma jagat utpādayitum yatate stimitam itarat tiṣṭhati teāyatvam avasīyate tathā ca ākāśa śarīram brahma ityādi śrutibhyaḥ api brahma ākāśayoḥ abheda upacāra siddhiḥ atas eva ca api ca sarvam kāryam utpadyamāam ākāśe a vyatirikta deśa kālam eva utpadyate brahmaṇā ca a vyatirikta deśa kālam eva ākāśam bhavati iti atas brahmaṇā tad kāryeṇa ca saha vijñātam eva ākāśam bhavati yathā kṣīra pūrṇe ghaṭe katicid abbidavaḥ prakṣiptāḥ satas kṣīra grahaṇe eva gṛhītā bhavati a hi kṣīra grahaṇāt ap bidu grahaṇam pariśiṣyate evam brahmaṇā tad kāryaiḥ ca a vyatirikta deśa kāla tvāt gṛhītam eva abhaḥ bhavati tasmāt bhāktam abhasaḥ saṃbhava śravaṇam iti evam prāpte idam āha pratijñā hāiḥ avyatirekāt śabdebhyaḥ bhavati amatam matam avijñātam vijñātam iti ātmani khalvare dṛṣṭe śrute mate vijñāte idam sarvam viditam iti kasmin bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati iti vidyā asti iti ca evaṃrūpā pratijñā vijñāyate tasyāḥ pratijñāyāḥ syāt yadi a vyatirekaḥ kṛtsasya vastu jātasya vijñeyāt brahmaṇaḥ syāt vyatireke hi sati sarvam vijñāyate iti iyam pratijñā hīyeta sa ca avyatirekaḥ evam upapadyate yadi kṛtsam vastu jātam ekasmāt brahmaṇaḥ utpadyeta śabdebhyaḥ ca prakṛti vikāra avyatireka eva pratijñā siddhiḥ avagamyate tathā hi bhavati iti pratijñāya mṛd ādi dṛṣṭātaiḥ kārya kāraṇa abheda pratipāda aparaiḥ pratijñā eṣā samarthyate tad sādhaāya eva ca uttare śabdāḥ sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam tat aikṣata tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti evam kārya jātam brahmaṇaḥ pradarśya a vyatirekam pradarśayati aitadātmyam id sarvam iti ārabhya ā prapāṭhaka parisamāpteḥ tat yadi ākāśam a brahma kāryam syāt a brahmaṇi vijñāte ākāśam vijñāyeta tatas ca pratijñā hāiḥ syāt a ca pratijñā hāyāḥ vedasya a prāmāṇyam yuktam kartum tathā hi te te śabdāḥ tea tea tām eva pratijñām jñāpayati idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā brahma eva idam amṛtam purastāt iti evamādayaḥ tasmāt jvala ādi vat eva gagaam api utpadyate yat uktam viyat utpadyate iti tat ayuktam viyat utpatti viṣaya śruti atarasya darśita tvāt tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti satyam darśitam viruddham tu tat tejaḥ sṛjate śrutyatareṇa ekavākya tvāt sarva śrutīām bhavatu ekavākya tvam aviruddhāām iha tu virodhaḥ uktaḥ sakṛt śrutasya sraṣṭuḥ sraṣṭavya dvaya asaṃbhavāt dvayoḥ ca prathama ja tva asaṃbhavāt vikalpa asaṃbhavāt ca iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ tejaḥ sargasya taittirīyake tṛtīya tva śravaṇāt tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ ākāśāt vāyuḥ vāyoḥ agiḥ iti aśakyā hi iyam śrutiḥ ayathā pariṇetum śakyā tu pariṇetum chādogya śrutiḥ tat ākāśam vāyum ca sṛṣṭvā tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti a hi iyam śrutiḥ satī śruti atara prasiddhām ākāśasya utpattim vārayitum ekasya vākyasya vyāpāra dvaya asaṃbhavāt sraṣṭā tu ekaḥ api krameṇa ekam sraṣṭavyam sṛjet iti ekavākya tva kalpaāyām saṃbhavatyām a viruddha artha tve śrutiḥ hātavyā ca asmābhiḥ sakṛt śrutasya sraṣṭuḥ sraṣṭavya dvaya saṃbandhaḥ abhipreyate sraṣṭavya atara upasaṃgrahāt yathā ca sarvam khalu idam brahma tat jalāḥ iti atra sākṣāt eva sarvasya vastu jātasya brahma ja tvam śrūyamāṇam a pradeśa atara vihitam tejaḥ pramukham utpatti kramam vārayati evam tejasaḥ api brahma ja tvam śrūyamāṇam a śrutyatara vihitam abhaḥ pramukham utpatti kramam vārayitum arhati śama vidhā artham etat vākyam upāsīta iti śruteḥ śruteḥ tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti etat sṛṣṭi vākyam tasmāt atra yathāśruti kramaḥ grahītavyaḥ iti ā iti ucyate hi viyat padārthaḥ parityaktavyaḥ bhavati padārtha dharma tvāt kramasya api ca tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti atra kramasya vācakaḥ kaścid śabdaḥ asti arthāt tu kramaḥ gamyate sa ca vāyoḥ agiḥ śruti atara prasiddhea krameṇa vikalpa samuccayau tu viyat tejasoḥ prathama ja tva viṣayau asaṃbhava aabhyupagamābhyām tasmāt asti śrutyoḥ vipratiṣedhaḥ api ca chādogye viyat utpattau upasaṃkhyātavyam kim aṅga saṃgṛhyate yat ca uktam ākāśasya sarveṇa āaya deśa kāla tvāt brahmaṇā tad kāryaiḥ ca saha viditam eva tat bhavati atas a pratijñā hīyate a ca ekam eva advitīyam iti śruti kopaḥ bhavati kṣīrodaka vat brahma abhasoḥ avyatireka upapatteḥ iti atra ucyate a sarva vijñāam etavyam mṛd ādi dṛṣṭāta praṇayaāt hi prakṛti vikāra eva idam sarva vijñāam etavyam iti gamyate ca sarva vijñāam a samyak vijñāam syāt a hi kṣīra jñā a gṛhītasya udakasya samyak vijñā a gṛhīta tvam asti a ca vedasya puruṣāṇām iva māyā alīka vañca ādibhiḥ artha avadhāraṇam upapadyate sa avadhāraṇā ca iyam ekam eva advitīyam iti śrutiḥ pīḍyeta ca sva kārya apekṣayā idam vastu eka deśa viṣayam ca iti yāyyam mṛd ādiṣu api hi tad saṃbhavāt bhavati śvetaketo yau somya idam bhavati śvetaketo yau somya idam tam ādeśam aprākṣyaḥ tasmāt aśeṣa vastu viṣayam eva idam sarva vijñāam sarvasya brahma kāryatā apekṣayā upayasyata iti draṣṭavyam yat puar etat uktam asaṃbhavāt gauṇī gaga asya utpatti śrutiḥ iti atra brūmaḥ yāvadvikāram tu vibhāgaḥ loka vat tuśabda ūsaṃbhava āśaṅkā vyāvṛtti arthaḥ a khalu ākāśa utpattau asaṃbhava āśaṅkā kartavyā yatas yāvat kiṃcid vikāra jātam dṛśyate ghaṭa ghaṭikā udañca ādi vā kaṭaka keyūra kuṇḍala ādi vā sūcī ārācaistriṃśa ādi vā vibhāgaḥ loke lakṣyate a tu avikṛtam kiṃcid kutaścid vibhaktam upalabhyate vibhāgaḥ ca ākāśasya pṛthivī ādibhyaḥ avagamyate tasmāt saḥ api vikāraḥ bhavitum arhati diś kāla maaḥ paramāṇu ādīām kārya tvam vyākhyātam ātmā api ākāśa ādibhyaḥ vibhaktaḥ iti tasya api kārya tvam ghaṭa ādi vat ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti śruteḥ yadi hi ātmā api vikāraḥ syāt tasmāt param śrutam iti ākāśa ādi sarvam kāryam kārya tve syāt tathā ca śūyavādaḥ prasajyeta ātma tvāt ca ātmanaḥ irā karaṇa śaṅkā upapattiḥ a hi ātmā āgatukaḥ kasyacid svayam siddha tvāt a hi ātmā ātmanaḥ pramāṇam apekṣya sidhyati tasya hi upādīyate hi ākāśa ādayaḥ padārthāḥ pramāṇaiḥ apekṣāḥ svayam siddhāḥ keacid abhyupagamyate ātmā tu pramāṇa ādi vyavahāra āśraya tvāt prāk eva pramāṇa ādi vyavahārāt sidhyati a ca īdṛśasya saṃbhavati āgatukam hi vastu irākriyate a svarūpam yaḥ eva hi irākartā tat eva tasya svarūpam hi ageḥ auṣṇyam agiā irākriyate tathā aham eva idāīm vartamāam vastu aham eva atītam atītataram ca ajñāsiṣam aham eva āgatam aāgatataram ca jñāsyāmi iti atīta a āgata vartamā abhāve a yathābhavati api jñātavye sarvadā vartamā asvabhāva tvāt tathā bhasmībhavati api dehe ātma ucchedaḥ vā a saṃbhāvayitum śakyam evam apratyākhyeya svabhāva tvāt akārya tvam ātmā aḥ kārya tvam ca ākāśasya yat tu uktam kāraṇa dravyam tat pratyucyate a tāvat samā ajātīyam eva ārabhate a hi tad saṃyogāām ca samā ajātīya tvam asti dravya guṇa tva abhyupagamāt ca imitta kāraṇāām api turī vema ādīām syāt etat samavāyi kāraṇa viṣaye eva kāraṇa atara viṣayaḥ iti tat api aaikātikam sūtra go vālaiḥ hi a eka jātīyaiḥ ekā rajjuḥ dṛśyate tathā sūtraiḥ ūrṇā ādibhiḥ ca sattva dravya tva ādi apekṣayā vā sama a jātīya tve sarvasya sarveṇa sama a jātīyaka tvāt āpya ekam eva ārabhate aikam iti aṇu maasoḥ ādya karma ārambha abhyupagamāt ekaikaḥ hi paramāṇuḥ maaḥ ca ādyam karma ārabhate aṇu maasoḥ ca ādyam karma ārabhate aṇu maasoḥ ca ādyam karma ārabhate aṇu maas ca ādyam karma ārabhate aṇu maas ca ādyam karma ārabhate aṇu maas ca ādyam karma ārabhate aṇu maas ca ādyam karma ārabhate dravya ataraiḥ saṃhatya iti abhyupagamyate dravya ārambhaḥ iti ced a pariṇāma abhyupagamāt bhavet eṣa iyamaḥ yadi saṃyoga sacivam dravyam dravya atarasya ārambhakam abhyupagamyeta tat eva tu dravyam kāryam tat ca kvacid a ekam pariṇamate mṛd bīja ādi kvacid ekam pariṇamate kṣīra ādi dadhi ādi bhāvea tathā ca uktam kṣīravat hi iti yat ca uktam ākāśasya utpattau a pūrva uttara kālayoḥ viśeṣaḥ saṃbhāvayitum śakyate iti tat ayuktam viśeṣeṇa pṛthivī ādibhyaḥ abhaḥ sva rūpa vat idāīm adhyavasīyate saḥ eva viśeṣaḥ prāk utpatteḥ āsīt iti gamyate yathā ca brahma a sthūla ādibhiḥ pṛthivī ādi svabhāvaiḥ svabhāvavat asthūlam aaṇu ityādi śrutibhyaḥ evam ākāśa svabhāve api a svabhāvavat aākāśam iti śruteḥ avagamyate tasmāt prāk utpatteḥ aākāśam iti sthitam yat api uktam pṛthivī ādi vaidharmyāt ākāśasya aja tvam iti tat api asat śruti virodhe sati utpatti asaṃbhava aumāasya ābhāsa tva upapatteḥ utpatti aumāasya ca darśita tvāt aityam ākāśam aitya guṇa āśraya tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat ityādi prayoga saṃbhavāt ca ātmaya aikātikam iti ced prati aitya guṇa āśraya tva asiddheḥ vibhu tva ca prati asiddha tvāt yat ca uktam etat śabdāt ca iti tatra amṛta tva śrutiḥ tāvat viyati amṛtāḥ divaukasaḥ iti vat draṣṭavyā utpatti pralayayoḥ upapādita tvāt ākāśa vat sarva gataḥ ca ityaḥ iti api kriyate ākāśa sama tvāya yathā iṣuḥ iva savitā dhāvati iti kṣipra gati tvāya ucyate a iṣu tulya gati tvāya tadvat ete ā atatva upamā aśrutiḥ vyākhyātā jyāyāḥ ākāśāt ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ca brahmaṇaḥ sakāśāt ākāśasya u parimāṇa tva siddhiḥ a tasya pratimā asti iti ca darśayati iti ca brahmaṇaḥ yeṣām ākāśa ādīām ārta tvam darśayati tapasi brahma śabda vat ākāśasya jama śruteḥ gauṇa tvam iti etat ākāśa saṃbhava śrutyā aumāābhyām parihṛtam tasmāt brahma kāryam viyat iti siddham mātariśvā vyākhyātaḥ mātariśva adhikaraṇam atideśaḥ yam viyat vyākhyāea mātariśvā api viyat āśrayaḥ vāyuḥ vyākhyātaḥ tatra api ete yathāyogam pakṣāḥ racayitavyāḥ vāyuḥ utpadyate chadogāām utpatti prakaraṇe āmāam iti ekaḥ pakṣaḥ asti tu taittirīyāṇām utpatti prakaraṇe ākāśāt vāyuḥ iti pakṣa ataram tatas ca śrutyoḥ vipratiṣedhe sati gauṇī vāyoḥ utpatti śrutiḥ asaṃbhavāt iti aparaḥ abhiprāyaḥ asaṃbhavaḥ ca sā eṣā astamitā devatā yat vāyuḥ iti astamaya pratiṣedhāt amṛta tva ādi śravaṇāt ca pratijñā uparodhāt yāvat vikāram ca vibhāga abhyupagamāt utpadyate vāyuḥ iti siddhātaḥ astamaya pratiṣedha upara vidyā viṣayaḥ āpekṣikaḥ ca amṛta tva ādi śravaṇam vāyoḥ ākāśasya ca tulyayoḥ utpatti prakaraṇe śravaṇa aśravaṇayoḥ ekam eva adhikaraṇam ubhaya viṣayam astu kim atideśe asati viśeṣaḥ iti ucyate satyam evam etat tathā api mada dhiyām śabda mātra kṛta āśaṅkā aivṛtti arthaḥ yam atideśaḥ kriyate saṃvarga vidyā ādiṣu hi upāsyata vāyoḥ mahābhāga tva śravaṇāt astamaya pratiṣedha ādibhyaḥ ca bhavati kasyacid iti asambhavaḥ tu satas upapatteḥ asaṃbhava adhikaraṇam utpattim upaśrutya brahmaṇaḥ api bhavet kutaścid utpattiḥ iti syāt kasyacid matiḥ tathā vikārebhyaḥ eva ākāśa ādibhyaḥ uttareṣām vikārāṇām utpattim upaśrutya ākāśasya api vikārāt eva brahmaṇaḥ utpattiḥ iti kaścid mayeta tām āśaṅkām apaetum idam sūtram asaṃbhavaḥ tu iti a khalu brahmaṇaḥ sat ātmakasya kutaścid ayataḥ saṃbhavaḥ utpattiḥ āśaṅkitavyā kasmāt aupapatteḥ samātram hi brahma tasya samātrāt eva utpattiḥ saṃbhavati asati atiśaye prakṛti vikāra bhāva aupapatteḥ sat viśeṣāt dṛṣṭa viparyayāt sāmāyāt viśeṣāḥ utpadyamāā dṛśyate mṛd ādeḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ a tu viśeṣebhyaḥ āpi asataḥ irā ātmaka tvāt katham asataḥ sat jāyeta iti ca ākṣepa śravaṇāt sa kāraṇam ca asya ca adhipaḥ iti ca brahmaṇaḥ jaayitāram vārayati viyat pavaayoḥ puar utpattiḥ pradarśitā a tu brahmaṇaḥ sā asti iti vaiṣamyam a ca vikārebhyaḥ vikāra atara utpatti darśaāt brahmaṇaḥ api vikāra tvam bhavitum arhati mūlaprakṛtyā abhyupagame avasthā prasaṅgāt yā mūlaprakṛtiḥ abhyupagamyate tat eva ca brahma iti avirodhaḥ brahma iti avirodhaḥ chādogye sa mūla tvam tejasaḥ śrāvitam taittirīyake tu vāyu mūla tvam tatra prati śruti vipratipattau satyām prāptam tāvat brahmayoikam tejaḥ iti kutas sa devaḥ iti upakramya tat tejaḥ sṛjataḥ iti upadeśāt sarvavijñāa pratijñāyāḥ ca brahma prabhava tve sarvasya saṃbhavāt tad jalāḥ iti ca aviśeṣa śruteḥ etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ iti ca upakramya śrutyatare sarvasya aviśeṣeṇa brahma ja tva upadeśāt taittirīyake ca sa tapaḥ taptvā idam sarvam asṛjata yat idam kiṃca iti aviśeṣa śravaṇāt tasmāt vāyoragiḥ iti krama upadeśaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti evam prāpte ucyate tejaḥ atas mātariśvaaḥ jāyate iti kasmāt tathā hi āha vāyoragiḥ iti avyavahite hi tejasaḥ brahma ja tve sati asati vāyu ja tve vāyoragiḥ iti iyam śrutiḥ kadarthitā syāt krama arthā eṣā bhaviṣyati iti uktam ā iti brūmaḥ tasmāt vai etasmāt ātman ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti purastāt ātmanaḥ pañcamībhiḥ deśāt tasya eva ca saṃbhavateḥ iha adhikārāt parastāt api tad adhikāre pṛthivyāḥ oṣadhayaḥ iti apādāa pañcamī darśaāt vāyoḥ agiḥ iti apādāa pañcamī eva eṣā iti gamyate api ca vāyoḥ ūrdhvam agiḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti kalpyaḥ upapadārtha yogaḥ klṛptaḥ tu kāraka artha yogaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti tasmāt eṣā śrutiḥ tejasā uvagamayati avitarā api śrutiḥ brahma yoitvam tejasā uvagamayati tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti a tasyāḥ pāraṃparya ja tve pi avirodhāt yadā api hi ākāśam vāyum ca sṛṣṭvā brahma kalpyate tadā api brahma ja tvam tejasaḥ virudhyate yathā tasyāḥ śrṛtam tasyāḥ dadhi tasyāḥ āmikṣā ityādi darśayati ca brahmaṇaḥ iti tathā ca īśvara smaraṇam bhavati buddhiḥ jñā asaṃmohaḥ bhavati bhāvāḥ bhūtāām mattaḥ eva pṛthagvidhāḥ iti yadi api buddhi ādayaḥ sva kāraṇebhyaḥ pratyakṣam bhavataḥ dṛśyate tathā api sarvasya bhāva jātasya sākṣāt praṇāḍyā vā īśvara vaṃśya tvāt śrutayaḥ vyākhyātāḥ tāsām sarvathā upapatteḥ tu ayathā upapatteḥ pratijñā api sat vaṃśya tva mātram apekṣate as vaṃśya tva mātram apekṣate avyavahita jaya tvam iti avirodhaḥ āpaḥ atas tathā hi āha āpaḥ atas tejasaḥ jāyate kasmāt tathā hi āha tat aposṛjata iti ageḥ apaḥ iti ca sati saṃśayaḥ tejasaḥ tu sṛṣṭim vyākhyāya pṛthivyāḥ vyākhyāsya apotariyām iti āpaḥ iti sūtrayāṃbabhūva pṛthivī adhikāra rūpa śabda atarebhyaḥ pṛthivī adhikāra adhikaraṇam tāḥ āpaḥ aikṣata bahvyaḥ syāma prajāyemahi iti tāḥ aam asṛjata iti śrūyate tatra saṃśayaḥ kim vrīhi yava ādi abhyavahāryam vai oda ādi ucyate kim vā pṛthivī iti tatra prāptam tāvat vrīhi yava ādi oda ādi vā parigrahītavyam iti tatra hi aa śabdaḥ prasiddhaḥ loke vākyaśeṣaḥ u pi etam artham upodbalayati tasmāt yatra kva ca a varṣati tat eva bhūyiṣṭham aam bhavati iti vrīhi yava ādi eva hi sati varṣaṇe bahu bhavati evam prāpte brūmaḥ pṛthivī eva iyam vivakṣyate iti kasmāt adhikārāt rūpāt śabda atarāt ca adhikāraḥ tāvat tat tejaḥ sṛjata tat apaḥ sṛjata iti mahābhūta viṣayaḥ vartate tatra krama prāptām pṛthivīm mahābhūtam vilaṅghya ākasmāt vrīhi ādi parigrahaḥ yāyyaḥ tathā rūpam api vākya śeṣe pṛthivī auguṇam dṛśyate yat kṛṣṇam tat iti a hi oda ādeḥ abhyavahāryasya kṛṣṇa tvaiyamaḥ sti vrīhi ādīām pṛthivyāḥ api ā eva kṛṣṇa tvaiyamaḥ sti payaḥ pāṇḍurasya aṅgāra rohitasya ca kṣetrasya darśaāt ā ayam doṣaḥ bāhulya apekṣa tvāt bhūyiṣṭham hi pṛthivyāḥ kṛṣṇam rūpam a tathā śvetarohite paurāṇikāḥ api pṛthivī chāyām śarvarīm upadiśati sā ca kṛṣṇa ābhāsā iti atas kṛṣṇam rūpam pṛthivyāḥ iti śliṣyate śrutyataram api adabhyaḥ pṛthivī iti bhavati tat yat apām śaraḥ āsīt tat samahayata sā pṛthivī abhavat iti ca pṛthivyāḥ tu vrīhi ādeḥ utpattim darśayati pṛthivyāḥ oṣadhayaḥ oṣadhībhyaḥ am iti ca evam adhikāra ādiṣu pṛthivyāḥ pratipādakeṣu satsu kutas vrīhi ādi pratipattiḥ prasiddhiḥ api adhikāra ādibhiḥ eva bādhyate asya tad dvāreṇa pṛthivyāḥ eva adbhyaḥ prabhava tvam sūcayati iti draṣṭavyam tasmāt pṛthivīyam a śabdaḥ iti tu tad liṅgāt saḥ tad abhidhyā adhikaraṇam kim imāi viyat ādīi bhūtāi svayam eva sva vikārān sṛjati āhosvit parameśvaraḥ eva tam tam vikāram sṛjati iti saṃdehe sati prāptam tāvat svayam eva sṛjati iti kutas ākāśāt vāyuḥ vāyoḥ agiḥ ityādi svātatrya śravaṇāt au acetaāām svatatrāṇām pravṛttiḥ pratiṣiddhā ā eṣa doṣaḥ tat tejaḥ aikṣata tāḥ āpaḥ aikṣata iti ca bhūtāām api cetas atva śravaṇāt iti evam prāpte abhidhīyate saḥ eva parameśvaraḥ avatiṣṭhamānaḥ abhidhyāya tam tam vikāram sṛjati iti kutas tad liṅgāt tathā hi śāstram yaḥ pṛthivyām pṛthivyāḥ ataraḥ yam pṛthivī veda yasya pṛthivī śarīram yaḥ pṛthivīm ataraḥ yamayati iti evaṃjātīyakam sādhyakṣāṇām eva bhūtāām pravṛttim darśayati tathā sā ukāmayata bahu syām prajāyeya iti iti prastutya sat ca tyad ca abhavat tat ātmā am svayam akuruta iti ca tasya eva ca sarva ātma bhāvam darśayati yat tu īkṣaṇa śravaṇam ap tejasoḥ tat parameśvara āveśa vaśāt eva draṣṭavyam draṣṭā iti īkṣitratara pratiṣedhāt prakṛta tvāt ca sataḥ īkṣituḥ tat aikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya iti iti atra viparyayeṇa tu krama ūtaḥ upapadyate ca viparyaya adhikaraṇam bhūtāām utpatti kramaḥ cititaḥ atha idāīm apyaya kramaḥ cityate krameṇa apyayaḥ uta utpatti krameṇa athavā trayaḥ api ca utpatti sthiti pralayāḥ bhūtāām brahma āyattāḥ śrūyate yatas vai imāi bhūtāi jāyate yea jātāi jīvati yat prayati abhisaṃviśati iti tatra aiyamaḥ viśeṣāt iti prāptam athavā utpatteḥ kramasya śruta tvāt pralayasya api krama ākāṅkṣiṇaḥ saḥ eva kramaḥ syāt iti evam prāptam tatas brūmaḥ viparyayeṇa tu pralaya kramaḥ atas utpatti kramāt bhavitum arhati tathā hi loke dṛśyate krameṇa sopāam ārūḍhaḥ tatas krameṇa avarohati iti api ca dṛśyate mṛdaḥ jātam ghaṭa śarāva ādi apyaya kāle mṛd bhāvam apyeti adbhyaḥ ca jātam himakaraka ādi ap bhāvam apyeti iti atas ca upapadyate etat yat pṛthivī adbhyaḥ jātā satī sthiti kāla vyatikrātau apaḥ apīyāt āpaḥ ca tejasaḥ jātāḥ satyaḥ tejaḥ apīyuḥ evam krameṇa sūkṣmam sūkṣmataram ca kāraṇam apītya sarvam kārya jātam parama kāraṇam parama sūkṣmam ca brahma apyeti iti veditavyam a hi sva kāraṇa vyatikrameṇa kāraṇa kāraṇe kārya apyayaḥ yāyyaḥ smṛtau api utpatti krama viparyayeṇa eva apyaya kramaḥ tatra tatra darśitaḥ jagat pratiṣṭhā deva ṛṣe pṛthivī apsu pralīyate jyotiṣi āpaḥ pralīyate jyotiḥ vāyau pralīyate iti evamādau utpatti kramaḥ tu utpattau eva bhavitum arhati a ca asau ayogya tvāt apyaye ākāṅkṣyate a hi kārye dhriyamāṇe kāraṇasya apyayaḥ yuktaḥ kāraṇa apyaye kāryasya avasthā a upapatteḥ kārya apyaye tu kāraṇasya avasthā yuktam mṛd ādiṣu evam dṛṣṭa tvāt atarā vijñāamaasī krameṇa tad liṅgāt iti ca iā aviśeṣāt bhūtāām utpatti pralayau auloma pratiloma kramābhyām bhavataḥ iti uktam ātma ādiḥ utpattiḥ pralayaḥ ca ātmā atas iti api uktam sa idriyasya tu maasaḥ buddheḥ ca sadbhāvaḥ prasiddhaḥ śruti smṛtyoḥ buddhim tu sārathim viddhi maaḥ pragraham eva ca idriyāṇi ityādi liṅgebhyaḥ tayoḥ api kasmiṃścid atarāle krameṇa utpatti pralayau upasaṃgrāhyau sarvasya vastu jātasya brahma ja tva abhyupagamāt api ca ātharvaṇe utpatti prakaraṇe etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ sarva idriyāṇi ca kham vāyuḥ jyotiḥ āpaḥ pṛthivī viśvasya dhāriṇī iti tasmāt pūrva ukta utpatti pralaya krama bhaṅga prasaṅgaḥ bhūtāām iti ced a aviśeṣāt yadi tāvat bhautikāi karaṇāi tatas bhūta utpatti pralayābhyām eva eṣām utpatti pralayau bhavataḥ iti ā etayoḥ mṛgyam bhavati ca bhautika tve liṅgam karaṇāām hi somya āpaḥ mayaḥ prāṇaḥ tejaḥ mayī vāc iti evaṃjātīyakam vyapadeśaḥ api kvacid bhūtāām karaṇāām ca etavyaḥ atha tu abhautikāi karaṇāi tathā api bhūta utpatti kramaḥ karaṇaiḥ viśiṣyate prathamam karaṇāt utpadyate caramam bhūta prathamam vā bhūtāt utpadyate caramam karaṇāi iti ātharvaṇe tu bhūtāām ca tatra utpatti kramaḥ ucyate tathā pṛthak eva bhūta kramāt karaṇa kramaḥ prajāpatiḥ vai idam agre āsīt saḥ ātmā amaikṣata sa maosṛjata tamaḥ eva āsīt tat ātmā amaikṣata tat vācam asṛjata ityādi tasmāt asti bhūta utpatti kramasya bhaṅgaḥ carācara vyapāśrayaḥ tu syāt tad vyapadeśaḥ bhāktaḥ tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt carācara vyapāśraya adhikaraṇam staḥ jīvasya api utpatti pralayau jātaḥ devadattaḥ mṛtaḥ devadattaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakāt laukika vyapadeśāt jātakarma ādi saṃskāra vidhāāt ca iti syāt kasyacid bhrātiḥ tāmapaudāmaḥ a jīvasya utpatti pralayau staḥ hi jīve hi jīve śarīra atara gata iṣṭa a iṣṭa prāpti parihāra arthau vidhi pratiṣedhau aarthakau syātām śrūyate ca jīva apetam vāva kila idam mriyate a jīvaḥ mriyate iti jama maraṇa vyapadeśaḥ jīvasya darśitaḥ satyam darśitaḥ bhāktaḥ tu eṣa jīvasya jama maraṇa vyapadeśaḥ kimāśrayaḥ mukhyaḥ yad apekṣayā bhāktaḥ iti ucyate carācara vyapāśrayaḥ sthāvara jaṅgama śarīra viṣayau jama maraṇa śabdau hi bhūta āi jāyate ca mriyate ca atas tad viṣayau jama maraṇa śabdau mukhyau satau tad sthe jīva ātmayupacaryete tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt śarīra prādurbhāva tirobhāvayoḥ hi satoḥ jama maraṇa śabdau bhavataḥ āsatoḥ hi jātaḥ mṛtaḥ vā kecid lakṣyate sa vai ayam puruṣaḥ jāyamāaḥ śarīram abhisaṃpadyamāaḥ saḥ utkrāma mriyamāṇaḥ iti ca śarīra saṃyoga viyoga aimittau eva jama maraṇa śabdau darśayati jātakarma ādi vidhāam api deha prādurbhāva apekṣam eva draṣṭavyam abhāvāt jīva prādurbhāvasya jīvasya parasmāt ātmā utpattiḥ viyat ādīām iva asti āsti vā iti etat uttareṇa sūtreṇa vakṣyati deha āśrayau tāvat jīvasya sthūlau utpatti pralayau staḥ iti etad aea sūtreṇa avocat ātma a śruteḥ iti atvāt ca tābhyaḥ ātma adhikaraṇam asti ātmā jīva ākhyaḥ śarīra idriya pañjara adhyakṣaḥ karma phala saṃbadhī sa kim vyoma ādi vat utpadyate brahmaṇaḥ āhosvit brahma vat eva ā utpadyate iti śruti vipratipatteḥ viśayaḥ kāsucid śrutiṣu parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ utpattiḥ āmāyate kāsucid tu avikṛtasya eva parasya brahmaṇaḥ jīva bhāvaḥ vijñāyate a ca utpattiḥ āmāyate iti tatra prāptam tāvat utpadyate jīvaḥ iti kutas pratijñā uparodhāt eva iti iyam pratijñā sarvasya vastu jātasya brahma prabhava tve sati oparudhyeta tattva atara tve tu jīvasya pratijñā iyam uparudhyeta a ca a vikṛtaḥ paramātmā eva jīvaḥ iti śakyate vijñātum lakṣaṇa bhedāt apahata pāpma tva ādi dharmakaḥ hi paramātmā tad viparītaḥ hi jīvaḥ vibhāgāt ca asya vikāra tva siddhiḥ yāvā hi ākāśa ādiḥ pravibhaktaḥ sa sarvaḥ vikāraḥ tasya ca ākāśa ādeḥ utpattiḥ samadhigatā jīvātmā api puṇya apuṇya karmā sukha duḥkha yuj pratiśarīram pravibhaktaḥ iti tasya api prapañca utpatti avasare utpattiḥ bhavitum arhati api ca yathā āgeḥ kṣudrāḥ visphuliṅgāḥ vyuccarati evam eva asmāt ātmanaḥ sarve prāṇāḥ iti prāṇa ādeḥ bhogya jātasya sṛṣṭim śiṣṭvā sarve ete vyuccarati iti bhoktṛṇām ātma pṛthak sṛṣṭim śāsti yathā su dīptāt pāvakāt visphuliṅgāḥ sahasraśas prabhavate sarūpāḥ tathā akṣarāt vividhāḥ somya bhāvāḥ prajāyate tatra ca eva apiyati iti ca utpatti pralayau ucyete sarūpa vacaāt hi bhavati caitaya yogāt ca kvacid aśravaṇam ayatra śrutam vārayitum arhati śruti atara gatasya api aviruddhasya adhikasya arthasya sarvatra upasaṃhartavya tvāt praveśa śrutiḥ api evam sati vikāra bhāva āpattyā eva vyākhyātavyā tadā ātmā aam svayam akuruta ityādi vat tasmāt utpadyate jīvaḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ ātmā jīvaḥ utpadyate iti kasmāt aśruteḥ a hi asya utpatti prakaraṇe śravaṇam asti bhūyaḥsu pradeśeṣu kvacid aśravaṇam ayatra śrutam a vārayati iti uktam satyam uktam utpattiḥ eva tvasya a saṃbhavati iti vadāmaḥ kasmāt itya tvāt ca tābhyaḥ caśabdāt aja tva ādibhyaḥ ca itya tvam hi asya śrutibhyaḥ uvagamyate tathā aja tvam avikāri tvam avikṛtasya eva brahmaṇaḥ ca iti ca evaṃrūpasya utpattiḥ upapadyate tāḥ kāḥ śrutayaḥ jīvaḥ mriyate sa vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ ātmā ajaroma romṛta ubhayaḥ brahma a jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit ajaḥ ityaḥ śāśvataḥ yam purāṇaḥ
