tat sṛṣṭvā tat eva auprāviśat āma rūpe vyākaravāṇi saḥ eṣaḥ iha praviṣṭaḥ ā akha agrebhyaḥ tat tvam asi aham brahma asmi ayam ātmā brahma sarva aubhūḥ iti evamādyāḥ satyaḥ jīvasya utpattim pratibadhati pravibhakta tvāt vikāraḥ vikāra tvāt ca utpadyate iti uktam atra ucyate pravibhāgaḥ svatas sti ekaḥ devaḥ sarva bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarva vyāpī sarva bhūta atarātmā iti śruteḥ buddhi ādi upādhi nimittam tu asya ākāśasya iva tathā ca śāstram sa vai ayam ātmā brahma vijñāa mayaḥ mao mayaḥ prāṇa mayaḥ cakṣuḥ mayaḥ śrotra mayaḥ iti evamādi brahmaṇaḥ eva avikṛtasya sataḥ asya ekasya a eka buddhi ādi maya tvam darśayati tamaya tvam ca asya tad vivikta svarūpa abhivyaktyā tad uparakta svarūpa tvam strī mayaḥ jālmaḥ ityādi vat draṣṭavyam yat api kvacid asya utpatti pralaya śravaṇam tat api atas upādhi utpattyā asya utpattiḥ ca pralayaḥ iti tathā ca darśayati eva etebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ samutthāya a pretya saṃjñā asti iti tathā upādhi pralaye eva ayam ātma vilayaḥ iti etat api atra eva mā vā aham imam vijāāmi a pretya saṃjñā asti iti praśa pūrvakam pratipādayati a vā are ham moham bravīmi aviāśī vai are iyam ātmā a ucchitti dharmā mātrā saṃsargaḥ tu asya bhavati iti pratijñā uparodhaḥ upi avikṛtasya eva brahmaṇaḥ jīva bhāva abhyupagamāt lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ upi a yoḥ upādhi imitte eva atas ūrdhvam vimokṣāya eva brūhi iti ca prakṛtasya eva sarva saṃsāra dharma pratyākhyāea paramātma bhāva pratipādaāt tasmāt eva ātmā utpadyate pravilīyate ca iti jñā utaḥ eva jñā adhikaraṇam sa kim āhosvit sāṃkhya iva iti acaitaya svarūpaḥ eva iti vādi vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam āgatukam ātma aścaitayam ātma maaḥ saṃyoga jam agi ghaṭa saṃyoga ja rohita ādi guṇavat iti prāptam iti acaitaya tve hi supta mūrchita graha āviṣṭāām api caitayam syāt te pṛṣṭāḥ sataḥ a kiṃcid vayam cetayemahi iti jalpati svasthāḥ ca cetayamānāḥ dṛśyate atas kādācitka caitaya tvāt āgatuka caitayaḥ ātmā iti evam prāpte abhidhīyate jñaḥ iti a caitayaḥ yam ātmā atas eva yasmāt eva otpadyate param eva brahma avikṛtam upādhi saṃparkāt jīva bhāve avatiṣṭhate parasya hi brahmaṇaḥ caitaya svarūpa tvam āmātam brahma satyam jñāamaatam brahma kṛtsaḥ eva ityādiṣu śrutiṣu tat eva ced param brahma jīvaḥ tasmāt jīvasya api gamyate vijñā amaya prakriyāyām ca śrutayaḥ bhavati a suptaḥ supta a abhicākaśīti atra ayam puruṣaḥ svayam jyotiḥ bhavati iti a hi vijñātuḥ vijñāteḥ viparilopaḥ vidyate iti evaṃrūpāḥ atha yaḥ veda idam jighrāṇi iti saḥ ātmā iti ca sarvaiḥ karaṇa dvāraiḥ idam veda idam veda iti tad rūpa tva siddhiḥ iti acaitaya svarūpa tve ghrāṇa ādi āarthakyam iti ced a gadha ādi viṣaya viśeṣa pariccheda artha tvāt tathā hi darśayati gadhāya ghrāṇam ityādi yat tu supta ādayaḥ cetayataḥ iti tasya śrutyā eva parihāraḥ abhihitaḥ suṣuptam prakṛtya yat vai paśyati hi draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭeḥ viparilopaḥ a tu tat dvitīyam asti tatas yat vibhaktam yat paśyet ityādiā etat uktam bhavati viṣaya abhāvāt iyam acetayamāatā a caitayābhāvāt iti yathā viyat āśrayasya prakāśasya prakāśya abhāvāt a abhivyaktiḥ a svarūpa abhāvāt tadvat vaiśeṣika ādi tarkaḥ ca śruti virodha ābhāsībhavati eva ātmā iti utkrātigati adhikaraṇam idāīm tu kiṃparimāṇaḥ jīvaḥ iti cityate kim aṇu parimāṇaḥ uta madhyama parimāṇaḥ āhosvit mahā parimāṇaḥ iti ca ātmā utpadyate ca ayam iti uktam atas ca paraḥ eva ātmā jīvaḥ iti āpatati parasya ca tatra kutas jīvasya parimāṇa citā avatāraḥ iti ucyate satyam etat tu jīvasya paricchedam prāpayati ca asya kvacid aṇu parimāṇa tvam tasya sarvasya ākula tva upapāda ayam ārambhaḥ tatra prāptam tāvat śravaṇāt jīvaḥ iti utkrātiḥ tāvat sa yadā asmāt śarīrāt utkrāmati saha eva etaiḥ sarvaiḥ utkrāmati iti gatiḥ api ye vai ke ca asmāt lokāt prayati ca cadramasam eva te sarve gacchati iti āgatiḥ api tasmāt lokāt puar aiti asmai lokāya karmaṇe iti āsām śravaṇāt tāvat jīvaḥ iti hi vibhoḥ aṇuḥ ātmā iti gamyate sva ātma ā ca uttarayoḥ utkrātiḥ kadācid acalataḥ api grāma svāmi aivṛtti vat deha svāmi aivṛttyā karma kṣayeṇa avakalpeta uttare tu gati āgatī ācalataḥ saṃbhavataḥ sva ātma ā hi tayoḥ bhavati gameḥ kartṛ stha kriyā tvāt amadhyama parimāṇasya ca gati āgatī aṇu tve eva saṃbhavataḥ satyoḥ ca gati āgatyoḥ utkrātiḥ api apasṛptiḥ eva dehāt iti pratīyate hi dehāt gati āgatī syātām deha pradeśāām ca utkrātau cakṣuṣṭoma vā mūrdhaḥ vāyebhyaḥ vā śaīra deśebhyaḥ iti saḥ etāḥ tejaḥ mātrāḥ samabhyādadai hṛdayam eva avavakrāmati śukram ādāya puaraiti iti ca atare api śarīre śārīrasya gati āgatī bhavataḥ tasmāt api asya aṇu tva siddhiḥ āṇuḥ a tad śruteḥ iti ced itara adhikārāt atha api syāt āṇuḥ ayam ātmā kasmāt a tad śruteḥ aṇu tva viparīta parimāṇa śravaṇāt iti arthaḥ sa vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ ātmā yaḥ yam vijñā a mayaḥ prāṇeṣu ākāśa vat sarva gataḥ ca satyam satyam brahma iti evaṃjātīyakā hi śrutiḥ ātma oṇu tve vipratiṣidhyeta iti ced ā eṣa doṣaḥ kasmāt itara adhikārāt parasya hi ātmanaḥ prakriyāyām eṣā parimāṇa atara śrutiḥ parasya eva ātmanaḥ prādhāyea prakṛta tvāt virajaḥ paras ākāśāt iti evaṃvidhāt ca parasya eva ātmanaḥ tatra tatra viśeṣa adhikārāt yaḥ yam vijñā a mayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti śārīre eva pratiirdiśyate śāstra dṛṣṭyā tu eṣaḥ irdeśaḥ vāmadeva vat draṣṭavyaḥ tasmāt prājña viṣaya tvāt parimāṇa atara śravaṇasya ca itas ca aṇuḥ ātmā yatas sākṣāt eva asya aṇu tva vācī śabdaḥ śrūyate eṣa uṇuḥ ātmā cetasā veditavyaḥ yasmin prāṇaḥ pañcadhā saṃviveśa iti jīvaḥ eva ayam aṇuḥ abhihitaḥ iti gamyate tathā umāam api jīvasya aṇimāam gamayati vāla agra śata bhāgasya śatadhā kalpitasya ca bhāgaḥ jīvaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ iti ārā agra mātraḥ hi avaraḥ api dṛṣṭaḥ iti ca a vaṇu tve sati eka deśa sthasya sakala deha gata upalabdhiḥ virudhyate dṛśyate ca sarva aṅga śaitya upalabdhiḥ idāgha samaye ca sakala śarīra paritāpa upalabdhiḥ iti atas uttaram paṭhati avirodhaḥ cadaa vat yathā hi śarīra eka deśa saṃbaddhaḥ api sa sakala deha vyāpiam āhlādam karoti evam ātmā api deha eka deśa sthaḥ sakala deha vyāpiīm upalabdhim kariṣyati tvac saṃbadhāt ca asya sakala śarīra gatā virudhyate tvac ātmaoḥ hi saṃbadhaḥ kṛtsāyām tvaci vartate tvac ca kṛtsa śarīra vyāpi iti avasthiti vaiśeṣyāt iti ced abhyupagamāt hṛdi hi atra āha yat uktam avirodhaḥ cadaa vat iti tat ayuktam dṛṣṭāta dārṣṭātikayoḥ atulya tvāt siddhe hi deha eka deśa stha tve bhavati pratyakṣam tu cadaasya avasthiti vaiśeṣyam eka deśa stha tvam sakala deha āhlādam ca ātmaaḥ ca sakala deha upalabdhi mātram pratyakṣam aikadeśavartitvam aumeyam tu tat iti yat api ucyeta sakala śarīra gatāḥ sataḥ kim vā vibhoḥ abhasaḥ iva āhosvit cada abidoḥ iva aṇoḥ eka deśa sthasya iti saṃśaya aativṛtteḥ iti atra ucyate doṣaḥ kasmāt abhyupagamāt abhyupagamyate hi deha eka deśa vṛtti tvam avasthiti vaiśeṣyam katham iti ucyate hṛdi hi eṣaḥ ātmā paṭhyate hṛdi hi eṣaḥ ātmā sa vai eṣaḥ ātmā hṛdi katamaḥ ātmā iti yaḥ yam vijñā a mayaḥ prāṇeṣu hṛdi atas jyotiḥ puruṣaḥ ityādi upadeśebhyaḥ tasmāt dṛṣṭa a ta dārṣṭātikayoḥ avaiṣamyāt yuktam eva etat avirodhaḥ ca daa vat iti guṇāt vā loka vat caitaya guṇa vyāpteḥ vā aṇoḥ api sataḥ jīvasya sakala deha vyāpi kāryam virudhyate yathā loke maṇi pradīpa prabhṛtīām apavaraka eka deśa vartiām api prabhā satī kāryam karoti tadvat syāt sakala dehe āhlādayitṛ tvam sakala dehe āhlādayitṛ tvam a tu aṇoḥ jīvasya avayavāḥ sati yaiḥ ayam sakala deham visarpet iti āśaṅkya guṇāt vā loka vat iti uktam katham varteta a hi paṭasya śuklaḥ guṇaḥ paṭa vyatirekeṇa a yatra dṛśyate pradīpa prabhāvat bhavet iti ced a tasyāḥ api dravya tva abhyupagamāt ibiḍa avayavam hi tejaḥ dravyam pradīpaḥ pravirala avayavam tu tejaḥ dravyam eva prabhā iti atas uttaram paṭhati vyatirekaḥ gadha vat yathā guṇasya api sataḥ gadhasya gadhavat dravya vyatirekeṇa vṛttiḥ bhavati aprāpteṣu api kusuma ādiṣu gadhavatsu kusuma gadha upalabdheḥ evam aṇoḥ api sataḥ jīvasya caitaya guṇa vyatirekaḥ bhaviṣyati atas ca aaikātikam etat guṇa tvāt rūpa ādi vat āśraya viśleṣa aupapattiḥ iti guṇasya eva sataḥ gadhasya āśraya viśleṣa darśaāt gadhasya api saha eva āśrayeṇa viśleṣaḥ iti ced a yasmāt mūla dravyāt viśleṣaḥ tasya kṣaya prasaṅgāt a kṣīyamāṇam api tat pūrva avasthātaḥ gamyate ayathā tat pūrva avasthaiḥ guru tva ādibhiḥ hīyeta syāt etat gadha āśrayāṇām viśliṣṭāām avayavāām alpatvāt sa api viśleṣaḥ opalakṣyate sūkṣmāḥ hi gadha paramāṇavaḥ sarvatas viprasṛtāḥ gadha buddhim utpādayati iti ced a ati idriya tvāt paramāṇūām sphuṭa gadha upalabdheḥ ca āga kesara ādiṣu a ca loke pratītiḥ gadha vat dravyam āghrātam iti gadhaḥ eva āghrātaḥ iti tu laukikāḥ pratiyati rūpa ādiṣu āśraya vyatireka a upalabdheḥ gadhasya api ayuktaḥ āśraya vyatirekaḥ iti ced a pratyakṣa tvāt aumāā pravṛtteḥ tasmāt yat yathā loke dṛṣṭam tat tathā eva aumatavyam hi rasaḥ guṇaḥ jihvayā upalabhyate iti atas rūpa ādayaḥ api guṇāḥ jihvayā eva upalabhyera eti śakyate tathā ca darśayati hṛdaya āyata atvam aṇu parimāṇa tvam ca abhidhāya tasya eva ā lomabhyaḥ ā akha agrebhyaḥ iti samasta śarīra vyāpi tvam darśayati pṛthak upadeśāt prajñayā śarīram samāruhya iti ca ātma prajñayoḥ kartṛ karaṇa bhāve pṛthak upadeśāt asya śarīra vyāpi tā gamyate tat eṣām prāṇāām vijñāam ādāya iti ca kartuḥ śārīrāt pṛthak vijñāasya upadeśaḥ etam eva abhiprāyam upodbalayati tasmāt aṇuḥ ātmā iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ tad guṇa sāra tvāt tu tad vyapadeśaḥ prājña vat tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati aitat asti aṇuḥ ātmā iti utpatti aśravaṇāt parasya eva tu brahmaṇaḥ praveśa śravaṇāt tādātmya upadeśāt ca param eva brahma jīvaḥ iti uktam param eva ced brahma jīvaḥ tasmāt yāvat param brahma tāvā eva jīvaḥ bhavitum arhati parasya ca brahmaṇaḥ vibhu tvam āmātam tasmāt vibhuḥ jīvaḥ tathā ca sa vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ ātmā yaḥ yam vijñā a mayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ jīva viṣayāḥ vibhu tva vādāḥ śrautāḥ smārtāḥ ca samarthitā bhavati ca aṇoḥ jīvasya sakala śarīra gatā upapadyate sakala śarīra gatā eva vedaā prasajyeta tvac kaṇṭakayoḥ hi saṃyogaḥ kṛtsāyām tvaci vartate tvac ca pāda tale eva tu pratilabhate ca aṇoḥ guṇa vyāptiḥ upapadyate guṇasya guṇi deśa tvāt guṇa tvam eva hi guṇi āśritya guṇasya hīyeta pradīpa prabhāyāḥ ca dravya ātara tvam vyākhyātam gadhaḥ api guṇa tva abhyupagamāt sa āśrayaḥ eva saṃcaritum arhati ayathā guṇa tva hāi prasaṅgāt tathā ca uktam bhagavatā dvaipāyaea upalabhya apsu ced gadham kecid brūyuḥ aaipuṇāḥ pṛthivyām eva tam vidyāt apaḥ vāyum ca saṃśritam iti yadi ca caitayam jīvasya samasta śarīram vyāpuyāt āṇuḥ jīvaḥ syāt caitayam eva hi asya svarūpam ageḥ iva auṣṇya prakāśau guṇa guṇi vibhāgaḥ vidyate iti śarīra parimāṇa tvam ca pratyākhyātam pariśeṣāt vibhuḥ jīvaḥ katham tarhi aṇu tva ādi vyapadeśaḥ iti atas āha tad guṇa sāra tvāt tu tad vyapadeśaḥ iti tasyāḥ buddheḥ guṇāḥ tad guṇāḥ icchā dveṣaḥ sukham duḥkham iti evamādayaḥ tad guṇāḥ sāraḥ pradhā yasya ātmaaḥ saṃsāri tve saṃbhavati sa tad guṇa sāraḥ tasya bhāvaḥ tad guṇa sāra tvam hi buddheḥ guṇaiḥ kevalasya ātmaaḥ saṃsāri tvam asti buddhi upādhi dharma adhyāsa nimittam hi kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva ādi lakṣaṇam saṃsāri tvam akartuḥ abhoktuḥ ca asaṃsāriṇaḥ iti amuktasya sataḥ ātmaaḥ tasmāt tad guṇa sāra tvāt buddhi parimāṇe ā asya parimāṇa vyapadeśaḥ tad utkrāti ādibhiḥ ca asya utkrāti ādi vyapadeśaḥ a svataḥ tathā ca vāla agra śata bhāgasya śatadhā kalpitasya ca bhāgaḥ jīvaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ sa ca āatyāya kalpate iti aṇu tvam jīvasya uktvā tasya eva puarāatyam āha tat ca evam eva samañjasam syāt yadi aupacārikam aṇu tvam jīvasya bhavet pāramārthikam a hi ubhayam mukhyam avakalpeta a ca āatyam aupacārikam iti śakyam vijñātum sarva upaiṣatsu brahma ātmabhāvasya pratipipādayiṣita tvāt tathā itarasmi api umāe ca eva ārā agra mātraḥ hi avaraḥ api dṛṣṭaḥ iti ca ārā agra mātra tām śāsti a eṣa uṇuḥ ātmā cetasā veditavyaḥ iti atra api a jīvasya aṇu parimāṇa tvam śiṣyate ca prakṛta tvāt jīvasya api ca mukhya aṇu parimāṇa tva aupapatteḥ tasmāt durjñāatva abhiprāyam idam aṇu tva vacaam upādhi abhiprāyam vā draṣṭavyam tathā prajñayā śarīram samāruhya iti evaṃjātīyakeṣu api bheda upadeśeṣu buddhyā eva upādhi bhūtayā jīvaḥ śarīram samāruhya iti evam yojayitavyam vyapadeśa mātram vā śilāputrakasya śarīram ityādi vat vidyate iti uktam buddheḥ eva tad āyata a tvāt tathā aham utkrātaḥ utkrātaḥ bhaviṣyāmi kasmivā pratiṣṭhite pratiṣṭhāsyāmi iti sa prāṇam asṛjata iti utkrāti abhāve hi gati āgatyoḥ api abhāvaḥ vijñāyate a hi dehāt gati āgatī syātām evam upādhi guṇa sāra tvāt jīvasya aṇu tva ādi vyapadeśaḥ prājña vat yathā prājñasya paramātmaaḥ sa guṇeṣu upāsaeṣu upādhi guṇa sāra tvāt aṇīyaḥ tva ādi vyapadeśaḥ aṇīyā vrīheḥ vā yavāt vā maomayaḥ prāṇa mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ sarvagadhaḥ sarva rasaḥ satya kāmaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ iti evaṃprakāraḥ tadvat syāt etat yadi buddhi guṇa sāra tvāt ātmanaḥ saṃsāri tvam kalpyeta tatas buddhi ātmaoḥ saṃyoga avasāam avaśyaṃbhāvi iti atas buddhi viyoge sati ātmanaḥ a ālakṣya tvāt asattvam asaṃsāri tvam vā prasajyeta iti atas uttaram paṭhati yāvat ātma bhāvi tvāt ca doṣaḥ tad darśaāt kasmāt yāvat ātma bhāvi tvāt buddhi saṃyogasya yāvat ayam ātmā saṃsārī bhavati yāvat asya samyak darśaiḥ saṃsāri tvam asya tāvat asya buddhyā saṃyogaḥ śāmyati yāvat eva ca ayam buddhi upādhi saṃbadhaḥ tāvat eva asya jīva tvam saṃsāri tvam ca paramārthataḥ tu buddhi upādhi parikalpita svarūpa vyatirekeṇa asti a hi iti a mukta svarūpāt sarvajñāt īśvara ādayaḥ dhātuḥ dvitīyaḥ dhātuḥ dvitīyaḥ dhātuḥ dvitīyaḥ dhātuḥ dvitīyaḥ dhātuḥ dvitīyaḥ draṣṭā śrotā matā vijñātā draṣṭṛ śrotṛ matṛ vijñātṛ tattvam asi aham brahma asmi ityādi śruti śatebhyaḥ katham yāvat ātma bhāvī buddhi saṃyogaḥ iti tad darśaāt iti āha tathā hi śāstram darśayati yaḥ yam vijñā a mayaḥ prāṇeṣu hṛdi atas jyotiḥ puruṣaḥ sa samāaḥ saubhau lokau ausaṃcarati dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva ityādi tatra vijñā amayaḥ iti buddhi mayaḥ iti etat uktam bhavati pradeśa atare vijñā amayaḥ mao mayaḥ prāṇa mayaḥ cakṣuḥ mayaḥ śrotra mayaḥ iti vijñā amayasya maa ādibhiḥ saha pāṭhāt buddhi maya tvam ca tad guṇa sāra tvam eva abhipreyate yathā loke strī mayaḥ devadattaḥ iti strī rāga ādi pradhāaḥ abhidhīyate tadvat sa saubhau iti ca iti ca tayā eva buddhyā iti gamyate tat ca darśayati dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva iti etat uktam bhavati ā ayam svatas dhyāyati ā api calati dhyāyatyām buddhau dhyāyati iva calatyām buddhau calati iva iti api ca buddhi upādhi saṃbadhaḥ ca mithyājñā asya samyagjñā ādayatra i vṛttiḥ asti iti atas yāvat brahma ātmatā avabodhaḥ tāvat ayam buddhi upādhi saṃbadhaḥ śāmyati darśayati ca veda aham etam puruṣam mahātam āditya varṇam tamasaḥ parastāt tam eva viditvā ati mṛtyum eti āyaḥ pathā iti suṣupta pralayayoḥ śakyate suṣupta pralayayoḥ śakyate suṣupta pralayayoḥ śakyate satā somya tadā bhavati svam api itas bhavati iti kṛt sa vikāra pralaya abhyupagamāt ca tat katham yāvadātmabhāvitvam buddhisaṃbadhasya iti atra ucyate puṃstva ādivat tvasya sataḥ abhivyakti yogāt yathā loke bīja ātman iva yauva ādiṣu āvirbhavati a avidyamāāī utpadyate ṣaṇḍa ādīām api tad utpatti prasaṅgāt evam ayam api buddhisaṃbadhaḥ śakti ātmaā eva suṣupta pralayayoḥ puas prabodha prasavayoḥ āvirbhavati evam hi etat yujyate a hi ākasmikī kasyacid utpattiḥ saṃbhavati atiprasaṅgāt darśayati ca suṣuptāt utthāam avidyā ātmaka bīja sadbhāva kāritam sati saṃpadya viduḥ sati saṃpadyāmahe iti te iha vyāghraḥ vā siṃhaḥ vā tasmāt siddham etat yāvat ātma bhāvī iti iti upalabdhi aupalabdhi prasaṅga uyataraiyamaḥ vā ayathā tat ca ātma upādhi bhūtam ataḥkaraṇam buddhiḥ cittam iti ca tatra tatra abhilapyate kvacid ca saṃśaya ādi vṛttikam iti ucyate iścaya ādi vṛttikam buddhiḥ iti tat ca evam bhūtam ataḥkaraṇam avaśyam asti iti abhyupagatavyam ayathā hi upalabdhi aupalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ syāt ātma idriya viṣayāṇām upalabdhi sādhaāām sati ityam eva upalabdhiḥ prasajyeta atha sati api hetu samavadhāe phala abhāvaḥ prasajyeta ca evam dṛśyate athavā idriyasya vā śakti pratibadhaḥ abhyupagatavyaḥ a ca ātmaaḥ śakti pratibadhaḥ saṃbhavati avikriya tvāt āpi idriyasya a hi tasya pūrva uttarayoḥ kṣaṇayoḥ apratibaddha śaktikasya satā ukasmāt śaktiḥ pratibadhyeta tasmāt tathā ca śrutiḥ ayatramaāḥ abhūvam ādarśam ayatramaāḥ abhūvam āśrauṣam iti maasā hi eva paśyati maasā śrṛṇoti iti ca kāma ādayaḥ ca asya vṛttayaḥ iti darśayati kāmaḥ saṃkalpaḥ vicikitsā śraddhā aśraddhā dhṛtiḥ adhṛtiḥ hrīḥ dhīḥ bhīḥ iti etat sarvam me eva iti tasmāt yuktam etat tad guṇa sāra tvāt tad vyapadeśaḥ iti kartā śāstra arthavat tvāt kartṛ adhikaraṇam tad guṇa sāra tva adhikāreṇa eva aparaḥ api jīva dharmaḥ prapañcyate kartā ca ayam ayam anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anyaḥ anya jīvaḥ syāt kasmāt śāstra arthavat tvāt evam ca yajeta juhuyāt dadyāt iti evaṃvidham vidhi śāstram arthavat vihāra upadeśāt itas ca jīvasya kartṛ tvam yat jīva prakriyāyām vihāram upadiśati saḥ īyate mṛtaḥ yatra kāmam iti sve śarīre yathākāmam parivartate iti ca upādāāt itas ca asya kartṛ tvam yat jīva prakriyāyām eva karaṇāām upādāam saṃkīrtayati tat eṣām prāṇāām vijñāea vijñāam ādāya iti prāṇāḥ gṛhītvā iti ca vyapadeśāt ca kriyāyām itas ca jīvasya kartṛ tvam yat asya laukikīṣu vaidikīṣu ca kriyāsu kartṛ tvam vyapadiśati śāstram yajñam taute karmāṇi ca iti vijñāa śabdaḥ buddhau samadhigataḥ katham aea jīvasya kartṛ tvam sūcyate iti ā iti ucyate jīvasya eva eṣa buddheḥ ced jīvasya syāt syāt tathā hi buddhi vivakṣāyām vijñāa śabdasya karaṇa vibhakti nirdeśaḥ dṛśyate tat eṣām prāṇāām iti iha tu yajñam taute iti kartṛ sāma ādhikaraṇyaiḥ deśāt buddhi vyatiriktasya eva ātmaaḥ kartṛ tvam sūcyate iti adoṣaḥ atra āha yadi buddhi vyatiriktaḥ jīvaḥ kartā syāt sa svatatraḥ sa priyam hitam saṃpādayet a viparītam viparītam api tu ca svatatrasya ātmanaḥ īdṛśī pravṛttiḥ aiyamena upapadyate iti atas uttaram paṭhati upalabdhi vat aiyamaḥ yathā ayam ātma upalabdhim prati ca upalabhate evam aiyameaiveṣṭam aiṣṭam ca saṃpādayiṣyati upalabdhau api asvātatryam upalabdhi hetu upādā upalambhāt iti ced upalabdhau tu api ca arthakriyāyām api ātyatam ātmanaḥ svātatryam asti deśa kāla aimitta viśeṣa apekṣa tvāt a ca sahāya apekṣasya kartuḥ kartṛ tvam iva ṛtate bhavati hi edha udaka ādi apekṣasya api paktuḥ paktṛ tvam sahakāri vaicitryāt ca iṣṭa aiṣṭa artha kriyāyām aiyamea pravṛttiḥ ātmanaḥ virudhyate śakti viparyayāt itas ca vijñā a vyatiriktaḥ jīvaḥ kartā bhavitum arhati yadi puar vijñā a śabda vācyā buddhiḥ eva kartrī syāt tatas śakti viparyayaḥ syāt karaṇa śaktiḥ buddheḥ hīyeta kartṛ śaktiḥ ca āpadyeta satyām ca buddheḥ kartṛ śaktau tasyāḥ eva ahaṃpratyaya viṣaya tvam abhyupagatavyam ahaṃkāra pūrvikāyāḥ eva pravṛtteḥ sarvatra darśaāt aham gacchāmi aham āgacchāmi aham bhuñje aham pibāmi iti ca tasyāḥ ca kartṛ śakti yuktāyāḥ sarva artha kāri karaṇam ayat kalpayitavyam śaktā upi hi sa kartā karaṇam upādāya kriyāsu pravartamāaḥ dṛśyate tatas ca saṃjñā mātre vivādaḥ syāt a vastu bhedaḥ kaścid karaṇa vyatiriktasya kartṛ tva abhyupagamāt samādhi abhāvāt ca ayam samādhiḥ upadiṣṭaḥ ātmā vai are draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ matavyaḥ ididhyāsitavyaḥ saḥ veṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ om iti evam dhyāyatha om iti evam dhyāyatha iti evaṃlakṣaṇaḥ saḥ api asati ātmaaḥ kartṛ tve opapadyeta tasmāt api asya kartṛ tva siddhiḥ yathā ca takṣā ubhayathā takṣa adhikaraṇam evam tāvat śāstra arthavat tva ādibhiḥ hetubhiḥ kartṛ tvam śārīrasya pradarśitam tat puas svābhāvikam vā syāt upādhi nimittam vā iti cityate tatra etaiḥ eva śāstra arthavat tva ādibhiḥ hetubhiḥ svābhāvikam kartṛ tvam apavāda hetu abhāvāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ a svābhāvikam kartṛ tvam saṃbhavati aiḥ mokṣa prasaṅgāt kartṛ tva svabhāva tve hi saṃbhavati ageḥ iva auṣṇyāt ca puruṣa artha siddhiḥ kartṛ tvasya duḥkha rūpa tvāt sthitāyām api kartṛ tva śaktau kartṛ tva kārya parihārāt puruṣa arthaḥ setsyati tad parihāraḥ ca imitta parihārāt yathā ageḥ daha a śakti yuktasya api kāṣṭha viyogāt daha a kārya abhāvaḥ tadvat a imittāām api atyata parihāra asaṃbhāvāt mokṣaḥ setsyati a aitya tvāt api ca iti aśuddha mukta ātma pratipādaāt mokṣa siddhiḥ abhimatā tādṛś ca abhimantā svābhāvike tasmāt upādhi dharma adhyāse eva ātmanaḥ kartṛ tvam a svābhāvikam tathā ca śrutiḥ dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva iti bhoktā iti āhuḥ maīṣiṇaḥ iti ca upādhi saṃpṛktasya eva ātmanaḥ bhoktṛ tva ādi viśeṣa lābham darśayati hi parasmāt kartā bhoktā vā vidyate draṣṭā ityādi śravaṇāt paraḥ eva tarhi saṃsārī kartā bhoktā ca prasajyeta parasmāt ayaḥ ced citimān jīvaḥ kartā syāt a avidyā pratyupasthāpita tvāt kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tvayoḥ tathā ca śāstram yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tat itaraḥ itaram paśyati iti avidyā avasthāyām kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tve darśayitvā vidyā avasthāyām te eva kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tve iva ārayati yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kea kam paśyet iti tathā svapa jāgaritayoḥ ātma upādhi saṃparka kṛtam śramam śyeasya iva ākāśe viparipatataḥ śrāvayitvā tad abhāvam suṣuptau saṃpariṣvaktasya śrāvayati tat vai asya etat āpta kāmam ātma kāmam akāmam rūpam śokātaram iti ārabhya eṣā asya paramā gatiḥ eṣā asya paramā saṃpad eṣā usya paramaḥ lokaḥ eṣā usya parama iti upasaṃhārāt tat etat āha ācāryaḥ yathā ca takṣa ubhayathāḥ iti tu arthe ca ayam caḥ paṭhitaḥ matavyam svābhāvikam eva ātmanaḥ kartṛ tvam ageḥ iva auṣṇyam iti yathā tu takṣā loke vāsi ādi karaṇa hastaḥ kartā duḥkhī bhavati saḥ eva sva gṛham prāptaḥ vimukta vāsi ādi karaṇaḥ svasthaḥ irvṛtaḥ irvyāpāraḥ sukhī bhavati evam avidyā pratyupasthāpita dvaita saṃpṛktaḥ ātmā svapa jāgarita avasthayoḥ kartā duḥkhī bhavati saḥ svam ātmā param brahma praviśya sukhī bhavati saṃprasāda avasthāyām tathā mukti avasthāyām api avidyā dhvātam vidyā pradīpea vidhūya ātmā eva sukhī bhavati takṣa dṛṣṭātaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ takṣā hi viśiṣṭeṣu takṣaṇa ādi vyāpāreṣu apekṣya eva karaṇāi kartā bhavati sva śarīreṇa tu akartā eva evam ayam ātmā sarva vyāpāreṣu apekṣya eva karaṇāi kartā bhavati tu kartā eva iti a tu takṣṇaḥ iva avayavāḥ sati yaiḥ hasta ādibhiḥ iva takṣā ātmā upādadīta yasya id vā yat tu uktam śāstra arthavat tva ādibhiḥ hetubhiḥ svābhāvikam ātmaaḥ kartṛ tvam iti te a vidhi śāstram tāvat yathāprāptam kartṛ tvam upādāya kartavya viśeṣam upadiśati a kartṛ tvam ātmanaḥ pratipādayati a ca svābhāvikam asya kartṛ tvam asti brahma ātmatva upadeśāt iti avocāma tasmāt avidyā kṛtam kartṛ tvam upādāya vidhi śāstram pravartiṣyate kartā vijñāātmā puruṣaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakam api śāstram auvāda rūpa tvāt yathāprāptam eva avidyā kṛtam kartṛ tvam parihṛte tayoḥ api saṃdhye prasupteṣu karaṇeṣu sve śarīre yathākāmam parivartate iti vihāraḥ upadiśyamāaḥ kevalasya ātmanaḥ kartṛ tvam āvahati tathā upādāe pi tat eṣām prāṇāām ādāya iti karaṇeṣu karma karaṇa vibhaktī śrūyamāṇe kevalasya ātmanaḥ kartṛ tvam gamayataḥ iti atra ucyate a tāvat ātmanaḥ karaṇa viramaṇam asti sa dhīḥ svapaḥ bhūtvā imam lokam atikrāmati iti tatra api dhī saṃbadha śravaṇāt tathā ca smarati idriyāṇām uparame yadi sevate viṣayāḥ eva tat vidyāt svapa darśam iti kāma ādayaḥ ca vṛttayaḥ iti śrutiḥ tāḥ ca svape dṛśyate tasmāt samaāḥ eva svapte viharati vihāraḥ api ca tatratyaḥ vāsa āmayaḥ eva a tu pāramārthikaḥ asti tathā ca śrutiḥ svapa vyāpāram varṇayati uta iva strībhiḥ saha jakṣat uta iva api iti laukikāḥ api tathā eva svapam kathayati ārukṣam iva giri śrṛṅgam adrākṣam iva vaarājim iti yadi api karaṇeṣu karma karaṇa vibhakti nirdeśaḥ tathā api tad saṃpṛktasya eva ātmaaḥ kartṛ tvam draṣṭavyam kevale kartṛ tva asaṃbhavasya darśita tvāt bhavati ca loke eka prakārā vivakṣā yudhyate yodhaiḥ rājā yudhyate iti api ca asmi karaṇa vyāpāra uparama mātram vivakṣyate a svātatryam kasyacid abuddhi pūrvakasya api svāpe karaṇa vyāpāra uparam asya dṛṣṭa tvāt yasya tu ayam vyapadeśaḥ darśitaḥ vijñāam yajñam taute iti sa buddheḥ eva kartṛ tvam prāpayati vijñāa śabdasya tatra prasiddha tvāt maoataram pāṭhāt ca tasya śraddhā eva śiraḥ iti ca śraddhā ādi avayava tva saṃkīrtaāt śraddhā ādīām ca buddhi dharma tva prasiddheḥ vijñāam devāḥ sarve brahma jyeṣṭham upāsate iti ca vākya śeṣāt jyeṣṭha tvasya ca prathama ja tvasya buddhau prasiddha tvāt saḥ eṣa vācaḥ cittasya uttarottara kramaḥ yat yajñaḥ iti ca śrutyatare yajñasya vāc buddhi sādhya tva avadhāraṇāt ca buddheḥ śakti viparyayaḥ karaṇāām kartṛ tva abhyupagame bhavati sarva kārakāṇām eva sva sva vyāpāreṣu kartṛ tvasya avaśyaṃbhāvi tvāt upalabdhi apekṣam tu eṣām karaṇāām karaṇa tvam sā ca ātmanaḥ ca tasyām api asya kartṛ tvam asti iti upalabdhi svarūpa tvāt ahaṃkāra pūrvakam api kartṛ tvam opalabdhuḥ bhavitum arhati ahaṃkārasya api upalabhyamāa tvāt ca evam sati karaṇa atara kalpa a prasaṅgaḥ buddheḥ karaṇa tva abhyupagamāt samādhi abhāvaḥ tu parihṛtaḥ yathāprāptam eva kartṛ tvam upādāya samādhi vidhāāt tasmāt kartṛ tvam api ātma upādhi nimittam eva iti sthitam parāt tu tat śruteḥ yat idam avidyā avasthāyām kartṛ tvam jīvasya abhihitam tat kim a apekṣya īśvaram bhavati āhosvit īśvara apekṣam iti bhavati vicāraṇā tatra prāptam tāvat eśvaram apekṣate jīvaḥ kartṛ tve iti kasmāt apekṣā prayoja ābhāvāt ayam hi jīvaḥ svayam eva rāga dveṣa ādi doṣa prayuktaḥ tasya kim īśvaraḥ kariṣyati tasya kim īśvaraḥ kariṣyati ca loke kṛṣi ādikāsu kriyāsu aaḍuha ādi vat īśvara upara upekṣitavyaḥ iti kleśa ātmake ca kartṛ tve īśvarasya airghṛṇyam prasajyeta viṣama phalam ca eṣām kartṛ tvam vidadhataḥ vaiṣamyam vaiṣamya aairghṛṇye a sāpekṣa tvāt iti uktam satyam uktam sati tu īśvarasya sāpekṣa tva saṃbhave sāpekṣa tvam ca īśvarasya saṃbhavati dharma adharmayoḥ tayoḥ ca sadbhāvaḥ sati jīvasya kartṛ tve tat eva ced kartṛ tvam īśvara apekṣam syāt kiṃviṣayam īśvarasya sāpekṣa tvam ucyeta akṛta abhyāgamaḥ ca evam jīvasya prasajyeta tasmāt svatas eva asya kartṛ tvam iti etām prāptim tuśabdena vyāvartya pratijāīte parāt iti avidyā avasthāyām kārya karaṇa saṃghāta aviveka jīvasya avidyā timira ādhasya sataḥ parasmāt ātmanaḥ karma adhyakṣāt sarva bhūta adhivāsāt sākṣiṇaḥ cetayituḥ īśvarāt tad aujñayā kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva lakṣaṇasya saṃsārasya siddhiḥ ca mokṣa siddhiḥ bhavitum arhati kutas tad śruteḥ yadi api doṣa prayuktaḥ sāmagrī saṃpaaḥ ca jīvaḥ yadi api ca loke kṛṣi ādiṣu karmasu eśvara kāraṇa tvam prasiddham tathā api sarvāsu eva pravṛttiṣu īśvaraḥ hetu kartā iti śruteḥ avasīyate tathā hi śrutiḥ bhavati eṣa hi eva sādhu karma kārayati tam yam ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ uiīṣate eṣa hi eva asādhu karma kārayati tam yam adhas iti yaḥ ātmai yamayati iti ca evaṃjātīyakāḥ evam īśvarasya kārayitṛ tve sati vaiṣamya airghṛṇye syātām akṛta abhyāgamaḥ ca jīvasya iti ā iti ucyata kṛta prayata apekṣaḥ tu vihita pratiṣiddha a vaiyarthya ādibhyaḥ tuśabdaḥ codita doṣa vyāvarta arthaḥ kṛtaḥ yaḥ prayataḥ jīvasya dharma adharma lakṣaṇaḥ tad apekṣaḥ eva eam īśvaraḥ kārayati atas ca ete coditāḥ doṣāḥ prasajyate jīva kṛta dharma adharma vaiṣamya apekṣaḥ eva tat tat phalāi viṣamam vibhajet parjaya vat imitta tva mātreṇa yathā loke guccha gulma ādīām vrīhi yava ādīām ca asādhāraṇebhyaḥ sva sva bījebhyaḥ jāyamāāām sādhāraṇam imittam bhavati parjayaḥ hi asati parjaye rasa puṣpa phala palāśa ādi vaiṣamyam teṣām jāyate sva sva bījeṣu evam jīva kṛta prayata apekṣaḥ īśvaraḥ teṣām śubha aśubham vidadhyāt iti śliṣyate kṛta prayata apekṣa tvam eva jīvasya parāyatte kartṛ tve ā eṣa doṣaḥ parāyatte api hi kartṛ tve karoti eva jīvaḥ kurvatam hi tam īśvaraḥ kārayati api ca pūrva prayatam apekṣya idāīm kārayati pūrvataram ca prayatam apekṣya pūrvam akārayat iti a ādi tvāt saṃsārasya iti aavadyam katham kṛta prayata apekṣaḥ īśvaraḥ iti vihita pratiṣiddha a vaiyarthya ādibhyaḥ iti āha evam hi svarga kāmaḥ yajeta brāhmaṇaḥ a hatavyaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakasya vihitasya pratiṣiddhasya ca avaiyarthyam bhavati ayathā tat aarthakam syāt īśvaraḥ eva atyata paratatra tvāt jīvasya tathā vihita kāriṇam api saṃsṛjet pratiṣiddha kāriṇam api tatas ca prāmāṇyam vedasya astam iyāt īśvarasya ca atyatā aapekṣa tve laukikasya api puruṣakārasya vaiyarthyam tathā deśa kālaimittāām pūrva ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ ca iti evaṃjātīyakam doṣa jātam ādi grahaṇena darśayati aṃśaḥ ca api dāśakitavādi tvam adhīyate eke ca api dāśakitavādi tvam adhīyate eke jīva īśvarayoḥ upakārya upakāraka bhāvaḥ uktaḥ sa ca saṃbaddhayoḥ eva loke dṛṣṭaḥ yathā svāmi bhṛtyayoḥ yathā vā agi visphuliṅgayoḥ tatas ca jīva īśvarayoḥ api upakārya upakāraka bhāva abhyupagamāt kim āhosvit agi visphuliṅga vat iti asyām vicikitsāyām aiyamaḥ vā athavā svāmi bhṛtya prakāreṣu eva īśitṛ īśitavya bhāvasya prasiddha tvāt tadvidhaḥ eva iti atas bravīti aṃśaḥ iti jīvaḥ īśvarasya aṃśaḥ bhavitum arhati yathā āgeḥ visphuliṅgaḥ aṃśaḥ iva aṃśaḥ hi hi iḥ avayavasya mukhyaḥ oṃśaḥ saṃbhavati kasmāt puaḥ iḥ avayava tvāt saḥ eva a bhavati ā ā vyapadeśāt saḥ u vā iṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ etam eva viditvā muiḥ bhavati yaḥ ātmai tiṣṭha ātmā amataraḥ yamayati iti ca evaṃjātīyakaḥ bhedaiḥ deśaḥ āsati bhede yujyate ca ayam sutarām svāmi bhṛtya sārūpye yujyate iti atas āha ayathā ca api iti ca ca kevalāt aṃśa tva pratipattiḥ kim tarhi ayathā ca api vyapadeśaḥ pratipādakaḥ tathā hi eke dāśa kitava ādi bhāvam brahmaṇaḥ āmaatya ātharvaṇikāḥ brahmasūkte brahma dāśāḥ brahma dāsāḥ brahma eva ime kitavāḥ dāśāḥ ye ete kaivartāḥ prasiddhāḥ ye ca amīdāsāḥ ye ca aye kitavāḥ dyūta kṛtaḥ te sarve brahmā eva iti sarveṣām eva āma rūpa kṛta kārya karaṇa saṃghāta praviṣṭāām jīvāām brahmatvam āha tathā brahma prakriyāyām eva ayam arthaḥ prapañcyate tvam strī tvam pumān asi tvam kumāraḥ uta vā kumārī tvam jīrṇaḥ tvam jātaḥ bhavati viśvatomukhaḥ iti sarvāṇi rūpāṇi vicitya iti ca iti āyotaḥ asti draṣṭā ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ca asya arthasya siddhiḥ caitayam ca aviśiṣṭam jīva īśvarayoḥ yathā agi visphuliṅgayoḥ auṣṇyam atas bheda abheda avagamābhyām aṃśa tva avagamaḥ kutas ca aṃśa tva avagamaḥ matravarṇāt ca matravarṇaḥ ca etam artham avagamayati tāvā asya mahimā tatas jyāyāḥ ca puruṣaḥ pādaḥ usya sarvā tri pādasya amṛtam divi iti atra bhūta śabde sthāvara jaṅgamāi irdiśati tīrthebhyaḥ iti prayogāt aṃśaḥ pādaḥ bhāgaḥ iti aarthātaram tasmāt api aṃśa tva avagamaḥ kutas ca aṃśa tva avagamaḥ api ca smaryate īśvaragītāsu api ca īśvara aṃśa tvam jīvasya smaryate mama eva aṃśaḥ jīva loke jīva bhūtaḥ iti tasmāt api aṃśa tva avagamaḥ yat tu uktam svāmi bhṛtya ādiṣu eva īśitṛ īśitavya bhāvaḥ loke prasiddhaḥ iti yadi api eṣā loke prasiddhiḥ tathā api śāstrāt tu atra aṃśa aṃśi tvam īśitṛ īśitavya bhāvaḥ ca iścīyate praśāsti iti a kiṃcid vipratiṣidhyate atra āha jīvasya īśvara aṃśa tva abhyupagame duḥkhi tvam syāt yathā loke devadattasya duḥkhi tvam tadvat tatas ca tad prāptāām mahattaram duḥkham prāpuyāt atas varam pūrva avasthaḥ saṃsāraḥ eva astu iti samyak darśa āarthakya prasaṅgaḥ syāt iti atra ucyate prakāśāt iva paraḥ yathā jīvaḥ saṃsāra duḥkham ubhavati paraḥ īśvaraḥ ubhavati iti pratijāīmahe jīvaḥ hi avidyā veśa vaśāt deha ādi ātma bhāvam iva gatvā duḥkhī aham iti avidyayā kṛtam duḥkha upabhogam parameśvarasya deha ādi ātma bhāvaḥ duḥkha abhimāaḥ vā asti jīvasya api eva duḥkha abhimāaḥ tu pāramārthikaḥ sti yathā ca sva deha gata dāha cheda ādi nimittam duḥkham tad abhimā abhrātyā ubhavati tathā putra mitra ādi gocaram api duḥkham aham eva putraḥ aham eva mitram iti evam putra mitra ādiṣu tatas ca etat avagamyate mithyā abhimā bhrama maimittaḥ eva duḥkha āubhavaḥ iti vyatireka darśaāt ca evam avagamyate tathā hi putra mitra ādimatsu bahuṣu upaviṣṭeṣu itareṣu ca putraḥ mṛtaḥ mitram mṛtam iti evam āghoṣite yeṣām eva putra mitra ādimattva abhimāaḥ teṣām eva taimittam duḥkham utpadyate parivrājaka ādīām atas ca laukikasya api puṃsaḥ samyak daśā arthavat tvam dṛṣṭam kim uta tasmāt asti samyak darśa āarthakya prasaṅgaḥ prakāśa ādi vat iti prakāśaḥ sauraḥ ca ādramasaḥ vā viyat vyāpya avatiṣṭhamāaḥ teṣu ṛju vakra ādi bhāvam pratipadyamāeṣu a paramārthataḥ tad bhāvam pratipadyate yathā ca ākāśaḥ ghaṭa ādiṣu gacchatsu gaccha eva vibhāvyamānaḥ api a paramārthataḥ tad bhāvam pratipadyate yathā ca ākāśaḥ ghaṭa ādiṣu gacchatsu gaccha eva vibhāvyamānaḥ api a paramārthataḥ tad bhāvam pratipadyate yathā ca ākāśaḥ ghaṭa ādiṣu gacchatsu gaccha eva a paramārthataḥ gacchati yathā ca uda śarāva ādi kampaāt tad gate sūrya pratibimbe tad gate sūrya pratibimbe evam avidyā pratyupasthāpite buddhi ādi upahite jīva ākhye aṃśe tad vā īśvaraḥ duḥkhāyate jīvasya api duḥkha prāptiḥ avidyā nimittā eva iti uktam tathā ca brahma bhāva vyudāsea brahma bhāvam eva jīvasya pratipādayati tattvam asi iti evamādayaḥ tasmāā asti duḥkhea paramātmanaḥ duḥkhi tva prasaṅgaḥ smarati ca smarati ca vyāsa ādayaḥ yathā jaivea paramātmā duḥkhāyate iti tatra yaḥ paramātmā hi saḥ irguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ a lipyate phalaiḥ ca api padma patram iva ambhasā karma ātmā tu aparaḥ yaḥ asau sa yujyate sa saptadaśakena api yujyate iti caśabdāt ca iti vākyaśeṣaḥ tayoḥ ayaḥ pippalam abhicākaśīti iti ekaḥ tathā sarva bhūta atarātmā a lipyate loka duḥkhea bāhyaḥ iti ca atra āha yadi tarhi ekaḥ eva sarveṣām syāt katham aujñā parihārau syātām laukikau vaidikau ca iti ca aṃśaḥ jīvaḥ īśvarasya iti uktam tad bhedāt ca aujñā parihārau tad āśrayau avyatikīrṇau upapadyete kim atra codyate iti ucyate aitadevam a aṃśa tvam api hi jīvasya abheda vādiyaḥ śrutayaḥ pratipādayati tat sṛṣṭvā tat eva auprāviśat draṣṭā mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpoti yaḥ iha ā eva paśyati tattvam asi aham brahma asmi iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ bheda abheda avagamābhyām aṃśa tvam sidhyati iti uktam syāt etat evam yadi ubhau api bheda abhedau pratipipādayiṣitau syātām abhedaḥ eva tu atra brahma ātmatva pratipattau puruṣa artha siddheḥ svabhāva prāptaḥ tu bhedaḥ uūdyate brahmaṇaḥ mukhyaḥ oṃśaḥ jīvaḥ saṃbhavati iti uktam tasmāt paraḥ eva ekaḥ sarveṣām bhūtāām atarātmā jīva bhāvena avasthitaḥ iti atas vaktavyā aujñāparihāra upapattiḥ tām brūmaḥ aujñāparihārau ṛtau bhāryām upeyāt iti aujñā opagacchet iti parihāraḥ tathā agīṣomīyam paśum saṃjñapayet iti aujñā agnīṣomīyam paśum saṃjñapayet iti aujñā agnīṣomīyam paśum saṃjñapayet iti aujñā agnīṣomīyam paśum saṃjñapayet iti aujñā agnīṣomīyam paśum saṃjñapayet iti aujñā agnīṣomīyam paśum saṃjñapayet iti aujñā agnīṣomīyam paśum saṃjñapayet iti aujñā agnīṣom hiṃsyāt sarvāḥ iti parihāraḥ evam loke pi mitram upasevitavyam iti aujñā śatruḥ parihartavyaḥ iti parihāraḥ evaṃprakārau aujñā parihārau ekatve pi ātmanaḥ syāt dehaiḥ saṃbadhaḥ deha saṃbadhaḥ kaḥ puar deha saṃbadhaḥ deha ādiḥ ayam saṃghātaḥ ham eva iti viparīta pratyaya utpattiḥ dṛṣṭā ca sā sarva aham gacchāmi aham āgacchāmi aham adhas aham aadhas aham mūḍhaḥ aham amūḍhaḥ iti evam ātmikā hi asyāḥ samyak darśaāt asti prāk tu pratatā eṣā bhrātiḥ sarva jatuṣu tat evam avidyā nimitta deha ādi upādhi saṃbadha kṛtāt viśeṣāt aikātmya abhyupagame pi aujñāparihārau avakalpete samyagdarśiṇaḥ tarhi aujñāparihāra āarthakyam prāptam a tasya kṛtārtha tvāt iyojya tva aupapatteḥ heya upādeyayoḥ hi iyojyaḥ syāt ātmā tu atiriktam heyam upādeyam vā vastu apaśya katham ca ātmā eva syāt śarīra vyatireka darśiḥ eva iyojya tvam iti ced a tad saṃhata tva abhimāāt satyam tathā api vyoma ādi vat deha ādi asaṃhata tvam a paśyataḥ eva hi deha ādi asaṃhata tva darśiḥ kasyacid api iyogaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kim uta aikātmya darśiḥ a ca iyoga abhāvāt samyak darśiḥ yatheṣṭa ceṣṭā prasaṅgaḥ sarvatra abhimāasya eva pravartaka tvāt abhimāa bhāvāt ca samyak darśiḥ jyotiḥ ādi vat yathā jyotiṣaḥ ekatve pi agiḥ kravyād parihriyate etaraḥ yathā ca prakāśaḥ ekasya api savituḥ amedhya deśa saṃbaddhaḥ parihriyate etaraḥ śuci bhūmiṣṭhaḥ tathā bhaumāḥ pradeśāḥ vajra vaiḍūrya ādayaḥ upādīyate bhaumāḥ api sataḥ ara kalebara ādayaḥ parihriyate tathā mūtra purīṣam gavām pavitra tayā parigṛhyate tat eva jātyatare parivarjyate tadvat asatateḥ ca avyatikaraḥ syātām deha viśeṣa yogāt yaḥ tu ayam sa ca aikātmya abhyupagame vyatikīryeta svāmi eka tvāt iti ced a saṃtateḥ a hi kartuḥ bhoktuḥ ca ātmaḥ saṃtataḥ sarvaiḥ śarīraiḥ hi jīvaḥ iti uktam upādhi asaṃtāāt ca tatas ca karma vyatikaraḥ phala vyatikaraḥ vā bhaviṣyati ābhāsaḥ eva ca ābhāsaḥ eva ca eṣa jīvaḥ parasya ātma o jala sūryaka ādi vat pratipattavyaḥ saḥ eva sākṣāt vastvataram atas ca yathā aikasmin jalasūryake jalasūryakātaram kampate evam aikasmin jīve karma phala jīvātarasya tad saṃbadhaḥ evam avyatikaraḥ eva karma phalayoḥ ābhāsasya ca avidyā kṛta tvāt tad āśrayasya saṃsārasya avidyā kṛta tva upapattiḥ iti ca pāramārthikasya brahma ātma bhāvasya upadeśa upapattiḥ yeṣām tu bahavaḥ ātmāaḥ te ca sarve sarva gatāḥ teṣām eva eṣa vyatikaraḥ katham bahavaḥ vibhavaḥ ca ātmā aḥ caitaya mātra svarūpāḥ iḥ guṇāḥ iḥ atiśayāḥ ca tad artham sādhāraṇam bhoga apavarga siddhiḥ iti sāṃkhyāḥ sati bahu tve vibhu tve ca ghaṭa kuḍya ādi samāḥ dravya mātra svarūpāḥ svatas acetaāḥ ātmā tad upakaraṇāi ca maāṃsi tatra ātma dravyāṇām ca saṃyogāt icchā ādayaḥ vaiśeṣikāḥ ātma guṇāḥ utpadyate te ca a vyatirekeṇa pratyekam ātmasu samavayati sa saṃsāraḥ teṣām mokṣaḥ iti kāṇādāḥ tatra tāvat caitaya svarūpa tvāt sarva ātmanām saṃidhā ādya viśeṣāt ca ekasya sukha duḥkha saṃbadhe sarveṣām sukha duḥkha saṃbadhaḥ syāt etat pradhā apravṛtteḥ puruṣa kaivalya artha tvāt vyavasthā bhaviṣyati ayathā hi sva vibhūti khyāpa arthā pradhā apravṛttiḥ syāt tathā ca aiḥ mokṣaḥ prasajyeta iti hi vyavasthā śakyā vijñātum upapattyā tu kayācid vyavasthā ucyeta asatyām tu vyavasthā hetu abhāvāt vyatikaraḥ kāṇādāām api yadā saṃyujyate tadā ātma ataraiḥ api ātarīyakaḥ saṃyogaḥ syāt tatas ca hetu aviśeṣāt phala aviśeṣaḥ iti ekasya ātmaaḥ sukha duḥkha yoge sarva ātmaām api sukha duḥkhi tvam prasajyeta syāt etat adṛṣṭa aimittaḥ iyamaḥ bhaviṣyati iti etya āha adṛṣṭa aiyamāt bahuṣu ātmasu ākāśa vat sarva gateṣu pratiśarīram bāhya abhyatara aviśeṣeṇa saṃihiteṣu dharma adharma lakṣaṇam adṛṣṭam upārjyate sāṃkhyāām tāvat tat a ātma samavāyi pradhā avarti pradhā a sādhāraṇyā a pratyātmam sukha duḥkha upabhogasya upapadyate kāṇādāām api pūrvavat hetu abhāvāt eṣaḥ eva doṣaḥ syāt etat aham idam phalam idam phalam idam pariharāṇi ittham prayatai ittham karavāṇi iti evaṃvidhāḥ abhisaṃdhyā ādayaḥ pratyātmam pravartamāāḥ adṛṣṭasya ātmanām ca sva svāmi bhāvam ca sva svāmi bhāvam iyaṃsyati iti etya āha abhisadhyā ādiṣu api ca evam sarva ātma saṃidhau kriyamāṇāām iyam ahetu tva aupapatteḥ ukta doṣa auṣaṅgaḥ eva pradeśāt iti ce ātarbhāvāt atha ucyeta vibhu tve pi saṃyogaḥ eva ātma pradeśe bhaviṣyati atas pradeśa kṛtā vyavasthā abhisaṃdhyā ādīām adṛṣṭasya sukha duḥkhayoḥ ca bhaviṣyati iti tat api opapadyate kasmāt atarbhāvāt vibhu tva aviśeṣāt dhi sarvaḥ eva ātmā sarva śarīreṣu tatra a vaiśeṣikaiḥ pi ātmaaḥ pradeśaḥ kalpayitum śakyaḥ pi ayam pradeśaḥ eva a pāramārthikam kāryam śarīram api sarva ātma saṃidhau asya eva ātmaaḥ etareṣām iti a iyatum śakyam pradeśa viśeṣa abhyupagame ca dvayoḥ ātmaoḥ ca dvayoḥ ātmaoḥ kadācid syāt samāa pradeśasya api dvayoḥ ātmaoḥ adṛṣṭasya saṃbhavāt tathā hi devadattaḥ yasmin pradeśe sukha duḥkham tasmāt pradeśāt apakrāte tad śarīre yajñadatta śarīre ca tam pradeśam tasya api itareṇa sukha duḥkha aubhavaḥ dṛśyate sa a syāt yadi devadatta yajñadattayoḥ a syāt svarga ādi aupabhoga prasaṅgaḥ ca pradeśa vādiḥ syāt brāhmaṇa ādi śarīra pradeśeṣu adṛṣṭa aiṣpatteḥ pradeśa atara varti tvāt ca svarga ādi upabhogasya sarvagata tva aupapattiḥ ca vada tāvat tvam ke bahavaḥ samāadeśāḥ ca iti rūpa ādayaḥ iti ced a teṣām api dharmi aṃśeā bhedāt lakṣaṇa bhedāt ca a tu ati aviśeṣa vaśāt bheda upapattiḥ iti ced a bheda ca itaretara āśraya tvāt ākāśa ādīām api vibhu tvam brahma vādinoḥ siddham kāryatva abhyupagamāt tasmāt ātma ekatva pakṣe eva sarva doṣa abhāvaḥ iti siddham iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye dvitīya adhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ murat dvitīyaḥ udhyāyaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ tathā prāṇāḥ prāṇa utpatti adhikaraṇam tathā prāṇāḥ iti katham tathā iti akṣara āulomyam prakṛta upamā ābhāvāt sarvagata ātma bahutva vādi dūṣaṇam prakṛtam saṃbhavati sādṛśya abhāvāt sādṛśye hi sati upamā am syāt yathā siṃhaḥ tathā balavarmā iti adṛṣṭa sāmya pratipāda artham iti yadi ucyeta yathā adṛṣṭasya sarva ātma saṃidhau utpadyamāasya aiyata tvam evam prāṇāām api sarva ātmanaḥ pratyaiyata tvam iti tat api bhavet ca prāṇāḥ upamīyera siddhāta virodhāt jīvasya hi autpattiḥ ākhyātā prāṇāām tu utpattiḥ ācikhyāsitā tasmāt tathā iti asaṃbaddham iva pratibhāti atra prāṇa utpatti vādi vākya jātam udāharaṇam etasmāt ātmanaḥ sarve prāṇāḥ sarve lokāḥ sarve devāḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāi vyuccarati iti evaṃjātīyakam tatra yathā loka ādayaḥ parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ utpadyate tathā prāṇāḥ api iti arthaḥ tathā etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ maaḥ sarva idriyāṇi ca kham vāyuḥ jyotiḥ āpaḥ pṛthivī viśvasya dhāriṇī iti evamādiṣu api kha ādi vat prāṇāām utpattiḥ iti draṣṭavyam athavā tadvat iti evamādiṣu yathā viyat ādayaḥ parasya brahmaṇaḥ vikārāḥ samadhigatāḥ tathā prāṇāḥ api parasya brahmaṇaḥ vikārāḥ iti yojayitavyam kaḥ puar prāṇāām vikāra tve hetuḥ śruta tvam eva keṣucid pradeśeṣu a prāṇāām utpattiḥ śrūyate iti uktam tat ayuktam pradeśa atareṣu śravaṇāt a hi kvacid aśravaṇam ayatra śrutam iva ārayitum utsahate tasmāt śruta tva aviśeṣāt ākāśa ādi vat prāṇāḥ api utpadyate iti sūktam gauṇī asambhavāt yat puaruktam prāk utpatteḥ sadbhāva śravaṇāt gauṇī prāṇa āām utpatti śrutiḥ iti tat pratyāha gauṇī asaṃbhavāt iti gauṇyāḥ asaṃbhavaḥ gauṇī asaṃbhavaḥ hi prāṇa āām utpatti śrutiḥ gauṇī saṃbhavati hi prāṇa āām utpatti śrutiḥ gauṇī saṃbhavati hi bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati iti hi sarva vijñāam pratijñāya etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ ityādi sā ca pratijñā prāṇa ādeḥ samastasya jagataḥ brahma vikāra tve sati prakṛti vyatirekeṇa vikāra abhāvāt sidhyati gauṇyām tu prāṇāām utpatti śrutau pratijñā iyam hīyeta tathā ca pratijñāta artham upasaṃharati puruṣaḥ eva idam viśvam karma tapaḥ brahma para amṛtam iti brahma eva idam viśvam idam variṣṭham iti ca tathā vai are darśayā śravaṇea matyā vijñāea idam sarvam viditam iti evaṃjātīyakāsu śrutiṣu eṣā eva pratijñā yojayitavyā katham puas prāk utpatteḥ prāṇāām sadbhāva śravaṇam aita mūlaprakṛti viṣayam aprāṇaḥ hi amaāḥ śubhraḥ hi akṣarāt paratas paraḥ iti mūlaprakṛteḥ prāṇa ādi samasta viśeṣa rahita tva avadhāraṇāt avātara prakṛti viṣayam tu etat sva vikāra apekṣam prāk utpatteḥ prāṇāām sadbhāva avadhāraṇam iti draṣṭavyam vyākṛta viṣayāṇām api bhūyasīām avasthāām śruti smṛtyoḥ prakṛti vikāra bhāva prasiddheḥ viyat adhikaraṇe hi gauṇī asaṃbhavāt iti pūrvapakṣa sūtra tvāt gauṇī jama śrutiḥ asaṃbhavāt iti vyākhyātam pratijñā hāyā ca tatra siddhātaḥ abhihitaḥ iha tu siddhāta sūtra tvāt gauṇyāḥ jama śruteḥ asaṃbhavāt iti vyākhyātam tu iha api gauṇī jama śrutiḥ asaṃbhavāt iti vyācakṣāṇaiḥ syāt tad prāk śruteḥ ca itas ca ākāśa ādīām iva prāṇāām api mukhyā eva jama śrutiḥ yat jāyate iti ekam jama vāci padam prāṇeṣu prāk śrutam sat uttareṣu ākāśa ādiṣu auvartate etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ iti atra ākāśa ādiṣu mukhyam jama iti pratiṣṭhāpitam tad sāma āyāt prāṇeṣu api mukhyam eva jama bhavitum arhati a hi ekasmin prakaraṇe ekasmin ca vākye ekaḥ śabdaḥ sakṛt uccaritaḥ bahubhiḥ kvacid mukhyaḥ kvacid gauṇaḥ iti adhyavasātum śakyam vairūpya prasaṅgāt tathā sa prāṇam asṛjata prāṇāt śraddhām iti atra api prāṇeṣu śrutaḥ sṛjatiḥ pareṣu api utpattimatsu śraddhā ādiṣu auṣajyate yatra api paścāt śrutaḥ utpatti vacaḥ śabdaḥ pūrvaiḥ saṃbadhyate tatra api eṣaḥ eva yāyaḥ yathā sarvāṇi vyuccarati iti ayam ate paṭhitaḥ vyuccarati śabdaḥ pūrvaiḥ api prāṇa ādibhiḥ saṃbadhyate tad pūrvaka tvāt vācaḥ yadi api tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti etasmin prakaraṇe prāṇāām utpattiḥ paṭhyate tejaḥ baāām eva trayāṇām bhūtāām utpatti śravaṇāt tathā api tad sāmāyāt ca sarveṣām eva prāṇāām brahma prabhava tvam siddham bhavati tathā hi asmin eva prakaraṇe tejaḥ baa pūrvaka tvam aa mayam hi somya āpaḥ mayaḥ prāṇaḥ tejaḥ mayī vāc iti tatra yadi tau amukhyam eva eṣām a ādi maya tvam tatas vartate eva brahma prabhava tvam atha bhāktam tathā api brahma kartṛkāyām āma rūpa vyākriyāyām śravaṇāt yeāśrutam śrutam bhavati iti ca upakramāt aitadātmyam idam sarvam iti ca upasaṃhārāt śruti atara prasiddheḥ ca brahma kārya tva prapañca prāṇāḥ prabhavati tasmāt iti kvacid aṣṭau prāṇāḥ guṇe saṃkīrtyate aṣṭau grahāḥ aṣṭau atigrahāḥ iti kvacid sapta vai śīrṣaṇyāḥ prāṇāḥ dvau avāñcau iti kvacid daśa ava vai puruṣe prāṇāḥ ābhiḥ daśamī iti kvacid ekādaśa daśa ime puruṣe prāṇāḥ ātmā ekādaśaḥ iti kvacid dvādaśa sarveṣām iti atra kvacid trayodaśa cakṣuḥ ca draṣṭavyam ca iti atra evam hi prāṇa iyattām prati śrutayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam sapta eva prāṇāḥ iti kutas gateḥ yatas tāvatā uvagamyate sapta prāṇāḥ prabhavati tasmāt iti evaṃvidhāsu śrutiṣu viśeṣitāḥ ca ete sapta vai śīrṣaṇyāḥ prāṇāḥ iti atra prāṇāḥ guhā āśayāḥ ihitāḥ sapta sapta iti iti uttara saṃkhyā aurodhāt tu ekādaśā eva te prāṇāḥ syuḥ tathā ca udāhṛtā śrutiḥ daśa ime puruṣe prāṇāḥ ātmā ekādaśaḥ iti ca atra ataḥkaraṇam parigṛhyate karaṇa adhikārāt au ekādaśa tvāt api adhike chidra bheda abhiprāyeṇa eva daśa prāṇāḥ ucyate a prāṇa tattva bheda abhiprāyeṇa ābhiḥ daśamī iti vacaāt hi kaścit prāṇaḥ prasiddhaḥ asti mukhyasya tu prāṇasya bhavati ābhiḥ api ekam atas ābhiḥ daśamī katham doṣaḥ tattva abhedāt vṛtti bhede pi sapta tva upapatteḥ tasmāt sapta eva prāṇāḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ hasta ādayaḥ tu apare saptabhyā utiriktāḥ prāṇāḥ pratīyate hastaḥ vai grahaḥ ityādi śrutiṣu graha tvam ca gṛhyate badhyate kṣetrajñaḥ graha saṃjñakea iti sa ca kṣetrajñaḥ ā ekasmin eva śarīre badhyate śarīra atareṣu api tulya tvāt badhaasya tasmāt śarīra atara saṃcāri idam graha adhikaraṇam prāṇāām eva aṇavaḥ ca ete prakṛtāḥ prāṇāḥ pratipattavyāḥ aṇu tvam ca eṣām saukṣmya paricchedau a paramāṇu tulya tvam sūkṣmāḥ ete prāṇāḥ sthūlāḥ ced syuḥ maraṇa kāle bilāt ahiḥ iva upalabhyera mriyamāṇasya pārśva sthaiḥ paricchiāḥ ca ete prāṇāḥ sarva gatāḥ ced syuḥ utkrāti gati āgati śruti vyākopaḥ syāt tad guṇa sāra tvam ca jīvasya sidhyet sarvagatāām api vṛtti lābhaḥ śarīra deśe syāt iti ced a vṛtti mātrasya karaṇa tva upapatteḥ yat eva hi upalabdhi sādhaam vṛttiḥ tasya eva karaṇa tvam saṃjñā mātre vivādaḥ iti tasmāt sūkṣmāḥ prāṇāḥ iti adhyavasyāmaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ ca prāṇa śraiṣṭhya adhikaraṇam mukhyaḥ ca prāṇa itara prāṇa vat brahma vikāraḥ iti atidiśati tat ca aviśeṣeṇa eva sarva prāṇāām brahma vikāra tvam ākhyātam etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ maaḥ sarva idriyāṇi ca iti sa idriya maaḥ vyatirekeṇa prāṇasya utpatti śravaṇāt sa prāṇam asṛjata ityādi śravaṇebhyaḥ ca kimarthaḥ adhika āśaṅkā vāraṇa arthaḥ āsadāsīye hi brahma pradhāe sūkte matra varṇaḥ bhavati a mṛtyuḥ āsīt amṛtam a tarhi a rātryā aha āsīt praketaḥ āīt avātam svadhayā tat ekam kiṃca āsa iti iti prāṇa karma upādāāt prāk utpatteḥ satam iva prāṇam sūcayati tasmāt ajaḥ prāṇaḥ iti jāyate kasyacid matiḥ tām atideśe apaudati āīt śabdaḥ api a prāk utpatteḥ prāṇa sadbhāvam sūcayati avātam iti viśeṣaṇāt aprāṇaḥ hi amaāḥ śubhraḥ iti ca mūlaprakṛteḥ prāṇa ādi samasta viśeṣa rahita tvasya darśita tvāt tasmāt kāraṇa sadbhāva pradarśa arthaḥ eva ayam āīt śabdaḥ iti śreṣṭhaḥ iti ca mukhyam prāṇam abhidadhāti prāṇaḥ vāva jyeṣṭhaḥ ca śreṣṭhaḥ ca iti śruti nirdeśāt jyeṣṭhaḥ ca prāṇaḥ śukra aiṣeka kālāt ārabhya tasya vṛtti lābhāt ced tasya tadāīm vṛtti lābhaḥ syāt saṃbhavet vā śrotra ādīām tu jyeṣṭha tvam śreṣṭhaḥ ca prāṇaḥ guṇa ādhikyāt a vai śakṣyāmaḥ tvat ṛte jīvitum iti śruteḥ a vāyu kriye pṛthak upadeśāt vāyu kriyā adhikaraṇam sa puarmukhyaḥ prāṇaḥ kiṃsvarūpaḥ iti idāīm jijñāsyate tatra prāptam tāvat śruteḥ vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ iti evam hi śrūyate yaḥ prāṇaḥ sa vāyuḥ saḥ eṣa vāyuḥ pañcavidhaḥ prāṇa upāaḥ vyāaḥ udāaḥ samāaḥ iti athavā tatra ātarīya abhiprāyāt samasta karaṇa vṛttiḥ prāṇaḥ iti prāptam evam hi tatra ātarīyāḥ ācakṣate sāmāyā karaṇa vṛttiḥ prāṇa ādyāḥ vāyavaḥ pañca iti atra ucyate a vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ karaṇa vyāpāraḥ kutas pṛthak upadeśāt vāyoḥ tāvat prāṇasya pṛthak upadeśaḥ bhavati prāṇaḥ eva brahmaṇaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ sa jyotiṣā bhāti ca tapati ca iti a hi vāyuḥ eva sa vāyoḥ pṛthak upadiśyeta tathā karaṇa vṛtteḥ api pṛthak upadeśaḥ bhavati tatra tatra vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ abhedāt hi karaṇa vyāpāraḥ eva sa karaṇebhyaḥ pṛthak upadiśyeta tathā etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ sarva idriyāṇi ca kham vāyuḥ iti evamādayaḥ api vāyoḥ karaṇebhyaḥ ca prāṇasya ca samastāām karaṇāām ekā vṛttiḥ saṃbhavati pratyekam eka eka vṛtti tvāt samudāyasya ca akāraka tvāt etat bhaviṣyati yathā eka pañjara varti anuprāṇi ekādaśa pakṣiṇaḥ pratyekam pratiiyata vyāpārāḥ sataḥ saṃbhūya ekam pañjaram cālayati evam eka śarīravartin ekādaśa prāṇāḥ pratyekam pratiiyata vṛttayaḥ sataḥ saṃbhūya ekām prāṇa ākhyām vṛttim pratilapsyate iti ā iti ucyate yuktam tatra pratyeka vṛttibhiḥ avātara vyāpāraiḥ pañjara cāla āurūpaiḥ eva upetāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ saṃbhūya ekam pañjaram cālayeyuḥ iti tathā dṛṣṭa tvāt iha tu śravaṇa ādi avātara vyāpāra upetāḥ prāṇāḥ a saṃbhūya prāṇyuḥ iti yuktam pramāṇa abhāvāt atyata vijātīya tvāt ca śravaṇa ādibhyaḥ tathā prāṇasya śreṣṭha tvāt yuddha ūṣaṇam guṇa bhāva upagamaḥ ca tam prati vāc ādīām a karaṇa vṛtti mātre prāṇa iva kalpate tasmāt ayaḥ vāyu kriyābhyām prāṇaḥ katham tarhi iyam śrutiḥ yaḥ prāṇaḥ sa vāyuḥ iti ucyate vāyuḥ eva ayam pañca vyūhaḥ prāṇaḥ bhaṇyate bheda abheda śrutī atas ca ubhe api bheda abheda śrutī virudhyete syāt etat prāṇaḥ api tarhi jīva vat asmi śarīre svātatryam śreṣṭha tvāt guṇa bhāva upagamāt ca tam prati tathā hi a ekavidhā vibhūtiḥ prāṇasya śrāvyate supteṣu vāc ādiṣu prāṇaḥ eva ekaḥ jāgarti prāṇaḥ eva ekaḥ mṛtyoḥ prāṇaḥ saṃvargaḥ vāc ādī saṃvṛṅkte prāṇaḥ mātā iva putrāḥ iti tasmāt prāṇasya api jīva vat svātatrya prasaṅgaḥ tam pariharati cakṣuḥ ādi vat tu tad saha śiṣṭi ādibhyaḥ tuśabdaḥ prāṇasya jīva vat svātatryam vyāvartayati yathā rāja prakṛti vat jīvasya kartṛ tvam bhoktṛ tvam ca prati upakaraṇāi svatatrāṇi tathā mukhyaḥ api prāṇaḥ rāja matri vat jīvasya upakaraṇa bhūtaḥ a svatatraḥ kutas tad saha śiṣṭi ādibhyaḥ taiḥ cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ saha eva prāṇaḥ śiṣyate prāṇa saṃvāda ādiṣu ca saha yuktam bṛhat rathaṃtara ādi vat ādi śabde saṃhata tva acetaa tva ādī prāṇasya svātatryaiḥ ākaraṇa hetū darśayati syāt etat yadi cakṣuḥ ādi vat prāṇasya jīvam prati karaṇa bhāvaḥ abhyupagamyeta viṣaya ātaram rūpa ādi vat prasajyeta rūpa āloca ādibhiḥ vṛttibhiḥ yathāsvam jīvam prati karaṇa bhāvaḥ bhavati api ca ekādaśa eva kārya jātāi parigaṇitāi yad artham ekādaśa prāṇāḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ tu dvādaśam aparam kārya jātam avagamyate yad artham ayam dvādaśaḥ prāṇaḥ pratijñāyate iti atas uttaram paṭhati akaraṇa tvāt ca a doṣaḥ tathā hi darśayati a tāvat viṣaya atara prasaṅgaḥ doṣaḥ akaraṇa tvāt prāṇasya a hi cakṣuḥ ādi vat prāṇasya viṣaya paricchede karaṇa tvam abhyupagamyate a ca asya etāvatā kārya abhāvaḥ eva kasmāt tathā hi śrutiḥ mukhya prāṇasya vaiśeṣikam kāryam darśayati prāṇa saṃvāda ādiṣu atha ha prāṇāḥ aham śreyasi vyūdire iti upakramya yasmin iva utkrāte śarīram pāpiṣṭhataram iva dṛśyeta sa vaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ iti ca upayasya pratyekam tad vṛtti mātra hīam yathāpūrvam darśayitvā prāṇa uccikramiṣāyām vāc ādi śaithilya āpattim śarīra pāta prasaṅgam ca darśayatī śrutiḥ prāṇa aimittām śarīra idriya sthitim darśayati tau ariṣṭhaḥ prāṇaḥ uvāca mā moham āpat yathā aham eva etat pañcadhā ātmā am pravibhajya etat bāṇam avaṣṭabhya vidhārayāmi iti ca etam eva artham śrutiḥ āha prāṇa iau kulāyam iti ca supteṣu cakṣuḥ ādiṣu prāṇa aimittām śarīra rakṣām darśayati yasmāt kasmāt ca aṅgāt prāṇaḥ utkrāmati tat eva tat śuṣyati iti yat aśāti yat pibati iti ca prāṇa aimittām śarīra idriya puṣṭim darśayati kasmin aham utkrātaḥ utkrātaḥ bhaviṣyāmi kasmin vā pratiṣṭhite pratiṣṭhāsyāmi iti sa prāṇam asṛjata iti ca prāṇa aimitte jīvasya utkrāti pratiṣṭhe darśayati pañca vṛttiḥ maaḥ vat vyapadiśyate itas ca asti mukhyasya prāṇasya vaiśeṣikam kāryam yatkāraṇam pañca vṛttiḥ ayam vyapadiśyate śrutiṣu prāṇa upāaḥ vyāaḥ udāaḥ samāaḥ iti vṛtti bhedaḥ ca ayam kārya bheda apekṣaḥ prāṇaḥ prāc vṛttiḥ ucchvāsa ādi karmā apāaḥ avāc vṛttiḥ riśvāsa ādi karmā vyāaḥ tayoḥ saṃdhau vīryavat karma hetuḥ udāaḥ ūrdhva vṛttiḥ utkrāti ādi hetuḥ samāaḥ samam sarveṣu aṅgeṣu iti evam pañca vṛttiḥ prāṇaḥ mao vat yathā maasaḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ evam prāṇasya api iti arthaḥ śrotra ādi nimittāḥ śabda ādi viṣayāḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ prasiddhāḥ a tu kāmaḥ saṃkalpaḥ bṛ u ityādyāḥ paripaṭhitāḥ gṛhyera pañca saṃkhyā atirekāt śrotra ādi irapekṣā bhūta bhaviṣyat ādi viṣayā aparā vṛttiḥ asti iti pañca saṃkhyā atirekaḥ evam tarhi para matam apratiṣiddham aumatam bhavati iti yāyāt iha api yoga śāstra prasiddhāḥ maasaḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ parigṛhyate bahu vṛtti tva mātreṇa vā prāṇasya iti draṣṭavyam jīva upakaraṇa tvam api prāṇasya pañca vṛtti tvāt mao vat iti vā yojayitavyam aṇuḥ ca śreṣṭha aṇu tva adhikaraṇam aṇuḥ ca ayam mukhyaḥ prāṇaḥ pratyetavyaḥ itara prāṇa vat aṇu tvam ca iha api saukṣmya paricchedau a paramāṇu tulya tvam pañcabhiḥ vṛttibhiḥ sūkṣmaḥ prāṇaḥ utkrātau vibhu tvam api prāṇasya samāmāyate samaḥ samaḥ ebhiḥ tribhiḥ lokaiḥ samaḥ sarveṇa iti evamādiṣu pradeśeṣu tat ucyate ādhidaivikea samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi rūpeṇa hairaṇyagarbheṇa prāṇa ātmā eva etat vibhu tvam āmāyate a ādhyātmikea api ca samaḥ prāṇasya paricchedaḥ eva pradarśyate tasmāt adoṣaḥ jyotiḥ ādi adhiṣṭhāam tu jyotiḥ ādi adhikaraṇam te puaḥ prakṛtāḥ prāṇāḥ kim sva mahimā eva svasmai svasmai kāryāya prabhavati āhosvit devatā dhiṣṭhitāḥ prabhavati iti vicāryate tatra prāptam tāvat yathāsvam kārya śakti yogāt sva mahimā eva prāṇāḥ pravarteraiti api ca devatā dhiṣṭhitāḥ prāṇāām pravṛttau abhyugamyamāāyām tāsām eva adhiṣṭhātrīṇām devatāām bhoktṛ tva prasaṅgāt śārīrasya bhoktṛ tvam pralīyeta atas sva mahimā eva eṣām pravṛttiḥ iti evam prāpte idam ucyate tu iti tuśabdena pūrvapakṣaḥ vyāvartyate jyotiḥ ādibhiḥ agi ādi abhimāiībhiḥ devatābhiḥ adhiṣṭhitam vāc ādi karaṇa jātam sva kāryeṣu pravartate iti hetum ca vyācaṣṭhe tat āmaaāt iti tathā hi agiḥ vāc bhūtvā mukham prāviśat ityādi ageḥ ca ayam vāc bhāvaḥ mukha praveśaḥ ca devatā ātmā adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam aṅgīkṛtya ucyate hi devatā saṃbadham pratyākhyāya ageḥ vāci mukhe vā kaścid viśeṣa saṃbadhaḥ dṛśyate tathā vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ bhūtvā āsike prāviśat iti evamādi api yojayitavyam tathā vāc eva brahmaṇaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ jyotiṣā bhāti ca tapati ca iti evamādiā vāc ādīām etam eva artham draḍhayati sa vai vācam eva prathamām atyavahat sā yadā mṛtyum atyamucyata iti ca evamādiā etam eva artham dyotayati sarvatra ca adhyātma adhidaivata vibhāge pratyāsattyā bhavati smṛtau api vāc adhyātmam iti prāhuḥ brāhmaṇāḥ tattva darśiṇaḥ vaktavyam adhibhūtam tu vahis tatra adhidaivatam ityādiā vāc ādīām agi ādi devatā dhiṣṭhita tvam sa prapañcam pradarśitam yat uktam sva kārya śakti yogāt sva mahimā eva prāṇāḥ pravarteraiti tat ayuktam śaktāām api śakaṭa ādīām aaḍuha ādi adhiṣṭhitāām pravṛtti darśaāt ubhayathā upapattau ca āgamāt vāc ādīām agi ādi devatā adhiṣṭhātām pravṛtti darśaāt ubhayathā upapattau ca āgamāt vāc ādīām devatā adhiṣṭhita tvam eva yat api uktam devatāām eva adhiṣṭhātrīṇām bhoktṛ tva prasaṅgaḥ a śārīrasya iti tat parihriyate prāṇavatā śabdāt satīṣu api prāṇāām adhiṣṭhātrīṣu devatāsu prāṇavatā kārya karaṇa saṃghāta śārīreṇa eva eṣām prāṇāām śruteḥ avagamyate tathā hi śrutiḥ atha yatra etat ākāśam auviṣaṇṇam cakṣuḥ sa cākṣuṣaḥ puruṣaḥ darśaāya cakṣuḥ atha yaḥ veda idam jighrāṇi iti saḥ ātmā gadhāya ghrāṇam iti evaṃjātīyakā śārīreṇa eva śrāvayati api ca a eka tvāt pratikaraṇam adhiṣṭhātrīṇām devatāām bhoktṛ tvam asmi ekaḥ hi ayam asmi śarīre śārīraḥ bhoktā pratisaṃdhā ādi saṃbhavāt avagamyate tasya ca itya tvāt tasya ca śārīrasya asmi śarīre puṇya pāpa upalepa saṃbhavāt sukha duḥkha upabhoga saṃbhavāt ca hi śarīre bhoktṛ tvam pratilabdhum arhati śrutiḥ ca bhavati puṇyam eva amum gacchati ha vai deva apāpam gacchati iti śārīreṇa eva ca prāṇānām saṃbadhaḥ utkrāti ādiṣu tad auvṛtti darśaāt tam utkrāmatam prāṇaḥ utkrāmati prāṇam a ūtkrāmatam sarve prāṇāḥ aūtkrāmati ityādi śrutibhyaḥ tasmāt satīṣu api karaṇāām iyatrīṣu devatāsu a śārīrasya bhoktṛ tvam apagacchati karaṇa pakṣasya eva hi devatā a bhoktṛ pakṣasya iti te idriyāṇi tad vyapadeśāt ayatra śreṣṭhāt idriya adhikaraṇam mukhyaḥ ca ekaḥ itare ca ekādaśa prāṇāḥ aukrātāḥ tatra idam a param saṃdihyate kim mukhyasya eva prāṇasya vṛtti bhedāḥ itare prāṇāḥ āhosvit tattva ātarāṇi iti kim tāvat prāptam mukhyasya eva itare vṛtti bhedāḥ iti kutas śruteḥ tathā hi śrutiḥ mukhyam itarān ca mukhya ātma tām itareṣām khyāpayati hata asya eva sarve rūpam asāma iti te etasya eva sarve rūpam abhavaḥ iti prāṇa eka śabda tvāt ca ekatva adhyavasāyaḥ itarathā hi ayāyyam a eka artha tvam prāṇa śabdasya prasajyeta ekatra vā mukhyasya itaratra lākṣaṇika tvam āpadyeta tasmāt yathā ekasya eva prāṇasya prāṇa ādyāḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ evam vāc ādyāḥ api ekādaśā iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ kutas vyapadeśa bhedāt kaḥ yam vyapadeśa bhedaḥ te prakṛtāḥ prāṇāḥ śreṣṭham varjayitvā avaśiṣṭāḥ ekādaśa idriyāṇi iti ucyate śrutau evam vyapadeśa bheda darśaāt etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ sarva idriyāṇi ca iti hi evaṃjātīyakeṣu pradeśeṣu pṛthak prāṇaḥ vyapadiśyate pṛthak ca idriyāṇi sati prāṇa vat syāt maaḥ sarva idriyāṇi ca iti pṛthak vyapadeśa darśaāt satyam etat smṛtau tu ekādaśa idriyāṇi iti śrotra ādi vat saṃgṛhyate prāṇasya tu idriya tvam a śrutau smṛtau vā prasiddham asti vyapadeśa bhedaḥ ca ayam tattva bheda pakṣe upapadyate tattva ekatve tu saḥ eva ekaḥ sa prāṇa idriya vyapadeśam labhate a labhate ca iti vipratiṣiddham tasmāt tattva atara bhūtāḥ mukhyāt itare kutas ca tattva atara bhūtāḥ bheda śruteḥ vāc ādibhyaḥ prāṇaḥ sarvatra śrūyate te ha vācam ūcuḥ iti upakramya upasaṃhṛtya vāc ādi prakaraṇam atha ha imam āsayam prāṇam ūcuḥ iti asura vidhvaṃsiḥ mukhyasya prāṇasya pṛthak upakramaṇāt tathā vācam prāṇam iti evamādyāḥ api bheda śrutayaḥ udāhartavyāḥ tasmāt api tattva atara bhūtāḥ mukhyāt itare kutas ca tattva atara bhūtāḥ vailakṣaṇyāt ca vailakṣaṇyam ca bhavati mukhyasya itareṣām ca supteṣu vāc ādiṣu mukhya antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar antar an ekaḥ jāgarti saḥ eva ca ekaḥ mṛtyuā a āptaḥ āptāḥ tu itare tasya eva ca sthiti utkrātibhyām idriyāṇām viṣaya āloca a hetu tvam ca idriyāṇām a prāṇasya iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ bhūyāt lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ prāṇa idriyāṇām tasmāt api eṣām tattva atara bhāva siddhiḥ yat uktam te etasya eva sarve rūpam abhavaḥ iti śruteḥ prāṇe eva idriyāṇi iti tat ayuktam tatra api paurvāparya ālocaāt bheda pratīteḥ tathā hi vadiṣyāmi eva aham iti vāc dadhre iti mṛtyuḥ śramaḥ bhūtvā upayeme tasmāt śrāmyati eva vāc iti ca śrama rūpeṇa mṛtyuā grasta tvam vāc ādīām abhidhāya atha imam eva madhyamaḥ prāṇaḥ iti pṛthak prāṇam mṛtyunā a abhibhūtam ayam vai śreṣṭhaḥ iti ca śreṣṭha tām asya avadhārayati tasmāt vāc ādiṣu parispada lābhasya prāṇa āyatta tvam vāc ādīām iti matavyam a tu tādātmyam atas eva ca prāṇa śabdasya idriyeṣu lākṣaṇika tva siddhiḥ tathā ca śrutiḥ te etasya eva sarve rūpam abhava tasmāt ete ete ākhyāyate prāṇāḥ iti mukhya prāṇa viṣayasya eva prāṇa śabdasya idriyeṣu lākṣaṇikīm vṛttim darśayati prāṇāt vāc ādīni idriyāṇi iti saṃjñā mūrti klṛptiḥ tu trivṛt kurvataḥ upadeśāt saṃjñā mūrti klṛpti adhikaraṇam sat prakriyāyām sṛṣṭim abhidhāya upadiśyate sā iyam devatā aikṣata hatā aham imāḥ tisraḥ devatāḥ āma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti tāsām trivṛtam trivṛtam ekaikām karavāṇi iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim jīva kartṛkam idam āma rūpa vyākaraṇam āhosvit parameśvara kartṛkam iti tatra prāptam tāvat jīva kartṛkam eva idam āma rūpa vyākaraṇam iti kutas iti viśeṣaṇāt yathā loke cāreṇa aham saṃkalayāi iti evaṃjātīyake prayoge cāra kartṛkam eva sat hetu kartṛ tvāt rājā hetu kartṛkam eva sat āma rūpa vyākaraṇam hetu kartṛ tvāt devatāḥ ātmayā adhyāropayati vyākaravāṇi iti uttamapuruṣa prayogeṇa api ca ḍittha ḍavittha ādiṣu āmasu ghaṭa śarāva ādiṣu ca rūpeṣu jīvasya eva vyākartṛ tvam dṛṣṭam tasmāt jīva kartṛkam eva idam āma rūpa vyākaraṇam iti evam prāpte abhidhatte saṃjñā mūrti klṛptiḥ tu iti tuśabde pakṣam vyāvartayati saṃjñā mūrti klṛptiḥ iti āma rūpa vyākriyā iti etat trivṛt kurvataḥ iti parameśvaram lakṣayati trivṛt karaṇe tasya yā iyam saṃjñā klṛptiḥ mūrti klṛptiḥ ca agiḥ ādityaḥ cadramāḥ vidyut iti tathā kuśa kāśa palāśa ādiṣu paśu mṛga mauṣya ādiṣu ca pratyākṛti prativyakti ca aeka prakārā sā khalu parameśvarasya eva kṛtiḥ bhavitum arhati kutas upadeśāt tathā hi sā iyam devatā iti upakramya vyākaravāṇi iti uttamapuruṣa prayogeṇa parasya eva brahmaṇaḥ vyākartṛ tvam iha upadiśyate iti viśeṣaṇāt jīva kṛrtṛka tvam vyākaraṇasya adhyavasitam saṃbadhyate aupraviśyaḥ saṃbadhyate vyākaravāṇi hi vyākaravāṇi iti ayam devatā viṣaye uttama puruṣa aupacārikaḥ kalpyeta ca giri adī samudra ādiṣu aāvidheṣu aīśvarasya jīvasya vyākaraṇa sāmarthyam asti yeṣu api ca asti sāmarthyam teṣu api parameśvara āyattam eva tat ca cāraḥ iva rājñaḥ iti viśeṣaṇāt jīva bhāvasya tad kṛtam api āma rūpa vyākaraṇam parameśvara kṛtam eva bhavati parameśvaraḥ eva ca āma rūpayoḥ vyākartā iti sarva upaiṣat siddhātaḥ ākāśaḥ ha vai āmaḥ āma rūpayoḥ irvahitā ityādi śrutibhyaḥ tasmāt parameśvarasya eva trivṛt kurvataḥ karma āma rūpa vyākaraṇam trivṛtkaraṇa pūrvakam eva idam iha āma rūpa vyākaraṇam vivakṣyate pratyekam āma rūpa vyākaraṇasya tat ca trivṛtkaraṇam agi āditya cadra vidyutsu śrutiḥ darśayati yat age rohitam rūpam tejasaḥ tat rūpam yat śuklam tat apām yat kṛṣṇam tat aasya iti ādiā tatra agiḥ iti idam rūpam vyākriyate sati ca rūpa vyākaraṇe viṣaya pratilambhāt agiḥ iti idam vyākriyate evam eva āditya ca dra vidyutsu api draṣṭavyam ca bhauma ambhasa taijaseṣu triṣu api dravyeṣu aviśeṣeṇa trivṛtkaraṇam uktam bhavati upakrama upasaṃhārayoḥ sādhāraṇa tvāt tathā hi aviśeṣeṇa eva upakramaḥ imāḥ tisraḥ devatāḥ trivṛt itravṛt ekaikā bhavati iti aviśeṣeṇa eva ca upasaṃhāraḥ yat u rohitam iva abhūt iti tejasaḥ tat rūpam iti evamādiḥ yat u avijñātam iva abhūt iti etāsām eva devatāām samāsaḥ iti evam atas tāsām tisṛṇām devatāām bahis trivṛt kṛtāām satīām adhyātmam aparam trivṛt karaṇam uktam imāḥ tisraḥ devatāḥ puruṣam prāpya trivṛt itravṛt ekaikā bhavati iti tat idāīm ācāryaḥ yathāśrutyā eva upadarśayati āśaṅkitam kaṃcid doṣam parihariṣya māṃsa ādi bhaumam yathāśabdam itarayoḥ ca bhūmeḥ trivṛtkṛtāyāḥ puruṣeṇa upabhujyamāāyāḥ māṃsa ādi kāryam yathāśabdam iṣpadyate tathā hi śrutiḥ tredhā vidhīyate tasya yaḥ sthaviṣṭhaḥ dhātuḥ tat purīṣam bhavati yaḥ madhyamaḥ tamāṃsam yoṇiṣṭhaḥ tamaaḥ iti trivṛtkṛtā bhūmiḥ eva eṣā adyate iti abhiprāyaḥ tasyāḥ ca sthaviṣṭham rūpam madhyamam adhyātmam māṃsam vardhayati aṇiṣṭham tu evam itarayoḥ ap tejasoḥ yathāśabdam kāryam avagatavyam mūtram lohitam prāṇaḥ ca apām kāryam asthi majjā vāc tejasaḥ iti atra āha yadi sarvam eva trivṛt kṛtam bhūta bhautikam aviśeṣa śruteḥ tāsām trivṛtam asthi trivṛtam ekaikām akarot iti kiṃkṛtaḥ tarhi ayam viśeṣa vyapadeśaḥ idam tejaḥ imāḥ āpaḥ idam aam iti tathā adhyātmam idam aasya aśitasya kāryam māṃsa ādi idam apām pītāām kāryam lohita ādi idam tejasā uśitasya kāryam asthi ādi iti atra ucyate vaiśeṣyāt tu tad vādaḥ tad vādaḥ ca uditam viśeṣasya bhāvaḥ vaiśeṣyam bhūyaḥ tvam iti yāvat sati api trivṛt karaṇe kvacid kasyacid bhūta dhātoḥ bhūyaḥ tvam upalabhyate ageḥ tejaḥ bhūyaḥ tvam udakasya ap bhūyaḥ tvam pṛthivyāḥ iti vyavahāra prasiddhi artham ca idam trivṛtkaraṇam vyavahāraḥ ca trivṛt kṛta rajju vat ekatva āpattau satyām a bhede bhūta traya gocaraḥ lokasya prasidhyet tasmāt sati api trivṛtkaraṇe vaiśeṣyāt eva bhūta bhautika viṣayaḥ upapadyate tad vādaḥ tad vādaḥ iti pada abhyāsaḥ adhyāya parisamāptim dyotayati iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye dvitīyaḥ udhyāyaḥ murat tṛtīyaḥ udhyāyaḥ prathamaḥ pādaḥ tad atara pratipattau raṃhati sampariṣvaktaḥ praśairūpaṇābhyām tad atara pratipatti adhikaraṇam dvitīye adhyāye smṛti yāya virodhaḥ parihṛtaḥ parapakṣāṇām ca a apekṣa tvam prapañcitam śruti vipratiṣedhaḥ ca parihṛtaḥ tatra ca jīva vyatiriktāi tattvāi jīva upakaraṇāi brahmaṇaḥ jāyate iti uktam atha idāīm upakaraṇa upahitasya jīvasya saṃsāra gati prakāraḥ tad avasthātarāṇi brahma tattvam vidyā bheda abhedau guṇa upasaṃhāra a upasaṃhārau samyagdarśaāt puruṣa artha siddhaḥ samyagdarśa upāya vidhi prabhedaḥ ca iti etad artha jātam tṛtīye adhyāye prasaṅga āgatam ca tatra prathame tāvat pāde pañcāgi vidyām āśritya saṃsāra gati prabhedaḥ pradarśyate vairāgya hetoḥ tasmāt jugupset iti ca ate śravaṇāt jīvaḥ mukhya prāṇa sacivaḥ sa idriyaḥ avidyā karma pūrva prajñā parigrahaḥ pūrva deham vihāya dehātaram pratipadyate iti etat avagatam atha īam ete prāṇāḥ iti evamādeḥ iti evamādeḥ kurute iti saṃsāra prakaraṇa sthāt śabdāt dharma adharma phala upabhoga saṃbhavāt ca sa kim deha bījaiḥ bhūta sūkṣmaiḥ asaṃpariṣvaktaḥ gacchati āhosvit saṃpariṣvaktaḥ iti cityate kim tāvat prāptam asaṃpariṣvaktaḥ iti kutas karaṇa upādāa vat bhūta upādāasya a śruta tvāt saḥ etāḥ tejaḥ mātrāḥ samabhyādadāaḥ iti hi atra tejaḥ mātrā śabda upādāam saṃkīrtayati vākya śeṣe cakṣuḥ ādi saṃkīrtaāt asti sulabhāḥ ca sarvatra bhūtamātrāḥ yatra eva dehaḥ ārabdhavyaḥ tatra eva sati tatas ca tāsām tasmāt asaṃpariṣvaktaḥ yāti iti evam prāpte paṭhati ācāryaḥ tad atara pratipattau raṃhati saṃpariṣvaktaḥ iti tad atara pratipattau deha atara pratipattau deha bījaiḥ bhūta sūkṣmaiḥ saṃpariṣvaktaḥ raṃhati gacchati iti avagatavyam kutas praśai rūpaṇābhyām tathā hi praśas vettha yathā pañcamyām āhutau āpaḥ puruṣa vacasaḥ bhavati iti ca prativacam dyu parjaya pṛthivī puruṣa yoṣitsu pañcasu agiṣu śraddhā soma vṛṣṭi a aretaḥ rūpāḥ pañca āhutīḥ darśayitvā iti tu pañcamyām āhutau āpaḥ puruṣa vacasaḥ bhavati iti tasmāt adbhiḥ pariveṣṭitaḥ jīvaḥ raṃhati vrajati iti gamyate au ayā śrutiḥ jalūkā vat pūrva deham a muñcati dehātaram ākramati iti darśayati tat yathā tṛṇajalāyukā iti tatra api ap pariveṣṭitasya eva jīvasya karma upasthāpita pratipattavya deha viṣaya bhāva ādīrghībhāva mātram jalūkayā upamīyate iti avirodhaḥ evam śruti ukte dehātara pratipatti prakāre sati yāḥ puruṣam ati prabhavāḥ ca deha atara pratipattau karma vaśāt vṛtti lābhaḥ tatra bhavati kevalasya eva ātmanaḥ vṛtti lābhaḥ tatra bhavati idriyāṇi tu deha vat abhiavāya iva tatra tatra bhogasthāe utpadyate maaḥ eva vā kevalam bhogasthāam abhipratiṣṭhate jīvaḥ eva vā utplutya dehāt dehātaram pratipadyate śukaḥ iva vṛkṣāt vṛkṣātaram iti evamādyāḥ tāḥ sarvāḥ eva śruti virodhāt udāhṛtābhyām praśa prativacaābhyām kevalābhiḥ adbhiḥ saṃpariṣvaktaḥ raṃhati iti ap śabda śravaṇa sāmarthyāt tatra katham pratijñāyate sarvaiḥ eva bhūta sūkṣmaiḥ saṃpariṣvaktaḥ raṃhati iti atas uttaram paṭhati tri ātmaka tvāt tu bhūyaḥ tvāt abhyupagamaḥ śeṣa karma sadbhāveiḥ mokṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti ayam api asthāe saṃbhramaḥ samyak darśaāt aśeṣa karma kṣaya śruteḥ tasmāt sthitam etat eva auśayavataḥ varohati iti te ca avarohataḥ yathetam aevam ca avarohati yathetam iti yathāgatam iti arthaḥ aevam iti tad viparyayeṇa iti arthaḥ dhūma ākāśayoḥ avarohe saṃkīrtaāt yathetam śabdāt ca yathāgatam iti pratīyate rātri ādi asaṃkīrtaāt abhra ādi upasaṃkhyāāt ca viparyayaḥ api pratīyate caraṇāt iti atha api syāt yā śrutiḥ auśaya sadbhāva pratipāda āya udāhṛtā tat ye iha ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ iti sā khalu caraṇāt darśayati āuśayāt caraṇam cāritram ācāraḥ śīlam iti aarthātaram auśayaḥ tu bhukta phalāt karmaṇā utiriktam karma abhipretam śrutiḥ ca karma caraṇe vyapadiśati yathā kārī yathā cārī tathā bhavati karmāṇi tāi sevitavyāi itarāṇi tāi tvayā upāsyāi iti ca tasmāt āuśaya siddhiḥ iti ced ā eṣa doṣaḥ yatas ouśaya upalakṣaṇa arthā eva eṣā caraṇa śrutiḥ iti kārṣṇājiiḥ ācāryaḥ mayate āarthakyam iti tat apekṣa tvāt syāt etat kasmāt puaścaraṇa śabde śrautam śīlam vihāya lākṣaṇikaḥ auśayaḥ pratyāyyate śīlasya eva śrautasya vihita pratiṣiddhasya sādhu asādhu rūpasya phalam bhaviṣyati avaśyam ca śīlasya api kiṃcid phalam abhyupagatavyam ayathā hi āarthakyam eva śīlasya prasajyeta iti ced ā eṣa doṣaḥ kutas tad apekṣa tvāt iṣṭa ādi hi karma jātam caraṇa apekṣam a hi sat ācāra hīaḥ kaścid adhikṛtaḥ syāt ācāra hīam a vedāḥ ityādi smṛtibhyaḥ puruṣa artha tve pi ācārasya āarthakyam iṣṭa ādau hi karma jāte phalam ārabhamāṇe tad apekṣaḥ eva ācāraḥ tatra eva kaṃcid atiśayam ārapsyate karma ca sarva artha kāri iti śruti smṛti prasiddhiḥ tasmāt karma eva śīla upalakṣitam auśaya bhūtam kāraṇam iti kārṣṇājieḥ matam a hi karmaṇi saṃbhavati śīlāt hi padbhyām palāyitum pārayamāṇaḥ raṃhitum arhati iti sukṛta duṣkṛte eva iti tu bādariḥ bādariḥ tu ācāryaḥ sukṛta duṣkṛte eva caraṇa śabde pratyāyyete iti caraṇam karma iti aarthātaram tathā hi aviśeṣeṇa karma mātre caratiḥ dṛśyate yaḥ hi iṣṭa ādi lakṣaṇam puṇyam karma karoti tam laukikāḥ ācakṣate dharmam carati eṣa mahātmā iti ca dharma viśeṣaḥ eva bheda vyapadeśaḥ tu karma caraṇayoḥ upapadyate tasmāt ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ praśasta karmāṇaḥ kapūya caraṇāḥ idita karmāṇaḥ iti aiṣṭa ādi kāriṇām api ca śrutam aiṣṭa ādi kāri adhikaraṇam iṣṭa ādi kāriṇaḥ ca dramasam gacchati iti uktam ye tu itare iṣṭa ādi kāriṇaḥ te api kim cadramasam gacchati uta a gacchati iti cityate tatra tāvat āha iṣṭa ādi kāriṇaḥ eva cadramasam gacchati iti etat a kasmāt yatas iṣṭa ādi kāriṇām api cadra maṇḍalam śrutam tathā hi aviśeṣeṇa kauṣītakiḥ samāmaati ye vai ke ca asmāt lokāt prayati cadramasam eva te sarve gacchati iti ca cadra prāptim avakalpate pañcamyām āhutau iti āhuti saṃkhyā iyamāt tasmāt sarve eva cadramasam āsīdeyuḥ iṣṭa ādi kāriṇām itareṣām ca yuktam iti ced a itareṣām cadra maṇḍale bhoga abhāvāt tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati sarve cadramasam gacchati iti kasmāt bhogāya eva hi cadra ārohaṇam pratyavarohāya eva yathā kaścid vṛkṣam ārohati puṣpa phala upādāāya pataāya eva bhogaḥ ca aiṣṭa ādi kāriṇām cadramasi āsti iti uktam tasmāt iṣṭa ādi kāriṇaḥ eva cadramasam ārohati etare te tu yama ālayam avagāhya puar eva imam lokam pratyavarohati evaṃbhūtau teṣām āroha avarohau bhavataḥ kutas tad gati darśaāt tathā hi śrutiḥ prayatām aiṣṭa ādi kāriṇām yama vaśya tām darśayati a sāṃparāyaḥ pratibhāti bālam mūḍham ayam paras iti puas puarvaśam āpadyate me iti vaivasvatam saṃgamaam iti evaṃjātīyakam ca bahu eva yam avaśya tā prāpti liṅgam bhavati smarati ca api ca mauvyāsa prabhṛtayaḥ śiṣṭāḥ pure yama āyattam kapūya karma vipākam smarati āciketa upākhyā ādiṣu api ca sapta api ca sapta arakāḥ raurava pramukhāḥ smaryate paurāṇikaiḥ kutas te cadram prāpuyuḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ viruddham idam yama āyattāḥ yātaāḥ pāpa karmāṇaḥ ubhavati iti yāvatā teṣu raurava ādiṣu citragupta ādayaḥ smaryate iti etya āha tatra api ca tad vyāpārāt avirodhaḥ teṣu api saptasu arakeṣu tasya eva yamasya adhiṣṭhātṛ tva vyāpāra abhyupagamāt avirodhaḥ yama prayuktāḥ eva hi te citragupta ādayaḥ adhiṣṭhātāraḥ smaryate vidyā karmaṇoḥ iti tu prakṛta tvāt pañcāgi vidyāyām vettha yathā asau saṃpūryate iti asya praśasya prativacaḥ avasare śrūyate atha etayoḥ pathoḥ bhūtaiḥ bhavati jāyasva mriyastva iti etat tṛtīyam saṃpūryate iti tatra etayoḥ pathoḥ iti vidyā karmaṇoḥ iti etat kasmāt prakṛta tvāt vidyā karmaṇī hi deva yāa pitṛyāṇayoḥ pathoḥ pratipade prakṛte tat ye ittham viduḥ iti vidyā tayā pratipattavyaḥ deva yāaḥ pathāḥ prakīrtitaḥ iṣṭāpūrte dattam iti karma pratipattavyaḥ pitṛyāṇaḥ pathāḥ prakīrtitaḥ tad prakriyāyām atha etayoḥ pathoḥ iti śrutam etat uktam bhavati ye pathi adhikṛtāḥ karmaṇā pitṛyāṇe teṣām eṣa kṣudrajatu lakṣaṇa usakṛt āvartī tṛtīyaḥ pathā bhavati iti tasmāt api a aiṣṭa ādi kāribhiḥ cadramāḥ prāpyate syāt etat cadra bimbam āruhya tatas uvaruhya kṣudrajatu tvam pratipatsyate iti tat api āsti āroha āarthakyāt api ca sarveṣu prayatsu cadra lokam prāpuvatsu asau lokaḥ prayadbhiḥ saṃpūryeta iti atas praśa viruddham prativacaam prasajyeta tathā hi prativacaam dātavyam yathā asau saṃpūryate avaroha abhyupagamāt asaṃpūraṇa upapattiḥ iti ced a aśruta tvāt satyam avarohāt api asaṃpūraṇam upapadyate śrutiḥ tu asaṃpūraṇam darśayati etat tṛtīyam asaṃpūraṇam darśayati etat tṛtīyam lokaḥ saṃpūryate iti a ārohāt eva a saṃpūraṇam iti yuktam avarohasya iṣṭa ādi kāriṣu api aviśiṣṭa tve sati tṛtīya sthā okti āarthakya prasaṅgāt tuśabdaḥ tu śākhātarīya vākya prabhavām aśeṣa gama āśaṅkām ucchiatti evam sati adhikṛta apekṣaḥ śākhātarīye vākye sarva śabdaḥ uvatiṣṭhate ye vai kecid adhikṛtāḥ asmāt lokāt prayati cat ramasam eva te sarve gacchati iti yat puaruktam deha lābha upapattaye sarve cat ramasam gatum arhati pañcamyām āhutau iti āhuti saṃkhyā iyamāt iti tat pratyucyate a tṛtīye tathā upalabdheḥ a tṛtīye deha lābhāya pañca saṃkhyā iyamaḥ kutas tathā upalabdheḥ tathā hi prakāreṇa tṛtīya sthā aprāptiḥ upalabhyate jāyasva mriyasva iti etat tṛtīyam iti api ca pañcamyām āhutau āpaḥ puruṣa vacasaḥ bhavati iti āhuti saṃkhyā kīrtyate puruṣa śabdasya api ca pañcamyām āhutau apām puruṣa vacaḥ tvam upadiśyate a apañcamyām āhutau puruṣa vacaḥ tvam pratiṣidhyate vākyasya dvi artha tā doṣāt tatra yeṣām āroha avarohau saṃbhavataḥ teṣām pañcamyām āhutau dehaḥ udbhaviṣyati tu tatra droṇa ādīām yoṣit viṣayā ekā āhutiḥ āsti dhṛṣṭadyuma ādīām tu yoṣit puruṣa viṣaye dve api āhutī staḥ yathā ca tatra bhavati evam ayatra api bhaviṣyati balākā api atareṇa eva retaḥ sekam garbham dhatte iti loka rūḍhiḥ darśaāt ca api ca caturvidhe bhūta grāme jarāyu ja aṇḍa ja sveda ja udbhid ja lakṣaṇe sveda ja udbhid jayoḥ atareṇa eva grāmya dharmam utpatti darśaāt āhuti saṃkhyā ādaraḥ bhavati evam ayatra api bhaviṣyati auteṣām khalu eṣām bhūtāām trīṇi eva bhavati āṇḍa jam jīva jam udbhijjam iti atra trividhaḥ eva bhūta grāmaḥ śrūyate katham caturvidha tvam bhūta grāmasya pratijñātam iti atra ucyate tṛtīya śabda avarodhaḥ saṃśoka jasya āṇḍa jam jīva jam udbhijjam iti atra tṛtīye udbhijja śabde eva sveda ja upasaṃgrahaḥ kṛtaḥ pratyetavyaḥ ubhayoḥ api sveda ja udbhijjayoḥ bhūmi udaka udbheda prabhava tvasya tulya tvāt sthāvara udbhedāt tu vilakṣaṇaḥ jaṅgama udbhedaḥ iti ayatra sveda ja udbhijjayoḥ bheda vādaḥ iti avirodhaḥ sābhāvya āpattiḥ upapatteḥ sābhāvya āpatti adhikaraṇam iṣṭa ādi kāriṇaḥ ca dramasam āruhya tasmin yāvat saṃpātam uṣitvā tatas sā auśayā avarohati iti uktam atha avaroha prakāraḥ parīkṣyate tatra iyam avaroha śrutiḥ bhavati atha etam eva adhvāam puarivartate yathā itam ākāśam ākāśāt vāyum vāyuḥ bhūtvā dhūmaḥ bhavati dhūmaḥ bhūtvā abhram bhavati abhram bhūtvā meghaḥ bhavati meghaḥ bhūtvā pravarṣati iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim ākāśa ādi svarūpam eva avarohataḥ pratipadyate kim vā ākāśa ādi sāmyam iti tatra prāptam tāvat ākāśa ādi svarūpam eva pratipadyate iti kutas evam hi śrutiḥ bhavati itarathā lakṣaṇā syāt śruti lakṣaṇā viśaye ca śrutiḥ yāyyā a lakṣaṇā tathā bhūtvā dhūmaḥ bhavati iti akṣaraṇi tat tad svarūpa āpattau avakalpate tasmāt ākāśa ādi sva rūpa pratipattiḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ ākāśa ādi sāmyam pratipadyate iti cadra maṇḍale yat am mayam śarīram upabhoga artham ārabdham tat upabhoga kṣaye sati sūkṣmam ākāśa samam bhavati tatas vāyoḥ vaśam eti tatas dhūma ādibhiḥ saṃpṛcyate iti tat etat ucyate yathā itam ākāśam ākāśāt vāyum iti evamādiā kutas etat upapatteḥ evam hi etat upapadyate a hi mukhyaḥ upapadyate ākāśa svarūpa pratipattau ca vāyu ādi krameṇa avarohaḥ upapadyate vibhu tvāt ca iti asaṃbaddha tvāt tad sādṛśya āpatteḥ ayaḥ ghaṭate śruti asaṃbhave ca lakṣaṇa āśrayaṇam yāyyam eva atas ākāśa ādi tulya tā āpattiḥ eva atra ākāśa ādi bhāvaḥ iti upacaryate āticireṇa viśeṣāt āticira adhikaraṇam tatra akāśa ādi pratipattau prāk vrīhi ādi bhāva āpatteḥ bhavati viśayaḥ kim dīrgham dīrgham kālam pūrva pūrva sādṛśyeṇa avasthāya uttara uttara sādṛśyam gacchati uta alpam alpam iti tatra aiyamaḥ iyama kāriṇaḥ śāstrasya abhāvāt iti evam prāpte idam āha āticireṇa iti alpam alpam kālam ākāśa ādi bhāvena avasthāya varṣa dhārābhiḥ saha imām bhuvam āpatati kutas etat viśeṣa darśaāt tathā hi vrīhi ādi bhāva āpatteḥ aataram viśiaṣṭi atas vai khalu iti takāraḥ ekaḥ chāt asyām prakriyāyām luptaḥ matavyaḥ duriṣprapatataram duriṣkramataram duḥkhataram asmāt vrīhi ādi bhāvāt saraṇam bhavati iti arthaḥ tat atra duḥkham bhavati iti arthaḥ tat atra duḥkham pradarśaya pūrveṣu sukham darśayati sukha duḥkha tā viśeṣaḥ ca ayam iṣprapataasya kāla alpatva dīrgha tva aimittaḥ tasmin avadhau śarīra aiṣpatteḥ upabhoga asaṃbhavāt tasmāt vrīhi ādi bhāva āpatteḥ prāk syāt iti pūrvavat abhilāpāt tasmin eva avarohe tasmin eva avarohe paṭhyate te iha vrīhi yavāḥ oṣadhi vaaspatayaḥ tila māṣāḥ iti jāyate iti tatra saṃśayaḥ bhavati āhosvit kṣetrajña atara dhiṣṭhiteṣu sthāvara śarīreṣu saṃśleṣa mātram gacchati iti kim tāvat prāptam bhavati iti kutas etat bhavati iti kutas etat bhavati iti kutas etat jaeḥ mukhya artha tva upapatteḥ sthāvara bhāvasya ca śruti smṛtyoḥ upabhoga sthāa tva prasiddheḥ paśu hiṃsā ādi yogāt ca iṣṭa ādeḥ karma jātasya a iṣṭa phala tva upapatteḥ tasmāt mukhyam eva idam auśayiām vrīhi ādi jama śva ādi jama vat yathā aśva yoim vā sūkara yoim vā cāṇḍāla yoim vā iti mukhyam eva auśayiām śva ādi jam tat sukha duḥkha āvitam bhavati evam vrīhi ādi jam api iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ ayaiḥ jīvaiḥ adhiṣṭhiteṣu vrīhi ādiṣu saṃsarga mātram auśayiḥ pratipadyate bhavati pūrvavat yathā tad saṃśleṣa mātram evam vrīhi ādi bhāvaḥ api jāti sthāvaraiḥ saṃśleṣa mātram kutas etat tadvat eva iha api abhilāpāt tadvat bhāvaḥ karma vyāpāram atareṇa yathā ākāśa ādiṣu a kiṃcid karma vyāpāram parāmṛśati evam vrīhi ādi jamaya pi tasmāā asti atra sukha duḥkha bhāj tvam auśayiām yatra tu sukha duḥkha bhāj tvam abhipraiti parāmṛśati tatra karma vyāpāram ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ kapūya caraṇāḥ iti api ca vrīhi ādi jamai vrīhi ādiṣu kaṇḍyamāeṣu pacyamāeṣu bhakṣyamāṇeṣu ca pravaseyuḥ yaḥ hi jīvaḥ yat śarīram abhimayate sa pravasati iti prasiddham tatra atas saṃsarga mātram auśayika āmaya dhiṣṭhiteṣu vrīhi ādiṣu bhavati jaeḥ mukhya artha tvam pratibrūyāt upabhoga sthāa tvam ca sthāvara bhāvasya ca vayam upabhoga sthāa tvam sthāvara bhāvasya avajāīmahe bhavatu ayeṣām sthāvara bhāvam upagatāām etat upabhoga sthāam sthāvara bhāvam upagatāām etat upabhoga sthāam sthāvara bhāvam upabhuñjataḥ iti ācakṣmahe aśuddham iti ce a śabdāt yat puar uktam paśu hiṃsā ādi yogāt aśuddham ādhvarikam karma tasya aiṣṭam api phalam avakalpate iti atas mukhyam vrīhi ādi jama astu tatra gauṇī kalpaā aarthikā iti tat parihriyate a śāstra hetu tvāt dharma adharma vijñāasya ayam dharmaḥ ayam adharmaḥ iti śāstram eva vijñāe kāraṇam ati idriya tvāt tayoḥ aiyata deśa kāla aimitta tvāt ca yasmin deśe kāle imitte ca yaḥ dharmaḥ uṣṭhīyate saḥ eva adharmaḥ bhavati śāstrāt ṛte dharma adharma viṣayam kasyacid asti śāstrāt ca hiṃsā augraha ādi ātmakaḥ jyotiṣṭomaḥ dharmaḥ iti avadhāritaḥ sa katham aśuddhaḥ iti śakyate vaktum hiṃs sarva iti śāstram eva bhūta viṣayām hiṃsām adharmaḥ iti avagamayati bāḍham utsargaḥ tu saḥ apavādaḥ yam ca agīṣomīyam paśum ālabheta iti utsarga apavādayoḥ ca vyavasthita viṣaya tvam tasmāt viśuddham karma vaidikam śiṣṭaiḥ ca tasya pratirūpam phalam jāti sthāvara tvam ca api bhavitum arhati tat hi ucyate iha vaiśeṣikaḥ kaścid sti atas vrīhi ādi saṃśleṣa mātram tad bhāva iti upacaryate retaḥ sic yogothaḥ itas ca vrīhi ādi saṃśleṣa mātram tad bhāvaḥ yat kāraṇam retaḥ sic bhāvaḥ āmāyate yaḥ yaḥ yaḥ retaḥ siñcati tat bhūyas eva bhavati iti a ca atra mukhyaḥ retaḥ sic bhāvaḥ saṃbhavati cira jātaḥ hi prāpta yauvaḥ retaḥ sic bhavati katham iva aupacaritam tad bhāvam pratipadyate tatra tāvat avaśyam retaḥ sic yogaḥ eva retaḥ sic bhāvaḥ abhyupagatavyaḥ tadvat vrīhi ādi bhāvaḥ api vrīhi ādi yogaḥ eva iti avirodhaḥ śarīram atha retaḥ sigbhāvasya ataram yoau retasi śarīram auśayiām auśaya phala upabhogāya jāyate iti āha śāstram tat ye iha ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ ityādi tasmāt api avagamyate āvarohe brāhya ādi bhāva avasare tat śarīram eva sukha duḥkha āvitam bhavati iti tasmāt vrīhi ādi saṃśleṣa mātram auśayiām siddham iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye tṛtīya adhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ tṛtīyaḥ udhyāyaḥ dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ sadhye sṛṣṭiḥ āha hi saṃdhyā adhikaraṇam saṃdhye sṛṣṭiḥ iti saṃdhyam iti su apasthāam ācaṣṭe vede prayoga darśaāt saṃdhyam iti dvayoḥ loka sthāayoḥ prabodha saṃprasāda sthāayoḥ vā saṃdhau bhavati iti saṃdhyam tasmin saṃdhye tathya rūpā eva sṛṣṭiḥ bhavitum arhati kutas yatas pramāṇa bhūtā śrutiḥ evam āha atha sṛjate ityādi sa hi kartā iti ca upasaṃhārāt evam eva avagamyate ca eke putra ādayaḥ ca api ca eke śākhiaḥ asmin eva saṃdhye sthāe yaḥ eṣa supteṣu jāgarti kāmam kāmam puruṣaḥ iti putra ādayaḥ ca tatra kāmāḥ abhipreyate kāmyate iti eva ucyera a śata āyuṣaḥ putra pautra vṛṇīṣva iti prakṛtya tvā kāma bhājam karomi iti prakṛteṣu tatra tatra putra ādiṣu kāma śabdasya prayukta tvāt prājñam prakaraṇa vākyaśeṣābhyām pratīmaḥ prājñasya hi idam prakaraṇam ayatra dharmāt ayatra adharmāt ityādi tad viṣayaḥ eva ca vākyaśeṣaḥ api tat eva śukram tat brahma tat eva amṛtam ucyate tasimat lokāḥ śritāḥ sarve tat u ātyeti kaḥ ca iti prājña kartṛkā ca sṛṣṭiḥ tathya rūpā samadhigatā jāgarita āśrayā tathā svapā āśrayā api sṛṣṭiḥ bhavitum arhati tathā ca śrutiḥ atha u khalu āhuḥ jāgarita deśe eva asya eṣa iti suptaḥ iti svapa jāgaritayoḥ samāayāyatām śrāvayati tasmāt tathya rūpā eva saṃdhye sṛṣṭiḥ iti evam prāpte pratyāha māyā mātram tu kārtsyeā abhivyakta sva rūpa tvāt tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati ā etat asti yat uktam saṃdhye sṛṣṭiḥ pāramārthikī iti māyā eva saṃdhye sṛṣṭiḥ kutas kārtsyeā abhivyakta sva rūpa tvāt a hi paramārtha vastu dharmeṇa abhivyakta svarūpaḥ svapaḥ kim puaratra kārtsyam abhipretam deśa kā laimitta saṃpattiḥ abādhaḥ ca a hi paramārtha vastu viṣayāṇi abādhaḥ ca svape saṃbhāvyate a tāvat svape ratha ādīām ucitaḥ deśaḥ saṃbhavati a hi saṃvṛte deha deśe ratha ādayaḥ vakāśam labhera syāt etat bahis dehāt svapam drakṣyati deśa ātarita dravya grahaṇāt
