darśayati ca śrutiḥ bahis dehāt svapam bahis kulāyāt amṛtaḥ caritvā saḥ īyate mṛtaḥ yatra kāmam iti sthiti gati pratyaya bhedaḥ ca a aiṣkrāte jatau sāmañjasyam aśuvīta iti ā iti ucyate a hi suptasya jatoḥ kṣaṇa mātreṇa deśam paryetum viparyetum ca tatas sāmarthyam saṃbhāvyate kvacid ca pratyāgama avarjitam svapam śrāvayati kuruṣu aham adya idrayā abhiplutaḥ svape pañcālāḥ abhigataḥ ca asmi pratibuddhaḥ ca iti dehāt ced apeyāt pañcāleṣu eva pratibudhyeta tāḥ asau abhigataḥ iti kuruṣu eva tu pratibudhyate ca ayam tamaye pārśvasthāḥ śaya adeśe eva paśyati ca ayam deśātarāṇi svape paśyati tathābhūtāya iva bhavati paridhāvan ced paśyet jāgrat vat vastu bhūtam artham ākalayet darśayati ca śrutiḥ atas eva dehe svapam sa yatra etat svapyayā carati iti upakramya sve śarīre yathākāmam parivartate iti atas ca śruti upapatti virodhāt bahis kulāya śrutiḥ gauṇī vyākhyātavyā bahis iva kulāyāt amṛtaḥ caritvā iti yaḥ hi śarīre karoti sa bahis iva śarīrāt bhavati iti sthiti gati pratyaya bhedaḥ upi evam sati vipralambha eva abhyupagatavyaḥ kāla visaṃvādaḥ api ca svape bhavati rajayām suptaḥ vāsaram bhārate varṣe tathā svape kadācid bahū varṣa pūgāḥ ativāhayati ca svape a buddhaye karmaṇe vā ucita vidyate karaṇa upasaṃhārāt hi asya aśva ratha ādi grahaṇāya cakṣuḥ ādīi sati kutas asya imeṣa mātreṇa sāmarthyam dārūṇi vā bādhyate ca ete ratha aśva ādayaḥ svapa dṛṣṭāḥ prabodhe svape eva ca ete sulabha bādhā bhavati ādya tayoḥ vyabhicāra darśaāt rathaḥ yam iti hi kadācid svape mauṣyaḥ saṃpadyate mauṣyaḥ yam iti vṛkṣaḥ spaṣṭam ca abhāvam ratha ādīām svape śrāvayati śāstram a tatra rathāḥ a ratha yogāḥ bhavati ityādi sūcakaḥ ca hi śruteḥ ācakṣate ca tad vidaḥ māyā mātra tvāt tarhi a kaścid svape ā iti ā iti ucyate sūcakaḥ ca hi svapaḥ bhavati bhaviṣyatoḥ sādhu asādhuoḥ tathā hi śrūyate yadā karmasu kāmyeṣu striyam svapeṣu paśyati samṛddhim tatra iti tathāpuruṣam kṛṣṇam kṛṣṇa datam paśyati iti evamādibhiḥ svapaiḥ acirajīvi tvam āvedyate iti śrāvayati ācakṣate ca svapa adhyāya vidaḥ svape dhayāi iti matra devatā dravya viśeṣa aimittāḥ ca kecid svapāḥ bhavati iti tatra api bhavatu satya tvam sūcakasya tu strī darśa ādeḥ bhavati eva vaitathyam bādhyamāa tvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ tasmāt svapasya māyā mātra tvam yat uktam āha hi iti tat evam sati bhāktam vyākhyātavyam yathā lāṅgalam iti imitta mātra tvāt evam ucyate a tu pratyakṣam eva lāṅgalam evam imitta mātra tvāt suptaḥ ratha ādī sṛjate sa hi kartā iti ca ucyate a tu pratyakṣam eva suptaḥ ratha ādī sṛjati imitta tvam tu asya sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ vaktavyam api ca jāgarite viṣaya idriya saṃyogāt āditya ādi jyotiḥ vyatikarāt ca ātmanaḥ svayam jyotiḥ tvam tat tatas syāt syāt tasmāt ratha ādi abhāva vacaam śrutyā ratha ādi sṛṣṭi vacaam tu bhaktyā iti vyākhyeyam vyākhyātam yat api uktam iti tat api asat vihatya svayam svea bhāsā svea jyotiṣā prasvapiti iti jīva vyāpāra śravaṇāt eṣa supteṣu jāgarti iti prasiddha auvādāt jīvaḥ eva ayam saṃkīrtyate tasya tu vākya śeṣeṇa tat eva śukram tat brahma iti jīva bhāvam vyāvartya brahma bhāvaḥ upadiśyate tat tvam asi ityādi vat iti a brahma prakaraṇam virudhyate a ca asmābhiḥ prājña vyāpāraḥ pratiṣidhyate tasya sarva īśvara tvāt sarvāsu api avasthāsu adhiṣṭhātṛ tva upapatteḥ pāramārthikaḥ tu saṃdhyā āśrayaḥ sargaḥ viyat ādi sarga vat iti etāvat pratipādyate ca viyat ādi sargasya api ātyatikam satya tvam asti pratipāditam hita daaya tvam ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhyaḥ iti atra samastasya prapañcasya māyā mātra tvam prāk tu brahma ātmatva darśaāt viyat ādi prapañcaḥ vyavasthita rūpaḥ bhavati saṃdhyā āśrayaḥ tu prapañcaḥ bādhyate iti atas vaiśeṣikam idam saṃdhyasya māyā mātra tvam uditam para abhidhyāāt tu tirohitam tatas hi asya atha api syāt parasya eva tāvat ātmā oṃśaḥ jīvaḥ ageḥ iva visphuliṅgaḥ tatra evam sati yathā agi visphuliṅgayoḥ daha aprakāśa aśaktī bhavataḥ evam jīva īśvarayoḥ api jñā aiśvarya śaktī tatas ca jīvasya jñā aiśvarya vaśāt sāṃkalpikī svape ratha ādi sṛṣṭiḥ bhaviṣyati iti atra ucyate sati api jīva īśvarayoḥ aṃśa aṃśi bhāve pratyakṣam eva jīvasya īśvara viparīta dharma tvam kim puar jīvasya īśvara samāa dharma tvam āsti eva a āsti eva vidyamāam api tat tirohitam avidyā ādi vyavadhāāt tat puas tirohitam sat parameśvaram abhidhyāyataḥ jatoḥ vidhūta dhvātasya timira tiraskṛtā iva dṛkśaktiḥ auṣadha vīryāt īśvara prasādāt saṃsiddhasya kasyacid eva āvirbhavati a svabhāvataḥ eva sarveṣām kutas tatas hi īśvarāt hetoḥ asya jīvasya badha mokṣau bhavataḥ īśvara sva rūpa aparijñāāt badhaḥ tad sva rūpa parijñāāt tu mokṣaḥ tathā ca śrutiḥ jñātvā devam sarva pāśa apahāiḥ kṣīṇaiḥ kleśaiḥ jama mṛtyu prahāṇiḥ tasya abhidhyāāt tṛtīyam dehabhede viśva aiśvaryam kevalaḥ āpta kāmaḥ iti evamādyā deha yogāt vā saḥ pi kasmāt puar jīvaḥ paramātma aṃśaḥ eva sa tiraskṛta jñā aiśvaryaḥ bhavati yuktam tu jñā aiśvaryayoḥ atiraskṛta tvam visphuliṅgasya iva iti ucyate satyam eva etat saḥ api tu jīvasya jñā aiśvarya tirobhāvaḥ deha yogāt deha idriya maaḥ buddhi viṣaya veda ādi yogāt bhavati asti ca atra upamā yathā ageḥ daha aprakāśa saṃpaasya api araṇi gatasya tirohite bhavataḥ yathā vā bhasmacchaasya evam avidyā pratyupasthāpita āma rūpa kṛta deha ādi upādhi yogāt tad aviveka bhrama kṛtaḥ jīvasya jñā aiśvarya tirobhāvaḥ vā śabdaḥ jīvasya īśvarāt avayaḥ eva jīvaḥ īśvarāt astu tiraskṛta jñā aiśvarya tvāt kim hi jīvasya īśvarāt upapadyate sā iyam devatā aikṣata iti upakramya iti ātma śabde jīvasya parāmarśāt tat satyam saḥ ātmā tattvam asi śvetaketo iti ca jīvāya upadiśati īśvara ātma tvam atas eva īśvarāt jīvaḥ sa deha yogāt tirohita jñā aiśvaryaḥ bhavati atas ca a sāṃkalpikī jīvasya svape ratha ādi sṛṣṭiḥ ghaṭate yadi ca sāṃkalpikī svape ratha ādi sṛṣṭiḥ syāt aiva aiṣṭam kaścid svapam paśyet hi kaścid aiṣṭam saṃkalpayate yat puaruktam jāgarita deśa śrutiḥ svapasya satya tvam khyāpayati iti satya tva abhiprāyam svayaṃjyotiṣṭva virodhāt śrutyā eva ca svape ratha ādi abhāvasya darśita tvāt svapasya tad tulyaiḥ bhāsa tva abhiprāyam tat tasmāt upapaam svapasya māyā mātra tvam tad abhāvaḥ ca tad abhāva adhikaraṇam svapa avasthā parīkṣitā suṣupta avasthā idāīm parīkṣyate tatra etāḥ suṣupta viṣayāḥ śrutayaḥ bhavati kvacid śrūyate tat yatra etat suptaḥ samastaḥ tadā āḍīṣu sṛptaḥ bhavati iti a yatra tu āḍīḥ eva ā ukramya śrūyate tābhiḥ pratyavasṛpya purītati śete iti tathā a yatra āḍīḥ eva ā ukramya tāsu tadā bhavati yadā suptaḥ svapam a kaṃcaa paśyati atha asmi prāṇaḥ eva ekadhā bhavati iti tathā yatra yaḥ eṣa utar hṛdaye ākāśaḥ tasmin śete iti tathā yatra satā somya tadā saṃpaaḥ bhavati svam api itas bhavati iti tathā saṃpariṣvaktaḥ a bāhyam kiṃca a veda ātaram iti ca tatra saṃśayaḥ kim parasparaiḥ apekṣa tayā suṣupti sthāam āhosvit paraspara apekṣa tayā ekam suṣupti sthāam iti kim tāvat prāptam iti kutas eka artha tvāt hi kvacid paraspara apekṣa tvam dṛśyate vrīhi yava ādīām āḍī ādīām ca eka artha tā suṣuptau dṛśyate āḍīṣu sṛptaḥ bhavati purītati śete iti ca tatra tatra saptamībhiḥ nirdeśasya tulya tvāt sati saptamīirdeśaḥ dṛśyate satā somya tadā bhavati iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ tatra api saptamī arthasya vākyaśeṣaḥ hi tatra āyataaiṣī jīvaḥ sat upasarpati iti āha prāṇam eva upaśrayate iti tatra prakṛtasya sataḥ upādāāt ca saptamī arthaḥ tatra vākyaśeṣe dṛśyate sati saṃpadya viduḥ sati saṃpadyāmahe iti sarvatra ca viśeṣa vijñā uparama lakṣaṇam suṣuptam viśiṣyate tasmāt eka artha tvāt vikalpea kadācid svāpāya upasarpati iti evam prāpte pratipādyate tad abhāvaḥ āḍīṣu ātmai ca iti tad abhāvaḥ iti tasya prakṛtasya svapa darśaasya abhāvaḥ suṣuptam iti arthaḥ āḍīṣu ca iti samuccayea svāpāya upasarpati iti arthaḥ kutas tad śruteḥ tathā hi sarveṣām eva tatra tatra suṣupti sthāa tvam śrūyate tat ca samuccaye saṃgṛhītam bhavati vikalpe hi eṣām pakṣe bādhaḥ syāt eka artha tvāt vikalpaḥ vrīhi yava ādi vat iti uktam hi eka vibhakti irdeśa mātreṇa eka artha tvam vikalpaḥ ca āpatati ā ārtha tva samuccayayoḥ api eka vibhakti irdeśa darśaāt prāsāde śete paryaṅke śete iti evamādiṣu tathā iha api āḍīṣu purītati brahmaṇi ca svapiti iti upapadyate samuccayaḥ tathā ca śrutiḥ tāsu tadā bhavati yadā suptaḥ paśyati atha asmi prāṇaḥ eva ekadhā bhavati iti samuccayam prāṇasya ca suṣuptau śrāvayati eka vākya upādāāt prāṇasya ca brahmatvam samadhigatam prāṇaḥ tathā āugamāt iti atra yatra api iva āḍīḥ śrāvayati āsu tadā āḍīṣu sṛptaḥ bhavati iti tatra api pradeśa atara prasiddhasya brahmaṇā upratiṣedhāt āḍī dvāreṇa brahmaṇi eva avatiṣṭhate iti pratīyate ca evam api āḍīṣu saptamī virudhyate āḍībhiḥ api brahma upasarpa sṛptaḥ eva āḍīṣu bhavati yaḥ hi gaṅgayā sāgaram gacchati gataḥ eva sa gaṅgāyām bhavati bhavati ca atra raśmi āḍī dvāra ātmakasya brahmaloka mārgasya vivakṣita tvāt āḍī stuti artham āḍīṣu sṛptaḥ bhavati iti uktvā ataṃ a kaḥ ca a pāpmā spṛśati iti bruva āḍīḥ praśaṃsati bravīti ca pāpma sparśa abhāve hetum tejasā hi tadā saṃpaaḥ bhavati iti tejasā āḍī gate a pitta ākhye a abhivyāpta karaṇaḥ a bāhyā viṣayaḥ īkṣate iti arthaḥ athavā tejasā iti brahmaṇaḥ eva ayam irdeśaḥ śrutyatare brahma eva tejaḥ eva iti tejaḥ śabdasya brahmaṇi prayukta tvāt brahmaṇā hi tadā bhavati āḍī dvāreṇa atas tam pāpmā spṛśati iti arthaḥ brahma saṃpattiḥ ca pāpma sparśa abhāve hetuḥ samadhigataḥ sarve brahmaṇā samuccayaḥ samadhigataḥ bhavati tathā purītataḥ api brahma prakriyāyām tad auguṇam eva suṣupti sthāa tvam jñāyate yaḥ eṣa utar hṛdaye ākāśaḥ tasmin śete iti hṛdaya ākāśe suṣupti sthāe prakṛte idam ucyate purītati śete iti purītat iti hṛdaya pariveṣṭaam ucyate hṛdaya ākāśe śakyate purītati śete iti vaktum prākāra parikṣipte api hi pure prākāre vartate iti ucyate hṛdaya ākāśasya ca brahmatvam samadhigatam dahara uttarebhyaḥ iti atra tathā āḍī purītat samuccaya upitābhiḥ pratyavasṛpya purītati śete iti eka vākya upādāāt avagamyate sat prājñayoḥ ca prasiddham eva brahma tvam evam etāsu śrutiṣu trīṇi eva suṣupti sthāāi saṃkīrtitāi āḍyaḥ purītat brahma ca iti tatra api dvāra mātram āḍyaḥ purītat ca brahmā eva tu ekam apāyi suṣupti sthāam api ca āḍyaḥ purītat vā jīvasya upādhi ādhāraḥ eva bhavati tatra asya iti svatas eva jīvasya ādhāraḥ kaścid saṃbhavati brahma a vyatirekeṇa sva mahima pratiṣṭhita tvāt brahma ādhāra tvam api asya suṣupte ā eva ādhāra ādheya bheda abhiprāyeṇa ucyate katham tarhi tādātmya abhiprāyeṇa yatas āha satā somya tadā saṃpaaḥ bhavati svam api itas bhavati iti sva śabde ātmā abhilapyate sva rūpam āpaḥ suptaḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ api ca a kadācid jīvasya brahmaṇā saṃpattiḥ āsti sva rūpasya a apāyi tvāt svapa jāgaritayoḥ tu upādhi saṃparka vaśāt para rūpa āpattim iva apekṣya tad upaśamāt suṣupteḥ sva rūpa āpattiḥ vivakṣyate svam api itas bhavati iti atas ca supta avasthāyām kadācid satā saṃpadyate saṃpadyate iti ayuktam api ca viśeṣa vijñā upaśama lakṣaṇam tāvat suṣuptam kvacid viśiṣyate tatra sati saṃpaaḥ tāvat ekatvāt yuktam tat kam iti śruteḥ āḍīṣu purītati ca a kiṃcid avijñāe kāraṇam śakyam vijñātum bheda viṣaya tvāt yatra vā ayat iva syāt tatra ayaḥ yat paśyet iti śruteḥ bheda viṣayasya api ati dūra ādi kāraṇam avijñāe syāt bāḍham evam syāt yadi jīvaḥ svatas a abhyupagamyeta yathā viṣṇumitraḥ pravāsī sva gṛhāḥ tu jīvasya upādhi vyatirekeṇa paricchedaḥ vidyate upādhi gatam eva ati dūra ādi kāraṇam iti yadi ucyeta tathā api upādheḥ upaśāta tvāt satī eva yuktam a ca vayam iha tulya vat āḍi ādi samuccayam pratipādayāmaḥ hi āḍyaḥ purītat ca hi etat vijñāa pratibaddham kiṃcid phalam śrūyate phalavataḥ kasyacid aṅgam upadiśyate brahma tu supti sthāam iti etat pratipādayāmaḥ tu tu jīvasya brahma ātmatva avadhāraṇam ca tasmāt ātmā eva supti sthāam atas prabodhaḥ usmāt yasmāt ca ātmā eva atas eva ca kāraṇāt asmāt ātmaaḥ prabodhaḥ svāpa adhikāre śiṣyate kutas etat āgāt ityasya praśasya prativacaḥ avasare yathā āgeḥ kṣudrā visphuliṅgāḥ vyuccarati evam eva asmāt ātmaaḥ sarve prāṇāḥ āgamya a viduḥ sataḥ āgacchāmahe iti ca tu suṣupti sthāeṣu pratibudhyate kadācid purītataḥ kadācid ātmaaḥ iti aśāsiṣyat tasmāt api ātmā eva supti sthāam iti saḥ eva tu karma ausmṛti śabda vidhibhyaḥ tasyāḥ puas sat saṃpatteḥ pratibudhyamānaḥ kim yaḥ eva sat saṃpaaḥ saḥ eva pratibudhyate uta saḥ vā ayaḥ vā iti cityate tatra prāptam tāvat aiyamaḥ iti kutas yadā hi jala rāśau kaścid jalabiduḥ prakṣipyate jala rāśiḥ eva sa tadā bhavati puas uddharaṇe ca saḥ eva jalabiduḥ bhavati iti duḥsaṃpādam tadvat suptaḥ pareṇa ekatvam āpaḥ saṃprasīdati iti a saḥ eva puas utthātum arhati tasmāt saḥ eva īśvaraḥ vā ayaḥ vā jīvaḥ pratibudhyate iti evam prāpte idam āha saḥ eva tu jīvaḥ suptaḥ svāsthyam gataḥ puar uttiṣṭhati āyaḥ kasmāt karma ausmṛti śabda vidhibhyaḥ vibhajya hetum darśayiṣyāmi tāvat saḥ eva utthātum arhati āyaḥ tathā hi karmaṇaḥ aparedyus karmaṇaḥ aparedyus sāmikṛtasya karmaṇaḥ ayaḥ śeṣa kriyāyām pravartitum utsahate atiprasaṅgāt tasmāt eka anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya anya any eva pūrvedyus aparedyus ca ekasya karmaṇaḥ kartā iti gamyate itas ca saḥ eva uttiṣṭhati yat kāraṇam aham adaḥ drākṣam iti pūrva au bhūtasya paścāt smaraṇam opapadyate saḥ ham asmi iti ca śabdebhyaḥ ca tasya eva utthāam avagamyate tathā hi puaḥ pratiyāyam pratiyoyā dravati etam brahma lokam iha vā siṃhaḥ vā vṛkaḥ vā varāhaḥ vā kīṭaḥ vā pataṅgaḥ vā daṃśaḥ vā maśakaḥ vā yat yat bhavati tadā bhavati iti evamādayaḥ śabdāḥ svāpa prabodha adhikāra paṭhitā sāmañjasyam īyuḥ karma vidyā vidhibhyaḥ ca evam eva avagamyate ayathā hi syuḥ hi supta mātraḥ mucyate iti āpadyeta evam ced syāt vada kim karmaṇā vidyayā vā kṛtam syāt api ca yadi tāvat śarīra atare vyavaharamāṇaḥ jīvaḥ uttiṣṭhet tatratya vyavahāra lopa prasaṅgaḥ syāt atha tatra suptaḥ uttiṣṭhet kalpa āarthakyam syāt yaḥ hi yasmi śarīre suptaḥ saḥ tasmi ā uttiṣṭhati śarīre suptaḥ śarīre uttiṣṭhati iti kaḥ syāt atha muktaḥ uttiṣṭhet āpadyeta ca puas utthāam aupapaam īśvarasya utthāam pratyuktam iti aivṛtta avidya tvāt akṛta abhyāgama kṛta vipraṇāśau ca syātām tasmāt saḥ eva uttiṣṭhati āyaḥ iti yat puas uktam yathā jala rāśau jala bidurā uddhartum śakyate evam sati jīvaḥ otpatitum arhati iti tat parihriyate yuktam tatra viveka kāraṇa abhāvāt jala bidoḥ auddharaṇam iha tu vidyate viveka kāraṇam karma ca avidyā ca iti vaiṣamyam dṛśyate ca durvivecayoḥ api asmad jātīyaiḥ kṣīra udakayoḥ saṃsṛṣṭayoḥ api ca a jīvaḥ vidyate yaḥ jalabiduḥ iva jalarāśeḥ vivicyeta sat eva tu upādhi saṃparkāt jīvaḥ iti upacaryate iti asakṛt prapañcitam evam sati yāvat eka upādhi gatā tāvat eka jīva vyavahāraḥ upādhi atara gatāyām tu iti atas saḥ eva jīvaḥ pratibudhyate iti yuktam mugdheḥ ṛdha sampattiḥ pariśeṣāt mugdha adhikaraṇam asti yam mūrchitaḥ iti laukikāḥ kathayati sa tu kimavasthaḥ iti parīkṣāyām ucyate tisraḥ tāvat avasthāḥ śarīra sthasya jīvasya prasiddhāḥ jāgaritam svapaḥ suṣuptam iti caturthī śarīrāt apasṛptiḥ a tu pañcamī kācid avasthā jīvasya śrutau smṛtau vā prasiddhā asti tasmāt catasṛṇām eva avasthāām ayatamā avasthā mūrchā iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ jāgarita avasthaḥ bhavitum arhati a hi ayam idriyaiḥ viṣayāḥ īkṣate syāt etat mugdhaḥ bhaviṣyati yathā iṣukāraḥ jāgrat api viṣayāḥ īkṣate evam mugdhaḥ jāgrat api āyāḥ viṣayāḥ īkṣate iti a iṣukāraḥ hi bravīti iṣum eva aham etāvatam kālam bhūvam iti mugdhaḥ tu labdha saṃjñaḥ bravīti tamasi aham etāvatam kālam prakṣiptaḥ bhūvam a kiṃci mayā cetitam iti jāgrataḥ ca eka viṣaya viṣakta cetasaḥ dehaḥ vidhriyate mugdhasya tu dehaḥ dharaṇyām patati tasmai jāgarti ā api svapā paśyati mṛtaḥ prāṇa ūṣmaṇoḥ bhāvāt mugdhe hi jatau mṛtaḥ yam syāa vā mṛtaḥ iti saṃśayāḥ ūṣmā asti āsti iti hṛdaya deśam ālabhate iścaya artham prāṇaḥ usti āsti iti ca āsikā deśam yadi prāṇa ūṣmaṇoḥ astitvam āvagacchati tatas mṛtaḥ yam iti adhyavasāya dahaāya araṇyam ayati atha tu prāṇam ūṣmāṇam vā pratipadyate ā ayam mṛtaḥ iti adhyavasāya saṃjñā lābhāya bhiṣajyati a diṣṭam gataḥ a hi yamam gataḥ yama rāṣṭrāt pratyāgacchati astu tarhi suṣuptaḥ a saṃjñā tvāt amṛta tvāt ca a vailakṣaṇyāt mugdhaḥ kadācid ciram api occhvasiti sa vepathuḥ asya dehaḥ bhavati ca ca visphārite etre suṣuptaḥ tu tulya kālam puas puas ucchvasiti imīlite asya etre bhavataḥ ca asya dehaḥ vepate pāṇi peṣaṇa mātreṇa ca suṣuptam utthāpayati a tu mugdham imitta bhedaḥ ca bhavati moha svāpayoḥ musala saṃpāta ādi imitta tva amohasya śrama aimitta tvāt ca svāpasya ca prasiddhiḥ mugdhaḥ suptaḥ iti pariśeṣāt ardha saṃpattiḥ mugdha tā iti avagacchāmaḥ iti katham puar ardha saṃpattiḥ mugdha tā iti śakyate vaktum yāvatā suptam prati tāvat uktam śrutyā satā somya tadā saṃpaaḥ bhavati iti atra steoḥ teo bhavati ai tam setum ahar rātre tarataḥ a jarā a mṛtyuḥ a śokaḥ a sukṛtam a duṣkṛtam ityādi jīve hi sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ prāptiḥ bhavati ca sukhi tva pratyayaḥ duḥkhi tva pratyayaḥ vā suṣupte vidyate mugdhe api tau pratyayau vidyete tasmāt upādhi upaśamāt kṛtsa saṃpattiḥ eva bhavitum arhati ārdha saṃpattiḥ iti atra ucyate brūmaḥ brūmaḥ mugdheḥ ṛdha saṃpattiḥ jīvasya brahmaṇā bhavati iti kim tarhi suṣupta pakṣasya bhavati mugdha tvam iti brūmaḥ darśite ca mohasya sāmya vaiṣamye dvāram ca etat maraṇasya yadā asya sa avaśeṣam karma bhavati tadā vāc maase pratyāgacchataḥ yadā tu karma bhavati tadā prāṇa ūṣmāṇau apagacchataḥ tasmāt ardha saṃpattim brahma vidaḥ icchati yat tu uktam a pañcamī kācid avasthā prasiddhā asti iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ kādācitkīyam avasthā iti a prasiddhā syāt prasiddhā ca eṣā loka āyurvedayoḥ ardha saṃpatti abhyupagamāt ca a pañcamī gaṇyate iti aavadyam parasya ubhaya liṅgam sarvatra hi ubhaya liṅga adhikaraṇam brahmaṇā suṣupti ādiṣu jīvaḥ upādhi upaśamāt saṃpadyate tasya idāīm svarūpam satī ubhaya liṅgāḥ śrutayaḥ brahma viṣayāḥ sarva karmā sarva kāmaḥ sarva gadhaḥ sarva rasaḥ iti evamādyāḥ sa viśeṣa liṅgāḥ asthūlam a aṇu a hrasvam adīrgham iti evamādyāḥ ca iḥ viśeṣa liṅgāḥ kim āsu śrutiṣu ubhaya liṅgam brahma pratipattavyam uttāyatara liṅgam yadā api ayatara liṅgam tadā api sa viśeṣam uta irviśeṣam iti mīmāṃsyate tatra ubhaya liṅga śruti augrahāt ubhaya liṅgam eva brahma iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ a tāvat svatas eva parasya brahmaṇaḥ ubhaya liṅga tvam upapadyate a hi ekam vastu svatas eva rūpa ādi viśeṣa upetam tad viparītam ca iti avadhārayitum śakyam virodhāt astu tarhi pṛthivī ādi upādhi yogāt iti tat api upapadyate hi upādhi yogāt api ayādṛśasya svabhāvaḥ saṃbhavati a hi svacchaḥ sa sphaṭikaḥ alaktaka ādi upādhi yogāt asvacchaḥ bhavati bhrama mātra tvāt asvaccha tā abhi iva īśasya ca avidyā pratyupasthāpita tvāt atas ca samasta viśeṣa rahitam brahma pratipattavyam a tad viparītam sarvatra hi brahma svarūpa pratipāda apareṣu vākyeṣu aśabdam asparśam arūpam avyayam iti evamādiṣu apāsta samasta viśeṣam eva brahma upadiśyate a bhedāt iti cea atha api syāt yat uktam svatas vai ubhaya liṅga tvam asti iti kasmāt bhedāt hi pratividyam brahmaṇaḥ ākārāḥ upadiśyate catuṣpād brahma ṣoḍaśa kalam brahma vāmaī tva ādi lakṣaṇam brahma trailokya śarīra vaiśvāara śabda uditam brahma iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ tasmāt sa viśeṣa tvam api brahmaṇā abhyupagatavyam uktam obhaya liṅga tvam brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhavati iti ayam api avirodhaḥ upādhi kṛta tvāt ākāra bhedasya ayathā hi bheda śāstram prasajyeta iti ced ā iti brūmaḥ kasmāt pratyekam atadvacaāt prati upādhi bhedam hi abhedam eva brahmaṇaḥ śrāvayati śāstram yaḥ ca ayam asyām pṛthivyām tejaḥ mayaḥ umṛta mayaḥ puruṣaḥ yaḥ ca ayam adhyātmam śārīraḥ tejaḥ mayaḥ umṛta mayaḥ puruṣaḥ yam eva sa yaḥ yam ātmā ityādi atas ca a bhiākāra yogaḥ brahmaṇaḥ śāstrīyaḥ iti śakyate vaktum bhedasya upāsa artha tvāt abhede tātparyāt api ca evam eke api ca evam eke eke bhoktā bhogyam preritāram ca matvā sarvam proktam trividham brahma me tat iti samastasya bhogya bhoktṛ iyatṛ lakṣaṇasya prapañcasya brahma eka svabhāva tām adhīyate katham ākāravat upadeśiīṣu a ākāra upadeśiīṣu ca brahma viṣayāsu śrutiṣu satīṣu a ākāram eva brahma avadhāryate iti atas uttaram paṭhati arūpavat eva hi rūpa ādi ākāra rahitam eva hi brahma avadhārayitavyam a rūpa ādimat kasmāt tat pradhā a tvāt sthūlam a aṇu a hrasvam adīrgham aśabdam asparśam arūpam avyayam ākāśaḥ vai āmaḥ āma rūpayoḥ te yat atarā tat brahma divyaḥ hi amūrtaḥ puruṣaḥ hi ajaḥ tat etat brahma apūrvam aaparam aataram abāhyam ayam ātmā brahma iti evamādīi vākyāi artha atara pradhāāi iti etat pratiṣṭhāpitam tat tu iti atra tasmāt evaṃjātīyakeṣu vākyeṣu yathāśrutam irā ākāram eva brahma avadhārayitavyam itarāṇi tu ākāravat brahma viṣayāṇi hi tāi teṣu asati virodhe yathāśrutam āśrayitavyam sati tu virodhe bhavati iti eṣa viigamaāyām hetuḥ ubhayīṣu api śrutiṣu satīṣu a ākāram eva brahma avadhāryate a puar viparītam iti kā tarhi ākāravat viṣayāṇām śrutīām gatiḥ iti atas āha prakāśavat ca a vaiyarthyāt yathā prakāśaḥ sauraḥ ca ādramasaḥ vā viyat vyāpya avatiṣṭhamānaḥ teṣu ṛju vakra ādi bhāvam tad bhāvam iva pratipadyate evam brahmā api tad ākāra tām iva pratipadyate tad ālambaḥ brahmaṇaḥ ākāra viśeṣa upadeśaḥ upāsa arthaḥ virudhyate evam a vaiyarthyam ākāravat brahma viṣayāṇām api vākyāām bhaviṣyati a hi veda vākyāām kasyacid arthavat tvam kasyacid aarthavat tvam iti yuktam pratipattum pramāṇa tva aviśeṣāt yat purastāt pratijñātam opādhi yogāt api ubhaya liṅga tvam brahmaṇoḥ ti iti tat virudhyate ā iti brūmaḥ upādhi nimittasya vastu dharma tva aupapatteḥ upādhīnām ca avidyā pratyupasthāpita tvāt satyām eva ca aisargikyām avidyāyām loka veda vyavahāra avatāraḥ iti tatra tatra avocāma āha ca ta mātram āha ca śrutiḥ caitaya mātram vilakṣaṇa rūpa atara rahitam brahma sa yathā kṛtsaḥ rasa ghaaḥ eva evam vā kṛtsaḥ prajñā aghaaḥ eva iti etat uktam bhavati āsye ātma otar bahis vā caitayādayat rūpam asti caitayam eva tu irataram asya svarūpam yathā saidhavaghaasya atas bahis ca lavaṇa rasaḥ eva irataraḥ bhavati a rasātaram tathā eva iti darśayati ca atho api smaryate darśayati ca śrutiḥ brahma brahma atha atas ādeśaḥ u eti eti ayat eva tat viditāt atha u a viditāt adhiyataḥ vācaḥ iva ārtate a prāpya maasā saha iti evamādyā ca bādhvaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ saḥ brahma provāca iti śrūyate sa ha uvāca adhīhi bho iti sa tūṣṇīm babhūva tam ha dvitīye tṛtīye vā vacaḥ uvāca brūmaḥ khalu tvam tu iti tathā smṛtiṣu api jñeyam yat tat pravakṣyāmi yat jñātvā amṛtam a ādimat param brahma a sattā asat ucyate iti evamādyāsu tathā viśva rūpa dharaḥ ārāyaṇaḥ āradam uvāca iti smaryate māyā hi eṣā mayā sṛṣṭā yamām paśyasi ārada sarva bhūta guṇaiḥ yuktam ā evam mām jñātum arhasi iti atas eva ca upamā sūryaka ādi vat yatas eva ca ayam ātmā vāc maasa atītaḥ para pratiṣedha upadeśyaḥ atas eva ca asya upādhi nimittām apāramārthikīm viśeṣavat tām abhipretya jala sūryaka ādi vat iti upamā upādīyate mokṣa śāstreṣu yathā hi ayam jyotiḥ ātmā vivasvā apaḥ kriyate bheda rūpaḥ devaḥ kṣetreṣu evam ajaḥ yam ātmā iti ekaḥ eva hi bhūtātmā bhūte bhūte vyavasthitaḥ ekadhā bahudhā ca eva dṛśyate jala cadravat iti ca evamādiṣu atra pratyavasthīyate ambu vat agrahaṇāt tu a tathātvam a jala sūryaka ādi tulya tvam iha upapadyate tadvat agrahaṇāt sūrya ādibhyaḥ hi mūrtebhyaḥ pṛthak bhūtam viprakṛṣṭa deśam mūrtam jalam gṛhyate tatra yuktaḥ sūrya ādi pratibimba udayaḥ tu ātmā mūrtaḥ ca asmāt pṛthak bhūtāḥ viprakṛṣṭa deśāḥ ca upādhayaḥ sarvagata tvāt sarva āaya tvāt ca tasmāt ayuktaḥ yam dṛṣṭātaḥ iti atra pratividhīyate vṛddhi hrāsa bhāktva matarbhāvāt ubhaya sāmañjasyāt evam yuktaḥ eva tu ayam dṛṣṭātaḥ vivakṣita aṃśa saṃbhavāt hi dṛṣṭāta dārṣṭātikayoḥ kvacid kaṃcid vivakṣitam aṃśam muktvā sarva sārūpyam keacid darśayitum śakyate sarva sārūpye hi darśa āt ca darśayati ca śrutiḥ parasya eva brahmaṇaḥ deha ādiṣu upādhiṣu atarau praveśam puras cakre dvipadaḥ puras cakre catuṣpadaḥ puras sa pakṣī bhūtvā puras puruṣa āviśat iti ca tasmāt yuktam etat atas eva ca upamā sūryaka ādi vat iti tasmāt brahma ubhaya liṅgam viparīta liṅgam vā iti siddham atra kecid dve adhikaraṇe kalpayati prathamam tāvat kim pratyastamita aśeṣa prapañcam eka ākāram brahma uta prapañcavat a eka ākāra upetam iti dvitīyam tu pratyastamita prapañca tve kim sat lakṣaṇam brahma uta bodha lakṣaṇam uta ubhaya lakṣaṇam iti atra vayam vadāmaḥ sarvathā api āarthakyam adhikaraṇa atara ārambhasya iti yadi tāvat a eka liṅga tvam parasya brahmaṇaḥ irā kartavyam iti ayam prayāsaḥ tat irā kṛtam iti uttaram adhikaraṇam prakāśavat ca iti etat vyartham eva bhavet a bhavat ca sat lakṣaṇam eva brahma a bodha lakṣaṇam iti śakyam baktum eva ityādi śruti vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt katham vā brahma jīvasya ātmatveā upadiśyeta bodha lakṣaṇam eva brahma a sat lakṣaṇam iti śakyam vaktum asti iti eva upalabdhavyaḥ ityādi śruti vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt katham vā irasta sattākaḥ bodhaḥ abhyupagamyeta āpi ubhaya lakṣaṇam eva brahma iti śakyam vaktum pūrva abhyupagama virodha prasaṅgāt sattā vyāvṛttyā ca bodhe bodha vyāvṛttayā ca sattayā upetam brahma tat eva pūrva adhikaraṇa pratiṣiddham sa prapañca tvam prasajyeta śruta tvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced a ekasya a eka svabhāva tva aupapatteḥ atha sattā eṣa bodhaḥ bodhaḥ eva ca sattā paraspara vyāvṛttiḥ asti iti yadi ucyeta tathā api kim sat lakṣaṇam brahma uta bodha lakṣaṇam uta ubhaya lakṣaṇam iti ayam eva syāt sūtrāṇi api ca brahma viṣayāsu śrutiṣu a ākāre brahmaṇi parigṛhīte avaśyam vaktavyā itarāsām śrutīām gatiḥ sūtrāṇi arthavattarāṇi saṃpadyate yat api āhuḥ śrutayaḥ śrutayaḥ aākāra pratipatti arthāḥ eva a pṛthak arthāḥ iti tat api lakṣyate katham ye hi paravidyā adhikāre kecid prapañcāḥ ucyate yathā yuktāḥ hi asya harayaḥ śatā daśa iti ayam vai vai daśa ca sahasrāṇi ca iti evamādayaḥ te bhavatu pravilaya arthāḥ tat etat brahma apūrvam aaparam aataram abāhyam iti upasaṃhārāt ye ucyate yathā maomayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ bhā rūpaḥ iti evamādayaḥ teṣām pravilaya artha tvam kratum kurvīta iti evaṃjātīyake prakṛtea eva teṣām teṣām śrutyā ca evaṃjātīyakāām guṇāām lakṣaṇayā pravilaya artha tvam avakalpate sarveṣām ca sādhāraṇe pravilaya artha tve sati a rūpa vat eva hi tad pradhā tvāt iti syāt phalam api eṣām yathopadeśam kvacid durita kṣayaḥ kvacid aiśvairya prāptiḥ kvacid krama muktiḥ iti avagamyate eva iti atas pārthagarthyam eva brahma vākyāām ca yāyyam a ekavākyatvam katham ca eṣām ekavākyatā utprekṣyate iti vaktavyam eka eyoga pratīteḥ prayāja darśa pūrṇamāsa vākya vat iti ced a brahma vākyeṣu iyoga abhāvāt vastu mātra paryavasāyi iti hi iti etat vistareṇa pratiṣṭhāpitam tat tu iti atra kiṃviṣayaḥ ca atra iti vaktavyam puruṣaḥ hi iti sva vyāpāre dvaita prapañca pravilayaḥ bhaviṣyati apravilāpite hi dvaita prapañce brahma tattva ābodhaḥ bhavati iti atas brahma tattva avabodha pratyaīka bhūtaḥ dvaita prapañcaḥ pravilāpyaḥ yathā svarga kāmasya upadiśyate evam apavarga kāmasya prapañca pravilayaḥ yathā ca tamasi vyavasthitam ghaṭa ādi tattvam avabubhutsamāea tad pratyaīka bhūtam tamaḥ pravilāpyate evam brahma tattvam avabubhutsamāea tad pratyaīka bhūtaḥ prapañcaḥ pravilāpayitavyaḥ brahma svabhāvaḥ hi prapañcaḥ a prapañca svabhāvam brahma brahma tea brahma tattva avabodhaḥ bhavati iti atra vayam pṛcchāmaḥ kaḥ yam prapañca pravilayaḥ kimagi pratāpa saṃparkāt ghṛta kāṭhiya pravilayaḥ iva prapañca pravilayaḥ kartavyaḥ āhosvit ekasmin cadre avidyā kṛtaḥ brahmaṇi āma rūpa prapañcaḥ vidyayā pravilāpayitavyaḥ iti tatra yadi tāvat vidyamānaḥ ayam prapañcaḥ deha ādi lakṣaṇaḥ ādhyātmikaḥ bāhyaḥ ca pṛthivī ādi lakṣaṇaḥ pravilāpayitavyaḥ iti ucyeta sa puruṣa mātreṇa aśakyaḥ pravilāpayitum iti tad pravilaya upadeśa uśakya viṣayaḥ eva syāt ca pṛthivī ādi pravilayaḥ kṛtaḥ iti idāīm jagat abhaviṣyat atha avidyā adhyastaḥ brahmaṇi ekasmin ayam prapañcaḥ vidyayā pravilāpyate iti brūyāt tatas brahma eva āvedayitavyam ekam eva advitīyam brahma tat satyam saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi iti tasmin āvedite vidyā svayam eva utpadyate tayā ca avidyā bādhyate tatas ca avidyā adhyastaḥ sakalaḥ yam āma rūpa prapañcaḥ svapa prapañca vat pravilīyate a āvedite tu kuru prapañca pravilayam ca iti prapañca pravilayaḥ vā jāyeta brahmaṇi prapañca pravilayaḥ vā jāyeta brahmaṇi syāt ubhaya siddheḥ hi avidyā adhyasta sarpa ādi prapañca pravilayaḥ ca bhavati ca kṛtam eva kriyate ca prapañca avasthāyām sa prapañca pakṣasya eva vā syāt brahma pakṣasya eva vā prathame vikalpe pṛthivī ādi vat jīvasya api pravilāpita tvāt kasya prapañca vilaye iyogaḥ ucyeta kasya vā iyoga eṣṭha tayā mokṣaḥ uvāptavyaḥ ucyeta dvitīye api brahma eva aiyojya svabhāvam jīvasya svarūpam jīva tvam tu avidyā kṛtam eva iti pratipādite brahmaṇi iyojya abhāvāt iyoga abhāvaḥ eva draṣṭavya ādi śabdāḥ api paravidyā adhikāra paṭhitāḥ tattva abhimukhīkaraṇa pradhāāḥ a tattva avabodha vidhi pradhāāḥ bhavati loke pi idam paśya idam ākarṇaya iti ca evaṃjātīyakeṣu praṇidhā a mātram kuru iti ucyate a sākṣāt jñāam eva kuru iti jñeya abhimukhasya api jñāam kadācid jāyate jāyate tasmāt tam prati jñā a viṣayaḥ eva darśayitavyaḥ jñāpayitu kāmaḥ tasmin darśite svayam eva yathāviṣayam yathāpramāṇam ca jñāam utpadyate ca pramāṇa atareṇa ayathā prasiddha ṛthe ayathājñāam iyuktasya api upapadyate yadi ayathā jñāam kuryāt ayathā tu tat jñāam kim tarhi māasī sā kriyā svayam eva ced ayathā utpadyeta bhrātiḥ eva syāt tu pramāṇa jayam yathā bhūta viṣayam ca kārayitum śakyate ca vārayitum śakyate a hi tat puruṣa tatram vastu tatram eva hi tat atas api iyoga abhāvaḥ kiṃca ayat iyoga eṣṭha tayā eva paryavasyati ā māye yat abhyupagatam aiyojya brahma ātmatvam jīvasya tat apramāṇakam eva syāt atha śāstram eva aiyojya brahma ātmatvam ācakṣīta tad avabodhe ca puruṣam iyuñjīta tatas brahma śāstrasya ekasya dvi artha para tā viruddha artha para tā ca prasajyeyātām iyoga para tāyām ca śruta hāiḥ a śruta kalpaā ca iti evamādayaḥ doṣāḥ a keacid parihartum śakyāḥ tasmāt eva brahma vākyāi atas ca eka eyoga pratīteḥ ekavākya tā iti ayuktam ca brahma vākyeṣu iyoga sadbhāve tad ekatvam sa prapañca upadeśeṣu ca asiddham hi sarvatra ekaḥ iyogaḥ iti śakyam āśrayitum prayāja darśa pūrṇamāsa vākyeṣu tu adhikāra aṃśe ā bhedāt yuktam ekatvam a tu iha kaścid ekatva kara oṃśo asti hi bhā rūpa tva ādayaḥ guṇāḥ prapañca pravilaya upakāriṇaḥ prapañca vilayaḥ bhā rūpa tva ādi guṇa upakārī paraspara virodhi tvāt a hi prapañca eka deśa apekṣaṇam ca ekasmin dharmiṇi yuktam samāveśayitum tasmāt asmad uktaḥ eva vibhāgaḥ ākāravat a ākāra upadeśāām yuktataraḥ iti prakṛta etāvat tvam hi pratiṣedhati tatas bravīti ca bhūyas prakṛta etāvat tva adhikaraṇam dve vāva brahmaṇaḥ rūpe mūrtam ca eva amūrtam ca iti upakramya pañca mahābhūtāi pravibhajya amūrta rasasya ca puruṣa śabda uditasya rūpāṇi darśayitvā puas paṭhyate atha atas ādeśaḥ eti eti a hi etasmāt iti eti ayat param asti iti tatra kaḥ sya pratiṣedhasya viṣayaḥ iti jijñāsāmahe a hi atra idam tat iti viśeṣitam kiṃcid pratiṣedhyam upalabhyate tu atra pratiṣedhyam kim api samarpyate eti ā iti iti iti paratvāt añ prayogasya iti śabdaḥ ca ayam saṃihita ālambaḥ evaṃśabda sama a vṛttiḥ dṛśyate iti ha sma upādhyāyaḥ kathayati iti evamādiṣu saṃihitam ca atra prakaraṇa sāmarthyāt rūpa dvayam sa prapañcam brahmaṇaḥ tat ca brahma yasya te dve rūpe tatra saṃśayaḥ upajāyate kim ayam pratiṣedhaḥ rūpe rūpavat ca ubhayam api pratiṣedhati āhosvit ekataram yadā api ekataram tadā api kim brahma pratiṣedhati rūpe pariśiaṣṭi āhosvit rūpe pratiṣedhati brahma pariśiaṣṭi iti tatra prakṛta tva aviśeṣāt ubhayam api pratiṣedhati iti āśaṅkāmahe dvau ca etau pratiṣedhau dvis eti śabda prayogāt tayoḥ eke sa prapañcam brahmaṇaḥ rūpam pratiṣidhyate apareṇa rūpavat brahma iti bhavati matiḥ athavā brahma eva rūpavat pratiṣidhyate tat hi pratiṣedha arham tu rūpa prapañcaḥ pratyakṣa ādi gocara tvāt pratiṣedha arhaḥ abhyāsaḥ tu ādara arthaḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ a tāvat ubhaya pratiṣedhaḥ upapadyate śūya vāda prasaṅgāt kaṃcid hi paramārtham ālambya aparamārthaḥ pratiṣidhyate yathā rajju ādiṣu sarpa ādayaḥ tat ca pariśiṣyamāṇe kasmiṃścid bhāve avakalpate tu koyaḥ bhāvaḥ pariśiṣyeta a pariśiṣyamāṇe yaḥ itaraḥ pratiṣeddhum ārabhyate pratiṣeddhum aśakya tvāt tasya eva paramārtha tva āpatteḥ pratiṣedha aupapattiḥ brahma pratiṣedhaḥ upapadyate brahma te bravāṇi ityādi upakrama virodhāt asaḥ eva sa bhavati asat brahma iti veda ced ityādi idā virodhāt asti iti eva upalabdhavyaḥ ityādi avadhāraṇa virodhāt sarva veda atavya ākopa prasaṅgāt ca brahmaṇaḥ a abhāva abhiprāyeṇa abhidhīyate hi mahatā param satyam brahma iti evamādiāḥ brahma pratipādya tasya eva hi paṅkasya dūrāt asparśaam varam iti hi pratipāda a prakriyā tu eṣā yatas vācaḥ a ṛtate a prāpya saha iti etat uktam bhavati iti aśuddha buddha mukta svabhāvam brahma iti tasmāt brahmaṇaḥ rūpa prapañcam pratiṣedhati brahma iti avagatavyam tat etat ucyate prakṛta etāvattvam hi pratiṣedhati iti prakṛtam yat etāvat mūrta amūrta lakṣaṇam brahmaṇaḥ rūpam tat eṣa śabdaḥ pratiṣedhati tat hi prakṛtam prapañcitam ca pūrvasmin rathe adhidaivatam adhyātmam ca tat jaitam eva ca aparam rūpam amūrta rasa bhūtam puruṣa śabda uditam liṅga ātma vyapāśrayam māhāraja ādi upamābhiḥ darśitam amūrta rasasya puruṣasya cakṣuḥ grāhya rūpa yogi tva aupapatteḥ tat etat sa prapañcam brahmaṇaḥ rūpam pratiṣedhakam prati upaīyate iti gamyate brahma tu rūpa viśeṣaṇa tvea ṣaṣṭhyā prapañcite ca tadīye rūpa dvaye rūpavataḥ svarūpa jijñāsāyām idam upakrātam atha atas ādeśaḥ eti eti iti tatra brahmaṇaḥ tad āspadam hi idam samastam kāryam eti eti iti pratiṣiddham yuktam ca kāryasya tu brahmaṇaḥ sarva kalpa ā mūla tvāt ca atra iyam āśaṅkā kartavyā katham hi śāstram svayam eva brahmaṇaḥ rūpa dvayam darśayitvā svayam eva puas pratiṣedhati hi paṅkasya dūrāt asparśaam varam iti yatas brahmaṇaḥ rūpa dvayam irdiśati loka prasiddham tu idam rūpa dvayam brahmaṇi kalpitam parāmṛśati pratiṣedhya tvāya śuddhabrahma svarūpa pratipādaāya ca iti dvau ca etau pratiṣedhau dve api mūrta amūrte pratiṣedhataḥ yat vā pūrvaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ bhūta rāśim pratiṣedhati uttaraḥ vā asaā rāśim athavā eti eti iti vīpsā iyam iti iti yāvat kiṃcid utprekṣyate tat sarvam bhavati iti arthaḥ parigaṇita pratiṣedhe hi kriyamāṇe yadi kim ayat brahma bhavet iti jijñāsā syāt vīpsāyām tu satyām samastasya viṣaya jātasya pratiṣedhāt aviṣayaḥ pratyagātmā brahma iti jijñāsā iva ārtate tasmāt prapañcam eva brahmaṇi kalpitam pratiṣedhati pariśiaṣṭi brahma iti itas ca eṣaḥ eva yatas tatas prapañca pratiṣedhāt bhūyaḥ brahma bravīti ayat param asti iti hi pratiṣedhe kriyamāṇe kim ayat param asti iti brūyāt tatra eṣā eti eti iti brahma ādiśya tam eva ādeśam puariḥ vakti eti eti iti asya kaḥ ṛthaḥ a hi etasmāt brahmaṇaḥ vyatiriktam asti iti atas eti eti iti ucyate a svayam eva āsti iti arthaḥ tat ca darśayati ayatparam apratiṣiddham brahma asti iti yadā puar evam akṣarāṇi yojyate hi etasmāt iti aiti a iti prapañca pratiṣedha rūpāt ādeśaāt brahmaṇaḥ asti iti tadā tatas bravīti ca bhūyas iti etat āmadheya viṣayam yojayitavyam atha āmadheya satyasya satyam iti prāṇāḥ vai satyam teṣām eṣa satyam iti hi bravīti iti tat ca brahmāvasāe pratiṣedhe samañjasam bhavati abhāvāvasāe tu pratiṣedhe kim satyasya satyam iti ucyeta tasmāt brahmāvasāaḥ ayam pratiṣedhaḥ ābhāvāvasāaḥ iti adhyavasyāmaḥ tat avyaktam āha hi yat tat pratiṣiddhāt prapañca jātāt ayat param brahma tat asti ced kasmai gṛhyate iti ucyate tat avyakta maidriya grāhyam sarva dṛśya sākṣi tvāt āha hi evam śrutiḥ a cakṣuṣā gṛhyate vācā āyaiḥ devaiḥ tapasā karmaṇā vāsaḥ eṣaḥ eti eti ātmā a gṛhyaḥ hi gṛhyate yat tat a dreśyam a grāhyam yadā hi eva eṣa ityādyā smṛtiḥ api avyaktaḥ yam acityaḥ yam avikāryaḥ yam ucyate ityādyā api ca saṃrādhae api ca saṃrādha a kāle paśyati yogaḥ saṃrādha am ca katham katham katham katham saṃrādha a kāle paśyati iti vyatṛṇat svayaṃbhūḥ tasmāt parāṅ paśyati kaścid dhīraḥ aikṣat āvṛtta cakṣuḥ amṛta tvam icche iti viśuddha sattvaḥ tatas tu tam paśyate iti ca evamādyā smṛtiḥ api ye viidrāḥ jita śvāsāḥ saṃtuṣṭāḥ saṃyata idriyāḥ jyotiḥ paśyati tasmai yoga ātmae amaḥ yogiaḥ tam prapaśyati bhagavatam iti ca evamādyāḥ saṃrādhya saṃrādhaka bhāva abhyupagamāt para apara ātmaoḥ aya tvam syāt iti ā iti ucyate prakāśa ādi vat ca a vaiśeṣyam prakāśaḥ ca karmaṇi abhyāsāt yathā prakāśa ākāśa savitṛ prabhṛtayaḥ aṅguli karaka udaka prabhṛtiṣu karmasu upādhi bhūteṣu sa viśeṣāḥ iva avabhāsate a ca svābhāvikīm aviśeṣa ātmatām jahati evam upādhi imittaḥ eva ayam ātma bhedaḥ svatas tu aikātmyam eva tathā hi asakṛt jīva prājñayoḥ abhedaḥ pratipādyate tathā hi liṅgam atas ca svābhāvika tvāt abhedasya avidyā kṛta tvāt ca bhedasya vidyayā avidyām vidhūya jīvaḥ pareṇa prājñea ātmā ekatām gacchati tathā hi liṅgam sa yaḥ ha vai tat paramam brahma veda brahma eva bhavati brahma eva sa brahmā apyeti ityādi ubhaya vyapadeśāt tu ahi kuṇḍala vat tasmin eva saṃrādhya saṃrādhaka bhāve matātaram upayasyati sva mata viśuddhaye kvacid jīva prājñayoḥ bhedaḥ vyapadiśyate tatas tu tam paśyate iti dhyātṛ dhyātavya tvea draṣṭṛ draṣṭavya tvea ca parātparam puruṣam upaiti divyam iti sarvāṇi bhūtāyataraḥ yamayati iti ca kvacid tu tayoḥ eva abhedaḥ vyapadiśyate tat tvam asi aham brahma asmi eṣa te ātmā sarva ataraḥ eṣa te ātmā ataryāmī amṛtaḥ iti tatra evam ubhaya vyapadeśe sati yadi abhedaḥ eva eka ātataḥ gṛhyate bheda vyapadeśaḥ eva syāt atas ubhaya vyapadeśa darśaāt ahi kuṇḍala vat atra tattvam bhavitum arhati yathā ahiḥ iti abhedaḥ ca bhedaḥ evam iha api iti prakāśa āśrayavat vā tejaḥ tvāt athavā prakāśa āśraya vat etat pratipattavyam yathā prakāśaḥ sāvitraḥ tad āśrayaḥ ca savitā ubhayoḥ api tejaḥ tva aviśeṣāt atha ca bheda vyapadeśa bhājau bhavataḥ evam iha api iti pūrvavat vā yathā vā pūrvam upayastam prakāśa ādi vat ca a vaiśeṣyam iti tathā eva etat bhavitum arhati tathā hi avidyā kṛta tvāt badhasya vidyayā mokṣaḥ upapadyate yadi puas paramārthataḥ eva baddhaḥ kaścid ātmā parasya ātmanaḥ ca eka deśa bhūtaḥ abhyupagamyeta tatas pāramārthikasya badhasya tiraskartum aśakya tvāt mokṣa śāstra vaiyarthyam prasajyeta ca atra ubhau api bheda abhedau śrutiḥ tulya vat vyapadiśati abhedam eva hi bhedam tu pūrva prasiddham eva āvadati artha atara vivakṣayā tasmāt prakāśa ādi vat ca a vaiśeṣyam iti eṣaḥ eva siddhātaḥ pratiṣedhāt ca itas ca eṣaḥ eva siddhātaḥ yatkāraṇam parasmāt ātmaoyam pratiṣedhati śāstram draṣṭā iti evamādi atha atas ādeśaḥ eti eti tat etat brahma apūrvam aaparam aataram abāhyam iti ca brahma vyatirikta prapañcaiḥ ākaraṇāt brahma mātra pariśeṣāt ca eṣaḥ eva iti gamyate yat etat brahma asmāt param ayat tattvam asti āsti iti śruti vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ kāicid hi vākyāi brahmaṇaḥ api param ayat tattvam pratipādayati iva teṣām hi parihāram abhidhātum ayam upakramaḥ kriyate param atas setu umāa sambadha bheda vyapadeśebhyaḥ param atas brahmaṇaḥ ayat tattvam bhavitum arhati kutas setu vyapadeśāt umāa vyapadeśāt saṃbadha vyapadeśāt bheda vyapadeśāt ca setu vyapadeśaḥ tāvat atha yaḥ ātmā sa setuḥ vidhṛtiḥ iti ātma śabda abhihitasya brahmaṇaḥ setu tvam saṃkīrtayati setu śabdaḥ ca hi loke jala saṃtā a viccheda kare mṛd dāru ādi pracaye prasiddhaḥ iha ca setu śabdaḥ prayuktaḥ iti laukika setoḥ iva ātma setoḥ rayasya vastu ostitvam gamayati setu iti ca tarati śabda prayogāt yathā laukikam setum tītrvā jāṅgalam asetum evam setum tītrvā setum iti gamyate umā a vyapadeśaḥ ca bhavati tat etat brahma catuṣpād aṣṭāśapham ṣoḍaśa kalam iti yat ca loke etāvat idam iti paricchiam kārṣāpaṇa ādi tatas yat vastu asti iti prasiddham tathā brahmaṇā upi umāāt vastuā bhavitavyam iti gamyate tathā bhavati satā somya tadā saṃpaaḥ bhavati iti saṃpariṣvaktaḥ iti ca ca dṛṣṭaḥ yathā arāṇām agareṇa jīvāām ca brahmaṇā vyapadiśati suṣuptau atas tatas gamyate bheda vyapadeśaḥ ca eam artham gamayati tathā hi atha yaḥ eṣa utarāditye hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣaḥ dṛśyate iti āditya ādhāram īśvaram vyapadiśya tatas akṣi ādhāram īśvaram vyapadiśati atha yaḥ eṣa ukṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate iti atideśam ca asya rūpa ādiṣu karoti tasya etasya tat eva rūpam yat amuṣya rūpam yau amuṣya geṣṇau tau geṣṇau iti saḥ avadhikam ca īśvara tvam ubhayoḥ vyapadiśati ye ca amuṣmāt parāñcaḥ lokāḥ teṣām ca iṣṭe deva kāmāām ca iti ekasya ye ca etasmāt arvāñcaḥ lokāḥ teṣām ca iṣṭe ca iti ekasya yathā idam māgadhasya rājyam idam vaidehasya iti evam etebhyaḥ setu ādi vyapadeśebhyaḥ brahmaṇaḥ param asti iti evam prāpte pratipādyate tuśabde pradarśitām prāptim pradarśitām prāptim a brahmaṇaḥ yat kiṃcid bhavitum arhati pramāṇa abhāvāt kiṃcid pramāṇam upalabhāmahe sarvasya hi jaimataḥ vastu jātasya brahmaṇaḥ bhavati iti ca kāraṇāt kāryasya a ca brahma vyatiriktam kiṃcid ajam saṃbhavati sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam iti avadhāraṇāt ca sarvavijñāa pratijñāāt a brahma vyatirikta vastu astitvam avakalpate setu ādi vyapadeśāḥ brahma vyatiriktam tattvam sūcayati iti uktam ā iti ucyate setu vyapadeśaḥ tāvat a brahmaṇaḥ bāhyasya sadbhāvam pratipādayitum kṣamate setuḥ ātmā iti hi āha a atas param asti iti tatra asati setu tvam iti param kim api kalpyeta ca etat yāyyam haṭhaḥ hi aprasiddha kalpaā api ca setu vyapadeśāt ātmā sa bāhya vastu tām prasañjayatā mṛd dāru maya tā api prāsaṅkṣyata a aja tva ādi śruti virodhāt setusāmāyāt tu setu śabdaḥ prayuktaḥ iti śliṣyate ca vidhāraka tvam setusāmāyam ātman atas setuḥ iva setuḥ iti prakṛtaḥ ātmā stūyate setum tītrvā iti api taratiḥ atikrama asaṃbhavāt eva vartate yathā vyākaraṇam tīrṇaḥ iti prāptaḥ ucyate a atikrātaḥ tadvat buddhi arthaḥ pāda vat yat api uktam umā a vyapadeśāt asti param iti tatra abhidhīyate umā a vyapadeśaḥ api a brahma vyatirikta vastu astitva pratipatti arthaḥ kimarthaḥ tarhi buddhi arthaḥ upāsa arthaḥ iti yāvat catuṣpād aṣṭāśapham ṣoḍaśakalam iti evaṃrūpā buddhiḥ katham brahmaṇi sthirā syāt iti vikāra dvāreṇa brahmaṇaḥ kriyate brahmaṇi sarvaiḥ puṃbhiḥ śakyā buddhiḥ sthāpayitum mada madhyama uttama buddhi tvāt puṃsām iti pāda vat yathā maa ākāśayoḥ adhyātmam adhidaivatam ca brahma pratīkayoḥ āmātayoḥ catvāraḥ vāc ādayaḥ pādāḥ kalpyate catvāraḥ ca agi ādayaḥ ākāśa saṃbadhiḥ tadvat athavā pāda vat iti yathā kārṣāpaṇe pāda vibhāgaḥ vyavahāra prācuryāya kalpyate hi hi sarvadā sarve vyavahartum īśate kraya vikraye tadvat iti arthaḥ sthā a viśeṣāt prakāśa ādi vat iha sūtre dvayoḥ api parihāraḥ abhidhīyate yat api uktam saṃbadha vyapadeśāt bheda vyapadeśāt ca param atas syāt iti tat api asat yatas ekasya api sthā a viśeṣa apekṣayā etau vyapadeśau upapadyete saṃbadha vyapadeśe tāvat ayam arthaḥ buddhi ādi upādhi sthā a viśeṣa yogāt udbhūtasya viśeṣa vijñāasya upādhi upaśame yaḥ upaśamaḥ sa paramātmā iti upādhi apekṣayā upacaryate a parimita tva apekṣayā tathā bheda vyapadeśaḥ api brahmaṇaḥ upādhi bheda apekṣayā eva upacaryate a svarūpa bheda apekṣayā prakāśa ādi vat iti yathā ekasya prakāśasya sauryasya ca ādramasasya vā upādhi yogāt upajāta viśeṣasya upādhi upaśamāt bhavati upādhi bhedāt ca bheda vyapadeśaḥ yathā vā sūcī pāśa ākāśa ādiṣu upādhi apekṣayā eva etau saṃbadha bheda vyapadeśau bhavataḥ tadvat upapatteḥ ca upapadyate ca atra īdṛśaḥ eva saṃbadhaḥ svam api itas bhavati iti hi sva rūpa saṃbadha ca a apāyi tvāt ghaṭate upādhi kṛta sva rūpa tirobhāvāt tu svam api itas bhavati iti upapadyate tathā bhedaḥ api saṃbhavati bahutara śruti prasiddha eka īśvara tva virodhāt tathā ca śrutiḥ ekasya api ākāśasya bheda vyapadeśam upapādayati yaḥ yam bahirdhā puruṣāt ākāśaḥ yaḥ yam atas puruṣaḥ ākāśaḥ yaḥ yam atas hṛdaye ākāśaḥ iti tathāya pratiṣedhāt evam setu ādi vyapadeśā saṃprati sva pakṣam hetu atareṇa upasaṃharati tathāya pratiṣedhā api a brahmaṇaḥ param vastu ataram asti iti gamyate tathā hi saḥ eva adhastāt aham eva adhastāt ātmā eva adhastāt sarvam tam parādāt yaḥ yatra ātma aḥ sarvam veda brahma eva idam sarvam ātmā eva idam sarvam eha ā asti kiṃca a yasmāt param ā aparam asti kiṃcid tat etat brahma apūrvam aaparam aataram abāhyam iti evamādīi vākyāi sva prakaraṇa sthāi pariṇetum aśakyāi brahma vyatiriktam vastu ataram vārayati sarvātara śruteḥ ca atarātmā asti iti avagamyate sarvagata tvam āyāma śabda ādibhyaḥ ca sarvagata tvam api ātmanaḥ siddham bhavati ayathā hi sidhyet setu ādi vyapadeśeṣu hi mukhyeṣu aṅgīkriyamāṇeṣu paricchedaḥ ātmaaḥ prasajyeta setu ādīām evam ātmaka tvāt tathā vastu vastu atarāt vyāvartate iti paricchedaḥ eva ātmaaḥ prasajyeta sarvagata tvam ca asya āyāma śabda ādibhyaḥ avagamyate āyāma śabdaḥ vyāpti vacaḥ śabdaḥ ayam ākāśaḥ tāvai eṣa utar hṛdaye ākāśaḥ ākāśa vat sarva gataḥ ca ityaḥ jyāyāt ivaḥ jyāyā ākāśāt ityaḥ sarva gataḥ sthāṇuḥ acalaḥ yam iti evamādayaḥ hi śruti smṛti yāyāḥ sarvagata tvam ātma uvabodhayati phalam atas upapatteḥ phala adhikaraṇam tasya eva brahmaṇaḥ vyāvahārikyām īśitṛ īśitavya vibhāga avasthāyām ayam ayaḥ svabhāvaḥ varṇyate yat etat iṣṭa a iṣṭa vyāmiśra lakṣaṇam karma phalam saṃsāra gocaram trividham prasiddham jatūām kim etat karmaṇaḥ bhavati āhosvit īśvarāt iti bhavati vicāraṇā tatra tāvat pratipādyate phalam atas īśvarāt bhavitum arhati kutas upapatteḥ sa hi sarva adhyakṣaḥ sṛṣṭi sthiti saṃhārāḥ vicitrāḥ vidadhat deśa kāla viśeṣa abhijña tvāt karmiṇām karma aurūpam phalam saṃpādayati iti upapadyate karmaṇaḥ tu kāla atara bhāvi phalam bhavati iti aupapaam abhāvāt bhāva autpatteḥ syāt etat karma viaśyat sva kālam eva svāurūpam phalam viaśyati tat phalam kāla ātaritam kartrā bhokṣyate iti tat api a pariśudhyati prāk bhoktṛ saṃbadhāt phala tva aupapatteḥ yatkālam hi yat sukham duḥkham vā ātmaā bhujyate tasya eva loke phala tvam prasiddham hi asaṃbaddhasya ātmā sukhasya duḥkhasya vā phala tvam laukikāḥ atha ucyeta mā phala utpādaḥ karma kāryāt apūrvāt phalam utpatsyate iti tat api opapadyate apūrvasya acetaasya kāṣṭha loṣṭa samasya cetaeā pravartitasya pravṛtti aupapatteḥ tad astitve eva pramāṇa abhāvāt arthāpattiḥ pramāṇam iti ced ā īśvara siddheḥ arthāpatti kṣayāt śruta tvāt ca a kevalam upapatteḥ eva īśvaram phala hetum kalpayāmaḥ kim tarhi śruta tvāt api īśvaram eva phala hetum tathā ca śrutiḥ bhavati sa vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ vasudāaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ dharmam jaimiiḥ atas eva jaimiiḥ tu ācāryaḥ dharmam phalasya dātāram atas eva hetoḥ śruteḥ upapatteḥ ca śrūyate tāvat ayam arthaḥ svarga kāmaḥ yajeta iti evamādiṣu vākyeṣu tatra ca vidhi śruteḥ viṣaya bhāva upagamāt yāgaḥ svargasya utpādakaḥ iti gamyate ayathā hi aauṣṭhātṛkaḥ yāgaḥ āpadyeta tatra asya upadeśa vaiyarthyam syāt karmaṇaḥ phalam opapadyate iti parityaktaḥ iyam pakṣaḥ ā eṣa doṣaḥ śruti prāmāṇyāt śrutiḥ ced pramāṇam yathā ayam śrutaḥ upapadyate tathā kalpayitavyaḥ ca autpādya kim api apūrvam karma atas karmaṇaḥ vā sūkṣmā kācid uttara avasthā phalasya vā pūrva avasthā apūrvam asti iti tarkyate upapadyate ca ayam artham prakāreṇa īśvaraḥ tu phalam dadāti iti aupapam avicitrasya kāraṇasya vicitra kārya aupapatteḥ vaiṣamya airghṛṇya prasaṅgāt tad auṣṭhā avaiyarthya āpatteḥ ca tasmāt dharmāt eva phalam iti pūrvam tu bādarāyaṇaḥ hetu vyapadeśāt bādarāyaṇaḥ tu ācāryaḥ pūrva uktam eva īśvaram phala hetum kevalāt karmaṇaḥ apūrvāt vā kevalāt phalam iti ayam pakṣaḥ tuśabdena vyāvartyate karma apekṣāt apūrva apekṣāt vā yathā tathā astu īśvarāt phalam iti siddhātaḥ kutas hetu vyapadeśāt dharma adharmayoḥ api hi kārayitṛ tve īśvaraḥ hetuḥ vyapadiśyate phalasya ca dātṛ tve eṣa hi eva sādhu karma kārayati tam yam ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ uiīṣate eṣaḥ u eva asādhu karma kārayati tam yam adhas iti smaryate ca ayam arthaḥ bhagavadgītāsu yaḥ yaḥ yām yām taum bhaktaḥ śraddhayā arcitum icchati tasya tasya acalām śraddhām tām eva vidadhāmi aham sa tayā śraddhayā yuktaḥ tasya ārādhaam īhate labhate ca tatas kāmāḥ mayā eva vihita ahitāḥ iti ca īśvara hetukāḥ eva sṛṣṭayaḥ vyapadiśyate tat eva ca īśvarasya phala hetu tvam yat sva karma aurūpāḥ prajāḥ sṛjati doṣāḥ kṛta prayata apekṣa tvāt īśvarasya a prasajyate iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye tṛtīya adhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ tṛtīyaḥ udhyāyaḥ tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ sarva vedāta pratyayam coda ādi aviśeṣāt sarva vedāta pratyaya adhikaraṇam tasmin tasmin bhavitum arhati kutas coda ādi aviśeṣāt abheda hetavaḥ iha ākṛṣyate saṃyoga rūpa coda ākhyā viśeṣāt iti arthaḥ yathā puruṣa prayataḥ tādṛśaḥ eva codyate juhuyāt iti evam yaḥ ha vai jyeṣṭham ca śreṣṭham ca veda iti vājasaeyiām chadogāām ca tādṛśī eva eva jyeṣṭhaḥ ca śreṣṭhaḥ ca bhavati iti rūpam api ubhayatra tat eva yat uta jyeṣṭha śreṣṭha ādi viśeṣaṇa āvitam prāṇa tattvam yathā ca dravya devate yāgasya rūpam evam vijñeyam rūpam vijñāasya hi tat rūpyate samākhyā api sā eva prāṇa vidyā iti tasmāt sarva vedāta pratyaya tvam vijñāāām evam pañcāgi vidyā vaiśvāara vidyā śāṇḍilya vidyā iti evamādiṣu api yojayitavyam ye tu āma rūpa ādayaḥ bheda hetvābhāsāḥ te prathame eva syāt iti ārabhya parihṛtāḥ iha api kaṃcid viśeṣam āśaṅkya pariharati ced ekasyām api syāt etat vijñāāām guṇa bhedāt upapadyate tathā hi vājasaeyiḥ pañcāgi vidyām prastutya ṣaṣṭham aparam agim āmaati tasya āgiḥ eva āgiḥ bhavati iti ādiā chadogāḥ tu tam pañca saṃkhyayā eva ca te upasaṃharati atha ha yaḥ etā evam pañcāgī vedaḥ iti yeṣām ca sa guṇaḥ usti yeṣām ca ā asti katham ubhayeṣām ekā vidyā upapadyeta ca atra guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ śakyate pratyetum pañca saṃkhyā virodhāt tathā prāṇa saṃvāde śreṣṭhāt caturaḥ prāṇāḥ vāc cakṣuḥ śrotra maāṃsi chadogāḥ āmaati vājasaeyiḥ tu pañcamam api āmaati retaḥ vai prajāpatiḥ prajāyate ha prajayā paśubhiḥ yaḥ evam veda iti āvāpa udvāpa bhedāt ca vedya bhedaḥ bhavati vedya bhedāt ca vidyā bhedaḥ dravya devatā bheda iva yāgasya iti ced ā eṣa doṣaḥ yatas ekasyām api vidyāyām evaṃjātīyakaḥ guṇa bhedaḥ upapadyate yadi api ṣaṣṭhasya āgeḥ upasaṃhāraḥ saṃbhavati tathā api ubhayatra a vidyā bhedaḥ bhavitum arhati a hi ṣoḍaśi grahaṇa agrahaṇayoḥ atirātraḥ bhidyate paṭhyate api ca chadogaiḥ tam pretam diṣṭam itas gayaḥ eva harati iti vājasaeyiḥ tu sāṃpādikeṣu pañcasu agiṣu auvṛttāyāḥ samidh dhūma ādi kalpaāyāḥ samidh samidh ityādi samāmaati saḥ atha api upāsa arthaḥ eṣa vādaḥ tathā api sa guṇaḥ śakyate chadogaiḥ api upasaṃhartum chadogaiḥ api upasaṃhartum ca atra pañca saṃkhyā virodhaḥ āśaṅkyaḥ sāṃpādikā āgi abhiprāyā hi eṣā pañca saṃkhyā iti āuvāda bhūtā a vidhi samavāyiī iti adoṣaḥ evam prāṇa saṃvāda ādiṣu api adhikasya guṇasya itaratra upasaṃhāraḥ virudhyate a ca āvāpa udvāpa bhedāt vedya bhedaḥ vidyā bhedaḥ ca āśaṅkyaḥ kasyacid vedya aṃśasya āvāpa udvāpayoḥ api bhūyasaḥ vedya rāśeḥ abheda avagamāt tasmāt aikavidyam eva svādhyāyasya tathātve hi samācāra adhikārāt ca sava vat ca taiyamaḥ yat api uktam ātharvaṇikāām vidyām prati śiraḥ vrata ādi apekṣaṇāt ca tad a apekṣaṇāt vidyā bhedaḥ iti tat pratyucyate svādhyāyasya eṣa dharmaḥ a vidyāyāḥ katham idam avagamyate yatas samācāre veda vrata upadeśa pare ātharvaṇikāḥ idam api vyākhyātam iti ca adhikṛta viṣayāt etad śabdāt adhyaya a śabdāt ca sva upaiṣadadhyayaa dharmaḥ eva eṣaḥ iti auteṣām eva etām brahma vidyām vadeta śirovratam vidhivat yaiḥ tu cīrṇam iti brahma vidyā saṃyoga śravaṇāt ekā eva sarvatra brahma vidyā iti saṃkīryeta eṣa dharmaḥ a tatra api etām iti prakṛta pratyavamarśāt prakṛta tvam ca brahma vidyāyāḥ gratha viśeṣa apekṣam iti gratha viśeṣa saṃyogī eva eṣa dharmaḥ sava vat ca taiyamaḥ iti yathā ca savāḥ sapta saurya ādayaḥ śata oda paryatāḥ ātharvaṇa udita ekāgī abhisaṃbadhāt ca iyamyate tathā eva ayam api dharmaḥ svādhyāya viśeṣa saṃbadhāt tatra eva tasmāt api aavadyam vidyā ekatvam darśayati ca darśayati ca vedaḥ upi vidyā ekatvam vedya ekatva upadeśāt sarve vedāḥ yat padam āmaati iti tathā etam hi eva bahvṛcāḥ mahati ukthe mīmāṃsate etam agau adhvaryavaḥ etam mahāvrate chadogāḥ iti ca tathā mahat bhayam vajram udyatam iti kāṭhake uktasya īśvara guṇasya bhaya hetu tvasya taittirīyake parāmarśaḥ dṛśyate yadā hi eva eṣa kurute atha tasya bhayam bhavati tat tu eva bhayam iti tathā vājasaeyake prādeśa mātra saṃpāditasya vaiśvāarasya chādogye siddha vat upādāam yaḥ tu etam evam prādeśa mātram abhivimāam ātmāam vaiśvāaram upāste iti tathā ayatra upāsaa vidhāāt upādāt ca upasaṃhāra adhikaraṇam idam sthite ca evam sarva vedāta pratyaya tve sarva vijñāāām ayatra uditāām vijñāa guṇāām ayatra api samāe vijñāe upasaṃhāraḥ bhavati artha abhedāt yaḥ eva hi teṣām guṇāām ekatra arthaḥ viśiṣṭa vijñā upakāraḥ saḥ eva ayatra api ubhayatra api hi tat eva ekam vijñāam tasmāt upasaṃhāraḥ vidhi śeṣa vat yathā vidhi śeṣāṇām agihotra ādi dharmāṇām tat eva ekam agihotra ādi karma sarvatra iti artha abhedāt upasaṃharaṇam evam iha api yadi hi vijñā abhedaḥ bhavet tatas prakṛti vikṛti bhāva abhāvāt ca a syāt upasaṃhāraḥ vijñā aikatve tu aivam iti asya eva tu prapañcaḥ sarva abhedāt iti ārabhya bhaviṣyati ayathātvam śabdāt iti ca iā aviśeṣāt ayathātva adhikaraṇam vājasaeyake te ha devāḥ ūcuḥ hata asura yajñe udgīthe atyayāma iti te ha vācam ūcuḥ tvam a udgāye iti prakramya mukhya prāṇa parigrahaḥ paṭhyate atha ha imam āsayam prāṇam ūcuḥ tvam udgāya iti tathā iti tebhyaḥ eṣa prāṇaḥ udagāyat iti tathā chādogye pitat ha devāḥ udgītham ājahruḥ abhibhaviṣyāmaḥ iti prakramya tathā eva mukhya prāṇa parigrahaḥ paṭhyate atha ha yaḥ eva ayam mukhyaḥ prāṇaḥ tam udgītham upāsāṃcakrire iti ubhayatra api ca prāṇa praśaṃsayā prāṇa vidyā vidhiḥ adhyavasīyate tatra saṃśayaḥ kim atra vidyā bhedaḥ syāt āhosvit vidyā ekatvam iti kim tāvat prāptam pūrveṇa vidyā ekatvam iti au a yuktam vidyā ekatvam prakrama bhedāt ayathā hi prakramate vājasaeyiḥ ayathā chadogāḥ tvam a udgāya iti vājasaeyia udgīthasya chadogāḥ tu udgītha tveatam udgītham upāsāṃcakrire iti tat katham vidyā ekatvam syāt iti ced ā eṣa doṣaḥ a hi etāvatā viśeṣeṇa vidyā eka tvam apagacchati aviśeṣasya api bahutarasya tathā hi deva asura saṃgrāma upakrama tvam asura atyaya abhiprāyaḥ udgītha upayāsaḥ vāc ādi saṃkīrtaam mukhya prāṇa vyapāśrayaḥ tad vīryāt ca asura vidhvaṃsaam iti evam bahavaḥ ṛthāḥ ubhayatra api aviśiṣṭāḥ pratīyate vājasaeyake pi ca udgītha sāma ādhikaraṇyam prāṇasya śrutam eṣaḥ u vai udgīthaḥ iti tasmāt chādogye api kartṛ tvam lakṣayitavyam tasmāt ca vidyā eka tvam iti a ca vā prakaraṇa bhedāt parovarīyaḥ tva ādi vat a vā vidyā eka tvam atra yāyyam vidyā bhedaḥ eva atra yāyyaḥ kasmāt prakaraṇa bhedāt prakrama bhedāt iti arthaḥ tathā hi iha prakrama bhedaḥ dṛśyate chādogye tāvat om iti etat akṣaram udgītham upāsīta iti evam udgītha avayavasya oṃkārasya upāsya tvam prastutya rasatama tva ādi guṇa upavyākhyāam tatra kṛtvā atha khalu etasya eva akṣarasya upavyākhyāam bhavati iti tam eva udgītha avayavam oṃkāram deva asura ākhyāyikā dvāreṇa tamprāṇam udgītham upāsāṃcakrire iti āha tatra yadi udgītha śabdena anuprāṇam udgītham upāsāṃcakrire iti āha tatra yadi udgītha śabdena anuprāṇam udgītham upāsāṃcakrire iti āha tatra yad sakalā bhaktiḥ abhipreyeta tasyāḥ ca kartā udgātā ṛtvij tatas upakramaḥ ca uparudhyeta lakṣaṇā ca prasajyeta upakrama tatreṇa ca ekasmin vākye upasaṃhāreṇa bhavitavyam tasmāt atra tāvat udgītha avayave oṃkāre prāṇa dṛṣṭiḥ upadiśyate vājasaeyake tu avayava grahaṇe kāraṇa abhāvāt sakalā eva bhaktiḥ āvedyate udgāye iti api tasyāḥ kartā udgātā ṛtvij iti prasthāātaram yat api tatra udgītha sāmāādhikaraṇyam prāṇasya tat api udgātṛ tve eva didarśayiṣitasya prāṇasya sarva ātma tva pratipāda artham iti a vidyā ekatvam āvahati sakala bhakti viṣaye eva ca tatra api udgītha śabdaḥ iti vaiṣamyam a ca prāṇasya udgātṛ tvam parityajyate udgītha bhāva vat udgātṛ bhāvasya api upāsa artha tvea upadiśyamāa tvāt prāṇa vīryeṇa eva ca udgātā audgātram karoti iti tathā ca tatra eva śrāvitam vācā ca hi eva sa prāṇe ca udagāyat iti ca vākya chāyā okāra mātreṇa yuktam tathā hi abhyudaya vākye paśu kāma vākye ca tredhā dātre puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālam kuryāt ityādi irdeśa sāmye api upakrama bhedāt abhyudaya vākye paśu kāma vākye tu yāga vidhiḥ tathā iha api upakrama bhedāt vidyā bhedaḥ parovarīyaḥ tva ādi vat yathā paramātma dṛṣṭi adhyāsa sāmye pi ākāśaḥ hi eva ebhyaḥ jyāyāḥ ākāśaḥ parāyaṇam saḥ eṣa paras varīyāḥ udgīthaḥ saḥ eṣaḥ atas iti parovarīyaḥ tva guṇa viśiṣṭam udgītha upāsaam akṣi āditya ādi gata hiraṇya śmaśru tva ādi guṇa viśiṣṭa udgītha upāsaāt ca itaretara guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ ekasyām api śākhāyām tadvat śākhātara stheṣu api evaṃjātīyakeṣu upāsaeṣu iti saṃjñātaḥ ced tad api anya api anya api anya api anya api anya api anya api anya api anya api anya api anya api anya api anya api anya api anya api anya api anya api any uktam asti tu tat api atha ucyeta saṃjñā eka tvāt vidyā eka tvam atra yāyyam ekā saṃjñā iti tat api opapadyate uktam hi etat a vā prakaraṇa bhedāt paraḥ varīyaḥ tva ādi vat iti tat eva ca atra yāyyataram śruti akṣara augatam hi tat saṃjñā eka tvam tu śruti akṣara bāhyam udgītha śabda mātra yogāt laukikaiḥ vyavahartṛbhiḥ upacaryate asti ca etat saṃjñā eka tvam prasiddha bhedeṣu api udgītha vidyā iti tathā prasiddha bhedāām api agihotra darśa pūrṇamāsa ādīām kāṭhaka eka gratha paripaṭhitāām kāṭhaka saṃjñā eka tvam dṛśyate tathā iha api bhaviṣyati yatra tu āsti kaścid evaṃjātīyakaḥ bheda hetuḥ tatra bhavatu saṃjñā eka tvāt vidyā eka tvam yathā saṃvarga vidyā ādiṣu vyāpteḥ ca samañjasam vyāptyā adhikaraṇam om iti etat akṣaram udgītham upāsīta iti atra akṣara udgītha śabdayoḥ sāmāādhikaraṇye śrūyamāṇe adhyāsa apavāda ekatva viśeṣaṇa pakṣāṇām pratibhāsaāt katamaḥ utra pakṣaḥ yāyyaḥ syāt iti vicāraḥ tatra dvayoḥ vastuoḥ dvayoḥ vastuoḥ evartitāyām eva ayatara buddhau itara buddhiḥ adhyasyate eva eva tasmi tad buddhiḥ adhyasta itara buddhiḥ adhyasta adhyasta itara buddhiḥ adhyasta itara buddhiḥ adhyasta itara buddhiḥ adhyasta itara buddhiḥ adhyasta itara buddhiḥ adhyasta itara buddhiḥ adhyasta itara buddhiḥ adhyasta itara buddhau adhyasta itara buddhau api yathā brahma buddhau adhyasyamāāyām api eva eva āma buddhiḥ brahma buddhyā iva ṛtate yathā vā pratimā ādiṣu viṣṇu ādi buddhi adhyāsaḥ evam iha api akṣare udgītha buddhiḥ adhyasyeta udgīthe vā akṣara buddhiḥ iti yatra kasmiṃścid vastui mithyā buddhau paścāt upajāyamāā yathārthā buddhiḥ bhavati yathā deha idriya saṃghāte ātma buddhiḥ ātmayā iva ātma buddhyā yathā vā diś bhrāti buddhiḥ diś yāthātmya buddhyā evam iha api akṣara buddhyā udgītha buddhiḥ iva ṛtyeta udgītha buddhyā vā akṣara buddhiḥ iti ekatvam tu akṣara udgītha śabdayoḥ aatirikta artha vṛtti tvam yathā dvijottamaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ bhūmidevaḥ iti viśeṣaṇam om iti etasya akṣarasya grahaṇa prasaṅge audgātra viśeṣasya samarpaṇam yathā īlam yat utpalam tat āaya iti evam iha api udgīthaḥ yaḥ oṃkāraḥ tam upāsīta iti evam etasmin sāmāādhikaraṇya vākye ete pakṣāḥ pratibhāti tatra āyatamaiḥ dhāraṇa kāraṇa abhāvāt aiḥ dhāraṇa prāptau idam ucyate vyāpteḥ ca samañjasam iti caśabdaḥ ūyam tuśabda sthā aiveśī tat iha trayaḥ pakṣāḥ sāvadyāḥ iti paryudasyate viśeṣaṇa pakṣaḥ eva ekaḥ iḥ avadyaḥ iti upādīyate tatra adhyāse tāvat yā buddhiḥ itaratra adhyasyate tad śabdasya lakṣaṇa āvṛtti tvam prasajyeta tad phalam ca kalpyeta śrūyate eva phala āpayitā ha vai bhavati ityādi iti ced tasya aya phala tvāt āpti ādi dṛṣṭi phalam hi tat odgītha adhyāsa phalam apavāde pi phala abhāvaḥ mithyājñā ai vṛttiḥ phalam iti ced a puruṣa artha upayoga avagamāt a ca kadācid api oṃkārāt okāra buddhiḥ iva rteta udgīthāt vā udgītha buddhiḥ a ca idam vākyam vastu tattva pratipāda aparam ekatva pakṣaḥ saṃgacchate hi tadā śabda dvaya uccāraṇam syāt vivakṣita artha samarpaṇāt ca hautra viṣaye ādhvaryava viṣaye vā akṣare oṃkāra śabda vācye udgītha śabda prasiddhiḥ asti sakalāyām sāmaḥ dvitīyāyām bhaktau udgītha śabda vācyāyām oṃkāra śabda prasiddhiḥ syāt pariśeṣāt viśeṣaṇa pakṣaḥ parigṛhyate vyāpteḥ sarva veda sādhāraṇyāt sarva vyāpi akṣaram iha mā iti atas udgītha śabde akṣaram viśeṣyate katham udgītha avayava bhūtaḥ oṃkāraḥ gṛhyeta iti pakṣe lakṣaṇā udgītha śabdasya avayava lakṣaṇa artha tvāt satyam evam etat lakṣaṇāyām api tu saṃikarṣa viprakarṣau bhavataḥ eva adhyāsa pakṣe hi arthātara buddhiḥ arthātare iti viprakṛṣṭā lakṣaṇā viśeṣaṇa pakṣe tu avayavaḥ samarpyate iti saṃikṛṣṭā samudāyeṣu hi pravṛttāḥ śabdāḥ avayaveṣu api dṛṣṭāḥ paṭa grāma ādiṣu atas ca vyāpteḥ hetoḥ om iti etat akṣaram iti etasya audgītham iti etat viśeṣaṇam iti samañjasam etat sarva abhedāt ayatra ime sarva abheda adhikaraṇam ca prāṇa saṃvāde śraiṣṭhya guṇa āvitasya prāṇasya upāsya tvam uktam vāc ādayaḥ api hi tatra vasiṣṭha tva ādi guṇa āvitāḥ uktāḥ te ca guṇāḥ prāṇe puas pratyarpitāḥ yat vai aham vasiṣṭha asmi tvam tat vasiṣṭhaḥ usi ityādiā ayeṣām api tu prāṇa saṃvādeṣu atha atas ha vai devatāḥ ahaṃśreyase iti evaṃjātīyakeṣu prāṇasya śraiṣṭhyam uktam a tu ime vasiṣṭha tva ādayaḥ api guṇāḥ uktāḥ tatra saṃśayaḥ kim ime vasiṣṭha tva ādayaḥ guṇāḥ kvacid uktāḥ a yatra api uta āsyera eti tatra prāptam tāvat āsyera eti kutas evaṃśabda saṃyogāt atha u yaḥ evam vidvā prāṇe iḥśreyasam viditvā iti hi tatra tatra vedyam vastu iva idyate evaṃśabdaḥ ca saṃihita avalambaḥ a śākhātara paripaṭhitam evaṃjātīyakam guṇa jātam śakoti ivedayitum tasmāt sva prakaraṇa sthaiḥ eva guṇaiḥ iḥ ākāṅkṣa tvam iti evam prāpte pratyāha asya ire ime guṇāḥ kvacid uktāḥ vasiṣṭha tva ādayaḥ ayatra api kutas sarva abhedāt sarvatra eva tat eva ekam prāṇa vijñāam abhiam pratyabhijñāyate prāṇa saṃvāda ādi sārūpyāt abhede ca vijñāasya katham ime guṇāḥ kvacid uktāḥ evaṃśabdaḥ tatra tatra bhede evaṃjātīyakam guṇa jātam vedya tvāya samarpayati iti uktam atra ucyate yadi api vājasaeyi brāhmaṇa gatam guṇa jātam a saṃśabditam a saṃihita tvāt tathā api tasmin eva vijñāe vājasaeyi brāhmaṇa gatam evaṃśabditam tat saṃśabditam iti a para śākhā gatam api guṇa jātam sva śākhā gatāt viśiṣyate ca evam sati vā bhavati ekasyām api hi śākhāyām śrutāḥ guṇāḥ śrutāḥ eva sarvatra bhavati guṇavataḥ bheda abhāvāt hi devadattaḥ sva deśe prasiddhaḥ deśātaram gataḥ tad deśyaiḥ avibhāvita śaurya ādi guṇaḥ api atadguṇaḥ bhavati yathā ca tatra paricaya viśeṣāt deśa atare pi devadatta guṇā vibhāvyate evam abhiyoga viśeṣāt śākhā atare pi upāsyāḥ guṇāḥ śākhā atare asyera tasmāt eka pradhā a saṃbaddhāḥ dharmāḥ ekatra api ucyamāāḥ sarvatra eva upasaṃhartavyāḥ iti āat ādayaḥ pradhā asya āat ādi adhikaraṇam brahma svarūpa pratipāda aparāsu śrutiṣu āat a rūpa tvam sarvagata tvam sarva ātma tvam iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ brahmaṇaḥ dharmāḥ kvacid kecid śrūyate teṣu saṃśayaḥ kimāat ādayaḥ brahma dharmāḥ yatra yāvataḥ śrūyate tāvataḥ eva tatra pratipattavyāḥ kim vā sarve sarvatra iti tatra yathāśruti vibhāgam dharma pratipattau prāptāyām idam ucyate brahmaṇaḥ dharmāḥ sarve sarvatra pratipattavyāḥ kasmāt sarva abhedāt eva sarvatra hi tat eva ekam viśeṣyam brahma a bhidyate tasmāt sārvatrika tvam brahma dharmāṇām evam sati priyaśiraḥ tva ādayaḥ api dharmāḥ sarve sarvatra saṃkīryera tathā hi taittirīyake āada mayam ātmā aam prakramya āmāyate tasya priyam eva śiraḥ modaḥ dakṣiṇaḥ pakṣaḥ pramodaḥ uttaraḥ pakṣaḥ āadaḥ ātmā brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti atas uttaram paṭhati priya śiraḥ tva ādi aprāptiḥ upacaya apacayau hi bhede priya śiraḥ tva ādīām dharmāṇām taittirīyake prāptiḥ yatkāraṇam priyam modaḥ pramodaḥ iti ete paraspara apekṣayā bhoktratara apekṣayā ca upacita apacita rūpā upalabhyate upacaya apacayau ca sati bhede saṃbhavataḥ tu brahma ekam eva advitīyam ityādi śrutibhyaḥ a ca ete priyaśiraḥ tva ādayaḥ brahma dharmāḥ kośa dharmāḥ tu ete iti upadiṣṭam asmābhiḥ iti atra api ca parasmi brahmaṇi ete parikalpyate a draṣṭavya tve evam api sutarām ayatra aprāptiḥ brahma dharmān tu brahma dharmān tu ācāryeṇa pradarśitam priyaśiraḥ tva ādi aprāptiḥ iti sa ca brahma dharmeṣu etavyaḥ saṃyat vāma tva ādiṣu satyakāma tva ādiṣu ca teṣu hi sati api upāsyasya brahmaṇaḥ ekatve prakrama bhedāt upāsā abhede sati a ayoya dharmāṇām prāptiḥ yathā ca dve āryau ekam ṛpatim upāsāte chatreṇa ayā cāmareṇa ayā tatra upāsya eka tve pi upāsa abhedaḥ dharma vyavasthā ca bhavati evam iha api iti upacita apacita guṇa tvam hi sati bheda vyavahāre saguṇe brahmaṇi upapadyate parasmin brahmaṇi atas a satya kāma tva ādīām dharmāṇām kvacid śrutāām sarvatra prāptiḥ iti arthaḥ itare tu artha sāmāyāt itare tu dharmāḥ brahma svarūpa pratipāda eva ucyamāāḥ artha sāmāyāt pratipādyasya brahmaṇaḥ dharmiṇaḥ ekatvāt sarve sarvatra pratīyera eti vaiṣamyam pratipatti mātra prayojaāḥ hi te iti ādhyāāya prayojaā abhāvāt ādhyāādhikaraṇam kāṭhake hi paṭhyate idriyebhyaḥ parāḥ hi arthāḥ arthebhyaḥ ca param maaḥ maasaḥ tu parā buddhiḥ iti ārabhya puruṣāḥ param kiṃcid sā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim ime sarve eva artha ādayaḥ tatas tatas pratipādyate uta puruṣaḥ eva ebhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ paraḥ pratipādyate iti tatra tāvat sarveṣām eva eṣām bhavati matiḥ tathā hi śrūyate idam asmāt param idam asmāt param iti bahuṣu artheṣu vākya bhedaḥ syāt doṣaḥ vākya bahutva upapatteḥ bahūyā iva hi prabhavati bahūarthā paratva upetā pratipādayitum tasmāt pratyekam eṣām paratva pratipādaam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ puruṣaḥ eva hi ebhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ paraḥ pratipādyate iti yuktam a pratyekam eṣām kasmāt prayojaa abhāvāt hi itareṣu kiṃcid prayojaam dṛśyate śrūyate vā puruṣe tu idriya ādibhyaḥ dṛśyate mokṣa siddhiḥ tathā ca śrutiḥ icāyya tad mṛtyu mukhāt pramucyate iti api ca kāṣṭhā śabde ca puruṣa viṣayam ādaram darśaya puruṣa pratipatti arthā eva pūrva apara pravāha uktiḥ iti darśayati ādhyāāya iti samyak darśaāya iti arthaḥ samyak darśa artham eva hi iha ādhyāam upadiśyate a tu ādhyāam eva sva pradhāam ātma śabdāt ca itas ca puruṣa pratipatti arthā eva iyam idriya ādi pravāha uktiḥ yatkāraṇam eṣa sarveṣu bhūteṣu gūḍha utmā prakāśate dṛśyate tu agryayā buddhyā sūkṣmayā sūkṣma darśibhiḥ iti prakṛtam puruṣam ātmā iti āha atas ca a ātma tvam itareṣām vivakṣitam iti gamyate tasya eva ca durvijñāa tām saṃskṛta mati gamya tām ca darśayati tad vijñāāya eva ca yacchet vāc maasī prājñaḥ iti vidadhāti tat vyākhyātam āumāikam api ekeṣām iti atra evam a eka prakāraḥ āśaya atiśayaḥ śruteḥ puruṣe lakṣyate etareṣu api tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam iti ukte kim tat adhvaḥ pāram viṣṇoḥ paramam padam iti asyām ākāṅkṣāyām parama pada pratipatti arthaḥ eva ayam āmāyaḥ iti avasīyate ātma gṛhītiḥ itara vat uttarāt ātma gṛhīti adhikaraṇam aitareyake śrūyate ātmā vā idam ekaḥ eva agre āsīt ā yat kiṃca a miṣat saḥ īkṣata lokāḥ u sṛjai iti saḥ imān lokāḥ asṛjata ambhaḥ marīcīḥ maramā apaḥ ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kim paraḥ eva ātmā iha ātma śabdena abhilapyate uta ayaḥ kaścid iti kim tāvat prāptam a paramātmā iha ātma śabda abhilapyaḥ bhavitum arhati iti kasmāt vākyāvaya darśaāt vākyāvayaḥ sutarām paramātma viṣayaḥ dṛśyate prāk utpatteḥ ātma ekatva avadhāraṇāt īkṣaṇa pūrvaka sraṣṭṛ tva vacaāt ca ā iti ucyate loka sṛṣṭi vacaāt hi sraṣṭari parigṛhyamāṇe mahābhūta sṛṣṭiḥ ādau vaktavyā loka sṛṣṭiḥ tu iha ādau ucyate lokāḥ ca mahābhūta saṃiveśa viśeṣāḥ tathā ca ambhaḥ prabhṛtī loka tve eva loka sṛṣṭiḥ ca apareṇa keacid īśvareṇa kriyata iti śruti smṛtyoḥ upalabhyate tathā hi śrutiḥ bhavati ātmā eva idam agre āsīt puruṣavidhaḥ ityādyā smṛtiḥ api sa vai śarīrī prathamaḥ sa vai puruṣaḥ ucyate ādikartā sa bhūtāām brahma agre samavartata iti aitareyiṇaḥ pi atha atas retasaḥ sṛṣṭiḥ prajāpateḥ retaḥ devāḥ iti atra pūrvasmi prakaraṇe prajāpati kartṛkām vicitrām sṛṣṭim āmaati ātma śabdaḥ pi dṛśyate ātmā eva idam agre āsīt puruṣavidhaḥ iti atra ekatva avadhāraṇam api prāk utpatteḥ sva vikāra apekṣam upapadyate īkṣaṇam api tasya ceta a tva abhyupagamāt api ca tābhyaḥ gām āayat tābhyaḥ śvam āayat tābhyaḥ puruṣam āayat tāḥ abruve iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ bhūyāḥ vyāpāra viśeṣaḥ laukikeṣu viśeṣavatsu ātmasu prasiddhaḥ tasmāt viśeṣavān eva kaścid iha ātmā syāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ paraḥ eva ātmā iha ātma śabde gṛhyate itaravat yathā itareṣu sṛṣṭi śravaṇeṣu tasmāt vai etasmāt ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti evamādiṣu parasya ātmanaḥ grahaṇam yathā ca itarasmin laukika ātma śabda prayoge pratyagātmā eva mukhyaḥ ātma śabde gṛhyate tathā iha api bhavitum arhati yatra tu ātmā eva idam agre āsīt iti evamādau puruṣavidhaḥ iti evamādi viśeṣaṇa ātaram śrūyate bhavet tatra viśeṣavataḥ ātmanaḥ grahaṇam atra puaḥ eva viśeṣaṇam api uttaram upalabhyate saḥ īkṣata lokāḥ u sṛjā iti saḥ imān llokāḥ asṛjata iti evamādi tasmāt tasya eva grahaṇam iti yāyyam avayāt iti ced syāt avadhāraṇāt vākya avaya darśaāt a paramātma grahaṇam iti yat uktam tat parihartavyam iti atra ucyate syāt avadhāraṇāt iti bhavet upapaam paramātmanaḥ grahaṇam kasmāt avadhāraṇāt paramātma grahaṇe hi prāk utpatteḥ ātma ekatva avadhāraṇam āñjasam avakalpate ayathā hi aāñjasam tat parikalpyeta loka sṛṣṭi vacaam tu śruti atara prasiddha mahābhūta sṛṣṭi aataram iti yojayiṣyāmi yathā tat tejaḥ sṛjataḥ iti etat śruti atara prasiddha viyat vāyu sṛṣṭi aataram iti ayūyujam evam iha api śruti atara prasiddhaḥ hi viśeṣaḥ śruti atareṣu upasaṃhartavyaḥ bhavati yaḥ api ayam iti evamādiḥ saḥ api vivakṣita artha avadhāraṇa āuguṇyeā eva grahītavyaḥ hi ayam sakalaḥ kathā prabadhaḥ vivakṣitaḥ iti śakyate vaktum tad pratipattau puruṣa artha abhāvāt brahma ātma tvam tu iha vivakṣitam tathā hi ambhaḥ prabhṛtīām lokāām lokapālāām sṛṣṭim śiṣṭvā ca śarīram upadiśya saḥ eva sraṣṭā a katham vidam mat ṛte syāt iti vīkṣya idam śarīram praviveśa iti darśayati saḥ etam eva sīmāam vidārya etayā dvārā prāpadyata iti vācā abhivyāhṛtam yadi prāṇe abhiprāṇitam iti evamādiā karaṇa vyāpāra vivecaa pūrvakam atha kaḥ ham iti vīkṣyase etam eva puruṣam brahma tatamam apaśyat iti brahma ātmatva darśaam avadhārayati tathā upariṣṭāt eṣa brahma eṣaḥ idraḥ ityādiā samastam bheda jātam saha mahābhūtaiḥ aukramya sarvam tat prajñāetram prajñāe pratiṣṭhitam prajñāetraḥ lokaḥ prajñā pratiṣṭhā prajñāam brahma iti brahma ātmatva darśaam eva avadhārayati tasmāt iha ātma gṛhītiḥ iti aapavādam aparā ātma gṛhītiḥ itaravat uttarāt vājasaeyaka ikatamaḥ ātmā iti vijñā mayaḥ prāṇeṣu puruṣaḥ iti ātma śabdena upakramya tasya eva brahma ātmatām avadhārayati tathā hi upasaṃharati sa vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ ātmā ajaroma romṛta ubhayaḥ brahma iti chādogye tusat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam iti atareṇa eva ātma śabdam upakramya ātmā tat tvam asi iti tādātmyam upadiśati tatra saṃśayaḥ tulya ārthatvam syāt atulya ārthatvam vā iti atulya ārthatvam iti tāvat prāptam atulya tvāt āmāayoḥ a hi sati artha sāmyam yuktam pratipattum vājasaeyake ca ātma śabda upakramāt ātma tattva upadeśaḥ iti gamyate chādogye tu upakrama viparyayāt upadeśa viparyayaḥ chadogāām api asti udarke tādātmya upadeśaḥ iti uktam satyam uktam upakrama tatra tvāt upasaṃhārasya tādātmya saṃpattiḥ sā iti tathā prāpte abhidhīyate ātma gṛhītiḥ sat eva somya idam agre āsīt iti atra chadogāām api bhavitum arhati itaravat yathā katamaḥ ātmā iti atra vājasaeyiām ātma gṛhītiḥ tathā eva kasmāt uttarāt iti ced avadhāraṇāt yat uktam upakrama āvayāt upakrame ca ātma śabda śravaṇa abhāvāt ātma gṛhītiḥ iti tasya kaḥ parihāraḥ iti ced sā abhidhīyate syāt avadhāraṇāt iti bhavet iha ātma gṛhītiḥ avadhāraṇāt tathā hi ye āśrutam śrutam bhavati amatam matam avijñātam vijñātam iti sarvavijñāam avadhārya tat saṃpipādayiṣayā asadevaḥ iti āha tat ca ātma gṛhītau satyām saṃpadyate ayathā hi yaḥ yam mukhyaḥ ātmā sa a vijñātaḥ iti ā eva sarvavijñāam saṃpadyeta tathā prāk utpatteḥ ekatva ādhāraṇam jīvasya ca ātma śabde parāmarśaḥ svāpa avasthāyām ca paricoda ā pūrvakam ca puas puas tattvam asi iti avadhāraṇam iti ca sarvam etat tādātmya pratipāda āyām eva avakalpate a tādātmya saṃpāda āyām a ca atra upakrama tatratva upayāsaḥ yāyyaḥ a hi upakrame vā asti sāmāya upakramaḥ ca a vākyaśeṣa gate a viśeṣeṇa virudhyate viśeṣa ākaṅkṣi tvāt sāmāyasya sat śabda arthaḥ api ca saṃbhavati atoyasya vastu jātasya ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhyaḥ ṛta tva upapatteḥ api āvaśyam artha vaiṣamyam āvahati āhara pātram pātram āhara iti evamādiṣu artha sāmye pi tad darśaāt tasmāt evaṃjātīyakeṣu vākyeṣu pratipāda a prakāra bhede pi pratipādya artha abheda iti siddham kārya ākhyā āda pūrvam kārya ākhyā adhikaraṇam chadogāḥ vājasaeyiaḥ ca prāṇa saṃvāde śva ādi maryādam prāṇasya tasya eva āpaḥ vāsaḥ āmaati ca chadogāḥ tasmāt vai etat a śiṣyataḥ purastāt ca upariṣṭāt ca adbhiḥ paridadhati iti tad vidvāṃsaḥ śrotriyāḥ a śiṣyataḥ ācāmati aśitvā ca ācāmati etam eva tad aamaagam kurvataḥ tasmāt evaṃvid a śiṣya ācāmet aśitvā ca ācāmet etam eva tad aamaagam kurute iti tatra ca ca prāṇasya pratīyate tat kim ubhayam api vidhīyate uta vicāryate kim tāvat prāptam ubhayam api vidhīyate iti kutas ubhayasya api ubhayam api ca etat apūrva tvāt vidhi arham athavā ācamaam eva vidhīyate vispaṣṭā hi tasmāt evaṃvid a śiṣya ācāmet aśitvā ca ācāmet iti tasya eva stuti artham prāpte brūmaḥ vidheya tvam upapadyate kārya ākhyāāt prāptam eva hi idam prāyatyā artham smṛti prasiddham avākhyāyate iyam śrutiḥ tasyāḥ smṛteḥ mūlam syāt iti ucyate viṣaya āātvāt sāmāya viṣayā hi smṛtiḥ puruṣa mātra saṃbaddham prāyatyā artham ācamaam prāpayati śrutiḥ tu prāṇa vidyā prakaraṇa paṭhitā tad viṣayam eva ācamaam vidadhatī vidadhyāt ca śruti smṛtyoḥ ca iyam śrutiḥ prāṇa vidyā saṃyogi apūrvam ācamaam vidhāsyati iti śakyam āśrayitum pūrvasya eva iha pratyabhijñāyamāa tvāt atas eva ca ca vākyam bhidyeta tasmāt prāptam eva ca ubhayatas iti prāṇasya aa gata akaraṇa saṃkalpaḥ vākyea ācamaīyāsu apsu upadiśyate a ca ayam aagata vādaḥ ācamaa stuti arthaḥ iti yāyyam ācamaasya avidheya tvāt svayam ca aagata asaṃkalpasya vidheya tva pratīteḥ a ca evam sati ekasya ācamaasya ubhaya arthatā abhyupagatā bhavati prāyatya arthatā paridhā arthatā ca iti kriyātara tva abhyupagamāt kriyātaram eva hi prāyatyā artham puruṣasya abhyupagamyate tadīyāsu tu apsu kriyātaram eva paridhā artham prāṇasya abhyupagamyate iti aavadyam api ca yat idam kiṃca ā kṛmibhyaḥ ā kīṭa pataṃgebhyaḥ iti atra tāvat a sarva a abhyavahāraḥ codyate iti śakyam vaktum aśabda tvāt aśakya tvāt ca sarvam tu iyam a dṛṣṭiḥ codyate tad sāhacaryāt ca apaḥ vāsaḥ iti atra api a sarva codyate prasiddhāsu eva tu ācamaīyāsu apsu paridhā adṛṣṭiḥ codyate iti yuktam hi ardhavaiśasam saṃbhavati api ca ācāmati iti śabdaḥ vidhi kṣamaḥ mayataḥ iti api satyam eva tat avaśya vidheye tu apām apūrvam vidhīyate pūrvavat hi tat iti upapāditam yat api uktam vispaṣṭā ca ācamae vidhi vibhaktiḥ iti tat api pratyuktam atas eva ācamaasya a vidhitsita tvāt etam eva iti atra eva kāṇvāḥ paryavasyati ityādi tasmāt pāṭhe evaṃvid tvam eva prakṛta prāṇa vāsaḥ vid tvam vidhīyate iti pratipattavyam yaḥ upi ayam abhyupagamaḥ kvacid vidhīyatām kvacid vāsas vijñāam iti saḥ api sādhuḥ apaḥ vāsaḥ iti ādikāyāḥ vākya pravṛtteḥ sarvatra aikarūpyāt tasmāt vāsaḥ vijñāam eva iha vidhīyate a ācamaam iti yāyyam evam ca abhedāt vājasaeyi śākhāyām agi rahasye vidyā vijñātā tatra ca guṇāḥ śrūyate saḥ ātmā aam upāsīta maaḥ mayam prāṇa śarīram bhā rūpam iti evamādayaḥ tasyām eva śākhāyām bṛhadāraṇyake puas paṭhyate maaḥ mayaḥ yam puruṣaḥ bhās satyaḥ tasmin atas hṛdaye yathā vrīhiḥ vā yavaḥ vā saḥ eṣa sarvasya īśāḥ sarvasya adhipatiḥ sarvam idam praśāsti yat idam kiṃca iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iyam ekā vidyā agi rahasya bṛhat āraṇyakayoḥ guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ ca uta dve ime vidye guṇa a upasaṃhāraḥ ca iti kim tāvat prāptam vidyā bhedaḥ guṇa vyavasthā ca iti kutas pauaruktya prasaṅgāt bhiāsu hi śākhāsu adhyetṛ veditṛ bhedāt pauaruktya parihāram ālocya vidyā ekatvam adhyavasāya ekatra atiriktāḥ guṇāḥ itaratra upasaṃhriyate prāṇa saṃvāda ādiṣu iti uktam ekasyām puas śākhāyām adhyetṛ veditṛ bheda abhāvāt aśakya parihāre pauaruktye a viprakraṣṭa deśa sthā ekā vidyā bhavitum arhati ca atra vidyā vidyā vidyā vidyā aparam guṇa vidhā artham iti vibhāgaḥ saṃbhavati tadā hi atiriktāḥ eva guṇāḥ itaratra itaratra ca a samāḥ api tu ubhayatra āmāyate maomaya tva ādayaḥ tasmāt āyoya guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ iti evam prāpte brūmahe yathā śākhāsu vidyā eka tvam guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ ca bhavati evam ekasyām api śākhāyām bhavitum arhati upāsya abhedāt tat eva hi brahma maomayatva ādi guṇakam ubhayatra api upāsyam upāsyam ca rūpam vidyāyāḥ ca rūpa abhede vidyā bhedam adhyavasātum śakumaḥ pauaruktya prasaṅgāt vidyā bheda udhyavasitaḥ eti ucyate artha vibhāga upapatteḥ ekam hi vidyā vidhā artham aparam guṇa vidhā artham iti a kiṃcid upapadyate evam sati yat apaṭhitam agi rahasye tat eva bṛhadāraṇyake paṭhitavyam saḥ eṣa sarvasya īśaḥ ityādi yat tu paṭhitam evam aomayaḥ ityādi paṭhitavyam ā eṣa doṣaḥ hi viprakṛṣṭa deśām śāṇḍilya vidyām pratyabhijñāpya tasyām īśa a tva ādi upadiśyate ayathā hi katham tasyām ayam guṇa vidhiḥ abhidhīyate api ca arthavati vākye saṃjāte prāpta aṃśa parāmarśasya upapadyamāa tvāt pratyabhijñā upekṣitum śakyate tasmāt atra vidyā ekatvam guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ ca iti upapaam bṛhadāraṇyake satyam brahma iti upakramya tat yat tat satyam asau saḥ ādityaḥ yaḥ eṣaḥ etasmin maṇḍale puruṣaḥ yaḥ ca ayam dakṣiṇa ikṣa puruṣaḥ iti tasya eva satyasya brahmaṇaḥ adhidaivatam adhyātmam ca āyata aviśeṣam upadiśya vyāhṛti śarīra tvam ca saṃpādya dve upaiṣadau ādiśyete tasya upaiṣadahaḥ iti adhidaivatam tasya upaiṣadaham iti adhyātmam tatra saṃśayaḥ kim avibhāge eva ubhe api upaiṣadau ubhayatra ausaṃdhātavye uta vibhāge ekā adhidaivatam ekā adhyātmam iti tatra sūtreṇa eva upakramate yathā śāṇḍilya vidyāyām guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ uktaḥ evam ayatra api evaṃjātīyake viṣaye bhavitum arhati eka vidyā abhisaṃbadhāt ekā hi iyam satya vidyā adhidaivatam adhyātmam ca adhītā upakrama abhedāt vyatiṣakta pāṭhāt ca katham tasyām uditaḥ dharmaḥ tasyām eva syāt yaḥ hi ācārye kaścid augama ādiḥ ācāraḥ coditaḥ sa grāma gata iraṇya gate ca tulya vat eva bhavati tasmāt ubhayoḥ api upaiṣadoḥ ubhayatra prāptiḥ iti evam prāpte pratividhatte a vā viśeṣāt ā eva ubhayoḥ ubhayatra prāptiḥ kasmāt viśeṣāt katham sthā a viśeṣa upaibadhaḥ iti ucyate yaḥ eṣa etasmin maṇḍale puruṣaḥ iti hi ādhidaivikam puruṣam prakṛtyā tasya upaiṣat ahar iti śrāvayati yaḥ yam dakṣiṇa īkṣa puruṣaḥ iti ca ādhyātmikam puruṣam prakṛtyā tasya upaiṣat aham iti tasya iti ca etat saṃihita avalambaam tasmāt āyata a viśeṣa vyapāśrayeṇa eva ete upaiṣadau upadiśyete kutas ubhayoḥ ubhayatra prāptiḥ ekaḥ eva ayam adhidaivatam adhyātmam ca puruṣaḥ ekasya eva satyasya brahmaṇaḥ satyam evam etat ekasya api tu upaiṣad viśeṣa upadeśāt tad avasthasya eva sā bhavitum arhati asti ca ayam dṛṣṭātaḥ sati api ācārya sva rūpa a apāye yat ācāryasya tat tiṣṭhataḥ bhavati yat ca tiṣṭhataḥ uktam a grāma araṇyayoḥ tu ācārya sva rūpa apāyāt ca dharmasya grāma araṇya kṛta viśeṣa abhāvāt ubhayatra tulyavat bhāvaḥ iti adṛṣṭātaḥ saḥ tasmāt vyavasthā darśayati ca api ca evaṃjātīyakāām dharmāṇām vyavasthā iti liṅga darśaam bhavati tasya etasya tat eva rūpam yat amuṣya rūpam yau amuṣya geṣṇau tau geṣṇau iti katham asya liṅga tvam iti tat ucyate dharmāḥ akṣi puruṣe upasaṃharati tasya etasya tat eva rūpam ityādi tasmāt vyavatiṣṭhete eva ete upaiṣadau iti ca atas saṃbhṛti adhikaraṇam brahma jyeṣṭhāḥ saṃbhṛtāi brahma agre jyeṣṭham divam ātatai iti evam rāṇāyaīyāām khileṣu vīrya saṃbhṛti dyuiveśa prabhṛtayaḥ brahmaṇaḥ vibhūtayaḥ paṭhyate teṣām eva ca upaiṣadi śāṇḍilya vidyā prabhṛtayaḥ brahma vidyāḥ paṭhyate tāsu brahma vidyāsu tāḥ brahma vibhūtayaḥ upasaṃhriyera a vā iti vicāraṇāyām evam paṭhati saṃbhṛti dyu vyāpti prabhṛtayaḥ vibhūtayaḥ śāṇḍilya vidyā prabhṛtiṣu opasaṃhartavyāḥ atas eva ca āyata aviśeṣa yogāt tathā hi śāṇḍilya vidyāyām hṛdaya āyata atvam brahmaṇaḥ uktam eṣa me ātmā atas hṛdaye iti tadvat eva dahara vidyāyām api daharam puṇḍarīkam veśma iti upakosala vidyāyām tu akṣi āyata atvam yaḥ eṣa ukṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate iti evam tatra tatra tat tat etāsu vidyāsu pratīyate ādhidaivikyaḥ tu etāḥ vibhūtayaḥ saṃbhṛti dyu vyāpti prabhṛtayaḥ tāsām kutas etāsu prāptiḥ avetāsu api ādhidaivikyaḥ vibhūtayaḥ śrūyate jyāyāḥ divaḥ jyāyāḥ ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ eṣaḥ u eva bhāmaīḥ eṣa hi sarveṣu lokeṣu bhāti yau ava ayam ākāśaḥ tāvā eṣa utar hṛdaye ākāśe ubhe asmin yāvāpṛthivī atas eva samāhite iti evamādyāḥ sati ca ayā api iha brahma vidyāḥ ṣoḍaśa kalā ādyāḥ satyam evam etat tathā api atra vidyate viśeṣaḥ hi pratyupasthāpitāsu viprakṛṣṭa deśāsu api vidyāsu viprakṛṣṭa deśa guṇāḥ upasaṃhriyera eti yuktam saṃbhṛti ādayaḥ tu śāṇḍilya ādi vākya gocarāḥ ca guṇāḥ paraspara vyāvṛtta svarūpa tvāt a ca ca brahma saṃbadha mātreṇa ca ucyate vidyā bhede pi tad upapatteḥ ekam api hi brahma upāsyate iti sthitiḥ paraḥ varīyaḥ tva ādi vat bheda darśaāt tasmāt śāṇḍilya vidyā ādiṣu aupasaṃhāraḥ iti puruṣa vidyāyām iva puruṣa vidyā adhikaraṇam asti tāṇḍiām paiṅgiām ca rahasyabrāhmaṇe puruṣa vidyā tatra puruṣaḥ yajñaḥ kalpitaḥ tadīyam āyuḥ tredhā vibhajya ca dīkṣā ādi bhāvea ca dīkṣā ādi bhāvea ca dharmāḥ tatra samadhigatāḥ āśīḥ matra prayoga ādayaḥ taittirīyakāḥ api kaṃcid puruṣa yajñam kalpayati tasya evaṃviduṣaḥ yajñasya ātmā yajamāaḥ śraddhā patī tatra saṃśayaḥ kim itaratra uktāḥ puruṣa yajñasya dharmāḥ taittirīyakeṣu upasaṃhartavyāḥ kim vā opasaṃhartavyāḥ iti puruṣa yajña tva aviśeṣāt upasaṃhāra prāptau ācakṣmahe opasaṃhartavyāḥ iti kasmāt tad rūpa pratyabhijñā ābhāvāt tat āha ācāryaḥ puruṣa vidyāyām iva iti yathā ekeṣām tāṇḍiām paiṅgiām ca puruṣa vidyāyām itareṣām taittirīyāṇām asti teṣām hi itara vilakṣaṇam eva yajña saṃpādaam dṛśyate tat api itara vilakṣaṇam eva yat prātar madhyaṃdina sāyam ca iti yat api kiṃcid maraṇa avabhṛtha tva ādi sāmāyam tat api alpīyaḥ tvāt bhūyasā ca taittirīyake puruṣasya yajña tvam śrūyate viduṣaḥ yajñasya iti hi a ca ete sama ā adhikaraṇe ṣaṣṭhyau vidvā eva yaḥ yajñaḥ tasya iti a hi puruṣasya mukhyam yajña tvam asti vyadhikaraṇe tu ete ṣaṣṭhyau viduṣaḥ yaḥ yajñaḥ tasya iti bhavati hi puruṣasya mukhyaḥ satyām ca gatau mukhyaḥ eva arthaḥ āśrayitavyaḥ a bhāktaḥ ātmā iti ca puruṣasya vaiyadhikaraṇyeā eva asya darśayati api ca tasya evaṃviduṣaḥ iti siddhavat auvāda śrutau satyām puruṣasya yajña bhāvam ca ca vākya bhedaḥ syāt api ca sa saṃyāsām ātma vidyām purastāt upadiśya paśyataḥ
