pūrva śeṣaḥ eva eṣa āmāyaḥ a svatatra iti pratīmaḥ tathā ca ekam eva phalam ubhayoḥ api auvākayoḥ upalabhāmahe brahmaṇaḥ mahimā iti itareṣām tu puruṣa vidyā māyaḥ āyuḥ abhivṛddhi phalaḥ ṣoḍaśam varṣa śatam jīvati yaḥ evam veda iti samabhivyāhārāt tasmāt śākhātara adhītāām puruṣa vidyā dharmāṇām āśīḥ matra ādīām aprāptiḥ taittirīyake vedha ādi artha bhedāt vedha ādi adhikaraṇam sarvam pravidhya hṛdayam pravidhya dhamaīḥ pravṛjya śirobhiḥ pravṛjya tridhā vipṛktaḥ ityādiḥ tāṇḍiām deva savitar prasuva yajñam ityādiḥ śāṭyāyaiām śvetāśvaḥ ityādiḥ kaṭhāām taittirīyāṇām ca śam o mitraḥ śam varuṇaḥ ityādiḥ vājasaeyiām tu upaiṣad ārambhe pravargya brāhmaṇam paṭhyate devāḥ ha vai satram ityādi kauṣītakiām api agiṣṭoma brāhmaṇam brahma vai agiṣṭomaḥ brahma eva tat ahar brahmaṇā eva te brahma upayati tāḥ imṛta tvam āpuvati yaḥ etat ahar upayati iti kim ime sarve pravidhi ādayaḥ matrāḥ ca karmāṇi vidyāsu upasaṃhriyera kim vā a upasaṃhriyera iti mīmāṃsāmahe kim tāvat pratibhāti upasaṃhāraḥ eva eṣām vidyāsu iti kutas samīpe pāṭhāt eṣām vidyā artha tayā opalabhāmahe bāḍham api tu saṃidhi sāmarthyāt hi saṃidheḥ arthavat tve saṃbhavati akasmāt asau a āśrayitum yuktaḥ ā eṣām matrāṇām vidyā viṣayam kiṃcid sāmarthyam paśyāmaḥ katham ca pravargya ādīni karmāṇi sati vidyā artha tve api pratipadyemahi iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ sāmarthyam tāvat matrāṇām vidyā viṣayam api kiṃcid śakyam kalpayitum hṛdaya ādi saṃkīrtaāt hi prāyeṇa upāsaeṣu tad dvāreṇa ca hṛdayam pravidhya iti evaṃjātīyakāām matrāṇām dṛṣṭaḥ ca upāsaeṣu api matra viiyogaḥ bhūḥ iti evamādiḥ tathā pravargya ādīām karmaṇām a yatra api viiyuktāām satām aviruddhaḥ vidyāsu viiyogaḥ vājapeyaḥ iva bṛhaspatisavasya iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ ā eṣām upasaṃhāraḥ vidyāsu iti kasmāt vedha ādi artha bhedāt hṛdayam pravidhya iti evaṃjātīyakāām hi matrāṇām hṛdaya vedha ādayaḥ bhiāḥ a abhisaṃbaddhāḥ te upaiṣat uditābhiḥ vidyābhiḥ a teṣām tābhiḥ saṃgatum sāmarthyam asti hṛdayasya hṛdayasya upāsa eṣu api upayogāt tad dvārakaḥ upayastaḥ eti ucyate hṛdaya mātra saṃkīrtaasya hi evam upayogaḥ kathaṃcid utprekṣyeta ca hṛdaya mātram atra matra arthaḥ hṛdayam pravidhya dhamaīḥ pravṛjya iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ hi a sakalaḥ matra arthaḥ vidyābhiḥ abhisaṃbadhyate abhicāra viṣayaḥ hi eṣaḥ ṛthaḥ tasmāt ābhicārikeṇa karmaṇā sarvam pravidhya iti etasya matrasya abhisaṃbadhaḥ tathā deva savitar prasuva yajñam iti asya yajña prasava liṅga tvāt karmaṇā tad viśeṣa saṃbadhaḥ tu pramāṇa atara ādau sartavyaḥ matrāṇām keṣāṃcid keṣāṃcid keṣāṃcid pramāṇa atareṇa iti evam artha atareṣu rahasya paṭhitāām api satām a saṃidhi mātreṇa vidyā śeṣa tva upapattiḥ durbalaḥ hi saṃidhiḥ śruti ādibhyaḥ iti uktam prathame tatre samavāye pāra daurbalyam artha viprakarṣāt iti atra tathā karmaṇām api a vidyā śeṣa tva upapattiḥ a hi eṣām vidyābhiḥ saha aikārthyam kiṃcid asti vājapeye tu bṛhaspatisavasya spaṣṭam viiyogātaram vājapeye iṣṭvā bṛhaspatisave yajeta iti api ca pravargyaḥ balīyasā viiyuktaḥ a durbale viiyogam arhati agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa tve hi pramāṇayoḥ evam syāt a tu balavat abalavatoḥ pramāṇayoḥ agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa tā saṃbhavati balavat abalavat tva viśeṣāt eva tasmāt evaṃjātīyakāām matrāṇām karmaṇām vā a saṃidhi pāṭha mātreṇa vidyā śeṣa tvam āśaṅkitavyam tu saṃidhi pāṭhaḥ iti saṃtoṣṭavyam tu upāya a śabda śeṣa tvāt tat uktam asti tāṇḍiām śrutiḥ aśvaḥ iva romāṇi vidhūya pāpam cadra madhu adhikaraṇam asti śrutiḥ aśvaḥ iva romāṇi vidhūya pāpam cadra madhu adhikaraṇam iva rāhoḥ mukhāt pramucya dhūtvā śarīram akṛtam kṛtātmā brahma lokam abhisaṃbhavāmi iti tathā ātharvaṇikāām tathā vidvāḥ āma rūpāt vimuktaḥ parāt param puruṣam upaiti divyam iti tathā śāṭyāyaiaḥ paṭhati tasya putrāḥ dāyam upayati suhṛdaḥ sādhu kṛtyām dviṣataḥ pāpa kṛtyām iti tathā eva kauṣītakiaḥ tat sukṛta duṣkṛte vidhūute tasya priyā jñātayaḥ sukṛtam upayati apriyāḥ duṣkṛtam iti tat iha kvacid sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ śrūyate kvacid tayoḥ eva vibhāge priyaiḥ apriyaiḥ kvacid tu ubhayam api ca tat yatra ubhayam śrūyate tatra tāvat a kiṃcid vaktavyam asti yatra api eva śrūyate tatra api arthāt eva hāam saṃipatati ātmīyayoḥ sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ āvaśyaka tvāt tat hāasya yatra tu hāam eva śrūyate tatra upāyaam saṃipatet vā a vā iti vicikitsāyām aśravaṇāt asaṃipātaḥ vidyā tara gocara tvāt ca śākhātarīyasya śravaṇasya api ca ātma kartṛkam sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ para kartṛkam tu tayoḥ asati āvaśyaka bhāve katham ākṣipyeta tasmāt a saṃipātaḥ hāau upāyaasya iti asyām prāptau paṭhati hāau iti hāau tu etasyām kevalāyām api śrūyamāṇāyām upāyaam saṃipatitum arhati tad śeṣa tvāt hā a śabda śeṣaḥ hi upāya a śabdaḥ samadhigataḥ kauṣītakirahasye tasmāt upāya āu vṛttiḥ yat uktam aśravaṇāt vidyā tara gocara tvāt a āvaśyaka tvāt ca a saṃipātaḥ iti tat ucyate bhavet eṣā vyavasthā uktiḥ yadi auṣṭheyam kiṃcid ayatra śrutam ayatra vā saṃkīrtyate vidyā stuti artham tu ittham mahābhāgā vidyā yad sāmarthyāt asya viduṣaḥ sukṛta duṣkṛte saṃsāra kāraṇa bhūte vidhūyete te ca asya suhṛd durhṛtsu iti stuti arthe ca asmi kvacid śruta tvāt ayatra api hāa śrutau stuti prakarṣa lābhāya prasiddhā ca arthavāda atara apekṣā arthavāda atara pravṛttiḥ ekaviṃśaḥ vai itas asau ādityaḥ iti evamādiṣu katham hi iha ekaviṃśatā ādityasya abhidhīyeta a apekṣyamāṇe rthavāda ātare dvādaśa māsāḥ pañca ṛtavaḥ trayaḥ ime lokāḥ asau ādityaḥ ekaviṃśaḥ iti asmi tathā triṣṭubhau bhavataḥ sa idriya tvāya iti evamādi vādeṣu idriyam vai triṣṭubh iti evamādi arthavāda atara apekṣā dṛśyate vidyā stuti artha tvāt ca asya upāyaa vādasya katham ayadīye sukṛta duṣkṛte upeyete iti upāya a śabda śeṣa tvāt iti ca śabda śabdam samuccāraya stuti arthām eva hāāu sūcayati guṇa upasaṃhāra vivakṣāyām hi upāya arthasya eva hāāu brūyāt tasmāt guṇa upasaṃhāra vicāra prasaṅgea stuti upasaṃhāra pradarśa artham idam sūtram iti upamā upādāam tat yathā kuśāḥ vāaspatyāḥ sthata mā pāta iti etasmin a game kuśāām aviśeṣeṇa iti audumbaryaḥ kuśāḥ āśrīyate yathā ca kvacid deva asuracchada sāma viśeṣeṇa paurvāparya prasaṅge deva chadāṃsi pūrvāṇi iti yathā ca ṣoḍaśi stotre keṣāṃcid kāla aviśeṣa prāptau samaya adhyuṣite sūrye iti ārca śruteḥ kāla viśeṣa pratipattiḥ yathā eva ca aviśeṣeṇa upagāaṃ iti kecid samāmaati viśeṣeṇa bhāllaviḥ yathā eteṣu kuśa ādiṣu evam hāau api upāya āvayaḥ iti arthaḥ śrutyatara kṛtam hi viśeṣam śrutyatare abhyupagacchataḥ sarvatra eva vikalpaḥ syāt sa ca ayāyyaḥ satyām gatau tat uktam dvādaśalakṣaṇyām api tu vākyaśeṣa tvāt itara paryudāsaḥ syāt pratiṣedhe vikalpaḥ syāt iti athavā etāsu eva sūtreṇa etat citayitavyam sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ hāam abhidhīyate kim vā arthātaram iti tatra ca evam prāpayitavyam iti smaraṇāt dodhūyate dhvaja agrāṇi iti ca cālyamāeṣu dhvaja agreṣu prayoga darśaāt tasmāt cālaam vidhūaam abhidhīyate cālaam tu sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ kaṃcid kālam phala pratibadhaāt iti evam prāpayya prativaktavyam hāāveva eṣa vidhūaa śabdaḥ vartitum arhati upāyaa śabda śeṣa tvāt hi para parigraha bhūtayoḥ sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ aprahīṇayoḥ paraiḥ upāyam saṃbhavati yadi api idam parakīyayoḥ sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ āñjasam saṃbhāvyate tathā api tad āuguṇyena śakyate kvacid api ca idam śrūyamāṇam kuśācchada stuti upagāa vat vidhūa a śrutyā sarvatra apekṣyamāṇam sārvatrikam irṇaya kāraṇam saṃpadyate ca dhvaja agra vat sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ mukhyam saṃbhavati adravya tvāt aśvaḥ ca romāṇi tyaja rajaḥ saha eva te romāṇi api śātayati aśvaḥ iva romāṇi vidhūya pāpam iti ca brāhmaṇam a eka artha tva abhyupagamāt ca dhātūām a smaraṇa virodhaḥ tat uktam iti vyākhyātam sāmparāye tartavya abhāvāt tathā sāṃparāya adhikaraṇam pathā paryaṅka stham brahma abhiprasthitasya sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ viyogam kauṣītakiaḥ paryaṅka vidyāyām āmaati saḥ etam deva yāam pathāam āsādya āgi lokam āgacchati iti āgacchati virajām tām maasā eva atyeti tat sukṛta duṣkṛte vidhūute iti tat kim yathāśrutam pratipattavyam āhosvit ādau eva dehāt apasarpaṇe iti vicāraṇāyām śruti prāmāṇyāt yathāśruti pratipatti prasaktau paṭhati sāṃparāye iti sāṃparāye eva dehāt apasarpaṇe idam vidyā sāmarthyāt sukṛta duṣkṛta hāam bhavati iti hetum ca ācaṣṭe tartavya abhāvāt iti a hi viduṣaḥ saṃparetasya vidyayā brahma saṃprepsataḥ atarāle sukṛta duṣkṛtābhyām kiṃcid prāptavyam asti yad artham katicid kṣaṇāḥ akṣīṇe te kalpeyātām vidyā viruddha phala tvāt ca tayoḥ kṣayaḥ sa ca yadā eva vidyā phala abhimukhī tadā eva bhavitum arhati tasmāt prāk eva sa ayam sukṛta duṣkṛta kṣayaḥ paścāt paṭhyate tathā hi śākhiaḥ tāṇḍiaḥ śāṭyāyaiaḥ ca prāc avasthāyām eva aśvaḥ iva romāṇi vidhūya pāpam iti tasya putrāḥ dāyam upayati suhṛdaḥ sādhu kṛtyām dviṣataḥ pāpa kṛtyām iti ca chadataḥ ubhaya avirodhāt yadi ca dehāt apasṛptasya pathā prasthitasya ardha pathe sukṛta duṣkṛta kṣayaḥ abhyupagamyeta tatas patite dehe yama eyama vidyā abhyāsa ātmakasya sukṛta duṣkṛta kṣaya hetoḥ puruṣa yatasya aupapattiḥ eva tad hetukasya sukṛta duṣkṛta kṣayasya syāt tasmāt pūrvam eva sādhaka avasthāyām tasya syāt tad pūrvakam ca iti draṣṭavyam evam imitta aimittikayoḥ upapattiḥ tāṇḍi śāṭyāya eśrutyoḥ ca saṃgatiḥ iti gateḥ arthavat tvam ubhayathā yathā hi virodhaḥ gateḥ arthavat tva adhikaraṇam kvacid śrūyate tatra saṃśayaḥ kim pathāḥ śrūyate hāāva viśeṣeṇa eva deva yāaḥ pathāḥ saṃipatet uta kvacid saṃipatet kvacid iti yathā tāvat hāāva viśeṣeṇa eva upāya āu vṛttiḥ uktā evam bhavitum arhati iti asyām prāptau ācakṣmahe gateḥ deva yāasya pathaḥ arthavat tvam ubhayathā vibhāge bhavitum arhati kvacid arthavatī gatiḥ kvacid iti a aviśeṣeṇa ayathā hi aviśeṣeṇa eva etasyām gatau aṅgīkriyamāṇāyām virodhaḥ syāt puṇya pāpe vidhūya irañjaḥ paramam sāmyam upaiti iti asyām śrutau deśa atara prāpaṇī gatiḥ virudhyeta katham hi irañjaogatā deśa ataram gacchet gatavyam ca paramam sāmyam a deśa atara prāpti āyattam iti āarthakyam eva atra gateḥ mayāmahe tad lakṣaṇa artha upalabdheḥ loka vat ubhayathā bhāvaḥ kvacid arthavatī gatiḥ tad lakṣaṇa artha upalabdheḥ gati kāraṇa bhūta ūrthaḥ paryaṅka vidyā ādiṣu saguṇeṣu upāsaeṣu upalabhyate tatra hi paryaṅka ārohaṇam brahmaṇā saha viśiṣṭa gadha ādi prāptiḥ ca iti evamādi bahu deśa atara prāpti āyattam phalam śrūyate tatra arthavatī gatiḥ a tu samyak darśae tad lakṣaṇa artha upalabdhiḥ asti a hi ātma ekatva darśi āpta kāmāām iha eva dagdha aśeṣa kleśa bījāām ārabdha bhoga karma āśaya kṣapaṇa vyatirekeṇa apekṣitavyam kiṃcid asti tatra aarthikā gatiḥ loka vat ca eṣa vibhāgaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ yathā loke grāma prāptau deśa atara prāpaṇaḥ pathā apekṣyate a ārogya prāptau evam iha api iti bhūyas ca vibhāgam caturtha adhyāye ipuṇataram upapādayiṣyāmaḥ aiyamaḥ sarvāsām avirodhaḥ śabda auma ābhyām aiyama adhikaraṇam saguṇāsu vidyāsu gatiḥ arthavatī paramātma vidyāyām iti uktam saguṇāsu api vidyāsu kāsucid gatiḥ śrūyate yathā paryaṅka vidyāyām upakosala vidyāyām pañcāgi vidyāyām dahara vidyāyām iti adhikaraṇam yathā madhu vidyāyām śāṇḍilya vidyāyām ṣoḍaśakala vidyāyām vaiśvāara vidyāyām iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim yāsu eṣā gatiḥ śrūyate tāsu eva iyamyeta uta aiyamea sarvābhiḥ eva evaṃjātīyakābhiḥ vidyābhiḥ abhisaṃbadhyeta iti kim tāvat prāptam iyamaḥ iti yatra eva śrūyate tatra eva bhavitum arhati prakaraṇasya iyāmaka tvāt yadi a yatra a śrūyamāṇā api gatiḥ vidyātaram gacchet śruti ādīām prāmāṇyam hīyeta sarvasya sarva artha tva prasaṅgāt api ca arciḥ ādikā ekā eva gatiḥ upakosala vidyāyām pañcāgi vidyāyām ca tulya vat paṭhyate tat syāt tasmāt aiyamaḥ iti evam prāpte paṭhati aiyamaḥ iti sarvāsām eva abhyudaya prāpti phalāām sa guṇāām vidyāām aviśeṣeṇa eṣā devayā ākhyā gatiḥ bhavitum arhati aiyama abhyupagame prakaraṇa virodhaḥ uktaḥ virodhaḥ śruti smṛtibhyām iti arthaḥ tathā hi śrutiḥ tat ye ittham viduḥ iti pañcāgi vidyāvatām devayāam avatārayati iye ceme iraṇye śraddhā tapaḥ iti upāsate iti vidyātara śīliām api pañcāgi vidyā vidbhiḥ samāa mārga tām gamayati katham vidyātara śīliām iyam gatiḥ iti śraddhā tapaḥ parāyaṇāām eva syāt ta mātra śravaṇāt ā eṣa doṣaḥ a hi kevalābhyām śraddhā tapobhyām atareṇa vidyā balam eṣā gatiḥ labhyate vidyayā tat ārohati yatra kāmāḥ parāgatāḥ a tatra dakṣiṇāḥ yati āvidvāṃsaḥ tapasviḥ iti śrutyatarāt tasmāt iha śraddhā tapobhyām vidyātara upalakṣaṇam vājasaeyiḥ tu pañcāgi vidyā adhikāre dhīyate yaḥ evam etat viduḥ ye ca amī araṇye śraddhām satyam upāsate iti tatra śraddhālavaḥ ye satyam brahma upāsate iti vyākhyeyam satya śabdasya brahmaṇi asakṛt prayukta tvāt pañcāgi vidyā vidām ca itthaṃvittayā eva upātta tvāt vidyā tara parāyaṇāām eva etat upādāam yāyyam atha ye etau pathau viduḥ te kīṭāḥ pataṅgāḥ yat idam dadaśūkam iti ca mārga dvaya bhraṣṭāām kaṣṭām adhogatim gamayatī śrutiḥ deva yāa pitṛyāṇayoḥ eva atas bhāvayati tatra api vidyā viśeṣāt eṣām smṛtiḥ api śukla kṛṣṇe gatī hi ete jagataḥ śāśvate mate ekayā puas iti yat puas devayāasya pathaḥ upakosala vidyāyām pañcāgi vidyāyām ca tat ubhayatra api aucita ārtham tasmāt aiyamaḥ yāvadadhikāram avasthitiḥ ādhikārikāṇām yāvat adhikāra adhikaraṇam viduṣaḥ deha ataram utpadyate vā iti cityate vidyāyāḥ saṃpattau kaivalyaiḥ vṛttiḥ syāt a vā iti citā upapadyate a hi odaaḥ bhavet a vā iti citā saṃbhavati ā api tṛpyet a vā iti cityate upapaā tu iyam citā brahma vidām api keṣāṃcid itihāsa purāṇayoḥ deha atara utpatti darśaāt tathā hi veda ācāryaḥ purāṇa ṛṣiḥ kali dvāparayoḥ saṃdhau kṛṣṇadvaipāyaaḥ saṃbabhūva iti smarati vasiṣṭhaḥ ca brahmaṇaḥ putraḥ saḥ imi śāpāt apagata pūrva dehaḥ puar brahmā ādeśāḥ mitrāvaruṇābhyām saṃbabhūva iti bhṛgu ādīām api brahmaṇaḥ eva māasa putrāṇām vāruṇe yajñe utpattiḥ smaryate saatkumāraḥ api brahmaṇaḥ eva māasaḥ putraḥ svayam rudrāya vara pradāāt prādurbabhūva evam eva dakṣa ārada prabhṛtīām bhūyasī deha atara utpattiḥ kathyate smṛtau śrutau api matra arthavādayoḥ prāyeṇa upalakṣyate te ca kecid patite pūrva dehe dehātaram ādadate kecid tu sthite eva yoga aiśvarya vaśāt sarve ca ete samadhigata sakala veda arthāḥ smaryate tat eteṣām deha atara utpatti darśaāt prāptam brahma vidyāyāḥ pākṣikam mokṣa hetu tvam ahetu tvam vā iti atas uttaram ucyate teṣām veda pravarta ādiṣu loka sthiti hetuṣu adhikāreṣu adhikāra tatra tvāt sthiteḥ yathā asau bhagavā savitā sahasra yuga paryatam jagataḥ dhikāram caritvā tad avasāe udaya astamaya varjitam kaivalyam atha tatas ūrdhvaḥ udetya a eva udetā āstametā ekalaḥ eva madhye sthātā iti śruteḥ yathā ca vartamāā brahma vidaḥ ārabdha bhoga kṣaye kaivalyam tasya tāvat eva ciram a vimokṣye saṃpatsye iti śruteḥ evam pi īśvarāḥ parameśvareṇa teṣu teṣu adhikāreṣu sataḥ sati api samyagdarśae kaivalya hetau akṣīṇa karmāṇaḥ yāvat adhikāram avatiṣṭhate ca iti aviruddham sakṛt pravṛttam eva hi te phalāt āāya karma āśayam ativāhayataḥ svātatryeṇa eva gṛhāt iva gṛhātaram ayam ayam deham saṃcarataḥ a parimuṣita smṛtaye eva deha idriya prakṛti vaśi tvāt yugapad krameṇa vā adhitiṣṭhati a ca ete jātismarāḥ iti ucyate te eva ete iti smṛti prasiddheḥ yathā hi vyudasya svam deham jāakam deham āviśya vyudya paścāt svam eva deham āviveśa iti smaryate yadi hi upayukte sakṛt pravṛtte karmaṇi karma ātaram deha atara ārambha kāraṇam āvirbhavet tatas ayat api adagdha bījam karma ataram tadvat eva prasajyeta iti brahmavidyāyāḥ pākṣikam mokṣa hetu tvam ahetu tvam vā śaṅkyeta a tu iyam āśaṅkā yuktā jñāāt karma bīja dāhasya śruti smṛti prasiddha tvāt tathā hi śrutiḥ bhidyate hṛdayagrathiḥ chidyate sarva saṃśayāḥ kṣīyate ca asya karmāṇi dṛṣṭe parāvare iti smṛti lambhe vipramokṣaḥ iti ca evamādyā smṛtiḥ api yathā edhāṃsi samiddhaḥ giḥ bhasmasāt kurute sarva karmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute tathā iti rohati yathā puas jñā a dagdhaiḥ tathā kleśaiḥ ātmā saṃpadyate iti ca evamādyāḥ ca avidyā ādi kleśa dāhe sati kleśa bījasya karma āśayasya eka deśa dāhaḥ eka deśa prarohaḥ ca iti upapadyate hi agi dagdhasya śāli bījasya eka deśa prarohaḥ dṛśyate pravṛtta phalasya tu karma āśayasya mukta iṣoḥ iva vega kṣayāt tasya tāvat eva ciram iti śarīrapātau adhikṣepa karaṇāt tasmāt yāvadadhikāram ādhikārikāṇām avasthitiḥ ca jñā a phalasya aaikātika tā tathā ca śrutiḥ aviśeṣeṇa eva sarveṣām jñāā mokṣam darśayati tat yaḥ yaḥ devāām prati abudhyata saḥ eva tat abhavat tathā ṛṣīṇām tathā mauṣyāṇām iti jñāātareṣu ca aiśvarya ādi phaleṣu āsaktāḥ syuḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ te paścāt aiśvarya kṣaya darśae irviṇṇāḥ paramātma jñāe pariiṣṭhāya kaivalyam prāpuḥ iti upapadyate brahmaṇā saha te sarve saṃprāpte pratisaṃcare kṛtātmā aḥ praviśati param padam iti smaraṇāt pratyakṣa phala tvāt ca jñāasya phala viraha āśaṅkā upapattiḥ karma phale hi svarga ādau aubhava ārūḍhe syāt āśaṅkā bhavet vā a vā iti aubhava ārūḍham tu jñā a phalam yat sāṃkṣāt aparokṣāt brahma iti śruteḥ tat tvam asi iti siddha vat upadeśāt a hi tat tvam asi iti asya vākyasya arthaḥ tat tvam mṛtaḥ bhaviṣyasi iti evam pariṇetum śakyaḥ tat ha etat paśya ṛṣiḥ vāmadevaḥ pratipede ham mauḥ abhavam sūryaḥ ca iti ca samyak darśa a kālam eva tad phalam sarva ātma tvam darśayati tasmāt aikātikī viduṣaḥ kaivalya siddhiḥ akṣara dhiyām tu avarodhaḥ sāma āya tad bhāvābhyām aupasada vat tat uktam akṣara dhi adhikaraṇam vājasaeyake śrūyate etat vai tat akṣaram gārgi brāhmaṇāḥ abhivadati a sthūlam a aṇu a hrasvam a dīrgham a lohitam a seham ityādi tathā ātharvaṇe śrūyate atha parā yayā tat akṣaram adhigamyate yat tat a dreśyam a grāhyam a gotram a varṇam ityādi tathā eva ayatra api viśeṣaiḥ ākaraṇa dvāreṇa akṣaram param brahma śrāvyate tatra ca kvacid kecid atiriktāḥ viśeṣāḥ pratiṣidhyate tāsām viśeṣa pratiṣedha buddhīām kim sarvāsām sarvatra prāptiḥ uta vyavasthā iti saṃśaye śruti vibhāgāt vyavasthā prāptau ucyate akṣara viṣayāḥ tu viśeṣa pratiṣedha buddhayaḥ sarvāḥ sarvatra avaroddhavyāḥ sāmāya tad bhāvābhyām hi sarvatra viśeṣaiḥ ākaraṇa rūpaḥ brahma pratipāda a prakāraḥ tat eva ca sarvatra pratipādyam brahma pratyabhijñāyate tatra kim iti ayatra kṛtāḥ buddhayaḥ ayatra a syuḥ tathā ca āad ādayaḥ iti atra vyākhyātam tatra vidhi rūpāṇi iha pratiṣedha rūpāṇi iti viśeṣaḥ prapañca arthaḥ ca ayam citā bhedaḥ aupasada vat iti yathā coditāsu puroḍāśa pradā amatrāṇām ageḥ veḥ hotram veḥ adhvaram iti evamādīām udgātṛ veda utpāām api adhvaryubhiḥ bhavati adhvaryu kartṛka tvāt puroḍāśa pradā asya evam iha api akṣara tatra tvāt tad viśeṣaṇāām yatra kvacid api akṣareṇa sarvatra abhisaṃbadhaḥ iti arthaḥ tat uktam prathame kāṇḍe guṇa mukhya vyatikrame veda saṃyogaḥ iti atra iyat adhikaraṇam dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyā vṛkṣam pariṣasvajāte tayoḥ ayaḥ pippalam abhicākaśīti iti adhyātma adhikāre matram ātharvaṇikāḥ śvetāśvatarāḥ ca paṭhati tathā kaṭhāḥ ṛtam pibatau sukṛtasya loke guhām praviṣṭau parame parārdhye chāyā ātapau brahma vidaḥ vadati pañca āgayaḥ ye ca triṇāciketāḥ iti kim atra vidyā eka tvam uta vidyāāātvam iti saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam vidyāāātvam iti kutas viśeṣa darśaāt dvā suparṇāḥ iti atra hi ekasya bhoktṛ tvam dṛśyate ekasya ca abhoktṛ tvam dṛśyate ṛtam pibatau iti atra ubhayoḥ api bhoktṛ tvam eva dṛśyate tat vedya rūpam vidyām bhidyāt iti evam prāpte bravīti vidyā ekatvam iti kutas yatas ubhayoḥ api aayoḥ matrayoḥ dvi tva upetam vedyam rūpam darśitaḥ rūpa bhedaḥ darśitaḥ rūpa bhedaḥ e ti ucyate ubhau api etau matrau jīva dvitīyam īśvaram pratipādayataḥ dvā suparṇāḥ iti atra tāvat ubhicākaśīti iti aśaāya ādi atītaḥ paramātmā pratipādyate vākyaśeṣe pi ca saḥ eva dṛśyate juṣṭam yadā paśyati ayam īśam asya mahimā iti ṛtam pibatau iti atra tu jīve pibati pibati iti upacaryate paramātma prakaraṇam hi etat ayatra dharmāt ayatra adharmāt iti upakramāt tad viṣayaḥ eva ca atra api vākyaśeṣaḥ bhavati yaḥ setuḥ īja akṣaram brahma yat param iti guhām praviṣṭau ātma au hi iti atra ca etat prapañcitam vedya bhedaḥ tasmāt ca vidyā eka tvam api ca triṣu api eteṣu paurvāparya ālocae paramātma vidyā eva avagamyate tādātmya vivakṣayā eva ca paramātma vidyāyām bheda abheda vicāra avatāraḥ asti iti uktam tasmāt prapañca arthaḥ eva eṣa prayogaḥ tasmāt ca adhika dharma upasaṃhāraḥ iti atarā bhūta grāma vat sva ātma atara tva adhikaraṇam yat sākṣāt aparokṣāt brahma yaḥ ātmā sarva ataraḥ iti evam dvis uṣastaka hola praśayoḥ airataryeṇa vājasaeyiḥ tatra saṃśayaḥ vidyā eka tvam vā syāt vidyā āā tvam vā iti vidyā āā tvam iti tāvat prāptam abhyāsa sāmarthyāt ayathā hi aarthakam eva syāt tasmāt yathā abhyāsāt karma bhedaḥ evam abhyāsāt vidyā bhedaḥ iti evam prāpte pratyāha sva ātmanaḥ vidyā eka tvam iti sarvātaraḥ hi sva ātmā ubhayatra api aviśiṣṭaḥ pṛcchayate pratyucyate ca a hi dvau ātmau ekasmin dehe sarvātarau saṃbhavataḥ tadā hi ekasya āñjasam sarvātaratvam avakalpeta ekasya tu bhūta grāma vat syāt yathā ca pañcabhūta samūhe dehe pṛthivyāḥ āpaḥ utarāḥ adbhyaḥ tejaḥ utaram iti sati api āpekṣika itaratve ā eva mukhyam sarvātaratvam bhavati tathā iha api iti arthaḥ athavā bhūta grāma vat iti śrutyataram darśayati yathā ekaḥ devāḥ sarva bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarva vyāpī sarva bhūta atarātmā iti asmin atre samasteṣu bhūta grāmeṣu ekaḥ eva sarvātaraḥ ātmā āmāyate evam aayoḥ api brāhmaṇayoḥ iti arthaḥ tasmāt vedya aikyāt vidyā eka tvam iti ayathā bheda aupapattiḥ iti ayathā bheda aupapattiḥ iti atha yat uktam vidyā bhede tat parihartavyam atra ucyate doṣaḥ upadeśa atara vat upapatteḥ yathā ṣaṣṭhe prapāṭhake saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi śvetaketo iti avakṛtvā upi upadeśe vidyā bhedaḥ bhavati evam iha api bhaviṣyati katham ca avakṛtvā upi upadeśe vidyā bhedaḥ bhavati upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām eka artha tā avagamāt bhūyas eva mā bhagavān āvijñāpayatu iti ca ekasya eva arthasya puas puas upakṣepāt ca asakṛt upadeśa upapatteḥ evam iha api iti ca parisamāpti aviśeṣāt upakrama upasaṃhārau tāvat eka artha viṣayau dṛśyeta iyat eva sākṣāt aparokṣāt brahma iti dvitīye praśe evakāram prayuñjāaḥ pūrva praśa gatam eva artham uttaratra ākṛṣyamāṇam darśayati pūrvasmin ca brāhmaṇe kārya karaṇa vyatiriktasya ātmaaḥ sadbhāvaḥ kathyate uttarasmin tu tasya eva aśaāya ādi saṃsāra dharma atīta tvam viśeṣaḥ kathyate iti eka artha tā upapattiḥ tasmāt ekā vidyā iti vyatihāraḥ viśiṃṣati hi itara vat vyatihāra adhikaraṇam yathā saḥ u sau yaḥ u sau saḥ u ham iti āditya puruṣam prakṛti aitareyiṇaḥ tathā jābālāḥ tvam vai aham asmi bhagavaḥ devatā iham vai tvam asi iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha vyatihāreṇa ubhaya rūpā matiḥ kartavyā uta eka rūpā eva iti eka rūpā eva iti tāvat āha a hi atra ātmanaḥ īśvareṇa ekatvam muktvā a yat kiṃcid citayitavyam asti yadi ca evam citayitavya viśeṣaḥ parikalpyeta saṃsāriṇaḥ ca īśvara ātmatvam īśvarasya saṃsāri ātmatvam iti tatra saṃsāriṇaḥ tāvat īśvara ātmatve utkarṣaḥ bhavet īśvarasya tu saṃsāri ātma tve ikarṣaḥ kṛtaḥ syāt tasmāt aikarūpyam eva mateḥ vyatihāra āmāyaḥ tu ekatva dṛḍhīkāra arthaḥ iti evam prāpte pratyāha vyatihāraḥ yam ādhyāāya āmāyate itaravat yathā itare guṇāḥ sarva ātma tva prabhṛtayaḥ ādhyāāya āmāyate tadvat tathā hi viśiṃṣati samā mātāraḥ ubhaya uccāraṇe tvam aham asmi aham ca tvam asi iti tat ca ubhaya rūpāyām matau kartavyāyām arthavat bhavati ayathā hi idam aarthakam syāt kṛta tvāt au artha viśeṣe devatāyāḥ saṃsāri ātma tva āpatteḥ ikarṣaḥ prasajyeta iti uktam doṣaḥ aikātmyasya eva evam sati sa eva ekatva dṛḍhīkāraḥ āpadyeta a vayam ekatva dṛḍhīkāram vārayāmaḥ kim tarhi vyatihāreṇa iha dvirūpā matiḥ kartavyā aikarūpā iti etāvat upapādayāmaḥ phalatas tu ekatvam api dṛḍhībhavati yathā satya kāma ādi guṇa upadeśe tad guṇaḥ īśvaraḥ prasidhyati tadvat tasmāt ayam ādhyātavyaḥ vyatihāraḥ ca viṣaye upasaṃhartavyaḥ bhavati iti sā eva hi satya ādayaḥ satya ādi adhikaraṇam sa yaḥ ha etam mahat yakṣam prathama jam veda satyam brahma ityādiā vājasaeyake satya vidyām saāma akṣara upāsaām vidhāya tat yat tat satyam asau saḥ ādityaḥ yaḥ eṣaḥ etasmin maṇḍale puruṣaḥ yaḥ ca ayam dakṣiṇa īkṣa puruṣaḥ ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kim dve ete satya vidye kim vai ekā eva iti dve iti tāvat prāptam hi phala saṃyogaḥ bhavati jayati imān lokān iti pāpmāam jahāti ca iti upariṣṭāt prakṛta ākarṣaṇam tu upāsya ekatvāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ ekā eva iyam satya vidyā iti kutas tat yat tat satyam iti prakṛta ākarṣaṇāt vidyā bhede pi prakṛta ākarṣaṇam upāsya ekatvāt upapadyate iti uktam aitadevam yatra tu vispaṣṭāt kāraṇātarāt vidyā bhedaḥ pratīyate tatra etat evam syāt atra tu ubhayathā saṃbhaveta yat tat satyam iti prakṛta ākarṣaṇāt pūrvavidyā saṃbaddham eva satyam uttaratra ākṛṣyate iti ekavidyā tva aiścayaḥ yat puaruktam phala atara śravaṇāt vidyātaram iti atra ucyate aham iti ca aṅga atara upadeśasya stāvakam idam phala atara śravaṇam iti adoṣaḥ api ca arthavādāt eva phale kalpayitavye sati vidyā eka tve ca avayaveṣu śrūyamāṇāi phalāi avayaviyām eva vidyāyām upasaṃhartavyāi bhavati tasmāt sā eva iyam ekā satya vidyā iti atas sarva eva satya ādayaḥ guṇāḥ ekasmin prayoge upasaṃhartavyāḥ kecid puarasmin sūtre idam ca vājasaeyakam akṣi āditya puruṣa viṣayam vākyam chādogye ca atha yaḥ eṣa utarāditye hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣaḥ dṛśyate yaḥ eṣa ukṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate iti udāhṛtya sā eva iyam akṣi āditya puruṣa viṣayā vidyā ubhayatra ekā eva iti kṛtvā satya ādi guṇāḥ vājasaeyibhyaḥ chadogāām upasaṃhāryāḥ sādhu lakṣyate chādogye hi udgītha vyapāśrayā vidyā vijñāyate tatra hi ādi madhya avasāeṣu bhavati iyam eva ṛgagiḥ sāma iti upakrametasya ṛc ca sāma ca geṣṇau tasmāt udgīthaḥ iti madhyeye evam gāyati iti upasaṃhāre aivam vājasaeyake kiṃcid asti tatra prakrama bhedāt vidyā bhede sati guṇa vyavasthā eva yuktā iti kāma ādi itaratra tatra ca āyata ādibhyaḥ kāma ādi adhikaraṇam atha yat idam asmi brahma pure daharam puṇḍarīkam veśma daharaḥ smi iti prastutya chadogāḥ adhīyate eṣaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā vijaraḥ vimṛtyuḥ viśokaḥ vijighatsaḥ pipāsaḥ satya kāmaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ ityādi tathā vājasaeyiḥ sa vai eṣa mahāḥ ajaḥ ātmā yaḥ yam prāṇeṣu yaḥ eṣa u tar hṛdaye ākāśaḥ tasmin śete sarvasya vaśī ityādi tatra vidyā eka tvam paraspara guṇa yogaḥ ca kim vā ā iti saṃśaye vidyā eka tvam iti tatra idam ucyate kāma ādi iti satya kāma ādi iti arthaḥ yathā devadattaḥ dattaḥ satyabhāmā bhāmā iti mahābhāṣya yat etat chādogye hṛdaya ākāśasya satya kāma tva ādi guṇa jātam upalabhyate tat itaratra vājasaeyake sa vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ ātmā iti atra saṃbadhyeta yat ca vājasaeyake vaśi tva ādi upalabhyate tat api itaratra chādogye eṣaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā iti atra saṃbadhyeta kutas āyataādi sāmāyāt hi ubhayatra api hṛdayam ca vedyaḥ īśvaraḥ ca tasya setu tvam iti evamādi bahu sāmāyam dṛśyate viśeṣaḥ api dṛśyate chādogye hṛdaya ākāśasya guṇa yogaḥ vājasaeyake tu ākāśa āśrayasya brahmaṇe iti a dahara uttarebhyaḥ iti atra chādogye pi ākāśa śabdam brahma eva iti pratiṣṭhāpita tvāt ayam tu atra vidyate viśeṣaḥ sa guṇā hi brahma vidyā chādogye upadiśyate atha yaḥ iha ātmā amaḥ u vidya vrajati etān ca satya akāmāḥ iti ātma vat kāmāām api vedya tva śravaṇāt vājasaeyake tu brahma upadiśyamāam dṛśyate atha urdhvam vimokṣāya brūhi a saṅgaḥ hi ayam puruṣaḥ vaśi tva ādi tu stuti artham eva guṇa jātam vājasaeyake saṃkīrtyate tathā ca upariṣṭāt saḥ eṣaḥ eti eti ātmā ityādi ā irguṇam eva brahma upasaṃharati guṇavataḥ tu brahmaṇaḥ ekatvāt vibhūti pradarśaāya ayam guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ sūtritaḥ iti draṣṭavyam ādarāt alopaḥ ādara adhikaraṇam chādogye vaiśvāara vidyām prakṛtya śrūyate tat yat bhaktam prathamam āgacchet tat homīyam sa yām prathamām āhutim juhuyāt tām juhuyāt prāṇāya svāhā ityādi tatra pañca prāṇa āhutayaḥ vihitāḥ tāsu ca parastāt agihotra śabdaḥ prayuktaḥ yaḥ etat evam vidvāḥ agihotram juhoti iti yathā iha kṣudhitā bālāḥ mātaram paryupāsate evam sarvāṇi bhūtāyagihotram upāsate iti ca tatra idam vicāryate kim bhoja a lope lopaḥ prāṇāgihotrasya uta a lopaḥ iti tat yat bhaktam iti bhakta āgama asaṃyoga śravaṇāt bhakta āgama asya ca bhoja artha tvāt bhoja a lope lopaḥ prāṇāgihotrasya iti evam prāpte a lupyeta iti tāvat āha kasmāt ādarāt tathā hi vaiśvāara vidyāyām eva jābālāām śrutiḥ yathā ha vai parasya juhuyāt evam tat iti atithi bhojaasya prāthamyam svāmi bhojaam prathamam prāpayatī ādaram karoti yā hi a prāthamya lopam sahate sā prāthamyavataḥ gihotrasya lopam saheta iti bhoja artha bhakta āgama asaṃyogāt bhoja a lope lopaḥ prāpitaḥ tasya dravya viśeṣa vidhā artha tvāt prākṛte hi a gihotre payaḥ prabhṛtīām dravyāṇām iyata tvāt iha api a gihotra śabdāt tad dharma prāptau satyām bhakta dravya tā guṇa viśeṣa vidhā artham idam vākyam tat yat bhaktam iti atas guṇa lope mukhyasya iti evam prāptam adbhiḥ vā vā dravyeṇa a viruddhea a iti atas uttaram paṭhati upasthita itas tad vacaāt upasthite bhojae atas tasmāt eva bhoja a dravyāt prathama upaipatitāt kasmāt tad vacaāt tathā hi tat yat bhaktam prathamam āgacchet tat homīyam iti siddha vat bhakta upaipāta parāmarśe parārtha dravya sādhya tām vidadhāti tāḥ satyaḥ katham bhoja a lope dravya ātaram pratidhāpayeyuḥ ca atra prākṛta āgihotra dharma prāptiḥ asti juhoti iti vidhi uddeśa gataḥ gihotra śabdaḥ tadvat bhāvam vidhāpayet iti yuktā tad dharma prāptiḥ iha arthavāda gataḥ gihotra śabdaḥ a tadvat bhāvam vidhāpayitum arhati tad dharma prāptau ca abhyupagamyamāāyām agi uddharaṇa ādayaḥ api prāpyera a ca asti saṃbhavaḥ agi uddharaṇam tāvat homa adhikaraṇa bhāvāya ca ayam agau homaḥ bhoja ārtha tā vyāghāta prasaṅgāt bhoja ārtha upaīta dravya saṃbadhāt ca āsyaḥ eva eṣa homaḥ tathā ca jābāla śrutiḥ pūrvaḥ utithibhyaḥ uśīyāt iti āsya ādhārām eva imām homaiḥ vṛttim darśayati atas eva ca iha api darśayati uraḥ eva vediḥ lomāi barhiḥ hṛdayam gārhapatyaḥ āsyam āhavaīyaḥ iti vedi śrutiḥ ca atra sthaṇḍila mātra upalakṣaṇa arthā draṣṭavyā mukhya āgihotre vedi abhāvāt tad aṅgāām ca iha ca saṃpipādayiṣita tvāt ca saṃyogāt upasthā ādayaḥ dharmāḥ kecid kathaṃcid virudhyate tasmāt bhoja a pakṣe eva ete matra dravya devatā saṃyogāt pañca homāḥ yat tu ādara darśa avacaam tat bhoja a pakṣe prāthamya vidhā artham a hi asti vacaasya atibhāraḥ a tu asya ityatā śakyate darśayitum tasmāt bhoja a lope lopaḥ eva prāṇa gihotrasya iti pṛthak hi a pratibadhaḥ phalam taiḥ dhāraṇa adhikaraṇam sati karma aṅga vyapāśrayāṇi om iti etat akṣaram udgītham upāsīta iti evamādīi kim syuḥ karmasu parṇa mayī tva ādi vat uta godoha ādi vat iti vicārayāmaḥ kim tāvat prāptam ityāi iti kutas prayoga vaca a parigrahāt hi udgītha ādi dvāreṇa kratu saṃbandhāt aṅga atara vat saṃspṛśyate yat tu eṣām sva vākyeṣu phala śravaṇam āpayitā ha vai bhavati ityādi tat vartamāna apadeśa rūpatvāt arthavāda mātram eva apāpa śloka śravaṇa ādi vat tasmāt a prakaraṇa paṭhitāām api juhū ādi dvāreṇa kratu praveśāt prakaraṇa paṭhita vat ityatā evam udgītha ādi upāsāām api iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ taiḥ dhāraṇāiyamaḥ iti udgītha ādi karma guṇa yāthātmyaiḥ dhāraṇāi rasatamaḥ āptiḥ samṛddhiḥ mukhya prāṇaḥ ādityaḥ iti evamādi ityavat karmasu iyamyera kutas tad dṛṣṭeḥ tathā hi aityatvam evaṃjātīyakāām darśayati śrutiḥ kurutaḥ yaḥ ca etat evam veda yaḥ ca a veda iti a viduṣaḥ api kriyā abhyaujñāāt prastāva ādi devatā vijñā a vihīāām api prastotṛ ādīām yāja ādhyavasā adarśaāt prastotar yāḥ devatā prastāvam avāyattā tām ced avidvā prastoṣyasi tām ced avidvā udgāsyasi tām ced avidvā pratihariṣyasi iti ca api ca evaṃjātīyakasya karma vyapāśrayasya vijñāasya pṛthak eva karmaṇaḥ phalam upalabhyate karma phala siddhi a pratibadhaḥ tad samṛddhiḥ atiśaya viśeṣaḥ kaścid te ubhau kurutaḥ yaḥ ca etat evam veda yaḥ ca a veda tu vidyā ca avidyā ca yat eva vidyayā karoti śraddhayā upaiṣadā tat eva vīryavattaram bhavati iti tu iti vidvat avidvat prayogayoḥ iti ca tarap pratyaya prayogāt iti ca tarap pratyaya prayogāt vīryavat iti gamyate tat ca aityatve vidyāyāḥ upapadyate ityatve tu katham tad vihīam karma sarva aṅga upasaṃhāre hi vīryavat karma iti sthitiḥ tathā loka sāma ādiṣu śiṣyate kalpate ha asmai lokāḥ ūrdhvāḥ ca āvṛttāḥ ca iti evamādi a ca idam phala śravaṇam arthavāda mātram yuktam pratipattum tathā hi guṇa vādaḥ āpadyeta phala upadeśe tu mukhya vāda upapattiḥ prayāja ādiṣu tu itikartavya tā ākāṅkṣasya kratoḥ prakṛta tvāt tādarthye sati yuktam phala śruteḥ arthavāda tvam tathā a ārabhya adhīteṣu api parṇa mayī tva ādiṣu hi godoha ādīām akriyā ātmakāām āśrayam atareṇa godoha ādīām hi prakṛta appraṇaya ādi āśraya lābhāt phala vidhiḥ tathā bailva ādīām api prakṛta yūpa ādi āśraya lābhāt upapaaḥ phala vidhiḥ a tu parṇa mayī tva ādiṣu evaṃvidhaḥ kaścid āśrayaḥ prakṛtaḥ asti tu juhū ādi āśrayatām vivakṣitvā phale api vidhim vivakṣataḥ vākya bhedaḥ syāt upāsaāām tu kriyā ātmaka tvāt viśiṣṭa vidhā upapatteḥ udgītha ādi āśrayāṇām phale virudhyate tasmāt yathā kratu āśrayāṇi api phala saṃyogāt aityāi evam udgītha ādi upāsaāi api iti draṣṭavyam atas eva ca kalpasūtra kārāḥ kratuṣu kalpayāṃcakruḥ tat uktam pradā adhikaraṇam vājasaeyaka vat iṣyāmi eva aham iti vāc dadhre iti atra adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam adhyātmam a vāc ādīām prāṇaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ uvadhāritaḥ adhidaivatam agi ādīām vāyuḥ tathā chādogyā iva āyuḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ iti atra adhidaivatam vāyuḥ saṃvargaḥ iti atra adhidaivatam prāṇaḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ iti atra adhyātmam vāc ādīām prāṇaḥ tatra saṃśayaḥ kim pṛthak eva imau vāyu prāṇau upagatavyau syātām uta apṛthak iti apṛthak iti tāvat prāptam tattva abhedāt hi tattve yāyyam darśayati ca śrutiḥ adhyātmam adhidaivatam ca tattva abhedam agiḥ vāc bhūtvā mukham prāviśat iti ārabhya tathā atas ete sarve eva samāḥ iti ādhyātmikāām prāṇāām ādhidaivikīm vibhūtim ātma bhūtām darśayati tathā tatra tatra adhyātmam adhidaivatam ca bahudhā tattva abheda darśaam bhavati kvacid cayaḥ prāṇaḥ sa vāyuḥ iti spaṣṭam eva vāyum prāṇam ca ekam karoti tathā udāhṛte api vājasaeyibrāhmaṇeyataḥ ca udeti sūryaḥ iti asmi upasaṃhāra śloke prāṇāt vai eṣaḥ udeti prāṇeḥ tam eti iti upasaṃhare ekatvam darśayati tasmāt ekam eva vratam caret prāṇyāt ca eva apāyāt ca iti ca prāṇa vrate eva eke upasaṃhare etat eva draḍhayati tathā chādogye pi devaḥ ekaḥ kaḥ sa jagāra bhuvaḥ asya gopāḥ iti ekam eva saṃvargam gayamati bravīti ekaḥ eva eṣām caturṇām saṃvargaḥ apara upareṣām iti tasmāt apṛthaktvam upagama asya iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ pṛthak eva vāyu prāṇau upagatavyau iti kasmāt pṛthak upadeśāt hi ayam adhyātma adhidaiva vibhāga upadeśaḥ saḥ asatya ādhyā apṛthaktve aarthakaḥ eva syāt uktam tattva abhedāt iti doṣaḥ tattva abhede pi avasthā bhedāt aucita abheda upapatteḥ śloka upayāsasya ca tattva abheda abhiprāyeṇa api upapadyamānasya pūrva udita dhyeya bhedaiḥ ākaraṇa sāmarthya abhāvāt sa yathā eṣām prāṇāām madhyamaḥ prāṇaḥ evam etāsām devatāām vāyuḥ iti ca upamā opameya karaṇāt vrata upayāsaḥ vyākhyātaḥ ekam eva vratam iti ca eva kāraḥ prāṇa vrata pratipatti arthaḥ bhaga vratāi hi mṛtyuḥ śramaḥ bhūtvā upayeme iti śruteḥ a vāyu vrata evṛtti arthaḥ atha atas vrata mīmāṃsā iti prastutya tulya vat vāyu prāṇayoḥ abhaga vrata tvasya ekam eva vratam caret iti ca uktvā eva etasyai devatāyai sāyujyam salokatām jayati iti vāyu prāptim phalam bruva darśayati devatā iti atra vāyuḥ syāt purastāt prayogāt ca sā eṣā astamitā devatā yat vāyuḥ iti tathā atau vai etau dvau saṃvargau vāyuḥ eva deveṣu prāṇaḥ prāṇeṣu iti vyapadiśati te vai ete pañcāye pañcāye daśa sataḥ tat kṛtam iti ca upasaṃharati tasmāt pṛthak eva yathā idrāya rājñe puroḍāśam ekādaśa kapālam idrāya adhirājāya idrāya sva rājñe iti asyām ityatas idrā bhedāt ca saha pradā āśaṅkāyām rāja ādi guṇa bhedāt yathāyāsam eva devatā pṛthaktvāt pradā a pṛthaktvam bhavati evam tattva abhede pi ādhyeya aṃśa pṛthaktvāt ādhyā apṛthaktvam iti arthaḥ tat uktam saṃkarṣe vā devatā iti tatra tu dravya devatā bhedāt yāga bhedaḥ vidyate aivam iha vidyā bhedaḥ usti upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām adhyātma adhidaiva upadeśeṣu ekavidyā vidhā apratīteḥ vidyā aikye api tu adhyātma adhidaiva bhedāt pravṛtti bhedaḥ bhavati a gihotre iva sāyam prātar kāla bhedāt iti etāvat abhipretya pradāa vat iti uktam liṅga bhūyaḥ tvāt tat hi balīyaḥ tāt api liṅga bhūyaḥ tva adhikaraṇam vājasaeyi ogi rahasye eva vai idam agre sadā āsīt iti etasmin brāhmaṇe adhīyate tat ṣaṭtriṃśatam sahasrāṇi apaśyat ātma ogī arka ama oma yāma aścitaḥ ityādi tathā eva vāc citaḥ prāṇa citaḥ cakṣuḥ citaḥ śrotra citaḥ karma citaḥ ogi citaḥ iti pṛthak agī sāṃpādikā teṣu saṃśayaḥ kim ete tad śeṣa bhūtāḥ uta svatatrāḥ kevala vidyā ātmakāḥ iti tatra prakaraṇāt kriyā upraveśe prāpte svātatryam tāvat pratijāīte liṅga bhūyaḥ tvāt iti bhūyāṃsi hi liṅgāi asmin brāhmaṇe kevalavidyā ātmaka tvam eṣām upodbalayati dṛśyate tat yat kiṃca imāi bhūtāi saṃkalpayati teṣām eva sā kṛtiḥ iti tā aha etāḥ evaṃvide sarvadā sarvāṇi svapate iti ca evaṃjātīyakāi tat hi liṅgam prakaraṇāt balīyaḥ tat api uktam pūrvasmin kāṇḍe samavāye pāra daurbalyam artha viprakarṣāt iti pūrva vikalpaḥ prakaraṇāt syāt kriyā svatatrāḥ etegayaḥ iti pūrvasya kriyā mayasya ageḥ prakaraṇāt tad viṣayaḥ eva ayam vikalpa viśeṣa upadeśaḥ syāt a svatatraḥ prakaraṇāt liṅgam balīyaḥ satyam evam etat liṅgam api tu evaṃjātīyakam a prakaraṇāt balīyaḥ bhavati hi etat sāṃpādika āgi praśaṃsā rūpa tvāt ca asatyām ayasyām prāptau a prakaraṇam bādhitum utsahate tasmāt sāṃpādikāḥ api etegayaḥ eva syuḥ māasa vat yathā daśarātrasya avivākye pṛthivyā pātreṇa samudrasya somasya prajāpataye devatāyai gṛhyamāṇasya māasāya iva sa ca graha kalpaḥ kriyā prakaraṇāt kriyā śeṣaḥ eva bhavati evam ayam api agi kalpaḥ iti arthaḥ atideśāt ca atideśaḥ ca eṣām agīām kriyā upraveśam upodbalayati ṣaṭtriṃśat sahasrāṇi agayoḥ ṛkāḥ teṣām ekaikaḥ eva iti sati hi sāmāye atideśaḥ pravartate tatas ca pūrveṇa eṣām dyotayati vidyā eva tu tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati vidyā ātmakāḥ eva ete svatatrāḥ maaścit āda yogayaḥ syuḥ a kriyā śeṣa bhūtāḥ tathā hi te ha ete vidyā citaḥ eva iti vidyayā ha eva ete evaṃvidaḥ citā bhavati iti ca darśaāt ca dṛśyate ca eteṣām svātatrye liṅgam tat purastāt darśitam liṅga bhūyaḥ tvāt iti atra liṅgam api asatyām ayasyām prāptau asādhakam kasyacid arthasya iti apāsya tat prakaraṇa sāmarthyāt kriyā śeṣa tvam adhyavasitam iti atas uttaram paṭhati śruti ādi balīyaḥ tvāt ca prakaraṇa sāmarthya atikraya aśeṣa tvam adhyavasāya svātatrya pakṣaḥ bādhitavyaḥ śruti ādeḥ balīyaḥ tvāt balīyāṃsi hi prakaraṇāt śruti liṅga vākyāi iti sthitam śruti liṅga sūtre ca iha svātatrya pakṣam sādhayati dṛśyate katham śrutiḥ tāvat te ha ete vidyā citaḥ eva iti tathā liṅgam sarvadā sarvāṇi bhūtāi svapate iti tathā vākyam api vidyayā ha eva ete evaṃvidaḥ citāḥ bhavati itividyā citaḥ eva iti hi sa avadhāraṇām iyam śrutiḥ pīḍitā syāt iti iyatā kṛta tvāt aarthakam avadhāraṇam bhavet sva rūpam eva hi eṣām abāhya sādhaatvam iti abāhya sādhaatve pi tu māasagraha vat avadhāraṇam arthavat bhaviṣyati tathā a svapate jāgrate ca evaṃvide sarvadā sarvāṇi iti sātatya darśam eṣām svātatrī eva kalpate yathā sāṃpādike vāc prāṇa maye gihotre prāṇam tadā vāci juhoti vācam tadā prāṇe juhoti iti ca uktvā ucyate ete aate amṛte āhutī jāgrat ca svapan ca satatam juhoti iti tadvat tu kriyā prayogasya alpa kāla tvāt eṣām prayogaḥ kalpeta ca idam arthavāda mātram iti yāyyam yatra hi vispaṣṭaḥ vidhāyakaḥ liṅ ādiḥ upalabhyate yuktam tatra saṃkīrtaa mātrasya arthavāda tvam iha tu eṣām tat ca yathā saṃkīrtaam eva kalpayitum śakyate iti sātatya darśaāt tathābhūtam eva kalpyate tatas ca sāmarthyāt eṣām svātatrya siddhiḥ saṃkalpayati teṣām eva sā kṛtiḥ ityādi vyākhyātam tathā vākyam api evaṃvide iti puruṣa viśeṣa saṃbadham eva eṣām ācakṣāṇam a kratu saṃbadham mṛṣyate tasmāt svātatrya pakṣaḥ eva jyāyāḥ iti aubadha ādibhyaḥ prajñātara pṛthaktva vat dṛṣṭaḥ ca tat uktam itas ca prakaraṇam upamṛdya svātatryam pratipattavyam yat kriyā avayavāḥ te maasā eva adhīyata maasā acīyata maasā eva grahāḥ agṛhyata saṃpad phalaḥ hi ayam aubadhaḥ ca pratyakṣāḥ kriyā avayavāḥ sataḥ saṃpadā lipsitavyāḥ ca atra udgītha ādi upāsa avat tad aupraveśi tvam āśaṅkitavyam śruti vairūpyāt a hi atra kriyā aṅgam kiṃcid ādāya vadati ṣaṭtriṃśat sahasrāṇi tu graha ādīn ca kalpayati puruṣa yajña ādi vat saṃkhyā ca iyam puruṣa āyuṣasya ahar su dṛṣṭā satī āropyate iti draṣṭavyam eva aubadhāt svātatryam ādi śabdāt atideśa ādi api yathāsaṃbhavam yojayitavyam tathā hi teṣām ekaikaḥ eva iti kriyā mayasya āgeḥ māhātmyam atidiśa kriyāyām a ādaram darśayati a ca sati eva vikalpaḥ pūrveṇa uttareṣām iti śakyam vaktum hi vyāpāreṇa pūrvaḥ kriyāyām upakaroti uttare upakartum śakuvati yat tu pūrvapakṣe pi atideśaḥ upodbalakaḥ iti uktam sati hi sāmāyā itideśaḥ pravartate iti tat asmad pakṣe pi agitva sāmāyeātideśa saṃbhavāt pratyuktam asti hi ca evam aubadha ādibhyaḥ kāraṇebhyaḥ svātatryam prajñātara pṛthaktva vat yathā prajñātarāṇi śāṇḍilya vidyā prabhṛtīi pṛthak eva karmabhyaḥ prajñātarebhyaḥ ca svatatrāṇi bhavati evam iti dṛṣṭaḥ ca rājasūya prakaraṇa paṭhitāyāḥ prakaraṇāt utkarṣaḥ rājayajña tvāt ca rājasūyasya tat uktam prathame kāṇḍe kratu arthāyām iti varṇa traya saṃyogāt iti hi loka āpattiḥ yat uktam māasa vat iti tat pratyucyate a kriyā śeṣa tvam kalpyam pūrva uktebhyaḥ śruti ādi hetubhyaḥ kevala puruṣa artha tva upalabdheḥ a hi kiṃcid kasyacid kaścit sāmāyam a saṃbhavati a ca tāvatā yathāsvam vaiṣamyam iva ārtate mṛtyu vat yathā āsa vai eṣaḥ eva mṛtyuḥ yaḥ eṣaḥ etasmin maṇḍale puruṣaḥ iti agiḥ vai mṛtyuḥ iti ca agi āditya puruṣayoḥ mṛtyu śabda prayoge mṛtyu śabda prayoge a atyata sāmya āpattiḥ yathā ca asau vāva lokaḥ gautama āgiḥ tasya ādityaḥ eva samidh iti atra a samidh ādi sāmāyāt lokasya āgi bhāva āpattiḥ tadvat pareṇa ca śabdasya tādvidhyam bhūyaḥ tvāt tvaubadhaḥ parastāt api ayam vāva lokaḥ iti asmi brāhmaṇe tādvidhyam kevalavidyā vidhi tvam śabdasya lakṣyate a śuddha karma aṅga vidhi tvam tatra hi vidyayā tat ārohati yatra kāmāḥ parāgatāḥ a tatra dakṣiṇā yati kevalam karma ca praśaṃse idam gamayati tathā purastāt api yat etam maṇḍalam tapati iti asmin brāhmaṇe vidyā pradhā atvam eva lakṣyate bhavati mṛtyuḥ hi asya ātmā bhavati iti upasaṃhārāt a karma pradhāa tā tad sāmāyāt iha api tathātvam bhūyān tu agi avayavāḥ saṃpādayitavyāḥ vidyāyām iti etasmāt kāraṇāt vidyā aubadhyate vidyā aubadhyate karma aṅga tvāt tasmāt kevalavidyā ātmaka tva siddhiḥ ekaḥ śarīre bhāvāt śarīrebhāva adhikaraṇam iha deha vyatiriktasya ātmaaḥ sadbhāvaḥ samarthyate badha mokṣa adhikāra siddhaye a hi asati deha vyatirikta ātmaiḥ para loka phalāḥ ca udaāḥ upapadyera kasya vā brahma ātmatvam upadiśyeta śāstra pramukhe eva prathame pāde śāstra phala upabhoga yogyasya deha vyatiriktasya ātma ostitvam uktam satyam uktam bhāṣyakṛtā a tu tatra ātma astitve sūtram asti iha tu svayam eva sūtrakṛtā tat astitvam ākṣepa puraḥsaram pratiṣṭhāpitam itas eva ca ākṛṣya ācāryeṇa śabarasvāmiā pramāṇa lakṣaṇe varṇitam atas eva ca bhagavatā upavarṣeṇa prathame tatre ātma astitva abhidhā aprasaktau śārīrake vakṣyāmaḥ iti uddhāraḥ kṛtaḥ iha ca idam vicāryamāṇeṣu ātma astitvam vicāryate api ca pūrvasmin adhikaraṇe prakaraṇa utkarṣa abhyupagame puruṣa artha tvam varṇitam kaḥ asau puruṣaḥ yad arthāḥ ete maaścit ādayaḥ iti asyām prasaktau idam deha vyatiriktasya ātma ustitvam ucyate tad astitva ākṣepa artham idam ādimam sūtram ākṣepa pūrvikā hi parihāra uktiḥ vivakṣite rthe dṛḍhām buddhim utpādayet iti atra eke lokāyatikāḥ deha vyatiriktasya bhāvam samasta vyasteṣu bāhyeṣu pṛthivī ādiṣu adṛṣṭam api caitayam śarīra ākāra pariṇateṣu bhūteṣu syāt iti saṃbhāvayataḥ tebhyaḥ caitayam mada śakti vat caitaya viśiṣṭaḥ kāyaḥ puruṣaḥ iti ca āhuḥ a svarga gamaāya apavarga gamaāya vā samarthaḥ deha vyatiriktaḥ ātmā asti yat kṛtam dehe syāt dehe eva tu cetaaḥ ca ātmā ca iti hetum ca ācakṣate śarīre bhāvāt iti yat hi yasmin sati bhavati asati ca a bhavati tat tad dharma tveā adhyavasīyate yathā ca ātma dharma tveā abhimatāḥ ātmavādiām te pi atarā iva dehe upalabhyamāāḥ bahis ca aupalabhyamāāḥ asiddhe deha vyatirikte dharmiṇi deha dharmāḥ eva bhavitum arhati tasmāt a vyatirekaḥ dehāt ātmā iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ vyatirekaḥ tad bhāva abhāvi tvā tu upalabdhi vat a tu etat asti yat uktam a vyatirekaḥ dehāt ātmā iti vyatirekaḥ eva asya dehāt bhavitum arhati tad bhāva abhāvi tvāt yadi deha bhāve bhāvāt deha dharma tvam ātma dharmāṇām tatas deha bhāve api abhāvāt a tad dharma tvam eva eṣām kim deha dharma vailakṣaṇyāt ye hi deha dharmāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ te yāvat deham bhavati prāṇa ceṣṭā ādayaḥ tu sati api dehe mṛta avasthāyām bhavati deha dharmāḥ ca rūpa ādayaḥ paraiḥ api upalabhyate a tu ātma dharmāḥ caitaya smṛti ādayaḥ api ca sati hi tāvat dehe jīvat avasthāyām eṣām bhāvaḥ śakyate tvad asati abhāvaḥ patite api kadācid asmi dehe jīvat avasthāyām eṣām bhāvaḥ śakyate a tu asati abhāvaḥ patite api kadācid asmi dehe deha atara saṃcāreṇa ātma dharmāḥ parapakṣaḥ pratiṣidhyate kimātmakam ca idam yasya bhūtebhyaḥ utpattim icchati iti paraḥ hi bhūta catuṭaya vyatirekeṇa lokāyatikaḥ kiṃcid tattvam pratyeti bhūta bhautikāām tat iti ced tarhi viṣaya tvāt teṣām a tad dharma tvam sva ātmai kriyā virodhāt a hi agiḥ uṣṇaḥ sa sva ātmā am dahati a hi aṭaḥ śikṣitaḥ sa svaskadham adhirokati a hi bhūta bhautika dharmeṇa satā bhūta bhautikāi a hi rūpa ādibhiḥ sva rūpam para rūpam vā viṣayīkriyate viṣayīkriyate tu atas ca yathā eva asyāḥ bhūta bhautika viṣayāyāḥ upalabdheḥ bhāvaḥ abhyupagamyate evam vyatirekaḥ api asyāḥ tebhyaḥ abhyupagatavyaḥ upalabdhi svarūpaḥ eva ca deha vyatirikta tvam ca upalabdheḥ aikarūpyāt yat tu uktam śarīre bhāvāt śarīra dharmaḥ upalabdhiḥ iti prakāreṇa pratyuktam api ca satsu pradīpa ādiṣu upakaraṇeṣu upalabdhiḥ bhavati asatsu a bhavati ca etāvatā pradīpa ādi dharme eva upalabdhiḥ bhavati evam sati deha upalabdhiḥ bhavati asati ca a bhavati iti a deha dhearmaḥ bhavitum arhati upakaraṇa tva mātreṇa api pradīpa ādi vat deha upayoga upapatteḥ ca atyatam dehasya upalabdhau upayogaḥ api dṛśyate api asmi dehe svape tasmāt aavadyam deha vyatiriktasya ātmanaḥ astitvam iti triṃśam aikātmya adhikaraṇam aṅga avabaddhāḥ tu a śākhāsu hi prativedam aṅga avabaddha adhikaraṇam samāptā prāsaṅgikī kathā saṃprati prakṛtām eva āvartāmahe om iti etat akṣaram udgītham upāsīta lokeṣu pañcavidham sāma upāsīta auktham uktham iti vai prajāḥ vadati tat idam eva uktham iyam eva pṛthivī ayam vāva lokaḥ eṣaḥ giḥ citaḥ iti evamādyāḥ ye udgītha ādi karma aṅga avabaddhāḥ pratyayāḥ prativedam śākhā bhedeṣu vihitāḥ te tad śākhā gateṣu eva udgītha ādiṣu bhaveyuḥ athavā sarva śākhā gateṣu iti viśayaḥ pratiśākham ca svara ādi bhedāt udgītha ādi bhedāḥ upādāya ayam upayāsaḥ kim tāvat prāptam sva śākhā gateṣu eva udgītha ādiṣu vidhīyera eti kutas udgītham upasīte iti hi sāmāya vihitāām viśeṣa ākāṅkṣāyām saṃikṛṣṭe eva viśeṣeṇa ākāṅkṣā ādi vṛtteḥ tad atilaṅghaea śākhātara vihita viśeṣa upādāe kāraṇam tasmāt pratiśākham vyavasthā iti evam prāpte bravīti aṅga avabaddhā astu iti tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati ā ete prativedam sva śākhāsu eva vyavatiṣṭhera api tu sarva śākhāsu auvartera kutas udgītha ādi śruti aviśeṣāt sva śākhā vyavasthāyām hi udgītham upāsīta iti sāmāya śrutiḥ aviśeṣa pravṛttā satī viśeṣe pīḍitā syāt ca etayāyyam śrutiḥ balīyasī ca sāmāya āśrayaḥ tasmāt svara ādi bhede sati api udgītha tva ādi aviśeṣāt sarva śākhā gateṣu eva udgītha ādiṣu evaṃjātīyakāḥ pratyayāḥ syuḥ matra ādi vat vā avirodhaḥ athavā ā eva atra virodhaḥ śaṅkitavyaḥ katham aya śākhā gateṣu udgītha ādiṣu aya śākhā vihitāḥ pratyayāḥ bhaveyuḥ iti matra ādi vat avirodha upapatteḥ tathā hi matrāṇām karmaṇām guṇāām ca śākhātara utpāām api śākhātare upasaṃgrahaḥ dṛśyate yeṣām api hi teṣām api asau viiyogaḥ dṛśyate kukkuṭaḥ asi iti aśmā ādatte kuṭaruḥ asi iti vā iti yeṣām api samidh ādayaḥ prayājāḥ āmātāḥ teṣām api teṣu guṇa vidhiḥ āmāyate ṛtavaḥ vai prayājāḥ samāḥ atra hotavyāḥ iti tathā yeṣām api iti jāti viśeṣa upadeśaḥ teṣām api tad viṣayaḥ matra varṇaḥ upalabhyate chāgasya vapāyāḥ medasaḥ ubrūhi iti tathā iti evamādi matrāṇām vedātare parigrahaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tathā bahvṛca paṭhitasya sūktasya yaḥ jātaḥ eva prathamaḥ iti asya adhvaryave sajaīyam śasyam iti atra parigrahaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tasmāt yathā āśrayāṇām karma aṅgāām sarvatra auvṛttiḥ evam āśritāām api pratyayāām iti avirodhaḥ bhūmaḥ kratu vat jyāyaḥ tvam tathā hi darśayati bhūma jyāyaḥ tva adhikaraṇam prācīaśālaḥ aupamayavaḥ iti asyām ākhyāyikāyām vyastasya samastasya ca vaiśvāarasya upāsaam śrūyate vyasta upāsaam tāvat aupamayava kam tvam ātmāam upāsse iti divam eva bhagavaḥ rājā eti ha uvāca eṣa vai su tejāḥ ātmā vaiśvāaraḥ yam tvam ātmāam upāsse ityādi tathā samasta upāsaam api tasya ha vai etasya ātmaaḥ vaiśvāarasya mūrdhā eva su tejāḥ cakṣuḥ viśva rūpaḥ prāṇaḥ pṛthak vartmā ātmā saṃdehaḥ bahulaḥ vastiḥ eva rayiḥ pṛthivī eva pādau ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha ubhayathā api syāt vyastasya samastasya ca uta samastasya eva iti kim tāvat prāptam pratyavayavam su tejaḥ prabhṛtiṣu upāsse iti kriyā pada śravaṇāt tasmāt tava sutam prasutam āsutam kule dṛśyate ityādi phala bheda śravaṇāt ca syuḥ iti prāptam tatas abhidhīyate bhūmaḥ padārtha upacaya ātmakasya samastasya vaiśvāara upāsaasya jyāyastvam asmi vākye vivakṣitam bhavitum arhati a pratyekam avayava upāsaāām api kratu vat yathā kratuṣu darśa pūrṇamāsa prabhṛtiṣu sāmastye sa aṅga pradhā a prayogaḥ eva ekaḥ vivakṣyate a vyastāām api prayogaḥ prayāja ādīām tadvat kutas etat bhūmā eva jyāyāḥ iti tathā hi śrutiḥ bhūmaḥ jyāyaḥ tvam darśayati eka vākyatā avagamāt ekam hi idam vākyam vaiśvāara vidyā viṣayam paurvāparya ālocaāt pratīyate tathā hi prācīaśāla prabhṛtayaḥ uddālaka avasāāḥ ṣaṭ ṛṣayaḥ vaiśvāara vidyāyām pariiṣṭhām a pratipadyamāāḥ aśvapatim kaikeyam rājāam abhyājagmuḥ iti upakramya ekaikasya ṛṣeḥ upāsyam dyu prabhṛtīām ekaikam śrāvayitvā mūrdhā tu eṣaḥ ātmā iti ha uvāca ityādiā mūrdha ādi bhāvam teṣām vidadhāti mūrdhā te vyapatiṣyat yamām āgamiṣyaḥ ityādiā ca vyasta upāsaam apavadati puas ca vyasta upāsaam vyāvartya samasta upāsaam sarveṣu lokeṣu sarveṣu bhūteṣu sarveṣu ātmasu amatti iti bhūma āśrayam eva phalam darśayati yat tu pratyekam su tejaḥ prabhṛtiṣu phala bheda śravaṇam tat evam sati iti draṣṭavyam tathā upāsse iti api pratyavayavam ākhyāta śravaṇam para abhiprāya āuvāda artham a vyasta upāsa a vidhā artham tasmāt samasta upāsa pakṣaḥ eva śreyāḥ iti kecid tu atra samasta upāsa a pakṣam jyāyāṃsam pratiṣṭhāpya jyāyas tva vacaāt eva kila vyasta upāsa a pakṣam api iti kalpayati tat ayuktam ekavākyatā avagatau satyām vākya bheda kalpa asya āyāyya tvāt mūrdhā te vyapatiṣyat iti ca evamādi idam avirodhāt spaṣṭe ca upasaṃhāra sthe samasta upāsa avagame tad abhāvasya pūrvapakṣe vaktum aśakya tvāt sautrasya ca pramāṇavat tva abhiprāyeṇa api śabda ādi bhedāt śabda ādi bheda adhikaraṇam pūrvasmin adhikaraṇe satyām api sutejaḥ prabhṛtīām phala bheda śrutau samastasya upāsaam jyāyaḥ iti uktam atas prāptā buddhiḥ samasyaḥ upāsiṣyate iti api ca vedya abhede vidyā bhedaḥ vijñātum śakyate vedyam hi rūpam vidyāyāḥ dravya daivatam iva yāgasya vedyaḥ ca eka eva īśvaraḥ śruti āātve pi avagamyate brahma kham brahma satya kāmaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ iti evamādiṣu tathā ekaḥ eva prāṇaḥ prāṇaḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ prāṇaḥ vāva jyeṣṭhaḥ ca śreṣṭhaḥ ca prāṇaḥ ha pitā prāṇaḥ mātā iti evamādiṣu vedya ekatvāt ca vidyā ekatvam śruti āātvam api asmin pakṣe guṇa atara paratvāt a arthakam tasmāt sva para śākhā vihitam eka vedya vyapāśrayam guṇa jātam upasaṃhartavyam vidyā kārtsyāya iti evam prāpte pratipādyate vedya abhede pi evaṃjātīyakā vidyā bhiā bhavitum arhati kutas śabda ādi bhedāt bhavati hi śabda bhedaḥ kratum kurvīta iti evamādiḥ śabda bhedaḥ ca karma bheda hetuḥ samadhigataḥ purastāt śabda atare karma bhedaḥ iti ādi grahaṇāt guṇa ādayaḥ api yathāsaṃbhavam bheda hetavaḥ yojayitavyāḥ auvedaḥ ityādiṣu śabda bhedaḥ eva avagamyate ayajati ityādi vat artha bhedaḥ sarveṣām eva eṣām artha atara asaṃbhavāt ca tat katham śabda bhedāt vidyā bhedaḥ iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ aubadha bhedāt vedya bhede sati vidyā bheda upapatteḥ ekasya api īśvarasya upāsyasya prati prakaraṇam vyāvṛttāḥ guṇāḥ śiṣyate tathā ekasya api prāṇasya tatra tatra upāsyasya abhede pi ayādṛś guṇaḥ yatra upāsitavyaḥ ayādṛś guṇaḥ ca ayatra iti evam aubadha bhedāt vidhi bhede sati vidyā bhedaḥ vijñāyate ca atra ekaḥ vidyā vidhiḥ itare guṇa vidhayaḥ iti śakyam vaktum viigamaāyām hetu abhāvāt a eka tvāt ca pratiprakaraṇam ca sataḥ satya kāma ādayaḥ guṇāḥ asakṛt śrāvayitavyāḥ pratiprakaraṇam ca ca ca idam iti airākāṅkṣya avagamāt aikavākya tā āpattiḥ ca atra vaiśvāara vidyāyām iva aparā asti bhūtvā ekavākyatām iyuḥ vedya eka tva aimitte ca vidyā eka tve sarvatra bhūtvā eka vākya tām iyuḥ vedya eka tva aimitte ca vidyā eka tve sarvatra iraṅkuśe pratijñāyamāe samasta guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ śakyaḥ pratijñāyeta tasmāt suṣṭhu ucyate śabda ādi bhedāt iti sthite ca etasmin adhikaraṇe draṣṭavyam vikalpaḥ viśiṣṭa phala tvāt vikalpa adhikaraṇam sthite vidyā bhede vicāryate kim āsām icchayā samuccayaḥ vikalpaḥ vā syāt athavā vikalpaḥ eva tatra sthita tvāt tāvat vidyā bhedasya a samuccaya aiyame kiṃcid kāraṇam asti samuccaya aiyamaḥ dṛśyate doṣaḥ ityatā śrutiḥ hi tatra kāraṇam hi tatra kāraṇam asti vikalpa aiyamaḥ vidyātara adhikṛtasya vidyātara a pratiṣedhāt pāriśeṣyāt yāthākāmyam āpadyate au a viśiṣṭa phala tvāt āsām vikalpaḥ yāyyaḥ tathā hi brahma kham brahma satya kāmaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ iti evamādyāḥ tulya vat īśvara tva prāpti phalā lakṣyate ā eṣa doṣaḥ samā a phaleṣu api svarga ādi sādhaeṣu karmasu yāthākāmya darśaāt tasmāt yāthākāmya prāptau ucyate vikalpaḥ eva āsām bhavitum arhati a samuccayaḥ kasmāt aviśiṣṭa phala tvāt aviśiṣṭam hi āsām phalam upāsya viṣaya sākṣātkaraṇam ca sākṣātkṛte upāsye viṣaye īśvara ādau dvitīyam aarthakam api ca asaṃbhavaḥ eva sākṣātkaraṇasya samuccaya pakṣe citta vikṣepa hetu tvāt sākṣātkaraṇa sādhyam ca vidyā phalam darśayati śrutayaḥ yasya syādaddhā a vicikitsā asti itidevaḥ bhūtvā devāḥ apyeti iti ca evamādyāḥ smṛtayaḥ ca sadā tad bhāva bhāvitaḥ iti evamādyāḥ tasmāt a viśiṣṭa phalāām vidyāām ayatamām ādāya tatparaḥ syāt yāvat upāsya viṣaya sākṣātkaraṇe tat phalam prāptam iti kāmyāḥ tu yathākāmam samuccīyeraa vā pūrva hetu abhāvāt kāmya adhikaraṇam a viśiṣṭa phala tvāt iti asya pratyudāharaṇam yāsu kāmyāsu vidyāsu saṃ yaḥ etam evam vāyum diśām vatsam veda a putra rodam roditi sa yaḥ āma brahma iti upāste yāva āmaḥ gatam tatra asya yathākāma cāraḥ bhavati iti ca evamādyāsu kriyā vat ātmīyam phalam sādhayatīṣu sākṣātkaraṇa apekṣā tāḥ yathākāmam samuccīyera a vā samuccīyera pūrva hetu abhāvāt pūrvasya a viśiṣṭa phala tvāt ityasya vikalpa hetoḥ abhāvāt aṅgeṣu yathā āśraya bhāvaḥ yathā āśraya bhāva adhikaraṇam karma aṅgeṣu udgītha ādiṣu ye āśritāḥ pratyayāḥ veda traya vihitāḥ kim te samuccīyera kim vā yathākāmam syuḥ iti saṃśaye yathā āśraya bhāvaḥ iti āha yathā eva eṣām āśrayāḥ stotra ādayaḥ saṃbhūya bhavati evam pratyayāḥ api śiṣṭeḥ ca yathā vā āśrayāḥ stotra ādayaḥ triṣu vedeṣu śiṣyate evam āśritāḥ api pratyayāḥ opadeśa kṛtaḥ api kaścid viśeṣaḥ aṅgāām tad āśrayāṇām ca pratyayāām iti arthaḥ samāhārāt iti ca praṇava udgītha ekatva vijñā māhātmyāt udgātā sva karmaṇi utpaam kṣatam hautrāt karmaṇaḥ pratisamādadhāti iti bruva vedātara uditasya pratyayasya sarva veda udita pratyaya upasaṃhāram sūcayati iti guṇa sādhāraṇya śruteḥ ca vidyā guṇam ca vidyā āśrayam satam oṃkāram veda traya sādhāraṇam śrāvayati te iyam trayī vidyā vartate om iti āśrāvayati om iti śaṃsati om iti udgāyati iti ca tatas ca āśraya sādhāraṇyāt āśrita sādhāraṇyam iti liṅga darśam eva athavā guṇa sādhāraṇya śruteḥ ca iti yadi ime karma guṇāḥ udgītha ādayaḥ sarve sarva prayoga sādhāraṇāḥ syuḥ a syāt tatas tad āśrayāṇām pratyayāām sahabhāvaḥ te tu udgītha ādayaḥ sarva aṅga grāhiṇā sarve sarva prayoga sādhāraṇāḥ śrāvyate tatas ca āśraya sahabhāvāt pratyaya sahabhāvaḥ iti a vā tad sahabhāva a śruteḥ a vā iti yathā āśraya bhāvaḥ āśritāām upāsaāām bhavitum arhati kutas tad sahabhāva a śruteḥ yathā hi tri veda vihitāām aṅgāām stotra ādīām sahabhāvaḥ śrūyate graham vā gṛhītvā camasam vā ūīya stotram upākaroti stutam auśaṃsati prastotar sāma gāya hotar etat yaja ityādiā aivam upāsaāām sahabhāva śrutiḥ asti eṣām sahabhāvam prāpayet ā iti brūmaḥ puruṣa artha tvāt upāsaāām prayoga vacaḥ hi kratu arthāām udgītha ādīām sahabhāvam prāpayet udgītha ādi upāsaāi tu kratu artha āśrayāṇi api godoha ādi vat puruṣa artha iti avocām apṛthak hi a pratibadhaḥ phalam iti atra ayam eva ca upadeśa āśrayaḥ viśeṣaḥ aṅgāām ca upāsaāām yat ekeṣām kratu artha tvam ekeṣām puruṣa artha tvam iti param ca liṅga dvayam akāraṇam upāsa asahabhāvasya ca ca pratiprayogam āśraya kārtsya upasaṃhārāt āśritāām api tathātvam vijñātum śakyam a tad prayukta tvāt upāsaāām āśraya tatrāṇi api hi kāmam āśraya abhāve mā tad sahabhāva aiyamam arhati tad sahabhāva aśruteḥ eva tasmāt yathākāmam eva darśaāt ca darśayati ca śrutiḥ asahabhāvam pratyayāām evaṃvid ha vai brahmā yajñam sarvān ca ṛtvijaḥ bhiḥ akṣati iti sarva pratyaya upasaṃhāre hi sarve sarva vidaḥ iti a vijñāavatā brahmaṇā paripālya tvam itareṣām saṃkīrtyeta tasmāt yathākāmam upāsaāām samuccayaḥ vikalpaḥ vā iti iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye tṛtīya adhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ tṛtīyaḥ udhyāyaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ śabdāt iti bādarāyaṇaḥ puruṣa artha adhikaraṇam puruṣa arthaḥ u te iti asmāt svatatrāt puruṣa arthaḥ sidhyati iti bādarāyaṇaḥ ācāryaḥ kutas etat avagamyate śabdāt iti āha tathā hi tarati śokam ātma vid sa yaḥ ha vai tat paramam brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati brahma vid param veda tasya tāvat eva ciram a vimokṣye saṃpatsye yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā iti upakramya sa sarvān ca lokān sarvān ca kāmān yaḥ tam ātmāam auvidya iti ātmā vai are draṣṭavyaḥ iti upakramya etāvat are khalu amṛta tvam iti evaṃjātīyakā śrutiḥ kevalāyāḥ vidyāyāḥ puruṣa artha hetu tvam śrāvayati atha atra pratyavatiṣṭhate śeṣa tvāt puruṣa artha vādaḥ yathā yeṣu iti jaimiiḥ api vrīhi prokṣaṇa ādi vat viṣaya dvāreṇa karma saṃbadhi eva iti atas tasmi avagata prayojae ātma jñāe yā phala śrutiḥ sā artha vādaḥ iti jaimiiḥ ācāryaḥ yathā ayeṣu dravya saṃskāra karmasu yasya parṇa mayī juhūḥ bhavati a sa pāpam ślokam śrṛṇoti yat āṅkte cakṣuḥ eva bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte yat prayāja aūyājāḥ ijyate varma vai etat yajñasya kriyate varma yajamāāya bhrātṛvya abhibhūtyai iti evaṃjātīyakā phala śrutiḥ arthavādaḥ tadvat katham asya a ārabhya adhītasya ātma jñāasya kratu praveśaḥ āśaṅkyate kartṛ dvāreṇa vākyāt iti ced a avyabhicāriṇā hi kaścit dvāreṇa vākya nimittaḥ kartā tu vyabhicāri dvāram laukika vaidika karma sādhāraṇyāt tasmāt tad dvāreṇa ātma jñāasya kratu saṃbadha siddhiḥ iti a vyatireka vijñāasya vaidikebhyaḥ karmabhyaḥ yatra aupayogāt a hi deha vyatirikta ātma jñāam laukikeṣu karmasu upayujyate sarvathā dṛṣṭārtha pravṛtti upapatteḥ vaidikeṣu tu dehapāta uttara kāla phaleṣu pravṛttiḥ opapadyate iti upayujyate vyatireka vijñāam apahata pāpma tva ādi viśeṣaṇāt asaṃsārya ātma viṣayam aupaiṣadam pravṛtti aṅgam syāt a priya ādi saṃsūcitasya saṃsāriṇaḥ eva draṣṭavya tva upadeśāt apahata pāpma tva ādi viśeṣaṇam tu stuti artham bhaviṣyati tatra tatra prasādhitam etat adhikam asaṃsāri brahma jagat kāraṇam tat eva ca saṃsāriṇaḥ pāramārthikam svarūpam upaiṣatsu upadiśyate iti satyam prasādhitam tasya eva tu phala dvāreṇa ākṣepa samādhāe kriyete dārḍhyāya ācāra darśaāt bhavati tathā uddālaka ādīām api vagamyate kevalāt ced jñāāt puruṣa artha siddhiḥ syāt kimartham karmāṇi te kuryuḥ videta kimartham parvatam vrajet iti yāyāt tad śruteḥ yat eva vidyayā karoti śraddhayā upaiṣadā tat eva vīryavattaram bhavati iti ca karma śeṣa tva śravaṇāt vidyāyāḥ a kevalāyāḥ puruṣa artha hetu tvam samavārambhaṇāt tam vidyā karmaṇī samavārabhete iti ca vidyā karmaṇoḥ phala ārambhe sāhitya darśaāt a svātatryam vidyāyāḥ tadvataḥ vidhāāt ācārya kulāt vedam adhītya yathāvidhāam guroḥ karma atiśeṣeṇa abhisamāvṛtya kuṭumbe śucau deśe svādhyāyam adhīyāaḥ iti ca evaṃjātīyakā śrutiḥ samasta veda artha vijñāavataḥ karma adhikāram darśayati tasmāt api a vijñāasya svātatryeṇa phala hetu tvam atra adhītya iti adhyaya a mātram vedasya śrūyate a ā eṣa doṣaḥ dṛṣṭārtha tvāt veda adhyayam artha avabodha paryatam iti sthitam iyamāt ca karmāṇi jijīviṣet śatam samāḥ evam tvayi a karma lipyate are iti tathā etat vai jarā maryam satram yat agihotram jarayā vā hi eva asmām ucyate mṛtyuḥ vā iti evaṃjātīyakāt iyamāt api karma śeṣa tvam eva vidyāyāḥ iti evam prāpte pratividhatte adhika upadeśāt tu bādarāyaṇasya evam tuśabdāt pakṣaḥ viparivartate yat uktam śeṣa tvāt puruṣa artha vādaḥ iti tat opapadyate kasmāt adhika upadeśāt yadi saṃsārī eva ātmā śārīraḥ kartā bhoktā ca śarīra mātra vyatirekeṇa upadiṣṭaḥ syāt tatas prakāreṇa phala śruteḥ arthavāda tvam syāt adhikaḥ tāvat śārīrāt ātmā asaṃsārī īśvaraḥ kartṛ tva ādi saṃsāri dharma rahita upahata pāpma tva ādi viśeṣaṇaḥ paramātmā karmaṇām pravartakam bhavati pratyuta karmāṇi ucchiatti iti vakṣyati upamardam ca iti atra tasmāt puruṣa artha ūtaḥ śabdāt iti ya matam bhagavataḥ bādarāyaṇasya tat tathā eva tiṣṭhati a śeṣa tva prabhṛtibhiḥ hetvābhāsaiḥ cālayitum śakyate tathā hi tam adhikam śārīrāt īśvaram ātmā darśayati śrutayaḥ yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vid bhīṣā asmāt vātaḥ pavate mahat bhayam vajram udyatam etasya vai akṣarasya praśāsae gārgi tat aikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya iti tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti evamādyāḥ yat tu priya ādi saṃsūcitasya saṃsāriṇaḥ eva vedya tayā aukarṣaṇam ātma astu kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati ātmā vā are draṣṭavyaḥ yaḥ prāṇea prāṇiti sa te ātmā sarvātaraḥ yaḥ eṣa ukṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate iti upakramya etam tu eva te bhūyas uvyākhyāsyāmi iti ca evamādi tat api asya mahataḥ bhūtasya iḥśvasitam etat yat ṛgvedaḥ śokam moham jarām mṛtyum atyeti param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svea rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate saḥ uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ iti evamādibhiḥ vākya śeṣaiḥ satyām eva adhika upadidikṣāyām atyata abheda abhiprāyam iti avirodhaḥ pārameśvaram eva hi śārīrasya pāramārthikam svarūpam upādhi kṛtam tu śārīra tvam tattvam asi draṣṭṛ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ sarvam ca etat vistareṇa asmābhiḥ purastāt tatra tatra varṇitam tulyam tu darśaam yat tu uktam ācāra darśaāt karma śeṣaḥ vidyā iti atra brūmaḥ tulyam ācāra darśaam a karma śeṣa tve pi vidyāyāḥ tathā hi śrutiḥ bhavati etat ha sma vai tad vidvāṃsaḥ āhuḥ ṛṣayaḥ kāvaṣeyāḥ kimarthāḥ vayam adhyeṣyāmahe kimarthāḥ vayam yakṣyāmahe etat ha sma vai tat pūrve juhavāṃcakrire etam vai tam ātmā am viditvā brāhmaṇāḥ putra eṣaṇāyāḥ ca vitta eṣaṇāyāḥ ca loka eṣaṇāyāḥ ca vyutthāya atha bhikṣā caryam carati iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ yājñavalkya ādīām api brahma vidām akarma eṣṭha tvam dṛśyate etāvat are khalu amṛta tvam iti ha uktvā yājñavalkyaḥ pravavrāje ityādi śrutibhyaḥ api ca yakṣyamāṇaḥ vai bhagavataḥ ham asmi iti etat liṅga darśaam vaiśvāara vidyā viṣayam saṃbhavati ca sa upādhikāyām brahma vidyāyām karma sāhitya darśaam a tu atra api karma aṅga tvam asti prakaraṇa ādi abhāvāt yat puaruktam tat śruteḥ iti atra brūmaḥ asārvatrikī yat eva vidyayā karoti iti eṣā śrutiḥ sarva vidyā viṣayā prakṛta vidyā abhisaṃbadhāt prakṛtā ca udgītha vidyā om iti etat akṣaram udgītham upāsīta iti atra vibhāgaḥ śata vat yat api uktam tam vidyā karmaṇī samavārabhete iti etat samavārambha vacam asvātatrye vidyāyāḥ liṅgam iti tat pratyucyate vibhāgaḥ utra draṣṭavyaḥ vidyā ayam puruṣam avārabhate karma ayam iti śatavat yathā śatam ābhyām dīyatām iti ukte vibhajya dīyate pañcāśat ekasmai pañcāśat aparasmai tadvat a ca idam mumukṣu viṣayam iti u kāmayamāaḥ iti saṃsāri viṣaya tva upasaṃhārāt atha a kāmayamāaḥ iti ca mumukṣoḥ pṛthak upakramāt tatra saṃsāri viṣaye vidyā vihitā pratiṣiddhā ca parigṛhyate viśeṣa abhāvāt karma api vihitam pratiṣiddham ca yathā prāpta āuvādi tvāt evam sati idam yat ca etat tadvataḥ iti uttaram paṭhati adhyaya a mātravataḥ ācārya kulāt vedam adhītya iti atra adhyaya a mātrasya śravaṇāt eva karma vidhiḥ iti adhyavasyāmaḥ evam sati avidyā tvāt a adhikāraḥ karmasu prasajyeta ā eṣa doṣaḥ a prasañjyeta vayam adhyaya a prabhavam karma avabodhaam adhikāra kāraṇam vārayāmaḥ kim tarhi svātatryeṇa eva a karma adhikāra kāraṇatām pratipadyate iti etat pratipādayāmaḥ yathā ca a kratvatara jñāam kratvatara adhikāreṇa apekṣyate evam etat api draṣṭavyam iti yat api uktam iyamāt ca iti atra abhidhīyate ā viśeṣāt kurva eva iha karmāṇi jijīviṣet iti evamādiṣu iyama śravaṇeṣu a viduṣaḥ iti viśeṣaḥ usti aviśeṣeṇa stuta yeumatiḥ vā kurve eva iha karmāṇi iti atra aparaḥ viśeṣaḥ ākhyāyate yadi api atra prakaraṇa sāmarthyāt vidvā eva kurve iti saṃbadhyeta tathā api vidyā stutaye etat draṣṭavyam a karma lipyate are iti hi vakṣyati etat uktam bhavati yāvajjīvam karma kurvati api tvayi viduṣi puruṣe a karma lepāya bhavati vidyā sāmarthyāt iti tat evam vidyā stūyate kāmakāreṇa ca eke api ca eke vidvāṃsaḥ pratyakṣīkṛta vidyā phalāḥ sataḥ tad avaṣṭambhāt phala atara sādhaeṣu prajā ādiṣu prayojaā bhāvam parāmṛśati kāmakāreṇa iti śrutiḥ bhavati vājasaeyiām etat ha sma vai tad pūrve vidvān upamardam ca api ca karma adhikāra hetoḥ kriyā kāraka phala lakṣaṇasya samastasya prapañcasya avidyā kṛtasya vidyā sāmarthyāt sva rūpa upamardam āmaati yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat ke kam paśyet tat ke kam jighret ityādiā karma adhikāra siddhim karma adhikāra ucchittiḥ eva prasajyeta tasmāt api svātatryam vidyāyāḥ ūrdhvaretaḥsu ca śabde hi ūrdhvaretaḥsu ca āśrameṣu vidyā śrūyate a ca tatra karma aṅga tvam vidyāyāḥ upapadyate karma abhāvāt hi vaidikāi karmāṇi teṣām sati syāt etat ūrdhvaretasaḥ āśramāḥ a śrūyate vedaḥ iti tat api hi vaidikeṣu śabdeṣu avagamyate trayaḥ dharmaskadhāḥ ye ca imā iraṇye śraddhā tapaḥ iti upāsate tapaḥ śraddhe ye hi upavasati araṇye etam eva pravrājiḥ lokam icchataḥ pravrajati brahmacaryāt eva pravrajet iti evamādiṣu ca ūrdhvaretaḥ tvam śruti smṛti prasiddham tasmāt api svātatryam vidyāyāḥ parāmarśam ca apavadati hi parāmarśa adhikaraṇam trayaḥ dharma skadhāḥ ityādayaḥ ye śabdāḥ ūrdhvaretasām āśramāṇām sadbhāvāya udāhṛtāḥ a te tad pratipāda āya prabhavati yatas parāmarśam eṣu śabdeṣu āśramātarāṇām jaimiiḥ ācāryaḥ a vidhim kutas a hi atra artha atara para tvam ca eṣu pratyekam upalabhyate trayaḥ dharma skadhāḥ iti atra tāvat prathamaḥ tapaḥ eva dvitīyaḥ brahmacārī ācārya kula vāsī ete puṇya lokāḥ bhavati iti parāmarśa pūrvakam āśramāṇām aātyatika phala tvam saṃkīrtya ātyatika phala tayā brahma saṃstha tā stūyate brahma saṃsthaḥ umṛta tvam eti iti parāmarśe api āśramāḥ gamyate eva satyam gamyate smṛti ācārābhyām tu teṣām prasiddhiḥ a pratyakṣa śruteḥ atas ca pratyakṣa śruti virodhe sati a ādaraṇīyāḥ te bhaviṣyati a adhikṛta viṣayāḥ vā gārhasthyam api saha eva ūrdhvaretobhiḥ parāmṛṣṭam prathamaḥ iti satyam evam tathā api tu gṛhastham prati eva karmaṇām śruti prasiddham eva hi tad astitvam tasmāt stuti arthaḥ eva ayam parāmarśaḥ a api ca apavadati hi pratyakṣā śrutiḥ āśramātaram vīra hā vā eṣa devāām yogim udvāsayate ācāryāya priyam dhaam āhṛtya mā vyavacchetsīḥ ā putrasya lokaḥ asti iti tat sarve paśavaḥ viduḥ iti evamādyā tathā ye ca imā iraṇye śraddhā tapa iti upāsate tapaḥ śraddhe ye hi upavasati araṇye iti ca āśramātara upadeśaḥ saṃdigdham ca tapaḥ eva dvitīyaḥ iti evamādiṣu tathā etam eva lokam icchataḥ pravrajati iti loka saṃstavaḥ yam brahmacaryāt eva pravrajet iti vispaṣṭam idam pratyakṣam jābālāām satyam evam etat a apekṣya tu etām śrutim ayam vicāra iti draṣṭavyam auṣṭheyam bādarāyaṇaḥ sāmya śruteḥ auṣṭheyam āśramātaram bādarāyaṇaḥ ācāryaḥ ca avaśya āuṣṭheya tvāt tad virodhāt a dhikṛta āuṣṭheyam āśramātaram iti hi imām matim irākaroti gārhasthya vat eva āśramātaram api aicchatā pratipattavyam iti kutas sāmya śruteḥ samā hi parāmarśa śrutiḥ dṛśyate trayaḥ dharma skadhāḥ ityādyā yathā iha śruti atara vihitam eva gārhasthyam parāmṛṣṭam evam āśramātaram api iti pratipattavyam yathā ca śāstra atara prāptayoḥ eva ivīta prācīāvītayoḥ parāmarśaḥ upavīta vidhi pare vākye tasmāt tulyam auṣṭheya tvam tathā etam eva lokam icchataḥ pravrajati iti asya samabhivyāhāraḥ ye cema iraṇye śraddhā tapaḥ iti upāsate iti asya ca pañcāgi vidyayā yat tu uktam tapaḥ eva dvitīyaḥ ityādiṣu āśrama ātarābhidhāam saṃdigdham iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ iścaya kāraṇa sadbhāvāt trayaḥ dharma skadhāḥ iti hi dharma skadha tri tvam pratijñātam a ca yajña ādayaḥ bhūyāṃsaḥ dharmāḥ sataḥ śakyate tatra yajña ādi liṅgaḥ gṛha āśramaḥ ekaḥ brahmacārī iti ca spaṣṭaḥ āśramaiḥ deśaḥ tapaḥ iti api ye ca imā iraṇye iti ca araṇya liṅgāt śraddhā tapobhyām āśrama gṛhītiḥ tasmāt vidhiḥ vā dhāraṇa vat vidhiḥ vā ayam āśramātarasya a parāmarśa mātram vidhi tva abhyupagame ekavākyatā pratītiḥ uparudhyeta pratīyate caṃ atra ekavākyatā puṇya loka phalāḥ trayaḥ dharma skadhāḥ brahma saṃsthatā tu amṛta tva phalā iti satyam etat satīm api tu ekavākyatā pratītim parityajya vidhiḥ eva abhyupagatavyaḥ apūrva tvāt vidhi atarasya ādarśaāt vispaṣṭāt ca āśrama ātara pratyayāt guṇavāda kalpaayā ekavākyatva yoja ā upapatteḥ dhāraṇa vat yathā adhastāt samidham ekavākya tā pratītau vidhīyate eva upari dhāraṇam apūrva tvāt tathā ca uktam śeṣa lakṣaṇe vidhiḥ tu dhāraṇe pūrva tvāt iti tadvat iha api āśrama parāmarśa śrutiḥ vidhiḥ eva iti kalpyate yadā api parāmarśaḥ eva ayam āśramātarāṇām tadā api brahma saṃstha tā tāvat saṃstava sāmarthyāt avaśyam vidheyā abhyupagatavyā sā ca kim caturṣu āśrameṣu yasya kasya cit āhosvit parivrājakasya eva iti vivektavyam yadi ca brahmacaryāteṣu āśrameṣu parāmṛśyamāeṣu parivrājakaḥ api parāmṛṣṭaḥ tatas caturṇām api āśramāṇām parāmṛṣṭa tva aviśeṣāt a āśrami tva aupapatteḥ ca yaḥ kaścid caturṣu āśrameṣu brahma saṃsthaḥ bhaviṣyati atha yaḥ kaścid caturṣu āśrameṣu brahma saṃsthaḥ bhaviṣyati atha yaḥ kaścid caturṣu āśrameṣu brahma saṃsthaḥ bhaviṣyati ath a parāmṛṣṭaḥ tatas pariśiṣyamāṇaḥ parivrāj eva brahma saṃsthaḥ iti setsyati tatra tapaḥ śabde vaikhāasa grāhiṇā parāmṛṣṭaḥ parivrāj api iti kecid tat ayuktam a hi satyām gatau parivrājakaḥ grahaṇam arhati yathā atra brahmacāri gṛhamedhiau asādhāraṇea eva svea svea viśeṣaṇea viśeṣitau evam bhikṣu vaikhāasau api iti yuktam tapaḥ ca asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ kāya kleśa pradhā tvāt tapaḥ śabdasya tatra rūḍheḥ bhikṣoḥ tu dharmaḥ idriya saṃyama ādiḥ lakṣaṇayā eva catuṣṭve ca prasiddhāḥ āśramāḥ tritve parāmṛśyate iti ayāyyam api ca bheda vyapadeśaḥ utra bhavati trayaḥ ete puṇya loka bhājaḥ ekaḥ umṛta tva bhāj iti pṛthaktve ca bheda vyapadeśaḥ uvakalpate a hi evam bhavati devadatta yajñadattau mada prajñau ayataraḥ tu a ayoḥ mahā prajñaḥ iti bhavati tu evam devadatta yajñadattau mada prajñau viṣṇumitraḥ tu mahā prajñaḥ iti tasmāt pūrve trayaḥ āśramiṇaḥ puṇya loka bhājaḥ pariśiṣyamāṇaḥ parivrāj amṛta tva bhāj katham brahma saṃstha śabdaḥ yogāt pravartamāaḥ sarvatra saṃbhava parivrājakaḥ eva avatiṣṭheta rūḍhi abhyupagame ca āśrama mātrāt amṛta tva prāpteḥ jñā āarthakya prasaṅgaḥ iti atra ucyate brahma saṃsthaḥ iti hi brahmaṇi parisamāptiḥ taiṣṭha tvam abhidhīyate tat ca trayāṇām āśramāṇām saṃbhavati sva āśrama vihita karma pratyavāya śravaṇāt parivrājakasya tu sarva karma saṃyāsāt pratyavāyaḥ saṃbhavati śama dama ādiḥ tu tadīyaḥ dharmaḥ brahma saṃsthāyāḥ upodbalakaḥ a virodhī brahmaiṣṭha tvam eva hi tasya śama dama ādi upabṛṃhitam sva āśrama vihitam karma ca itareṣām tad vyatikrame ca tasya pratyavāyaḥ tathā ca yāsaḥ iti brahmā brahmā hi paraḥ paraḥ hi brahmā vai tapāṃsi yāsaḥ eva atyarecayat saṃyāsa yoga ādi atayaḥ śuddha sattvāḥ ityādyāḥ śrutayaḥ smṛtayaḥ ca ityādyāḥ brahma saṃsthasya karma abhāvam darśayati tasmāt parivrājakasya āśrama mātrāt amṛta tva prāpteḥ jñā āāarthakya prasaṅgaḥ iti eṣaḥ api doṣaḥ āvatarati tat evam parāmarśe pi itareṣām āśramāṇām pārivrājyam tāvat brahma saṃstha tā lakṣaṇam labhyeta eva a apekṣya eva jābāla śrutim āśramātara vidhāyiīm ayam ācāryeṇa vicāraḥ pravartitaḥ vidyate eva tu āśramātara vidhi śrutiḥ pratyakṣā brahmacaryam samāpya gṛhī bhavet gṛhī bhūtvā vaī bhavet vaī bhūtvā pravrajet yadi vā itarathā brahmacaryāt eva pravrajet gṛhāt vā iti a ca iyam śrutiḥ aadhikṛta viṣayā śakyā vaktum aviśeṣa śravaṇāt atha vratī vā avratī vā sātakaḥ vā a sātakaḥ vā vā ityādiā brahma jñā a paripāka aṅga tvāt ca pārivrājyasya tat ca darśayati atha parivrāj vivarṇa vāsāḥ muṇḍa uparigrahaḥ śuciḥ adrohī bhaikṣāṇaḥ brahma bhūyāya bhavati iti tasmāt siddhāḥ ūrdhvaretasām āśramāḥ siddham ca ūrdhvaretaḥsu vidhāāt vidyāyāḥ svātatryam iti stuti mātram upādāāt iti ca iāpūrva tvāt stuti mātra adhikaraṇam saḥ eṣa rasāām rasatamaḥ paramaḥ parārdhyaḥ aṣṭamaḥ yat udgīthaḥ iyam eva ṛgagiḥ sāma ayam vāva lokaḥ tat idam eva uktham iyam eva pṛthivī iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ śrutayaḥ kim udgītha ādeḥ stuti arthāḥ āhosvit upāsa āvidhi arthāḥ iti asmin saṃśaye stuti arthāḥ iti yuktam udgītha ādi karma aṅgāi upādāya śravaṇāt yathā iyam eva juhūḥ ādityaḥ kūrmaḥ svargaḥ lokaḥ āhavaīyaḥ ityādyāḥ juhū ādi stuti arthāḥ tadvat iti ced etya āha a hi stuti mātram āsām śrutīām yuktam apūrva tvāt vidhi artha tāyām hi apūrvaḥ ṛthaḥ vihitaḥ bhavati stuti artha tāyām tu āarthakyam eva syāt vidhāyakasya hi śabdasya vākyaśeṣa bhāvam stutiḥ upayujyate iti uktam tu ekavākya tvāt stuti arthe vidhīām syuḥ iti atra pradeśa atara vihitāām tu udgītha ādīām iyam pradeśa atara paṭhitā stutiḥ vākyaśeṣa bhāvam apratipadyamāā aarthikā eva syāt iyam eva juhūḥ ityādi tu vidhi saṃidhau eva amātam iti vaiṣamyam tasmāt vidhi arthāḥ eva evaṃjātīyakāḥ śrutayaḥ bhāva śabdāt ca udgītham upāsīta sāma upāsīta aham uktham asmi iti vidyāt ityādayaḥ ca vispaṣṭāḥ vidhi śabdāḥ śrūyate te ca stuti mātra prayojaa tāyām vyāhayera tathā ca smaraṇam kuryāt kriyeta kartavyam bhavet syāt iti pañcamam etat syāt sarva vedeṣu iyatam vidhi lakṣaṇam iti liṅ ādi arthaḥ vidhiḥ iti evam smarati prati prakaraṇam ca śrāvyate āpayitā ha vai kāmāām bhavati eṣa hi eva kalpate ha asmai lokāḥ ūrdhvāḥ ca āvṛttāḥ ca tasmāt api udgītha ādi śrutayaḥ pāriplava arthāḥ iti viśeṣita tvāt pāriplava adhikaraṇam atha ha yājñavalkyasya dve bhārye babhūvatuḥ maitreyī ca kātyāyaī ca pratardaaḥ ha vai daivodāsiḥ idrasya priyam dhāma upajagāma jāaśrutiḥ ha pautrāyaṇaḥ śraddhā deyaḥ bahu dāyī bahu pākyaḥ āsa iti evamādiṣu saṃśayaḥ kim imāi pāriplava prayoga arthāi āhosvit saṃihita vidyā pratipatti arthāḥ iti pāriplava arthāḥ imāḥ ākhyā aśrutayaḥ ākhyā a sāmāyāt ākhyā a prayogasya ca pāriplave codita tvāt tatas ca vidyā pradhā a tvam syāt matra vat prayoga śeṣa tvāt iti ced kasmāt viśeṣita tvāt pāriplavam ācakṣīta iti hi prakṛtya mauḥ vaivasvataḥ rājā iti evamādi kāicid eva tatra viśeṣyate ākhyā a sāmāyāt ced sarva gṛhītiḥ syāt aarthakam eva idam viśeṣaṇam bhavet tasmāt a pāriplava arthā etāḥ ākhyā aśrutayaḥ tathā ca ekavākyatā upabadhāt asati ca pāriplava artha tve ākhyāāām saṃihita vidyā pratipāda upayogi tā eva yāyyā ekavākyatā upabadhāt tathā hi tatra tatra saṃihitābhiḥ vidyābhiḥ ekavākyatā dṛśyate praroca upayogāt pratipatti saukarya upayogāt ca maitreyībrāhmaṇe tāvat ātmā vai are draṣṭavyaḥ ityādyayā vidyayā ekavākyatā dṛśyate prāṇaḥ asmi prajñā ātmā ityādyayā iti atra api vāyuḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ ityādyayā yathā saḥ ātman o vapām udakhidat iti evamādīām karma śruti gatāām ākhyāām saṃihita vidhi stuti artha tā tadvat tasmāa pāriplava artha tvam atas eva ca āgīdha ādi aapekṣā agīdha ādi adhikaraṇam puruṣa artha utas śabdāt iti etat vyavahitam api saṃbhavāt atas iti parāmṛśyate atas eva ca vidyāyāḥ puruṣa artha hetu tvāt agīdha ādīya āśrama karmāṇi vidyayā sva artha siddhau āpekṣitavyāi iti ādyasya eva adhikaraṇasya phalam upasaṃharati adhika vivakṣayā sarva apekṣā ca yajña ādi śruteḥ aśva vat sarva apekṣā adhikaraṇam idam idāīm cityate kim vidyāyāḥ atyatam eva a apekṣā āśrama karmaṇām uta asti kācid apekṣā iti tatra atas āśrama karmāṇi vidyayā sva artha siddhau āpekṣyate evam atyatam eva a apekṣāyām prāptāyām idam ucyate sarva apekṣā ca iti apekṣate ca vidyā sarvāṇi āśrama karmāṇi ātyatam aapekṣā eva viruddham idam apekṣate ca āśrama karmāṇi vidyā āpekṣate ca iti eti brūmaḥ hi vidyā phala siddhim prati a kiṃcid ayat apekṣate utpattim prati tu apekṣate kutas yajña ādi śruteḥ tathā hi śrutiḥ tam etam brāhmaṇāḥ vividiṣati iti vidyā sādha abhāvam darśayati vividiṣā saṃyogāt ca eṣām utpatti sādha abhāvaḥ avasīyate atha yat yajñaḥ iti ācakṣate brahmacaryam eva tat iti atra ca vidyā sādhaa bhūtasya brahmacaryasya yajña ādibhiḥ saṃstavāt yajña ādīām api hi sādhaa bhāvaḥ sūcyate sarve vedāḥ yat padam tapāṃsi sarvāṇi ca yat vadati yat icchataḥ brahmacaryam carati tat te padam saṃgraheṇa bravīmi iti evamādyā ca śrutiḥ āśrama karmaṇām vidyā sādha abhāvam sūcayati smṛtiḥ api kaṣāya paktiḥ karmāṇi tu paramā gatiḥ kaṣāye karmabhiḥ pakve tatas jñāam pravartate iti evamādyā aśva vat iti yathā ca lāṅgala ākarṣaṇe yujyate rathacaryāyām tu yujyate evam āśrama karmāṇi vidyayā phala siddhau āpekṣyate utpattau ca apekṣyate iti śama dama ādi upetaḥ syāt tathā api tu tad vidheḥ tad aṅga tayā teṣām avaśya auṣṭheya tvāt yadi kaścid cimayeta yajña ādīām vidyā sādha abhāvaḥ vidhi abhāvāt vividiṣati iti evaṃjātīyakā hi śrutiḥ auvāda svarūpā vidyā abhiṣṭava parā a yajña ādi vidhi parā ittham mahābhāgā vidyā yat yajña ādibhiḥ etām avāptum icchati iti tathā api tu śama dama ādi upetaḥ syāt vidyā arthī tasmāt evam vicchātaḥ dātaḥ uparataḥ titikṣuḥ samāhitaḥ bhūtvā ātmayā iva ātmānam paśyati iti śama dama ādīām vidhāāt vihitāām ca atra api bhūtvā paśyati iti upalabhyate a vidhiḥ ā iti brūmaḥ tasmāt iti prakṛta praśaṃsā parigrahāt vidhi tva pratīteḥ paśyet iti ca mādhyaṃdiāḥ vispaṣṭam eva vidhim adhīyate tasmāt yajña ādi aapekṣāyām api śama ādīya pekṣitavyā ai tu apekṣitavyā yajña ādi śruteḥ eva uktam yajña ādibhiḥ vividiṣati iti atra a vidhiḥ upalabhyate iti satyam uktam tathā api tu apūrva tvāt saṃyogasya vidhiḥ parikalpyate a hi ayam yajña ādīām vividiṣā saṃyogaḥ pūrvam prāptaḥ tasmāt pūṣā prapiṣṭabhāga udatakaḥ hi iti evamādiṣu ca aśruta vidhikeṣu api vākyeṣu apūrva tvāt vidhim parikalpya pauṣṇam peṣaṇam vikṛtau pratīyeta ityādi vicāraḥ prathame tatre pravartitaḥ tathā ca uktam vidhiḥ vā dhāraṇa vat iti smṛtiṣu api bhagavadgītā ādyāsu bhavati iti prapañcitam tasmāt yajña ādīi śama dama ādīi ca yathāśramam sarvāṇi eva āśrama karmāṇi vidyā utpattau apekṣitavyāi tatra api evaṃvid iti vidyā saṃyogāt vidyā sādhaāi śama ādīi vividiṣā saṃyogāt tu bāhyatarāṇi vivektavyam sarvāāumatiḥ ca prāṇa atyaye tad darśaāt sarvāāumati adhikaraṇam prāṇa saṃvāde śrūyate chadogāām a ha vai evaṃvidi kiṃcaāaam bhavati iti tathā vājasaeyiām a ha vai jagdham bhavati āaam pratigṛhītam iti sarvam asya adaīyam eva bhavati iti arthaḥ kim idam śama ādi vat vidyā aṅgam vidhīyate uta stuti artham saṃkīrtyate iti saṃśaye vidhiḥ iti tāvat prāptam tathā hi pravṛtti viśeṣa karaḥ upadeśaḥ bhavati atas prāṇa vidyā saṃidhāāt tad aṅga tve iyam evam sati bhakṣya abhakṣya vibhāga śāstra vyāghātaḥ syāt doṣaḥ sāmāya viśeṣa bhāvāt bādha upapatteḥ yathā prāṇi hiṃsā pratiṣedhasya bādhaḥ yathā ca a bādhaḥ yathā ca striyam pariharet tat vratam vāmadevya vidyā viṣayeṇa sarva strī aparihāra vacaea sāmāya viṣayam gamya agamya vibhāga śāstram bādhyate evam aeā api prāṇa vidyā viṣayeṇa bhakṣya abhakṣya vibhāga śāstram bādhyeta iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ vidhīyate iti anena artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha artha arth hi atra vidhāyakaḥ śabdaḥ upalabhyate a ha vā evaṃvidi bhavati iti ca asatyām api vidhi pratītau pravṛtti viśeṣa karatva lobhe eva vidhiḥ abhyupagatum śakyate api ca śva ādi maryādam prāṇasyāam iti uktvā idam ucyate aivaṃvidaḥ kiṃcid aaam bhavati iti ca śva ādi maryādam aam māuṣeṇa dehena upabhoktum śakyate śakyate tu prāṇasyāam idam sarvam iti vicitayitum tasmāt prāṇa avijñā a praśaṃsā arthaḥ yam arthavādaḥ tat darśayati sarva aumatiḥ ca prāṇa atyaye iti etat uktam bhavati prāṇa atyayaḥ eva hi parasyām āpadi tad darśaāt tathā hi śrutiḥ cākrāyaṇasya ṛṣeḥ kaṣṭāyām avasthāyām abhakṣya bhakṣaṇe pravṛttim darśayati maṭacī hateṣu kuruṣu iti asmi brāhmaṇe cākrāyaṇaḥ kila ṛṣiḥ āpad gataḥ sāmi khāditā kulmāṣān cakhāda aupāam tu tadīyam ucchiṣṭa doṣāt pratyācacakṣe kāraṇam ca atra uvāca a vā ajīviṣyam imā akhādaḥ iti kāmaḥ me iti ca uttaredyus tāḥ eva sva para ucchiṣṭa a paryuṣita a kulmāṣāḥ bhakṣayāṃbabhūva iti tat etat ucchiṣṭa ucchiṣṭa paryuṣita bhakṣaṇam darśayatyāḥ śruteḥ āśaya atiśayaḥ lakṣyate prāṇa atyaya prasaṅge prāṇa saṃdhāraṇāya abhakṣyam api bhakṣayitavyam iti svastha avasthāyām tu kartavyam vidyāvatā api iti aupāa pratyākhyāāt gamyate tasmāt artha vādaḥ a ha vā evaṃvidi iti evamādiḥ abādhāt ca evam ca sati āhāra śuddhau sattva śuddhiḥ iti evamādi bhakṣya abhakṣya vibhāga śāstram abādhitam bhaviṣyati api ca smaryate api ca āpadi sarva a bhakṣaṇam api smaryate viduṣaḥ viduṣaḥ ca aviśeṣeṇa jīvita atyayam āpao yaḥ am atti yatas tatas lipyate padma patram iva ambhasā iti tathā madyam brāhmaṇaḥ surā pasya brāhmaṇasya uṣṇām āsiñceyuḥ surā pāḥ kṛmayaḥ bhavati abhakṣya bhakṣaṇāt iti ca smaryate śabdaḥ kāmakāre śabdaḥ ca pratiṣedhakaḥ saṃhitāyām śrūyate tasmāt brāhmaṇaḥ surām a pibet iti saḥ api a ha vā evaṃvidi iti asya arthavāda tvāt upapaataraḥ bhavati tasmāt evaṃjātīyakāḥ arthavādāḥ a vidhayaḥ iti vihita tvāt ca āśrama karma api āśrama karma adhikaraṇam sarva apekṣā ca iti atra āśrama karmaṇām vidyā sādhaatvam avadhāritam idāīm tu kim amumukṣoḥ api āśrama mātraiṣṭhasya vidyām a kāmayamā asya uta aho brāhmaṇāḥ vividiṣati ityādiā āśrama karmaṇām vidyā sādhaa tvea vihita tvāt vidyām a icchataḥ phalātaram kāmayamā asya atha tarhi eṣām vidyā sādhaa tvam tarhi eṣām vidyā sādhaa tvam ityāitya saṃyoga virodhāt iti asyām prāptau paṭhati āśrama mātraiṣṭhasya api amumukṣoḥ kartavyāya iva karmāṇi yāvajjīvam agihotram juhoti vihita tvāt hi kaścid asti atha yat uktam sati vidyā sādhaatvam eṣām syāt iti atas uttaram paṭhati ca vidyā sahakārīṇi ca syuḥ vihita tvāt eva tam etam brāhmaṇāḥ vividiṣati tat uktam sarva apekṣā ca yajña ādi śruteḥ
