aśva vat iti ca idam vidyā sahakāri tva vacaam āśrama karmaṇām prayāja ādi vat vidyā phala viṣayam matavyam avidhi lakṣaṇa tvāt vidyāyāḥ asādhya tvāt ca vidyā phalasya vidhi lakṣaṇam hi darśa pūrṇamāsa ādi svarga phala siṣādhayiṣayā sahakāri sādhaātaram apekṣate vidyā tathā ca uktam atas eva iti tasmāt utpatti sādhaatve eva eṣām sahakāri tva vācoyuktiḥ ca atra āśaṅkyaḥ karma abhede pi saṃyoga bhedāt hi ekaḥ saṃyogaḥ yāvajjīva ādi vākya kalpitaḥ tasya vidyā phala tvam aityaḥ tu aparaḥ saṃyogaḥ tam etam ityādi vākya kalpitaḥ tasya vidyā phala tvam yathā ekasya api khādira tvasya saṃyoge kratu artha tvam saṃyoge puruṣa artha tvam tadvat sarvathā api tu te eva ubhaya liṅgāt sarvathā api āśrama karma tva pakṣe vidyā sahakāri tva pakṣe ca te eva agihotra ādayaḥ dharmāḥ auṣṭheyāḥ te eva iti avadhāraya ācāryaḥ kim karma bheda śaṅkām iti brūmaḥ yathā māsam agihotram juhvati iti atra ityāt agihotrāt karmātaram upadiśyate ā evam iha karma bhedaḥ usti iti arthaḥ kutas ubhaya liṅgāt śruti liṅgāt smṛti liṅgāt ca śruti liṅgam tāvat tam etam brāhmaṇāḥ vividiṣati iti siddha vat utpa rūpāṇi eva vividiṣāyām viiyuṅkte a tu juhvati ityādi vat apūrvam eṣām rūpam utpādayati iti smṛti liṅgam api a āśritaḥ karma phalam kāryam karma karoti yaḥ iti vijñāta kartavyatākam eva karma vidyā utpatti artham darśayati yasya ete ṣṭācatvāriṃśat saṃskārāḥ iti ādyā ca saṃskāra tva prasiddhiḥ vaidikeṣu karmasu tad saṃskṛtasya vidyā utpattim abhipretya smṛtau bhavati tasmāt sādhu idam abheda avadhāraṇam a abhibhavam ca darśayati sahakāri tvasya eva etad upodbalakam liṅga darśaam a abhibhavam ca darśayati śrutiḥ rāga ādibhiḥ kleśaiḥ eṣa hi ātmā a aśyati yam brahmacaryeṇa a uvidate tasmāt yajña ādīya āśrama karmāṇi ca bhavati vidyā sahakārīṇi ca iti sthitam ca api tu tad dṛṣṭeḥ vidhura adhikaraṇam vidhura ādīām dravya ādi saṃpad rahitāām ca ayatam āśrama pratipatti hīām kim vidyāyām adhikāraḥ u sti kim vā āsti iti saṃśaye āsti iti tāvat prāptam āśrama karmaṇām vidyā hetu tva avadhāraṇāt āśrama karma asaṃbhavāt ca eteṣām iti evam prāpte idam āha atarā tu vidyāyām adhikriyate kutas tad dṛṣṭeḥ raikva vāca kavī prabhṛtīām evaṃbhūtāām api brahma vid tva śruti upalabdheḥ api ca smaryate saṃvarta prabhṛtīām ca a ga caryā ādi yogāt a apekṣita āśrama karmaṇām api mahā yogi tvam smaryate itihāse liṅgam idam kā u khalu prāptiḥ iti sā abhidhīyate viśeṣa augrahaḥ ca teṣām api ca aviruddhaiḥ puruṣa mātra saṃbadhibhiḥ japa upavāsa devatā ārādha ādibhiḥ dharma viśeṣaiḥ augrahaḥ vidyāyāḥ saṃbhavati tathā ca smṛtiḥ tu saṃsidhyet brāhmaṇaḥ saṃśayaḥ vā kuryām maitraḥ brāhmaṇaḥ ucyate iti asaṃbhavat āśrama karmaṇaḥ api japya adhikāram darśayati ca āśrama karmabhiḥ saṃbhavati eva vidyāyāḥ augrahaḥ tathā ca smṛtiḥ aikajama saṃsiddhaḥ tatas yāti parām gatim iti saṃskāra viśeṣāḥ vidyāyām darśayati dṛṣṭārthā ca vidyā pratiṣedha abhāva mātreṇa api arthiam adhikaroti śravaṇa ādiṣu tasmāt vidhura ādīām api adhikāraḥ virudhyate atas tu itarat jyāyaḥ liṃṅgāt ca atas tu a tarāla varti tvāt itarat āśrama varti tvam jyāyaḥ vidyā sādhaam śruti smṛti saṃdṛbdha tvāt śruti liṅgāt ca brahma vid puṇya kṛt taijasaḥ ca iti aāśramī a tiṣṭheta diam ekam api dvijaḥ saṃvatsaram aāśramī sthitvā kṛcchram ekam caret iti ca smṛti liṅgāt caturthaḥ udhyāyaḥ prathamaḥ pādaḥ āvṛttiḥ asakṛt upadeśāt āvṛti adhikaraṇam ātmā vai are draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ matavyaḥ ididhyāsitavyaḥ tam eva dhīraḥ vijñāya prajñām kurvīta saḥ u veṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ iti ca evamādi śravaṇeṣu saṃśayaḥ kim sakṛt pratyayaḥ kartavyaḥ āhosvit āvṛttyā iti kim tāvat prāptam sakṛt pratyayaḥ syāt prayāja ādi vat tāvatā śāstrasya kṛtārtha tvāt aśrūyamāṇāyām hi āvṛttau kriyamāṇāyām aśāstra arthaḥ kṛtaḥ bhavet asakṛt upadeśāḥ udāhṛtāḥ śrotavyaḥ matavyaḥ ididhyāsitavyaḥ iti evamādayaḥ evam api yāvacchabdam āvartayet sakṛt śravaṇam ca iti ātiriktam sakṛt upadeśeṣu tu vedaḥ upāsīta iti evamādiṣu a āvṛttiḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ pratyaya āvṛttiḥ kartavyā kutas asakṛt upadeśāt śrotavyaḥ matavyaḥ ididhyāsitavyaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ hi asakṛt upadeśaḥ pratyaya āvṛttim sūcayati uktam yāvacchabdam eva āvartayet ādhikam iti a darśa a paryavasāa tvāt eṣām hi hi tadvat api ca upāsaam ididhyāsaam ca iti atarṇīta āvṛtti guṇā eva kriyā abhidhīyate tathā hi loke gurum upāste rājā aam upāste iti ca yaḥ tātparyeṇa saḥ evam ucyate tathā dhyāyati patim iti yā iratara smaraṇā patim prati sa utkaṇṭhā sā evam abhidhīyate vidi upāstyoḥ ca a vyatirekeṇa prayogaḥ dṛśyate kvacid vidiā upakramyaḥ upāsiā upasaṃharati yathā yaḥ tat veda yat sa veda sa mayā etat uktaḥ iti atra me etām bhagavaḥ devatām śādhi yām devatām upāsse iti kvacid ca upāsiā upakramya vidiā upasaṃharati yathā brahma iti upāsīta iti atra bhāti ca tapati ca kīrtyā yaśasā brahmavarcase yaḥ evam veda iti tasmāt sakṛt upadeśeṣu api āvṛtti siddhiḥ asakṛt upadeśaḥ tu āvṛtteḥ sūcakaḥ liṅgāt ca liṅgam api pratyaya āvṛttim pratyāyayati tathā hi udgītha vijñāam prastutya ādityaḥ udgīthaḥ iti etat eka putra tā doṣeṇa apodya raśmīn tvam paryāvartayāt iti raśmi bahu tva vijñāam bahu putra tāyai vidadhat siddha vat pratyaya āvṛttim darśayati sarva pratyayeṣu āvṛtti siddhiḥ atra āha bhavatu āma sādhya phaleṣu pratyayeṣu āvṛttiḥ teṣu āvṛtti sādhyasya atiśayasya saṃbhavāt yaḥ tu para brahma viṣayaḥ iti aśuddha buddha mukta svabhāvam eva ātma bhūtam param brahma samarpayati tatra kimarthā āvṛttiḥ iti sakṛt śrutau ca brahma ātmatva pratīti aupapatteḥ āvṛtti abhyupagamaḥ iti ced a āvṛttau api tad aupapatteḥ yadi hi tat tvam asi iti evaṃjātīyakam vākyam sakṛt śrūyamāṇam brahma ātmatva pratītim ā utpādayet tatas tat eva āvartyam āam utpādayiṣyati iti kā pratyāśā syāt atha ucyeta a kevalam vākyam kaṃcid artham sākṣātkartum śakoti atas yukti apekṣam brahma ātmatvam iti tathā api āvṛtti āarthakyam eva sā api hi yuktiḥ sakṛt pravṛttā eva svam artham aubhāvayiṣyati atha api syāt yuktyā vākyea ca sāmāya viṣayam eva kriyate a viśeṣa viṣayam yathā asti me hṛdaye śūlam iti atas vākyāt gātra kampa ādi liṅgāt ca śūla sadbhāva sāmāyam eva paraḥ pratipadyate yathā saḥ eva śūlī viśeṣa aubhavaḥ ca avidyāyāḥ tad arthā āvṛttiḥ iti ced a asakṛt api tāvamātre kriyamāṇe viśeṣa vijñā utpatti asaṃbhavāt a hi sakṛt prayuktābhyām śāstra yuktibhyām a avagataḥ viśeṣaḥ śata kṛtvā upi śakyate tasmāt yadi śāstra yuktibhyām viśeṣaḥ pratipādyeta yadi vā sāmāyam eva ubhayathā api sakṛt pravṛtte eva te sva kāryam kurutaḥ iti āvṛttyā aupayogaḥ ca sakṛt prayukte śāstra yuktī kasyacid api aubhavam otpādayataḥ iti śakyate iyatum vicitra prajña tvāt pratipattṛṇām api ca laukike padārthe sāmāya viśeṣavati ekam aṃśam avadhārayati apareṇa aparam iti syāt api abhyāsa upayogaḥ yathā dīrgha prapāṭhaka grahaṇa ādiṣu a tu i rviśeṣe brahmaṇi sāmāya viśeṣa rahite caitaya mātra ātmake pramā utpattau abhyāsa apekṣā yuktā iti atra ucyate bhavet āvṛtti āarthakyam tam prati yaḥ tat tvam asi iti sakṛt uktam eva śakuyāt yaḥ tu a śakoti tam prati upayujyate eva āvṛttiḥ tathā hi chādogye tat tvam asi śvetaketo iti upadiśya bhūyas eva mā bhagavān vijñāpayatu iti puaḥ tat tad āśaṅkā kāraṇam tat tad āśaṅkā kāraṇam tat tvam asi iti eva asakṛt upadiśati tathā ca śrotavyaḥ matavyaḥ ididhyāsitavyaḥ ityādi darśitam uktam sakṛt śrutam ced tattvamasi vākyam svam artham aubhāvayitum an tatas śakṣyati iti doṣaḥ hi dṛśyate hi sakṛt śrutāt vākyāt mad apratītam vākya artham āvartayataḥ samyak pratipadyamānaḥ api ca tat tvam asi iti etat vākyam tvam padārthasya tad padārtha bhāvam ācaṣṭe ca prakṛtam sat brahma īkṣitṛ jagataḥ ca adṛṣṭam draṣṭṛ avijñātam vijñātṛ ajam ajaram amaram asthūlam aaṇu ahrasvam adīrgham iti ādi śāstra siddham tatra aja ādi śabdaiḥ jama ādayaḥ bhāva vikārāḥ asthūla ādi śabdaiḥ ca sthaulya ādayaḥ dravya dharmāḥ vijñā ādi śabdaiḥ ca caitaya prakāśa ātmaka tvam uktam eṣa vyāvṛtta sarva saṃsāra dharmakaḥ ubhava ātmakaḥ brahma saṃjñakaḥ tad padārthaḥ prasiddhaḥ tathā tvam padārthaḥ api pratyagātmā śrotā dehāt ārabhya pratyagātma tayā tatra yeṣām etau padārthau ajñā a saṃśaya viparyaya pratibaddhau teṣām tat tvam asi iti etat vākyam svārthe pramām ā utpādayitum śakoti padārtha jñā a pūrvaka tvāt vākya artha jñā asya ityatas eṣṭavyaḥ padārtha viveka prayojaḥ śāstra yukti abhyāsaḥ yadi api ca pratipattavyaḥ ātmā tathā api adhyāropitam bahu aṃśa tvam deha idriya maaḥ buddhi viṣaya veda ādi lakṣaṇam tatra ekam aṃśam apohati apareṇa aparam iti yujyate tatra kramavatī pratipattiḥ tat tu pūrvarūpam eva ātma pratipatteḥ yeṣām punar a ajñā asaṃśaya viparyaya lakṣaṇaḥ padārtha viṣayaḥ te sakṛt uktam eva tattvamasi vākya artham āvṛtti āarthakyam iṣṭam eva sakṛt utpaā eva hi ātma pratipattiḥ avidyām kaścid api kramaḥ abhyupagamyate satyam evam yujyeta yadi kasyacid evam pratipattiḥ bhavet balavatī hi ātma obhavat duḥkhi tva ādi pratipattiḥ atas a duḥkhi tva ādi abhāvam kaścid pratipadyate iti ced a deha ādi abhimāa vat duḥkhi tva ādi abhimāasya mithyā abhimāa tva upapatteḥ pratyakṣam hi dehe chidyamāe dahyamāe vā aham chidye dahye iti ca mithyā abhimāaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tathā bāhyatareṣu api putra mitra ādiṣu aham eva saṃtapye iti adhyāropaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tathā duḥkhi tva ādi abhimāaḥ api syāt deha ādi vat eva suṣupta ādiṣu ca suṣupta ādiṣu ca caitayasya tu suṣupte pi yat vai paśyati tasmāt tasmāt ca evam ca evam kiṃcid ayatkṛtyam avaśiṣyate tathā ca śrutiḥ kim prajayā kariṣyāmaḥ yeṣām ā oyam ātmā ayam lokaḥ iti ātma vidaḥ kartavya abhāvam darśayati smṛtiḥ api yaḥ tu ātma ratiḥ eva syāt ātma tṛptaḥ ca māavaḥ ātmayā iva ca saṃtuṣṭaḥ tasya kāryam as vidyate iti yasya tu a eṣaḥ uubhavaḥ drāk iva jāyate tam prati aubhava arthaḥ eva āvṛtti abhyupagamaḥ tatra api a tattvamasi vākya arthāt pracyāvya āvṛttau pravartayet a hi vara ghātāya kayām udvāhayati ca asmi adhikṛtaḥ aham kartā mayā idam kartavyam iti avaśyam brahma pratyayāt viparīta pratyayaḥ utpadyate yaḥ tu svayam eva mada matiḥ apratibhā tam vākya artham jihāset tasya etasmin eva vākya arthe sthirīkāraḥ āvṛtti ādi vācoyuktyā abhyupeyate tasmāt para brahma viṣaye api pratyaye tad upāya upadeśeṣu āvṛtti siddhiḥ ātmā iti tu upagacchati grāhayati ca ātma tva upāsa adhikaraṇam yaḥ śāstra ukta viśeṣaṇaḥ paramātmā sa kim aham iti grahītavyaḥ kim vā madayaḥ iti etat vicārayati katham puar ātma śabde pratyagātma viṣaye śrūyamāṇe saṃśayaḥ iti ucyate ayam ātma śabdaḥ mukhyaḥ śakyate abhyupagatum sati jīva īśvarayoḥ abheda saṃbhave itarathā tu gauṇaḥ ūyam abhyupagatavyaḥ iti mayate kim tāvat prāptam a aham iti grāhyaḥ hi apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇaḥ śakyate grahītum viparīta guṇaḥ vā apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇa tve apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇaḥ ca parameśvaraḥ tad viparīta guṇaḥ tu śārīraḥ īśvarasya ca saṃsāri ātma tve īśvara abhāva prasaṅgaḥ tatas śāstra āarthakyam saṃsāriṇaḥ api īśvara ātma tve adhikārī abhāvāt eva pratyakṣa ādi virodhaḥ ca tādātmya darśaam śāstrāt kartavyam pratimā ādiṣu iva viṣṇu ādi darśaam iti ced kāmam evam bhavatu a tu saṃsāriṇaḥ mukhya ātmā īśvaraḥ iti etat prāpayitavyam evam prāpte brūmaḥ ātmā iti eva parameśvaraḥ pratipattavyaḥ tathā hi parameśvara prakriyāyām jābālāḥ etam upagacchati tvam vai aham asmi bhagavaḥ devatā iham vai tvam asi devate iti tathā aham brahma asmi iti evamādayaḥ ātma tva upagamāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ grāhayati ca īśvaram eṣa te ātmā sarva ataraḥ eṣa te ātmā ataryāmī amṛtaḥ tat satyam saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi iti evamādi yat uktam pratīka darśaam idam bhaviṣyati iti tat ayuktam gauṇa tva prasaṅgāt vākya vairūpyāt ca yatra hi pratīka dṛṣṭiḥ abhipreyate sakṛt eva tatra bhavati yathā brahma ādityaḥ brahma ityādi iha puas tvam aham asmi aham ca tvam asi iti āha atas pratīka śruti vairūpyāt abheda pratipattiḥ bheda dṛṣṭi apavādāt ca tathā hi atha yaḥ yām devatām upāste iya usau asmi iti a sa veda mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum yaḥ iha paśyati sarvam tam parādāt yaḥ yatra ātmā sarvam veda iti evamādyā bhūyasī śrutiḥ apavadati yat tu uktam a viruddha guṇayoḥ iti doṣaḥ viruddha guṇa tāyāḥ mithyātva upapatteḥ yat uktam īśvara abhāva prasaṅgaḥ iti tat asat śāstra prāmāṇyāt a abhyupagamāt ca a hi īśvarasya saṃsāri ātmatvam pratipādyate iti abhyupagacchāmaḥ kiṃtarhi saṃsāriṇaḥ īśvara ātmatvam iti evam ca sati advaita īśvarasya apahatapāpmatva ādi guṇatā viparīta guṇatā tu itarasya mithyā iti vyavatiṣṭhate yat api uktam adhikāri abhāvaḥ pratyakṣa ādi virodhaḥ ca iti tat api asat prāk prabodhāt saṃsāri tva abhyupagamāt tad viṣaya tvāt ca pratyakṣa ādi vyavahārasya yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kam paśyet ityādiā hi prabodhe pratyakṣa ādi abhāvam darśayati pratyakṣa ādi abhāve śruteḥ api abhāva prasaṅgaḥ iti ced a iṣṭa tvāt atra pitā a pitā bhavati iti upakramya vedāḥ a vedāḥ iti vacaāt iṣyate eva asmābhiḥ śruteḥ api abhāvaḥ prabodhe kasya ayam aprabodhaḥ iti ced yaḥ tvam pṛcchasi tasya te iti vadāmaḥ aham īśvara eva uktaḥ śrutyā yadi evam pratibuddhaḥ asi āsti kasyacid aprabodhaḥ yaḥ api doṣaḥ codyate kaiḥ cid avidyayā kila ātmā sa dvitīya tvāt advaita aupapattiḥ iti saḥ upi tasmāt ātmā iti eva īśvare dadhīta a pratīke a hi saḥ pratīka adhikaraṇam brahma iti upāsīta iti adhyātmam atha adhidaivatam brahma iti tathā ādityaḥ brahma iti ādeśaḥ sa yaḥ āma brahma iti upāste iti evamādiṣu pratīka upāsaeṣu saṃśayaḥ kim teṣu api ātma grahaḥ kartavyaḥ a vā iti kim tāvat prāptam teṣu api ātma grahaḥ eva yuktaḥ kartum kasmāt brahmaṇaḥ śrutiṣu prasiddha tvāt pratīkāām api brahma vikāra tvāt brahma tve sati ātma tva upapatteḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ a pratīkeṣu ātma matim badhīyāt a pratīkeṣu ātma matim badhīyāt hi saḥ upāsakaḥ ākalayet yat puas brahma vikāra tvāt pratīkānām brahmatvam tatas ca ātmatvam iti tat asat pratīka abhāva prasaṅgāt vikāra svarūpa upamardea hi āma ādi jātasya brahmatvam eva āśritam bhavati sva rūpa upamarde ca kutas pratīka tvam ātma grahaḥ vā ca brahmaṇaḥ ātma tvāt brahma dṛṣṭi upadeśeṣu ātma dṛṣṭiḥ kalpyā kartṛ tva ādyaiḥ ākaraṇāt kartṛ tva ādi sarva saṃsāra dharmaiḥ ākaraṇe hi brahmaṇaḥ ātma tva upadeśaḥ ca atas ca upāsakasya pratīkaiḥ sama tvāt ātma grahaḥ upapadyate hi rucaka svastikayoḥ itaretara ātma tvam asti suvarṇa ātmā eva tu brahma ātmā ekatve pratīka abhāva prasaṅgam avocāma atas a pratīkeṣu ātma dṛṣṭiḥ kriyate brahma dṛṣṭiḥ utkarṣāt brahma dṛṣṭi adhikaraṇam teṣu eva udāharaṇeṣu ayaḥ saṃśayaḥ kim āditya ādi dṛṣṭayaḥ brahmaṇi adhyasitavyāḥ kim vā brahma dṛṣṭiḥ āditya ādiṣu iti kutas saṃśayaḥ sāmāādhikaraṇye kāraṇa aavadhāraṇāt atra hi brahma śabdasya āditya ādi śabdaiḥ sāmāādhikaraṇyam upalabhyate āditya upāstiḥ anupūrvaḥ anupūrvaḥ anupūrvaḥ anupūrvaḥ anupūrvaḥ anupūrvaḥ anupūrvaḥ anupūrvaḥ anupūrva brahma prāṇaḥ brahma vidyut brahma ityādi sama a vibhakti nirdeśāt a ca atra āñjasam sāmāādhikaraṇyam avakalpate artha ataravacaatvāt brahma āditya ādi śabdāām a hi bhavati gauḥ aśvaḥ iti sāmāādhikaraṇyam prakṛti vikāra bhāvāt brahma āditya ādīām mṛd śarāva ādi vat sāmāādhikaraṇyam syāt ā iti ucyate vikāra pravilayaḥ hi evam prakṛti sāmādhikaraṇyāt syāt tatas ca pratīka abhāva prasaṅgam avocāma paramātma vākyam ca idam syāt tatas ca upāsa adhikāraḥ bādhyeta ca vyartham tasmāt ityādi vat ityādi vat ca vyartham tasmāt sati kva kiṃdṛṣṭiḥ adhyasyatām iti saṃśayaḥ tatra aiyamaḥ iyama kāriṇaḥ śāstrasya abhāvāt iti evam prāptam athavā āditya ādi dṛṣṭayaḥ eva brahmaṇi kartavyāḥ iti evam prāptam evam hi āditya ādi dṛṣṭibhiḥ brahma upāsitam bhavati brahma upāsaam ca phalavat iti śāstra maryādā tasmāt a brahma dṛṣṭiḥ āditya ādiṣu iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ brahma dṛṣṭiḥ eva āditya ādiṣu syāt iti kasmāt utkarṣāt evam utkarṣeṇa āditya ādayaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ bhavati utkṛṣṭa dṛṣṭeḥ teṣu adhyāsāt tathā ca laukikaḥ yāyougataḥ bhavati utkṛṣṭa dṛṣṭiḥ hi laukikaḥ yāyaḥ yathā rāja dṛṣṭiḥ kṣattari sa ca viparyaye pratyavāya prasaṅgāt asitavyaḥ hi kṣattṛ dṛṣṭi parigṛhītaḥ rājā śreyase syāt śāstra prāmāṇyāt pratyavāya prasaṅgaḥ ca śāstra arthe etat evam syāt saṃdigdhe tu prati laukikaḥ api virudhyate ca utkṛṣṭa dṛṣṭi adhyāse śāstra artha avadhāryamāṇe śliṣyate prāthamyāt ca āditya ādi śabdāām mukhya artha tvam avirodhāt grahītavyam taiḥ sva artha vṛttibhiḥ avaruddhāyām buddhau paścāt avatarataḥ brahma śabdasya mukhyayā vṛttyā sāmāādhikaraṇya asaṃbhavāt brahma dṛṣṭi vidhā artha tā eva avatiṣṭhate iti para tvāt api brahma śabdasya eṣaḥ eva arthaḥ yāyyaḥ tathā hi brahma iti ādeśaḥ brahma iti upāsīta brahma iti upāste iti ca sarvatra iti param brahma śabdam uccārayati śuddhān tu āditya ādi śabdā tatas ca yathā śuktikām rajatam iti pratyeti iti atra eva śuktikā śabdaḥ rajata śabdaḥ tu rajata pratīti lakṣaṇa arthaḥ pratyeti eva hi kevalam rajatam iti tu tatra rajatam asti evam atra api āditya ādī brahma iti pratīyāt iti gamyate vākyaśeṣaḥ upi ca upāsti kriyayā sa yaḥ etat evam vidvāḥ ādityam brahma iti upāste yaḥ vācam brahma iti upāste yaḥ saṃkalpam brahma iti upāste iti ca yat tu uktam brahma upāsaam eva atra ādaraṇīyam phalavat tvāya iti tat ayuktam āditya ādīām eva upāsya tva avagamāt phalam tu atithi ādi upāsaaḥ iva brahmā eva dāsyati sarva adhyakṣa tvāt varṇitam ca etat phalam atas upapatteḥ iti atra īdṛśam ca atra brahmaṇaḥ upāsya tvam yat pratīkeṣu tad dṛṣṭi adhyāropaṇam pratimā ādiṣu iva viṣṇu ādīnām āditya ādi matayaḥ ca aṅge upapatteḥ āditya ādi mati adhikaraṇam yaḥ eva asau tapati tam udgītham upāsīta lokeṣu pañcavidham sāma upāsīta vāci saptavidham sāma upāsīta iyam eva ṛgagiḥ sāmaḥ iti evamādiṣu aṅga avabaddheṣu upāsa eṣu saṃśayaḥ kim āditya ādiṣu udgītha ādi dṛṣṭayaḥ vidhīyate kim vā udgītha ādiṣu eva āditya ādi dṛṣṭayaḥ iti tatra aiyamaḥ iyam akāraṇa abhāvāt iti prāptam a hi atra brahmaṇaḥ iva kasyacid utkarṣa viśeṣaḥ avadhāryate brahma hi samasta jagat kāraṇatvāt apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇa yogāt ca āditya ādibhyaḥ utkṛṣṭam iti śakyam avadhārayitum a tu āditya udgītha ādīām vikāra tva aviśeṣāt kiṃcid utkarṣa viśeṣa avadhāraṇe kāraṇam asti athavā udgītha ādi matayaḥ āditya ādiṣu adhyasyera kasmāt karma ātmaka tvāt udgītha ādīām karmaṇaḥ ca phala prāpti prasiddheḥ āditya ādayaḥ karma ātmakāḥ sataḥ phala hetavaḥ bhaviṣyati tathā ca iyam eva ṛgagiḥ sāma iti atra tat etat etasyām ṛci adhyūḍham sāma iti ṛc śabde pṛthivīm sāma śabde āgim tat ca pṛthivī agyoḥ ṛk sāma dṛṣṭi cikīrṣāyām avakalpate a ṛk sāmayoḥ pṛthivī agi dṛṣṭi cikīrṣāyām kṣattari hi rāja dṛṣṭi karaṇāt rāja śabdaḥ upacaryate a kṣattṛ śabdaḥ api ca lokeṣu pañcavidham sāma upāsīta iti adhikaraṇaiḥ deśāt lokeṣu sāma adhyasitavyam iti pratīyate etat gāyatram prāṇeṣu protam iti ca etat eva darśayati prathamaiḥ diṣṭeṣu ca āditya ādiṣu caramaiḥ diṣṭam brahma adhyastam ādityaḥ brahma iti ādeśaḥ ityādiṣu prathamaiḥ diṣṭāḥ ca pṛthivī ādayaḥ caramaiḥ diṣṭāḥ hiṃkāra ādayaḥ pṛthivī hiṃkāraḥ ityādi śrutiṣu atas a aṅgeṣu āditya ādiṣu aṅgam atikṣepaḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ āditya ādi matayaḥ eva aṅgeṣu udgītha ādiṣu kṣipyera kutas upapatteḥ upapadyate hi evam apūrva saṃikarṣāt āditya ādi matibhiḥ saṃskriyamāṇeṣu udgītha ādiṣu karma samṛddhiḥ yat eva vidyayā karoti śraddhayā upaiṣadā tat eva vīryavattaram bhavati iti ca vidyāyāḥ karma samṛddhi hetu tvam darśayati bhavatu karma samṛddhi phaleṣu evam svatatra phaleṣu tu katham yaḥ etat evam vidvān lokeṣu pañcavidham sāma upāste ityādiṣu teṣu api adhikṛta adhikārāt prakṛta apūrva saṃikarṣeṇa eva phala kalpaāḥ yuktāḥ godoha ādi iyama vat phala ātmaka tvāt ca udgītha ādibhyaḥ karma ātmakebhyaḥ utkarṣa upapattiḥ āditya ādi prāpti lakṣaṇam hi karma phalam śiṣyate śrutiṣu api ca om iti etat akṣaram udgītham upāsīta khalu etasya eva akṣarasya upavyākhyā bhavati iti ca udgītham eva upāsya tveā upakramya āditya ādi matīḥ vidadhāti yat tu uktam udgītha ādi matibhiḥ upāsyamānāḥ āditya ādayaḥ karma bhūyam bhūtvā phalam kariṣyati iti tat ayuktam svayam eva upāsaasya karma tvāt phalavat tva upapatteḥ āditya ādi bhāve api ca tat etat etasyām ṛci adhyūḍham sāma iti tu lākṣaṇikaḥ eva ṛk sāma śabda prayogaḥ lakṣaṇā ca yathāsaṃbhavam viprakṛṣṭe vā sva artha pravartate tatra yadi api ṛk sāmayoḥ pṛthivī agi dṛṣṭi cikīrṣā tathā api prasiddhayoḥ ṛk sāmayoḥ pṛthivī agi dṛṣṭi cikīrṣā tathā api prasiddhayoḥ ṛk sāmayoḥ pṛthivī agyoḥ ca saṃidhāāt tayoḥ eva eṣaḥ ṛk sāma śabda prayogaḥ ṛk sāma saṃbadhāt iti kṣattṛ śabdaḥ api hi kutaścid kāraṇāt rājāam upasarpe iva ārayitum pāryate iyam eva ṛc iti ca yathā akṣara yāsam ṛcaḥ eva pṛthivī tvam avadhārayati pṛthivyāḥ hi ṛc tu eva dhāryamāṇe iyam ṛc eva iti akṣara yāsaḥ syāt yat evam gāyati iti ca aṅga āśrayam upasaṃharati a pṛthivī ādi āśrayam tathā lokeṣu pañcavidham sāma upāsīta iti yadi api saptamīiḥ diṣṭāḥ lokāḥ tathā api sāmi eva te adhyasyera sāmaḥ upāsya tva avagamāt hi lokeṣu adhyasyamāeṣu sāma loka ātma upāsitam bhavati ayathā puas lokāḥ sāma ātma ā upāsitāḥ syuḥ ete etat gāyatram prāṇeṣu protam ityādi vyākhyātam yatra api tulyaḥ dvitīya airdeśaḥ atha khalu amum ādityam saptavidham sāma upāsīta iti tatra api samastasya khalu sāma tu pañcavidhasya atha saptavidhasya iti ca sāmaḥ eva upāsya tva upakramāt tasmin eva āditya ādi adhyāsaḥ etasmāt eva ca sāmaḥ upāsya tva avagamāt pṛthivī hiṃkāraḥ ityādi nirdeśa viparyaye pi hiṃkāra ādiṣu eva pṛthivī ādi dṛṣṭiḥ tasmāt a aṅga āśrayāḥ āditya ādi matayaḥ aṅgeṣu udgītha ādiṣu kṣipyera eti siddham sambhavāt āsīādhikaraṇam karma aṅga saṃbaddheṣu tāvat upāsaeṣu karma tatra tvāt samyagdarśae vastu tatra tvāt vijñāasya itareṣu tu upāsaeṣu kim tiṣṭha vā pravarteta uta eva iti citayati tatra aiyamaḥ śarīra sthiteḥ iti evam prāpte bravīti eva upāsīta iti kutas saṃbhavāt ca tat gacchataḥ dhāvataḥ vā saṃbhavati gati ādīām citta vikṣepa kara tvāt tiṣṭhataḥ api dehadhāraṇe vyāpṛtam bhavati akasmāt eva abhibhūyate tu evaṃjātīyakaḥ bhūyādoṣaḥ supariharaḥ iti saṃbhavati dhyā āt ca api ca dhyāyati arthaḥ eṣaḥ yat samāa pratyaya pravāha karaṇam dhyāyatiḥ ca praśithila aṅga ceṣṭeṣu pratiṣṭhita dṛṣṭiṣu eka viṣaya ākṣipta citteṣu upacaryamāṇaḥ dṛśyate dhyāyati bakaḥ dhyāyati proṣita badhuḥ iti ca bhavati tasmāt api acala tvam ca apekṣya api ca dhyāyati iva pṛthivī iti atra pṛthivī ādiṣu acalatvam eva apekṣya dhyāyativādaḥ bhavati tat ca liṅgam smarati ca smarati api ca śiṣṭāḥ śucau deśe pratiṣṭhāpya sthiram ityādiā atas eva atas eva upadeśaḥ yoga śāstre yatra ekāgra tā tatra aviśeṣāt ekāgra tā adhikaraṇam diś deśa kāleṣu saṃśayaḥ kim asti vā iti prāyeṇa vaidikeṣu ārambheṣu diś ādi iyama darśaāt syāt iha api kaścid iyamaḥ iti yasya matiḥ tam pratyāha diś deśa kāleṣu artha lakṣaṇaḥ eva iyamaḥ yatra eva asya diśi deśe kāle vā maasaḥ saukaryeṇa ekāgra tā bhavati tatra eva upāsīta prācī diś pūrvāhṇa prācī apravaṇa ādi vat viśeṣa aśravaṇāt ekāgra tāyāḥ iṣṭāyāḥ sarvatra aviśeṣāt viśeṣam api same śucau śarkarā vahi vālukā vivarjite śabda jala āśraya ādibhiḥ tu cakṣu pīḍae prayojayet iti yathā iti ucyate satyam asti evaṃjātīyakaḥ iyamaḥ sati tu etasmin tad gateṣu viśeṣeṣu aiyamaḥ iti suhṛd bhūtvā ācāryaḥ ācaṣṭe maoukūle iti ca eṣā śrutiḥ yatra ekāgra tā tatra eva eti etat eva darśayati āprāyaṇāt tatra api hi dṛṣṭam āprāyaṇa adhikaraṇam āvṛttiḥ sarva upāsaeṣu ādartavyā iti sthitam ādye adhikaraṇe tatra tāvat avaghāta ādi vat kārya paryavasāāi iti jñātam eva eṣām āvṛttiṃparimāṇam a hi samyak darśae kārye kiṃcid śāsitum śakyam aiyojya brahma ātmatva pratipatteḥ śāstrasya aviṣaya tvāt teṣu eṣā citā kim kiyataṃcid kālam pratyayam āvartya uparamet uta yāvajjīvam āvartayet iti kim tāvat prāptam kiyataṃcid kālam pratyayam abhyasya utsṛjet āvṛtti viśiṣṭasya upāsa a śabda arthasya kṛta tvāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ ā prāyaṇāt eva āvartayet pratyayam ati a pratyaya vaśāt adṛṣṭa phala prāpteḥ karmāṇi api hi phalam ārabhamāṇāi prāyaṇa kāle ākṣipati sa vijñāaḥ bhavati sa vijñāam eva avakrāmati prāṇam āyāti prāṇaḥ tejasā yuktaḥ saha ātmaā yathā saṃkalpitam lokam iti ca evamādi śrutibhyaḥ tṛṇa jalūkā ai darśaāt ca pratyayāḥ tu ete muktvā kim ayat prāyaṇa kāla bhāvi apekṣera tasmāt ye pratipattavya phala bhāva ātmakāḥ pratyayāḥ teṣu ā prāyaṇāt āvṛttiḥ tathā ca śrutiḥ sa yāvat kratuḥ ayam asmāt lokāt praiti iti prāyaṇa kāle api pratyaya āvṛttim darśayati smṛtiḥ api yam yam vā api smara bhāvam tyajatyate kalebaram tam tam eva eti kautaya sadā tad bhāva bhāvitaḥ iti prayāṇa kāle iti ca sota velāyām etat trayam pratipadyeta iti ca maraṇa velāyām api kartavya śeṣam śrāvayati tad adhigame uttara pūrva aghayoḥ aśleṣa viāśau tad vyapadeśāt tad adhigama adhikaraṇam gataḥ tṛtīya śeṣaḥ atha idāīm brahma vidyā phalam prati citā pratāyate brahma adhigame sati tad viparīta phalam duritam kṣīyate a kṣīyate vā iti saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam phala artha tvāt karmaṇaḥ phalam a dattvā a saṃbhāvyate kṣayaḥ phala dāyiī hi asya śaktiḥ śrutyā samadhigatā yadi tat atareṇa eva phala upabhogam apavṛjyeta śrutiḥ kadarthitā syāt smarati ca a hi karma kṣīyate iti sati prāyaścitta upadeśaḥ arthakaḥ ā eṣa doṣaḥ prāyaścittāām aimittika tva upapatteḥ gṛha dāha iṣṭi ādi vat api ca prāyaścittāām doṣa saṃyoge doṣa kṣapaṇa artha tā tu evam brahmavidyāyām brahma vidaḥ karma kṣaye tad phalasya avaśya bhoktavya tvāt brahma vidaḥ karma kṣaye tad phalasya avaśya bhoktavya tvāt syāt ucyate deśa kāla aimitta apekṣaḥ mokṣaḥ karma phala vat bhaviṣyati tasmāt a brahma adhigame iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ tad adhigame brahma adhigame sati uttara pūrvayoḥ aghayoḥ aśleṣa viāśau bhavataḥ uttarasya aśleṣaḥ pūrvasya viāśaḥ kasmāt tad vyapadeśāt tathā hi brahma vidyā prakriyāyām viduṣaḥ vyapadiśati yathā puṣkarapalāśe śliṣyate evam evaṃvidi pāpam karma śliṣyate iti tathā viāśam api pūrva upacitasya duritasya vyapadiśati tat yathā iṣīkā tūlam agau protam pradūyeta evam ha asya sarve pāpmā pradūyate iti ayam aparaḥ karma kṣaya vyapadeśaḥ bhavati bhidyate hṛdaya gradhiḥ chidyate sarva saṃśayāḥ kṣīyate ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare iti yat uktam aupabhukta phalasya karmaṇaḥ kṣaya kalpaāyām śāstram kadarthitam syāt iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ a hi vayam karmaṇaḥ phala dāyiīm śaktim avajāīmahe vidyate eva sā sā tu kāraṇa atareṇa pratibadhyate iti vadāmaḥ śakti sadbhāva mātre ca śāstram vyāpriyate a pratibadha a pratibadhayoḥ api a hi karma kṣīyate iti etat api smaraṇam autsargikam a hi bhogāt ṛte karma kṣīyate tad artha tvāt iti iṣyate eva tu tasya kṣayaḥ sarvam pāpmā tarati tarati brahmahatyām yaḥ uśvamedhea yajate yaḥ u ca evam veda ityādi śruti smṛtibhyaḥ yat tu uktam bhaviṣyati iti tat asat doṣa saṃyoge doṣaiḥ ghāta phala saṃbhave phala atara kalpa ā upapatteḥ yat puar etat uktam a prāyaścitta vat doṣa kṣaya uddeśe a vidyā vidhāam asti iti atra brūmaḥ saguṇāsu tāvat vidyāsu vidyate eva tāsu ca vākyaśeṣe aiśvarya prāptiḥ vidyāvataḥ ucyate tayoḥ ca avivakṣā kāraṇam āsti iti atas pāpma prahāṇa pūrvaka aiśvarya prāptiḥ tāsām phalam iti tu vidyāyām yadi api tathā api akartṛ ātmatva bodhāt karma pradāha siddhiḥ aśleṣaḥ iti ca āgāmiṣu karmasu kartṛ tvam eva a pratipadyate brahma vid iti darśayati atikrāteṣu tu yadi api mithyājñāāt kartṛ tvam pratipede iva tathā api vidyā sāmarthya a mithyājñā ai vṛtteḥ pravilīyate iti āha viāśaḥ iti pūrva siddha kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva viparītam hi triṣu api kāleṣu akartṛ tva abhoktṛ tva svarūpam brahma aham asmi etaḥ pūrvam api kartā bhoktā vā aham āsam bhaviṣyat kāle iti brahma vid avagacchati evam eva ca mokṣaḥ upapadyate ayathā hi a ādi kāla pravṛttāām karmaṇām kṣaya abhāve mokṣa abhāvaḥ syāt ca deśa kāla aimitta apekṣaḥ mokṣaḥ karma phala vat bhavitum arhati aitya tva prasaṅgāt parokṣa tva aupapatteḥ ca jñā a phalasya tasmāt brahma adhigame durita kṣayaḥ iti sthitam itarasya api evam asaṃśleṣaḥ pāte tu itara asaṃśleṣa adhikaraṇam pūrvasmin adhikaraṇe badha hetoḥ aghasya svābhāvikasya aśleṣa viāśau jñā aimittau śāstra vyapadeśa airūpitau dharmasya puaḥ śāstrīya tvāt śāstrīyeṇa avirodhaḥ iti āśaṅkya taiḥ ākaraṇāya pūrva adhikaraṇayāya atideśaḥ kriyate itarasya api puṇyasya karmaṇaḥ evam agha vat asaṃśleṣaḥ viāśaḥ ca bhavataḥ kutas tasya api sva phala hetu tveai jñā a phala pratibadhi tva prasaṅgāt ubhe u ha eva eṣa ete tarati ityādi śrutiṣu ca duṣkṛta vat sukṛtasya api praṇāśa vyapadeśāt akartṛ ātmatva bodha aimittasya ca karma kṣayasya sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ tulya tvāt kṣīyate ca asya karmāṇi iti ca aviśeṣa śruteḥ yatra api kevalaḥ eva pāpma śabdaḥ paṭhyate tatra api puṇyam api ākalitam iti draṣṭavyam jñā āpekṣayā ikṛṣṭa phala tvāt asti ca śrutau puṇye api pāpma śabdaḥ setum ahar rātre tarataḥ iti atra saha sukṛtam api aukramya sarve iti aviśeṣeṇa eva prakṛte puṇye pāpma śabda prayogāt pāte tu iti tuśabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ evam dharma adharmayoḥ badha hetvoḥ vidyā sāmarthyāt aśleṣa viāśa siddheḥ viduṣaḥ śarīrapāte muktiḥ iti avadhārayati aārabdha kārye eva tu pūrve tad avadheḥ aārabdha adhikaraṇam pūrvayoḥ adhikaraṇayoḥ sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ sa kim aviśeṣeṇa ārabdha kāryayoḥ aārabdha kāryayoḥ ca bhavati uta viśeṣeṇa aārabdha kāryayoḥ eva iti vicāryate tatra ubhe u ha eva eṣa ete tarati iti evamādi śrutiṣu aviśeṣa śravaṇāt aviśeṣeṇa eva kṣayaḥ iti evam prāpte pratyāha aārabdha kārye eva tu iti apravṛtta phale eva pūrve asmi api ca prāk jñā utpatteḥ saṃcite sukṛta duṣkṛte jñā adhigamāt kṣīyete a tu ārabdha kārye sāmi bhukta phale yābhyām etat kutas etat tasya tāvat eva ciram a vimokṣye saṃpatsye iti śarīrapātau adhikaraṇāt kṣema prāpteḥ itarathā hi jñāāt aśeṣa karma kṣaye sati sthiti hetu abhāvāt eva kṣemam tatra śarīrapāta pratīkṣām ācakṣīta ayam akartṛ ātma avabodhaḥ karmāṇi kṣapaya katham kāicid kṣapayet kāicid ca upekṣeta a tāvat a āśritya ārabdha kāryam karma āśayam jñā utpattiḥ upapadyate āśrite ca tasmin kulāla cakra vat pravṛtta vegasya a tarāle pratibadha asaṃbhavāt bhavati vega kṣaya pratipālaam hi bādhitam api tu mithyājñāam eva api ca vivaditavyam brahma vidā kaṃcid kālam śarīram dhriyate a vā dhriyate iti katham hi ekasya sva hṛdaya pratyayam dehadhāraṇam ca apareṇa pratikṣeptum śakyeta śruti smṛtiṣu ca etat eva tasmāt a ārabdha kāryayoḥ eva sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ vidyā sāmarthyāt kṣayaḥ iti agihotra ādi tu tad kāryāya eva tad darśaāt agihotra ādi adhikaraṇam sa utideśaḥ sarva puṇya viṣayaḥ iti āśaṅkya prativakti agihotra ādi tu iti tuśabdaḥ āśaṅkām apaudati yaityam karma vaidikam agihotra ādi tat tad kāryāya eva bhavati yat kāryam tat eva asya api kāryam iti arthaḥ kutas tam etam brāhmaṇāḥ vividiṣati ityādi darśaāt au jñā a karmaṇoḥ vilakṣaṇa kārya tvāt kārya ekatva aupapattiḥ ā eṣa doṣaḥ jvara maraṇa kāryayoḥ api dadhi viṣayoḥ guḍa matra saṃyuktayoḥ tṛpti puṣṭi kārya darśaāt tadvat karmaṇaḥ api jñā a saṃyuktasya mokṣa kārya upapatteḥ au a ārabhyaḥ mokṣaḥ katham asya karma kārya tvam ucyate ā eṣa doṣaḥ ārāt upakāraka tvāt karmaṇaḥ jñāasya eva hi prāpakam sat karma praṇāḍyā mokṣa kāraṇam iti upacaryate atas eva ca atikrāta viṣayam etat kārya ekatva abhidhāam hi brahma vidaḥ āgāmi a gihotra ādi saṃbhavati aiyojya brahma ātmatva pratipatteḥ śāstrasya aviṣaya tvāt saguṇāsu tu vidyāsu kartṛ tvā ativṛtteḥ saṃbhavati āgāmi api tasya api kārya atara abhāvāt vidyā saṃgati upapattiḥ kiṃviṣayam kiṃviṣayam vā adaḥ tasyāḥ eṣa viiyogaḥ uktaḥ ekeṣām suhṛdaḥ sādhu kṛtyām upayati iti tasyāḥ eva ca idam itarasya api evam asaṃśleṣaḥ iti tathā jātīyakasya kāmyasya karmaṇaḥ vidyām prati aupakāraka tve saṃpratipattiḥ ubhayoḥ api jaimii bādarāyaṇayoḥ ācāryayoḥ yat eva vidyayā iti hi vidyā jñā asādhaatva adhikaraṇam samadhigatam etat aatara adhikaraṇe karma mumukṣuṇā kṛtam upātta durita kṣaya hetu dvāreṇa sattva śuddhi kāraṇatām pratipadyamāam brahma vidyayā saha eka kāryam bhavati iti tatra agihotra ādi karma aṅga vyapāśraya vidyā saṃyuktam kevalam ca asti yaḥ evam vidvā yajati yaḥ evam vidvān juhoti yaḥ evam vidvān śaṃsati yaḥ evam vidvān gāyati tasmāt evaṃvidam eva brahmāṇam kurvīta te ubhau kurutaḥ yaḥ ca etat evam veda yaḥ ca a veda ityādi vacaebhyaḥ vidyā saṃyuktam asti kevalam api asti tatra idam vicāryate kim vidyā saṃyuktam eva a gihotra ādikam karma mumukṣoḥ vidyā hetutvā tayā saha eka kāryatvam pratipadyate a kevalam uta vidyā saṃyuktam kevalam ca aviśeṣeṇa iti kutas saṃśayaḥ tam etam ātmā yajñe vividiṣati iti śravaṇāt vidyā saṃyuktasya ca a gihotra ādeḥ viśiṣṭa tva avagamāt kim tāvat prāptam vidyā saṃyuktam eva karma agihotra ādi ātma vidyā śeṣa tvam pratipadyate vidyā upetasya viśiṣṭa tva avagamāt vidyā vihīāt yat ahar eva juhoti tat ahar puar mṛtyum apajayati evam vidvāḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ buddhyā yuktaḥ yayā pārtha karma badham prahāsyasi dūreṇa hi avaram karma buddhi yogāt haaṃjayaḥ ityādi smṛtibhyaḥ ca iti evam prāpte pratipādyate yat eva vidyayā iti hi satyam etat vidyā saṃyuktam karma agihotra ādikam vidyā vihīāt karmaṇaḥ gihotrāt viśiṣṭam vidvāḥ iva brāhmaṇaḥ vidyā vihīāt brāhmaṇāt tathā api vidyā vihīam karma agihotra ādikam kasmāt tam etam ātmāam yajñe vividiṣati iti aviśeṣeṇa agihotra ādeḥ vidyā hetu tve śruta tvāt vidyā saṃyuktasya agihotra ādeḥ viśiṣṭa tva avagamāt vidyā vihīam agihotra ādi ātma vidyā hetu tve aapekṣam eva iti yuktam yogāt ātma jñāam prati kaścid kāraṇatva atiśayaḥ bhaviṣyati a tathā vidyā vihīasya iti yuktam kalpayitum a tu vividiṣati iti atra aviśeṣeṇa ātma jñā aṅgatve śrutasya āgihotra ādeḥ śrutasya āgihotra ādeḥ a aṅgatvam śakyam abhyupagatum tathā hi śrutiḥ yat eva vidyayā karoti śraddhayā upaiṣadā tat eva vīryavattaram bhavati iti vidyā saṃyuktasya sva kāryam prati kaṃcid atiśayam bruvāṇāḥ tasya eva tad prayojaam prati vīryavat tvam darśayati karmaṇaḥ ca vīryavat tvam tat yat sva prayojaa sādha asahatvam tasmāt vidyā saṃyuktam ca ubhayam api mumukṣuṇā mokṣa prayojaa uddeśea iha ca prāk jñā utpatteḥ kṛtam tat yathā sāmarthyam brahma adhigama pratibadha kāraṇa upātta durita kṣaya hetutva dvāreṇa brahma adhigama kāraṇa tvam pratipadyamāam śravaṇa maaa śraddhā tātparya ādya taraṅga kāraṇa apekṣam brahma vidyayā saha eka kāryam bhavati iti sthitam tu itare kṣapayitvā sampadyate itara kṣapaṇa adhikaraṇam a ārabdha kāryayoḥ puṇya pāpayoḥ vidyā sāmarthyāt kṣaya adhikaraṇam a ārabdha kāryayoḥ puṇya pāpayoḥ vidyā sāmarth uktaḥ itare tu ārabdha kārye puṇya pāpe upabhoge kṣapayitvā brahma saṃpadyate tasya tāvat eva ciram yāvat saṃpatsye iti brahma eva sa brahmā apyeti iti ca evamādi śrutibhyaḥ sati api samyagdarśae yathā prāk dehapātāt bheda darśaam evam paścāt api uu varteta a imitta ābhavāt upabhoga śeṣa kṣapaṇam hi tatra au vṛtti imittam ca tādṛśam atra kiṃcid asti aparaḥ tasya dagdha bīja tvāt mithyājñā a avaṣṭambham hi karma ātaram dehapātaḥ upabhoga ātaram ārabheta tat ca mithyājñāam dagdham iti atas sādhu etat ārabdha kārya kṣaye viduṣaḥ kaivalyam avaśyam bhavati iti iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara asya somya asya somya asya somya asya somya asya somya asya somya asya somya asya somya asya somya asya somya asya somya asya somya asya somya asya somya puruṣasya prayataḥ vāc maasi saṃpadyate maaḥ prāṇe prāṇaḥ tejasi tejaḥ parasyām devatāyām iti kim iha vācaḥ eva vṛttimattyāḥ maasi saṃpattiḥ ucyate uta vāc vṛtteḥ iti viśayaḥ tatra vāc eva tāvat maasi saṃpadyate iti prāptam tathā hi śrutiḥ augṛhītā bhavati itarathā lakṣaṇā syāt śruti lakṣaṇā viśaye ca śrutiḥ yāyyā a lakṣaṇā tasmāt vācaḥ eva ayam maasi pralayaḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ vāc vṛttiḥ maasi saṃpadyate iti katham vāc vṛttiḥ iti vyākhyāyate yāvatā vāc maasi iti eva ācāryaḥ paṭhati satyam etat paṭhiṣyati tu parastāt avibhāgaḥ iti tasmāt atra vṛtti upaśama mātram vivakṣati iti gamyate tattva pralaya vivakṣāyām tu sarvatra eva avibhāga sāmyāt kim paratra eva viśiṃṣyāt avibhāgaḥ iti tasmāt atra vṛtti upasaṃhāra vivakṣā vāc vṛttiḥ pūrvam upasaṃhriyate mao vṛttau avasthitāyām iti arthaḥ kasmāt darśaāt dṛśyate hi vāc vṛtteḥ pūrva upasaṃhāraḥ mao vṛttau vidyamāāyām a tu vācaḥ eva vṛttimattyā maasi upasaṃhāraḥ keacid api draṣṭum śakyate śruti sāmarthyāt vācaḥ eva ayam maasi apyayaḥ yuktaḥ iti uktam etya āha a tad prakṛti tvāt yasya hi yatas utpattiḥ tasya tatra pralayaḥ yāyyaḥ mṛdi iva śarāvasya ca vāc utpadyate iti kiṃca a pramāṇam asti vṛtti udbhava abhibhavau tu a prakṛti samāśrayau api dṛśyete pārthivebhyaḥ hi taijasasya ageḥ vṛttiḥ udbhavati apsu ca upaśāmyati katham tarhi asmipakṣe śabdaḥ vāc maasi saṃpadyate iti atas āha śabdāt ca iti vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ abheda upacārāt iti arthaḥ atas eva ca tasmāt upaśāta tejāḥ iti atra aviśeṣeṇa sarveṣām eva idriyāṇām maasi saṃpattiḥ śrūyate tatra api atas eva vācaḥ iva cakṣuḥ ādīām api sa vṛttike maasi avasthite vṛtti lopa darśaāt tattva pralaya asaṃbhavāt śabda upapatteḥ ca vṛtti dvāreṇa eva sarvāṇi idriyāṇi sarveṣām karaṇāām sati vācaḥ pṛthak grahaṇam vāc maasi saṃpadyate iti udāharaṇa prāṇa uttarāt samadhigatam etat vāc maasi saṃpadyate iti atra vṛtti saṃpatti vivakṣā iti atha yat uttaram vākyam maasi prāṇe iti kim atra api vṛtti saṃpattiḥ eva vivakṣyate uta vṛttimat saṃpattiḥ iti vicikitsāyām vṛttimat saṃpattiḥ eva atra iti prāptam śruti augrahāt tad prakṛti tva upapatteḥ ca tathā hi aamayam hi somya maa āpaḥ mayaḥ prāṇaḥ iti ca prāṇam āpaḥ ca amasṛjata iti śrutiḥ atas ca yam aaḥ prāṇe pralīyate aam eva tat apsu pralīyate aam hi āpaḥ ca prāṇaḥ prakṛti vikāra abhedāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ tat api āgṛhīta bāhya idriya vṛtti vṛtti dvāreṇa eva prāṇe pralīyate iti uttarāt vākyāt avagatavyam tathā hi suṣupsoḥ mumūrṣoḥ ca prāṇa vṛttau parispada ātmikāyām avasthitāyām dṛśyate ca maasaḥ svarūpa apyayaḥ prāṇe saṃbhavati a tad prakṛti tvāt darśitam maasaḥ prāṇa prakṛti tvam hi hi tad prakṛti tve maaḥ prāṇe saṃpattum arhati evam api hi ae maaḥ saṃpadyeta apsu ca aam apsu eva ca prāṇaḥ hi etasmin api pakṣe prāṇa bhāva pariṇatābhyaḥ udbhyaḥ maaḥ jāyate iti kiṃca a pramāṇam asti tasmāt prāṇe svarūpa apyayaḥ vṛtti apyaye pi tu śabdaḥ uvakalpate vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ abheda upacārāt iti darśitam saḥ udhyakṣe tad upagama ādibhyaḥ adhyakṣa adhikaraṇam sthitam etat yasya yatas otpattiḥ tasya a svarūpa pralayaḥ a svarūpa pralayaḥ iti idam idāīm prāṇaḥ tejasi iti atra cityate kim yathāśruti prāṇasya tejasi eva vṛtti upasaṃhāraḥ kim vā deha idriya pañjara adhyakṣe jīve iti tatra śruteḥ a atiśaṅkya tvāt prāṇasya tejasi eva saṃpattiḥ syāt a śruta kalpa āyāḥ ayāyya tvāt iti evam prāpte pratipadyate saḥ udhyakṣaḥ iti sa prakṛtaḥ prāṇaḥ adhyakṣe avidyā karma pūrva prajñā upādhike vijñā ātmaiḥ avatiṣṭhate tad pradhāā prāṇa vṛttiḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ kutas tad upagama ādibhyaḥ evam eva imam ātmā amata kāle sarve prāṇāḥ yatra etat ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva
