ūrdhva ūrdhva ū iti pañca vṛtteḥ prāṇasya adhyakṣa augāmi tām darśayati ca itareṣām sarve prāṇāḥ aūtkrāmati iti bhavati iti ca adhyakṣasya tasmin apīta karaṇa grāmasya prāṇasya avasthāam gamayati prāṇaḥ tejasi iti śrūyate katham prāṇa udhyakṣe iti adhika āvāpaḥ kriyate ā eṣa doṣaḥ adhyakṣa pradhā a tvāt utkramaṇa ādi vyavahārasya śruti atara gatasya api ca viśeṣasya apekṣaṇīya tvāt katham tarhi prāṇaḥ tejasi iti śrutiḥ iti atas āha bhūteṣu tad śruteḥ sa prāṇa saṃpṛkta adhyakṣaḥ tejaḥ sahacariteṣu bhūteṣu deha bīja bhūteṣu sūkṣmeṣu avatiṣṭhate iti avagatavyam prāṇaḥ tejasi iti śruteḥ ca iyam śrutiḥ prāṇasya tejasi sthitim darśayati a prāṇa saṃpṛktasya adhyakṣasya ā eṣa doṣaḥ saḥ adhyakṣe iti adhyakṣasya api atarāle upasaṃkhyāta tvāt yaḥ api hi srughāmathurām gatvā mathurāyāḥ pāṭaliputram vrajati saḥ upi srughāt pāṭaliputram yāti iti śakyate vaditum tasmāt prāṇaḥ tejasi iti prāṇa saṃpṛktasya adhyakṣasya eva etat tejaḥ sahacariteṣu bhūteṣu katham tejaḥ sahacariteṣu bhūteṣu iti ucyate yāvatā ekam eva tejaḥ śrūyate prāṇaḥ tejasi iti atas āha hi hi ekasmin eva tejasi śarīra atara prepsā velāyām jīvaḥ vatiṣṭhate kāryasya śarīrasya a eka ātmaka tva darśaāt darśayataḥ ca etam artham āpaḥ puruṣa vacasaḥ iti tat vyākhyātam tri ātmaka tvāt tu bhūyaḥ tvāt iti atra śruti smṛtī ca etam artham darśayataḥ śrutiḥ pṛthvī mayaḥ āpaḥ mayaḥ vāyu mayaḥ ākāśa mayaḥ tejaḥ mayaḥ ityādyā smṛtiḥ api aṇvyaḥ tu yāḥ smṛtāḥ tābhiḥ sārdham idam sarvam saṃbhavati aupūrvaśas ityādyāḥ ca upasaṃhṛteṣu vāc ādiṣu karaṇeṣu śarīra atara prepsā velāyām kva ayam tadā puruṣaḥ bhavati iti upakramya śrutyataram karma āśraya tām tau ha yat ūcatuḥ karma ha eva tat ūcatuḥ atha ha yat praśaśaṃsatuḥ karma ha eva tat praśaśaṃsatuḥ iti atra ucyate tatra karma prayuktasya grahātigraha saṃjñakasya idriya viṣaya ātmakasya pravṛttiḥ iti karma āśraya tā uktā iha puaḥ deha atara utpattiḥ iti bhūta āśraya tvam uktam praśaṃsā śabdāt api tatra prādhāya mātram karmaṇaḥ pradarśitam a tu tasmāt avirodhaḥ samāā ca āsṛti upakramāt amṛta tvam ca a upoṣyaḥ āsṛti upakrama adhikaraṇam sā iyam utkrātiḥ kim vidvat aviduṣoḥ kim vā viśeṣavatī iti viśayāām viśeṣavatī iti tāvat prāptam bhūta āśraya viśiṣṭā hi eṣā puarbhavāya ca bhūtāya āśrīyate a ca viduṣaḥ puarbhavaḥ saṃbhavati amṛta tvam hi iti sthitiḥ tasmāt aviduṣaḥ eva eṣā utkrātiḥ vidyā prakaraṇe viduṣaḥ eva eṣā bhavet a svāpa ādi vat yathāprāpta āukīrtaāt yathā hi yatra etat puruṣaḥ svapiti āma aśiśiṣati āma pipāsati iti ca sarva prāṇi sādhāraṇā eva vidyā prakaraṇe pi tu viduṣaḥ viśeṣavataḥ vidhitsyate evam iyam api utkrātiḥ yasyām parasyām devatāyām puruṣasya prayataḥ tejaḥ saṃpadyate saḥ ātmā tattvam asi iti etat pratipādayitum pratiṣiddhā ca eṣā viduṣaḥ a tasya prāṇā utkrāmati iti tasmāt a viduṣaḥ eva eṣā iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ samāā ca eṣā utkrātiḥ vāc maasi ityādyā vidvat aviduṣoḥ āsṛti upakramāt bhavitum arhati aviśeṣa śravaṇāt avidvāḥ bhūta sūkṣmāṇi āśritya karma prayuktaḥ deha grahaṇa maubhava saṃsarati vidvān tu mokṣa āḍī dvāram āśrayate tat etat ā sṛti upakramāt iti uktam au amṛta tvam viduṣā prāptavyam ca tad deśa atara āyattam tatra kutas bhūta āśraya tvam sṛti upakramaḥ vā iti atra ucyate ca idam a dagdhvā atyatam avidyā ādi kleśāḥ apara vidyā sāmarthyāt āpekṣikam amṛta tvam prepsate saṃbhavati tatra sṛti upakramaḥ bhūta āśraya tvam ca gatiḥ upapadyate tasmāt adoṣaḥ tadā apīteḥ saṃsāra vyapadeśāt saṃsāra vyapadeśa adhikaraṇam tejaḥ parasyām devatāyām iti atra prakaraṇa sāmarthyāt tat yathā prakṛtam tejaḥ sa adhyakṣam sa prāṇam sa karaṇa grāmam bhūta atara sahitam prayataḥ puṃsaḥ parasyām devatāyām saṃpadyate iti etat uktam bhavati kīdṛśī puar iyam saṃpattiḥ syāt iti cityate tatra ātyatikaḥ eva tāvat sva rūpa pravilayaḥ iti prāptam tad prakṛti tva upapatteḥ sarvasya hi jaimataḥ vastu jātasya prakṛtiḥ parā devatā iti pratiṣṭhāpitam tasmāt ātyatikī iyam avibhāga āpattiḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ tat tejaḥ ādi bhūta sūkṣmam śrotra ādi karaṇa āśraya bhūtam āpīteḥ ā saṃsāra mokṣāt samyagjñā aimittāt avatiṣṭhate prapadyate śarīra tvāya yathākarma yathāśrutam ityādi saṃsāra vyapadeśāt ayathā hi sarvaḥ prāyaṇa samaye eva upādhi prati astamayāt atyatam brahma saṃpadyeta tatra vidhi śāstram aarthakam syāt vidyā śāstram ca mithyājñā aimittaḥ ca samyagjñā ādṛte visraṃsitum arhati tasmāt tat prakṛti tve pi suṣupti pralaya vat bīja bhāva avaśeṣā eva eṣā sat saṃpattiḥ iti sūkṣmam pramāṇataḥ ca tathā upalabdheḥ tat ca itara bhūta sahitam tejaḥ jīvasya asmāt śarīrāt pravasataḥ āśraya bhūtam svarūpataḥ parimāṇataḥ ca sūkṣmam bhavitum arhati tathā hi āḍīiṣkramaṇa śravaṇa ādibhyaḥ saukṣmyam upalabhyate tatra tautvāt saṃcāra upapattiḥ svaccha tvāt ca apratighāta upapattiḥ atas eva ca pārśva sthaiḥ upalabhyate atas eva ca sūkṣma tvāt atas eva ca sūkṣma tvāt sthūlasya śarīrasya upamarde dāha ādi nimitte itarat sūkṣmam śarīram upamṛdyate asya eva ca upapatteḥ eṣaḥ ūṣmā asya eva ca sūkṣmasya śarīrasya eṣaḥ ūṣmā yam etasmin jīvat śarīre saṃsparśe ūṣmāṇam tathā hi mṛta avasthāyām avasthite pi dehe vidyamāeṣu api ca rūpa ādiṣu deha guṇeṣu a ūṣmā upalabhyate jīvat avasthāyām eva tu upalabhyate iti atas upapadyate prasiddha śarīra vyatirikta vyapāśrayaḥ eva eṣaḥ ūṣmā iti tathā ca śrutiḥ uṣṇaḥ eva jīviṣyan śītaḥ mariṣye iti pratiṣedhāt iti śārīrāt pratiṣedha adhikaraṇam amṛta tvam ca a upoṣyaḥ iti atas viśeṣaṇāt ātyatika imṛtatve gati utkrātyoḥ abhāvaḥ abhyupagataḥ tatra api utkrātim āśaṅkya pratiṣedhati yokāmaḥ iṣkāmaḥ āpta kāmaḥ ātma kāmaḥ bhavati a tasya prāṇāḥ utkrāmati brahma eva sa brahma apyeti iti atas para vidyā viṣayāt pratiṣedhāt a para brahma vidaḥ dehāt prāṇānām utkrātiḥ asti iti ced ā iti ucyate yatas śārīrāt ātmā eṣaḥ utkrāti pratiṣedhaḥ prāṇāām a śarīrāt katham avagamyate a tasmāt prāṇāḥ utkrāmati iti śākhātare pañcamī prayogāt hi ṣaṣṭhī śākhātara gatayā pañcamyā vyavasthāpyate tasmāt iti ca prādhāyāt abhyudaya aiḥśreyasa adhikṛtaḥ dehī saṃbadhyate a dehaḥ a tasmāt uccikramiṣoḥ jīvāt prāṇāḥ apakrāmati saha eva te bhavati iti arthaḥ sa prāṇasya ca pravasataḥ bhavati utkrātiḥ dehāt iti evam prāpte pratyucyate spaṣṭaḥ hi ekeṣām yat uktam para brahma vidaḥ api dehāt asti utkrātiḥ utkrāti pratiṣedhasya dehi a pādāa tvāt iti yatas deha apādāaḥ eva utkrāti pratiṣedhaḥ ekeṣām spaṣṭaḥ upalabhyate tathā hi ārtabhāgapraśe yatra ayam puruṣaḥ mriyate ud asmāt prāṇāḥ krāmati āho eti iti atra ā iti ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ iti autkrāti pakṣam parigṛhya tarhi ayam autkrāteṣu prāṇeṣu mṛtaḥ iti asyām āśaṅkāyām atra eva samavaīyate iti pravilayam pratijñāya tad siddhaye saḥ ucchvayati ādhmāyati ādhmātaḥ mṛtaḥ śete iti sa śabda parāmṛṣṭasya prakṛtasya dehasya ca syuḥ tad sāmāyāt tasmāt prāṇāḥ utkrāmati atra eva samavaīyate iti atra api abheda upacāreṇa utkramaṇasya pratiṣedhaḥ yadi api iti vyākhyeyam yeṣām pañcamī pāṭhaḥ yeṣām tu ṣaṣṭhī pāṭhaḥ teṣām utkrātiḥ pratiṣidhyate iti prāpta utkrāti pratiṣedha artha tvāt asya vākyasya sā pratiṣiddhā bhavati dehāt utkrātiḥ prāptā api ca cakṣuṣṭas vā mūrdhaḥ vāyebhyaḥ vā śarīra deśebhyaḥ tam utkrāmatam prāṇaḥ u utkrāmati prāṇam a utkrāmatam sarve prāṇāḥ a utkrāmati iti evam avidvat viṣaye sa prapañcam utkramaṇam saṃsāra gamaam ca darśayitvā iti u iti upasaṃhṛtya avidvat kathām iti vyapadiśya vidvāṃsam yadi tad viṣaye pi utkrātim eva prāpayet asamañjasaḥ eva vyapadeśaḥ syāt tasmāt avidvat viṣaye prāptayoḥ gati utkrātyoḥ vidvat viṣaye pratiṣedhaḥ iti evam eva vyākhyeyam vyapadeśa arthavat tvāya as ca brahma vidaḥ sarvagata brahma ātma bhūtasya prakṣīṇa kāma karmaṇaḥ utkrātiḥ gatiḥ vā upapadyate imitta abhāvāt atra brahma iti ca evaṃjātīyakāḥ śrutayaḥ gati utkrātyoḥ abhāvam sūcayati smaryate ca smaryate api ca mahābhārate gati utkrātyoḥ abhāvaḥ sarva bhūta ātma bhūtasya samyak bhūtāi paśyataḥ devāḥ api mārge muhyati apadasya pada eṣiṇaḥ iti gatiḥ api brahma vidaḥ sarva gata brahma ātma bhūtasya smaryate śukaḥ kila vaiyāsakiḥ mumukṣuḥ āditya maṇḍalam abhipratasthe pitrā ca āugamya āhūtaḥ bho iti pratiśuśrāva iti a sa śarīrasya eva ayam viśiṣṭa deśa prāpti pūrvakaḥ śarīra utsargaḥ iti draṣṭavyam sarva bhūta dṛśya tva ādi upayāsāt a hi aśarīram gacchatam sarva bhūtāi draṣṭum śakuyuḥ tathā ca tatra eva upasaṃhṛtam śukaḥ tu mārutāt śīghrām gatim kṛtvā ātarikṣa gaḥ darśayitvā prabhāvam svam sarva bhūta gataḥ bhavat iti tasmāt abhāvaḥ para brahma vidaḥ gati utkrātyoḥ gati śrutīām tu viṣayam upariṣṭāt vyākhyāsyāmaḥ pare tathā vāc ādi laya adhikaraṇam tāi puaḥ prāṇa śabda uditāi idriyāṇi ca para brahma vidaḥ tasmin eva parasmin ātmai pralīyate kasmāt tathā hi āha śrutiḥ evam eva asya paridraṣṭuḥ imāḥ ṣoḍaśa kalāḥ puruṣāyaṇāḥ puruṣam prāpya astam gacchati iti gatāḥ kalāḥ pañcadaśa pratiṣṭhāḥ iti vidvat viṣayā eva aparā śrutiḥ sma sā khalu vyavahāra apekṣā pārthiva ādyāḥ kalāḥ pṛthivī ādīḥ eva sva prakṛtīḥ apiyati iti itarā tu vidvat pratipatti apekṣā kṛtsam kalā jātam para brahma vidaḥ brahma eva saṃpadyate iti tasmāt adoṣaḥ avibhāgaḥ vacaāt avibhāga adhikaraṇam sa puar viduṣaḥ kalā pralayaḥ kim itareṣām iva sa avaśeṣaḥ bhavati āhosvit avaśeṣaḥ iti tatra pralaya sāmāyāt śakti avaśeṣa tā prasaktau bravīti avibhāga āpattiḥ eva iti kutas vacaāt tathā hi kalā pralayam uktvā vakti bhidyete tāsām āma rūpe puruṣaḥ iti evam procyate saḥ eṣa ukalaḥ mṛtaḥ bhavati iti avidyā nimittāām ca a vidyā nimitte pralaye sa avaśeṣa tva upapattiḥ tasmāt avibhāgaḥ eva iti tad oka ugra jvalaam tad prakāśita dvāraḥ vidyā sāmarthyāt tad śeṣa gati ausmṛti yogāt ca śata adhikayā tad oka udhikaraṇam samāptā prāsaṅgikī para vidyā gatā citā saṃprati tu apara vidyā viṣayām eva citām auvartayati samāā ca ā sṛti upakramāt vidvat a viduṣoḥ utkrātiḥ iti uktam tam idāīm sṛti upakramam darśayati tasya upasaṃhṛta vāc ādi kalāpasya uccikramiṣataḥ vijñā ātmanaḥ okaḥ hṛdayam saḥ etāḥ tejaḥ mātrāḥ samabhyādadānaḥ hṛdayam eva avavakrāmati iti śruteḥ tad agra prajvala a pūrvikā cakṣuḥ ādi ca utkrātiḥ śrūyate tasya ha etasya hṛdayasya agram pradyotate ātmā iṣkrāmati cakṣuṣṭas vā mūrdhaḥ vāyebhyaḥ vā śarīra deśebhyaḥ iti sā vidvat aviduṣoḥ bhavati atha asti kaścid viduṣaḥ viśeṣa aiyamaḥ iti vicikitsāyām śruti aviśeṣāt aiyama prāptau ācaṣṭe hi vidvat aviduṣoḥ hṛdaya agra pradyotae tad prakāśita dvāra tve ca mūrdha sthāāt eva vidvāiṣkrāmati sthāātarebhyaḥ tu itare kutas vidyā sāmarthyāt yadi vidvā api itara vat yatas kutaścid deha deśāt utkrāmet ā eva utkṛṣṭam lokam labheta tatra aarthikā eva vidyā syāt vidyā śeṣa gatyā ausmṛti yogāt ca vidyā śeṣa bhūtā ca mūrdhayaāḍī saṃbaddhā gatiḥ auśīlayitavyā vidyā viśeṣeṣu vihitā tām abhyasya tayā eva pratiṣṭhate iti yuktam tasmāt brahmaṇā su upāsite augṛhītaḥ tad bhāvam vidvāḥ mūrdhayayā eva śata adhikayā śatāt atiriktayā ekaśatatamyā āḍyā iṣkrāmati itarābhiḥ itare tathā hi hārdavidyām prakṛtya śatam ca ekā ca hṛdayasya āḍyaḥ tāsām tayā ūrdhvamāya amṛta tvam eti viṣvaṅṅayā utkramaṇe bhavati iti raśmyausārī raśmi adhikaraṇam asti hārdavidyā atha yat idam asmin brahmapure daharam puṇḍarīkam veśma iti upakramya vihitā tad prakriyāyām atha yāḥ etāḥ hṛdayasya āḍyaḥ iti upakramya sa prapañcam uktam atha yatra etat asmāt śarīrāt utkrāmati atha etaiḥ eva raśmibhiḥ ūrdhvam ākramate iti tayā ūrdhvam āya amṛta tvam eti iti tasmāt śata adhikayā āḍyā iṣkrāma raśmī ausārī iṣkrāmati iti gamyate tat kim aviśeṣeṇa eva rātrau vā mriyamāṇasya raśmyausāri tvam āhosvit ahayā iva iti saṃśaye sati aviśeṣa śravaṇāt aviśeṣeṇa eva tāvat raśmyausārī iti pratijñāyate yāvaddehabhāvi tvāt darśayati ca asti ahai āḍīraśmisaṃbadha iti ahai mṛtasya syāt raśmyausāri tvam rātrau tu pretasya a syāt āḍīraśmisaṃbadhavicchedāt iti ced a āḍīraśmisaṃbadhasya yāvaddehabhāvi tvāt yāvaddehabhāvī hi śirā kiraṇa saṃparkaḥ darśayati ca etam artham śrutiḥ amuṣmāt ādityāt pratāyate tāḥ āsu āḍīṣu sṛptāḥ ābhyaḥ āḍībhyaḥ pratāyate tāḥ amuṣmin āditye sṛptāḥ iti idāgha samaye ca iśāsu api kiraṇa āu vṛttiḥ upalabhyate pratāpa ādi kārya darśaāt stoka āuvṛtteḥ tu durlakṣya tvam śaiśireṣu iva ahar eva etat rātrau dadhāti iti ca etat eva darśayati yadi ca rātrau pretaḥ raśmi ausāreṇa ūrdhvam ākrameta raśmi ausāra āarthakyam bhavet a hi etat viśiṣya abhidhīyate yaḥ divā praiti sa raśmī apekṣya ūrdhvam ākramate yaḥ tu rātrau saḥ apekṣya eva iti atha tu vidvā api rātri prāyaṇa aparādha mātreṇa ā ūrdhvam ākrameta pākṣika phalā vidyā iti apravṛttiḥ eva tasyām syāt atha api rātrau uparataḥ hara āgamam udīkṣeta ahar āgame pi asya kadācid śarīram syāt pāvaka ādi saṃparkāt sa yāvat kṣipya imaḥ tāvat ādityam gacchati iti ca śrutiḥ audīkṣām darśayati tasmāt aviśeṣeṇa eva idam rātriṃdivam dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇāyai adhikaraṇam atas eva ca u dīkṣā upapatteḥ a pākṣika phala tvāt ca vidyāyāḥ aiyata kāla tvāt ca mṛtyoḥ dakṣiṇāyai pi mriyamāṇaḥ vid vā prāpa iti eva vidyā phalam uttarāyaṇa maraṇa prāśastya prasiddheḥ bhīṣmasya ca pratīkṣā darśaāt māsān tāḥ iti ca śruteḥ apekṣitavyam uttarāyaṇam iti imām āśaṅkām prāśastya prasiddhiḥ avidvat viṣayā bhīṣmasya ācāra paripālaa artham pitṛ prasāda labdha svacchada mṛtyu tā khyāpa artham ca śruteḥ tu artham vakṣyati ātivāhikāḥ tad liṅgāt iti ca yatra kāle ca eva yogiḥ prayātā yāti tam kālam vakṣyāmi bharata ṛṣabhaḥ iti upakramya ahar ādi kāla viśeṣaḥ smṛtau aāvṛttaye iyataḥ katham rātrau vā prayātaḥ āvṛttim yāyāt iti atra ucyate yogiḥ prati ca smaryate smārte ca ete yogiḥ prati ca ayam ahar ādi kāla viiyogaḥ a āvṛttaye smaryate smārte ca ete yoga sāṃkhye a śraute atas viṣaya bhedāt pramāṇa viśeṣāt ca smārtasya kāla viiyogasya śrauteṣu vijñāeṣu avatāraḥ agiḥ jyotiḥ ahar śuklaḥ ṣaṣ māsāḥ uttarāyaṇam dhūmaḥ rātriḥ tathā kṛṣṇaḥ ṣaṣ māsāḥ iti ca śrautau etau devayāa pitṛyāṇau pratyabhijñāyete smṛtau api iti ucyate tam kālam vakṣyāmi iti smṛtau kāla pratijñāāt virodham āśaṅkya ayam parihāraḥ uktaḥ yadā puas smṛtau api agi ādyāḥ devatāḥ eva ātivāhikyaḥ gṛhyate tadā kaścid virodhaḥ iti iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye caturtha adhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ murat caturthaḥ udhyāyaḥ tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ tad prathiteḥ arciḥ ādi adhikaraṇam arciḥ ādi iti sarvaḥ brahma prepsuḥ arciḥ ādi eva adhvaā raṃhati iti kutas tad prathiteḥ prathitaḥ hi eṣa mārgaḥ sarveṣām viduṣām tathā hi pañcāgi vidyā prakaraṇe ye ca amī araṇye śraddhām satyam upāsate iti arciḥ ādikā sṛtiḥ śrāvyate syāt etat yāsu vidyāsu a kācid gatiḥ ucyate tāsu iyam arciḥ ādikā upatiṣṭhatām yāsu tu ayā śrāvyate tāsu kim iti arciḥ ādi āśrayaṇam iti atra ucyate bhavet etat evam yadi atyata bhiāḥ eva etāḥ sṛtayaḥ syuḥ ekā eva tu eṣā sṛtiḥ kvacid keacid viśeṣaṇe upalakṣitā iti vadāmaḥ sarvatra eka deśa pratyabhijñāāt itaretara viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva upapatteḥ prakaraṇa bhede pi hi vidyā eka tve bhavati itaretara viśeṣaṇa upasaṃhāra vat gati viśeṣaṇāām api upasaṃhāraḥ vidyā bhede pi tu gati eka deśa pratyabhijñāāt gata vyā bhedāt ca gati abhedaḥ eva tathā hi te teṣu brahma lokeṣu parāḥ parāvataḥ vasati śāśvatīḥ samāḥ sā yā brahmaṇaḥ jitiḥ yā vyuṣṭiḥ tām jitim jayati tām vyuṣṭim vyaśute tat yaḥ eva etam brahma lokam brahmacaryeṇa auvidati iti ca tatra tatra tat eva ekam phalam brahma loka prāpti lakṣaṇam pradarśyate yat tu etaiḥ eva iti avadhāraṇam arciḥ ādi āśrayaṇe a syāt iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ raśmi prāpti para tvāt asya a hi ekaḥ eva śabdaḥ raśmīn ca prāpayitum arhati arciḥ ādīn ca vyāvartayitum tasmāt eva ayam avadhāryate iti draṣṭavyam tvarā vacaam tu arciḥ ādi apekṣāyām api kṣaiprya artha tvāt oparudhyate yathā imeṣa mātreṇa atra āgamyate iti api ca atha etayoḥ pathoḥ iti mārga dvaya bhraṣṭāām kaṣṭam tṛtīyam sthāam ācakṣāṇā pitṛyāṇa vyatiriktam ekam eva prathayati bhūyāṃsi arciḥ ādi parvāṇam prathayati bhūyāṃsi arciḥ ādi sṛtau mārga parvāṇi alpīyāṃsi bhūyasām ca alpīyasām tad prathiteḥ iti uktam vāyum abdāt aviśeṣa viśeṣābhyām vāyu adhikaraṇam saṃiveśa viśeṣeṇa gati viśeṣaṇāām itaretara viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ iti tat etat suhṛd bhūtvā ācāryaḥ grathayati saḥ etam deva yāam pathāam āsādya āgi lokam āgacchati sa vāyu lokam sa varuṇa lokam saḥ idra lokam sa prajāpati lokam sa brahma lokam iti kauṣītakiām deva yāḥ pathāḥ paṭhyate tatra arciḥ agi loka śabdau tāvat eka arthau saṃiveśa kramaḥ vāyuḥ tu arciḥ ādau vartmai iti ucyate tā ṛciṣam eva abhisaṃbhavati arciṣā uhar ahar āpūryamāṇapakṣam āpūryamāṇapakṣa ādyāḥ ṣaṣ udaṅ eti māsān tā māsebhyaḥ saṃvatsaram saṃvatsarāt ādityam iti atra saṃvatsarāt parāñcam ādityāt arvāñcam vāyum abhisaṃbhavati kasmāt aviśeṣa viśeṣābhyām tathā hi sa vāyu lokam iti atra aviśeṣa upadiṣṭasya vāyoḥ śrutyatareṇa viśeṣa upadeśaḥ dṛśyate yadā vai puruṣaḥ asmāt lokāt praiti sa vāyum āgacchati tasmai sa tatra vijihīte yathā ratha cakrasya kham saḥ ūrdhvam ākramate saḥ ādityam āgacchati iti etasmāt ādityāt vāyoḥ pūrva tva darśaāt viśeṣāt abda ādityayoḥ atarāle vāyuḥ iva īśayitavyaḥ kasmāt puarageḥ paratva darśaāt viśeṣāt arciṣoataram vāyuḥ iva īśyate ā eṣa asti viśeṣaḥ iti vadāmaḥ śrutiḥ saḥ etam deva yāam āsādya āgi lokam āgacchati sa vāyu lokam sa varuṇa lokam iti ucyate kevalaḥ tra pāṭhaḥ paurvāparyeṇa avasthitaḥ krama vacaḥ kaścid sti padārtha upadarśa amātram hi atra kriyate etam etam ca āgacchati iti itaratra ratha cakra mātreṇa chidreṇa ūrdhvam ākramya ādityam āgacchati iti avagamyate kramaḥ tasmāt sūktam aviśeṣa viśeṣābhyām iti vājasaeyiḥ tu māsebhyaḥ deva lokam deva lokāt ādityam iti tatra deva lokāt vāyum abhisaṃbhaveyuḥ vāyum abdāt iti tu chadoga śruti apekṣayā uktam chādogya vājasaeyakayoḥ tu ekatra deva lokaḥ a vidyate paratra saṃvatsaraḥ tatra śruti dvaya pratyayāt ubhau api ubhayatra grathayitavyau tatra api māsa saṃbadhāt saṃvatsaraḥ pūrvaḥ paścimaḥ deva lokaḥ iti vivektavyam taḍitaḥ dhi varuṇaḥ sambadhāt taḍit adhikaraṇam ādityāt cadramasam cadramasaḥ vidyutam iti asyāḥ vidyutaḥ upariṣṭāt sa varuṇa lokam iti ayam varuṇaḥ saṃbadhyeta asti hi vidyut varuṇayoḥ yadā hi viśālāḥ vidyutaḥ jīmūta udareṣu praṛtyati atha āpaḥ prapatati vidyotate staayati varṣiṣyati vā iti ca brāhmaṇam apām ca adhipatiḥ varuṇa iti śruti smṛti prasiddhiḥ varuṇāt adhi sthāātara abhāvāt pāṭha sāmarthyāt ca api varuṇa ādīām eva iva īśaḥ vaiśeṣika sthāā abhāvāt vidyut ca atyā arciḥ ādau ātivāhikāḥ tad liṅgāt ātivāhika adhikaraṇam teṣu eva arciḥ ādiṣu saṃśayaḥ kim uta bhogabhūmayaḥ athavā iti tatra mārga lakṣaṇa bhūtāḥ arciḥ ādayaḥ iti tāvat prāptam tad svarūpa tvāt upadeśasya yathā hi loke kaścid grāmam agaram vā gaccha itas tvam amum girim tatas yagrodham tatas adīm tatas grāmam tatas agaram vā prāpsyasi iti evam iha api arciṣaḥ har ahar āpūryamāṇapakṣam ityādi āha atha vā bhogabhūmayaḥ iti prāptam tathā hi agi lokam āgacchati ityādi loka śabdaḥ ca prāṇiām bhāṣyate mauṣya lokaḥ pitṛ lokaḥ deva lokaḥ iti ca tathā ca brāhmaṇam ahar rātreṣu te lokeṣu sajjate ityādi tasmai ātivāhikāḥ arciḥ ādayaḥ aceta a tvāt api eṣām ātivāhika tva aupapattiḥ cetaāḥ hi loke puruṣāḥ durgeṣu mārgeṣu ativāhyāḥ ativāhayati iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ ātivāhikāḥ eva ete bhavitum arhati kutas tad liṅgāt tathā hi vidyutam tad puruṣaḥ māavaḥ saḥ etā brahma gamayati iti siddha vat gamayitṛ tvam darśayati tad viṣayam eva upakṣīṇam iti ced viśeṣaṇasya yadi arciḥ ādiṣu puruṣāḥ gamayitāraḥ prāptāḥ te ca māavāḥ tatas yuktam puruṣa viśeṣaṇam amāavaḥ iti tat liṅga mātram agamakam doṣaḥ ubhaya vyāmohāt tad siddheḥ ye tāvat arciḥ ādi mārga gāḥ te deha viyogāt saṃpiṇḍita karaṇa grāmāḥ iti asvatatrāḥ arciḥ ādīām api acetaa tvāt asvātatryam iti atas arciḥ ādi abhimāiaḥ cetaā devatā viśeṣāḥ atiyātrāyām iti gamyate loke hi matta mūrchita ādayaḥ saṃpiṇḍita karaṇāḥ bhavati a avasthita tvāt api arciḥ ādīnām mārga lakṣaṇa tva upapattiḥ hi rātrau pretasya ahar sva rūpa abhisaṃbhavaḥ upapadyate ca asti iti uktam purastāt dhruva tvāt tu doṣaḥ bhavati arciḥ ādi śabda tā ca eṣām upapadyate arciṣaḥ haḥ ityādi nirdeśaḥ tu ātivāhika tve virudhyate arciṣā hetuā ahar abhisaṃbhavati ahar hetuā āpūryamāṇapakṣam iti tathā ca loke prasiddheṣu api ātivāhikeṣu evaṃjātīyakaḥ upadeśaḥ dṛśyate gaccha tvam itas balavarmāṇam tatas jayasiṃham tatas kṛṣṇaguptam iti api ca upakrame te rciḥ abhisaṃbhavati iti saṃbadha mātram uktam a saṃbadha viśeṣaḥ kaścid upasaṃhāre tu saḥ etāḥ brahma gamayati iti saḥ eva upakrame saṃpiṇḍita karaṇa tvāt eva ca tatra bhoga saṃbhavaḥ loka śabdaḥ tu aupabhuñjāeṣu api gatṛṣu gamayitum śakyate bhogabhūmi tvāt atas agi svāmikam lokam prāptaḥ ativāhyate vāyu svāmikam prāptaḥ iti yojayitavyam katham ātivāhika tva pakṣe varuṇa ādiṣu tad saṃbhavaḥ vidyutaḥ hi adhi varuṇa ādayaḥ upakṣiptāḥ vidyutaḥ tu ā brahma prāpteḥ amāavasya eva puruṣasya gamayitṛ tvam śrutam iti atas uttaram paṭhati tatas tad śruteḥ tatas vidyut abhisaṃbhavaāt ūrdhvam puruṣeṇa brahma lokam gacchati iti avagatavyam saḥ etya brahma lokam gamayati iti tasya eva gamayitṛ tva śruteḥ varuṇa ādayaḥ tu tasya eva vā keacid augrāhakāḥ iti avagatavyam tasmāt sādhu uktam ātivāhikāḥ devatā ātmā orciḥ ādayaḥ iti kāryam bādariḥ asya gati upapatteḥ kārya adhikaraṇam saḥ eā brahma gamayati iti atra vicikitsyate kim kāryam aparam brahma gamayati āhosvit param eva avikṛtam mukhyam brahma iti kutas saṃśayaḥ brahma śabda prayogāt gati śruteḥ ca tatra kāryam eva sa guṇam aparam brahma puruṣaḥ iti bādariḥ ācāryaḥ kutas asya gati upapatteḥ asya hi kārya brahmaṇaḥ gatavya tvam upapadyate pradeśavat tvāt a tu brahmaṇi gatṛ tvam gatavya tvam gatiḥ vai avakalpate sarvagata tvāt pratyagātma tvāt ca gatṛṇām viśeṣita tvāt ca brahma lokāḥ gamayati te teṣu brahma lokeṣu parāḥ parāvataḥ vasati iti ca śruti atare viśeṣita tvāt kārya brahma viṣayā eva gatiḥ iti gamyate hi viśeṣaṇam parasmin brahmaṇi avakalpate kārye tu avasthā bheda upapatteḥ saṃbhavati loka śrutiḥ api vikāra gocarāyām eva bhogabhūmau āñjasī gauṇī brahmā eva lokaḥ eṣa samrāj ityādiṣu adhikaraṇa adhikartavyaiḥ deśaḥ api parasmin brahmaṇi syāt tasmāt kārya viṣayam eva idam kārya viṣaye pi hi samastasya jagataḥ hi samastasya jagataḥ hi brahma iti sthāpitam iti atra ucyate tad vyapadeśaḥ tuśabdaḥ āśaṅkā vyāvṛtti arthaḥ para brahma sāmīpyāt aparasya brahmaṇaḥ brahma śabda prayogaḥ virudhyate param eva hi brahma kvacid kaiścid vikāra dharmaiḥ maomayatva ādibhiḥ aparam iti sthitiḥ kārya prāptau ghaṭate hi parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ yatra saṃbhāvayati darśayati ca pathā pratipadyamāā imam āvartam āvartate iti teṣām iha iti ca atra brūmaḥ kārya atyaye tad adhyakṣeṇa saha atas param abhidhāāt kārya brahmaloka pralaya pratyupasthāe sati tatra eva satas tad adhyakṣeṇa hiraṇyagarbheṇa saha atas para pariśuddham viṣṇoḥ paramam padam pratipadyate iti ittham krama muktiḥ a āvṛtti ādi śruti abhidhā ebhyaḥ abhyupagatavyā a hi añjasā eva gati pūrvikā para prāptiḥ saṃbhavati iti upapāditam smṛteḥ ca smṛtiḥ api etam artham aujāāti brahmaṇā saha te sarve saṃprāpte pratisaṃcare kṛtātmā praviśati param padam iti tasmāt kārya brahma viṣayāḥ eva gati śrutayaḥ iti siddhātaḥ kaṃ puas pūrvapakṣam āśaṅkya ayam siddhātaḥ pratiṣṭhāpitaḥ kāryam bādariḥ saḥ idāīm sūtraiḥ eva upadarśyate param jaimiiḥ mukhya tvāt jaimiiḥ tu ācāryaḥ saḥ gamayati iti atra param eva brahma prāpayati iti kutas mukhya tvāt param hi brahma brahma śabdasya mukhyam gauṇam aparam mukhya gauṇayoḥ ca mukhye saṃpratyayaḥ bhavati darśaāt ca tayoḥ ūrdhva māyā amṛta tvam eti iti ca gati pūrvakam amṛta tvam darśayati amṛta tvam ca parasmin brahmaṇi upapadyate a kārye atha atha para viṣayā eva ca eṣā gatiḥ kaṭhavallīṣu paṭhyate a hi tatra vidyā tara prakramaḥ usti ayatra dharmāt ayatra adharmāt iti parasya eva brahmaṇaḥ prakrāta tvāt a ca kārye pratipatti abhisadhiḥ api ca prajāpateḥ sabhām veśma prapadye iti kārya viṣayaḥ pratipatti abhisaṃdhiḥ te yat atarā tat brahma iti kārya vilakṣaṇasya parasya eva brahmaṇaḥ prakṛta tvāt yaśaḥ ham bhavāmi brāhmaṇāām iti ca sarva ātma tve upakramaṇāt a tasya pratimā asti yasya āma mahat yaśaḥ iti ca parasya eva brahmaṇaḥ yaśaḥ āma tva prasiddheḥ sā ca iyam veśma pratipattiḥ gati pūrvikā hārdavidyāyām uditā tad aparājitā pūḥ brahmaṇaḥ prabhu vimitam hiraṇmayam iti atra padeḥ api ca gati artha tvāt mārga apekṣa tā avasīyate tasmāt para brahma viṣayāḥ gati śrutayaḥ iti pakṣātaram tau etau dvau pakṣau ācāryeṇa sūtritau gati upapatti ādibhiḥ ekaḥ mukhya tva ādibhiḥ aparaḥ tatra gati upapatti ādayaḥ prabhavati a tu mukhya tva ādayaḥ gati upapatti ādī iti ādyaḥ eva siddhātaḥ vyākhyātaḥ dvitīyaḥ tu pūrvapakṣaḥ a hi asati api saṃbhave mukhyasya eva arthasya grahaṇam iti kaścid ājñāpayitā vidyate para vidyā prakaraṇe api ca tad stuti artham upapadyate utkramaṇe bhavati iti vat prajāpateḥ sabhām veśma prapadye iti tu kārye api virudhyate saguṇe api ca brahmaṇi sarva ātma tva saṃkīrtaam sarva karmā sarva kāmaḥ ityādi vat avakalpate tasmāt apara viṣayāḥ eva gati śrutayaḥ pūrvāṇi pūrvapakṣa sūtrāṇi bhavati uttarāṇi siddhāta sūtrāṇi iti etām vyavasthām aurudhyamāāḥ para viṣayāḥ eva gati śrutīḥ pratiṣṭhāpayati tat aupapaam gatavya tva aupapatteḥ brahmaṇaḥ yat sarva gatam sarvātaram sarva ātmakam ca param brahma ākāśa vat sarva gataḥ ca ityaḥ yat sākṣāt aparokṣāt brahma yaḥ ātmā sarvātaraḥ ātmā eva idam sarvam brahma eva idam viśvam idam variṣṭham tasya gatavya tā a kadācid api upapadyate a hi gatam eva gamyate ayaḥ hi ayat gacchati iti prasiddham loke loke gatasya api gatavya tā deśa atara viśiṣṭasya dṛṣṭā yathā pṛthivī sthaḥ eva pṛthivīm deśa atara dvāreṇa gacchati tathā bālasya kāla atara viśiṣṭam vārdhakam svātma bhūtam eva gatavyam dṛṣṭam tadvat brahmaṇaḥ api sarva śakti upeta tvāt kathaṃcid gatavya tā syāt iti a pratiṣiddha sarva viśeṣa tvāt brahmaṇaḥ iṣkalam iṣkriyam śātam a sthūlam a aṇu a hrasvam a dīrgham sa bāhya abhyataraḥ hi ajaḥ sa vai eṣa mahā ajaḥ ātmā aja roma romṛta ubhayaḥ brahma saḥ eṣaḥ eti eti ātmā ityādi śruti smṛti yāyebhyaḥ deśa kāla ādi viśeṣa yogaḥ kalpayitum śakyate syāt bhū vayasoḥ tu pradeśa avasthā ādi viśeṣa yogāt upapadyate deśa kāla viśiṣṭā gatavyatā jagat utpatti sthiti pralaya hetutva śruteḥ a eka śakti tvam brahmaṇaḥ iti ced a brahmanaḥ iti viśeṣaiḥ ākaraṇa śrutīām aaya artha tvāt utpatti ādi śrutīām api samāa amaaya artha tvam iti ced a tāsām ekatva pratipāda aparatvāt mṛd ādi dṛṣṭātaiḥ hi sataḥ brahmaṇaḥ ekasya satya tvam vikārasya ca aṛta tvam pratipādayat śāstram ā utpatti ādi param bhavitum arhati kasmāt utpatti ādi śrutīām viśeṣaiḥ ākaraṇa śruti śeṣa tvam ucyate viśeṣaiḥ ākaraṇa śrutīām hi ātma ekatva etya tva śuddha tva ādi avagatau satyām bhūyas kācid ākāṅkṣā upajāyate puruṣa artha samāpti buddhi utpatteḥ tatra kaḥ mohaḥ kaḥ śokaḥ eka tvam aupaśyataḥ abhayam vai jaaka prāptaḥ asi vidvāa bibheti tapati kim ah sādhu ākaravam kim aham pāpam akaravam ityādi śrutibhyaḥ tathā eva ca viduṣām tuṣṭi aubhava ādi darśaāt vikāra aṛta abhisaṃdhi apavādāt ca mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpoti yaḥ iha paśyati iti atas a viśeṣaiḥ ākaraṇa śrutīām aya śeṣa tvam avagatum śakyam asti pratyakṣam tu tāsām aya artha tvam tathā hi tatra etat śuṅgam utpatitam somya ā idam amūlam bhaviṣyati iti upayasya udarke sataḥ eva ekasya jaga mūlasya vijñeya tvam darśayati yatas vai imāi bhūtāi jāyate jīvati yat prayati abhisaṃviśati tat vijijñāsasva tat brahma iti ca evam utpatti ādi śrutīām aikātmya avagama paratvāt brahmaṇaḥ atas ca gatavya tva aupapattiḥ a tasya prāṇāḥ utkrāmati brahma eva sa brahma apyeti iti ca parasmin brahmaṇi gatim iva ārayati tat vyakhyātam spaṣṭaḥ hi ekeṣām iti atra gati kalpa āyām ca gatā jīvaḥ gatavyasya brahmaṇaḥ avayavaḥ vikāraḥ ayaḥ vā tatas syāt atyata tādātmye yadi evam tatas kim syāt atas ucyate yadi eka deśaḥ iti aprāpta tvāt ca vikāra pakṣe pi etat tulyam vikāreṇa api iti aprāpta tvāt hi ghaṭaḥ mṛd ātmatām parityajya avatiṣṭhate parityāge vā abhāva prāpteḥ vikāra avayava pakṣayoḥ ca tadvataḥ sthira tvāt brahmaṇaḥ atha aya atha atha eva jīvaḥ brahmaṇaḥ saḥ oṇuḥ vyāpī madhyama parimāṇaḥ vā bhavitum arhati vyāpi tve madhyama parimāṇa tve ca aitya tva prasaṅgaḥ aṇu tve pratiṣiddhe ca aṇu tva madhyama parimāṇa tve vistareṇa purastāt parasmāt ca aya tve jīvasya tattvam asi ityādi śāstra bādha prasaṅgaḥ vikāra avayava pakṣayoḥ api doṣaḥ vikāra avayavayoḥ tadvataḥ aya tvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced a mukhya ekatva aupapatteḥ sarveṣu ca eteṣu pakṣeṣu saṃsāri ātma tva aivṛtteḥ vā sva rūpa āśa prasaṅgaḥ brahma ātma tva abhyupagamāt ca yat tu kaiścid jalpyate aimittikāi ca pratyavāya a utpattaye kāmyāi pratiṣiddhāi ca parihriyate svarga araka avāptaye sāṃprata deha upabhogyāi ca kṣipyate iti atas vartamā a dehapātāt ūrdhvam deha atara pratisaṃdhā akāraṇa abhāvāt svarūpa avasthā alakṣaṇam kaivalyam brahma ātma tayā evaṃvṛttasya setsyati iti tat asat pramāṇa abhāvāt a hi etat śāstreṇa ke acid pratipāditam mokṣa arthī ittham samācaret iti sva maīṣayā tu etat tarkitam yasmāt karma aimittaḥ saṃsāraḥ bhaviṣyati iti a ca etat tarkayitum śakyate imitta abhāvasya durjñāa tvāt bahūi hi karmāṇi jātyatara saṃcitāi iṣṭa aiṣṭa vipākāi ekaikasya saṃbhāvyate teṣām viruddha phalāām yugapad upabhoga asaṃbhavāt kāicid labdha avasarāṇi idam jamaḥ irmimate kāicid tu deśa kāla aimitta pratīkṣāṇi āsate iti atas teṣām avaśiṣṭāām kṣapaṇa asaṃbhavāt a yathā varṇita caritasya api vartamāa dehapāte deha atas aimitta abhāvaḥ śakyate karma śeṣa sadbhāva siddhiḥ ca tat ye iha ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ tatas śeṣeṇa ityādi śruti smṛtibhyaḥ syāt etat teṣām kṣepakāṇi bhaviṣyati iti tat a virodha abhāvāt sati hi virodhe kṣepya kṣepaka bhāvaḥ bhavati a ca su kṛtāām iti aaimittikaiḥ asti virodhaḥ śuddhi rūpa tva aviśeṣāt duritāām tu aśuddhi rūpa tvāt sati virodhe bhavatu kṣapaṇam a tu tāvatā sukṛta aimitta tva upapatteḥ duritasya api aśeṣa kṣapaṇa avagamāt ca iti aaimittika āuṣṭhāāt pratyavāya a utpatti mātram a puaḥ phala ātara utpattiḥ iti pramāṇam asti phala atarasya api auiṣpādiḥ saṃbhavāt smarati hi āpastambaḥ tat yathā āmre phala arthe imitte chāyā gadhau utpadyete evam dharmam caryamāṇam iti ca asati samyak darśae sarva ātmanā kāmya pratiṣiddha varjaam jama prāyaṇa atarāle śakyam sūkṣma aparādha darśaāt saṃśayitavyam tu bhavati tathā api imitta abhāvasya durjñāatvam eva a ca brahma ātmatve kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva svabhāvasya ātmaaḥ kaivalyam ākāṅkṣitum śakyam svabhāvasya aparihārya tvāt syāt etat kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva kāryam arthaḥ a tad śaktiḥ kārya parihārāt upapaaḥ mokṣaḥ iti tat ca a śakti sadbhāve kārya prasavasya durivāra tvāt atha api syāt a kevalā śaktiḥ kāryam ārabhate a apekṣya atas ekākiī sā sthitā api āparādhyati iti tat ca iti asaṃbaddha tvāt tasmāt kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva svabhāve sati asatyām vidyā gamyāyām brahma ātmatāyām a kathaṃcaa mokṣam prati asti śrutiḥ ca āyaḥ pathā iti mokṣa mārgam vārayati parasmāt jīvasya sarva vyavahāra lopa prasaṅgaḥ pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa apravṛtteḥ iti ced a prāk prabodhāt svapa vyavahāra vat tad upapatteḥ śāstram ca yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tad itaraḥ itaram paśyati ityādiā aprabuddha viṣaye pratyakṣa ādi vyavahāram uktvā puas prabuddha viṣaye yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kam paśyet ityādinā tad abhāvam darśayati tat evam para brahma vidaḥ bādhita tvāt a gatiḥ upapādayitum śakyā kiṃviṣayāḥ puargati śrutayaḥ iti ucyate sa guṇa vidyā viṣayā bhaviṣyati tathā hi kvacid pañcāgi vidyām prakṛtya gatiḥ ucyate kvacid paryaṅka vidyām kvacid vaiśvāara vidyām yatra api brahma prakṛtya gatiḥ ucyate yathā prāṇaḥ brahma kam brahma kham brahma iti atha yat idam asmin brahmapure daharam puṇḍarīkam veśma iti ca tatra api vāma aī tva ādibhiḥ satya kāma ādibhiḥ ca guṇaiḥ sa guṇasya eva upāsya tvāt saṃbhavati gatiḥ a kvacid para brahma viṣayā gatiḥ śrāvyate yathā gati pratiṣedhaḥ śrāvitaḥ a tasya prāṇāḥ utkrāmati iti brahma vid param ityādiṣu tu sati api āpoteḥ gati artha tve varṇite deśa atara prāpti asaṃbhavāt svarūpa pratipattiḥ eva iyam avidyā adhyāropita āma rūpa pravilaya apekṣayā abhidhīyate brahma eva sa brahma apyeti ityādi vat iti draṣṭavyam api ca para viṣayā gatiḥ vyākhyāyamāā prarocaāya vā syāt aucitaāya vā tatra tāvat gati uktyā kriyate avyavahite vidyā samarpite svāsthye tad siddheḥ a ca iti asiddhaiḥśreyasa eva idam asādhya phalasya vijñāasya kācid apekṣā upapadyate tasmāt apara viṣayā gatiḥ tatra aparasmin brahmaṇi gati śrutayaḥ gati śrutayaḥ parasmin adhyāropyate kim dve brahmaṇī param aparam ca iti bāḍham etat vai satyakāma param ca aparam ca brahma yat oṃkāraḥ iti ādi darśaāt kim puas param brahma kim aparam iti ucyate yatra avidyā kṛta āma rūpa ādi viśeṣa pratiṣedhāt asthūla ādi śabdaiḥ brahma upadiśyate tat param tat eva yatra āma rūpa ādi viśeṣeṇa keacid viśiṣṭam upāsaāya upadiśyate maomayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ bhā rūpaḥ ityādi śabdaiḥ tat aparam evam advitīya śrutiḥ uparudhyeta a avidyā kṛta āma rūpa upādhika tayā parihṛta tvāt tasya ca apara brahma upāsaasya tad saṃidhau śrūyamāṇam sa yadi pitṛ loka kāmaḥ bhavati ityādi jagat aiśvarya lakṣaṇam saṃsāra gocaram eva phalam bhavati tasya ca deśa viśeṣa avabaddha tvāt tad prāpti artham sarvagata tve pi ca ātmanaḥ ākāśasya iva ghaṭa ādi gamae buddhi ādi upādhi gamae gama aprasiddhiḥ iti avādiṣma tad guṇa sāra tvāt iti atra tasmāt kāryam bādariḥ iti eṣaḥ eva sthitaḥ pakṣaḥ param jaimiiḥ iti tu pakṣa atara pratibhā amātra pradarśaam prajñā vikāsaāya iti draṣṭavyam bādarāyaṇaḥ ubhayathā doṣāt tad kratuḥ ca apratīka ālamba adhikaraṇam sthitam etat kārya viṣayā gatiḥ a para viṣayā iti idam idāīm saṃdihyate kim sarva a vikāra ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamba ālamb aviśeṣeṇa eva amāavaḥ puruṣaḥ prāpayati brahma lokam uta kāṃścid eva iti kim tāvat prāptam sarveṣām eva eṣām viduṣām ayatra parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ gatiḥ syāt tathā hi aiyamaḥ sarvāsām iti atra aviśeṣeṇa eva eṣā vidyā atareṣu avatāritā iti evam prāpte pratyāha brahma lokam iti bādarāyaṇaḥ ācāryaḥ a hi evam ubhayathā bhāva abhyupagame kaścid doṣaḥ asti aiyamayāyasya pratīka vyatirikteṣu api upāsaeṣu upapatteḥ tad kratuḥ ca asya ubhayathābhāvasya samarthakaḥ hetuḥ draṣṭavyaḥ yaḥ hi brahma kratuḥ sa brāhmam aiśvaryam āsīdet iti śliṣyate tam yathā yathā upāsate tat eva bhavati iti śruteḥ a tu pratīkeṣu brahmakratu tvam asti pratīka pradhāa tvāt upāsaasya au abrahmakratuḥ api brahma gacchati iti śrūyate yathā pañcāgi vidyāyām gamayati iti bhavatu yatra evam āhatya vādaḥ upalabhyate tad abhāve tu autsargikeṇa tad prāptiḥ iti gamyate viśeṣam ca darśayati āma ādiṣu pratīka upāsaeṣu pūrvasmāt pūrvasmāt phala viśeṣam uttarasmi uttarasmi upāsae darśayati yāvaāmaḥ gatam tatra asya yathākāma cāraḥ bhavati vāc vāva āmaḥ bhūyasī yāvat vācaḥ gatam tatra asya yathākāma cāraḥ bhavati vācaḥ bhūyaḥ ityādiā sa ca ayam phala viśeṣaḥ pratīka tatratvāt upāsaāām upapadyate brahma tatratve tu brahmaṇaḥ viśiṣṭa tvāt katham phala viśeṣaḥ syāt tasmāt itaraiḥ tulya phala tvam iti iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye caturtha adhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ murat caturthaḥ udhyāyaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ sampadi āvirbhāvaḥ sva śabdāt saṃpadi āvirbhāva adhikaraṇam kevalā eva ātmā āvirbhavati a dharma atareṇa iti kutas sve rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate iti sva śabdāt ayathā hi viśeṣaṇam aavaklṛptam syāt ātmīya abhiprāyaḥ sva śabdaḥ bhaviṣyati a tasya avacaīya tvāt yena eva hi keacid rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate tasya eva ātmīya tva upapatteḥ viśeṣaṇam aarthakam syāt ātmavacaatāyām tu arthavat ātma rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate ātma rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate iti kaḥ pūrva avasthāsu iha ca sva rūpa aapāya sāmye sati iti atas āha muktaḥ yaḥ atra abhiiṣpadyate iti uktaḥ sa śuddhaḥ eva ātmā avatiṣṭhate pūrvatra bhavati api roditi iva ca avasthā traya kaluṣitaḥ ātmā iti ayam viśeṣaḥ katham bhavati iti pratijñāāt iti āha tathā hi etam tu eva te bhūyas uvyākhyāsyāmi iti avasthā traya doṣa vihīam pratijñāya aśarīram a priya apriye spṛśataḥ iti ca upayasya svea rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate saḥ uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ iti ca upasaṃharati tathā ākhyāyikā upakrame pi yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā ityādi mukta ātma viṣayam eva phalatva prasiddhiḥ api mokṣasya yat api abhiiṣpadyate iti utpatti paryāya tvam tat api a apūrva avasthā apekṣam yathā iti tadvat tasmāt adoṣaḥ ātmā prakaraṇāt katham puarmuktaḥ iti ucyate yāvatā param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadye iti kārya gocaram eva śrāvayati jyotiḥ śabdasya bhautike jyotiṣi rūḍha tvāt ca a ativṛttaḥ vikāra viṣayāt kaścid muktaḥ bhavitum arhati vikārasya ārta tva prasiddheḥ iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ yatas ātmā eva atra jyotiḥ śabdena āvedyate prakaraṇāt yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā vijaraḥ vimṛtyuḥ iti prakṛte a akasmāt bhautikam jyotiḥ śakyam grahītum prakṛta hāā prakṛta prakriyā prasaṅgāt jyotiḥ śabdaḥ tu dṛśyate tat devāḥ jyotiṣām jyotiḥ iti prapañcitam ca etat jyotiḥ darśaāt iti atra avibhāge dṛṣṭa tvāt avibhāga adhikaraṇam param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya sve rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate yaḥ sa kim parasmāt ātmaaḥ pṛthak eva bhavati uta avibhāge eva avatiṣṭhate iti vīkṣāyām sa tatra paryeti iti adhikaraṇa adhikartavyaiḥ deśāt jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya iti ca kartṛ karmaiḥ deśāt yasya matiḥ tam vyutpādayati avibhaktaḥ eva pareṇa ātmā ā muktaḥ avatiṣṭhate kutas dṛṣṭa tvāt tathā hi tattvam asi aham brahma asmi yatra āyat paśyati a tu tat dvitīyam asti tatas yat vibhaktam yat paśyet iti evamādi darśayati yathādarśaam eva ca phalam yuktam yathā udakam śuddhe śuddham āsiktam tādṛś eva bhavati evam ātmā bhavati gautamaḥ iti ca evamādīi ca evamādi darśayati ca bhedaiḥ deśaḥ tu abhede pi upacaryate sa bhagavaḥ ca evamādi darśa āt brāhmeṇa jaimiiḥ upayāsa ādibhyaḥ brāhma adhikaraṇam sthitam etat svea rūpeṇa iti atra ātma mātra rūpeṇa abhispadyate tu tad viśeṣa bubhutsāyām abhidhīyate svam asya rūpam brāhmam tathā sarvajña tvam sarva īśvara tvam ca sva rūpeṇa abhiiṣpadyate iti jaimiiḥ ācāryaḥ kutas upayāsa ādibhyaḥ tathātva avagamāt tathā hi yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā ityādiā satya kāmaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ iti evamatea upayāsea evamātmaka tām ātmanaḥ bodhayati tathā sa tatra paryeti jakṣat krīḍa ramamāṇaḥ iti aiśvarya rūpam āvedayati tasya sarveṣu lokeṣu kāmacāraḥ bhavati iti ca sarvajñaḥ sarva īśvaraḥ ityādi vyapadeśāḥ ca bhaviṣyati iti tad ātmaka tvāt iti auḍulomiḥ yadi api apahatapāpma tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ tathā api śabda vikalpa jāḥ eva ete pāpma ādi ivṛtti mātram hi tatra gamyate tu asya ātmanaḥ svarūpam iti sva rūpeṇa abhiiṣpattiḥ yuktā tathā ca śrutiḥ evam vai areyam ātmā ataraḥ bāhyaḥ kṛtsaḥ prajñā agha aḥ eva iti evaṃjātīyakā bhaviṣyati satya kāma tva ādayaḥ tu yadi api vastu svarūpeṇa eva dharmāḥ ucyate satyāḥ kāmāḥ asya iti tathā api sva rūpa tva saṃbhavaḥ a eka ākāra tva pratiṣedhāt pratiṣiddham hi parasya ubhaya liṅgam iti atra atas eva ca duḥkha abhāva mātra abhiprāyam stuti artham ātma ratiḥ ityādi vat a hi śakyate varṇayitum dvitīya viṣaya tvāt teṣām śakyate varṇayitum dvitīya viṣaya tvāt teṣām bodha ātmaā abhiiṣpadyate iti auḍulomiḥ ācāryaḥ evam api upayāsāt pūrva bhāvāt avirodham bādarāyaṇaḥ evam api pāramārthika caitaya mātra svarūpa abhyupagame vyavahāra apekṣayā pūrvasya api upayāsa ādibhyaḥ vagatasya brāhmasya aiaiśvarya rūpasya a pratyākhyāāt avirodham bādarāyaṇaḥ ācāryaḥ saṃkalpāt eva tu tad śruteḥ saṃkalpa adhikaraṇam hārdavidyāyām śrūyate sa yadi pitṛ loka kāmaḥ bhavati saṃkalpāt eva asya pitaraḥ samuttiṣṭhati ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kim saṃkalpaḥ eva kevalaḥ pitṛ ādi samutthāe hetuḥ uta imitta atara sahitaḥ iti tatra sati api saṃkalpāt eva iti śravaṇe loka vat imitta atara apekṣa tā yuktā yathā loke saṃkalpāt gama ādibhyaḥ ca hetubhyaḥ pitṛ ādi saṃpattiḥ bhavati evam muktasya api syāt evam dṛṣṭa viparītam a kalpitam bhaviṣyati saṃkalpāt eva iti tu rājñaḥ iva saṃkalpita artha siddhi karīm sādhaātara sāmagrīm sulabhām apekṣya yokṣyate ca saṃkalpa mātra samutthāāḥ pitṛ ādayaḥ maoratha vijṛmbhita vat cañcala tvāt puṣkalam bhogam samarpayitum paryāptāḥ syuḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ saṃkalpāt eva tu kevalāt iti kutas tad śruteḥ saṃkalpāt eva asya pitaraḥ samuttiṣṭhati ityādikā hi śrutiḥ imittātara apekṣāyām pīḍyeta imittātaram api tu yadi eva syāt bhavatu a tu prayata atara saṃpādyam imittātaram iṣyate prāk saṃpatteḥ vadhya saṃkalpa tva prasaṅgāt a ca śruti avagamye rthe loka vat iti sāmāyataḥ dṛṣṭam kramate saṃkalpa balāt eva ca eṣām yāvat sthairya upapattiḥ prākṛta saṃkalpa vilakṣaṇa tvā mukta saṃkalpasya atas eva ca āaya adhipatiḥ atas eva ca avadhya saṃkalpa tvāt vidvāḥ bhavati āsya ayaḥ dhipatiḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ hi saṃkalpaya satyām gatau saṃkalpayati śrutiḥ ca etat darśayati atha yaḥ iha ātmā am vrajati etān ca satyā kāmān teṣām sarveṣu lokeṣu kāmacāraḥ bhavati iti abhāvam bādariḥ āha hi evam abhāva adhikaraṇam saṃkalpāt eva asya pitaraḥ samuttiṣṭhati iti atas śruteḥ tāvat saṃkalpa sādhaam siddham śarīra idriyāṇi prāpta aiśvaryasya viduṣaḥ sati a vā sati iti samīkṣyate tatra bādariḥ tāvat ācāryaḥ śarīrasya idriyāṇām ca abhāvam viduṣaḥ kasmāt evam hi āha kāmā paśya ramate yaḥ ete brahma loke iti yadi maasā śarīra idriyaiḥ ca vihareta syāt tasmāt abhāvaḥ śarīra idriyāṇām mokṣe bhāvam jaimiiḥ jaimiiḥ tu ācāryaḥ śarīrasya api sa idriyasya bhāvam muktam prati yatas saḥ ekadhā bhavati tridhā bhavati ityādiā a ekadhābhāva vikalpam a hi a ekavidha tā śarīrabhede āñjasī syāt yadi api bhūmavidyāyām ayam a ekadhābhāva vikalpaḥ paṭhyate tathā api eva idam saguṇa avasthāyām aiśvaryam bhūmavidyā stutaye saṃkīrtyate iti atas upatiṣṭhate iti ucyate dvādaśa aha vat ubhayavidham bādarāyaṇaḥ ācāryaḥ atas eva ubhaya liṅga śruti darśaāt ubhayavidha tvam sādhu yadā sa śarīra tām saṃkalpayati tadā sa śarīraḥ bhavati yadā tu aśarīra tām tadā aśarīraḥ iti satya saṃkalpa tvāt saṃkalpa vaicitryāt ca dvādaśa aha vat yathā dvādaśa ahaḥ satram ca bhavati ubhaya liṅga śruti darśaāt evam idam api iti tavabhāve sadhya vat upapatteḥ yadā taoḥ sa idriyasya śarīrasya abhāvaḥ tadā yathā saṃdhye śarīra idriya viṣayeṣu a vidyamāeṣu api upalabdhi mātrāḥ eva pitṛ ādi kāmāḥ bhavati evam mokṣe syuḥ evam hi etat upapadyate bhāve jāgrat vat bhāve puaḥ yathā jāgarite eva pitṛ ādi kāmā bhavati evam muktasya api upapadyate pradīpa vat āveśaḥ tathā hi darśayati pradīpa adhikaraṇam bhāvam iti atra sa śarīra tvam muktasya uktam tatra tridhā bhāva ādiṣu kim śarīrāṇi dāruyatra vat sṛjyate kim vā asmat ādi śarīra vat iti bhavati vīkṣā tatra ca ātma maasoḥ bheda aupapatteḥ śarīreṇa yogāt itarāṇi śarīrāṇi iti evam prāpte pratipadyate pradīpa vat āveśaḥ iti yathā pradīpaḥ ekaḥ a eka pradīpa bhāvam āpadyate vikāra śakti yogāt evam ekaḥ api sa vidvāḥ aiśvarya yogāt a eka bhāvam āpadya sarvāṇi śarīrāṇi āviśati kutas tathā hi darśayati śāstram ekasya a eka bhāvam saḥ ekadhā bhavati tridhā bhavati pañcadhā saptadhā avadhā ityādi jīvātara āveśe ca śarīrāṇām pravṛttiḥ saṃbhavati yat tu ātma maasoḥ bheda aupapatteḥ a eka śarīra yoga asaṃbhavaḥ iti ā eṣa doṣaḥ eva aparāṇi śarīrāṇi satya saṃkalpa tvāt srakṣyati sṛṣṭeṣu ca teṣu upādhi bhedāt bhedena adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam yokṣyate eṣā eva ca yoga śāstreṣu a eka śarīra yoga prakriyā katham muktasya a eka śarīra āveśa ādi lakṣaṇam aiśvaryam abhyupagamyate yāvatā tat tu tad dvitīyam asti tatas yat vibhaktam yat salilaḥ ekaḥ draṣṭā advaitaḥ bhavati iti ca evaṃjātīyakā śrutiḥ viśeṣa vijñāam vārayati iti atas uttaram paṭhati sva apyaya sampattyoḥ ayatara apekṣam āviṣkṛtam hi sva apyayaḥ suṣuptam svam apītaḥ bhavati tasmāt eam svapiti iti ācakṣate iti śruteḥ saṃpattiḥ kaivalyam brahma eva sa brahma apyeti iti śruteḥ tayoḥ ayatarām avasthām apekṣya etat kvacid suṣupta avasthām apekṣya ucyate kvacid kaivalya avasthām katham avagamyate yatas tatra eva etat adhikāra vaśāt āviṣkṛtam etebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ samutthāya a pretya saṃjñā asti iti yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva bhūt yatra suptaḥ kaṃcaa kāmam kāmayate a kaṃcaa svapam paśyati ityādi śrutibhyaḥ tu etat svarga ādi vat avasthātaram yatra etat aiśvaryam upavarṇyate tasmāt adoṣaḥ jagat vyāpāra varjam prakaraṇāt asaṃihita tvāt ca jagat vyāpāra adhikaraṇam ye saguṇa brahma upāsa ātmanaḥ saha eva īśvara sāyujyam vrajati kim teṣām iravagraham aiśvaryam bhavati āhosvit sāvagraham iti saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam iraṅkuśam eva eṣām aiśvaryam bhavitum arhati svārājyam sarve smai devāḥ balim āvahati teṣām sarveṣu lokeṣu kāmacāraḥ bhavati ityādi śrutibhyaḥ iti evam prāpte paṭhati jagat vyāpāra varjam iti jagat utpatti ādi vyāpāram varjayitvā ayat aṇima ādi ātmakam aiśvaryam muktāām bhavitum arhati jagat vyāpāraḥ tu iti asiddhasya eva īśvarasya kutas tasya tatra prakṛta tvāt asaṃihita tvāt ca itareṣām paraḥ eva hi īśvaraḥ jagat vyapāra idhi kṛtaḥ tam eva prakṛtya utpatti ādi upadeśāt tam eva prakṛtya utpatti ādi upadeśāt ca tad aveṣaṇa vijijñāsaa pūrvakam tu itareṣām aṇima ādi aiśvaryam śrūyate samaaska tvāt eva ca eteṣām aaikamatye kasyacid sthiti abhiprāyaḥ kasyacid saṃhāra abhiprāyaḥ iti evam virodhaḥ api kadācid syāt atha kasyacid saṃkalpa mau ayasya saṃkalpaḥ iti avirodhaḥ samarthyeta tatas parameśvara ākūta tatratvam eva itareṣām iti vyavatiṣṭhate pratyakṣa upadeśāt iti ced ādhikārika maṇḍala stha ukteḥ atha yat uktam āpaḥ iti svārājyam ityādi pratyakṣa upadeśāt irava graham aiśvaryam viduṣām yāyyam iti tat parihartavyam atra ucyate doṣaḥ ādhikārika maṇḍala stha ukteḥ ādhikārikaḥ yaḥ savitṛ maṇḍala ādiṣu paraḥ īśvaraḥ tad āyattā eva iyam svārājya prāptiḥ ucyate yatkāraṇam maasaspatim iti āha yaḥ hi sarva maasām patiḥ pūrva siddhaḥ īśvaraḥ tam prāpa iti iti etat uktam bhavati tad ausāreṇa eva ca vākpatiḥ cakṣuṣpatiḥ śrotra patiḥ vijñāa patiḥ ca bhavati iti āha evam ayatra api yathāsaṃbhavam iti asiddha īśvara āyattam eva itareṣām aiśvaryam yojayitavyam vikāra āvarti ca tathā hi sthitim āha vikāra āvarti api ca iti amuktam pārameśvaram rūpam asya kevalam vikāra mātra gocaram savitṛ maṇḍala ādi adhiṣṭhāam tathā hi asya dvi rūpām sthitim āha mahimā tatas jyāyāḥ ca puruṣaḥ pādaḥ sya tri pādasya amṛtam divi iti evam ādiḥ ca tat iḥ vikāra rūpam prāpuvati iti śakyam vaktum a tad kratu tvāt teṣām atas ca yathā eva dvirūpe parameśvare iḥ guṇam rūpam a avāpya sa guṇaḥ eva avatiṣṭhate evam sa guṇe api iḥ avagraham aiśvaryam a avāpya sa avagrahaḥ eva avatiṣṭhate iti draṣṭavyam darśayataḥ ca evam darśayataḥ ca vikāra āvarti tvam parasya jyotiṣaḥ śruti smṛtī a tatra sūryaḥ bhāti a cadra tārakam ā imāḥ vidyutaḥ bhāti kutas yam agiḥ iti a tat bhāsayate sūryaḥ a śaśāṅkaḥ a pāvakaḥ iti ca tat evam vikāra āvarti tvam parasya jyotiṣaḥ prasiddham iti abhiprāyaḥ bhoga mātra sāmya liṅgāt ca itas ca aiśvaryam yasmāt bhoga mātram eva eṣām iti śrūyate tam āha apaḥ vai khalu mīyate iti sa yathā etām devatām sarvāṇi bhūtāy avati evam ha evaṃvidam sarvāṇi bhūtāy avati etasyai devatāyai sāyujyam salokatām jayati ityādi bheda vyapadeśa liṅgebhyaḥ evam sati sātiśaya tvāt a tavat tvam aiśvaryasya syāt tatas ca eṣām āvṛttiḥ prasajyeta iti atas uttaram bhagavā bādarāyaṇaḥ ācāryaḥ paṭhati a āvṛttiḥ śabdāt a āvṛttiḥ śabdāt arciḥ ādi parvaṇā pathā ye brahma lokam śāstra ukta viśeṣaṇam gacchati ca ha vai madīyam saraḥ yasmi aśvatthaḥ somasavaḥ yasmi aparājitā pūḥ brahmaṇaḥ yasmin ca prabhu vimitam hiraṇmayam veśma yaḥ ca a ekadhā matra arthavāda ādi pradeśeṣu prapañcyate te tam prāpya a cadra lokāt iva bhukta bhogāḥ āvartate kutas amṛta tvam eti teṣām a puar āvṛttiḥ etea pratipadyamāā imam māavam āvartam āvartate brahma lokam abhisaṃpadyate abhisaṃpadyate ca āvartate iti ādi śabdebhyaḥ tu aiśvaryasya yathā a āvṛttiḥ tathā varṇitam kārya atyaye tat adhyakṣeṇa saha atas param iti atra samyak darśa avidhvasta tamasām tu iti asiddha irvāṇa parāyaṇāām siddhā eva hi saguṇa śaraṇāām api a āvṛtti siddhiḥ iti a āvṛttiḥ śabdāt a āvṛttiḥ śabdāt iti sūtra abhyāsaḥ śāstra parisamāptim dyotayati iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācārya asya śrī govida bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye caturtha adhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ iti śrīmat śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣyam saṃpūrṇam murat
